

Mokṣopāya with Bhāskarakaṇṭha's Ṭīkā

Prakaraṇa Vairāgya

oṃ

svātantryākhyaguṇeritena satataṃ saṅkṣobhyamāṇān nijād icchāmandarakeṇa sārabharitād rūpād alolāt sadā ।
svāntaḥsthaṃ svamayaṃ svabhinnasadṛśaṃ tattvāliratnoccayam bodhāhvaḥ pratibhāsayan parasarinnātho jayaty adbhutaḥ ।।

śuddhaṃ sphāṭikadarpaṇena sadṛśaṃ nityaṃ svaśaktyutthitair acchatvāt svamayīkṛtam bahuvidhair bāhyāntaraiḥ svair malaiḥ ।
śaktyaitān api sarvadātmani layīkurvāṇam ādyaṃ śivam bodhāhvam praṇato asmi devam anaghaṃ ṣaṭkośadāvānalam ।।

bodhābodhavibhedabhāsanaparam bodhānvitair bodhitam bodhābodhavihīnamūrtim amalam bodhaikasāraṃ vibhum ।
bodhābodhavibhedagopanakaraṃ svasmiṃs tu tasyāpy anu bodhaṃ taṃ śaraṇaṃ śrayāmi satataṃ sadbodhasamprāptaye ।।

svacchatvāśrayamātṛbhāvabhajanād vaiḍūryanāmārhatām āsādyānv avatāranāmakalanām etyācchameyāspadām ।
tattvaṃ svam prakaṭaṃ vidhāya ca tataḥ svam bhāvam evāgato yas tasmai satataṃ svabhāvagurave nairguṇyadhāmne namaḥ ।।

acchācchasvavimarśane api kuśalo vaiḍūryanāmnāśrito yāto ato anv avatārabhāvam amalaṃ tattvopadeśecchayā ।
śiṣyāṇām upadiśya tattvam atha yaḥ svaṃ rūpam evāgatas tasmai śrīnidhaye prakāśagurave sadbodhadātre namaḥ ।।

dehādristhamanodrumotthakalanāśākhālisandhyantarād draṣṭuṃ jāḍyaharaṃ vimarśavibhavād unmeṣarūpaṃ ravim ।
lagnā ye satataṃ tadekamayatām paśyanta ātmany atho saṃsāre api ca tatprakāśavaśato bhāte astu tebhyo namaḥ ।।

apūrvaṃ sāmarthyaṃ kim api hṛdayāgocara idam paricchedātītaṃ jayati laghumukhyam bhagavataḥ ।
vivṛttyākhye karmaṇy atimahati vākpatyaviṣaye yadāviṣṭo amuṣminn api bhajati mūko apy adhikṛtim ।।

svataḥsiddhāl labdham paramagahanaṃ yat svajanakād rahasyaṃ saṅkṣepān niratiśayam ābhyantaram alam ।
tad etat sarveṣu prakaṭayitum evātra vihito mayāsāv udyogo na nijadhiṣaṇākhyāpanadhiyā ।।

svabhāvenaivāndhāḥ katicid apare roṣatamasā pareṣāṃ nāpekṣā bhavati ca nijālokavibhavāt ।
ato vyākhyādīpe aprakaṭa iva nātrāsty adhikṛto bhaved vā ko apīti bhramata iha yatnas tu racitaḥ ।।

avatārakaṇṭhaputraḥ pautro vaiḍūryakaṇṭhapādānām ।
bhāskarakaṇṭho racayati vidvatkaṇṭhe vibhūṣaṇaṃ vyākhyām ।।

śaktyādīnām abhāve me pravṛttasya pade pade ।
skhalitāni bhaviṣyanti santu santo avalambanam ।।

nutvā gaṇeśaṃ vibudheśavandyaṃ vāgdevatāṃ ca pratibhāsvarūpām ।
gurūṃs tathā kaulanarottamādīn karomi ṭīkāṃ śrutipātrapeyām ।।

gurūṇāṃ caraṇau smṛtvā kṛtvā svātmārcanaṃ svataḥ ।
mokṣopāyābhidhe granthe vyākhyāṃ kurve samāsataḥ ।।

iha khalu kaścin mahāpuruṣaḥ śrīvālmīkinibaddhaśrīmahārāmāyaṇākhyasāgarādikāṇḍasthaśrīrāmajñānotpādakaśrīvasiṣṭhopadeśaratnaiḥ svayam āsāditasamyagjñānākhyaprakāśaḥ athānyān prati dayayā prakaṭīkaraṇārtham proktasāgarāt tāny uddhartukāmas taduddhṛtinirvighnasamāptigamanāya paradevatāsvarūpam paramātmānaṃ stauti

divi bhūmau tathākāśe bahir antaś ca me vibhuḥ ।
yo avabhāty avabhāsātmā tasmai viśvātmane namaḥ ।।

tasmai prasiddhāya । viśvātmane sarvasāratvena sthitatvāt sarveṣām ātmabhūtāyārthāt paramātmane namaḥ । aparimitāyāṃ tatsattāyām parimitasvasattānyagbhāvarūpaḥ prahvībhāvaḥ astu । tatsattāyām eva svasattāṃ līnām bhāvayāmīti yāvat । tasmai kasmai । avabhāsātmā bāhyāntarālokagatanānāvidhabāhyāntarapadārthavṛndaviṣayajñānasārabhūtaḥ । yaḥ viśvātmā । avabhāti pratyakṣam eva sphurati । yataḥ pratyakṣaṃ sphurantaḥ nānābhāsāḥ vicāraviṣayīkṛtāḥ santaḥ anirvācyatāsvarūpāyām paramātmatāyām eva viśrāmyanti । tataḥ nānāvabhāsāvabhāsena paramātmaivāvabhātīti bhāvaḥ । yaḥ kathambhūtaḥ । me parimitapramātṛtāsādanena cinmātrarūpāparimitapramātṛbhāvāc cyutasyāta eva paricchinnavācakāsmacchabdavācyatāṃ gatasya parimitapramātuḥ । ahantāviṣayatām anīte pradeśe iti yāvat । antaś ca ahantāviṣayatāṃ nīte pradeśe ca । divi samastasurādhārabhūtasvargalokarūpe । tathā bhūmau samastanarādinānāvidhabhūtādhārabhūtabhūlokarūpe । ākāśe śūnyamātrādhārabhūtākāśalokasvarūpe । etena caturdaśabhuvanānāṃ grahaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ । antaś ca kiṃrūpe । divi dyotanamātrasvarūpasvapnāvasthārūpe । bhūmau sthūlatvasādṛśyāj jāgradavasthārūpe । ākāśe śūnyamātrādhāratvasādṛśyāt suṣuptyavasthāsvarūpe । atra ca paramātmanaḥ vyāpakatvaṃ śaktiprādhānyenopādānatayā sthitatvāt svaprādhānyena sākṣitayā sthitatvāc ceti dvividhaṃ jñeyam । evam abhīṣṭasamu-citadevatānamaskāralakṣaṇam maṅgalaṃ kṛtvā uddhariṣyamāṇasyāsya granthasyādhikāryādyanubandhacatuṣṭayaṃ vaktukāmaḥ sa evoddhṛtikāraḥ abhidheyasambandhaprayojanāny arthāt sūcayan adhikārinirūpaṇaṃ sākṣātkaroti ।।

aham baddho vimuktaḥ syām iti yasyāsti niścayaḥ ।
nātyantatajjño nātajjñaḥ so asmiñ śāstre adhikāravān ।।

śrībhagavatkṛpākaṭākṣapātrībhūtasya yasya puruṣasya । ahamparimitapramātṛrūpaḥ aham baddhaḥ svātmabhāvena niścitadehopayogibhogajālāsaktacittaḥ । asmi katham iti śeṣaḥ । proktajālānāsaktacittaḥ kathaṃ syām bhave-yam । iti evam । niścayaḥ manasi satatam anusandhānaṃ । syāt । asminn uddhariṣyamāṇe mokṣopāyākhye granthe । tasyaivedaṃ śāstraṃ vicāraṇīyam ity arthaḥ । nātyantaṃ tajjñaḥ nātyantatajjñaḥ । muktikāmatvena samyagjñānarahita ty arthaḥ । samyagjñānī hi muktim api na kāṅkṣati । kāṅkṣāmātrasyaiva bandhatvāt । punaḥ kathambhūtaḥ । bhogākāṅkṣāyāḥ muktatvāt । atajjño hi bhogākāṅkṣāṃ tyaktuṃ na śaknoti । atyantatajjñe kṛtakṛtyatvāt asmiñ śāstre anadhikāraḥ । atajjñe tu ayogyatayeti vibhāgaḥ । atra paramātmatattvaikyam abhidheyam । pade pade tasyaivābhidhānāt svaviṣayajñānadvāreṇa mokṣākhyaparamaprayojanasādhakatvāc ca । sarvaśāstreṣv abhidheyasyaiva paramaprayojanasādhakatvadarśanāt । tadviṣayaṃ samyagjñānam avāntaraprayojanam । anyathā tatkāṅkṣiṇaḥ amūrkhasyāvāntarādhikāritvaṃ na syāt । paramaprayojaṇam muktir । anyathā tatkāṅkṣiṇaḥ mumukṣoḥ paramādhikāritvaṃ na syāt । śāstrāvāntaraprayojanayoḥ abhidheyaparamaprayojanayoś ca sādhyasādhanabhāvaḥ sambandhaḥ । adhikārī tu svakaṇṭhenaivokta iti sarvaṃ svastham ।।

evam adhikāryādi nirūpya śāstroddhāram ārabhate
vālmīkir uvāca
iti । vālmīkiḥ vālmīkināmā ṛṣiḥ । uvāca uktavān । śrīrāmam prati iti śeṣaḥ । kim uvācety āśaṅkāyām āha
kathopāyān vicāryādau mokṣopāyān imān atha ।
yo vicārayati prājño na sa bhūyo abhijāyate ।।

kathārūpā upāyāḥ kathopāyāḥ । kathānām api samyagjñānam prati pravartakatvenopāyatvaṃ jñeyam । nanu śrīvālmīkiḥ śrīrāmavṛttāntamayaṃ śrīmahārāmāyaṇaṃ śrīrāmam praty eva katham uvācānyasyaiva hy anyavṛttāntakathanam ucitam iti cet । adyakalpe bhavaḥ śrīvālmīkir adyakalpe bhavaṃ śrīrāmam prati purātanakalpaśrīvālmīkikṛtam purātanaśrīrāmavṛttāntamayaṃ śrīmahārāmāyaṇam uvāceti kecid atra samādadhate । kim asmākaṃ vyākhyāmātrapravṛttānām etadyuktatvāyuktatvacintanena । asti cātra kim api nigūḍham bījam api pauruṣam ādeyam ityādivakṣyamāṇaślokasūcitam । tac ca pratibhāvatāṃ svayam eva gamyam । anyeṣāṃ tatkathanam ayuktam । ity alaṃ rahasyodghāṭanena ।।

asmin rāmāyaṇe rāma kathopāyān mahāphalān ।
etāṃs tu prathamaṃ kṛtvā purāham arimardana ।।

śiṣyāyāsmai vinītāya bharadvājāya dhīmate ।
ekāgro dattavān ramyān maṇīn abdhir ivārthine ।।

rāmety āmantraṇam । rāmasyaiva pratipādyatvāt । etān tvayā asmin samaya eva dṛṣṭān । ādau kṛtvā sampādya । asmai agre sthitāya । ekāgraḥ etasya vinayena etasmiṃl lagnacittaḥ । yugalakam ।।

tata ete kathopāyā bharadvājena dhīmatā ।
kasmiṃścin merugahane brahmaṇo agra udāhṛtāḥ ।।

udāhṛtāḥ kathitāḥ ।।

athāsya tuṣṭo bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।
varam putra gṛhāṇeti samuvāca mahāśayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bharadvājaḥ kathayati

bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa varo ayam me adya rocate ।
yeneyaṃ janatā duḥkān mucyate tad udāhara ।।

bhūtabhavyeśātītānāgatayor īśātītānāgatajñeti yāvat ।।

bharadvājavākyaṃ śrutvā śrībrahmā kathayati

guruṃ vālmīkim atrāśu prārthayasva prayatnataḥ ।
tenedaṃ yat samārabdhaṃ rāmāyaṇam aninditam ।।

tasmiñ jñāte naro mohāt samagrāt santariṣyati ।
setunevāmbudheḥ pāram apāraguṇaśālinā ।।

yugalakam । pāram iti pūrvārdhenāpi yojyam । ambudher iti pañcamī brahmavākyam upasaṃharati ।।

ity uktvā sa bharadvājam parameṣṭhī mamāśramam ।
abhyāgamat samaṃ tena bharadvājena bhūtakṛt ।।

parame cinmātrākhye uttame pade tiṣṭhati śuddhamanorūpatvād iti parameṣṭhī ।।

tūrṇaṃ sampūjito devaḥ so arghyapādyādinā mayā ।
avocan mām mahāsattvaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।। [BhG V ]

spaṣṭam ।।

brahmā kathayati

rāmasvabhāvakathanād asmād varamune tvayā ।
nodyogaḥ samparityājya ā samāpter aninditāt ।।

ā samāpteḥ samāptiparyantam ।।

nanu kimartham udyogaṃ na tyajāmīty । atrāha

jñātenānena loko ayam asmāt saṃsārasaṅkaṭāt ।
samuttariṣyati kṣipram potenevātha sāgarāt ।।

athaśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ ।।

vaktuṃ tavaitam evārtham aham āgatavān ayam ।
kuru lokahitārthaṃ tvaṃ śāstram ity uktavān ajaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam । brahmaṇo vākyam upasaṃharati ity uktavān iti ।।

rāma puṇyāśramāt tasmāt kṣaṇād antardhim āgataḥ ।
muhūrtād udyataḥ proccais taraṅga iva vāriṇaḥ ।।

puṇyāśramāt pavitrāt madāśramāt । tasmāt tasmin samaye gṛhītāt । munayo
hi navīnāni navīnāny āśramāṇi gṛhṇanti । yathā vāriṇaḥ udyataḥ pūrvam utthitaḥ taraṅgaḥ । muhūrtād antardhim āgacchati tathety arthaḥ ।।

tasmin prayāte bhagavaty ahaṃ vismayam āgataḥ ।
punas tatra bharadvājam apṛcchaṃ svacchayā dhiyā ।।

bharadvājaṃ kathambhūtam । anyathā pṛcchanam ayuktam eva syād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

kim apṛccha ity । atrāha

kim etad brahmaṇā proktam bharadvāja vadāśu me ।
ity uktena punaḥ proktam bharadvājena me anagha ।।

anagha he doṣarahita rāma ।।

bharadvājaḥ kathayati

etad uktam bhagavatā yathā rāmāyaṇaṃ kuru ।
sarvalokahitāyāśu saṃsārārṇavapotakam ।।

etatpadākāṅkṣām pūrayati yatheti ।।

nanu tatas tava kim ity । atrāha

mahyaṃ ca bhagavan brūhi kathaṃ saṃsārasaṅkaṭe ।
rāmo vyavahṛto apy asmin bharataś ca mahāmanāḥ ।।

vyavahṛtaḥ vyavahāraṃ kṛtavān । apiśabdaḥ asambhāvanādyotakaḥ saṃsārasaṅkaṭe ity anena sambadhyate ।।

śatrughno lakṣmaṇaś cāpi sītā cāpi yaśasvinī ।
rāmānuyāyinas te vā mantriputrā mahādhiyaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nirduḥkhatāṃ yathaite tu prāptās tad brūhi me sphuṭam ।
tathaivāhaṃ tariṣyāmi tato janatayā saha ।।

ete rāmādayaḥ ।।

śrīvālmīkiḥ śrīrāmam prati kathayati

bharadvājena rājendra yadety ukto asmi sādaram ।
tadā kartuṃ vibhor ājñām ahaṃ vaktum pravṛttavān ।।

asmi aham । iti pūrvoktaprakāreṇa । uktaḥ kathitaḥ ।।

pravṛttim eva sphuṭayati

śṛṇu vatsa bharadvāja yathāpṛṣṭaṃ vadāmi te ।
śrutena yena sammoham alaṃ dūre kariṣyasi ।।

alam atiśayena । śṛṇv iti pratijñāṃ sampādayitum prastāvaṃ karoti ।।

tathā vyavahara prājña yathā vyavahṛtaḥ sukhī ।
sarvāsaṃsaktayā buddhyā rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ ।।

sarvāsaṃsaktayā samastaphalāsaṅgarahitayā ।।

na kevalaṃ rāma eva kiṃ tv anye apīty abhiprāyeṇa kathayati
lakṣmaṇo bharataś caiva śatrughnaś ca mahāmanāḥ ।
kausalyā ca sumitrā ca sītā daśarathas tathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kṛtāsthaś cāvirodhaś ca bodhapāram upāgataḥ ।
vasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca mantriṇo aṣṭau tathetare ।।

kṛtāstha iti nāma avirodha iti ca । aṣṭau mantriṇaḥ aṣṭāv amātyās । tathetare anye apy aṣṭau mantriṇaḥ । tena ṣoḍaśa mantriṇa iti paramārthaḥ ।।

itara ity asyārthaṃ sphuṭaṃ kathayati

ghṛṣṭir vikunto bhāmaś ca satyavardhana eva ca ।
vibhīṣaṇaḥ suṣeṇaś ca hanumān indrajit tathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ete aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ proktāḥ samanīrāgacetasaḥ ।
jīvanmuktā mahātmāno yathāprāptānuvartinaḥ ।।

yathāprāptānuvartinaḥ । na tu svaprayatnaniṣṭhā iti yāvat ।।

ebhir yathā hṛtaṃ dattaṃ gṛhītam uṣitaṃ smṛtam ।
tathā ced vartase putra mukta evāsi saṅkaṭāt ।।

ebhiḥ rāmādibhiḥ ।।

bharadvājasya praśnāvasaradānārthaṃ sargāntaślokena tāvat svavākyam upasaṃharati

apārasaṃsārasamudrapātī labdhvā parāṃ yuktim udārasattvaḥ ।
na śokam āyāti na dainyam eti gatajvaras tiṣṭhati nityatṛptaḥ ।।

apāraḥ yaḥ saṃsārasamudraḥ । tatra pātī patanaśīlaḥ । udārasattvaḥ utkṛṣṭadhairyayuktaḥ puruṣaḥ । yuktiṃ dṛśyātyantābhāvajñānalakṣaṇāṃ vakṣyamāṇāṃ yuktiṃ । śokam apekṣālakṣaṇaṃ śokaṃ । tathā dainyam dīnatvam । naiti । pratyuta gatajvaraḥ apekṣāsvarūpajvararahitaḥ । ata eva nityatṛptaḥ tiṣṭhatīti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe prathamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

bharadvājaḥ pṛcchati jīvanmuktasthitim brahman kṛtvā rāghavam āditaḥ ।
kramāt kathaya me nityam bhaviṣyāmi sukhī yathā ।।

brahman śrīvālmīke । jīvanmuktasthitiṃ jīvanmuktamaryādāṃ । āditaḥ kṛtvā । me kathaya śrīrāmavṛttāntadvāreṇa kathayeti bhāvaḥ । nanu kimarthaṃ kathayāmīty । ahaṃ yathā yena jīvanmuktasthitikathanena । nityasukhī jīvanmuktyākhyamahāsukhayukto ।।

śrīvālmīkiḥ śrīrāmavṛttāntaśravaṇādhikāritvasampādanārthaṃ tāvat sāmānyenopadeśaṃ karoti

bhramasya jāgatasyāsya jātasyākāśavarṇavat ।
apunaḥsmaraṇam manye sādho vismaraṇaṃ varam ।।

he sādho । aham asya puraḥ sphurataḥ । jāgatasya jagatsambandhinaḥ । tadviṣayasyeti yāvat । tathā ākāśavarṇavat ākāśanīlimavat । jātasya prādurbhūtasya । mithyābhātasyeti yāvat । bhramasya jagattvajñānarūpasya mithyājñānasya । apunaḥsmaraṇam punaḥsmṛtiviṣayabhāvānayanam । vismaraṇam vismṛtiṃ । upekṣā evātra yuktā । tasyāḥ jāḍyavyāptatvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu tad apunaḥsmaraṇaṃ kenopāyena bhaviṣyatīty । atrāha

dṛśyātyantābhāvabodhaṃ vinā tan nānubhūyate ।
kadācit kenacin nāma sa bodho anviṣyatām ataḥ ।।

nāma niścaye । tad apunaḥsmaraṇaṃ । dṛśyasya ajñānasughanākārā ghanāhaṅkāraśālinī ।
punar janmakarī proktā malinā vāsanā budhaiḥ ।।

paṇḍitaiḥ vāsanā malinā uktā । ajñānena cinmātrājñānena । sughanaḥ ākāraḥ yasyāḥ । cinmātrājñānenaiva hi vāsanā ghanībhavanti । anyathā śuddhacinmātraikyena vāsanā kiṃviṣayā syāt । punaḥ kathambhūtā । yaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ dehādiviṣayaḥ ahambhāvaḥ । vāsanāvaśenaiva hi dehādiniṣṭhaḥ ahaṅkāro ghanībhavati । punaḥ janmakarī punar api bhavakarī । padārthabhāvena vyaktībhāvāt ।।

śuddhāyāḥ svarūpaṃ kathayati

punarjanmāṅkuratyaktā sthitā sambhṛṣṭabījavat ।
dehāntaṃ dhriyate jñātajñeyā śuddheti socyate ।।

paṇḍitaiḥ sā vāsanā । yā dehāntaṃ dehasthitiparyantam eva । na tu tadanantaram api । dhriyate avatiṣṭhate । punarjanmākhyenāṅkureṇa tyaktā । yataḥ sambhṛṣṭabījavat bharjitabījavat । yathā sambhṛṣṭam bījam ākāramātreṇa tiṣṭhati । aṅkurasamarthaṃ na bhavati । tathā śuddhā vāsanāpy ākāramātreṇaiva tiṣṭhati । janmāṅkurotpādanasamarthā na bhavatīty arthaḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtā । jñātaṃ jñeyam avaśyajñeyatvena sthitam paramātmatattvam । yayā hetubhūtayā । śāstravicārādirūpayā śuddhayā vāsanayaiva hi paramātmatattvaṃ jñāyate ।।

śuddhāyā āśrayaviśeṣaṃ kathayati

apunarjanmakaraṇī jīvanmukteṣu dehiṣu ।
vāsanā vidyate śuddhā dehe cakra iva bhramaḥ ।।

jīvanmukteṣu dehiṣu jīveṣu । apunarjanmakaraṇī punarjanmākārikā । śuddhā vāsanā dehe vidyate । yathā bhramaḥ cākrākāreṇa bhramaṇaṃ । jīvanmuktānāṃ vāsanā phalādyanusandhānānutpādikā evāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

jīvanmuktalakṣaṇaṃ kathayati

ye śuddhavāsanā bhūyo na janmānarthabhājanam ।
jñātajñeyās ta ucyante jīvanmuktā mahādhiyaḥ ।।

śuddhā vāsanā yeṣāṃ ।।

sāmānyenopadeśaṃ kṛtvā śrīrāmavṛttāntam ārabhate

jīvanmuktapadam prāpto yathā rāmo mahāmatiḥ ।
tat te aham sampravakṣyāmi jarāmaraṇaśāntaye ।।

nanu kimarthaṃ śrīrāmajīvanmuktiprāptiṃ kathayasīty । śrīrāmajīvanmuktipadaprāptiśravaṇena hi tavāpi tadvyavahārānusāreṇa jarādiśāntir bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu bahūpadeśakāṅkṣiṇo mama kiṃ rāmakramamātrakathanenety । atrāha

bharadvāja mahābuddhe rāmakramam imaṃ śubham ।
śṛṇu vakṣyāmi tenaiva sarvaṃ jñāsyasi sarvathā ।।

sarvathety anena tataḥ kāpy ākāṅkṣā tava na syād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tad eva kathayati

vidyāgṛhād viniṣkramya rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ ।
divasāny anayad gehe līlābhir akutobhayaḥ ।।

divasāni । avidyamānaṃ kuto api bhayaṃ yasya saḥ akutobhayaḥ । nirbhaya ity arthaḥ ।।

atha gacchati kāle atra pālayaty avaniṃ nṛpe ।
prajāsu vītaśokāsu sthitāsu vigatajvaram ।।

tīrthamunyāśramaśreṇīṃ draṣṭum utkaṇṭhitam manaḥ ।
rāmasyābhūd bhṛśaṃ tatra kadācid guṇaśālinaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rāghavaś cintayitvaivam upetya caraṇau pituḥ ।
haṃsaḥ padmāv iva navau jagrāha navakesarau ।।

pādavandanaṃ cakārety arthaḥ ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pitaram prati kathayati

tīrthāni devasadmāni vanāny āyatanāni ca ।
draṣṭum utkaṇṭhitaṃ tāta mamedaṃ hi bhṛśam manaḥ ।।

hi niścaye ।।

tad etām arthanām pūrvāṃ saphalīkartum arhasi ।
na so asti bhuvane tāta tvayā yo arthī vimānitaḥ ।।

mayādya tāvat tava kāpi prārthanā na kṛteti pūrvām ity asyābhiprāyaḥ ।।

śrīrāmaprārthanām upasaṃharati

iti samprārthito rājā vasiṣṭhena samaṃ tadā ।
vicāryāmuñcad evainaṃ rāmam prathamam arthinam ।।

vicāryaiva । na tu vicāram akṛtvā । prathamam arthinaṃ tatpūrvam arthibhūtam ।।

śubhe nakṣatradivase bhrātṛbhyāṃ saha rāghavaḥ ।
maṅgalālaṅkṛtavapuḥ kṛtasvastyayano dvijaiḥ ।।

vasiṣṭhaprahitair vipraiḥ śāstratajjñaiḥ samanvitaḥ ।
snigdhaiḥ katipayair eva rājaputravaraiḥ saha ।।

ambābhir vihitāśīrbhir āliṅgyāliṅgya bhūṣitaḥ ।
niragāt sa gṛhāt tasmāt tīrthayātrārtham udyataḥ ।।

āliṅgyāliṅgyety anena snehātiśayo dyotyate ।।

nirgataḥ svapurāt paurais tūryaghoṣeṇa vardhitaḥ ।
pīyamānaḥ purandhrīṇāṃ netrair bhṛṅgaughabhaṅguraiḥ ।।

grāmīṇalalanālokahastapadmāpavarjitaiḥ ।
lājavarṣair vikīrṇātmā himair iva himācalaḥ ।।

āvarjayan vipragaṇān pariśṛṇvan prajāśiṣaḥ ।
ālokayan digantāṃś ca paricakrāma jaṅgale ।।

paricakrāma pādacāreṇa gatavān । tīrthayātrāyāṃ hi pādacāreṇa gamanam puṇyāvaham ।।

athārabhya svakāt tasmāt kramāt kosalamaṇḍalāt ।
snānadānatapodhyānapūrvakaṃ sa dadarśa ha ।।

haśabdaḥ nipātaḥ ।।

kiṃ dadarśeti karmāpekṣāyām āha

nadīs tīrthāni puṇyāni vanāny āyatanāni ca ।
jaṅgalāni vanānteṣu taṭāny abdhimahībhṛtām ।।

vanānteṣu sthitāni jaṅgalāni sajalāḥ deśāḥ ।।

mandākinīm indunibhāṃ kālindīṃ cotpalāmalām ।
sarasvatīṃ śatadruṃ ca candrabhāgām irāvatīm ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

veṇāṃ ca kṛṣṇaveṇāṃ ca nirvindhyāṃ sarayūṃ tathā ।
carmaṇvatīṃ vitastāṃ ca vipāśām bāhudām api ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

prayāgaṃ naimiṣaṃ caiva dharmāraṇyaṃ gayāṃ tathā ।
vārāṇasīṃ śrīgiriṃ ca kedāram puṣkaraṃ tathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mānasaṃ ca kramasaras tathaivottaramānasam ।
vaḍavām maḍavāṃ caiva tīrthavṛndaṃ sasodaram ।।

tīrthavṛndaṃ kathambhūtaṃ । sasodaraṃ sodarākhyatīrthasahitam ।।

agnitīrtham mahātīrtham indradyumnasaras tathā ।
sarāṃsi sarasīś caiva tathā vāpīhradāvalīm ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

svāminaṃ kārttikeyaṃ ca sāligrāmahariṃ tathā ।
sthānāni ca catuṣṣaṣṭiṃ harasya girijāpateḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nānāścaryavicitrāṇi caturabdhitaṭāni ca ।
vindyakandarakuñjāṃś ca kulaśailasthalāni ca ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rājarṣīṇāṃ ca mahatām brahmarṣīṇāṃ tathaiva ca ।
devānām brāhmaṇānāṃ ca pāvanān āśramāñ śubhān ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhūyo bhūyaḥ sa babhrāma bhrātṛbhyāṃ saha mānadaḥ ।
caturṣv api diganteṣu sarvān eva mahītaṭān ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena tīrthayātrābhramaṇam upasaṃharati

amarakinnaramānavamānitaḥ samavalokya mahīm akhilām imām ।
upayayau svagṛhaṃ raghunandano vihṛtadik śivalokam iveśvaraḥ ।।

īśvaraḥ kathambhūtaḥ । vihṛtadik vihṛtāḥ vihāraviṣayīkṛtāḥ diśaḥ yena । tādṛśaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe dvitīyaḥ sargaḥ ।।

śrīrāmasya gṛhapraveśaṃ kathayati

lājapuṣpāñjalivrātair vikīrṇaḥ pauravāsibhiḥ ।
sa viveśa gṛhaṃ śrīmāñ jayanto viṣṭapaṃ yathā ।।

vikīrṇaḥ bharitaḥ । jayantaḥ indraputraḥ ।।

praṇanāmātha pitaraṃ vasiṣṭham mātṛbāndhavān ।
brāhmaṇān guruvṛddhāṃś ca rāghavaḥ prathamāgataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

suhṛdbhir mātṛbhiś caiva pitrā dvijagaṇena ca ।
muhur āliṅganācārai rāghavo na mamau tadā ।।

rāghavas tadā suhṛdādibhiḥ sahakṛtaiḥ āliṅganācāraiḥ āliṅganarūpaiḥ lokācāraiḥ । na mamau mahānandayukto jāta iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tasmin dṛḍhair dāśarathau priyaprakathanair mithaḥ ।
jughūrṇur madhurair āśā mṛduvaṃśasvanair iva ।।

tasmin dāśarathau mithaḥ priyaprakathanaiḥ śrīrāmaviṣayaiḥ anyo'nyam priyakathanaiḥ । śrīrāmo gṛham prāpta ity evaṃrūpaiḥ parasparam priyakathanair iti yāvat । āśāḥ diśaḥ । jughūrṇuḥ ghūrṇim prāpuḥ । maṅgalavācibhūkampotthānād iyam uktiḥ । priyaprakathanaiḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । dṛḍhais tathā madhuraiḥ karṇasukhaiḥ । priyaprakathanaiḥ kair iva । mṛduvaṃśasvanair iva । yathā taiḥ puruṣāḥ ghūrṇanti । tathety arthaḥ ।।

bahūny āsa dināny atra rāmāgamanam utsavaḥ ।
mahānande janān muñcan kelikolāhalākulaḥ ।।

atra daśarathapure । rāmāgamanam utsavaḥ āsa abhūt । kiyantaṃ kālaṃ । bahudinaparyantam ity arthaḥ । utsavaḥ kiṃ kurvan । janān mahānande muñcan । āseti prayoga ārṣaḥ ।।

uvāsa sa sukhaṃ gehe tataḥ prabhṛti rāghavaḥ ।
varṇayan vividhācārān deśācārān itas tataḥ ।।

itas tataḥ yatra tatra ।।

prātar utthāya rāmo asau kṛtvā sandhyāṃ yathāvidhi ।
sabhāsaṃsthaṃ dadarśendrasamaṃ svapitaraṃ tadā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kathābhiḥ suvicitrābhiḥ sa vasiṣṭhādibhiḥ saha ।
sthitvā dinacaturbhāgaṃ jñānagarbhābhir ādṛtaḥ ।।

jagāma pitranujñāto mahatyā senayāvṛtaḥ ।
varāhamahiṣākīrṇaṃ vanam ākheṭakecchayā ।।

ākheṭecchayā mṛgayākāṅkṣayā ।।

tata āgatya sadane kṛtvā snānādikaṃ kramāt ।
samitrabāndhavo bhuktvā nināya sasuhṛn niśām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

evaṃrūpam ācāram asau naikasminn eva dine kṛtavān api tu sarvadaivety abhiprāyeṇa kathayati

evamprāyadinācāro bhrātṛbhyāṃ saha rāghavaḥ ।
āgatya tīrthayātrāyāḥ samuvāsa pitur gṛhe ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokenaitad upasaṃharati

nṛpatisaṃvyavahāramanojñayā sujanacetasi candrikayā tathā ।
parinināya dināni sa ceṣṭayā śrutasudhārasapeśalayānaghaḥ ।।

saḥ anaghaḥ doṣarahitaḥ śrīrāmaḥ । evaṃvidhayā ceṣṭayā dināni parinināya laṅghitavān । kiṃvidhayā । nṛpativyavahāreṇa prajāvicārādinā rājavyavahāreṇa । manojñayā hṛdyayā । tathā sujanacetasi satpuruṣamanasi । candrikayā sujanahṛdayāhlādikayeti yāvat । tathā śrute śravaṇe । sudhārasavat peśalayā । dṛṣṭatve tu kiṃ vācyam iti bhāvaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe tṛtīyaḥ sargaḥ ।।

athonaṣoḍaśe varṣe vartamāne raghūdvahe ।
rāmānuyāyini tathā śatrughne lakṣmaṇe api ca ।।

bharate saṃsthite nityam mātāmahagṛhe sukham ।
pālayaty avaniṃ rājñi yathāvad akhilām imām ।।

janyatrārthaṃ ca putrāṇām pratyahaṃ saha mantribhiḥ ।
kṛtamantre mahāprājñe tajjñe daśarathe nṛpe ।।

kṛtāyāṃ tīrthayātrāyāṃ rāmo nijagṛhasthitaḥ ।
jagāmānudinaṃ kārśyaṃ śaradīvāmalaṃ saraḥ ।।

tathā ūnaṣoḍaśavarṣe satīty arthaḥ । janyatrārthaṃ vivāhārtham । kārśyaṃ kṣīṇatām ।।

kārśyam eva kathayati

kramād asya viśālākṣam pāṇḍutām mukham ādadhe ।
pākaphulladalaṃ śuklaṃ sālimālam ivāmbujam ।।

kṛśatāyāṃ hi mukhasya pāṇḍimā jāyate ।।

kapolatalasaṃlīnapāṇiḥ padmāsanasthitaḥ ।
cintāparavaśas tūṣṇīm avyāpāro babhūva saḥ ।।

saḥ śrīrāmaḥ ।।

kṛśāṅgaś cintayā yuktaḥ khedī paramadurmanāḥ ।
novāca kasyacit kiñcil lipikarmārpitopamaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

khedāt parijanenāsau prārthyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
cakārāhnikam ācāram parimlānamukhāmbujaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

evam muniviśiṣṭaṃ taṃ rāmaṃ guṇagaṇākaram ।
ālokya bhrātarāv asya tām evāyayatur daśām ।।

muniviśiṣṭam utkṛṣṭam muniṃ । asya tām eva daśāṃ rāmasambandhinīṃ kārśyādirūpām evāvasthām ।।

tathā teṣu tanūjeṣu khedavatsu kṛśeṣu ca ।
sapatnīko mahīpālaś cintāvivaśatāṃ yayau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kā te putra ghanā cintety evaṃ rāmam punaḥ punaḥ ।
apṛcchat snigdhayā vācā na cākathayad asya saḥ ।।

saḥ rāmaḥ ।।

na kiñcit tāta me duḥkam ity uktvā pitur aṅkagaḥ ।
rāmo rājīvapatrākṣas tūṣṇīm eva sma tiṣṭhati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tato daśaratho rājā rāmaḥ kiṃ khedavān iti ।
apṛcchat sarvakāryajñaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ vadatāṃ varam ।।

sarvakāryajñaṃ sarveṣu kāryeṣu nipuṇam । anyathā pṛcchanam ayuktam eva syād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

asty atra kāraṇaṃ śrīman mā rājan duḥkham astu te ।
ity uktaś cintayā yukto vasiṣṭhamuninā nṛpaḥ ।।

śrīmat jñānākhyaphalakāritvāt । kāraṇaṃ vairāgyākhyaṃ kiñcid । asmin samaye vaktum ayuktam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

upasaṃhṛtam api vasiṣṭhavākyaṃ sargāntaślokena punaḥ kathayati
kopaṃ viṣādakalanāṃ vitataṃ ca harṣaṃ
nālpena kāraṇavaśena vahanti santaḥ ।
sargeṇa saṃhatijavena vinā jagatyām
bhūtāni bhūpa na mahānti vikārayanti ।।

santaḥ sādhavaḥ । kāraṇavaśena vitataṃ kopaṃ vitatāṃ viṣādakalanāṃ vitataṃ harṣaṃ ca । na vahanti na dhārayanti । alpeneti viśeṣaṇasya kāraṇety anenārthikaḥ sambandhaḥ । atra vyatirekeṇa dṛṣṭāntam āha sargeṇeti । mahānti bhūtāni mahābhūtāni । sargeṇa vinā mahāsṛṣṭiṃ vinā । tathā saṃhatijavena vinā saṃhārākhyavegena vinā । na vikārayanti kāryotpattyākhyavikārayuktāni tathā nāśākhyavikārayuktāni ca na bhavanti । tat karoti tad ācaṣṭe iti ṇic । vikāravantīti vā pāṭhaḥ । sthityavasthāyām avāntarasargasaṃhatirūpeṇālpena kāraṇena na bhavantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe caturthaḥ sargaḥ ।।

śrīvālmīkir bharadvājam prati kathayati

ity ukte munināthena sandehavati pārthive ।
khedavaty āsthite maunaṃ kañcit kālam pratīkṣiṇi ।।

parikhinnāsu sarvāsu rājñīṣu nṛpasadmasu ।
sthitāsu sāvadhānāsu rāmaceṣṭāsu sarvataḥ ।। etasminn eva kāle tu viśvāmitra iti śrutaḥ ।
maharṣir āgamad draṣṭuṃ tam ayodhyāṃ narādhipam ।।

āgamat āgacchati sma ।।

nanu kimartham asau āgata ity । atrāha tasya yajño atha rakṣobhis tadā vilulupe kila ।
māyāvīryabalonmattair dharmakāmasya dhīmataḥ ।।

rakṣārthaṃ tasya yajñasya draṣṭum aicchat sa pārthivam ।
na hi śakto hy avighnena tam āptuṃ sa muniḥ kratum ।।

nanu kimarthaṃ taṃ rakṣārthaṃ draṣṭum aicchad ity ।।

tatas teṣāṃ vināśārtham udyatas tapasāṃ nidhiḥ ।
viśvāmitro mahātejā ayodhyām abhyayāt purīm ।। [Rām I ]

abhyayāt abhigacchati sma ।।

sa rājño darśanākāṅkṣī dvārādhyakṣān uvāca ha ।
śīghram ākhyāta mām prāptaṃ kauśikaṃ gādhinaḥ sutam ।। [Rām I ]

haśabdaḥ nipātaḥ । kim uvāceti karmāpekṣāyām uttarārdhaṃ karmatvena kathayati śīghram iti । ākhyāta kathayata । gādhinaḥ gādhirājasya ।।

tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā dvāḥsthā rājagṛhaṃ yayuḥ ।
sambhrāntamanasaḥ sarve tena vākyena coditāḥ ।। [Rām I ]

tena vākyena viśvāmitroktena vākyena ।।

te gatvā rājabhavanaṃ viśvāmitram ṛṣiṃ tataḥ ।
prāptam āvedayām āsuḥ pratīhārapatiṃ tadā ।। [Rām I ]

pratīhārapatiṃ dvāsthādhikāriṇam ।।

athāsthānagatam bhūpaṃ rājamaṇḍalam āsthitam ।
samupetya tvarāyukto yāṣṭīko asau vyajijñapat ।।

asau yāṣṭīkaḥ pratīhārapatiḥ ।।

kiṃ vyajijñapad ity । atrāha

deva dvāri mahātejā bālabhāskarasannibhaḥ ।
jvālāruṇajaṭājūṭaḥ pumāñ śrīmān avasthitaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sa cāmarapatākāḍhyaṃ sāśvebhapuruṣāyudham ।
kṛtavāṃs tam pradeśaṃ yas tejobhiḥ kīrṇakāñcanam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vakty asmān āśu yāṣṭīkā nivedayata rājani ।
viśvāmitro muniḥ prāpta ity anuddhatayā girā ।।asau puruṣaḥ asmān anuddhatayā gireti vaktīti sambandhaḥ ।
yāṣṭīkā ity āmantraṇam । yūyam ity adhyāhāryam ।।

iti yāṣṭīkavacanam ākarṇya nṛpasattamaḥ ।
sa samantrī sasāmantaḥ prottasthe hemaviṣṭarāt ।।

hemaviṣṭarāt suvarṇapīṭhāt ।।

padātir eva mahatāṃ rājñāṃ vṛndena pālitaḥ ।
vasiṣṭhavāmadevābhyāṃ saha sāmantasaṃstutaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jagāma tatra yatrāsau viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ ।
dadarśa muniśārdūlaṃ dvārabhūmāv adhiṣṭhitam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kīdṛśaṃ dadarśety apekṣāyām āha

kenāpi kāraṇenorvītalam arkam ivāgatam ।
brāhmeṇa tejasākrāntaṃ kṣātreṇa ca mahaujasā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jarājaraḍhayā nityaṃ tapaḥprasararūkṣayā ।
jaṭāvallyā vṛtaskandhaṃ sasandhyābhram ivācalam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

upaśāntaṃ ca kāntaṃ ca dīptam apratighaṃ tathā ।
nibhṛtaṃ corjitākāraṃ dadhānam bhāsvaraṃ vapuḥ ।।

apratigham apratighātākāram ।।

peśalenātibhīmena prasannenākulena ca ।
gambhīreṇātipūrṇena tejasā rañjitaprajam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

anantajīvitadaśāsakhīm ekām aninditām ।
dhārayantaṃ kare ślakṣṇāṃ vīṇām amlānamānasam ।।

ślakṣṇām peśalām ।।

karuṇākrāntacetastvāt prasannamadhurekṣitaiḥ ।
īkṣaṇair amṛteneva saṃsiñcantam imāḥ prajāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sitāsitatatāpāṅgaṃ dhavalapronnatabhruvam ।
ānandaṃ ca bhayaṃ cāntaḥ prayacchantam avekṣituḥ ।।

avekṣituḥ paśyataḥ । atipeśalatvāt ānandadānaṃ । satejaskatvāt bhayadānam ।।

munim ālokya bhūpālo dūrād evānatākṛtiḥ ।
praṇanāma galanmaulimaṇimālitabhūtalam ।।

galad ityādi kriyāviśeṣaṇam ।।

munir apy avaner īśam bhāsvān iva śatakratum ।
tatrābhivādayāṃ cakre madhurodārayā girā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tato vasiṣṭhapramukhāḥ sarva eva dvijātayaḥ ।
svāgatādikrameṇainam pūjayām āsur ādṛtāḥ ।।

enaṃ viśvāmitram ।।

daśarathaḥ kathayati

aśaṅkitopanītena bhāsvatā darśanena te ।
sādho svanugṛhītāḥ smo raviṇevāmbujākarāḥ ।।

aśaṅkitam śaṅkarāhitam । upanītena prāptena ।।

yad anādi yad akṣubdhaṃ yad apāyavivarjitam ।
tad ānandasukham prāptā adya tvaddarśanān mune ।।

tvaddarśanena vayam brahmānandam prāptā iti bhāvaḥ ।।

adya vartāmahe nūnaṃ dharmyāṇāṃ dhuri dharmataḥ ।
bhavadāgamanasyeme yad vayaṃ lakṣyatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

vartāmahe tiṣṭhāmaḥ । lakṣyatām āśrayatvam । viṣayatvam iti yāvat ।।

evam prakathayanto atra rājāno atha maharṣayaḥ ।
āsaneṣu sabhāsthānam āsthāya samupāviśan ।।

samupāviśan upaviṣṭāḥ ।।

sa dṛṣṭvā jvalitaṃ lakṣmyā bhītas tam ṛṣim āgatam ।
prahṛṣṭavadano rājā svayam arghyaṃ nyavedayat ।। [Rām I ]

nyavedayad arpitavān ।।

sa rājñaḥ pratigṛhyārghyaṃ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।
pradakṣiṇam prakurvantaṃ rājānam paryapūjayat ।। [Rām I b ]

spaṣṭam ।।

sa rājñā pūjitas tena prahṛṣṭavadanas tadā ।
kuśalaṃ cāvyayaṃ caiva paryapṛcchan narādhipam ।। [Rām I d]

spaṣṭam ।।

vasiṣṭhena samāgamya prahasya munipuṅgavaḥ ।
yathārhaṃ cārcayitvainam papracchānāmayaṃ tataḥ ।। [Rām I b ]

spaṣṭam ।।

kṣaṇaṃ yathārham anyo'nyam pūjayitvā sametya ca ।
te sarve hṛṣṭamanaso mahārājaniveśane ।। [Rām I b ]

spaṣṭam ।।

yathocitāsanagatā mithaḥ saṃvṛddhatejasaḥ ।
paraspareṇa papracchuḥ sarve anāmayam ādarāt ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

upaviṣṭāya tasmai sa viśvāmitrāya dhīmate ।
pādyam arghyaṃ ca gāś caiva bhūyo bhūyo nyavedayat ।। [Rām I b;ef]

spaṣṭam ।।

arcayitvā ca vidhivad viśvāmitram abhāṣata ।
prāñjaliḥ prayato vākyam idam prītamanā nṛpaḥ ।। [Rām I -j]

spaṣṭam ।।

yathāmṛtasya samprāptir yathā varṣam avarṣake । [Rām I b]
yathāndhasyekṣaṇaprāptir bhavadāgamanaṃ tathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yatheṣṭadhanasamparkaḥ putrajanmāprajāvataḥ । [Rām I d]
svapnadṛṣṭārthalābhaś ca bhavadāgamanaṃ tathā ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

yathepsitena saṃyoga iṣṭasyāgamanaṃ yathā । [Rām I ]
praṇaṣṭasya yathā lābho bhavadāgamanaṃ tathā ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।। yathā harṣo nabhogatyā mṛtasya punar āgamāt ।
tathā tvadāgamād brahman svāgataṃ te mahāmune ।। [Rām I -h ]

mṛtasya punar āgamād । ity atra yatheti śeṣaḥ । he mahāmune ।।

brahmalokanivāso hi kasya na prītim āvahet ।
mune tavāgamas tadvat satyam eva bravīmi te ।। [Rām I f;]

spaṣṭam ।।

kaś ca te paramaḥ kāmaḥ kiṃ ca te karavāṇy aham ।
pātrabhūto asi me vipra prāptaḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।। [Rām I -d]

he vipra । me pātrabhūtaḥ prāptaḥ ।।

pūrvaṃ rājarṣiśabdena tapasā dyotitaprajaḥ ।
brahmarṣitvam anu prāptaḥ pūjyo asi bhagavan mama ।। [Rām I ]

he bhagavan । pūrvaṃ rājarṣiśabdenaiva pūjyaḥ । anu paścāt । tapasā dyotitaprajaḥ san । brahmarṣitvam prāptaḥ tvam ।।

gaṅgājalābhiṣekeṇa yathā prītir bhaven mama ।
tathā tvaddarśanāt prītir antaḥ śītayatīva mām ।। [Rām I -c]

antaḥ manasi ।।

vigatecchābhayakrodho vītarāgo nirāmayaḥ ।
idam atyadbhutam brahman yad bhavān mām upāgataḥ ।।

mām upāgamānarham iti bhāvaḥ ।।

śubhakṣetragataṃ cāham ātmānam apakalmaṣam । [Rām I ]
candrabimba ivonmagnaṃ vedmi vedyavidāṃ vara ।।

unmagnam uditam ।।

sākṣād iva brahmaṇo me tavābhyāgamanam matam ।
pūto asmy anugṛhīto asmi tavābhyāgamanān mune ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

tvadāgamanapuṇyena sādho yad anurañjitam ।
adya me saphalaṃ janma jīvitaṃ tat sujīvitam ।। [Rām I f]

tvadāgamanāt utpannena puṇyena । me janma me jīvitaṃ ca । yat anurañjitam svoparaktaṃ kṛtaṃ । me janma saphalam bhavati । me jīvitaṃ sujīvitam bhavati ।।

tvām ihābhyāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā pratipūjya praṇamya ca । [Rām I ]
ātmany eva namāmy antar dṛṣṭendur jaladhir yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yat kāryaṃ yena cārthena prāpto asi munipuṅgava ।
kṛtam ity eva tad viddhi mānyo asi hi bhṛśam mama ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

svakāryeṇa vimarśaṃ tvaṃ kartum arhasi kauśika ।
bhagavan nāsty adeyaṃ hi tvayi yat pratipadyate ।। [Rām I b ]

he kauśika । svakāryeṇa saha vimarśaṃ kartum arhasi kim mama kāryam astīti vicāraṃ kartum arhasīti bhāvaḥ । nanu kimartham ahaṃ svakāryeṇa saha vimarśaṃ karomīty । atrāha bhagavann iti । he bhagavan । tvayi yat pratipadyate upayujyate । tat adeyaṃ nāsti । tad dadāmy evety arthaḥ ।।

kāryasya ca vicāraṃ tvaṃ kartum arhasi dharmataḥ ।
kartā cāham aśeṣaṃ te daivatam paramam bhavān ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena daśarathavinayoktyā muner harṣagamanaṃ kathayati

idam atimadhuraṃ niśamya vākyaṃ śrutisukham arthavidā vinītam uktam ।
prathitaguṇavaśād guṇair viśiṣṭaṃ munivṛṣabhaḥ paramaṃ jagāma harṣam ।। [Rām I ]

atimadhuram utkṛṣṭamadhurākhyaguṇaviśiṣṭaṃ । śrutisukhaṃ karṇasukham । arthavidā paramārthajñena daśarathena । vinītaṃ savinayaṃ yathā bhavati tathoktaṃ kathitaṃ । tathā prathitāḥ ye guṇāḥ vākyaguṇās । tadvaśāt guṇaiḥ viśiṣṭam । prathitaguṇaviśiṣṭam iti yāvat । īdṛśaṃ vākyaṃ niśamya saḥ munivṛṣabhaḥ muniśreṣṭhaḥ kauśikaḥ । paramaṃ harṣaṃ jagāma । dātṛvinayena hi arthino mahān harṣo jāyate । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe pañcamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

tac chrutvā rājasiṃhasya vākyam adbhutavistaram ।
hṛṣṭaromā mahātejā viśvāmitro abhyabhāṣata ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

sadṛśaṃ rājaśārdūla tavaivaitan mahītale ।
mahāvaṃśaprasūtasya vasiṣṭhavaśavartinaḥ ।। [Rām I ]

tavaiva na tv anyasyety arthaḥ ।।

yat tu me hṛdgataṃ vākyaṃ tasya kāryavinirṇayam ।
kuru tvaṃ rājaśārdūla dharmaṃ samanupālaya ।। [Rām I ]

tuśabdaḥ vākyavācyasya kāryasyātikaṣṭaṃ sampādanīyatāṃ dyotayati । tasya kāryanirṇayam hṛdgatavākyavācyakāryanirṇayam ity arthaḥ । nanu kimarthaṃ karomīty । atrāha dharmam iti । tavānena dharmapālanam bhaviṣyatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

hṛdgataṃ vākyam prakaṭīkaroti

ahaṃ niyamam ātiṣṭhe siddhyartham puruṣarṣabha ।
tasya vighnakarā ghorā rākṣasā mama saṃsthitāḥ ।। [Rām I ]

ātiṣṭhe āśrayāmi ।।

yadā yadā tu yajñena yaje ahaṃ vibudhavrajam ।
tadā tadā me yajñaṃ taṃ vinighnanti niśācarāḥ ।।

yaje pūjayāmi ।।

bahuśo vihite tasmin mama rākṣasanāyakāḥ ।
akiraṃs te mahīṃ yāge māṃsena rudhireṇa ca ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

avadhūte tathābhūte tasmin yāgakadambake ।
kṛtaśramo nirutsāhas tasmād deśād apāgamam ।। [Rām I ]

apāgamam apagataḥ ।।

na ca me krodham utsraṣṭum buddhir bhavati pārthiva ।
tathābhūtaṃ hi tat karma na śāpas tasya vidyate ।। [Rām I ]

śāpadānena sa yajñaḥ naśyatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

īdṛśī ca kṣamā rājan mama tasmin mahākratau ।
tvatprasādād avighnena prāpayeyam mahāphalam ।।

he rājan । ataḥ mama tasmin mahākratau īdṛśī kṣamā bhavati । ataḥ aham mahāphalam taṃ kratuṃ । tvatprasādāt prāpayeyam prāpnuyām । prāpayeyam iti svārthe ṇic ārṣaḥ ।।

trātum arhasi mām ārtaṃ śaraṇārthinam āgatam ।
arthināṃ yan nirāśatvaṃ satām abhibhavo hi saḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nanu kena prakāreṇāhaṃ tvattrāṇaṃ karomīty । atrāha

tavāsti tanayaḥ śrīmān dṛptaśārdūlavikramaḥ ।
mahendrasadṛśo vīro rāmo rakṣovidāraṇaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nanu tataḥ kim ity । atrāha

tam putraṃ rājaśārdūla rāmaṃ satyaparākramam ।
kākapakṣadharaṃ śūraṃ jyeṣṭham me dātum arhasi ।। [Rām I ]

tenaiva rakṣāparaparyāyaṃ trāṇam me bhaviṣyatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu kathaṃ śiśurūpo asau rākṣasebhyas tava makhaṃ rakṣiṣyatīty । atrāha

śakto hy eṣa mayā gupto divyena svena tejasā ।
rākṣasā ye apakartāras teṣām mūrdhavinigrahe ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

śreyaś cāsmin kariṣyāmi bahurūpam anantakam ।
trayāṇām api lokānāṃ yena pūjyo bhaviṣyati ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

nanu katham asau tādṛśānāṃ rākṣasānām puraḥ sthātuṃ śaknotīty । atrāha
na ca tena samāsādya sthātuṃ śaktā niśācarāḥ । [Rām I b]
kruddhaṃ kesariṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā raṇe vana ivaiṇakāḥ ।।

tena iti dvitīyāsthāne tṛtīyā ārṣī ।।

teṣāṃ ca nānyaḥ kākutsthād yoddhum utsahate pumān । [Rām I d]
ṛte kesariṇaḥ kruddhān mattānāṃ kariṇām iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vīryotsiktā hi te pāpāḥ kālakūṭopamā raṇe । [Rām I b]
kharadūṣaṇayor bhṛtyāḥ kṛtāntāḥ kupitā iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rāmasya rājaśārdūla sahiṣyante na sāyakān । [Rām I d]
anāratāgatā dhārā jaladasyeva pāṃsavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

na ca putragataṃ snehaṃ kartum arhasi pārthiva । [Rām I b]
na tad asti jagaty asmin yan na deyam mahātmanaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

hanta nūnaṃ vijānāmi hatāṃs tān viddhi rākṣasān । [Rām I d]
na hy asmadādayaḥ prājñāḥ sandigdhe sampravṛttayaḥ ।।

hanta harṣe । ahaṃ tān rākṣasān hatān jānāmi । nanu katham ahaṃ tvatkathanamātreṇa jānāmīty । yeṣāṃ ।।

ahaṃ vedmi mahātmānaṃ rāmaṃ rājīvalocanam ।
vasiṣṭhaś ca mahātejā ye cānye dīrghadarśinaḥ ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

yadi dharmo mahattvaṃ ca yaśas te manasi sthitam ।
tan mahyaṃ svam abhipretam ātmajaṃ dātum arhasi ।। [Rām I ]

manasi sthitaṃ kāṅkṣitam । abhipretam proktaṃ kāryārtham iṣṭam ।।

daśarātraś ca me yajño yasmin rāmeṇa rākṣasāḥ । [Rām I d]
hantavyā vighnakartāro mama yajñasya vairiṇaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atrābhyanujñāṃ kākutstha dadatām tava mantriṇaḥ ।
vasiṣṭhapramukhāḥ sarve tena rāmaṃ visarjaya ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

nātyeti kālaḥ kālajña yathāyam mama rāghava ।
tathā kuruṣva bhadraṃ te mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।। [Rām I ]

atyeti gacchati ।।

kāryam aṇv api kāle tu kṛtam ety upakāratām ।
mahad apy upakāreṇa riktatām ety akālataḥ ।।

akālataḥ akāle ।।

ity evam uktvā dharmātmā dharmārthasahitaṃ vacaḥ ।
virarāma mahātejā viśvāmitro munīśvaraḥ ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena daśarathatūṣṇīmbhāvaṃ kathayati

śrutvā vaco munivarasya mahāprabhāvas tūṣṇīm atiṣṭhad upapannam idaṃ sa vaktum ।
no yuktiyuktakathanena vinaiti toṣaṃ dhīmān apūritamano'bhimataś ca lokaḥ ।।

mahāprabhāvo mahānubhāvayuktaḥ । munivarasya viśvāmitrasya । vacaḥ śrutvā tūṣṇīm atiṣṭḥat । no kiñcid apy uktavān ity arthaḥ । idaṃ tūṣṇīm āsanam । yataḥ dhīmān buddhiyuktaḥ । yuktiyuktakathanena vinā vaktuṃ kathayituṃ toṣaṃ naiti । na kathayatīty arthaḥ । apūritamano'bhilaṣitaḥ vaktuṃ toṣaṃ naiti । ataḥ yuktirahitaṃ viśvāmitrasya vākyaṃ śrutvā daśarathaḥ tuṣṇīm abhūd iti bhāvaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ ।।

tac chrutvā rājaśārdūlo viśvāmitrasya bhāṣitam ।
muhūrtam āsīn niśceṣṭaḥ sadainyaṃ caivam abravīt ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

ūnaṣoḍaśavarṣo ayaṃ rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ ।
na yuddhayogyatām asya paśyāmi saha rākṣasaiḥ ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

iyam akṣauhiṇī pūrṇā yasyāḥ patir aham prabho ।
tayā parivṛto yuddhaṃ dāsyāmi piśitāśinām ।। [Rām I ]

piśitāśināṃ rākṣasānām ।।

ime hi śūrā vikrāntā bhṛtyā astraviśāradāḥ । [Rām I b]
ahaṃ caiṣāṃ dhanuṣpāṇir goptā samaramūrdhani ।।

[Rām I b]

spaṣṭam ।।

ebhiḥ saha tavārīṇām mahendramahatām api ।
dadāmi yuddham mattānāṃ kariṇām iva kesarī ।।

hi yasmād । ete bhṛtyā bhavanti । aham caiṣāṃ samaramūrdhani goptāsmi । ataḥ aham ebhiḥ saha tavārīṇāṃ yuddhaṃ dadāmīti sambandhaḥ ।।

bālo rāmas tv anīkeṣu na jānāti balābalam । [Rām I b]
antaḥpurād ṛte dṛṣṭā nānenānyā raṇāvaniḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

na cāstraiḥ paramair yukto na ca yuddhaviśāradaḥ ।
na bhaṭabhrūkuṭīnāṃ ca tajjñaḥ samaramūrdhasu ।।

eṣa iti śeṣaḥ ।।

kevalam puṣpaṣaṇḍeṣu nagaropavaneṣu ca ।
udyānavanakuñjeṣu sadaiva pariśīlitaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vihartum eṣa jānāti saha rājakumārakaiḥ ।
kīrṇapuṣpopakārāsu svakāsv ajirabhūmiṣu ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

adya tv atitarām brahman mama bhāgyaviparyayāt ।
himenevāhataḥ padmas sampanno haritaḥ kṛśaḥ ।।

haritaḥ pāṇḍuḥ ।।

nāttum annāni śaknoti na vihartuṃ gṛhāvanau ।
antaḥkhedaparītātmā tūṣṇīṃ tiṣṭhati kevalam ।।

attum bhakṣitum ।।

sadāraḥ sahabhṛtyo ahaṃ tatkṛte munināyaka ।
śaradīva payovāho nūnaṃ niḥsahatāṃ gataḥ ।।

niḥsahatām utkṛśatāṃ ।।

īdṛśo asau suto bāla ādhinā vivaśīkṛtaḥ ।
kathaṃ dadāmi taṃ tubhyaṃ yoddhuṃ saha niśācaraiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

api bālāṅganāsaṅgād api sādho sudhārasāt ।
rājyād api sukhāyaiṣa putrasneho mahāmate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ye durantā mahārambhās triṣu lokeṣu khedadāḥ ।
putrasnehena santo api kurvate te na saṃśrayam ।।

santaḥ api sthitā api । putrasnehena te vismṛtiṃ gacchantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

asavo atha dhanaṃ dārās tyajyante mānavaiḥ sukham ।
na putrā muniśārdūla svabhāvo hy eṣa jantuṣu ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rākṣasāḥ krūrakarmāṇaḥ kūṭayuddhaviśāradāḥ । [Rām I f]
rāmas tān yodhayatv ittham uktir evātiduḥsahā ।।

kūṭayuddhaṃ chalayuddham । uktir eveti anuṣṭhānasya kā katheti bhā-vaḥ ।।

viprayukto hi rāmeṇa muhūrtam api notsahe ।
jīvituṃ jīvitākāṅkṣī na rāmaṃ netum arhasi ।। [Rām I ]

notsahe samartho na bhavāmi । jīvituṃ jīvanakriyākartṛtām anubhavitum । jīvitākāṅkṣī mama jīvitākāṅkṣīty arthaḥ ।।

navavarṣasahasrāṇi mama yātāni kauśika ।
duḥkhenotpāditās tv ete catvāraḥ putrakā mayā ।। [Rām I ]

anukampitāḥ putrāḥ putrakāḥ ।।

pradhānabhūtas teṣv eṣu rāmaḥ kamalalocanaḥ ।
taṃ vinā te trayo apy anye dhārayanti na jīvitam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sa eva rāmo bhavatā nīyate rākṣasān prati ।
yadi tat putrahīnaṃ tvam mṛtam evāśu viddhi mām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

caturṇām ātmajānāṃ hi prītir atra hi me parā ।
jyeṣṭhaṃ dharmamayaṃ tasmān na rāmaṃ netum arhasi ।। [Rām I ]

nirdhāraṇe ṣaṣṭhī ।।

niśācarabalaṃ hantum mune yadi tavepsitam ।
caturaṅgasamāyuktaṃ mayā saha balaṃ naya ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kiṃvīryā rākṣasās te tu kasya putrāḥ kathaṃ ca te ।
kiyatpramāṇāḥ ke caite iti varṇaya me sphuṭam ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

kathaṃ tena prahartavyaṃ teṣāṃ rāmeṇa rākṣasām । māmakair vā balair brahman mayā vā kūṭayodhinām ।। [Rām I ]

rāmasyāgre sthitatvābhāvāt tenety uktam ।।

sarvam me śaṃsa bhagavan yathā teṣām mayā raṇe ।
sthātavyaṃ duṣṭasattvānāṃ vīryotsiktā hi rākṣasāḥ ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

śrūyate hi mahāvīro rāvaṇo nāma rākṣasaḥ ।
sākṣād vaiśravaṇabhrātā putro viśravaso muneḥ ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

astu saḥ । atrāha

sa cet tava makhe vighnaṃ karoti kila durmatiḥ ।
tat saṅgrāme na śaktāḥ asmo vayaṃ tasya durātmanaḥ ।। [Rām I d]

tat tadā ।।

nanu katham asau tādṛgvīryaḥ astīty । atrāha

kāle kāle pṛthag brahman bhūrivīryavibhūtayaḥ ।
bhūteṣv abhyudayaṃ yānti pralīyante ca kālataḥ ।।

bhūrivīryavibhūtayaḥ mahadvīryasampadyuktāḥ । bhūteṣv iti nirdhāraṇe sap-tamī ।।

adyāsmiṃs te vayaṃ kāle rāvaṇādiṣu śatruṣu ।
na samarthāḥ puraḥ sthātuṃ niyater eṣa niścayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tasmāt prasādaṃ dharmajña kuru tvaṃ mama putrake ।
mama caivālpabhāgyasya bhavān hy asamadaivatam ।। [Rām I ]

alpabhāgyasyeti । anyathā tvaṃ rāmaṃ na yācitavān iti bhāvaḥ ।।

devadānavagandharvā yakṣaplavagapannagāḥ ।
na śaktā rāvaṇaṃ yoddhuṃ kiṃ punaḥ puruṣā yudhi ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mahāvīryavatāṃ vīryam ādatte sa sudhābhujām ।
tena sārdhaṃ na śaktā smas saṃyuge tasya vāvarāḥ ।। [Rām I -d]

ādatte gṛhṇāti । pratibadhnātīti yāvat । mahāvīryān sudhābhujo apy asau vīryarahitān karotīti bhāvaḥ । avarās tadapekṣayā nīcāḥ । vāśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ ।।

nanu rāmasya sajjanatvenaivāvaśyaṃ jayaḥ syād ity । atrāha

ayam anyatamaḥ kālaḥ pelavīkṛtasajjanaḥ ।
rāghavo api gato dainyaṃ yatra vārdhakajarjaraḥ ।।

apiśabdaḥ rāghavasya mahāsajjanatvaṃ dyotayati । vārdhakeneva jarjaraḥ vārdhakajarjaraḥ ।।

atha vā lavaṇam brahman yajñaghnaṃ tam madhoḥ sutam ।
kathaya tvaṃ suraprakhya kveva mokṣyāmi putrakam ।।

atha vā madhoḥ sutaṃ taṃ prasiddhaṃ । yajñaghnaṃ lavaṇaṃ yoddhuṃ na śaktāḥ smaḥ iti vyavahitādhyāhṛtaiḥ saha sambandhaḥ । lavaṇo api cet tava yajñavighnakārī asti tam api yoddhuṃ na śaktāḥ sma iti bhāvaḥ । ahaṃ putrakaṃ kveva kutreva । na mokṣyāmīti bhāvaḥ ।।

atha necchasi ced brahmaṃs tad vidheyo aham eva te ।
anyathā tu na paśyāmi śāśvataṃ jayam ātmanaḥ ।।

atha pakṣāntare । tvam putrāmokṣaṇaṃ cet yadi । necchasi । tadā aham evāgacchāmīty arthaḥ । anyathā sahajavicāre kriyamāṇe । aham ātmanaḥ śāśvataṃ jayaṃ na paśyāmi । na jānāmīty arthaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokena daśarathavacanam upasaṃharati

ity uktvā mṛduvacanam bhayākulo asāv ālole munimatasaṃśaye nimagnaḥ ।
nājñāsīt kaṇam api niścayaṃ mahātmā prodvīcāv iva jaladhau samuhyamānaḥ ।।

munimatasya saṃśaye anuṣṭhānānanuṣṭhānarūpe sandehe । ata eva bhayākulaḥ । mahātmā asau daśarathaḥ । mṛduvacanaṃ komalavacanam । kaṇam api stokam api । niścayaṃ na ajñāsīt na jñātavān । asau kathambhūtaḥ iva । prodvīcau jaladhau samuhyamāna iva । jaladhau samuhyamāno api kutra gacchāmīti niścayaṃ na jānātīti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe saptamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya snehaparyākulākṣaram ।
samanyuḥ kauśiko vākyam pratyuvāca mahīpatim ।। [Rām I ]

tasya daśarathasya ।।

viśvāmitraḥ kathayati
kariṣyāmīti saṃśrutya pratijñāṃ hātum icchasi । [Rām I b]
sattvavān kesarī bhūtvā mṛgatām abhivāñchasi ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rāghavānām ayukto ayaṃ kulasyāsya viparyayaḥ । [Rām I d]
na kadācana jāyante śītāṃśau kṛṣṇaraśmayaḥ ।।

nanu kathaṃ rāghavānāṃ kulasyāyaṃ viparyayaḥ ayukto bhavatīty । atra dṛṣṭāntam āha । na kadācaneti ।।

yadi tvaṃ na kṣamo rājan gamiṣyāmi yathāgataḥ ।
hīnapratijñaḥ kākutstha sukhī bhava sabāndhavaḥ ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

śrīvālmīkiḥ bharadvājam prati kathayati

tasmin kopaparīte atha viśvāmitre mahātmani ।
cacāla vasudhā kṛtsnā surāś ca bhayam āviśan ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

krodhābhibhūtaṃ vijñāya jaganmitram mahāmunim ।
dhṛtimān suvrato dhīmān vasiṣṭho vākyam abravīt ।। [Rām I ]

jaganmitraṃ viśvāmitram ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ kathayati
ikṣvākūṇāṃ kule jātaḥ sākṣād dharma ivāparaḥ । [Rām I b]
bhavān daśarathaḥ śrīmāṃs trailokye guṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nītimān suvrato bhūtvā na dharmaṃ hātum arhasi । [Rām I d]
munes tribhuvaneśasya vacanaṃ kartum arhasi ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

triṣu lokeṣu vikhyāto dharmeṇa yaśasā yutaḥ ।
svadharmam pratipadyasva na dharmaṃ hātum arhasi ।। [Rām I ]

pratipadyasva svīkuru ।।

kariṣyāmīti saṃśrutya tat te rājann akurvataḥ ।
iṣṭāpūrtaḥ pated dharmas tasmād rāmaṃ visarjaya ।। [Rām I ]

iṣṭāpūrtaḥ iṣṭāpūrtasvarūpaḥ । pratijñātākaraṇena hi sarvo dharmaḥ naśyati ।।

guptam puruṣasiṃhena jvalanenāmṛtaṃ yathā । [Rām I d]
kṛtāstram akṛtāstraṃ vā nainaṃ drakṣyanti rākṣasāḥ ।। [Rām I b]

kṛtāstraṃ śikṣitāstram ।।

ikṣvākuvaṃśajāto api svayaṃ daśaratho api san ।
na pālayasi ced vākyaṃ ko aparaḥ pālayiṣyati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yuṣmadādipraṇītena vyavahāreṇa jantavaḥ ।
maryādāṃ na vimuñcanti tāṃ na hātum ihārhasi ।।

tām maryādām ।।

eṣa vigrahavān dharma eṣa vīryavatāṃ varaḥ ।
eṣa buddhyādhiko loke tapasāṃ ca parāyaṇaḥ ।। [Rām I ]

parāyaṇaḥ āśrayaḥ ।।

eṣo astraṃ vividhaṃ vetti trailokye sacarācare ।
naitad anyaḥ pumān vetti na ca vetsyati kaścana ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

na ca devarṣayaḥ kecin nāmarā na ca rākṣasāḥ ।
na nāgayakṣagandharvā anena sadṛśā nṛpa ।। [Rām I ]

spaṣṭam ।।

astram asmai kṛśāśvena paraiḥ paramadurjayam । [Rām I ;]
kauśikāya purā dattaṃ yadā rājyaṃ samanvaśāt ।। [Rām I d]

paraiḥ anyaiḥ । paramadurjayam atyantaṃ jetum aśakyaṃ । samanvaśāt sa-mapālayat ।।

nanu kimarthaṃ kṛśāśvenāsmai astrāṇi dattānīty । atrāha

te hi putrāḥ kṛśāśvasya prajāpatisutopamāḥ ।
enam anvacaran vīrā dīptimanto mahaujasaḥ ।। [Rām I ]

hi yasmāt । prajāpatisutopamās te prasiddhāḥ । kṛśāśvasya putrāḥ । anvacaran anucaranti sma । ataḥ putrasnehena dattavān iti bhāvaḥ ।।

te putrāḥ ke ity apekṣāyām āha

jayā ca suprabhā caiva dākṣāyaṇyau sumadhyame ।
tayos tu yāny apatyāni śatam paramadurjayam ।।

jayā ca suprabhā caiveti ye । dākṣāyaṇyau dakṣasya strīrūpe apatye । sumadhyame striyau । tayoḥ yāni paramadurjayaṃ śataṃ apatyāni āsan । atra ca pūrvaślokāpekṣayottaravākyagatatvād yacchabdasya tacchabdāpekṣā nāsti ।।

nanu kasyāḥ katy apatyāni āsann ity apekṣāyām āha

pañcāśataḥ sutāñ jajñe jayā labdhavarā purā ।
vadhāyāsurasainyānāṃ te akṣayāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ ।। [Rām I ]

akṣayāḥ nāśarahitāḥ ।।

suprabhā janayām āsa putrān pañcāśataḥ parān ।
saṅgharṣān nāma durdharṣān durākrośān balīyasaḥ ।। [Rām I ]

durdharṣān parābhavitum aśakyān । durākrośān śatrubhiḥ samare āhvātum aśakyān ।।

prāsaṅgikam upasaṃhṛtya prakṛtam anusarati

evaṃvīryo mahātejā viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ ।
na rāmagamane buddhiṃ viklavāṃ kartum arhasi ।। [Rām I ]

pūrvārdham uttarārdhasya hetutvena yojyam ।।

sargāntaślokena śrīvasiṣṭho vākyaṃ samāpayati

asmin mahāsattvamaye munīndre sthite samīpe puruṣas tu sādhuḥ ।
prāpte api mṛtyāv amaratvam eti mā dīnatāṃ gaccha yathā vimūḍhaḥ ।।

yathā vimūḍhaḥ । mūḍhavad ity arthaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe aṣṭamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

śrīvālmīkir bharadvājam prati kathayati

tathā vasiṣṭhe bruvati rājā daśarathaḥ sutam ।
samutsraṣṭumanā rāmam ājuhāva salakṣmaṇam ।। [Rām I ]

samutsraṣṭumanāḥ dātumanāḥ ।।

daśarathaḥ pratīhāram prati kathayati

pratīhāra mahābāhuṃ rāmam satyaparākramam ।
salakṣmaṇam avighnena munyarthaṃ śīghram ānaya ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

daśarathavākyam upasaṃharati

iti rājñā visṛṣṭo asau gatvāntaḥpuramandiram ।
muhūrtamātreṇāgatya samuvāca mahīpatim ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pratīhāraḥ kathayati

deva dordalitāśeṣaripo rāmaḥ svamandire ।
vimanāḥ saṃsthito rātrau ṣaṭpadaḥ kamale yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

āgacchāmi kṣaṇeneti vakti dhyāyati caikakaḥ ।
na kasyacic ca nikaṭe sthātum icchati khinnadhīḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ity ukte tena bhūpālas taṃ rāmānucaraṃ janam ।
sarvam āśvāsayām āsa papraccha ca yathākramam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rājapraśnam eva kathayati

kathaṃ kīdṛk sthito rāma iti pṛṣṭo mahībhṛtā ।
rāmabhṛtyajanaḥ khinno vākyam āha mahīpatim ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dehayaṣṭim imāṃ deva dhārayanta ime vayam ।
khinnāḥ khedaparimlāne vibho rāme sute tava ।।

he deva he rājan । dehayaṣṭiṃ dehalatāṃ । rāme rāmākhye । tava sute tava sutanimittaṃ । carmaṇi dvīpinaṃ hantītivat ।।

rāmo rājīvapatrākṣo yataḥprabhṛti cāgataḥ ।
savipras tīrthayātrāyās tataḥprabhṛti durmanāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yatnaprārthanayāsmākaṃ nijavyāpāram āhnikam ।
sāyam amlānavadanaḥ karoti na karoti vā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

snānadevārcanācāraparyante parikhedavān ।
prārthito api hi nā tṛpter aśnāty aśanam īśvaraḥ ।।

ā tṛpteḥ tṛptiparyantam ।।

lolāntaḥpuranārībhiḥ kṛtadolābhir aṅgane ।
na ca krīḍati līlābhir varādbhir iva cātakaḥ ।।

varādbhiḥ sarojalaiḥ । cātakaḥ pakṣiviśeṣaḥ । sa hi varṣābindūn eva pibati ।।

māṇikyamuktāsamprotā keyūrakaṭakāvalī ।
nānandayati taṃ rājan dyauḥ pātavivaśaṃ yathā ।।

pātavivaśam patantam ।।

krīḍadvadhūviloleṣu vahatkusumavāyuṣu ।
latāvalayageheṣu bhavaty ativiṣādavān ।।

latāvalayageheṣu latāmaṇḍalayukteṣu gṛheṣu ।।

yad ramyam ucitaṃ svādu peśalaṃ cittahāri vā ।
bāṣpapūrekṣaṇa iva tenaiva parikhidyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kim imā duḥkhadāyinyaḥ prasphuranti purogatāḥ ।
iti nṛttavilāseṣu kāminīḥ parinindati ।।

imāḥ etāḥ kāminyaḥ ।।

bhojanaṃ śayanam pānaṃ vilāsaṃ snānam āsanam ।
unmattaveṣṭitam iva nābhinandati ninditam ।।

ninditaṃ nindāviṣayīkṛtam ।।

kiṃ sampadā kiṃ vipadā kiṃ gehena kim īhitaiḥ ।
sarvam evāsad ity uktvā tūṣṇīm eko avatiṣṭhate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nodeti parihāseṣu na bhogeṣu nimajjati ।
na ca tiṣṭhati kāryeṣu maunam evāvalambate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vilolālakavallaryo helāvalitalocanāḥ ।
nānandayanti taṃ nāryo mṛgyo vanataruṃ yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ekānteṣu diganteṣu tīreṣu vipineṣu ca ।
ratim āyāty araṇyeṣu vikrītavad ajantuṣu ।।

vikrīto hi palāyanārthaṃ janturahite eva deśe ratim āyāti ।।

vastrapānāśanādānaparāṅmukhatayā tayā ।
parivraḍdharmiṇāṃ rājan so anuyāti tapasvinām ।।

tapasvinām anuyāti tapasvisambandhicaritam anukarotīty arthaḥ । na māṣāṇām aśnīyād itivat prayogaḥ ।।

eka eva vasan deśe janaśūnye janeśvara ।
na hasaty ekayā buddhyā na gāyati na roditi ।।

ekayā buddhyā sarvatyāgarūpayā matyā upalakṣitaḥ ।।

punaḥ kiṃ karotīty apekṣāyām āha

baddhapadmāsanaḥ śūnyamanā vāmakarasthale ।
kapolatalam ādāya kevalam paritiṣṭhati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nābhimānam upādatte nāpi vāñchati rājatām ।
nodeti nāstam āyāti sukhaduḥkhānuvṛttiṣu ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

na vidmaḥ kim asau jātaḥ kiṃ karoti kim īhate ।
kiṃ dhyāyati kim āyāti kathaṃ kim anudhāvati ।।

na vidma ity asya karmāpekṣāyām āha kim asau jātaḥ kimartham asau jātaḥ । jananaṃ hi bhogādisevanārtham iti bhāvaḥ ।।

pratyahaṃ kṛśatāṃ yāti pratyahaṃ yāti pāṇḍutām ।
virāgam pratyahaṃ yāti śaradanta iva drumaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

anuyātau tam evaitau rājañ śatrughnalakṣmaṇau ।
tādṛśāv eva tasyaiva pratibimbāv iva sthitau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhṛtyai rājabhir ambābhiḥ sa pṛṣṭo api punaḥ punaḥ ।
uktvā na kiñcid eveti tūṣṇīm āste nirīhitaḥ ।।

saḥ śrīrāmaḥ । nirīhitaḥ ceṣṭitarahitaḥ । itiśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ śrīrāmottaravākyasvarūpanirdeśaparo vā jñeyaḥ ।।

āpātamātrahṛdyeṣu mā bhogeṣu manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।
iti pārśvagatam bhavyam anuśāsti suhṛjjanam ।।

bhavyam anuśāsanayogyam ।।

nānāvibhavaramyāsu strīṣu goṣṭhīkathāsu ca ।
puraḥsthitam ivāsneho nāśam evānupaśyati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rītimādhuryasāyāsapadasaṃsthitivarjitaiḥ ।
ceṣṭitair eva kākalyā bhūyo bhūyaḥ pragāyati ।।

saḥ rāmaḥ । rītimādhuryasāyāsapadasaṃsthitivarjitaiḥ ceṣṭitair eva kevalaiḥ abhinayair evopalakṣitayā kākalyā kalasūkṣmadhvaninā । gāyati ।।

samrāḍ bhaveti pārśvasthaṃ vadantam anujīvinam ।
pralapantam ivonmattaṃ hasaty anyamanā muniḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

na proktam ākarṇayati prekṣate na purogatam ।
karoty avajñāṃ sarvatra sumahaty api vastuni ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

apy ākāśasarojinyām apy ākāśamahāvane ।
ittham etat katham iti vismayo asya na jāyate ।।

vismayasya svarūpaṃ darśayati ittham etat katham iti ।।

kāntāmadhyagatasyāpi mano asya madaneṣavaḥ ।
na bhedayanti durbhedaṃ dhārā iva mahopalam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

āpadām ekam āvāsam abhivāñchasi kiṃ dhanam ।
anuśāsyeti sarvasvam arthine samprayacchati ।।

anuśāsya anuśāsanaṃ kṛtvā ।।

iyam āpad iyaṃ saṃpad ity ayaṃ kalpanāmayaḥ ।
manasy abhyudito moha iti śokāt pragāyati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

hā hato aham anātho aham ity ākrandaparo api san ।
na jano yāti vairāgyaṃ citram ity eva vakty asau ।।

ākrandaparasya vairāgyaṃ yuktam evety apiśabdena dyotyate ।।

raghukānanasālena rāmeṇa ripughātinā ।
bhṛśam itthaṃ sthitenaiva vayaṃ khedam upāgatāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

na vidmaḥ kim mahābāho tasya tādṛśacetasaḥ ।
kurmaḥ kamalapatrākṣa gatir atra hi no bhavān ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rājānam atha vā vipram upadeṣṭāram agragam ।
hasan paśum ivāvyagraḥ so avadhīrayati prabho ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

prapañco ayam iha sphāraṃ jagannāma yad utthitam ।
naitad vastu na caivāham iti nirṇīya saṃsthitaḥ ।।

yaḥ ayam prapañcaḥ utthitam idaṃ sphāraṃ jagannāma bhavati । etad vastu paramārthasat । na bhavati । evaśabdaḥ apiśabdasyārthe । aham api vastu na ca bhavāmi । nirṇīyāsau rāmaḥ saṃsthitaḥ ।।

nārau nātmani no mitre na rājye na ca mātari ।
na saṃpadāpador nāntas tasyāsthā na vibhor bahiḥ ।।

āsthā ratiḥ ।।

nirastāstho nirāśo asau nirīho asau nirāspadaḥ ।
mohe na ca vimukto asau tena tapyāmahe vayam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kiṃ dhanena kim ambābhiḥ kiṃ rājyena kim īhayā ।
iti niścayavān antaḥ prāṇatyāgamanāḥ sthitaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhogeṣv āyuṣi rājye ca mitre pitari mātari ।
param udvegam āyātaś cātako avagrahe yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tasya tādṛksvabhāvasya samagravibhavānvitam ।
saṃsārajālam ābhogi prabho prativiṣāyate ।।

prativiṣam ivācarate prativiṣāyate ।।

tādṛśaḥ syān mahāsattvaḥ ka ivāsmin mahītale ।
prakṛte vyavahāre taṃ yo niveśayituṃ kṣamaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

iti no yeyam āyātā śākhāprasaraśālinī ।
āpat tām alam uddhartuṃ samudetu dayā parā ।।

samudetu taveti śeṣaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokena rāmabhṛtyavacanaṃ samāpayati

manasi moham apāsya mahāmanāḥ sakalam ārtimataḥ kila sādhutām ।
saphalatāṃ nayatīha tamo haran dinakaro bhuvi bhāskaratām iva ।।

mahāmanāḥ puruṣaḥ । ārtimataḥ ārtiyuktasya puruṣasya । manasi sakalam moham ārtisvarūpaṃ samastam moham । sādhutām svasmin sthitaṃ sādhubhāvaṃ । ka iva । yathā dinakaraḥ bhuvi tamaḥ haran bhāskaratām saphalatāṃ nayati । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe navamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

rāmabhṛtyavacanaṃ śrutvā viśvāmitraḥ kathayati

evaṃ cet tan mahāprājñam bhavanto raghunandanam ।
ihānayantu tvaritaṃ hariṇaṃ hariṇā iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

eṣa moho raghupater nāpadbhyo na ca rāgataḥ ।
vivekavairāgyakṛto bodha eṣa mahodayaḥ ।।

mahān udayaḥ muktilakṣaṇaḥ yasmāt saḥ mahodayaḥ ।।

ihāyātu kṣaṇād rāmas tad ihaiva vayaṃ kṣaṇāt ।
mohaṃ tasyāpaneṣyāmo maruto adrer ghanaṃ yathā ।।

vayaṃ ke iva । yathā marutaḥ vāyavaḥ । adreḥ ghanaṃ megham ।।

etasmin mārjite yuktyā mohe ca raghunandanaḥ ।
viśrāntim eṣyati pade tasmin vayam ivottame ।।

tasmin pade cinmātrākhye viśrāntisthāne ।।

satyatām muditām prajñāṃ viśrāntiṃ ca sametya saḥ ।
pīnatāṃ varavarṇatvam pītāmṛta ivaiṣyati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nijāṃ ca prakṛtām eva vyavahāraparamparām ।
paripūrṇamanā mānya ācariṣyaty akhaṇḍitām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhaviṣyati mahāsattvo jñātalokaparāvaraḥ ।
sukhaduḥkhadaśāhīnaḥ samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥ ।। [BhG VI; XIV ]

jñāte samyak niścite । lokānām parāvare parāvācī । pāradvayam iti yāvat ।।

viśvāmitravākyam upasaṃharati

ity ukte munināthena rājā sampūrṇamānasaḥ ।
prāhiṇod rāmam ānetum bhūyo dūtaparamparām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

etāvatā ca kālena rāmo nijagṛhāsanāt ।
pituḥ sakāśam āgantum utthito arka ivācalāt ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vṛtaḥ katipayair bhṛtyair bhrātṛbhyāṃ cājagāma ha ।
tat puṇyam pitur āsthānaṃ svargaṃ surapater iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dūrād eva dadarśāsau rāmo daśarathaṃ tadā ।
vṛtaṃ rājasamūhena devaugheneva vāsavam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vasiṣṭhaviśvāmitrābhyāṃ sevitam pārśvayor dvayoḥ ।
sarvaśāstrārthatajjñena mantrivṛndena pālitam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

cārucāmarahastābhiḥ kāntābhiḥ samupāsitam ।
kakubbhir iva mūrtābhiḥ saṃsthitābhir yathocitam ।।

kakubbhiḥ digbhiḥ ।। vasiṣṭhaviśvāmitrādyās tathā daśarathādayaḥ ।
dadṛśū rāghavaṃ dūrād upāyāntaṃ guhopamam ।।

guhopamaṃ kumārasadṛśam ।।

sattvāvaṣṭambhagarveṇa śaityeneva himālayam ।
śritaṃ sakalasevyena gambhīreṇa svareṇa ca ।।

sattvasyāvaṣṭambhena hastāvalambena yaḥ garvaḥ । pūrvasya ślokasya viśeṣaṇatvena yojyam ।।

saumyaṃ samaśubhākāraṃ vinayodāram ūrjitam ।
kāntopaśāntavapuṣam parasyārthasya bhājanam ।।

parasyārthasya mokṣasya ।।

samudyadyauvanārambham udyogaśamaśobhitam ।
anudvignam anāyāsam pūrṇaprāyamanoratham ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vicāritajagadyātram pavitraguṇagocaram ।
mahāsattvaikalobhena guṇair iva samāśritam ।।

mahāsattvasya mahādhairyasya । tatsaṅgalobhaḥ iti yāvat ।।

udārasāram āpūrṇam antaḥkaraṇakoṭaram ।
avikṣubhitayā vṛttyā darśayantam anuttamam ।।

rāmam punaḥ kathambhūtam । īdṛśyā vṛttyā īdṛśam antaḥkaraṇaṃ darśayantam iti sambandhaḥ । āpūrṇam bhogān prati alaulyena samantāt pūrṇam ।।

śrīrāmaviśeṣaṇāny upasaṃharati

evam guṇagaṇākīrṇo dūrād eva raghūdvahaḥ ।
parimeyasitācchācchasvahārāmbarapallavaḥ ।।

praṇanāma calaccārucūḍāmaṇimarīcinā ।
śirasā vasudhākampalolamānācalaśriyā ।।

parimeyāḥ parimitāḥ । sitāḥ acchācchāḥ svahārāmbarapallavāḥ yasya । saḥ tādṛśaḥ । śirasā kathambhūtena । vasudhāyāṃ yaḥ kampaḥ । tena lolamānasyā-calasya śrīḥ yasya । tat ।।

kān praṇanāmety apekṣāyām āha

prathamam pitaram paścān munīn mānyaikam ānataḥ ।
tato viprāṃs tato bandhūṃs tato adhikaguṇān gurūn ।।

pitaraṃ kathambhūtaṃ । mānyānām madhye ekam mānyaikam ।।

jagrāha cātmanā dṛṣṭvā manāk svādugirā tathā ।
rājalokena vihitāṃ sa praṇāmaparasparām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vihitāśīr munibhyāṃ tu rāmaḥ saśamamānasaḥ ।
āsasāda pituḥ puṇyaṃ samīpaṃ surasundaraḥ ।।

samīpaṃ nikaṭam ।।

pādābhivandanarataṃ tam athāsau mahīpatiḥ ।
śirasy abhyāliliṅgāśu cucumba ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।

śatrughnaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva tathaiva paravīrahā ।
āliliṅga ghanasnehaṃ rājahaṃso ambujaṃ yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

utsaṅge vatsa tiṣṭheti vadaty atha mahīpatau ।
bhūmau parijanāstīrṇe so aṃśuke atha nyavikṣata ।।

nyavikṣata upāviśat । athaśabdadvayaṃ sambandhibhedenānantaryadvayavācakam ।।

daśarathaḥ kathayati

putra prāptavivekas tvaṃ kalyāṇānāṃ ca bhājanam ।
janavaj jīrṇayā buddhyā khedāyātmā na dīyate ।।

tvayā na dīyate na deya ity arthaḥ । khedāyeti sampradāne caturthī ।।

vṛddhavipraguruproktaṃ tvādṛśenānutiṣṭhatā ।
padam āsādyate puṇyaṃ na moham anudhāvatā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tāvad evāpado dūre tiṣṭhanti paripelavāḥ ।
yāvad eva na mohasya prasaraḥ putra dīyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ kathayati

rājaputra mahābāho śūras tvaṃ vijitās tvayā ।
durucchedā durārambhā apy amī viṣayārayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kim atajjña ivājñānāṃ yogye vā mohasāgare ।
vinimajjasi kallolagahane jāḍyaśālini ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

viśvāmitra āha

calannīlotpalavyūhasamalocana lolatām ।
brūhi cetaḥkṛtāṃ tyaktvā hetunā kena muhyasi ।।

he calannīlotpalavyūhasamalocana tvaṃ । cetaḥkṛtāṃ lolatāṃ tyaktvā brūhi । karmāpekṣāyāṃ vākyaṃ karmatvena kathayati hetuneti । tvaṃ kimarthaṃ muhyasīty arthaḥ ।।

kiṃniṣṭhāḥ kiyatā kena kiyantaḥ kāraṇena te ।
ādhayo nu vilumpanti mano geham ivākhavaḥ ।।

te kiyantaḥ ādhayaḥ । kiṃniṣṭhāḥ kiṃviṣayāḥ santaḥ । kiyatā kena kāraṇena manaḥ nu vilumpanti । yathā ākhavaḥ gehaṃ vilumpanti । nuśabdaḥ praśnadyotakaḥ ।।

manye nānucitānāṃ tvam ādhīnām padam uttamaḥ ।
āpatsu cāpto yo dhīro nirjitās tena cādhayaḥ ।।

āptaḥ vicārakārī । na hy ucitasyānucitapadatvaṃ yuktam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

yathābhimatam āśu tvam brūhi prāpsyasi cānagham ।
sarvam eva punar yena tava bhetsyanti nādhayaḥ ।।

yena sarvaprāpaṇena ।।

viśvāmitravākyaṃ sargāntaślokenopasaṃharati

ity uktam asya sa mune raghuvaṃśaketur ākarṇya vākyam ucitārthavilāsagarbham ।
tatyāja khedam abhigarjati vārivāhe barhī yathābhyanumitābhimatārthasiddhiḥ ।।

abhyanumitā garjanahetukenānumānena jñātā । abhimatārthasya siddhiḥ yas-ya । sa ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe daśamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

iti pṛṣṭo munīndreṇa samāśvāsya ca rāghavaḥ ।
uvāca vacanaṃ cāru dhīrapūrṇārthamantharam ।।

dhīraṃ ca tat pūrṇārthena mantharaṃ nirbharaṃ ca dhīrapūrṇārthamantharam ।।

itaḥ paraṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇārambhaḥ ।

smṛtvā tattvam paramagahanaṃ svasvarūpākhyam ādyaṃ
spṛṣṭvā mūrdhnā gurucaraṇayor dhūlipuñjam prayatnāt 
kṛtvā devaṃ śaraṇam aniśaṃ vighnarājaṃ ca ṭīkā
vairāgyākhye prakaraṇavare tanyate bhāskareṇa 

samāśvāsanaparaṃ śrīvasiṣṭhaśrīviśvāmitrayor vākyaṃ śrutvā śrīrāmo hṛdgataṃ vairāgyam prakaṭīkaroti

bhagavan bhavatā pṛṣṭo yathāvad adhunā kila ।
kathayāmy aham ajño api ko laṅghayati sadvacaḥ ।।

bhavateti kulaguruṃ vasiṣṭham praty uktiḥ । kimarthaṃ kathayasīty । atrāha ko laṅghayatīti ।।

svayaṃ kṛtām pratijñāṃ sampādayati

ahaṃ tāvad ayaṃ jāto nije asmin pitṛsadmani ।
krameṇa vṛddhiṃ samprāptaḥ prāptavidyaś ca saṃsthitaḥ ।।

tāvacchabdo vipratipattyabhāvavācakaḥ ।।

tataḥ sadācāraparo bhūtvāham munināyaka ।
vihṛtas tīrthayātrārtham urvīm ambudhimekhalām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

etāvatātha kālena saṃsārāsthām imām mama ।
svaviveko jahārāntar oghas taṭalatām iva ।।

svavivekaḥ ko aham iti vicāraḥ ।।

vivekena parītātmā tenāhaṃ tad anu svayam ।
bhoganīrasayā buddhyā pravicāritavān idam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kiṃ tvayā pravicāritam ity । atrāha

kiṃ nāmedaṃ vata sukhaṃ yo ayaṃ saṃsārasaṃsṛtiḥ ।
jāyate mṛtaye loko mriyate jananāya ca ।।

vata kaṣṭe । idaṃ sukhaṃ kiṃ nāma bhavati । na bhavatīty arthaḥ । saṃsāre saṃsṛtiḥ saṃsaraṇaṃ yasya । yaḥ ayaṃ lokaḥ । jananāya ca yan mriyate ।।

mṛtijananarūpasya saṃsaraṇasya duḥkhatvam uktvā tadāśrayabhūtānām bhāvānāṃ duḥkhayuktatvaṃ kathayati

svasthitāḥ sarva eveme sacarācaraceṣṭitāḥ ।
āpadām patayaḥ pāpā bhāvā vibhavabhūmayaḥ ।।

sacarācaraceṣṭitāḥ calanasthitirūpakriyāyuktāḥ । sarve eveme anubhūyamānāḥ । bhāvāḥ sthāvarajaṅgamarūpāḥ padārthāḥ । āpadām patayaḥ āpadyuktāḥ bhavanti । pūrvaślokoktajananamaraṇarūpaduḥkhāśrayatvād ity arthaḥ । bhāvāḥ kathambhūtāḥ । svasthitāḥ svasmin sthitāḥ । na tu parasparaṃ sambandhayuktāḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtāḥ । vibhavabhūmayaḥ yathāsvaṃ śaktiyuktāḥ ।।

nanu katham bhāvāḥ svasthitāḥ bhavanti । parasparaṃ teṣāṃ nānāvidhasambandhadarśanād ity । atrāha

ayaḥśalākāsadṛśāḥ parasparam asaṅginaḥ ।
śliṣyante kevalam bhāvā manaḥkalpanayā svayā ।।

ayam mama putrādiḥ ayam mama pitrādir iti manaḥkalpitena saṅkalpenaiva bhāvānām parasparaṃ sambandho asti । na tu paramārthata iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu manasaḥ katham etāvatī śaktir astīty । atrāha

manaḥsamāyattam idaṃ jagad ābhogi dṛśyate ।
manaś cāsad ihābhāti kena smaḥ parimohitāḥ ।।

ābhogi vistārayuktam । manasaḥ asattvam asatyabhūtapadārthānusandhānamātrarūpatvena jñeyam ।।

asataiva vayaṃ kaṣṭaṃ vikrītā mūḍhabuddhayaḥ ।
mṛgatṛṣṇāmbhasā dūre vane mugdhamṛgā iva ।।

asatā eva । na tu satyabhūtena । manaseti śeṣaḥ ।।

na kenacic ca vikrītā vikrītā iva saṃsthitāḥ ।
vata mūḍhā vayaṃ sarve janānā api śambaram ।।

śambaram māyām ।।

kim eteṣu prapañceṣu bhogā nāma sudurbhagāḥ ।
mudhaiva hi vayam mohāt saṃsthitā baddhabhāvanāḥ ।।

eteṣu prapañceṣu madhye । sudurbhagāḥ atiśayena durbhagatvākhyaguṇayuktāḥ । bhogā nāma kim bhavanti । āpātamātraramaṇīyatvāt na kiñcid api bhavantīty arthaḥ । hiśabdaḥ ataḥśabdārthe । vayam eteṣu bhogeṣu । mohāt mudhaiva saṃsthitāḥ vyarthatvāt ।।

ajñāte bahukālena vyartha eva vayaṃ ghane ।
mohe nipatitā mugdhāḥ śvabhre mugdhamṛgā iva ।।

mohe bhogabhāvanākhye mohe । bahukālena bahukālaṃ tāvat ।।

kim me rājyena kim bhogaiḥ ko ahaṃ kim idam āgatam ।
yan mithyaivāstu tan mithyā kasya nāma kim āgatam ।। [BhG I d]

yat mithyā bhavati tat mithyaivāstu iti sambandhaḥ ।।

avāntaram upasaṃhāraṃ karoti

evaṃ vimṛśato brahman sarveṣv eva tato mama ।
bhāveṣv aratir āyātā pathikasya maruṣv iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

svābhimatam āviṣkaroti

tad etad bhagavan brūhi kim idam parinaśyati ।
kim idaṃ jāyate bhūyaḥ kim idam parivardhate ।।

kim iti katham ity asyārthe ।।

jarāmaraṇam āpac ca jananaṃ sampadas tathā ।
āvirbhāvatirobhāvair vivartante punaḥ punaḥ ।।

bhāveṣu iti śeṣaḥ । bhāvair iti itthambhāve tṛtīyā । vivartante rūpāntaraṃ gacchanti ।।

bhāvais tair eva tair eva tucchair vayam ime kila ।
paśya jarjaratāṃ nītā vātair iva giridrumāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

acetanā iva janāḥ pavanaiḥ prāṇanāmabhiḥ ।
dhvanantaḥ saṃsthitā vyarthaṃ yathā kīcakaveṇavaḥ ।।

kīcakaveṇavo hi vyarthaṃ dhvananti ।।

śāmyatīdaṃ kathaṃ duḥkham iti tapto asmi cintayā ।
jaraddruma ivogreṇa koṭarasthena vahninā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃsāraduḥkhapāṣāṇanīrandhrahṛdayo apy aham ।
nijalokabhayād eva galadbāṣpair na rodimi ।।

saṃsāraduḥkhāny eva pāṣāṇāḥ । taiḥ nīrandhraṃ hṛdayaṃ yasya । saḥ tādṛśaḥ ।।

śūnyasanmukhavṛttīs tu śuṣkarodananīrasāḥ ।
viveka eva hṛtsaṃstho mamaikānteṣu paśyati ।।

śūnyā vyarthāś ca tāḥ । sanmukhavṛttayaḥ sanmukhavyāpārāḥ tāḥ । ekānteṣu vivekaikapara evāsmīti bhāvaḥ ।।

bhṛśam muhyāmi saṃsmṛtya bhāvābhāvamayīṃ sthitim ।
dāridryeṇeva subhago dūre saṃsāracintayā ।।

sthitiṃ jagadākhyāṃ sthitim । yathā subhagaḥ dāridryeṇa muhyati । ataḥ saṃsāracintayā dūre । sā dūre bhavatv ity arthaḥ ।।

evaṃ sāmānyena saṃsārapadārthānāṃ duḥkhadatām uktvā tad viśeṣeṣu pradhānabhūtāyāḥ śriyaḥ kathayati

mohayanti manovṛttiṃ khaṇḍayanti guṇānalam ।
duḥkhajālam prayacchanti vipralambhaparāḥ śriyaḥ ।।

mohayanti avivekayuktatāṃ kurvanti । aiśvaryamadagrastā hi pūrvāparavicāraśūnyā eva bhavanti । vipralambhaparāḥ vañcanaparāḥ ।।

evaṃ śriyaḥ duḥkhadatvam uktvā tat pradhānāvayavabhūtasya dhanasyāpi duḥkhadatvaṃ kathayati

cintānicayavakrāṇi nānandāya dhanāni me ।
samprasūtakalatrāṇi gṛhāṇy ugrāpadāṃ yathā ।।

cintānicayenārjanādyartham prayuktena cintāsamūhena । ugrāpadāṃ hi bahukalatrāṇi gṛhāṇi duḥkhāyaiva bhavanti ।।

saṅgraheṇa svāsvāsthyaṃ kathayati

vividhadoṣadaśāparicintanaiḥ satatabhaṅgurakāraṇakalpitaiḥ ।
mama na nirvṛtim eti mano mune nigaḍitasya yathā vanahastinaḥ ।।

vividhā yāḥ doṣadaśāḥ । tāsām paricintanaiḥ । kathambhūtaiḥ । satataṃ bhaṅgurāṇi yāni kāraṇāni bhogarūpāṇi kāraṇāni । taiḥ kalpitaiḥ svaviṣayatayā prakaṭīkṛtaiḥ ।।

sarvadoṣamūlakāraṇabhūtān viṣayān sargāntaślokena nindati

khalāḥ kāle kāle niśi niśitamohaikamihikā gatāloke loke viṣayahaṭhacaurāḥ sucaturāḥ ।
pravṛttāḥ prodyuktā diśi diśi vivekaikaharaṇe raṇe śaktās teṣāṃ vadata vibudhāḥ ke adya subhaṭāḥ ।।

khalāḥ atyantaduḥkhakāritvāt durjanasadṛśās । tathā sucaturāḥ aticāturyayuktāḥ । viṣayahaṭhacaurāḥ । niśi lakṣaṇayā avidyārūpāyāṃ rātrau । niśitā tīkṣṇā yā mohaikamihikā । tayā gatāloke dūre gatavicārākhyaprakāśe । loke asmin saṃsāre । kāle kāle sarveṣu kāleṣu । diśi diśi sarvāsu dikṣu । prodyuktāḥ prakṛṣṭodyogabhājaḥ । ata eva vivekasya samyagvicārasya । yad ekaṃ haraṇaṃ kevalaṃ haraṇaṃ । tatra pravṛttāḥ bhavanti । vadatādya asmin samaye । teṣāṃ viṣayahaṭhacaurāṇāṃ raṇe ke subhaṭāḥ śaktāḥ bhavanti । na ke apīti bhāvaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe ekādaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

samanantaram eva prakṛtāṃ śrīnindāṃ vistareṇa kathayati

iyam asmin vinodāya saṃsāre parikalpitā ।
śrīr mune parimohāya sāpi nūnam anarthadā ।।

nūnaṃ niścayena । anarthadeti viśeṣaṇadvārahetuḥ ।।

anarthadatvam evāsyāḥ kathayati

ullāsabahulān antaḥ kallolān akramākulān ।
jaḍān prasravati sphārān prāvṛṣīva taraṅgiṇī ।।

iyaṃ śrīḥ ullāsabahulān ullāsapūrṇān । akramākulān kramollaṅghananirbha-rān । tathā jaḍān jāḍyadāyitvāt jaḍarūpān । kallolān darpākhyān mahātaraṅgān । prasravati utpādayati । yathā taraṅgiṇī prāvṛṣi varṣākāle । uktaviśeṣaṇān mahātaraṅgān prasravati ।।

cintāduhitaro bahvyo bhūridurlaliteritāḥ ।
cañcalāḥ prabhavanty asyās taraṅgāḥ sarito yathā ।।

bhūrīṇi yāni durlalitāni durvilāsāḥ । tair īritāḥ cañcalitāḥ । utthāpitā iti yāvat ।।

eṣā hi padam ekatra na nibadhnāti durbhagā ।
mugdhevāniyatācāram itaś cetaś ca dhāvati ।।

hi niścaye । aniyatācāraṃ kāmacārata ity arthaḥ । kriyāviśeṣaṇam etat ।।

janayantī paraṃ dāham parāmṛṣṭāṅgikā satī ।
vināśam eva dhatte antar dīpalekheva kajjalam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

guṇāguṇavicāreṇa vinaiva kila pārśvagam ।
rājaprakṛtivan mūḍhā durārūḍhāvalambate ।।

rājaprakṛtivat rājasvabhāvavat । rājāpi hi guṇāguṇavicārarahitam eva pārśvagam avalambate ।।

karmaṇā tena tenaiṣā vistāram upagacchati ।
doṣāśīviṣavegasya yat kṣīravisarāyate ।।

kṣīrasya visaraḥ sekaḥ । sa ivācarate kṣīravisarāyate ।।

tāvac chītamṛdusparśaḥ parasve ca jane janaḥ ।
vātyayeva himaṃ yāvac chriyā na paruṣīkṛtaḥ ।।

śrīsparśe janaḥ svasmin pare ca mahākaṭhina eva bhavatīti piṇḍārthaḥ । vātyā hi himam paruṣīkarotīty upamānatvena gṛhītā ।।

prājñāḥ śūrāḥ kṛtajñāś ca peśalā mṛdavaś ca ye ।
pāṃsumuṣṭyeva maṇayaḥ śriyā te malinīkṛtāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

na śrīḥ sukhāya bhagavan duḥkhāyaiva hi kalpate ।
guptaṃ vināśanaṃ dhatte mṛtiṃ viṣalatā yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śrīmān ajananindyaś ca śūraś cāpy avikatthanaḥ ।
samadṛṣṭiḥ prabhuś caiva durlabhāḥ puruṣās trayaḥ ।।

śriyā spṛṣṭaḥ sāhaṅkāratvena jananindya eva bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

eṣā hi viṣamā duḥkhabhogināṃ gahanā guhā ।
ghanamohagajendrāṇāṃ vindhyaśailamahāṭavī ।।

spaṣṭaṃ ।।

punaḥ kīdṛśy astīty apekṣāyām āha

satkāryapadmarajanī duḥkhakairavacandrikā ।
saddṛṣṭidīpikāvātyā kallolaughataraṅgiṇī ।।

kallolāḥ darparūpāḥ mahātaraṅgāḥ ।।

sambhramābhrādipadavī viṣādaviṣavardhinī ।
kedārikā vikalpānāṃ khadā kubhayabhoginām ।।

khadā guhā । kubhayāni eva bhoginaḥ sarpāḥ । teṣām ।।

himaṃ vairāgyavallīnāṃ vikārolūkayāminī ।
rāhudaṃṣṭrā vivekendoḥ saujanyāmbhojacandrikā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

indrāyudhavad ālolanānārāgamanoharā ।
lolā taḍid ivotpannadhvaṃsinī jaḍasaṃśrayā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

capalā varjitā ratyā nakulī nakulīnajā ।
vipralambhanatātparyahetūgramṛgatṛṣṇikā ।।

capalā cāpalyaguṇasahitā । ata eva ratyā varjitā kutrāpi ratim akurvatīty arthaḥ । tathā nakulī aticāpalatvena nakulastrīsarūpā । tathā nakulīnajā duṣṭā । akulīnajo hi duṣṭo bhavati । tathā vipralambhane paravañcane । yat tātparyam । tasya hetuś cāsau ugramṛgatṛṣṇikā kaṭhinamṛgatṛṣṇāsvarūpā ।।

laharīvaikarūpeṇa kṣaṇam padam akurvatī ।
calā dīpaśikhevāti durjñeyāgatigocarā ।।

na gatau gamane gocarā agatigocarā । dīpaśikhāpi gatau agocarā eva bhavati ।।

siṃhīva vigrahavyagrakarīndrakulapātinī ।
khaḍgadhāreva śiśirā tīkṣṇā tīkṣṇāśayāśrayā ।।

vigrahavyagraṃ yuddhavyagraṃ । yat karīndrakulaṃ hastikulaṃ । tatra patatīti tādṛśī tatsādhyatvāt । siṃhī cedṛśī bhavati । śiśirā āmukhe santāpaharitvāt । tīkṣṇāśayāḥ kaṭhinacintāḥ । āśrayaḥ yasyāḥ ।।

nānayopahatārthinyā durādhiparipīnayā ।
paśyāmy abhavyayā lakṣmyā kiñcid duḥkhād ṛte sukham ।।

upahatān ajñānabādhitān । arthate ālambanatvena kāṅkṣatīti tādṛśyā ।।

dvāreṇotsāritā lakṣmīḥ punar eti tamo'riṇā ।
aho vata hṛtasthānā nirlajjā durjanāspadā ।।

tamo'riṇā gehāntargatatamonivāraṇārthaṃ kalpitena kṣudradvāreṇa ।।

sargāntaślokena śrīnindāṃ samāpayati

manoramā karṣati cittavṛttiṃ kadaryasādhyā kṣaṇabhaṅgurā ca ।
vyālāvalīgarbhanivṛttadehā śvabhrotthitā puṣpalateva lakṣmīḥ ।।

kadaryasādhyā kukarmasādhyā । śrīpakṣe vyālāvalī duḥkhāvalī । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe dvādaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ śrīnindāṃ kṛtvā jīvitanindāṃ karoti

āyuḥ pallavakoṇāgralambāmbukaṇabhaṅguram ।
unmattam iva santyajya yāty akāṇḍe śarīrakam ।।

āyuḥ jīvitaṃ । tatsammatirūpaṃ samayam ullaṅghyeti yāvat ।।

viṣayāśīrviṣāsaṅgaparijarjaracetasām ।
aprauḍhātmavivekānām āyur āyāsakāraṇam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ye tu vijñātavijñeyā viśrāntā vitate pade ।
bhāvābhāvasamāśvastā āyus teṣāṃ sukhāyate ।।

viśrāntā ātmatve niścitāḥ । bhāvābhāveṣu pravāhāgateṣu nāśotpādeṣu । samāśvastāḥ svabhāvād apracyutāḥ ।।

vayam parimitākārapariniṣṭhitaniścayāḥ ।
saṃsārābhrataḍitpuñje mune nāyuṣi nirvṛtāḥ ।।

parimitaḥ pārimityayuktaḥ । yaḥ ākāraḥ dehādirūpaḥ ākāraḥ । tatra pariniṣṭhitaḥ niṣṭhāṃ gataḥ । niścayaḥ ātmaniścayaḥ । yeṣāṃ । nirvṛtir hi aparimitasvarūpaniṣṭhatvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

yujyate veṣṭanaṃ vāyāv ākāśasya ca khaṇḍanam ।
grathanaṃ ca taraṅgāṇām āsthā nāyuṣi yujyate ।।

āsthā dṛḍhatāviśvāsaḥ ।।

pelavaṃ śaradīvābhram asneham iva dīpakam ।
taraṅgakam ivālolaṃ gatam evopalakṣyate ।।

āyur iti śeṣaḥ ।।

taraṅgapratibimbenduṃ taḍitpuñjaṃ nabho'mbudam ।
grahītum āsthām badhnāmi na tv āyuṣi gatasthitau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

aviśrāntamanāḥ śūnyam āyur ātatam īhate ।
duḥkhāyaiva vimūḍho antar garbham aśvatarī yathā ।।

aśvatarī kharastriyām aśvāj jātā vaḍavā । tasyā garbhaḥ kukṣipāṭanaṃ vinā na niryāti ।।

saṃsārasaṃsṛtāv ambhaḥpheno asmin sargasāgare ।
kāyavallyāṃ raso rājañ jīvitam me na rocate ।।

sargasāgare kathambhūte । saṃsāre saṃsṛtiḥ saṃsaraṇaṃ । yasya । ambhaḥphenaḥ ambhovikāraḥ phenaḥ । daśaratham prati iyam uktiḥ ।।

prāpyaṃ samprāpyate yena bhūyo yena na śocyate ।
parāyā nirvṛteḥ sthānaṃ yat taj jīvitam ucyate ।।

parāyā utkṛṣṭāyāḥ ।।

taravo api hi jīvanti jīvanti mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ।
sa jīvati mano yasya mananena na jīvati ।।

mananena bhogānusandhānena ।।

jātās ta eva jagati jantavaḥ sādhujīvitāḥ ।
ye punar neha jāyante śeṣā jānīta gardabhāḥ ।।

yūyaṃ jānīta । kim ity apekṣāyām āha । śeṣā iti । śeṣā gardabhāḥ bhavanti ।।

bhāro avivekinaḥ śāstram bhāro jñānaṃ ca rāgiṇaḥ ।
aśāntaṃ ca mano bhāro bhāro anātmavido vapuḥ ।।

avivekinaḥ vivekarahitasya । bhāratvaṃ ca śāstrādeḥ samyagjñānādyarthakriyākāritvābhāvena jñeyam ।।

rūpam āyur mano buddhir ahaṅkāras tathehitam ।
bhāro bhāradharasyeva sarvaṃ duḥkhāya durdhiyaḥ ।।

durdhiyaḥ buddhirahitasya । buddhirahito hi rūpādau samatayā pāravaśyaṃ yāti । tataś ca duḥkhe nimajjati ।।

aviśrāntamanaḥpūrṇam āpadām paramāspadam ।
nīḍo rogavihaṅgānām āyur āyāsanaṃ dṛḍham ।।

āyuḥ kathambhūtam । aviśrāntam paramapadaviśrāntirahitaṃ । yan manas ।।

pratyahaṃ khedam utsṛjya śanair alam anāratam ।
āśv eva janmanaḥ śvabhraṃ kālena vinikhanyate ।।

kālanāśyatvaṃ hi āyuṣaḥ prasiddham ।।

śarīrabilaviśrāntair viṣadāhapradāyibhiḥ ।
rogair nipīyate raudrair vyālair iva vanānilaḥ ।।

āyur iti śeṣaḥ ।।

prasuvānair avacchedaṃ tucchair antaravāsibhiḥ ।
duḥkhair ākṛṣyate krūrair ghuṇair iva jaraddrumaḥ ।।

avacchedaṃ chedanam । prasuvānair utpādayadbhiḥ । ākṛṣyate svavaśaṃ nīyate ।।

nūnaṃ nigiraṇāyāśu ghanagarvam anāratam ।
ākhur mārjārakeṇeva maraṇenāvalokyate ।।

avalokyate kadā etat grase iti dṛśyate ।।

garvādiguṇagarbhiṇyā śūnyayāśaktivaśyayā ।
annam mahāśaneneva jarasā parijīryate ।।

aśaktivaśyayā aśaktigrastayā ।।

dinaiḥ katipayair eva parijñāya gatādaram ।
durjanaḥ sajjaneneva yauvanenāvamucyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vināśasuhṛdā nityaṃ jarāmaraṇabandhunā ।
rūpaṃ śiḍgavareṇeva kṛtāntenābhilaṣyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena jīvitanindāṃ samāpayati

sthiratayā sukhahāritayā tayā satatam ujjhitam uttama phalgu ca ।
jagati nāsti tathā guṇavarjitam maraṇamārjitam āyur idaṃ yathā ।।

uttamety āmantraṇam । maraṇena mārjitaṃ saṅkṣiptam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe trayodaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

adhunāhaṅkāranindām prastauti

mudhaivābhyutthito mohān mudhaiva parivardhate ।
mithyāmayena bhīto asmi durahaṅkāraśatruṇā ।।

mithyāmayena mithyāsvarūpeṇa ।।

ahaṅkāravaśād eva doṣakośaḥ kadarthanām ।
dadāti dīnadīnānāṃ saṃsāro vividhākṛtiḥ ।।

kadarthanāṃ duḥkham ।।

ahaṅkāravaśād āpad ahaṅkārād durādhayaḥ ।
ahaṅkāravaśād īhāpy ahaṅkāro mahāmayaḥ ।।

īhā bhogārthaṃ ceṣṭā ।।

tam ahaṅkāram āśritya paramaṃ ciravairiṇam ।
na bhuñje na pibāmy ambhaḥ kim u bhogān bhaje mune ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃsārarajjur ādīrghā mama cetasi mohinī ।
tatāhaṅkāradoṣeṇa kirāteneva vāgurā ।।

ahaṅkāradoṣeṇāhaṅkārākhyena doṣeṇa ।।

yāni duḥkhāni dīrghāṇi viṣamāṇi mahānti ca ।
ahaṅkārāt prasūtāni tāny agāt khadirā iva ।।

agāt parvatāt ।।

śamendoḥ saiṃhikeyāsyaṃ guṇipadmamahāśanim ।
jñānameghaśaratkālam ahaṅkāraṃ tyajāmy aham ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ahaṅkāratyāgam eva karoti

nāhaṃ rāmo na me vāñchā bhāveṣu na ca me manaḥ ।
śānta āsitum icchāmi svātmany eva jino yathā ।।

dehasyaiva rāmatvāt । mama cinmātratvād iti bhāvaḥ । śāntaḥ ahaṅkārarahitaḥ ।।

ahaṅkāravaśād yad yan mayā bhuktaṃ kṛtaṃ hṛtam ।
sarvaṃ tat tad avastv eva vastv ahaṅkārariktatā ।।

ahaṅkārariktatā ahaṅkārarāhityam ।।

aham ity asti ced brahmann aham āpadi duḥkhitaḥ ।
sampatsu sukhitas tasmād anahaṅkāritā dhanaḥ ।।

dhanayuktasya eva hi āpatsu sampatsu ca duḥkhādisparśo na bhavatīti pūrvavākye bhāvaḥ । phalitam āha tasmād iti । tasmāt tato hetoḥ । anahaṅkāritā dhanaḥ dhanam bhavati । dehātmatve niścitaḥ puruṣo hi dehārtham bhogajālam icchan bhogarāhityarūpāyām āpadi duḥkhī bhavati । tatsampattirūpāyāṃ sampadi sukhī bhavati । cinmātrātmatve niścito ahaṃ na tādṛśo bhavāmīti bhāvaḥ ।।

ahaṅkāram parityājya mune śāntamanās tathā ।
avatiṣṭhe gatodvego bhogaughe abhaṅgurāspadam ।।

avatiṣṭhe tiṣṭhāmi । ahaṅkāraṃ kathambhūtam । bhogaughe bhogasamūhe । abhaṅgurāspadam anaśvarapratiṣṭham ।।

brahman yāvad ahaṅkāravāridaḥ pravijṛmbhate ।
tāvad vikāsam āyāti tṛṣṇākuṭajamañjarī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ahaṅkāraghane śānte tṛṣṇānavataḍillatā ।
śāntadīpaśikhāvṛttyā kvāpi yāsyati satvaram ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ahaṅkāramahāvindhye manomattamataṅgajaḥ ।
visphūrjati ghanāsphoṭaiḥ stanitair iva vāridaḥ ।।

visphūrjati vilasati । ghanāsphoṭaiḥ niviḍakarṇatālaiḥ ।।

iha dehamahādaryāṃ ghanāhaṅkārakesarī ।
yo ayam ullasati sphāraṃ tenedaṃ jagad ātatam ।।

anahaṅkāritve hi sad api jagan nāsti apekṣāviṣayatvābhāvāt ।।

tṛṣṇātantulavaprotā bahujanmaparamparā ।
ahaṅkārograśiḍgena kaṇṭhe muktāvalī kṛtā ।।

śiḍgo hi tantuprotām muktāvalīṃ kaṇṭhe karoti ।।

putradārakalatrāṇi tantram mantravivarjitam ।
prasāritam aneneha durahaṅkāravairiṇā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pramārjite aham ity asmin pade svayam akhidyatā ।
pramārjitā bhavanty eva sarvā eva durādhayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

aham ity ambude śānte śanaiḥ suśamaśālini ।
manomananasammohamihikā kvāpi gacchati ।।

manasaḥ yaḥ mananasammohaḥ mananarūpaḥ । sa eva mihikā nīhāraḥ ।।

nirahaṅkāravṛtter me maurkhyāc chokena sīdataḥ ।
yat kiñcid ucitam brahmaṃs tad ākhyātum ihārhasi ।।

prathamam ahaṅkāraṃ svayam eva tyajāmi । paścāt tvaduktaṃ karomīti bhāvaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokenāhaṅkāranindāṃ samāpayati

sarvāpadāṃ nilayam adhruvam antarastham unmuktam uttamaguṇena na saṃśrayāmi ।
yatnād ahaṅkṛtipadam parito atiduḥkham śeṣeṇa māṃ samanuśādhi mahānubhāva ।।

ahaṅkṛtipadam ahaṅkṛtyākhyaṃ sthānam । śeṣeṇeti ahaṅkārāśrayaṇaṃ tyaktvā yat kiñcit samājñāpayasi tat sampādayāmīti bhāvaḥ । ahaṅkāraś ca idantāviṣayatvayogye dehe ahantāviṣayatvasañjananaṃ jñeyam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe caturdaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evam ahaṅkāranindāṃ kṛtvā cittanindām prastauti

doṣair jarjaratāṃ yātaṃ satkāryād āryasevitāt ।
vātāttapiñchalavavac cetaś calati cañcalam ।।

doṣaiḥ rāgādidoṣaiḥ । satkāryāt calati satkārye sthairyeṇa na tiṣṭhatīty arthaḥ ।।

itaś cetaś ca suvyagraṃ vyartham evābhidhāvati ।
dūrād dūrataraṃ dīnaṃ grāme kauleyako yathā ।।

kauleyakaḥ śvā ।।

na prāpnoti kvacit kiñcit prāptair api mahādhanaiḥ ।
nāntaḥ sampūrṇatām eti karaṇḍaka ivāmbubhiḥ ।।

kiñcit prāpto hi punaḥ kiñcid api na prārthayed iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nityam eva manaḥ śūnyaṃ kadāśāvāgurāvṛtam ।
na manāṅ nirvṛtiṃ yāti mṛgo yūthād iva cyutaḥ ।।

śūnyaṃ niḥsāram ।।

taraṅgataralāṃ vṛttiṃ dadhad ālūnaśīrṇatām ।
parityajya kṣaṇam api na mano yāti nirvṛtim ।।

ālūnaśīrṇatāṃ hastasparśāsahatvam । maticāñcalyam iti yāvat ।।

mano mananavikṣubdhaṃ diśo daśa vidhāvati ।
mandarāhananodbhūtaṃ kṣīrārṇavapayo yathā ।।

mananavikṣubdham bhogānusandhānakṣubdham ।।

kallolakalanāvartam māyāmakaramālitam ।
na niroddhuṃ samartho asmi manomohamahārṇavam ।।

kallolarūpā yā kalanā saṅkalpaḥ । māyā viparyayajñānam ।।

bhogadūrvāṅkurākāṅkṣī śvabhrapātam acintayan ।
manohariṇako brahman dūraṃ viparidhāvati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

na kadācana me cetas tām ālūnaviśīrṇatām ।
tyajaty ākulayā vṛttyā cañcalatvam ivārṇavaḥ ।।

ālūnaviśīrṇatāṃ hastasparśāsahatvaṃ । maticāñcalyam iti yāvat ।।

cetaś cañcalayā vṛttyā cintānicayacañcuram ।
dhṛtim badhnāti naikatra kesarī pañjare yathā ।।

cintānicayena cintāsamūhena । cañcuraṃ nirbharam ।।

mano moharathārūḍhaṃ śarīrāc chamatāsukham ।
haraty upagatodyogaṃ haṃsaḥ kṣīram ivāmbhasaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

analpakalpanātalpe nilīnāś cittavṛttayaḥ ।
munīndra na prabudhyante tena tapto aham ākulaḥ ।।

kalpanāgrastam eva sadāsanmano astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

kroḍīkṛtadṛḍhagranthitṛṣṇāsūtrombhitātmanā ।
vihago jālakeneva brahman baddho asmi cetasā ।।

granthayo atra rāgādirūpā jñeyāḥ ।।

satatāmarṣadhūmena cintājvālābilena ca ।
vahnineva tṛṇaṃ śuṣkam mune dagdho asmi cetasā ।।

satatam amarṣaḥ krodha eva ।।

krūreṇa jaḍatāṃ yātas tṛṣṇābhāryānugāminā ।
śavaḥ kauleyakeneva brahman bhukto asmi cetasā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

taraṅgataralāsphālavṛttinā jaḍarūpiṇā ।
taṭavṛkṣa ivaughena brahman nīto asmi cetasā ।।

taraṅgavat taralāsphālā atyantacañcalā ।।

avāntaranipātāya śūnyenākramaṇāya ca ।
tṛṇaṃ caṇḍānileneva dūre nunno asmi cetasā ।।

avāntareṣu bhogarūpeṣu paramaviśrāntirahiteṣu padeṣu । ākramaṇāya ākramaṇārthaṃ । śūnyeneti manoviśeṣaṇam ।।

saṃsārajaladher asmān nityam uttaraṇonmukhaḥ ।
setuneva payaḥpūro rodhito asmi kucetasā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pātālād gacchatā pṛṣṭham pṛṣṭhāt pātālagāminā ।
kūpakāṣṭhaṃ kudāmneva veṣṭito asmi kucetasā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।
