mithyaiva sphārarūpeṇa vicāraviśarāruṇā ।
bālo vetālakeneva gṛhīto asmi svacetasā ।।

gṛhītaḥ svavaśīkṛtaḥ ।।

vahner uṣṇataraḥ śailād api kaṣṭatarakramaḥ ।
vajrād api dṛḍho brahman durnigrahamanograhaḥ ।।

kaṣṭataraḥ kramaḥ ullaṅghanaṃ yasya । saḥ kaṣṭatarakramaḥ । durnigrahaṃ duḥkhena nirgrahītuṃ śakyaṃ । tasya grahaḥ grahanaṃ । durnigrahamanograhaḥ ।।

cetaḥ patati kāryeṣu vihagaś cāmiṣeṣv iva ।
kṣaṇena viratiṃ yāti bālaḥ krīḍanakād iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jaḍaprakṛtir ālolo vitatāvartavṛttimān ।
mano'bdhir īhitavyālo dūrān nayati tāta mām ।।

jaḍaprakṛtiḥ jaḍasvabhāvaḥ śītaprakṛtiś ca । vitatāvartā eva vṛttayaḥ yasya । saḥ । īhitāni kāṅkṣitāni eva vyālāḥ sarpāḥ । yasya । ceṣṭāyuktasarpāś ca yasmin । dūrān nayati nānāviṣayeṣu bhramayati ।।

yadīdṛśam manas tavāsti tarhi tasya nigrahaṃ kurv ity । atrāha

apy abdhipānān mahataḥ sumerūllaṅghanād api ।
api vahnyaśanāt sādho viṣamaś cittanigrahaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nanu cittanigraho duḥsādhya eva bhavatu । kiṃ tena setsyatīty । atrāha cittaṃ kāraṇam arthānāṃ tasmin sati jagattrayam ।
tasmin kṣīṇe jagat kṣīṇaṃ tac cikitsyam prayatnataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

cittād imāni sukhaduḥkhaśatāni nūnam abhyāgatāny agavarād iva kānanāni ।
tasmin vivekavaśatas tanutām prayāte manye mune nipuṇam eva galanti tāni ।।

imāni anubhūyamānāni । agavarāt parvataśreṣṭhāt । nipuṇaṃ samyak ।।

sargāntaślokena cittanindāṃ samāpayati

sakalaguṇajayāśā yatra baddhā mahadbhis tam arim iha vijetuṃ cittam abhyutthito aham ।
vigataratitayāntar nābhinandāmi lakṣmīṃ jaḍamalinaviśālām meghamālām ivenduḥ ।।

yatra yasmin manasi । abhyutthitaḥ udyogayukto jātaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe pañcadaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evam manonindāṃ kṛtvā tṛṣṇānindām prastauti

hārdāndhakāraśarvaryā tṛṣṇayeha durantayā ।
caranti cetanākāśe doṣakauśikapaṅktayaḥ ।।

cetanākāśe cittākāśe । yuktaṃ ca śarvaryāṃ kauśikaca-raṇam ।।

antardāhapradāyinyā samūḍharasamārdavaḥ ।
paṅka ādityadīptyeva śoṣaṃ nīto asmi cintayā ।।

samūḍhaṃ dhṛtaṃ । rasamārdavam āsvādakṛtaṃ jalakṛtaṃ ca mārdavaṃ ye-na । saḥ । cintā cātra tṛṣṇā eva jñeyā । tṛṣṇāyāḥ cintārūpatvānapāyāt । evam uttaratrāpi jñeyam ।।

mama cittamahāraṇye vyāmohatimirākule ।
śūnye tāṇḍavinī mattā bhṛśam āśā piśācikā ।।

āśā tṛṣṇā ।।

rajoracitanīhārā kāñcanāvacayojjvalā ।
nūnaṃ vikāsam āyāti cintā me aśokamañjarī ।।

nūnaṃ niścaye । cintā aśokamañjarī me vikāsam āyāti । kathambhūtā । rajasā svayam utpāditena lobhena । racitaḥ nīhāraḥ jāḍyaṃ yayā । nīhāraḥ yayā seti ca । kāñcanāvacayena kāñcanasaṅgraheṇa । ujjvalā jvalantī । kāñcanāvacayavat ujjvalā ca ।।

alam antar bhramāyaiṣā tṛṣṇā kavalitāśayā ।
āyātā vimalollāsam ūrmir ambunidhāv iva ।।

antar manasi । bhramāya mithyājñānāya ।।

uddāmakallolaravā dehādrau vahatīva me ।
taraṅgitatarākārā taratṛṣṇātaraṅgiṇī ।।

tarantī cāsau tṛṣṇātaraṅgiṇī taratṛṣṇātaraṅgiṇī ।।

vegaṃ saṃroddhum udito vātyayeva jarattṛṇam ।
nītaḥ kaluṣayā kvāpi dhiyāyaṃ cittacātakaḥ ।।

vegaṃ svakīyaṃ vegaṃ । dhiyā tṛṣṇāviṣṭayā buddhyā ।।

yāṃ yām aham adhītāsthām āśrayāmi guṇaśriyam ।
tāṃ tāṃ kṛntati me tṛṣṇā tantrīm iva kumūṣikā ।।

adhītāsthām śikṣitadārḍhyaṃ ।।

payasīva jaratparṇaṃ vāyāv iva jarattṛṇam ।
nabhasīva śaranmeghaś cintācakre bhramāmy aham ।।

cintācakre tṛṣṇācakre ।।

gantum āspadam ātmīyam asamarthadhiyo vayam ।
cintājāle vimuhyāmo jāle śakunayo yathā ।।

ātmīyam āspadam paramātmatattvākhyaṃ nijaṃ sthānam ।।

tṛṣṇābhidhānayā tāta dagdho asmi jvālayā tathā ।
yathā dāhopaśamanam āśaṅke nāmṛtair api ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dūraṃ dūram ito gatvā sametya ca punaḥ punaḥ ।
bhramaty āśu diganteṣu tṛṣṇonmattā turaṅgamī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jaḍasaṃsaṅgiṇī tṛṣṇā kṛtordhvādhogamāgamā ।
kṣubdhā granthimatī nityam araghaṭṭograrajjuvat ।।

granthimatī rāgādigranthiyuktā ।।

antar grathitayā dehe sambhramocchidyamānayā ।
rajjvevāśu balīvardas tṛṣṇayā vāhyate janaḥ ।।

dehe śarīre । sambhrameṇa na tu yuktyā । ucchidyamānayā nāśayitum ārabdhayā । vāhyate yatra tatra nīyate ।।

putradārakalatrāditṛṣṇayā nityakṛṣṇayā ।
khageṣv iva kirātyeha jālaṃ lokeṣu racyate ।।

putrādibhir eva hi lokaḥ saṃsāre bandham āpnoti ।।

bhāyayaty api dhīreham andhayaty api sekṣaṇam ।
khedayaty api sānandaṃ tṛṣṇā kṛṣṇeva śarvarī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kuṭilā komalasparśā viṣavaiṣamyaśaṃsinī ।
dahaty api manāk spṛṣṭā tṛṣṇā kṛṣṇeva bhoginī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhinatti hṛdayam puṃsām māyāmayavidhāyinī ।
daurbhāgyadāyinī dīnā tṛṣṇā kṛṣṇeva rākṣasī ।।

māyā evāmayaḥ rogas । taṃ karotīti tādṛśī । daurbhāgyadāyinī vaivarṇyakāriṇī ।।

tandrātantrīgaṇaṃ kośe dadhānā pariveṣṭitam ।
nānande rājate brahmaṃs tṛṣṇājarjaravallakī ।।

tandrāḥ viṣayeṣv avasādāḥ । taṃ pariveṣṭitaṃ samyak baddhaṃ । ānande viśrāntyavasthārūpe ānande nāṭye ca ।।

nityam evātimalinā kaṭukonmādaśālinī ।
dīrghā tanvī ghanasnehā tṛṣṇāgahvaravallarī ।।

tṛṣṇā eva gahvaravallarī śvabhralatā ।।

anānandakarī śūnyā niṣphalātyartham unnatā ।
amaṅgalakarī krūrā tṛṣṇā kṣīṇeva mañjarī ।।

kṣīṇā mañjarī nissārā mañjarī ।।

anāvarjitacittāpi sarvam evānudhāvati ।
na cāpnoti phalaṃ kiñcit tṛṣṇā jīrṇeva kāminī ।।

anāvarjitacittā aramyatvād avaśīkṛtajanahṛdayā ।।

saṃsāranṛtte mahati nānārasasamākule ।
bhuvanābhogaraṅgeṣu tṛṣṇā jaraḍhanartakī ।।

nānārasāḥ sukhādirūpāḥ śṛṅgārādirūpāś ca ।।

jarā kusumitā rūḍhā pātotpātaphalāvaliḥ ।
saṃsārajaṅgale dīrghe tṛṣṇāviṣalatā tatā ।।

rūḍhā prarohaṃ gatā ।।

yan na śaknoti tatrāpi dhatte tāṇḍavitāṃ gatim ।
nṛtyaty ānandarahitaṃ tṛṣṇā jīrṇeva nartakī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhṛśaṃ sphurati nīhāre śāmyaty āloka āgate ।
duḥkhaugheṣu padaṃ dhatte tṛṣṇācapalavarhiṇī ।।

nīhāre mohe ।।

jaḍakallolabahalā ciraṃ śūnyatarāntarā ।
kṣaṇam ullāsam āyāti tṛṣṇāprāvṛṭtaraṅgiṇī ।।

jaḍakallolaiḥ jāḍyarūpaiḥ kallolaiḥ jalakallolaiś ca ।।

naṣṭam utsṛjya tiṣṭhantaṃ vṛkṣād vṛkṣam ivā param ।
puruṣāt puruṣaṃ yāti tṛṣṇā loleva pakṣiṇī ।।

tṛṣṇā naṣṭam puruṣam utsṛjya puruṣāt tasmān naṣṭāt puruṣāt । tiṣṭhantaṃ sthitiyuktam । kā iva । yathā pakṣiṇī naṣṭaṃ vṛkṣam parityajya vṛkṣāt tasmāt naṣṭāt । tiṣṭhantaṃ vṛkṣaṃ yāti ।।

padaṃ karoty alaṅghye api tṛptāpi phalam īhate ।
ciraṃ tiṣṭhati naikatra tṛṣṇācapalamarkaṭī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

idaṃ kṛtvedam āyāti sarvam evāsamañjasam ।
anārataṃ ca yatate tṛṣṇā ceṣṭeva daivikī ।।

daivikī daivasambandhinī ।।

kṣaṇam āyāti pātālaṃ kṣaṇaṃ yāti nabhastalam ।
kṣaṇam bhramati dikkuñje tṛṣṇāhṛtpadmaṣaṭpadī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sarvasaṃsāradoṣāṇāṃ tṛṣṇaikā dīrghaduḥkhadā ।
antaḥpurastham api yā yojayaty atisaṅkaṭe ।।

doṣāṇām iti nirdhāraṇe ṣaṣṭhī । dīrghaduḥkhatvam evottarārdhena kathayati antaḥpurastham iti ।।

prayacchati paraṃ jāḍyam paramālokarodhinī ।
mohanīhāragahanā tṛṣṇājaladamālikā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sarveṣāṃ jantujālānāṃ saṃsāravyavahāriṇām ।
pariprotamanomālās tṛṣṇā bandhanarajjavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vicitravarṇā viguṇā dīrghā malinasaṃsthitiḥ ।
śūnyāśūnyāspadā tṛṣṇā śakrakārmukadharmiṇī ।।

malināspadatvaṃ śakrakārmukapakṣe meghāśrayatvena jñeyam ।।

aśanir guṇasasyānām phalitā śarad āpade ।
himaṃ sampatsarojinyās tamasāṃ dīrghayāminī ।।

tṛṣṇā kā । phalitā śarat phalayuktā śarad । āpatpradety arthaḥ ।।

saṃsāranāṭakanaṭī kāyālayavihaṅgamī ।
mānasāraṇyahariṇī smarasaṅgītavallakī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vyavahārābdhilaharī mohamātaṅgaśṛṅkhalā ।
mārganyagrodhasubhagā duḥkhakairavacandrikā ।।

mārge nyagrodhacchāyāvat pariṇāmaduḥkhāvahety arthaḥ ।।

jarāmaraṇaduḥkhānām ekā ratnasamudgikā ।
ādhivyādhivilāsānāṃ nityamattā vilāsinī ।।

samudgikā peṭikā ।।

kṣaṇam ālokavimalā sāndhakāralavā kṣaṇam ।
vyomavīthīsamā tṛṣṇā nīhāragahanā kṣaṇam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

gacchatūpaśamaṃ tṛṣṇā kāryavyāyāmaśāntaye ।
tamī ghanatamaḥkṛṣṇā yathā rakṣonivṛttaye ।।

kāryakṛtaḥ yaḥ vyāyāmaḥ ।।

tāvan muhyaty ayaṃ loko mūko vilulitāśayaḥ ।
yāvad evānusandhatte tṛṣṇāviṣaviṣūcikām ।।

viṣaviṣūcikā viṣabhakṣaṇakṛto rogaviśeṣaḥ ।।

loko ayam akhilaṃ duḥkhaṃ cintayojjhita ujjhati ।
cintāviṣūcikāmantraś cintātyāgo hi kathyate ।।

duḥkhaṃ cintāsvarūpaṃ duḥkhaṃ ।।

tṛṇapāṣāṇakāṣṭhādi sarvam āmiṣaśaṅkayā ।
ādadhānā sphuraty antas tṛṣṇā matsyī hrade yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rogārtir aṅgagā tṛṣṇā gambhīram api mānavam ।
uttānatāṃ nayaty āśu sūryāṃśava ivāmbujam ।।

uttānatām uttānapāṇitvaṃ । yācakabhāvam iti yāvat ।।

aho bata mahac citraṃ tṛṣṇām api mahādhiyaḥ ।
duśchedām api kṛntanti vivekenāmalāsinā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nāsidhārā na vajrāgnir na taptāyaḥkaṇārciṣaḥ ।
tathā tīkṣṇā yathā brahmaṃs tṛṣṇeyaṃ hṛdi saṃsthitā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kajjalāsitatīkṣṇāgrāḥ snehadīrghadaśāparāḥ ।
prakāśā dāhadasparśās tṛṣṇā dīpaśikhā iva ।।

kajjalāsitāś ca tāḥ tīkṣṇāgrāś ca । snehaḥ rāgaḥ tailaṃ ca । daśā avasthā vartiś ca ।।

api merūpamam prājñam api śūram api sthiram ।
tṛṇīkaroti tṛṣṇaikā nimeṣeṇa narottamam ।।

tṛṇīkaroti laghūkarotīty arthaḥ ।।

vistīrṇagahanā bhīmā ghanajālarajomayī ।
sāndhakārogranīhārā tṛṣṇā vindhyamahāṭavī ।।

vistīrṇā cāsau gahanā ca । vindhyamahāṭavīpakṣe vistīrṇāni gahanāni yasyāḥ । seti । ghanā cāsau bandhakatvāt jālarūpā ca । tādṛśī cāsau rajomayī ca rajoguṇamayī ca । meghajālena rajasā ca vyāptety aṭavīpakṣe । sāndhakārā ajñānāndhyayuktā । ugranīhārā kaṭhinamohayuktā ।।

sargāntaślokena tṛṣṇānindāṃ samāpayati

ekaiva sarvabhuvanāntaralabdhalakṣyā durlakṣatām upagataiva puraḥsthiteva ।
tṛṣṇā sthitā jagati cañcalavīcimāle kṣīrārṇavāmbupaṭale madhureva śaktiḥ ।।

durlakṣatām upagataivātyantāsattvād iti bhāvaḥ । madhurā śaktiḥ mādhuryākhyo guṇaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe ṣoḍaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ tṛṣṇānindāṃ kṛtvā śarīranindām prastauti

ārdrāntratantrīgahano vikārī paritāpavān ।
dehaḥ sphurati saṃsāre so api duḥkhāya kevalam ।।

ārdrā raktārdrāḥ । tābhiḥ gahanaḥ durgamaḥ ।।

deham eva vistareṇa viśinaṣṭi ajño api tajjñasadṛśo valitātmacamatkṛtiḥ ।
yuktyā bhavyo apy abhavyo me na jaḍo nāpi cetanaḥ ।।

ajño api pāṣāṇatulyatvenācetano api । tajjñasadṛśaḥ pramātṛtvena bhāsamānatvāt । valiteti dehāhambhāvanayaiva paramātmacamatkāro vyavadhānaṃ yāti । yuktyā yogādirūpayā yuktyā । bhavyo api śreṣṭho api mokṣasādhanatvāt । me abhavyaḥ maddṛṣṭyābhavyaḥ ।।

jaḍājaḍadṛśor madhye dolāyitadurāśayaḥ ।
na vivekī na mūḍhātmā moham eva prayacchati ।।

jaḍatve pāṣāṇavat ceṣṭāśrayo na syāt । ajaḍatve grāhyatāṃ na yāyād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

stokenānandām āyāti stokenāyāti khinnatām ।
nāsti dehasamaḥ śocyo nīco guṇabahiṣkṛtaḥ ।।

nīco hi stokenānandam āyāti khinnatāṃ cāyāti ।।

āgamāpāyinā nityaṃ dantakesaraśālinā ।
vikāsismitapuṣpeṇa pratikṣaṇam alaṅkṛtaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhujaśākhaughanamito dvijānustambhasusthitaḥ ।
locanālivanākrāntaḥ śiraḥpīṭhabṛhatphalaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sravadasrurasasrotā hastapādasupallavaḥ ।
gulphavān kāryasaṅghātavihaṅgamatatāspadam ।।

kāryasaṅghātavihaṅgamānām tataṃ vistīrṇam ।।

sacchāyo dehavṛkṣo ayaṃ jīvapānthagaṇāspadam ।
kasyātmīyaḥ kasya para āsthānāsthe kilātra ke ।।

āsthānāsthe iti upekṣā evātra yukteti bhāvaḥ ।।

bhārasantāraṇārthena gṛhītāyām punaḥ punaḥ ।
nāvi dehalatāyāṃ ca kasya syād ātmabhāvanā ।।

dehapakṣe bhārasantāraṇārthena saṃsārabhārasamāptaye । dehaṃ vinā hi saṃsāro naśyati ।।

dehanāmni vane śūnye bahugartasamākule ।
tanūruhāsaṅkhyatarau viśvāsaṃ ko adhigacchati ।।

gartāḥ atra viṣayāḥ ।।

carmasnāyvasthivalite śarīrapaṭahe dṛḍhe ।
mārjāravad ahaṃ nāntas tiṣṭhāmy aviratadhvanau ।।

snāyavaḥ sūkṣmanāḍyaḥ paṭahāntare । mārjāro hi tatra na tiṣṭhati ।।

saṃsārāraṇyasaṃrūḍho vilasaccittamarkaṭaḥ ।
cintāmañjarikākāro dīrghaduḥkhaghuṇakṣataḥ ।।

tṛṣṇābhujaṅgamīdehaḥ kopakākakṛtālayaḥ ।
smitapuṣpo drumaḥ śrīmāñ śubhāśubhamahāphalaḥ ।।

suskandho dorlatājālo hastastabakasundaraḥ ।
pavanaspanditāśeṣasvāṅgāvayavapallavaḥ ।।

sarvendriyakhagādhāraḥ sujānuḥ sutvag unnataḥ ।
sarasacchāyayā yuktaḥ kāmapānthaniṣevitaḥ ।।

mūrdhni sañjanitādīrghaśiroruhatṛṇāvaliḥ ।
ahaṅkārajaradgṛddhakulāyasuṣirodaraḥ ।।

ucchinnavāsanājālamūlatvād durbalākṛtiḥ ।
vyāyāmaviramaḥ kāyavṛkṣo ayaṃ na sukhāya me ।।

ahaṅkāra eva gṛddhaḥ । tasya kulāyabhūtaṃ yat suṣiraṃ vivaraṃ । tat udare yasya । durbalākṛtiḥ śithilākṛtiḥ । vāsanayā ahambhāvena gṛhīta eva hi dehaḥ dṛḍhākṛtiḥ bhavati । vyāyāmena āghātena । viramaḥ nāśo yasya ।।

kalevaram ahaṅkāragṛhasthasya mahāgṛham ।
luṭhatv abhyetu vā sthairyaṃ kim anena mune hi me ।।

na hi paragṛhasya luṭhane sthairye vā sukhaduḥkhe yukte iti bhāvaḥ ।।

paṅktibaddhendriyapaśuṃ valgattṛṣṇāgṛhāṅganam ।
rajorañjitasarvāṅgaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

anena dehasya grāmīṇagṛhasadṛśatvam uktam ।।

kāṣṭhāsthikāṣṭhasaṅghaṭṭaparisaṅkaṭakoṭaram ।
antradāmabhir ābaddhaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

kāṣṭha iti kāṣṭharūpam asthikāṣṭhaṃ । tasya yaḥ saṅghaṭṭaḥ niḥsandhibandham avasthānaṃ । tena parisaṅkaṭaṃ paritaḥ sambādhaṃ । antradāmabhir antrarajjubhiḥ ।।

prasṛtasnāyutantrīkaṃ raktāmbukṛtakardamam ।
jarāmakkoladhavalaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

citrakṛtyabhṛtānantaceṣṭāvaṣṭabdhasaṃsthiti ।
mithyāmohamahāsthūṇaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

citrakṛtyeṣu nānāvidhakāryeṣu । tābhir avaṣṭabdhā bharitā । gṛhapakṣe citrakṛtyāni ālekhyāni । mithyāmohaḥ mithyājñānam eva mahāsthūṇā yasya । tat tādṛśaṃ । mithyājñānenaiva hi deho dhāryate ।।

duḥkhārbhakakṛtākrandaṃ sukhaśayyāmanoharam ।
durīhādagdhadāsīkaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

sukhāny eva śayyāḥ । durīhāḥ kutsitāḥ kāṅkṣā eva dagdhadāsyaḥ hatadāsyaḥ yasya ।।

malāḍhyaviṣayivyūhabhāṇḍopaskarasaṅkaṭam ।
ajñānakṣāravalitaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

viṣayīṇi indriyāṇi ।।

gulphagulguluviśrāntajānūccastambhamastakam ।
dīrghadordārusudṛḍhaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

gulguluḥ stambhādhārabhūtā śilā ।।

prakaṭākṣagavākṣāntaḥ krīḍatprajñāgṛhāṅganam ।
cintāduhitṛkam brahman neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mūrdhajacchādanacchannakarṇaśrīcandraśālikam ।
ādīrghāṅguliniryūhaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

channā āvṛtā । candraśālikā śirogṛham । niryūhaḥ bahirgatadāru ।।

sarvāṅgakuḍyasañjātaghanaromayavāṅkuram ।
saṃśūnyapīṭhapiṭhiraṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

pīṭhapiṭhiram madhyadeśaḥ ।।

nakhorṇanābhanilayaiḥ śāram āraṇitāntaram ।
bhāṅkārakāripavanaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

nilayāḥ ālayāḥ ।।

praveśanirgamavyagravātavegam anāratam ।
vitatākṣagavākṣaṃ ca neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

vātaḥ prāṇavātaḥ ।।

jihvāmarkaṭikākrāntavadanadvārabhīṣaṇam ।
dṛṣṭadantāsthiśakalaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tvaksudhālepamasṛṇaṃ yantrasañcāracañcalam ।
manomandākhunotkhātaṃ neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

yantravad yaḥ sañcāraḥ ।।

smitadīpaprabhābhāsi kṣaṇam ānandasundaram ।
kṣaṇaṃ vyāptam prabhāpūrair neṣṭaṃ dehagṛham mama ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

samastarogāyatanaṃ valīpalitapattanam ।
sarvādhisāraṅgavanaṃ neṣṭam mama kalevaram ।।

sarvādhaya eva sārangāḥ ।।

akṣarkṣakṣobhaviṣamā śūnyā niḥsārakoṭarā ।
tamogahanahṛtkuñjā neṣṭā dehāṭavī mama ।।

akṣāṇi eva ṛkṣās । tamaḥ ajñānam andhakāraṃ ca ।।

dehālayaṃ dhārayituṃ na śakto asmi munīśvara ।
paṅkamagnaṃ samuddhartuṃ gajam alpabalo yathā ।।

dehālayaṃ dehākhyaṃ gṛham ।।

kiṃ śriyā kiṃ ca kāyena kim mānena kim īhayā ।
dinaiḥ katipayair eva kālaḥ sarvaṃ nikṛntati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

raktamāṃsamayasyāsya sabāhyābhyantaram mune ।
nāśaikadharmiṇo brūhi keva kāyasya ramyatā ।।

nāśasya ekaḥ dharmī nāśaikadharmī ।।

maraṇāvasare kāyā jīvaṃ nānusaranti ye ।
teṣu tāta kṛtaghneṣu kevāsthā vata dhīmataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mattebhakarṇāgracalaḥ kāyo lambāmbubhaṅguraḥ ।
na santyajati māṃ yāvat tāvad enaṃ tyajāmy aham ।।

ahantāviṣayatvenāgrahaṇād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

pavanaspandataralaḥ pelavaḥ kāyapallavaḥ ।
jarjaras tanuvṛttaś ca neṣṭo ayaṃ kaṭunīrasaḥ ।।

tanuś cāsau vṛttaś ca tanuvṛttaḥ ।।

bhuktvā pītvā ciraṃ kālam bālapallavapelavam ।
tanutām ety ayatnena vināśam anudhāvati ।।

ādau tanutām eti । tato ayatnena vināśam anudhāvati ।।

tāny eva sukhaduḥkhāni bhāvābhāvamayāny asau ।
bhūyo apy anubhavan kāyaḥ prākṛto hi na lajjate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

suciram prabhutāṃ kṛtvā saṃsevya vibhavaśriyam ।
nocchrāyam eti na sthairyaṃ kāyaḥ kim iti pālyate ।।

kim iti kimarthaṃ ।।

jarākāle jarām eti mṛtyukāle tathā mṛtim ।
samam eva viśeṣajña kāyo bhogidaridrayoḥ ।।

he viśeṣajña । bhogidaridrayoḥ kāyaḥ samam eva nirviśeṣam eva । jarākāle jarām eti । tathā mṛtikāle mṛtim eti । ataḥ śarīrabhogasādhanārthaṃ yatno vyartha eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

saṃsārāmbhodhijaṭhare tṛṣṇākuharakāntare ।
suptas tiṣṭhati mukteho mūko ayaṃ kāyakacchapaḥ ।।

kacchapaḥ kūrmaḥ । kuharakaṃ randhram ।।

dahanaikārthayogyāni kāyakāṣṭhāni bhūriśaḥ ।
saṃsārābdhāv ivohyante kañcit teṣu naraṃ viduḥ ।।

dahanākhyo yaḥ ekaḥ arthaḥ prayojanaṃ । kañcit jñātajñeyajīvāśrayam ity arthaḥ । teṣu iti nirdhāraṇe saptamī । anye paśava iva iti bhāvaḥ ।।

dīrghadaurātmyacalayā nipātaphalayānayā ।
na dehalatayā kāryaṃ kiñcid asti vivekinaḥ ।।

nipātaphalayā nāśaphalayā । vivekinaḥ ātmavicārayuktasya ।।

majjan kardamakośeṣu jhagity evaṃ jarāṃ gataḥ ।
na jñāyate yāty acirāt kva kathaṃ dehadarduraḥ ।।

deha eva darduraḥ bhekaḥ ।।

niḥsārasakalārambhāḥ kāyāś capalavāyavaḥ ।
rajomārgeṇa gacchanto dṛśyante neha kenacit ।।

rajomārgeṇa lobhamārgeṇa dhūlimargeṇa ca ।।

vāyor dīpasya manaso gacchato jñāyate gatiḥ ।
āgacchataś ca bhagavan na śarīraśarasya naḥ ।।

naḥ asmatsambandhina ity arthaḥ ।।

baddhāśā ye śarīreṣu baddhāśā ye jagatsthitau ।
tān mohamadironmattān dhig dhig astu punaḥ punaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nāhaṃ dehasya no deho mama nāyam ahaṃ tathā ।
iti viśrāntacittā ye te mune puruṣottamāḥ ।।

ahaṃ tathā tadvat ।।

mānāvamānabahulā bahulābhamanoramāḥ ।
śarīramātrabaddhāsthaṃ ghnanti doṣadṛśo naram ।।

doṣadṛśaḥ rāgādirūpāḥ । bahulābhamanoramatvam āmukhe jñeyam ।।

śarīrasaṅgaśāyinyā piśācyā peśalāṅgayā ।
ahaṅkāracamatkṛtyā chalena cchalitā vayam ।।

śarīrotsaṅgeti vā pāṭhaḥ ।।

prajñā varākī sarvaiva kāyabaddhāsthayānayā ।
mithyājñānakurākṣasyā chalitā kaṣṭam ekikā ।।

rākṣasī hi ekakam eva cchalayati ।।

na kiñcid api yasyāsti satyaṃ tena hatātmanā ।
citraṃ dagdhaśarīreṇa janatā vipralabhyate ।।

kiñcid api vipralambhakaraṇaṃ kim api vastu । vipralabhyate vañcyate ।।

dinaiḥ katipayair eva nirjharāmbukaṇo yathā ।
pataty ayam ayatnena jarjaraḥ kāyapallavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kāyo ayam acirāpāyo budbudo ambunidhāv iva ।
vyarthaṃ kāryaparāvarte parisphurati niṣphalaḥ ।।

kāryaparāvarte saṃsāre ।।

mithyājñānavikāre asmin svapnasambhramapattane ।
kāye sphuṭatarāpāye kṣaṇam āsthā na me dvija ।।

svapnasambhramapattane svapnasambhramadṛṣṭapattanatulye ity arthaḥ ।।

taḍitsu śaradabhreṣu gandharvanagareṣu ca ।
sthairyaṃ yena vinirṇītaṃ sa viśvasiti vigrahe ।।

viśvasiti viśvāsaṃ karoti ।।

sargāntaślokena śarīranindāṃ samāpayati

satatabhaṅgurakāryaparamparā- vijayi jātajayaṃ śaṭhavṛttiṣu ।
sakaladoṣam idaṃ kukalevaraṃ tṛṇam ivāham upojjhya sukhaṃ sthitaḥ ।।

satatabhaṅgurāḥ yāḥ kāryaparamparāḥ । tāsu vijayaḥ asyāstīti tādṛśaṃ । bhaṅgurakāryaparamparāsādhanam iti yāvat । ata eva śaṭhavṛttiṣu kutsitavyāpāreṣu । jātajayam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe saptadaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ śarīranindāṃ kṛtvā tatprathamāvasthārūpasya bālyasya nindām prastauti

labdhvāpi taralākāre kāryabhārataraṅgiṇi ।
saṃsārasāgare janma bālyaṃ duḥkāya kevalam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tatkṛtaṃ duḥkham eva vistareṇa kathayati

aśaktir āpadas tṛṣṇā mūkatā mūḍhabuddhitā ।
gṛdhnutā lolatā dainyaṃ sarvam bālye pravartate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

roṣarodanaraudrīṣu dainyajarjaritāsu ca ।
daśāsu bandhanam bālyam ālānaṃ kariṇīṣv iva ।।

daśāsv iti vaiṣayike ādhāre saptamī । badhyate asminn iti bandhanam ।।

na mṛtau na jarāroge na cāpadi na yauvane ।
tāś cintā na nikṛntanti hṛdayaṃ śaiśaveṣu yāḥ ।।

jarā eva rogaḥ jarārogas ।।

tiryagjātisamārambhaḥ sarvair evāvadhīritaḥ ।
lolo bālajanācāro maraṇād api duḥkhadaḥ ।।

tiryagjātivat samārambhaḥ yasya । paśujātitulyasamārambha ity arthaḥ ।।

pratibimbaṃ ghanājñānāṃ nānāsaṅkalpapelavam ।
bālyam ālūnasaṃśīrṇamanaḥ kasya sukhāvaham ।।

bālyaṃ kathambhūtam । ālūnasaṃśīrṇam atyantacañcalaṃ । manaḥ yasmin । ghanājñānām atyantajaḍānāṃ । pratibimbaṃ dṛṣṭāntaḥ ।।

jaḍaśyāmalayājasraṃ jātabhītyā pade pade ।
yad bhayaṃ śaiśave buddhyā kasyām āpadi tad bhavet ।।

buddhyā bhayaṃ buddhikṛtam bhayaṃ । na kasyām apīti bhavaḥ ।।

līlāsu durvilāseṣu durīhāsu durāśaye ।
paramam moham ādatte bālo balavadāpadam ।।

durāśaye kutsite citte । mohaṃ kathambhūtam balavatī āpad yasmāt । tat tādṛśam ।।

vikalpakalilārambhaṃ durvilāsaṃ durāspadam ।
śaiśavaṃ śāsanāyaiva puruṣasya na śāntaye ।।

śāsanāya māraṇāya ।।

ye doṣā ye durācārā duṣkramā ye durādhayaḥ ।
te sarve saṃsthitā bālye durgarta iva kauśikāḥ ।।

kauśikāḥ ghūkāḥ ।।

bālyaṃ ramyam iti vyarthabuddhayaḥ kathayanti ye ।
tān mūrkhapuruṣān brahman dhig astu hatacetasaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yatra lolākṛti manaḥ parisphurati vṛttiṣu ।
trailokyarājyam api tat kathaṃ vahati tuṣṭaye ।।

trailokyarājyam api trailokyarājyarūpam api ।।

sarveṣām eva sattvānāṃ sarvāvasthāsu caiva hi ।
manaś cañcalatām eti bālye daśaguṇaṃ mune ।।

tuśabdo adhyāhāryaḥ । bālye tu manaḥ daśaguṇaṃ cañcalatām eti ।।

manaḥ prakṛtyaiva calam bālyaṃ ca calatāvaram ।
tayoḥ saṃśliṣṭayoḥ tāta kenaivāntaḥ kucāpale ।।

calatāyāṃ varam pradhānam । bahucalam ity arthaḥ । he tāta । tayoḥ manobālatayoḥ । saṃśliṣṭayoḥ satyoḥ । kucāpale kenaiva prakāreṇāntaḥ avasānaṃ syāt । na kenāpīty arthaḥ ।।

strīlocanais taḍitpuñjair jvālāmālais taraṅgakaiḥ ।
cāpalaṃ śikṣitam brahmañ śaiśavān manaso atha vā ।।

strīlocanādibhyo api śaiśavaṃ calam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

śaiśavaṃ ca manaś caiva sarvāsv eva hi vṛttiṣu ।
bhrātarāv iva lakṣyete satatam bhaṅgurasthitī ।।

bhaṅgurasthitī calasthitī ।।

sarvāṇi duṣṭabhūtāni sarve doṣā durāśayāḥ ।
bālyam evopajīvanti śrīmantam iva mānavāḥ ।।

durāśayāḥ kaṭhināḥ । upajīvanti apekṣante ।।

navaṃ navam prītikaraṃ na śiśuḥ pratyahaṃ yadi ।
prāpnoti tad asau yāti viṣavegasya mūrchanām ।।

navaṃ navaṃ navīnaṃ navīnaṃ vastu ।।

stokena vaśam āyāti stokenaiti vikāritām ।
amedhya eva ramate bālaḥ kauleyako yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ajasram bāṣpavadanaḥ kardamāntar jaḍāśayaḥ ।
varṣokṣitasya taptasya sthalasya sadṛśaḥ śiśuḥ ।।

kardamāntaḥ kardamamadhye । jaḍaḥ āśayaḥ yasya । saḥ tādṛśaḥ । varṣokṣitaṃ taptasthalam apīdṛśam eva bhavati ।।

bhayāhāraparaṃ dīnaṃ yathādṛṣṭābhilāṣi ca ।
lolabuddhiḥ vapur dhatte bālo duḥkhāya kevalam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

svasaṅkalpābhilaṣitān bhāvān aprāpya taptadhīḥ ।
duḥkham ety abalo bālo vinikṛtta ivāśaye ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

durīhālabdhalakṣyāṇi bahupakṣolvaṇāni ca ।
bālasya yāni duḥkhāni mune tāni na kasyacit ।।

durīhābhis tatkartṛkābhiḥ duśceṣṭābhiḥ । labdhaṃ lakṣyam āspadaṃ yaiḥ । tāni । bahuḥ yaḥ pakṣaḥ svavargaḥ । tena ulvaṇāni kaṭhināni । śarāṇām atropamānatvaṃ vyaṅgyam ।।

bālo balavatāśvena manorathavilāsinā ।
manasā tapyate nityaṃ grīṣmeṇeva vanasthalam ।।

aśvenety । atrāśv eveti pāṭhaḥ ।।

vidyāgṛhagato bālaḥ parām eti kadarthanām ।
ālāna iva nāgendro viṣavaiṣamyabhīṣaṇam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nānāmanorathamayī mithyākalpitakalpanā ।
duḥkhāyātyantadīrghāya bālatā pelavāśayā ।।

pelavaḥ jaḍaḥ ।।

sambhṛṣṭaṃ tuhinam bhoktum indum ādātum ambarāt ।
vāñchyate yena maurkhyeṇa tat sukhāya katham bhavet ।।

sambhṛṣṭam bharjitam ।।

antaściter aśaktasya śītātapanivāraṇe ।
ko viśeṣo mahābuddhe bālasyorvīruhasya ca ।।

antaściteḥ na tu vikasitaciteḥ । citiḥ śītātapajñānam ।।

uḍḍīnam abhivāñchanti pakṣābhyāṃ kṣutparāyaṇāḥ ।
bhayāhāraparā nityam bālā vihagadharmiṇaḥ ।।

bhayāhārayoḥ parāḥ bhayāhāraparāḥ ।।

śaiśave guruto bhītir mātṛtaḥ pitṛtas tathā ।
janato jyeṣṭhabālāc ca śaiśavam bhayamandiram ।।

jyeṣṭhabālo hi kaniṣṭhabālam parābhavatīti jyeṣṭhabālāc cety uktam ।।

sargāntaślokena bālyanindāṃ samāpayati

sakaladoṣadaśāvihatāśayaṃ śaraṇam apy avivekavilāsinaḥ ।
iha na kasyacid eva mahāmune bhavati bālyam alam parituṣṭidam ।।

aviveka eva vilāsī । tasya śaraṇaṃ gṛham । avivekāspadam ity arthaḥ । apiśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe aṣṭādaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evam bālyanindāṃ kṛtvā kramaprāptāṃ yauvananindām prastauti

bālyānartham atha tyaktvā pumān abhihatāśayaḥ ।
ārohati nipātāya yauvanaṃ śvabhrasambhramam ।।

śvabhravat sambhramo yasmiṃs tādṛśam । pātaś cātra jarāgamanarūpaḥ jñeyaḥ ।।

tatratyaṃ nipātaṃ vistareṇa kathayati

tatrānantavilāsasya lolasya svasya cetasaḥ ।
vṛttīr anusaran yāti duḥkhād duḥkhāntaraṃ jaḍaḥ ।।

jaḍaḥ na tu jñānī ।।

svacittabilasaṃsthena nānāsambhramakāriṇā ।
balāt kāmapiśācena vivaśaḥ paribhūyate ।।

pūrvaślokasthaṃ tatreti padam atrāpy anuvartanīyam ।।

cintānāṃ lolavṛttīnāṃ lalanānām ivābhitaḥ ।
arpayaty avaśaś ceto jvālānām ātmajo yathā ।।

cintānāṃ kuṭumbabharaṇādiviṣayāṇāṃ । yauvane puruṣaḥ yathā lalanānāṃ cetaḥ arpayati tathā cintānām apīti piṇḍārthaḥ । ko yathātmajo bālaḥ yathā । yathā saḥ jvālānāṃ cetaḥ arpayati । tathety arthaḥ ।।

te te doṣā durārambhās tatra taṃ tādṛśāśayam ।
taruṇam pravilumpanti dṛśyās te naiva ye mune ।।

taruṇaṃ yauvanāviṣṭam puruṣam । pravilumpanti viśrānteḥ cyāvayanti । te te ke । ye doṣāḥ dṛśyāḥ naiva bhavanti । tebhyo niṣkrāntatvād iti bhāvaḥ । atha vā ye doṣāḥ te naiva nānyena dṛśyāḥ bhavantīti yojyam ।।

mahānarakabījena santatabhramadāyinā ।
yauvanena na ye naṣṭā naṣṭā nānyena te janāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nānārasamayī cintāvṛttāntanicayombhitā ।
bhīmā yauvanabhūr yena tīrṇā dhīraḥ sa ucyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nimeṣabhāsurākāram ālolaghanagarjitam ।
vidyutprakāśam aniśaṃ yauvanam me na rocate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vividhāvartabahulam paṅkalagnaṃ jaḍāśayam ।
taraṅgabhaṅguram bhīmaṃ yauvanam me na rocate ।।

āvartāḥ kāmavegāḥ । paṅkalagnam pāpagrastam । jaḍaḥ āśayaḥ yasmiṃs ।।

sarvasyāgresaram puṃsaḥ kṣaṇamātramanoharam ।
gandharvanagaraprakhyaṃ yauvanam me na rocate ।।

sarvasya puṃsa iti jātau ekavacanam । agresaram avyabhicārīty arthaḥ ।।

iṣuprapātamātraṃ hi sukhadaṃ duḥkhabhāsuram ।
dāhadoṣapradaṃ nityaṃ yauvanam me na rocate ।।

iṣuprapātamātraṃ kṣanamātram ity arthaḥ ।।

madhuraṃ svādu tiktaṃ ca dūṣaṇaṃ doṣabhūṣaṇam ।
surākallolasadṛśaṃ yauvanam me na rocate ।।

madhuram āpāte ।।

asatyaṃ satyasaṅkāśam acirād vipralambhadam ।
svapnāṅganāsaṅgasamaṃ yauvanam me na rocate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kṣaṇaprakāśataralam mithyāracitacakrikam ।
alātacakrapratimaṃ yauvanam me na rocate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mṛdusphāratarodāram antaḥśūnyaṃ kṣaṇāt kṣatam ।
śaradambudasaṅkāśaṃ yauvanam me na rocate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

āpātamātraramaṇaṃ sadbhāvarahitāntaram ।
veśyāstrīsaṅgamaprakhyaṃ yauvanam me na rocate ।।

sadbhāvaḥ sattvaṃ snehaś ca ।।

ye kecana durārambhās te sarve sarvaduḥkhadāḥ ।
tāruṇye sannidhiṃ yānti mahotpātā iva kṣaye ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

hārdāndhakārakāriṇyā bhairavākāravān api ।
yauvanākārayāminyā bibheti bhagavān api ।।

hārdaṃ hṛtsambandhi । andhakāraṃ karotīti tādṛśyā । bhagavān śrīmahādevaḥ । anyeṣāṃ tu kā kathety apiśabdābhiprāyaḥ ।।

suvismṛtaśubhācāram buddhivaidhuryadāyinam ।
dadāty atitarām eṣa bhramaṃ yauvanavibhramaḥ ।।

suvismṛtaḥ śubhācāraḥ yasmiṃs ।।

kāntāviyogajātena hṛdi durdharṣavahninā ।
yauvane dahyate jantus tarur dāvāgninā yathā ।।

durdharṣavahninā durnivāryeṇa kāmāgninā ।।

vistīrṇāpi prasannāpi pāvany api hi yauvane ।
matiḥ kaluṣatām eti prāvṛṣīva taraṅgiṇī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śakyate ghanakallolabhīmā rodhayituṃ nadī ।
na tu tāruṇyataralā tṛṣṇātaralitāntarā ।।

tāruṇyataralety anena yauvananindaiveyaṃ jñātavyā ।।

sā kāntā tau stanau pīnau te vilāsās tad ānanam ।
tāruṇya iti cintābhir yāti jarjaratāṃ janaḥ ।।

tāruṇye yauvane ।।

tarattaralatṛṣṇārtaṃ yuvānam iha sādhavaḥ ।
pūjayanti na tucchehaṃ jarattṛṇalavaṃ yathā ।।

tarantī cañcalatāṃ gacchantī ।।

nāśāyaiva madāndhasya doṣamauktikadhāriṇaḥ ।
abhimānamahebhasya nityālānaṃ hi yauvanam ।।

doṣāḥ rāgādayaḥ । abhimāna evāhaṅkāra eva mahebhas । tasya ।।

manovipulamūlānāṃ doṣāśīviṣadhāriṇām ।
roṣarodanavṛkṣāṇāṃ yauvanaṃ navakānanam ।।

roṣeṇa yāni rodanāni ।।

rasakesarasambādhaṃ kuvikalpadalākulam ।
duścintācañcarīkāṇām puṣkaraṃ viddhi yauvanam ।।

tvaṃ yauvanaṃ । duścintāḥ eva bhogaviṣayāḥ kucintā eva । cañcarīkāḥ bhramarāḥ । teṣām puṣkaram ādhārabhūtam padmaṃ । viddhi jānīhi । rasāḥ viṣayāsvādā eva । taiḥ sambādhaṃ saṅkaṭaṃ । tathā kuvikalpāḥ kutsitāḥ vikalpā eva dalāni । taiḥ ākulaṃ nirbharitam ।।

kṛtākṛtakupakṣāṇāṃ hṛtsarastīracāriṇām ।
ādhivyādhivihaṅgānām ālayo navayauvanam ।।

kṛtākṛtau vihitāvihitau eva । vihitasyāpi dharmākhyaśuddhāśuddhivyutthāpakatvena kṛtākṛtety uktam ।।

jaḍānāṃ gatasaṅkhyānāṃ kallolānāṃ vilāsinām ।
anapekṣitamaryādo vāridhiḥ pūrṇayauvanam ।।

anapekṣitamaryādaḥ maryādarahita ity arthaḥ ।।

sarveṣāṃ guṇaparṇānām apanetuṃ rajastataḥ ।
apanetuṃ sthito dakṣo viṣamo yauvanānilaḥ ।।

apanetuṃ sthitaḥ sarvāpanayanaśīlaḥ । rajasā rajoguṇena dhūlyā ca । tataḥ vyāptaḥ । viṣamaḥ yauvanānilaḥ sarveṣāṃ guṇaparṇānām apanetuṃ dūrīkartuṃ । dakṣaḥ bhavati ।।

nayanti pāṇḍutāṃ vaktram ākulāvakarotkaṭāḥ ।
ārohanti parāṃ koṭiṃ rūkṣā yauvanapāṃsavaḥ ।।

ākulaḥ cañcalaḥ । yaḥ avakaraḥ saṅkaraḥ । marjanīsaṅkṣiptaṃ raja iti yāvat । tadvat utkaṭāḥ udbhaṭāḥ ।।

udbodhayati doṣālīṃ nikṛntati guṇāvalim ।
narāṇāṃ yauvanollāso vilāso duṣkṛtaśriyāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śarīrapaṅkajarajaś cañcalām matiṣaṭpadīm ।
nibadhya mohayaty eṣa naraṃ yauvanacandramāḥ ।।

yauvanavaśenaiva puruṣaḥ śarīrāsakto bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

śarīraṣaṇḍakodbhūtā ramyā yauvanavallarī ।
lagnam eva manobhṛṅgam madayaty unnatiṃ gatā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śarīramarutāpotthāṃ yuvatām mṛgatṛṣṇikām ।
manomṛgāḥ pradhāvantaḥ patanti viṣamāṭavīm ।।

śarīram eva maruḥ । tatra tāpotthāṃ śarīramarutāpotthāṃ । viṣamāṭavīṃ strītyādiviṣayarūpaṃ viṣamāraṇyam ।।

śarīraśarvarījyotsnā cittakesariṇaḥ saṭā ।
laharī jīvitāmbhodher yuvatā me na rocate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dināni katicid yeyam phalitā dehajaṅgale ।
yuvatāśarad asyāṃ hi na samāśvāsam arhatha ।।

phalitā kāntābhogādiphalayuktā ।।

jhagity eṣa prayāty eva śarīrād yuvatākhagaḥ ।
kṣaṇenaivālpabhāgyasya hastāc cintāmaṇir yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yadā yadā parāṃ koṭim abhyārohati yauvanam ।
valganti sarasāḥ kāmās tadā nāśāya kevalam ।।

sarasāḥ viṣayarasapūrṇāḥ ।।

tāvad eva vivalganti rāgadveṣapiśācikāḥ ।
nāstam eti samastaiṣā yāvad yauvanayāminī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nānādhikārabahale varāke kṣaṇanāśini ।
kārunyaṃ kuru tāruṇye mriyamāṇe sute yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

harṣam āyāti yo mohāt puruṣaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅginā ।
yauvanena mahāmugdhaḥ sa vai naramṛgaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mānamohamadonmattaṃ yauvanaṃ yo abhilaṣyati ।
acireṇa sudurbuddhiḥ paścāttāpena yujyate ।।

paścāttāpena tannāśakṛtena ity arthaḥ ।।

te dharmyās te mahātmānas ta eva puruṣā bhuvi ।
ye sukhena samuttīrṇāḥ sādho yauvanasaṅkaṭāt ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sukhena tīryate ambhodhir utkṛṣṭamakarākaraḥ ।
na kallolavanollāsi sadoṣaṃ hatayauvanam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena yauvananindāṃ samāpayati

vinayabhūṣitam āryajanāspadaṃ karuṇayojjvalam āvalitaṃ guṇaiḥ ।
iha hi durlabham aṅga suyauvanaṃ jagati kānanam ambaragaṃ yathā ।।

etādṛśaṃ yauvanam praśastam eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe ekonaviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ yauvananindāṃ sampādya tatprasaṅgena strīnindām prastauti

māṃsaputtalikāyāś ca yantralolāṅgapañjare ।
snāyvasthigranthiśālinyāḥ striyāḥ kim iva śobhanam ।।

puttalikāyāḥ putrikāyāḥ । yantravat lolaṃ yat aṅgapañjaraṃ । tasmin । putrikāpi yantrasthā bhavati । na hi kiñcid api striyāḥ śobhanam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tvaṅmāṃsaraktabāṣpāsru pṛthak kṛtvā vilocanam ।
samālokaya ramyaṃ cet kim mudhā parimuhyasi ।।

sarvāṅgānām upalakṣaṇam etat ।।

itaḥ keśā ito raktam itīyam pramadātanuḥ ।
kim etayā ninditayā karotu vipulāśayaḥ ।।

vipulāśayasyātra ratir na yukteti bhāvaḥ ।।

vāsovilepanair yāni lālitāni punaḥ punaḥ ।
tāny aṅgāny avalumpanti kravyādāḥ sarvadehinām ।।

ataḥ strīṇām api kravyādā avalumpantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

meroḥ śṛṅgataṭollāsigaṅgājalarayopamā ।
dṛṣṭā yasmin stane muktā hārasyollāsaśālinaḥ ।।

śmaśāneṣu diganteṣu sa eva lalanāstanaḥ ।
śvabhir āsvādyate kāle laghupiṇḍa ivāndhasaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

raktamāṃsādidigdhāni karabhasya yathā vane ।
tathaivāṅgāni kāminyās tat praty api hi ko grahaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

āpātaramaṇīyatvaṃ kalpyate kevalaṃ striyāḥ ।
manye tad api nāsty atra mune mohaikakāraṇe ।।

atra strīśarīre ।।

vipulollāsadāyinyā madonmathanapūrvakam ।
ko viśeṣo vikāriṇyā madirāyā iha striyāḥ ।।

madirāyā iti pañcamī ।।

lalanālānasaṃlīnā mune mānavadantinaḥ ।
prabodhaṃ nādhigacchanti dīrghair api śamāṅkuśaiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

keśakajjaladhāriṇyas tīkṣṇāḥ prakṛtitaḥ sadā ।
duṣkṛtāgniśikhā nāryo dahanti tṛṇavan naram ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

te vandyās te mahātmānas ta eva puruṣā bhuvi ।
ye sukhena samuttīrṇāḥ sādho yauvatasaṅkaṭāt ।।

yauvatasaṅkaṭāt strīsamūhākhyāt ।।

jvalatām atidūre api sarasā api nīrasam ।
striyo hi narakāgnīnāṃ dāru cāru ca dāruṇam ।।

sarasā api striyaḥ nīrasaṃ dāru bhavantīti virodhābhāsaḥ ।।

kīrṇāndhakārakavarī tarattārakalocanā ।
pūrṇendubimbavadanā kumudotkarahāsinī ।।

līlāvilolapuruṣā kāryasaṃhārakāriṇī ।
paraṃ vimohanam buddheḥ kāminī dīrghayāminī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

puṣpābhirāmamadhurā karapallavalāsinī ।
bhramarabhrūvilāsāḍhyā stabakastanadhāriṇī ।।

puṣpakesaragaurāṅgī naramāraṇatatparā ।
dadāty uttamavaivaśyaṃ kāntā viṣamahālatā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sītkārocchvāsamātreṇa bhujaṅgadalanotkayā ।
kāntayoddhriyate jantuḥ kariṇyevorago bilāt ।।

bhujaṅgāḥ viṭāḥ sarpāś ca । uddhriyate ākṛṣyate ।।

kāmanāmnā kirātena vikīrṇā mugdhacetasām ।
nāryo naravihaṅgānām aṅgabandhanavāgurāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

lalanāvipulālāne manomattamataṅgajaḥ ।
ratiśṛṅkhalayā brahman baddhas tiṣṭhati mūkavat ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

janmapalvalamatsyānāṃ karmakoṭaravāriṇām ।
puṃsāṃ durvāsanārajjur nārī baḍiśapiṇḍikā ।।

baḍiśe hi matsyagrahaṇārtham annādipiṇḍikā sthāpyate ।।

mandureva turaṅgānām ālānam iva dantinām ।
puṃsām abjam ivālīnām bandhanaṃ vāmalocanāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nānārasamayī citrā bhogabhūmir iyam mune ।
striyam āśritya saṃyātā parām iha hi saṃsthitim ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sarveṣāṃ doṣaratnānāṃ susamudgikayānayā ।
duḥkhaśṛṅkhalayā nityam alam astu mama striyā ।।

alam astu dūre bhavatu ।।

kiṃ stanena kim akṣṇā vā kiṃ nitambena kim bhruvā ।
māṃsamātraikasāreṇa karomy aham avastunā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ito māṃsam ito raktam ito asthīni ca vāsaraiḥ ।
brahman katipayair eva yāti strī viśarārutām ।।

itiśabda adhyāhāryaḥ ।।

yās tā niṣparuṣais tūlair lālitāḥ patibhiḥ striyaḥ ।
tā mune pravibhaktāṅgyaḥ svapanti pitṛbhūmiṣu ।।

niṣparuṣaiḥ komalaiḥ । tūlaiḥ tūlavikāraiḥ śayanīyaiḥ । pitṛbhūmiṣu śmaśāneṣu ।।

yasmin ghananavasneham mukhe pattrāṅkuraśriyaḥ ।
kāntena racitā brahmañ śīryate tat tu jaṅgale ।।

ghanaḥ navaḥ snehaḥ yatra । kriyāviśeṣaṇam etat ।।

keśāḥ śmaśānavṛkṣeṣu yānti cāmaraleśatām ।
asthīny uḍuvad ābhānti dinair avanimaṇḍale ।।

dinaiḥ svalpakālenety arthaḥ ।।

pibanti pāṃsavo raktaṃ kravyādāś cāpy anekaśaḥ ।
carmānalaśikhā bhuṅkte khaṃ yānti prāṇavāyavaḥ ।।

ity eṣā lalanāṅgānām acireṇaiva bhāvinī ।
sthitir mayā vaḥ kathitā kim bhrāntim anudhāvatha ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhūtapañcakasaṅghaṭṭasaṃsthānaṃ lalanābhidham ।
rasād abhivahatv etat kathaṃ nāma dhiyānvitaḥ ।।

bhūtapañcakasya yaḥ saṅghaṭṭaḥ । tasya saṃsthānaṃ racanāviśeṣaḥ । rasād abhilāṣāt । abhivahatu anuyātu ।।

śākhāvitānagahanā kaṭvamlaphalaśālinī ।
pratānottālatām eti cintā kāntānusāriṇī ।।

vitānaṃ samūhaḥ । pratānair upaśākhābhir । yā uttālatā udbhaṭatā । kāntānusāriṇī kāntāviṣayā । kāntānusāriṇī cintā atyantaṃ ghanībhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

śocyatām paramām eti taruṇas taruṇīrataḥ ।
nibaddhaḥ kariṇīlobhād vindhyakhāte yathā dvipaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yasya strī tasya bhogecchā niḥstrīkasya na bhogabhūḥ ।
striyaṃ tyaktvā jagat tyaktaṃ jagat tyaktvā sukhī bhavet ।।

bhogeṣu stryādirūpeṣu । bhogabhūḥ bhogecchā ।।

sargāntaślokena strīnindāṃ samāpayati

āpātamātramadhureṣu duruttareṣu bhogeṣu nāham alipakṣatipelaveṣu ।
brahman rame maraṇarogajarādibhītyā śāmyāmy aham param upaimi vanam prayatnāt ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe viṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ prasaṅgāyātāṃ strīnindāṃ kṛtvā prakaraṇaprāptaṃ jarānindām prastauti

aparyāptaṃ hi bālatvam bālyam pibati yauvanam ।
yauvanaṃ ca jarā paścāt paśya karkaśatām mithaḥ ।।

pibati grasate ।।

himāśanir ivāmbhojaṃ vātyeva śaradambudam ।
dehaṃ jarā jarayati sarit tīrataruṃ yathā ।।

jarayati jīrṇatāṃ nayati ।।

śithilādīrghasarvāṅgaṃ jarājīrṇakalevaram ।
samam paśyanti kāminyaḥ puruṣaṃ karabhaṃ tathā ।।

tathāśabdaḥ samuccaye ।।

śvāsāyāsakadarthinyā gṛhīte jarasā jane ।
palāyya gacchati prajñā sapatnyeva hatāṅganā ।।

śvāsāyāsaiḥ kadarthayatīti tādṛśyā ।।

dāsāḥ putrāḥ striyaś caiva bāndhavāḥ suhṛdas tathā ।
hasanty unmattakam iva naraṃ vārdhakakampitam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

duṣprajñaṃ jaraḍhaṃ dīnaṃ hīnaṃ guṇaparākramaiḥ ।
gṛdhro vṛkṣam ivādīrghaṃ gardho hy abhyeti vṛddhatām ।।

dainyadoṣamayī dīrghā hṛdi dāhapradāyinī ।
sarvāpadām ekasakhī vardhate vārdhake spṛhā ।।

ādīrghaṃ samantād dīrgham । vṛddhatām vārdhakam ।।

kartavyaṃ kim mayā kaṣṭam paratrety atidāruṇam ।
apratīkārayogyaṃ hi vārdhake vardhate bhayam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ko ahaṃ varākaḥ kim iva karomi katham eva vā ।
tiṣṭhāmi maunam eveti dīnatodeti vārdhake ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

gardho abhyudeti sollāsam upabhoktuṃ na śakyate ।
hṛdayaṃ dahyate nūnaṃ śaktidausthyena vārdhake ।।

gardhaḥ upabhogalobhaḥ । sollāsam iti kriyāviśeṣaṇam ।।

jarājīrṇabakī yāvat kāsakreṅkārakāriṇī ।
rauti rogoragākīrṇā kāyadrumaśiraḥsthitā ।।

tāvad āgata evāśu kuto api paridṛśyate ।
ghanāndhatimirākāṅkṣī mune maraṇakauśikaḥ ।।

kāsaḥ rogaviśeṣaḥ ।।

sāyaṃsandhyāprajātaiva tamaḥ samanudhāvati ।
jarā vapuṣi dṛṣṭaiva mṛtiṃ samanudhāvati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jarākusumitaṃ dehadrumaṃ dṛṣṭvaiva dūrataḥ ।
mṛtibhṛṅgī drutam brahman narasyāyāti sūtsukā ।।

suṣṭhu utsukā sūtsukā ।।

śūnyaṃ nagaram ābhāti bhāti cchinnalato drumaḥ ।
bhāty anāvṛṣṭimān deśo na jarājarjaraṃ vapuḥ ।।

śūnyanagarādibhyo api aśubham eva vṛddhatvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

kṣaṇān nigiraṇāyaiva kāsakvaṇitakāriṇī ।
gṛdhrīvāmiṣam ādatte tarasaiva naraṃ jarā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dṛṣṭvaiva sūtsukevāśu pragṛhya śirasi kṣaṇāt ।
pralunāti jarā dehaṃ kumārī kairavaṃ yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sītkārakāriṇī pāṃsuparuṣā parijarjaram ।
śarīraṃ śātayaty eṣā vātyeva tarupallavam ।।

eṣā jarā । jarāgṛhītaḥ vātagṛhītaś ca puruṣaḥ sītkāraṃ karoti ।।

jarasopahato deho dhatte jarjaratāṃ gataḥ ।
tuṣāranikarākīrṇaparimlānāmbujaśriyam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jarājyotsnoditaiveyaṃ śiraḥśikharipṛṣṭhataḥ ।
vikāsayati saṃrabdhavātāṃ kāsakumudvatīm ।।

saṃrabdhaḥ ārabdhaḥ । vātaḥ vātarogaḥ yayā । sā ।।

paripakvaṃ samālokya jarākṣāravidhūsaram ।
śiraḥkuṣmāṇḍakam bhuṅkte puṃsaḥ kālaḥ kileśvaraḥ ।।

śira eva kuṣmāṇḍakam phalaviśeṣaḥ ।।

jarājahnusutodyuktā mūlāny asya nikṛntati ।
śarīratīravṛkṣasya calasyāyūṃṣi satvaram ।।

udyuktā pravṛttā । āyūṃṣi mūlāni āyurākhyāni mūlāni ।।

jarāmārjārikā bhuktayauvanākhutayendhitā ।
param ullāsam āyāti śarīrāmiṣagardhinī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kācid asti jagaty asmin nāmaṅgalakarī tathā ।
yathā jarākrośakarī dehajaṅgalajambukī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kāsaśvāsasasītkārā duḥkhadhūmatamomayī ।
jarājvālā jvalaty eṣā yayāsau dagdha eva hi ।।

asau vṛddhaḥ ।।

jarasā vakratām eti śuklāvayavapallavā ।
tāta tanvī tanur nṝṇāṃ latā puṣpānatā yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jarākarpūradhavalaṃ dehakarpūrapādapam ।
mune maraṇamātaṅgo nūnam uddharati kṣaṇāt ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

maraṇasya mune rājño jarādhavalacāmarā ।
āgacchato agre niryāti svādhivyādhipatākinī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

na jitāḥ śatrubhiḥ saṅkhye ye niṣpiṣṭādrikoṭayaḥ ।
te jarājīrṇarākṣasyā paśyāśu vijitā mune ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jarātuṣāradhavale śarīrasadanāntare ।
śaknuvanty akṣaśiśavaḥ spandituṃ na manāg api ।।

akṣaśiśavaḥ indriyabālakāḥ ।।

saṃsārasaṃsṛter asyā gandhakuṭyāḥ śirogatā ।
dehayaṣṭyā jarānāmnī cāmaraśrīr virājate ।।

gandhakuṭyāḥ śirasi cāmaraṃ sthāpyate । ghaṭakuṭyā iti vā pāṭhaḥ ।।

jarācandrodayasite śarīranagare sthite ।
kṣaṇād vikāsam āyāti mune maraṇakairavam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jarāsudhālepasite śarīrāntaḥpurāntare ।
aśaktir ādhir ārtiś ca tiṣṭhanti sukham aṅganāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

abhāvāgre sarā yatra jarā jayati jantuṣu ।
kas tatreha samāśvāso mama mandamater mune ।।

abhāvasya maraṇasyāgre sarā ।।

sargāntaślokena jarānindāṃ samāpayati

kiṃ tena durjīvitadurgraheṇa jarāṃ gatenāpi hi jīvyate yat ।
jarā jagatyām ajitā narāṇāṃ sarvaiṣaṇās tāta tiraskaroti ।।

tena prasiddhena । durjīvitadurgraheṇa kutsitajīvitākhyena duṣṭagraheṇa । jarāgatenāpi satā kiṃ jīvyate kimarthaṃ jīvyate । vyarthaṃ jīvyate iti yāvat । hi niścaye । yad yasmāt kāraṇāt । ajitā jarā narāṇāṃ sarvaiṣaṇāḥ samastāḥ ceṣṭāḥ । tiraskaroti nayati । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe ekaviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ jarānindāṃ kṛtvā kālanindām prastauti

vikalpakalpanānalpakalpitair alpabuddhibhiḥ ।
bhedair uddharatāṃ nītaḥ saṃsārakuhakabhramaḥ ।।

bhedaiḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । vikalpakalpanābhiḥ analpam atyantaṃ । kalpitaiḥ । asatyabhūtair ity arthaḥ । saṃsāra eva kuhakabhramaḥ mithyābhramaḥ ।।

satāṃ katham ivāstheha jāyate jālapañjare ।
bālā evāttum icchanti phalam makurabimbitam ।।

iha jālapañjare indrajālapañjararūpe saṃsāre ity arthaḥ । bhāmetivat prayogaḥ । attum bhakṣitum ।।

ihāpi vidyate yaiṣā pelavā sukhabhāvanā ।
ākhus tantum ivāśeṣaṃ kālas tām api kṛntati ।।

aśeṣam iti kriyāviśeṣaṇam ।।

na tad astīha yad ayaṃ kālas sakalaghasmaraḥ ।
grasate na jagajjātam mahābdhim iva vāḍavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

samastasāmānyatayā bhīmaḥ kālo maheśvaraḥ ।
dṛśyasattām imāṃ sarvāṃ kavalīkartum udyataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mahatām api no devaḥ pratipālayati kṣaṇāt ।
kālaḥ kavalitānantaviśvo viśvātmatāṃ gataḥ ।।

no pratipālayati na pratīkṣate । viśvātmatāṃ vyāpakatāṃ ।।

yugavatsarakalpākhyaiḥ kiñcit prakaṭatāṃ gataḥ ।
rūpair alakṣyarūpātmā sarvam ākramya tiṣṭhati ।।

sūryavārādivaśena jñātair iti śeṣaḥ ।।

ye ramyā ye śubhārambhāḥ sumeruguravo api ye ।
kālena vinigīrṇās te karabheṇeva pallavāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nirdayaḥ kaṭhinaḥ krūraḥ karkaśaḥ kṛpaṇo adhamaḥ ।
na tad asti yad adyāpi na kālo nigiraty ayam ।।

paunaruktyaprayogaḥ krodhāveśabāhulyaṃ sūcayati ।।

kālaḥ kavalanaikāntamatir atti girīn api ।
anantair api bhogaughair nāyaṃ tṛpto mahāśanaḥ ।।

mahāśanaḥ bahvāśī ।।

haraty ayaṃ nāśayati karoty atti nihanti ca ।
kālaḥ saṃsāranṛtye hi nānārūpair yathā naṭaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhinatti pravibhāgastho bhūtabījāny anāratam ।
jagaty asattayā cañcvā dāḍimāni yathā śukaḥ ।।

pravibhāge tiṣṭhatīti tādṛśaḥ । pravibhāgakārīty arthaḥ ।।

śubhāśubhaviṣāṇāgravilūnajanapallavaḥ ।
sphūrjati sphītajanatājīvarājīvinīgajaḥ ।।

sphītā sphāratvaṃ gatā । jīvarājīvinī jīvayuktā padminī ।।

viriñcamajjabrahmāṇḍabṛhadvilvaphaladrumam ।
brahmakānanam ābhogi param āvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।।

brahmāṇḍe hi viriñca eva sārabhūto bhavatīti viriñcamajjety uktaṃ । etena brahmaṇy api kālasparśa uktaḥ ।।

yāminībhramarīpūrṇā racayan dinamañjarīḥ ।
varṣakalpakalāvallīr na kadācana khidyate ।।

kāla iti śeṣaḥ । varṣakalpakalāvallī racayann iti yojyam ।।

bhidyate nāvabhagno api dagdho api hi na dahyate ।
dṛśyate nātidṛśyo api dhūrtacūḍāmaṇir mune ।।

atidṛśyatvaṃ kālasya ṛtuguṇādidarśanena jñeyam । na dṛśyate ākārābhāvāt । dhūrto api evaṃvidho bhavatīti dhūrtacūḍāmaṇir ity uktam ।।

ekenaiva nimeṣeṇa kiñcid utthāpayaty alam ।
kiñcid vināśayaty uccair manorājyavad ātataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

durvilāsavilāsinyā ceṣṭayā paripuṣṭayā ।
darvyeva sūpakṛt sūpaṃ janam āvartayan sthitaḥ ।।

āvartayan bhramayan ।।

tṛṇam pāṃsum mahendraṃ ca sumerum parṇam arṇavam ।
ātmasphāratayā sarvam ātmasātkartum udyataḥ ।।

ātmanaḥ yā sphāratā vyāpakatā । ātmasātkartum svādhīnaṃ kartum ।।

krauryam atraiva paryāptaṃ lubdhatātraiva saṃsthitā ।
sarvaṃ daurbhāgyam atraiva sarvam atraiva cāpalam ।।

atraiva asmin kāle eva ।।

prerayaṃl līlayārkendū krīḍatīha nabhastale ।
nikṣiptavīṭāyugalo nije bāla ivāṅgane ।।

vīṭā kandukaṃ ।।

sarvabhūtāsthimālābhir āpādavalitākṛtiḥ ।
vilasaty eṣa kalpānte kālaḥ kalpitakalpanaḥ ।।

kalpitāḥ kalpanāḥ jagadrūpāḥ kalpanāḥ ।।

asyoḍḍāmaranṛttasya kalpānte aṅgavinirgataiḥ ।
prasphuraty ambare merur bhūrjatvag iva vāyubhiḥ ।।

sphurati ākāśe bhramati ।।

rudro bhūtvā bhavaty eṣa mahendro atha pitāmahaḥ ।
śukro vaiśravaṇaś cāpi punar eva na kiñcana ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dhatte ajasrotthitadhvastān sargān amitabhāsurān ।
anyān anyān apy ananyān vīcīn abdhir ivātmani ।।

ajasram utthitāṃś ca tān dhvastāṃś ca sargān sṛṣṭīn । anyān anyān iti vīpsā । apiśabdaḥ ananyān ity anena sambadhyate ।।

mahākalpābhidhānebhyo vṛkṣebhyaḥ pariśātayan ।
devāsuragaṇān pakvān phalabhārān avasthitaḥ ।।

pariśātayan chedayan ।।

ālolabhūtamaṣakaghuṅghumānām prapātinām ।
brahmāṇḍoḍumbaraughānām bṛhatpādapatāṃ gataḥ ।।

ghuṅghumeti śabdānukaraṇam । uḍumbaraḥ phalaviśeṣaḥ । tatra hi maṣakāḥ bāhulyena tiṣṭhanti ।।

sattāmātrakumudvatyā cijjyotsnāpariphullayā ।
vapur vinodayaty eṣaḥ kriyāpriyatamānvitaḥ ।।

kriyāpriyatamānvitaḥ saḥ kālaḥ । cid eva prakāśarūpatvāt jyotsnā । tayā pariphullayā prakaṭībhūtayā । sattāmātrakumudvatyā । vapuḥ ātmānaṃ । vinodayati sadāsattayā kriyayā yuto bhavatīti ।।

anantāpāyaparyantam baddhapīṭhaṃ nijaṃ vapuḥ ।
mahāśailavad uttuṅgam avalambya vyavasthitaḥ ।।

anantāpāyaparyantam antāpāyaparyantarahitaṃ । nāśarahitam ity arthaḥ ।।

kvacic chyāmatamaḥśyāmaṃ kvacit kāntiyutaṃ tatam ।
dvayenāpi kramād riktaṃ svabhāvam bhāvayan sthitaḥ ।।

śyāmaṃ yat tamaḥ । [svabhāvam bhāvayan] svarūpaṃ sampādayann iti yāvat । etena rātridivase sandhyā ceti trayam uktam ।।

saṃlīnāsaṅkhyasaṃsārasārayā svātmasattayā ।
gurvīva bhāraghanayā nibaddhapadatāṃ gataḥ ।।

saṃlīnaḥ asaṅkhyasaṃsārāṇāṃ sāro yasyāṃ । gurvī hi nibaddhapadatāṃ gacchati iti gurvīty uktam ।।

na khidyate na mriyate na tiṣṭhati na gacchati ।
nāstam eti na codeti mahākalpaśatair api ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kevalaṃ jagadārambhalīlayā ghanahelayā ।
yāpayaty ātmanātmānam anahaṅkāram ānatam ।।

ghanā helā yasyāṃ । yāpayati samāpayati । ahaṅkārābhave hi kālo naśyati । svanāśakrīḍām api svayam eva karotīti bhāvaḥ ।।

yāminīpaṅkakalilāṃ dinakokanadāvalīm ।
kriyābhramarikām mandaṃ saraḥsu āropayan sthitaḥ ।।

saraḥsu arthāt bhuvanarūpeṣu । sūryarūpeṇeti śeṣaḥ ।।

gṛhītvā bhīṣaṇaḥ kṛṣṇāṃ rajanīṃ jīrṇamārjanīm ।
ālokakanakakṣodam āharaty abhito avanim ।।

āharati sammārjayati । rātriṃ vidhāya prakāśam upasaṃharatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

sañcārayan kriyāṅgulyā koṇakeṣv arkadīpikām ।
jagatsadmani kāruṇyāt kva kim astīti vīkṣate ।।

koṇakeṣu dikkoṇeṣu । anyo api hi dīpikām prajvālya sadmani kva kim astīti paśyati ।।

prekṣyāhāni nimeṣeṇa sūryākṣṇā pākavanty alam ।
lokapālaphalāny atti jagajjīrṇavanād ayam ।।

sūryākṣṇā sūryākhyena cakṣuṣā । ahāni prekṣya kañcit kālam pratīkṣyety arthaḥ ।।

jagajjīrṇakuṭīkīrṇān arpayaty ugrakoṭare ।
krameṇa guṇavallokamaṇīn mṛtyusamudgake ।।

jagajjīrṇakuṭyāṃ kīrṇān vikṣiptān । anyo api hi kuṭyāṃ vikṣiptān maṇīn samudgake arpayati ।।

guṇair āpūryate yaiva lokaratnāvalī bhṛśam ।
bhūṣārtham iva tām aṅge kṛtvā bhūyo nikṛntati ।।

anyo api rājādiḥ ratnāvalīm aṅge kṛtvā līlayā kṛntati ।।

dinahaṃsānusṛtayā niśendīvaramālayā ।
tārākesarayājasraṃ capalo valayaty alam ।।

valayati āvṛttaṃ sampādayati । bhuvanam iti śeṣaḥ ।।

śailorṇadyudharāśṛṅgajagadūrṇāyusaunikaḥ ।
pratyaham pibati prekṣya tārāraktakaṇān api ।।

śailā eva ūrṇā yasya । dyudhare dyāvāpṛthivyau eva śṛṅge yasya । īdṛśaṃ ca yat jagat tad eva ūrṇāyuḥ meṣaḥ । tasya saunikaḥ hiṃsakaḥ ।।

tāruṇyanalinīsoma āyurmātaṅgakesarī ।
na tad asti na yasyāyaṃ tucchātucchasya taskaraḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kalpakelivilāsena piṣṭapātitajantunā ।
nyagbhāvodbhavahāsena ramate svātmanātmani ।।

piṣṭāḥ cūrṇīkṛtāḥ । ata eva pātitāḥ jantavo yena । saḥ । tṛtīyāntatrayaṃ svātmanety asya viśeṣaṇatvena yojyam ।।

kartā bhoktātha saṃhartā smartā sarvam padaṃ gataḥ ।
sarvam eva karotīdaṃ na karoti ca kiñcana ।।

nakiñcidrūpatvāt na kiñcit karaṇaṃ jñeyam ।।

sargāntaślokena kālanindāṃ samāpayati

sakalam apy akalākalitāntaraṃ subhagadurbhagarūpadharaṃ vapuḥ ।
prakaṭayan sahasaiva ca gopayan vilasatīha hi kālabalaṃ nṛṣu ।।

sakalatvākalatvādikaṃ viṣayavibhāgena jñeyaṃ । prakaṭayan gopayan ity atra sarvanāmasthānābhāve api numāgama ārṣaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe dvāviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ kālanindāṃ kṛtvā kālavilāsaṃ kathayati

asyoḍḍāmaralīlasya dūrāstasakalāpadaḥ ।
saṃsāre rājaputrasya kālasyākalitaujasaḥ ।।

asminn ācarato dīnair mugdhair bhūtamṛgavrajaiḥ ।
ākheṭakaṃ jarjarite jagajjaṅgalajālake ।।

ekadeśollasaccāruvaḍavānalapaṅkajā ।
krīḍāpuṣkariṇī ramyā kalpakālamahārṇavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kaṭutiktāmlabhūtāḍhyaiḥ sadadhikṣīrasāgaraiḥ ।
tair eva taiḥ paryuṣitair jagadbhiḥ kālyavartanam ।।

kaṭutiktāmlāḥ atyantatāmasikatāmasikarājasikāḥ । kaṭvādirasaviśeṣayuktāś ca ye bhūtāḥ carācarāḥ bhūtāḥ siddhadravyāṇi ca । taiḥ āḍhyaiḥ yuktaiḥ । paredyuḥ uṣitaiḥ paryuṣitaiḥ । na tu navair ity arthaḥ । kālyavartanam prābhātikabhojanaṃ । asyeti sargādyaślokasthaṃ sarvatra yojyam ।।

caṇḍī caturasañcārā sarvamātṛgaṇānvitā ।
saṃsāravanavinyastanaraiṇākarṣaṇī vṛkī ।।

asya kālasya caṇḍīti nāmadheyā śaktiḥ । vṛkī bhavatīti sambandhaḥ । mātṛgaṇaḥ prasiddhaḥ । rājaputro api ākheṭakārthaṃ vṛkīm pālayati ।।

pṛthvī karatale pṛthvī pānapātrī rasānvitā ।
kamalotpalakalhāralolajālakamālitā ।।

pṛthvī vistīrṇā ।।

virāvī vikaṭāsphālo nṛsiṃho bhujapañjare ।
saṭāvikaṭapīnāṃsaḥ kāntaḥ krīḍāśakuntakaḥ ।।

nṛsiṃhaḥ narasiṃhaḥ । rājaputrasyāpi vilāsārtham pañjare siṃho bhavati ।।

alābuvīṇāmadhuraḥ śaradvyomāmalacchaviḥ ।
devaḥ kila mahākālo līlākokilabālakaḥ ।।

mahākālaḥ saṃhārādhikārī devaviśeṣaḥ ।।

ajasrasphūrjitākāro vāntaduḥkhaśarāśaniḥ ।
abhāvanāmakodaṇḍaḥ parisphurati sarvataḥ ।।

vāntāḥ udgīrṇāḥ । duḥkhāny eva śarāśanayaḥ । yena । abhāvanāmā cāsau kodaṇḍaḥ abhāvanāmakodaṇḍaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokena kālavilāsavarṇanaṃ samāpayati

anuttamasphuritavilāsavardhito bhraman haran parivilasan vidārayan ।
jarajjagaj jaraḍhavilolamarkaṭaḥ parisphuradvapur iha kāla īhate ।।

īhate nānāvidhāḥ ceṣṭāḥ karoti ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe trayoviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ kālavilāsam uktvā daivavilāsam prastauti

atraiva durvilāsānāṃ cūḍāmaṇir ivāparaḥ ।
karoty astīti lokena daivaṃ kālaś ca kathyate ।।

karoti iti kriyākathanam । astīti sattākathanaṃ । kālo atra kṛtānto abhipretaḥ । tasyaiva daivaparyāyatvāt ।।

kriyāmātrād ṛte yasya svaparispandarūpiṇaḥ ।
nānyad ālakṣyate rūpaṃ karmaṇo na samīhitam ।।

teneyam akhilā bhūtasantatir nityapelavā ।
tāpena himamāleva nītā vidhuratām bhṛśam ।।

yasya daivasya । na rūpam ālakṣyate । nāpi karmaṇaḥ samīhitaṃ karmālambanaṃ kāṅkṣitam । ayaṃ kiñcit karotīti teneyam bhūtasantatir vidhuratāṃ nītā ।।

yad idaṃ dṛśyate kiñcij jagadābhogimaṇḍalam ।
tat tasya nartanāgāram ihāsāv abhinṛtyati ।।

tasya daivasya ।।

asya nāmāntarakathanābhiprāyeṇāha

tṛtīyaṃ ca kṛtānteti nāma bibhrat sudāruṇam ।
kāpālikavapur mattaṃ daivaṃ jagati nṛtyati ।।

kāpālikavapuḥ kāpālikatulyaḥ ।।

asyaiva sarvādhāratvaṃ kathayati

nṛtyato hi kṛtāntasya nitāntam avirāgiṇaḥ ।
nityaṃ niyatikāntāyā mune paramakāminaḥ ।।

śeṣaḥ śaśikalāśubhro gaṅgāvāhaś ca tau tridhā ।
upavīte avītābhe ubhe saṃsāravakṣasi ।।

tau kau । śeṣaḥ gaṅgāvāhaś ca । avītābhe śobhāyukte । saṃsāra eva vakṣas । tatra ।।

candrārkamaṇḍale hemakaṭake karamūlayoḥ ।
līlāsarasijaṃ haste brāhmam brahmāṇḍakarṇikam ।।

brāhmam brahmaṇaḥ āsanabhūtam padmam । brahmāṇḍasya karṇikam karnikābhūtaṃ । tanmadhyavartitvāt ।।

tārābinducitaṃ lolapuṣkarāvartapallavam ।
ekārṇavapayodhautam ekam ambaram ambaram ।।

ambaram ākāśam ।।

evaṃrūpasya tasyāgre niyatir nityakāminī ।
anastamitasaṃrambham ārambhaiḥ parinṛtyati ।।

ārambhaiḥ yamaniyamarūpaiḥ । nartakasya samīpe hi nartakī api nṛtyati ।।

tasyā nartanalolāyā jaganmaṇḍapakoṭare ।
aruddhaspandarūpāyā āgamāpāyacañcure ।।

cārubhūṣaṇam aṅgeṣu devalokāntarāvalī ।
āpātālaṃ nabho lambaṃ kavarīmaṇḍalam bṛhat ।।

devānām yāni lokāntarāṇi । teṣām āvalī aṅgeṣu cārubhūṣaṇam bhavati । nabhaḥ kathambhūtam । āpātālam pātālaṃ tāvat । lambaṃ vyāpakaṃ । nṛtyantyāś ca kavarī lambā bhavati ।।

narakālī ca mañjīramālā kalakalākulā ।
protā duṣkṛtasūtreṇa pātālacaraṇe calā ।।

mañjīramālā kiṅkiṇīmālā ।।

kastūrikātilakakaṃ kriyāsakhyopakalpitam ।
citritaṃ citraguptena yāme vadanapaṭṭake ।।

yāme yamasambandhini । vadanapaṭṭake mukhapaṭṭake । arthāt yamaśāsanapaṭṭarūpake mukhe । citraguptena citritaṃ citraguptakartṛkaṃ citritaṃ । citraguptalikhitā lipir iti yāvat । kastūrikātilakam bhavati । kathambhūtaṃ । kriyāsakhyā kriyāśaktirūpayā sakhyā । upakalpitam citraguptam āviśya racitam । sakhī hi sakhyās tilakaṃ karoti ।।

kālīrūpam upasthāya kalpānteṣu kriyākulam ।
nṛtyaty eṣā punar devī sphuṭacchailaghanāravam ।।

kālī kālaśaktiḥ । tasyā rūpam upasthāya āśritya । pūrvavṛttāpekṣayā punar iti prayogaḥ ।।

paścātpralambavibhrāntakaumārarathabarhibhiḥ ।
netratrayabṛhadrandhrabhūribhāṅkārabhīṣaṇaiḥ ।।

lambalolaśaraccandravitīrṇaharamūrdhajaiḥ ।
uccaraccārumandāragaurīkavaricāmaraiḥ ।।

uttāṇḍavācalākārabhairavādaratumbakaiḥ ।
raṇatsahasrarandhrendradehabhikṣākapālakaiḥ ।।

śuṣkā śarīrakhaṭvāṅgabhaṅgair āpūritāmbaram ।
bhāyayaty ātmanātmānam api kṛṣṇair ghanāsitam ।।

kulakam । śuṣkā śoṣaṇadharmayuktā । prakṛtatvāt iyaṃ niyatiḥ । ātmanā ghanāsitam atyantakṛṣṇam । ātmānam api bhāyayati bhayāviṣṭaṃ karoti । anyeṣāṃ tu kā katheti bhāvaḥ । ātmānam kathambhūtam । śarīrasya ye khaṭvāṅgabhaṅgāḥ arthāt khaṭvāṅgabhaṅgarūpāḥ avayavāḥ । taiḥ āpūritāmbaram । śarīrakhaṭvāṅgaiḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । paścād ityādi । paścātpralambaḥ ata eva vibhrāntaḥ bhraman । kaumāraḥ kumārasambandhī । bhāṅkārāḥ vātakṛtāḥ jñeyāḥ । lambaś cāsau lolaś ca yaḥ śaraccandras । tena vitīrṇāḥ dattāḥ । haravat mūrdhajāḥ yeṣāṃ । yathā harasya keśāḥ candrakalayā bhāsitāḥ bhavanti । tathāsyāḥ pūrṇena śaraccandreṇeti bhāvaḥ । uccaraccārumandārā vilasaccārumandārā । sā eva cāmaraṃ yeṣāṃ । uttāṇḍavaḥ cāsau acalākāraḥ । bhairavaḥ mahābhairavaḥ । sa evādaratumbakaḥ ādaraviṣayaḥ vādyabhāṇḍaviśeṣaḥ yeṣāṃ । raṇanti sahasrarandhrāṇi netrarūpāṇi randhrasahasrāṇi yasya । tādṛśaḥ yaḥ indradehaḥ । sa eva bhikṣākapālakaṃ yeṣāṃ । idaṃ ca sthūladṛṣṭyartham bāhyadhyānam uktam । sūkṣmadṛṣṭīn prati tu bhaṅgyā kumārādiṣv api niyatisparśaḥ uktaḥ ।।

viśvarūpaśiraścakracārupuṣkaramālayā ।
tāṇḍaveṣu vivalgantī mahākalpeṣu rājate ।।

viśvarūpasya virājo । tad eva cārupuṣkaramālā ।।

pramattapuṣkarāvartaḍamarūḍḍāmarāravaiḥ ।
tasyāḥ kila palāyante kalpānte tumburādayaḥ ।।

ḍamaravaḥ vādyabhāṇḍaviśeṣāḥ । uḍḍāmarāḥ udbhaṭāḥ । tumbureti gandharvanāma ।।

nṛtyato ante kṛtāntasya candramaṇḍalahāsinaḥ ।
tārakācandrakācāruvyomapiñchāvacūlinaḥ ।।

ekasmiñ śravaṇe dīrghā himavān asti mudrikā ।
apare api mahāmeruḥ kāntā kāñcanakarṇikā ।।

ante kalpānte । candramaṇḍalam eva hāsaḥ । tadyuktasya । tad avacūlaṃ śirobhūṣaṇaṃ yasya । mudrikā śvetaḥ karṇābharaṇaviśeṣaḥ ।।

atraiva kuṇḍale lole candrārkau gaṇḍamaṇḍale ।
lokālokācalaśreṇī sarvataḥ kaṭimekhalā ।।

gaṇḍamaṇḍale gaṇḍabhittau । kaṭisthā mekhalā kaṭimekhalā ।।

itaś cetaś ca gacchantī vidyudvalayavarṇikā ।
anilāndolitā bhāti nīradāṃśukapaṭṭikā ।।

vidyudvalaya eva varṇikā bhūṣaṇaviśeṣaḥ yasyās । tādṛśī vidyudvalayavarṇikā ।।

musulaiḥ paṭṭisaiḥ śūlaiḥ prāsais tomaramudgaraiḥ ।
tīkṣṇaiḥ kṣīṇajagadvrātakṛtāntair iva sambhṛtaiḥ ।।

saṃsārabandhanādīrghe pāśe kālakaracyute ।
śeṣabhogamahāsūtre protair mālāsya śobhate ।।

saṃsārabandhanārtham । asya samanantaroktasya । daivāparaparyāyasya kṛtāntasya ।।

jīvollasanmakarikāratnatejobhir ujjvalā ।
saptābdhikaṅkaṇaśreṇī bhujayor asya bhūṣaṇam ।।

jīvena ullasantaḥ । kaṅkaṇeṣv api makarikāḥ bhavanti ।।

vyavahāramahāvartā sukhaduḥkhaparamparā ।
rajaḥpūrṇā tamaḥśyāmā romālī tasya rājate ।।

vyavahārāṇām mahāvartāḥ punaḥ punar āgamanāni yasyāṃ । tādṛśī sukhaduḥkhaparamparā tasya romālī rājate । rajaḥpūrṇā rajoguṇabharitā । tathā tamaḥśyāmā tamoguṇamalinā । romālī api āvartayuktā rajaḥpūrṇā tamaḥśyāmā ca bhavati ।।

evamprāyāṃ sa kalpānte kṛtāntas tāṇḍavodbhaṭām ।
upasaṃhṛtya nṛtyehāṃ sṛṣṭyā saha maheśvaraḥ ।।

punar hāsyamayīṃ nṛttalīlāṃ sarvasvarūpiṇīm ।
tanotīmāṃ jarāduḥkhaśokābhinayabhūṣitām ।।

sṛṣṭyā saha niyatyā saha ।।

sargāntaślokenaitat samāpayati

bhūyaḥ karoti bhuvanāni vanāntarāṇi lokāntarāṇi janajālakakalpanāṃ ca ।
ācāracārukalanāṃ ca calācalāṃ ca paṅkād yathārbhakajano racanām akhinnaḥ ।।

calācalām atyantacalām ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe caturviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ daivavilāsam uktvā phalitam āha

vṛtte asminn eva caiteṣāṃ kālādīnām mahāmune ।
saṃsāranāmni kaivāsthā mādṛśānām bhavatv iha ।।

ata iti śeṣaḥ । ādiśabdena daivādīnāṃ grahaṇam ।।

vikrītā iva tiṣṭhāma etair daivādibhir vayam ।
dhūrtaiḥ prapañcacaturair mugdhā vanamṛgā iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

eṣo anāryasamācāraḥ kālaḥ kavalanonmukhaḥ ।
jagaty avirataṃ lokam pātayaty āpadarṇave ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dahaty ante durāśābhir daivo dāruṇaceṣṭayā ।
lokam puṣpanikāśābhir jvālābhir dahano yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dhṛtiṃ vidhurayaty ekāmayadārūpavallabhā ।
strītvāt svabhāvacapalā niyatir niyamonmukhī ।।

āmayadā rogadāyinī । na rūpeṇa vallabhā arūpavallabhā ।।

grasate aviratam bhūtajālaṃ sarpa ivānilam ।
kṛtāntaḥ karkaśācāro jarāṃ nītvā jagadvapuḥ ।।

jagad eva vapuḥ yasya ।।

yamanirghṛṇarājendro nārtaṃ nāmānukampate ।
sarvabhūtadayācāro jano durlabhatāṃ gataḥ ।।

ārtaṃ dīnam ।।

sarvā eva mune phalguvibhavā bhūtajātayaḥ ।
duḥkhāyaiva durantāya dāruṇā lobhabhūmayaḥ ।।

phalguvibhavāḥ nissāravibhavayuktāḥ ।।

āyur atyantataralam mṛtyur ekas tu niṣṭhuraḥ ।
tāruṇyaṃ cātitaralam bālyaṃ jaḍatayā hṛtam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kalākalaṅkito loko bandhavo bhavabandhanam ।
bhogā bhavamahārogās tṛṣṇā ca mṛgatṛṣṇikā ।।

kalābhiḥ paravañcanākhyābhiḥ kalābhiḥ ।।

śatravaś cendriyāṇy eva satyaṃ yātam asatyatām ।
praharaty ātmanaivātmā mana eva manoripuḥ ।।

ātmā । durvikalpair iti śeṣaḥ । mana eva aśuddhamanaḥ eva । manoripuḥ śuddhasya manaso ripuḥ bhavati ।।

ahaṅkāraḥ kalaṅkāya buddhayaḥ paripelavāḥ ।
kriyā duṣphaladāyinyo līlāḥ strīniṣṭhatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

paripelavā atīkṣṇāḥ ।।

vāñchāviṣayaśālinyaḥ sacamatkṛtayaḥ kṛtāḥ ।
nāryo doṣapatākinyo rasā nīrasatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

vāñchāviṣayāś ca tāḥ śālinyaś ca āpātaramaṇīyāś ca । sacamatkṛtayaḥ camatkārayuktāḥ । bhāvitā iti yāvat । rāgādidoṣamayatvāt rāgādidoṣapatākinyaḥ । rasāḥ śāstrādiviṣayāḥ abhilāṣāḥ । nīrasatāṃ śuṣkatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

vastv avastutayā cāttaṃ dattaṃ cittam ahaṅkṛtau ।
abhāvarodhitā bhāvā bhavānto nādhigamyate ।।

asmābhiḥ । vastu satyaṃ vastu । avastutayā deho aham ity evaṃrūpeṇa avastubhāvenāttaṃ gṛhītaṃ । tathā cittam ahaṅkṛtau dattam ahaṅkāragrastaṃ kṛtam ity arthaḥ । bhāvāḥ abhāvarodhitāḥ nāśagṛhītāḥ । na jñātā iti śeṣaḥ । ataḥ bhavāntaḥ nādhigamyate na prāpyate ।।

tapyate kevalaṃ sādho matir ākulitāntarā ।
rāgorago vilasati virāgaṃ nopagacchati ।।

virāgaṃ rāgābhāvaḥ । nopagacchati nāgacchati ।।

rajoguṇahatā dṛṣṭis tamaḥ samparivardhate ।
na cādhigamyate sattvaṃ tattvam atyantadūrataḥ ।।

tattvam paramārthaḥ ।।

sthitir asthiratāṃ yātā mṛtir āgamanonmukhī ।
dhṛtir vaidhuryam āyāti ratir nityam avastuni ।।

avastuni avastubhūte dehādau ।।

matir māndyena malinā pātaikaparamaṃ vapuḥ ।
jvalatīva jarā dehe pravisphūrjati duṣkṛtam ।।

māndyena jāḍyena ।।

yatnenāyāti yuvatā dūre sajjanasaṅgatiḥ ।
gatir na vidyate kācit kvacin nodeti satyatā ।।

yuvatā lakṣaṇayā stryāsaktiḥ ।।

mano vimuhyatīvāntar muditā dūrato gatā ।
nojjvalā karuṇodeti dūrād āyāti nīcatā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dhīratādhīratām eti pātotpātaparo janaḥ ।
sulabho durjanāśleṣo durlabhaḥ sādhusaṅgamaḥ ।।

dhīratā adhīratām eti naśyatīty arthaḥ ।।

āgamāpāyino bhāvā bhāvanā bhavabandhanī ।
nīyate kevalaṃ kvāpi nityam bhūtaparamparā ।।

nīyate ।।

diśo api hi na dṛśyante deśo apy avyapadeśabhāk ।
śailā api hi śīryante kaivāsthā mādṛśe jane ।।

deśaḥ avyapadeśabhāk deśeti vyapadeśaṃ na bhajatīti tādṛk syāt । deśasyāpi deśeti nāma kālena na syād ity arthaḥ । yatredṛśānām īdṛśā daśā bhaviṣyanti tatra mādṛśe jane kā eva āsthā ko viśvāsaḥ syād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

dravanty api samudrāś ca śīryante tārakā api ।
siddhā api na sidhyanti kaivāsthā mādṛśe jane ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

adyate asattayāpi dyaur bhuvanaṃ cāpi bhajyate ।
dharāpi yāti vaidhuryaṃ kaivāsthā mādṛśe jane ।।

asattayā nāśena । dyaur api adyate grasyate ।।

dānavā api dīryanti dhruvo apy adhruvajīvitaḥ ।
amarā api māryante kaivāsthā mādṛśe jane ।।

māryante ।।

śakro apy ākramyate śakrair yamo api hi niyamyate ।
vāyor apy asty avāyuṣṭvaṃ kaivāsthā mādṛśe jane ।।

śakraiḥ navīnaiḥ śakraiḥ ।।

somo api vyomatām eti mārtāṇḍo apy eti khaṇḍanam ।
rugṇatām agnir apy eti kaivāsthā mādṛśe jane ।।

vyomatām ।।

parameṣṭhy apy aniṣṭhāvān harate harim apy ajaḥ ।
bhavo apy abhavatāṃ yāti kaivāsthā mādṛśe jane ।।

bhavo apy śrīmahādevo api । abhavatām amahādevabhāvam ।।

kālaḥ śakalatām eti niyatiś cāpi nīyate ।
kham apy ālīyate anante kaivāsthā mādṛśe jane ।।

anante antarahite kasmiṃścid vastuni ।।

aśravyāvācyadurdarśatantreṇājñātamūrtinā ।
bhuvanāni viḍambyante kenāpi bhramadāyinā ।।

aśravyaṃ tathā avācyaṃ tathā durdarśaṃ tantraṃ vañcanopāyaḥ । kenāpīti anirvācyenety arthaḥ ।।

ahaṅkārakalām etya sarvatrāntaravāsinā ।
na so asti triṣu lokeṣu yas teneha na badhyate ।।

dehādau ātmabhāvaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ । tena kenāpīty arthaḥ ।।

śilāśailakaṭapreṣu sāśvasūto divākaraḥ ।
vanapāṣāṇavan nityam avaśaḥ paridolyate ।।

śilāyuktāḥ śailāḥ śilāśailāḥ । teṣāṃ kaṭaprāḥ samūhāḥ । teṣu paridolyate dolanaṃ kāryate ।।

dharāgolakam antaḥsthasurāsuragaṇāspadam ।
veṣṭyate dhiṣṇyacakreṇa pakvākṣoṭam iva tvacā ।।

dharāgolakam bhūgolaṃ । veṣṭyate veṣṭanayuktaṃ kriyate । dhiṣṇyacakreṇeti karaṇe tṛtīyā ।।

divi devā bhuvi narāḥ pātāle asurabhoginaḥ ।
kalpitāḥ kalpamātreṇa nīyante jarjarāṃ daśām ।।

asurabhoginaḥ daityasarpāḥ । kalpamātreṇa kalpamātraparimāṇena ।।

kāmaś ca jagatīśānaraṇalabdhaparākramaḥ ।
akrameṇaiva vikrānto lokam ākramya valgati ।।

īśānena yaḥ raṇaḥ । tena labdhaḥ parākramaḥ । yena ।।

vasanto mattamātaṅgo madaiḥ kusumavarṣanaḥ ।
āmoditakakupcakraś ceto nayati vakratām ।।

madaiḥ madavāribhiḥ । vakratāṃ kāmakalāvidagdhatvam । kāmaprasaṅgeneha vasantābhidhānam ।।

anuraktāṅganālokalocanālokitākṛti ।
spaṣṭīkartum manaḥ śakto na viveko mahān api ।।

mahān api vivekaḥ manaḥ spaṣṭīkartuṃ śuddhīkartuṃ । manaḥ kathambhūtaṃ । anurakto yaḥ aṅganālokaḥ । tasya yat locanālokitam dṛṣṭipātas । tadvad ākṛtiḥ yasya । atyantacalam ity arthaḥ ।।

paropakārakāriṇyā parārtyā paritaptayā ।
buddha eva sukhī manye svārthaśītalayā dhiyā ।।

buddhaḥ jñānī । svārthe svaprayojane । śītalayā । na svārthanimittam paritaptayeti yāvat ।।

utpannadhvaṃsinaḥ kālavaḍavānalapātinaḥ ।
saṅkhyātuṃ kena śakyante kallolā jīvitāmbudheḥ ।।

jīvitāmbudheḥ kallolāḥ jīvā ity arthaḥ ।।

sarva eva narā mohād durāśāpāśapātinaḥ ।
doṣagulmakasāraṅgā nigīrṇā janmajaṅgale ।।

doṣagulmakasāraṅgāḥ doṣapriyā ity arthaḥ । mṛgo gulmapriyo bhavati । nigīrṇāḥ grastāḥ । sāraṅgā api pāśapātinaḥ jaṅgale kirātena grastā bhavanti ।।

saṅkṣīyate jagati janmaparamparāsu lokasya tair iha kukarmabhir āyur etat ।
ākāśapādapalatākṛtapāśakalpaṃ yeṣām phalaṃ na hi vicāravido api vidmaḥ ।।

ākāśapādapalatākṛtapāśakalpam asad ity arthaḥ । iha karma kurvantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokenaitat samāpayati

adyotsavo ayam ṛtur eṣa tatheha yātrā te bāndhavāḥ sukham idaṃ sa viśeṣabhogaḥ ।
itthaṃ mudhaiva kalayan svavikalpajālam ālolapelavamatir galatīha lokaḥ ।।

ālolapelavamatir aticañcalasvalpabuddhir ity arthaḥ । svavikalpajālam ity anena utsavādīnām atyantāsattvam uktam । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe pañcaviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

punar api saṃsāradurvilasitam eva kathayati

anyac ca tātātitarām aramye manorame veha jagatsvarūpe ।
na kiñcid apy eti tad arthajātaṃ yenātiviśrāntim upaiti cetaḥ ।।

aham bravīmīti śeṣaḥ । he tātāham anyac ca bravīmi । kim bravīṣīty apekṣāyām āhātitarām iti । manorame vā manorame iva । arthajātam padārthasamūhaḥ । atyantaviśrāntau hi satyām anyārthaviṣayākāṅkṣā na punar udbhaved iti bhāvaḥ ।।

bālye gate kalpitakelilole vayomṛge dāradarīṣu kīrṇe ।
śarīrake jarjaratām prayāte vidūyate kevalam eva lokaḥ ।।

vayomṛge yauvanākhye mṛge । jarjaratāṃ vṛddhatvaṃ । vidūyate santapyate ।।

jarātuṣārābhihatāṃ śarīra- sarojinīṃ dūratare vihāya ।
kṣaṇād gate jīvitacañcarīke janasya saṃsārasaro viśuṣkam ।।

vihāya tyaktvā । jīvitacañcarīke jīvitākhye bhramare ।।

yadā yadā pākam upaiti nūnaṃ tadā tadeyaṃ navam ātanoti ।
jarābharānalpanavaprasūnaṃ vijarjarā kāyalatā narāṇām ।।

nūnaṃ niścaye । navam iti kriyāviśeṣaṇam । tena na paunaruktyam । āścaryaṃ ca pākaṃ gatāyāḥ latāyāḥ navaprasūnasya navam ātananam ।।

tṛṣṇānadī sāratarapravāha- grastākhilānantapadārthajātā ।
taṭasthasantoṣasuvṛkṣamūla- nikāṣadakṣā vahatīha loke ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śarīranauś carmanibaddhabandhā bhavāmbudhāv ālulitā bhramantī ।
pravroḍyate pañcabhir indriyākhyair adho vahantī makarair adhīnā ।।

pañcabhir indriyākhyaiḥ makaraiḥ śarīranauḥ pravroḍyate magnā sampādyate iti sambandhaḥ । ālulitaṃ samantāc cañcalam ।।

tṛṣṇālatākānanacāriṇo amī śākhāśataṃ kāmamahīruheṣu ।
paribhramantaḥ kṣapayanti kāmam manomṛgā no phalam āpnuvanti ।।

kāmaṃ niścaye । tṛṣṇālatānāṃ yat kānanam । tatra carantīti tādṛśās । tathā paribhramantaḥ paribhramaṇaśīlāḥ । amī manomṛgāḥ । kāmamahīruheṣu kānanagateṣu paramakāmākhyavṛkṣeṣu । gatam śākhāśataṃ । arthāt avāntarakāmarūpaṃ śākhāśataṃ । kṣapayanti cālayanti । svaviṣayaṃ kurvantīti yāvat । tathāpi phalaṃ no āpnuvanti ।।

kṛcchreṣu dūrāstaviṣādamohāḥ svāmyeṣv anutsiktamanoḥbhirāmāḥ ।
sudurlabhāḥ samprati sundarībhir anāhatāntaḥkaraṇā mahāntaḥ ।।

kṛcchreṣu āpatsu । anutsiktaṃ darparahitaṃ sat । tenābhirāmāḥ ।।

taranti mātaṅgaghaṭātaraṅgaṃ raṇāmbudhiṃ ye mayi te na śūrāḥ ।
śūrās ta eveha manastaraṅgaṃ ye svendriyāmbhodhim imaṃ taranti ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

akliṣṭaparyantaphalābhirāmā na dṛśyate kasyacid eva kācit ।
kriyā durāśāhatacittavṛtter yām etya viśrāntim upaiti lokaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kīrtyā jagad dikkuharam pratāpaiḥ śriyā gṛhaṃ sattvabalena lakṣmīm ।
ye pūrayanty akṣatadhairyabandhā na te jagatyāṃ sulabhā mahāntaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

apy antarasthaṃ giriśailabhitter vajrālayābhyantarasaṃsthitaṃ vā ।
sarvaṃ samāyānti samiddhavegāḥ sarvāḥ śriyaḥ santatam āpadaś ca ।।

śilānām iyaṃ śailā । sā cāsau bhittiḥ śailabhittiḥ । gireḥ śailabhittiḥ giriśailabhittis ।।

putrāś ca dārāś ca dhanaṃ ca buddhyā prakalpyate tāta rasāyanaṃ ca ।
sarvaṃ tu tan nāma karoty athānte yatrātiramyā viṣamūrchanaiva ।।

prakalpyate kalpanayā bhāvyate । ante pariṇāme ।।

viṣādayukto viṣamām avasthām upāgataḥ kāyavayo'vasāne ।
bhāvān smaran svān abhidharmariktāñ jano jarāvān abhidahyate antaḥ ।।

kāyavayo'vasāne vṛddhatve । abhitaḥ dharmeṇa riktān abhidharmariktān ।।

kāmārthadharmāptikṛśāntarābhiḥ kriyābhir ādau divasāni nītvā ।
cetaś caladbarhiṇapiñchalolaṃ viśrāntim āgacchatu kena puṃsām ।।

kāmārthadharmāṇāṃ yā āptiḥ । tayā kṛśāntarābhiḥ niḥsārābhiḥ । mokṣārthaṃ na kaścit kriyāṃ karotīti bhāvaḥ ।।

purogatair apy anavāptarūpais taraṅgiṇītuṅgataraṅgakalpaiḥ ।
kriyāphalaiḥ daivavaśād upetair viḍambyate bhinnarucir hi lokaḥ ।।

hi niścaye । viḍambyate vañcyate । kriyāphalānāṃ ca anavāptarūpatvaṃ kṣaṇanaśvaratvena jñeyam ।।

imāny amūnīti vibhāvitāni kāryāṇy aparyantamanoramāṇi ।
janasya jāyājanarañjanena jaṭājarāntaṃ jarayanti cetaḥ ।।

jāyājanarañjaneneti hetau tṛtīyā ।।

parṇāni śīrṇāni yathā tarūṇāṃ sametya janmāśu layam prayānti ।
tathaiva lokāḥ svavivekahīnāḥ sametya gacchanti kuto apy ahobhiḥ ।।

svavivekahīnāḥ ātmavicārarahitāḥ ।।

itas tato dūrataraṃ vihṛtya praviśya gehaṃ divasāvasāne ।
vivekilokāśrayisādhukarma- rikte ahni yāte ka upaiti nidrām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vidrāvite śatrujane samaste samāgatāyām abhitaś ca lakṣmyām ।
sevyanta etāni sukhāni yāvat tāvat samāyāti kuto api mṛtyuḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kuto api saṃvardhitatuccharūpair bhāvair amībhiḥ kṣaṇadṛṣṭanaṣṭaiḥ ।
vilobhyamānā janatā jagatyāṃ na vetty upāyātam aho na yātam ।।

kuto api anirvācyāt kasmāccid vastunaḥ । bhāvaiḥ padārthaiḥ । upāyātam bhāvaviṣayajanma । yātam bhāvaviṣayasaraṇam ।।

yiyāsubhiḥ kālamukhaṃ kriyante janaiḍakais te hatakarmabandhāḥ ।
ye pīnatām eva balād upetya śarīrabandhe nanu te bhavanti ।।

janaiḍakaiḥ janākhyaiḥ meṣaiḥ । te hatakarmabandhāḥ kutsitakarmaprapañcāḥ । kriyante । ye pratisvaṃ sthitāḥ ye balād haṭhena । pīnatām eva na tu kṣīnatām । śarīrabandhe śarīrabandhārthaṃ । nanu bhavanti niścayena bhavantīty arthaḥ । karmavaśād eva hi puruṣaḥ dehabandham prāpnoti ।।

ajasram āgacchati satvareyam anārataṃ gacchati satvaraiva ।
kuto api lolā janatā jagatyāṃ taraṅgamālā kṣaṇabhaṅgureva ।।

janatā janasamūhaḥ ।।

prāṇāpahāraikaparā narāṇām mano manohāritayā haranti ।
raktacchadāḥ ṣaṭpadacañcalākṣyo viṣadrumālolalatāḥ striyaś ca ।।

haranti svavaśīkurvanti mohayanti ca । raktacchadāḥ raktapattrāḥ raktādharāś ca । lolalatāḥ lolaśākhāḥ । lakṣaṇayā lolabhujāś ca ।।

ito anyataś copagatā mudhaiva samānasaṅketanibandhabhāvā ।
yātrāsamāsaṅgasamā narāṇāṃ kalatramitravyavahāramāyā ।।

saṅketaḥ gantavyo deśaḥ । yathā yātrāyām mārge janā anyo'nyaṃ rātrau militvā prabhāte samānaṃ gantavyaṃ deśaṃ gacchanti । tathā saṃsāre api putrādibhiḥ militvā mṛtvā paralokākhyaṃ deśaṃ gacchanti । atas teṣu bhāvabandhanaṃ na yuktam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

pradīpaśāntiṣv iva bhuktabhūri- daśāsv atisnehanibandhanīṣu ।
saṃsāramāyāsu calācalāsu na jñāyate tattvam atāttvikīṣu ।।

atisnehaḥ rāgādhikyaṃ tailādhikyaṃ ca । sa nibandhanaṃ kāraṇaṃ yāsāṃ । tāḥ । tādṛśīṣu calācalāsu aticañcalāsu । atāttvikīṣu asatyāsu ।।

saṃsārasaṃrambhakucakrikeyam prāvṛṭpayobudbudabhaṅgurāpi ।
asāvadhānasya janasya buddhau cirasthirapratyayam ātanoti ।।

atyantam bhramyamāṇā cakrikāpi asāvadhānasya janasya buddhau sthiratāpratyayam ādadhāti । atyantavairāgyāviṣṭatvāt kuśabdaprayogaḥ ।।

śobhojjvalā dainyavaśād vinaṣṭā guṇāḥ sthitāḥ samprati jarjaratve ।
āśvāsanā dūrataram prayātā janasya hemanta ivāmbujasya ।।

jarjaratve nāśaunmukhye । janasyāśvāsanā janakartṛkam āśvāsanam ।।

punaḥ punar daivavaśād upetya svadehabhāreṇa kṛtāpakāraḥ ।
vilūyate yatra taruḥ kuṭhārair āśvāsane tatra hi kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ ।।

yatra daivavaśāt punaḥ punaḥ upetya upāgatya । svadehabhāreṇa śākhopaśākhabhāreṇa । kṛtaḥ apakāro yasya । saḥ taruḥ kuṭhāraiḥ janena lūyate । hi niścaye । tatra tasmin saṃsāre । āśvāsane kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ kā yuktatā bhavati । upetyety asya kṛtety anena sahaikakartṛtvam bṛhadbhayāya eva bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

manoramasyāpy atidoṣavṛtter antar vighātāya samutthitasya ।
viṣadrumasyeva janasya saṅgād āsādyate samprati mūrcchanaiva ।।

atiśayena doṣe vṛttir yasya ।।

kās tā dṛśo yāsu na santi doṣāḥ kās tā diśo yāsu na duḥkhadāhaḥ ।
kās tāḥ prajā yāsu na bhaṅguratvaṃ kās tāḥ kriyā yāsu na nāma māyā ।।

māyā kapaṭaḥ ।।

kalpābhidhānakṣaṇajīvino api kalpaughasaṅkhyākalane viriñcāḥ ।
ataḥ kalāśālini kālajāle laghutvadīrghatvadhiyo apy asatyāḥ ।।

kalpaughānāṃ kalane gaṇane । kriyamāṇe iti śeṣaḥ । kriyamāṇe sati viriñcā api brahmāṇaḥ api । kalpābhidhānakṣaṇajīvinaḥ bhavanti । phalitam āhāta iti । kalāḥ kalpādirūpāḥ । tābhih śālini ।।

sarvatra pāṣāṇamayā mahīdhrā mṛdā mahī dārubhir eva vṛkṣāḥ ।
māṃsair janāḥ pauruṣabaddhabhāvā nāpūrvam astīha vikārahīnam ।।

pauruṣe puruṣakāre । baddhāḥ bhāvāḥ yeṣāṃ । te ।।

ālokyate cetanayānuviddhaḥ payonibaddho aṇucayo nabhaḥsthaḥ ।
pṛthagvibhāgena padārthalakṣmyā etaj jagan netarad asti kiñcit ।।

cetanayā anuviddhaḥ vyāptaḥ । nabhaḥsthaḥ payonibaddhaḥ jalāvaṣṭabdhaḥ । aṇucayaḥ paramāṇusamūhaḥ । padārthalakṣmyāḥ pṛthagvibhāgena padārthalakṣmīsambandhinā pṛthak vibhāgena । ālokyate । uktaviśeṣaṇāḥ paramāṇava eva nānārthabhāvena dṛśyante iti yāvat । etaj jagad asti । kiñcij jagan nāsti । padārthanānābhāvasyaiva jagattvāt । ataś cātra kiṃ ramyatvaṃ kiṃ vāramyatvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

camatkṛtiś ceha manasviloke cetaścamatkārakarī narāṇām ।
svapne api sādho viṣayaṃ kadācit keṣāñcid apy eti na citrarūpā ।।

iha saṃsāre । manasviloke iti nirdhāraṇe । teṣām api manasvinām madhye saṃsāre cittānandakarī keṣām api camatkṛtir nāstīti piṇḍārthaḥ ।।

adyāpayāte tv api kalpanāyā ākāśavallīphalavanmahattve ।
udeti nālobhalavāhatānām udāravṛttāntamayī kathaiva ।।

adyāsmin vairāgyasamaye । kalpanāyāḥ saṃsārakalpanāyāḥ । udāravṛttāntamayī kathā adhyātmaśāstrakathā । alobhalavāhatānāṃ lobharahitānām asmākam ity arthaḥ । etadanubhave tu kā kathety evaśabdābhiprāyaḥ ।।

ādātum icchan padam uttamānāṃ svacetasaivopahato adya lokaḥ ।
pataty aśaṅkam paśur adrikūṭād ānīlavallīdalavāñchayeva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

avāntaranyastanirarthakāṃsa- cchāyālatāpattraphalaprasūnāḥ ।
śarīra eva kṣatasampadaś ca śvabhradrumā adyatanā narāś ca ।।

śvabhradrumāḥ kathambhūtāḥ । avāntare na tu viśrāntisthāne । nyastāni sthāpitāni । nirarthakāni anyeṣām upayogitvābhāvena arthaśūnyāni । aṃsacchāyālatāpattraphalaprasūnāni yaiḥ । adyatanāḥ narāḥ kathambhūtāḥ । śarīre eva svaśarīrārtham eva । na tu paropakārārthaṃ । aṃsaśabdo atra lakṣaṇayā drumaskandavācakaḥ । anyat svayam abhyūham ।।

kvacij janā mārdavasundareṣu kvacit karāleṣu ca sañcaranti ।
daśāntarāleṣu nirantareṣu vanāntaṣaṇḍeṣv iva kṛṣṇaśārāḥ ।।

daśāntarāleṣu daśāmadhyeṣu ।।

dhātur navāni divasam prati bhīṣaṇāni ramyāṇi cāvalulitākhilamānavāni ।
kāryāṇi kaṣṭaphalapākahatodayāni vismāpayanti na śaṭhasya manāṃsi keṣām ।।

dhātuḥ daivasya । divasam prati pratidivasaṃ । avalulitāḥ cāñcalyaṃ nītāḥ । akhilāḥ mānavāḥ yaiḥ । tāni । śaṭhasyeti dhātāram prati kopātiśayaṃ sūcayati ।।

sargāntaślokenaitat samāpayati

janaḥ kāmāsakto vividhakukalāvedanaparaḥ samaḥ svapne apy asmiñ jagati sulabho nādya sujanaḥ ।
kriyā duḥkhāsaṅgād vidhuravidhurā nūnam akhilā na jāne netavyā katham iva daśā jīvitamayī ।।

kāmāsaktaḥ svapnayojanamātraparaḥ । āvedanam prakaṭīkaraṇam । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe ṣaḍviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ jagato nityatām uktvātha tadviparyāsaṃ kathayati

yac cedaṃ dṛśyate kiñcij jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam ।
tat sarvam asthiram brahman svapnasaṅgamasannibham ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

asthiratvam eva vistarataḥ kathayati

śuṣkasāgarasaṅkāśo nikhāto yo adya dṛśyate ।
sa prātar abhrasaṃvīto nagaḥ sampadyate mune ।।

nikhātaḥ gartaḥ ।।

yo vanavyūhavistīrṇo vilīḍhagagano acalaḥ ।
dinair eva sa yāty urvīsamatāṃ kūpatāṃ ca vā ।।

vilīḍhagaganaḥ vyāptākāśaḥ ।।

yad aṅgam adya saṃvītaṃ kauśeyasragvilepanaiḥ ।
digambaraṃ tad eva śvo dūre viśaritāvaṭe ।।

śvo dine । viśaritā viśīrṇo bhavitā ।।

yatrādya nagaraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vicitrācāracañcalam ।
tatraivodeti divasaiḥ saṃśūnyāraṇyadhanvatā ।।

dhanvā maruḥ ।।

yaḥ pumān adya tejasvī maṇḍalāny adhitiṣṭhati ।
sa bhasmakūṭatāṃ rājan divasair adhigacchati ।।

maṇḍalāni deśān । bhasmakūṭatām bhasmacayabhāvam ।।

araṇyānī mahābhīmā yā nabhomaṇḍalopamā ।
patākācchāditākāśā saiva sampadyate purī ।।

spaṣṭam।।

yā latāvalitā bhīmā bhāty adya vipināvalī ।
divasair eva sā yāti mune marumahīpadam ।।

marumahīpadam marumahībhāvam ।।

salilaṃ sthalatāṃ yāti sthalī bhavati vāribhūḥ ।
viparyasyati sarvaṃ hi sakāṣṭhāmbutṛṇaṃ jagat ।।

viparyasyati viparyāsaṃ yāti ।।

anityaṃ yauvanam bālyaṃ śarīraṃ dravyasañcayāḥ ।
bhāvād bhāvāntaraṃ yānti taraṅgavad anāratam ।।

bhāvāt ekasmāt svarūpāt । bhāvāntaram anyat svarūpam ।।

vātāttadīpakaśikhālolaṃ jagati jīvitam ।
taḍitsphuraṇasaṅkāśā padārthaśrīr jagattraye ।।

vātāttā vātagṛhītā ।।

viparyāsam iyaṃ yāti bhūribhūtaparamparā ।
bījarāśir ivājasram prathamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।

prathamānaḥ upyamānaḥ ।।

manaḥpavanaparyastabhūribhūtarajaḥpaṭā ।
pātotpātaparāvartavarābhinayabhūṣitā ।।

ālakṣyate sthitir iyaṃ jāgatī janitabhramā ।
nṛttāveśavivṛtteva saṃsārārabhaṭīnaṭī ।।

manaḥpavanena paryastāḥ īritāḥ । te eva rajaḥpaṭaḥ rajovṛtaḥ paṭaḥ । sā । parāvartaḥ punarāvṛttirūpo bhramaḥ । jāgatī sthitiḥ jagadrūpā sthitiḥ । tatra vivṛttā pravṛttā । saṃsāre saṃsārākhye raṅge । ārabhaṭī raudrarasavṛttiviśeṣaḥ ।।

gandharvanagarākāraviparyāsavidhāyinī ।
apāṅgabhaṅgurodāravyavahāramanoramā ।।

taḍittaralam ālokam ātanvānā punaḥ punaḥ ।
saṃsārarañjanā brahman nṛttamatteva rājate ।।

saṃsārasya rañjanā rāgaḥ । nṛttamatteva rājate । kathambhūtā । gandharvanagarākāraḥ yaḥ viparyāsaḥ । taṃ vidadhātīti tādṛśī । tathāpāṅgavat bhaṅguraḥ । apāṅgeṣu ca bhaṅguraḥ । yaḥ udāravyavahāraḥ । tena manoramā । tathā taḍittaralam aticañcalam । ālokaṃ svaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ svaśarīraprakāśanaṃ ca । punaḥ punaḥ ātanvānā ।।

divasās te mahāntas te saṃpadas tāḥ kriyāś ca tāḥ ।
sarvaṃ smṛtipadaṃ yātaṃ yāmo vayam api kṣaṇāt ।।

te divasā iti sambandhaḥ । tacchabdena pūrvānubhūtānāṃ divasānāṃ smaraṇam ।।

pratyahaṃ kṣayam āyāti pratyahaṃ jāyate punaḥ ।
adyāpi hatarūpāyā nānto asyā dagdhasaṃsṛteḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tiryaktvam puruṣā yānti tiryañco naratām api ।
devāś cādevatāṃ caite kim eveha vibho sthiram ।।

tiryagādīnām puruṣatvādigamanaṃ svabhāvadvāreṇa jñeyam atha vā janmadvāreṇa ।।

racayan raśmijālena rātryahāni punaḥ punaḥ ।
ativāhya raviḥ kāyaṃ vināśāvadhim īkṣate ।।

ativāhya pravartayitvā ।।

brahmā viṣṇuś ca rudraś ca sarvā vā bhūtajātayaḥ ।
nāśam evānudhāvanti salilānīva vāḍavam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dyauḥ kṣamā vāyur ākāśam parvatāḥ sarito diśaḥ ।
vināśavāḍavasyaitat sarvaṃ saṃśuṣkam indhanam ।।

sudāhyatvasūcakaṃ saṃśuṣkam iti ।।

dhanāni bandhavo bhṛtyā mitrāṇi vibhavāś ca ye ।
vināśabhayabhītasya sarvaṃ nīrasatāṃ gatam ।।

mameti śeṣaḥ ।।

svadante tāvad evaite bhāvā jagati dhīmataḥ ।
yāvat smṛtipathaṃ yāti na vināśakurākṣasaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kṣaṇam aiśvaryam āyāti kṣaṇam eti daridratā ।
kṣaṇaṃ vigatarogatvaṃ kṣaṇam āgatarogatā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pratikṣaṇaṃ viparyāsadāyinā mahatāmunā ।
jagadbhrameṇa ke nāma dhīmanto api na mohitāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tamaḥpaṅkasamālabdhaṃ kṣaṇam ākāśamaṇḍalam ।
kṣaṇaṃ kanakaniḥṣyandakomalālokasundaram ।।

kṣaṇaṃ jaladanīlābjamālāvalitakoṭaram ।
kṣaṇam uḍḍāmararavaṃ kṣaṇam mūkam avasthitam ।।

kṣaṇaṃ tārāvilasitaṃ kṣaṇam arkeṇa bhūṣitam ।
kṣaṇam indukṛtāhlādaṃ kṣaṇaṃ sarvabahiṣkṛtam ।।

āgamāpāyaparayā sthityā saṃsthitanāśayā ।
na bibhetīha saṃsāre dhīro api ka ivānayā ।।

sthityā jagatsthityā । adhīrasya tu kā katheti bhāvaḥ ।।

āpadaḥ kṣaṇam āyānti kṣaṇam āyānti sampadaḥ ।
kṣaṇaṃ janmātha maraṇam mune kim iva na kṣaṇam ।।

sarvaṃ kṣaṇe eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

prāg āsīd anya eveha tātas tv anyetaro dinaiḥ ।
apy ekarūpam bhagavan kiñcid asti na susthitam ।।

tātaḥ daśarathaḥ । anyasmāt itaraḥ anyetaraḥ ।।

ghaṭasya paṭatā dṛṣṭā paṭasyāpi ghaṭasthitiḥ ।
na tad asti na yad dṛṣṭaṃ viparyasyati saṃsṛtau ।।

dṛṣṭeti kālāntare mṛttvādidvāreṇa viparyasyati viparyāsaṃ gacchati ।।

aśūreṇa hataḥ śūra ekenāpi śataṃ hatam ।
prākṛtāḥ prabhutāṃ yātāḥ sarvam āvartate jagat ।।

āvartate parivṛttim bhajate ।।

janateyaṃ viparyāsam ajasram anugacchati ।
jaḍaspandaparāmarśāt taraṅgānām ivāvalī ।।

janatā janasamūhaḥ । tena parāmarśāt sparśāt । jalaspande yaḥ parāmarśaḥ ।।

bālyam adya dinair eva yauvanaśrīs tato jarā ।
dehe api naikarūpatvaṃ kāsthā bāhyeṣu vastuṣu ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kṣaṇam ānanditām eti kṣaṇam eti viṣāditām ।
kṣaṇam saumyatvam āyāti sarvasmin naṭavan manaḥ ।।

sarvasmin sarveṣu prāṇiṣu ।।

itaś cānyad itaś cānyad itaś cānyad ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।
racayan vastu nāyāti khedaṃ līlāsv ivārbhakaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

cinoty unmādayaty atti nihanty āhanti cātmasāt ।
jagajjātam idaṃ dhātā pātotpātaśatair iha ।।

cinoti vardhayati । unmādayati unmādayuktaṃ karoti । atti bhakṣayati । ātmasāt svādhīnaṃ karoti । āhanti samantān nāśayati ।।

kṣaṇenānyad dinenānyat prātar anyad itas tataḥ ।
racayan vañcanādakṣo vidhir dṛṣṭo na kenacit ।।

na dṛṣṭaḥ indriyāviṣayatvāt ।।

yad adya tat tu na prātar yat prātas tat tu nādya ca ।
yad anyadā tu tan nādya sarvam āvartatetarām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

santatānīha duḥkhāni sukhāni viralāni ca ।
satataṃ rātryahānīva vivartante naram prati ।।

santatāni avicchinnāni । naram prati pratipuruṣam ।।

āvirbhāvatirobhāvabhāgino bhavabhāvinaḥ ।
janasya sthiratāṃ yānti nāpado na ca sampadaḥ ।।

āvirbhāvatirobhāvau bhajatīti tādṛśasya । bhāvaḥ prādurbhāvaḥ asyāstīti tādṛśasya ।।

padāt padam ayam pāpaḥ sarvam āpadi pātayan ।
helāvivalitāśeṣaḥ khalaḥ kālalavaḥ sthitaḥ ।।

gacchann iti śeṣaḥ । helayā na tu yatnena । vivalitaṃ rūpāntaraṃ nītam ।।

sargāntaślokenaitat samāpayati

samaviṣamadaśāvipākabhinnās tribhuvanabhūtaparamparāphalaughāḥ ।
samayapavanapātitāḥ patanti pratidinam ātatasaṃsṛtidrumebhyaḥ ।।

samaviṣamadaśānāṃ yaḥ vipākaḥ pariṇāmaḥ । tadyuktā iti yāvad ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe saptaviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ jagadviparyāsam uktvā tatkṛtāṃ viraktatām pratipādayati

iti medhopadāvāgnidagdhe mahati cetasi ।
prasphuranti na bhogāśā mṛgatṛṣṇāḥ sarassv iva ।।

iti medhā eva upadāvāgni davāgnisamīpaṃ ।।

pratyahaṃ cātikaṭutām eti saṃsārasaṃsthitiḥ ।
kālapākavaśollāsirasā nimbalatā yathā ।।

kālena yaḥ pākaḥ । tasya vaśena ullāsī rasaḥ । yasyāḥ ।।

vṛddhim āyāti daurjanyaṃ saujanyaṃ yāti tānavam ।
karañjakarkaśe rājan pratyahaṃ janacetasi ।।

rājann iti daśaratham prati kathanaṃ । karañjavat kaṇṭakavat । karkaśe । ato janasaṅgān mama viratiḥ jāteti bhāvaḥ । evam uttaratrāpi bhāvayojanā kāryā ।।

bhajyate bhuvi maryādā jhagity eva diśam prati ।
śuṣkeva māṣaśimikā ṭāṅkārakaṭhināravam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rājyebhyo bhogapūgebhyaś cintāvanto mahīśvarāḥ ।
nirastacintākalikā varam ekāntaśīlatā ।।

rājyebhyaḥ rājyārthaṃ । phalitam āha nirasteti । ata ity adhyāhāryam ।।

nānandāya mamodyānaṃ na sukhāya mama śriyaḥ ।
na harṣāya mamārthāśā śāmyāmi manasā saha ।।

śāmyāmi nakiñcidbhāvanārūpāṃ śāntiṃ gacchāmi ।।

anityaś cāsukho lokas tṛṣṇā tāta durutsahā ।
cāpalopahataṃ cetaḥ kathaṃ yāsyāmi nirvṛtim ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nābhinandāmi maraṇaṃ nābhinandāmi jīvitam ।
yathā tiṣṭhāmi tiṣṭhāmi tathaiva vigatajvaram ।।
