anena ca jīvanmuktapadaprāptiḥ sūcitā । yathāsthitatvaṃ hi jīvanmuktiṃ vinā na sambhavati ।।

kim me rājyena kim bhogaiḥ kim arthena kim īhitaiḥ ।
ahaṅkāravaśād etat sa eva galito mama ।।

ahaṅkārābhāve hi nakiñcidrūpaḥ puruṣaḥ kiṃ rājyādibhiḥ karoti ।।

janmāvalivaratrāyām indriyagranthayo dṛḍhāḥ ।
ye lagnās tadvimokṣārthaṃ ye yatante ta uttamāḥ ।।

tadvimokṣārtham indriyagranthīnāṃ vimokṣārtham ।।

dalitam māninīlokair mano makaraketunā ।
komalaṃ khuraniṣpeṣaiḥ kamalaṃ kariṇā yathā ।।

māninīlokair iti karaṇe tṛtīyā । makaraketuneti kartari ।।

adya cet svasthayā buddhyā munīndra na cikitsyate ।
bhūyaś cittacikitsāyāṃ kaḥ kilāvasaraḥ kutaḥ ।।

adya sakalasāmagryānvite samaye । svasthayā sāmagrīcintāhīnayā ।।

nanu viṣayasevanaṃ tyaktvā kimarthaṃ cikitsāparo bhavatīty । atrāha

viṣaṃ viṣayavaiṣamyaṃ na viṣaṃ viṣam ucyate ।
janmāntaraghnā viṣayā ekadehaharaṃ viṣam ।।

viṣayakṛtaṃ vaiṣamyam viṣayavaiṣamyam । janmāntare ghnanti janmāntaraghnāḥ vāsanārūpeṇa sthitatvāt ।।

te eva tvāṃ kathaṃ tyajantīty । atrāha

na sukhāni na duḥkhāni na mitrāṇi na bandhavaḥ ।
na jīvitaṃ na maraṇam bandhāya jñasya cetasaḥ ।।

bandhāya rāgadveṣarūpabandhārtham । jñasya vivekayuktasya ।।

nanu tava jñatvam kuto astīty apekṣāyāṃ jñatvakaraṇam eva prārthayate

tad bhavāmi yathā brahman pūrvāparavidāṃ vara ।
vītaśokabhayāyāso jñas tathopadiśāśu me ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vāsanājālavalitā duḥkhakaṇṭakasaṅkaṭā ।
nipātotpātabahalā bhīmarūpājñatāṭavī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

krakacograviniṣpeṣaṃ soḍhuṃ śakto asmy aham mune ।
saṃsāravyavahārotthaṃ nāśāviṣamavaiśasam ।।

āśayā kṛtaṃ viṣamaṃ kaṭhinaṃ ।।

idaṃ nāstīdam astīti vyavahārijanabhramaḥ ।
dhunotīdaṃ calaṃ ceto rajorāśim ivānilaḥ ।।

dhunoti kampayati ।।

tṛṣṇātantulavaprotajīvasañcayamauktikam ।
cidacchāṅgatayā nityam prakaṭaṃ cittanāyakam ।।

saṃsārahāram aratiḥ kālavyālavibhūṣaṇam ।
troṭayāmy aham akrūrāṃ vāgurām iva kesarī ।।

cid eva accham aṅgaṃ svarūpaṃ । tasya bhāvaḥ tattā । cinmayatvenety arthaḥ । prakaṭaṃ vedyatāṃ gataṃ । anyathā hy acinmayatvād vedyaṃ kathaṃ syāt । cidaviruddhasya cidviṣayībhūtasyaiva vedyatvayogāt । hāro api prakaṭo viśado bhavati । cittam eva nāyakaḥ utpādakaḥ madhyamaṇiś ca yasya । akrūrāṃ komalām ।।

nīhāraṃ hṛdayāṭavyām manastimiram āśu me ।
kenacij jñānadīpena bhinddhi tattvavidāṃ vara ।।

hṛdayaṃ hṛtkamalam eva aṭavī araṇyaṃ । kenacit mayā vaktum aśakyenety arthaḥ ।।

vidyanta eveha na te mahātman durādhayo na kṣayam āpnuvanti ।
ye saṅgamenottamamānasānāṃ niśātamāṃsīva niśākareṇa ।।

he mahātman । te durādhayo na vidyante ye uttamānāṃ saṅgamena kṣayaṃ nāpnuvanti uttamamānasasaṅgamena durādhayo naśyantīti bhavaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokenaitat samāpayati

āyur vāyuvighaṭṭitābjapaṭalīlambāmbuvad bhaṅguram bhogā meghavitānamadhyavilasatsaudāminīcañcalāḥ ।
lolo yauvanalālanājalarayaś cety ākalayya drutam mudraivādridṛḍhārpitā nanu mayā citte ciraṃ śāntaye ।।

vitānaṃ samūhaḥ । viṣayāvedanam iti yāvat । adrivat parvatavat ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe aṣṭāviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ viraktatām pratipādya vairāgyakṛtāvasthākathanam prastauti

evam abhyutthitānarthasārthasaṅkaṭakoṭaram ।
jagad ālokya nirmagnam manomananakardame ।।

mano me bhramatīvedaṃ sambhramaś copajāyate ।
gātrāṇi parikampante pattrāṇīva jarattaroḥ ।।

abhyutthitaḥ abhyudayaṃ gataḥ । yaḥ anarthasārtha anarthasamūhaḥ । tena saṅkaṭaṃ sambādhaṃ । koṭaram madhyaṃ yasya । tat । manasaḥ yat mananam saṅkalpāparaparyāyo mananākhyo dharmaḥ । sa eva kardamaḥ ।।

anāptottamasantoṣacaryotsaṅgākulā matiḥ ।
śūnyāspadā bibhetīha bālevālpabaleśvarā ।।

anāptaḥ । uttamasantoṣasya caryāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ । utsaṅgaḥ aṅkaḥ । ata evākulā ca । bālāpi anāptapriyasakhyutsaṅgā ākulā bhavati । alpabalaḥ īśvaraḥ patir । alpabaleśvarā śūnyāspadā ca bālā hi sphuṭam eva bibheti ।।

vikalpebhyo luṭhanty etāś cāntaḥkaraṇavṛttayaḥ ।
śvabhrebhya iva sāraṅgyas tucchālambaviḍambitāḥ ।।

vikalpebhyaḥ luṭhanti anyasmād vikalpād anyaṃ vikalpaṃ yāntīty arthaḥ । atha vā mohaṃ gacchantīti । antaḥkaraṇavṛttayaḥ kathambhūtāḥ । tucchāḥ āpātamātramadhuratvena niḥsārāḥ । ye ālaṃbāḥ viṣayās । tair viḍambitāḥ vañcitāḥ । svonmukhāḥ kṛtā iti yāvat ।।

avivekāspadabhraṣṭāḥ kaṣṭe rūḍhā na satpade ।
andhakūpam ivāpannā varākāś cakṣurādayaḥ ।।

kaṣṭe viṣayākhye kaṭhine pade ity arthaḥ ।।

nāvasthitim upāyāti na ca yāti yathepsitam ।
cintā jīveśvarāyattā kāntevāpriyasadmani ।।

avasthitiṃ sthairyam । yathepsitaṃ svepsitam artham । jīva eva īśvaraḥ patiḥ ।।

jarjarīkṛtya vastūni tyajantī bibhratī tathā ।
mārgaśīrṣāntavallīva dhṛtir vidhuratāṃ gatā ।।

jarjarīkṛtya nirvidya । dhṛtiḥ lakṣaṇayā dhairyayuktā buddhiḥ ।।

apahastitasarvārtham anavasthitir āsthitā ।
gṛhītvotsṛjya cātmānam avasthitir avasthitā ।।

apahastitāḥ hastād atītāḥ । sarve arthāḥ yatra । tat । niṣprayojanam ity arthaḥ । anavasthitiḥ aratiḥ । āsthitā dṛḍhībhūtā । avasthitiḥ ratiḥ । ātmānaṃ gṛhītvā utsṛjya cāvasthitā śithilāsthitety arthaḥ ।।

calitācalitenāntar avaṣṭambhena me matiḥ ।
daridrācchinavṛkṣasya mūleneva viḍambyate ।।

daridrair ācchinno mūladeśaṃ tāvac chinnaś cāsau vṛkṣas । calitācalitena kṣaṇam acalitena । avaṣṭambhena dhairyeṇa । upalakṣitā me matiḥ karmabhūtā । viḍambyate anukriyate । mama matiḥ chinnavṛkṣamūlavad aṅkurajananāsamarthāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

cetaś cañcalam ābhogi bhuvanāntarvihāri ca ।
sambhramaṃ na jahātīdaṃ svavimānam ivāmaraḥ ।।

ābhogi vikalpākhyābhogayuktam ।।

ato atuccham anāyāsam anupādhi gatabhramam ।
kiṃ tat sthitipadaṃ sādhu yatra śaṅkā na vidyate ।।

sthiteḥ yogyam padaṃ sthitipadaṃ ।।

sarvārambhasamārambhāḥ sujanā janakādayaḥ ।
vyavahāraparā eva katham uttamatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

sarvārambheṣu samārambhaḥ yeṣāṃ । sarvakāriṇa iti yāvat ।।

lagnenāpi kilāṅgeṣu bahunā bahumānada ।
kathaṃ saṃsārapaṅkena pumān iha na lipyate ।।

na lipyate svāveśenotpāditaiḥ sukhaduḥkhaiḥ pāpapuṇyaiḥ vā na gṛhyate ।।

kāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ samupāśritya bhavanto vītakalmaṣāḥ ।
mahānto vicarantīha jīvanmuktā mahāśayāḥ ।।

tāṃ mamāpi kathayeti bhāvaḥ ।।

lobhayanto bhayāyaiva viṣayābhogabhoginaḥ ।
bhaṅgurākāravibhavāḥ katham āyānti bhavyatām ।।

bhayāyaiva na tu sukhāya । bhogayuktāḥ bhoginaḥ bhogabhoginaḥ । puṣṭaśarīrayuktasarpasvarūpā ity arthaḥ । bhaṅgurākāraḥ naśvarasvabhāvaḥ । vibhavaḥ utpattisthānaṃ yeṣāṃ । bhavyatām rāgānutpādakatvena ramaṇīyatām ।।

mohamātaṅgamṛditā kalaṅkakalitāntarā ।
param prasādam āyāti śemuṣīsarasī katham ।।

kalaṅko atra bhogānusandhānarūpo jñeyaḥ ।।

saṃsāra eva nivasañ jano vyavaharann api ।
na bandhaṃ katham āyāti padmapattre payo yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ātmavat tṛṇavad vedaṃ sakalaṃ janayañ jagat ।
katham uttamatām eti manomanmatham aspṛśan ।।

janayan utpādayan । lakṣaṇayā jānan ity arthaḥ । mano hi jñānadvāreṇaiva sarvaṃ janayati । ubhayathāpi mokṣa eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

kam mahāpuruṣam pāram upayātam bhavodadheḥ ।
ācāreṇānusṛtyāyaṃ jano yāti na duṣkṛtam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kiṃ tad yad ucitaṃ śreyaḥ kiṃ tat syād ucitam phalam ।
vartitavyaṃ ca saṃsāre kathaṃ nāmāsamañjase ।।

asamañjase viṣame ।।

tat tvaṃ kathaya me kiñcid yenāsya jagataḥ prabho ।
vedmi pūrvāparāṃ dhātuś ceṣṭitasyāsamasthitim ।।

yena kathitena । pūrvāparām antadvayayuktāṃ । samagrām iti yāvat । asamasthitiṃ viṣamāṃ sthitiṃ । jagataḥ kathambhūtasya । dhātuś ceṣṭitasya brahmaceṣṭitarūpasya ।।

hṛdayākāśaśaśinaś cetaso malamārjanam ।
yathā me jāyatām brahmaṃs tathā nirvighnam ācara ।।

malamārjanam saṃśayākhyamalamārjanam ।।

kim iha syād upādeyaṃ kiṃ vā heyam athetarat ।
kathaṃ viśrāntim āyātu cetaś capalam adrivat ।।

atha itarad upekṣyaṃ kim asti ।।

kena pāvanamantreṇa duḥsaṃsṛtiviṣūcikā ।
śāmyatīyam anāyāsam āyāsaśatakāriṇī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kathaṃ śītalatām antar ānandatarumañjarīm ।
pūrṇacandra ivākṣīṇāṃ rākām āsādayāmy aham ।।

rākām pūrṇimām ।।

prāpyāntaḥpūrṇatām antar na śocāmi yathā punaḥ ।
santo bhavantas tattvajñās tathaivopadiśantu mām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokenaitat samāpayati

anuttamānandapadapradhāna- viśrāntiriktaṃ hi mano mahātman ।
kadarthayantīha bhṛśaṃ vikalpāḥ śvāno vane deham ivālpajīvam ।।

kadarthayanti mathnanti ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe ekonatriṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

evaṃ vairāgyakṛtām avasthām uktvopāyam praṣṭum prastāvaṃ karoti

proccavṛkṣacalatpattralambāmbulavabhaṅgure ।
āyuṣīśānaśītāṃśukalāmṛduni dehake ।।

kedāraviraṭadbhekakaṇṭhatvakkoṇabhaṅgure ।
vāgurāvalaye jantoḥ suhṛtsvajanasaṅgame ।।

vāsanāvātavalitakadāśātaḍiti sphuṭe ।
mohaughamihikāmeghe ghanaṃ sphūrjati garjati ।।

nṛtyaty uttāṇḍavaṃ caṇḍe lole lobhakalāpini ।
suvikāsini sasphoṭam anarthakuṭajadrume ।।

krūre kṛtāntamārjāre sarvabhūtākhuhāriṇi ।
aśrutaspandasañcāre kuto apy uparipātini ।।

ka upāyo gatiḥ kā vā kā cintā kaḥ samāśrayaḥ ।
keneyam aśubhodarkā na bhavej jīvitāṭavī ।।

īśānaśītāṃśukalā śrīmahādevaśiraḥsthā candrakalā । raṭataḥ bhekasya kaṇṭhatvak atyantabhaṅgurā bhavati । iti tasyā upamānatvena grahaṇam । mihikāmeghe nīhārayukte meghe । kathambhūte । vāsanāvātena valitā yā kadāśā । sā eva taḍit yasya । uttāṇḍavam udbhaṭaṃ । sasphoṭaṃ sphoṭanayuktaṃ । saśabdam ity arthaḥ । kṛtāntamārjāre kathambhūte । aśrutaspandaḥ sañcāro yasya । aśubhodarkā aśubhottaraphalā । jīvitam evāṭavī vanam ।।

na tad asti pṛthivyāṃ vā divi deveṣu vā kvacit ।
sudhiyas tuccham apy etad yan na yāti naramyatām ।।

naramyatām iti nasamāso ayam । aramyatām ity arthaḥ । sarvatra sarvaṃ sudhiyaḥ aramyatām eva yātīti bhāvaḥ । apiśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ ।।

ayaṃ hi dagdhasaṃsāro nīrandhrakalanākulaḥ ।
kathaṃ susvādutām eti nīraso mūrkhatāṃ vinā ।।

mūrkhatābhāve tu susvādutāṃ naitīti bhāvaḥ ।।

āśāprativiṣā kena kṣīrasnānena ramyatām ।
upaiti puṣpaśubhreṇa madhuneva suvallarī ।।

āśā eva prativiṣā tiktadravyaviśeṣaḥ ।।

apamṛṣṭamalodeti kṣālanenāmṛtadyutiḥ ।
manaścandramasaḥ kena tena kāmakalaṅkinaḥ ।।

apamṛṣṭaṃ naṣṭaṃ । tena keneti praśnaḥ । manaścandramasaḥ kathambhūtasya । kāma eva kalaṅkaḥ asyāstīti tādṛśasya ।।

dṛṣṭasaṃsāragatinā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭavināśinā ।
kena vā vyavahartavyaṃ saṃsāravanavīthiṣu ।।

dṛṣṭā saṃsāragatiḥ yena । tathā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭayoḥ vināśaḥ asyāstīti tādṛśena । padārthadharmādharmādyatītena jīvanmukteneti yāvat । kena kena prakāreṇa । saṃsāravanavīthiṣu vyavahartavyaṃ vyavahāraḥ kartavyaḥ ।।

rāgadveṣamahārogā bhogapūrvātipūtayaḥ ।
kathaṃ jantor na bādhante saṃsārāraṇyacāriṇaḥ ।।

rāgadveṣā eva mahārogāḥ । te saṃsārāraṇyacāriṇo jantoḥ kathaṃ na bādhante । kathambhūtāḥ । bhogāḥ pūrvaṃ kāraṇaṃ yeṣāṃ । te । tādṛśāś ca te atipūtayaś cātiśayena pūtigandhāś ca । rāgādigataḥ pūtiḥ । arthād dharṣāmarṣau jñeyau । rogapakṣe tu prasiddhārtha eva ।।

kathaṃ ca vīravairāgnau patatāpi na dahyate ।
pāvake pārateneva rasena rasaśālinā ।।

kṣatriyajātitvād iyam uktiḥ । pāratena rasena pāratākhyena rasena ।।

tarhi vyavahāram eva mā kurv ity । atrāha

yasmāt kila jagaty asmin vyavahārakriyāṃ vinā ।
na sthitiḥ sambhavaty abdhau patitasyājalā yathā ।।

sthitiḥ avasthānam ।।

rāgadveṣavinirmuktā sukhaduḥkhavivarjitā ।
kṛśānor dāhahīneva śikhā nāstīha satkriyā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

manomananamāninyāḥ satāpābhuvanatraye ।
kṣayayuktiṃ vinā nāsti brūta tām alam uttamāḥ ।।

satāpam ā samantād । manomananamāninyāḥ kṣayayuktiṃ vinā nāsti । tāpanivārakam iti śeṣaḥ । yūyaṃ tāṃ kṣayayuktiṃ । brūta kathayatety arthaḥ । ābhuvanatrayam ity atra āṅśabdo abhivyāpakatve samasyate ।।

vyavahāravato yuktyā duḥkhaṃ nāyāti me yayā ।
atha vāvyavahārasya brūta tāṃ gatim uttamāḥ ।।

avyavahārasya vyavahārarahitasya ।।

tat kathaṃ kena vā kiṃ vā kṛtam uttamacetasā ।
pūrvaṃ yenaiti viśrāmam paramam pāvanam manaḥ ।।

kenottamacetasā pūrvaṃ tat kiṃ kṛtaṃ kathaṃ vā kṛtaṃ । tat kim mameti śeṣaḥ । yena mama manaḥ pāvanaṃ sat paramaṃ viśrāmam eti ।।

yathā jānāsi bhagavaṃs tathā mohanivṛttaye ।
brūhi me sādhavo yena yūyaṃ nirduḥkhatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

nanu katham ahaṃ vaktuṃ śaknomīty atrāha sādhava iti ।।

atha vā tādṛśī brahman yuktir yadi na vidyate ।
na yuktim mama vā kaścid vidyamānām api sphuṭam ।।

svayaṃ caiva na cāpnomi tāṃ viśrāntim anuttamām ।
tad ahaṃ tyaktasarveho nirahaṅkāratāṃ gataḥ ।।

na bhokṣye na pibāmy ambu nāham paridadhe ambaram ।
karomi nāhaṃ vyāpāraṃ snānadānāśanādikam ।।

he brahmann । atha vā yadi tādṛśī yuktir na vidyate । vidyamānām api yuktiṃ kaścin mama na । svayaṃ ca tāṃ viśrāntiṃ yathātathālabdhayā yuktyā kṛtaṃ viśrāmam । tadāhaṃ nirahaṅkāratāṃ gato ata eva tyaktasarvehaḥ san ।।

na ca tiṣṭhāmi kāryeṣu sampatsv āpaddaśāsu ca ।
na kiñcid api vāñchāmi dehatyāgād ṛte mune ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kevalaṃ vigatāśaṅko nirmamo gatamatsaraḥ ।
maunam eveha tiṣṭhāmi lipikarmasv ivārpitaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha krameṇa santyajya saśvāsocchvāsasaṃvidam ।
sanniveśaṃ tyajāmīmam anarthaṃ dehanāmakam ।।

śvāsaś cocchvāsaś ca । tābhyāṃ saha vartate iti saśvāsocchvāsā । tāṃ । sanniveśaṃ saṃsthānam ।।

nanu samatāviṣayatvena svasambandhitayā sthitasya dehasya tyāgaḥ kathaṃ sidhyatīty । atrāha

nāham asya na me dehaḥ śāmyāmy asnehadīpavat ।
sarvam eva parityajya tyajāmīdaṃ kalevaram ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena śrīrāmavākyam upasaṃharati

ity uktavān amalaśītakarābhirāmo rāmo mahattaravivekavikāsicetāḥ ।
tūṣṇīm babhūva purato mahatāṃ ghanānāṃ kekāravaśramavaśād iva nīlakaṇṭhaḥ ।।

nīlakaṇṭhaḥ mayūraḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe triṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

śrīvālmīkiḥ śrībharadvājam prati kathayati

vadaty evam manomohavinivṛttikaraṃ vacaḥ ।
rāme rājīvapattrākṣe tasmin rājakumārake ।।

sarve babhūvus tatrasthā vismayotphullalocanāḥ ।
dhṛtāmbarā deharuhair giraḥ śrotum ivodgataiḥ ।।

virāmavāsanāpāstasamastabhavavāsanāḥ ।
muhūrtam amṛtāmbhodhivīcīvilulitā iva ।।

deharuhaiḥ romabhiḥ । dhṛtāmbarāḥ dhṛtavastrāḥ । romakañcukānvitāḥ ity arthaḥ । deharuhaiḥ kathambhūtair iva । giraḥ śrīrāmagiraḥ śrotum udgataiḥ utthitair iva । virāmavāsanayā nivṛttivāsanayā । apāstāḥ tyaktāḥ । samastāḥ bhavavāsanāḥ yaiḥ । te vilulitāḥ cañcalīkṛtāḥ ।।

tā giro rāmabhadrasya tasya citrārpitair iva ।
saṃśrutāḥ śṛṇukair antar ānandaparipīvaraiḥ ।।

śṛṇukaiḥ śrotṛbhiḥ ।।

śṛṇukān eva viśeṣeṇa kathayati

vasiṣṭhaviśvāmitrādyair munibhiḥ saṃsadi sthitaiḥ ।
jayantaghṛṣṭipramukhair mantribhir mantrakovidaiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nṛpair daśarathaprakhyaiḥ pauraiḥ pāraśavādibhiḥ ।
sāmantai rājaputraiś ca brāhmaṇair brahmavādibhiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tathā bhṛtyair amātyaiś ca pañjarasthaiś ca pakṣibhiḥ ।
krīḍāmṛgair gataspandais turaṅgair gatacarvaṇaiḥ ।।

gatacarvaṇaiḥ tyaktabhojanaiḥ ।।

kausalyāpramukhaiś caiva nijavātāyanasthitaiḥ ।
saṃśāntabhūṣaṇārāvair aspandair vanitāgaṇaiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

udyānavallīnilayair viṭaṅkanilayair api ।
akṣubdhapakṣatatibhir vihagair viratāravaiḥ ।।

siddhair nabhaścaraiś caiva tathā gandharvakinnaraiḥ ।
nāradavyāsapulahapramukhair munipuṅgavaiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

anyaiś ca devadeveśavidyādharamahoragaiḥ ।
rāmasya tā vicitrārthā mahodārā giraḥ śrutāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha tūṣṇīṃ sthitavati rāme rājīvalocane ।
tasmin raghukulākāśaśaśāṅkasamasundare ।।

sādhuvādagirā sārdhaṃ siddhasārthasamīritā ।
vitānakasamā vyomnaḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ha ।।

spaṣṭaṃ ।।

puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ viśinaṣṭi

mandārakośaviśrāntabhramaradvandvanādinī ।
madirāmodasaundaryamuditonmadamānavā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vyomavātavinunneva tārakāṇām paramparā ।
patiteva dharāpīṭhaṃ svargastrīhasitacchaṭā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vṛṣṭiṣv ekaśaranmeghalavāvalir iva cyutā ।
haiyaṅgavīnapiṇḍānām īriteva paramparā ।।

vṛṣṭiṣu vṛṣṭyantaḥ ।।

himavṛṣṭir ivodārā muktāhāracayopamā ।
aindavīraśmimāleva kṣīrormīṇām ivātatiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam।।

kiñjalkāmodavalitā bhramadbhṛṅgakadambakā ।
sītkāragāyadāmodamadhurāniladolitā ।।

sītkāreti śabdānukaraṇam ।।

prabhramatketakavyūhā prasaratkairavotkarā ।
prapatatkundavalayā valatkuvalayālayā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

āpūritāṅganārāmagṛhacchādanacatvarā ।
udgrīvapuravāstavyavaranārīvilokitā ।।

aṅganāni cārāmāś ca gṛhacchādanāni ca catvarāṇi ca । tāni āpūritāni aṅganādīni yayā । sā । darśanotsuko hi udgrīvo bhavati ।।

nirabhrotpalasaṅkāśavyomavṛṣṭir anākulā ।
adṛṣṭapūrvā sarvasya janasya janitasmayā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

adṛṣṭapūrvasiddhaughakarotkarasamīritā ।
sā muhūrtacaturbhāge puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ha ।।

ha iti nipātaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ ।।

āpūritasabhāloke śānte kusumavarṣaṇe ।
imān siddhagaṇālāpāñ śuśruvus te sabhāgatāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

siddhagira eva kathayati

ākalpaṃ siddhasenāsu bhramadbhir abhito divam ।
apūrvam adya tv asmābhiḥ śrutaṃ śrutirasāyanam ।।

śrutau karṇe ।।

yad anena kilodāram uktaṃ raghukulendunā ।
vītarāgatayā tad dhi vākpater apy agocaram ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

aho vata mahat puṇyam adyāsmābhir idaṃ śrutam ।
vaco rāmamukhodbhūtam amṛtāhlādakaṃ dhiyaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokaṃ kathayati

upaśamāmṛtasundaram ādarād adhigatottamatāpadam eṣa yat ।
kathitavān ucitaṃ raghunandanaḥ sapadi tena vayam pratibodhitāḥ ।।

pratibodhitāḥ jñānayuktāḥ sampāditāḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe ekatriṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

siddhā eva parasparaṃ kathayanti pāvanasyāsya vacasaḥ proktasya raghuketunā ।
nirṇayaṃ śrotum ucitaṃ vakṣyamāṇam maharṣibhiḥ ।।

nāradavyāsapulahapramukhā munipuṅgavāḥ ।
āgacchatāśv avighnena sarva eva maharṣayaḥ ।।

patāmaḥ paritaḥ puṇyām etāṃ dāśarathīṃ sabhām ।
nīrandhrakanakāmbhojām padminīm iva ṣaṭpadāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śrīvālmīkiḥ śrībharadvājam prati kathayati

ity uktvā sā samastaiva vyomāvāsanivāsinī ।
tām papāta sabhāṃ tatra divyā muniparamparā ।।

vyomni yaḥ āvāsaḥ । tatra nivasatīti tādṛśī ।।

muniparamparāṃ viśinaṣṭi

agrasthitamarutpṛṣṭharaṇadvīṇamunīśvarā ।
payaḥpīnaghanaśyāmavyāsamecakitāmbarā ।।

agre sthitāḥ marutaḥ yasyāṃ । tādṛśī cāsau pṛṣṭhe ca raṇadvīṇāḥ munīśvarāḥ yasyāṃ । tādṛśī ।।

bhṛgvaṅgiraḥpulastyādimunināyakamaṇḍitā ।
cyavanoddālakośīraśaralomādipālitā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

parasparaparāmarśād duḥsaṃsthānamṛgājinā ।
lolākṣamālāvalayā sukamaṇḍaludhāriṇī ।।

parāmarśāt saṅghaṭṭāt ।।

tārāvalir ivānyonyakṛtaśobhātiśāyinī ।
kausumī vṛṣṭir anyeva dvitīyevārkamaṇḍalī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tārājāla ivāmbhodo vyāso hy atra vyarājata ।
tāraugha iva śītāṃśur nārado atra vyarājata ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

deveṣv iva svarādhīśaḥ pulastyo atra vyarājata ।
āditya iva devānām aṅgirāś ca vyarājata ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

athāsyāṃ siddhasenāyām patantyāṃ nabhaso rasāt ।
uttasthau munisampūrṇā tadā dāśarathī sabhā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

miśrībhūtā virejus te nabhaścaramahīcarāḥ ।
parasparavṛtāṅgābhā bhāsayanto diśo daśa ।।

parasparaṃ vṛtā aṅgānām ābhā yaiḥ ।।

nabhaścaramahīcarān viśinaṣṭi

veṇughaṇṭāvṛtakarā līlākamaladhāriṇaḥ ।
dūrvāṅkurākrāntaśikhāḥ sacuḍāmaṇimūrdhajāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jaṭākaṭaprakapilā maulimālitamastakāḥ ।
prakoṣṭhagākṣavalayā māṇikyavalayānvitāḥ ।।

jaṭākaṭapreṇa jaṭāsamūhena ।।

cīravalkalasaṃvītāḥ srakkauśeyāvaluṇṭhitāḥ ।
vilolamekhalāpāśāś calanmuktākalāpinaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vasiṣṭhaviśvāmitrau tān pūjayām āsatuḥ kṣaṇāt ।
arghyaiḥ pādyair vacobhiś ca nabhaścaramahāgaṇān ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sarvācāreṇa siddhaugham pūjayām āsa bhūpatiḥ ।
siddhaugho bhūpatiṃ caiva kuśalapraśnavārtayā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tais taiḥ praṇayasaṃrambhair anyo'nyam prāptasatkriyāḥ ।
upāviśan viṣṭareṣu nabhaścaramahīcarāḥ ।।

praṇayasaṃrambhaiḥ snehasaṃrambhaiḥ ।।

vacobhiḥ puṣpavarṣeṇa sādhuvādena cābhitaḥ ।
rāmaṃ tam pūjayām āsuḥ puraḥ praṇatam āsthitam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

āsāṃ cakre ca tatrāsau rājalakṣmyā virājitaḥ ।
viśvāmitro vasiṣṭhaś ca vāmadevaś ca mantriṇaḥ ।।

asau śrīrāmaḥ ।।

nārado devaputraś ca vyāsaś ca munipuṅgavaḥ ।
marīcir atha durvāsā munir āṅgirasas tathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kratuḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ śaralomā munīśvaraḥ ।
vātsyāyano bharadvājo vālmīkir munipuṅgavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

uddālaka ṛcīkaś ca śaryātiś cyavanas tathā ।
ūṣmapāś ca ghṛtārciś ca śāluḍir vāluḍis tathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ete cānye ca bahavo vedavedāṅgapāragāḥ ।
jñātajñeyā mahātmānaḥ saṃsthitās tatra nāyakāḥ ।।

nāyakāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ ।।

vasiṣṭhaviśvāmitrābhyāṃ saha te nāradādayaḥ ।
idam ūcur anūcānā rāmam ānamitānanam ।।

anūcānāḥ sāṅgavedajñāḥ ।।

aho vata kumāreṇa kalyāṇaguṇaśālinī ।
vāg uktā paramodāravirāgarasagarbhiṇī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pariniṣṭhitavākyārthasubodham ucitaṃ sphuṭam ।
udāram priyacaryārham avihvalam aviplutam ।।

abhivyaktapadaṃ caiva niṣṭhaṃ spaṣṭaṃ ca tuṣṭimat ।
karoti rāghavaproktaṃ vacaḥ kasya na vismayam ।।

pariniṣṭhitaḥ ākāṅkṣārahitaḥ । tat pariniṣṭhitavākyārthaṃ । tādṛśam ca tat subodhaṃ ca tat । sphuṭam prakaṭārtham । priyacaryām priyavyavahāram arhatīti tādṛśam । avihvalaṃ vyākulatārahitam । aviplutaṃ kenāpi bādhitum aśakyam । tuṣṭimat śrotuḥ tuṣṭikāritvena tuṣṭimat ।।

śatād ekatamasyaiva sarvodāracamatkṛteḥ ।
īpsitārthārpaṇaikāntadakṣā bhavati bhāratī ।।

sarvebhyaḥ udārā udbhaṭā । camatkṛtiḥ camatkāro । yasya । na tu sarve etādṛśāḥ bhavantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

śrīrāmam prati kathayati

kumāra tvāṃ vinā kasya vivekaphalaśālinī ।
evaṃ vikāsam āyāti prajñā vanalatā yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

prajñādīpaśikhā yasya rāmasyeva hṛdi sthitā ।
prajvalaty alam ālokakāriṇī sa pumān smṛtaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

raktamāṃsāsthiyantrāṇi bahūny atitatāni ca ।
padārthān apakarṣanti nāsti teṣu sacetanam ।।

atitatāni bahūni raktamāṃsāsthiyantrāṇi dehaniṣṭhāḥ puruṣā iti yāvat । santi kathambhūtāni । padārthān apakarṣanti jāḍyena jetṝṇi । kiṃ tu teṣu kiñcid api raktamāṃsāsthiyantram sacetanaṃ vicārayuktaṃ । nāsti । kaścid api puruṣaḥ sacetano nāstīty arthaḥ ।।

janmamṛtyujarāduḥkham anuyānti punaḥ punaḥ ।
vimṛśanti na saṃsārapaśavaḥ parimohitāḥ ।।

vimṛśantīty atrāpi janmamṛtyujarāduḥkham ity etad eva karma । saṃsārapaśavaḥ ajñāninaḥ ।।

kathañcit kvacid evaiko dṛśyate vimalāśayaḥ ।
pūrvāparavicārārho yathāyam arisūdanaḥ ।।

pūrvāparavicārārhaḥ samyagvicārayogyaḥ ।।

anuttamacamatkāraphalāḥ subhagamūrtayaḥ ।
bhavyā hi viralā loke sahakāradrumā iva ।।

bhavyāḥ vivekayuktāḥ ।।

samyagdṛṣṭir jagajjātau svavivekacamatkṛtiḥ ।
asmin bhavyamatāv antar iyam anyeva dṛśyate ।।

asmābhiḥ । bhavyamatau asmin garbharūpe śrīrāme । samyagdṛṣṭiḥ samyagdṛṣṭisvarūpā । iyaṃ svavivekacamatkṛtiḥ ātmavivekacamatkāraḥ । jagajjātau jagatsthitau । anyā iva navīnā iva । dṛśyate ।।

sulabhāḥ subhagā lokāḥ phalapallavaśālinaḥ ।
jāyante taravo deśe na tu candanapādapāḥ ।।

subhagāḥ ākāramātreṇa manoharāḥ ।।

vṛkṣāḥ prativane santi satyaṃ suphalapallavāḥ ।
na tv apūrvacamatkāro lavaṅgaḥ sulabhaḥ sadā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jyotsneva śītā śaśinaḥ sutaror iva mañjarī ।
puṣpād āmodalekheva dṛṣṭā rāmāc camatkṛtiḥ ।।

camatkṛtiḥ vairāgyarūpety arthaḥ ।।

asmād uddāmadaurātmyadaivanirmāṇanirmiteḥ ।
dvijendrā dagdhasaṃsārāt sāro hy atyantadurlabhaḥ ।।

he dvijendrāḥ । dagdhasaṃsārāt kathambhūtāt । atyantavaiṣamyakāritvena uddāmadaurātmyaṃ yad daivaṃ vidhiḥ । tasya yat nirmāṇaṃ racanaṃ । tataḥ nirmitiḥ sampattir । nirmāṇanirmityoḥ sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvena bhedo draṣṭavyaḥ । atra vairāgyotkarṣāt daivam prati asūyā na yukteti nānyathā śaṅkitavyam ।।

yatante sārasamprāptau ye yaśonidhayo dhiyā ।
dhanyā dhuri satāṃ gaṇyās tā eva puruṣottamāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

na rāmeṇa samo astīha triṣu lokeṣu kaścana ।
vivekavān udārātmā mahātmā ceti no matiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena vairāgyaprakaraṇaṃ samāpayati

sakalalokacamatkṛtikāriṇo apy abhimataṃ yadi rāghavacetasaḥ ।
phalati no tad ime vayam eva hi sphuṭataram munayo hatabuddhayaḥ ।।

abhimataṃ samanantaroktasya praśnasyottaram ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyaprakaraṇe dvātriṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

śrotṝṇām bhāvanāveśasatkṛtasvāntaśālinām 
vairāgyākhyaprakaraṇavyākhyā satphaladāstv iyam 
yacchaktyāveśavaśataḥ sāmarthyaṃ kāryagocaram 
bhāvānām astu yatno ayaṃ tatkāryatvena niścitaḥ 
vāsanābījarāgākhyadrumonmūlanapaṇḍitaḥ 
vairāgyākhyaḥ payaḥpūraḥ sphuratān mama mānase 

iti śivam ।।

iti śrīkāśmīramaṇḍalāntarvartyārādhyapādamahāmāheśvaravaiḍūryakaṇṭhātmajaśrīmadavatārakaṇṭhaputraśrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ vairāgyākhyam prakaraṇaṃ samāptam ।। Prakaraṇa Mumukṣuvyavahāra 

[dvau huḍāv iva yudhyete puruṣārthau samāsamau ।
ātmīyaś cānyadīyaś ca jaya]ty atibalas tayoḥ ।।

samāsamau arthānarthotpādakatvāt samaviṣamau । ātmīyaḥ ucchāstraḥ । anyadīyaḥ śāstroktaḥ iti । dvau puruṣārthau huḍāv iva yudhyete yuddhaṃ kurutaḥ । tatrāpi samaḥ śāstroktaḥ । asamaḥ ucchāstra iti vibhāgaḥ । tatra tayoḥ dvayoḥ puruṣārthayoḥ madhye । huḍaḥ śṛṅgasahito mṛgaviśeṣaḥ ।।

tad evāha anarthaḥ prāpyate yatra śāstritād api pauruṣāt ।
anarthakaṃ tu balavat tatra jñeyaṃ svapauruṣam ।।

yatra puruṣeṇa śāstritād api pauruṣāt anarthaḥ prāpyate tatra anarthakam anarthotpādakaṃ svapauruṣam aśāstrīyaṃ pauruṣaṃ । tanmadhye praviṣṭād balavataḥ svapauruṣād evāsau anartha utpanna iti jñeyam iti bhāvaḥ । arthāt tu yatra anarthaḥ na prāpyate tatra śāstrīyam eva balavaj jñeyam । dvayoḥ pauruṣayoś ca sarvatra sandhir asti asahāyasyaikakasyotthānāsaṃbhavāt ।।

puruṣasya kartavyaṃ darśayati

paraṃ pauruṣam āśritya dantair dantān vicūrṇayan ।
śubhenāśubham udyuktaḥ prāktanaṃ pauruṣaṃ jayet ।।

paraṃ pauruṣam śāstroktaṃ pauruṣam । udyuktaḥ udyogayuktaḥ । prāktanaṃ pauruṣam vāsanākhyam prāktanam । api śubhaṃ śubhakāry eva । yataḥ śubhā vāsanaiva mokṣadāyinī proktety aśubham ity uktam ।।

prāktanaḥ puruṣārtho asau māṃ niyojayatīti dhīḥ ।
balād adhaspadīkāryā pratyakṣād adhikā na sā ।।

pratyakṣeṇa tu pauruṣasyaiva niyojane sāmarthyaṃ dṛṣṭam ity etad abhipretya pratyakṣād adhikā na sety uktam ।।

tāvat tāvat prayatnena yatitavyaṃ svapauruṣaṃ ।
prāktanaṃ pauruṣaṃ yāvad aśubhaṃ śāmyati svayam ।।

svapauruṣaṃ yatitavyam śāstrānusāreṇa svaviṣayaṃ prati yatnayuktaṃ kāryaṃ । yatitavyam iti ṇicyuktaḥ prayogaḥ ।।

doṣaḥ śāmyaty asandehaṃ prāktano adyatanair guṇaiḥ ।
dṛṣṭānto atra hyastanasya doṣasyādyaguṇaiḥ kṣayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

asaddaivam adhaḥ kṛtvā nityam udyuktayā dhiyā ।
saṃsārottaraṇaṃ bhūtyai yatetādhātum ātmani ।।

bhūtyai muktirūpāyaiśvaryāya ।।

na gantavyam anudyogaiḥ sāmyaṃ puruṣagardabhaiḥ ।
udyogas tu yathāśāstraṃ lokadvitayasiddhaye ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃsārakuharād asmān nirgantavyaṃ svayaṃ balāt ।
pauruṣaṃ yatnam āśritya hariṇevāripañjarāt ।।

saṃsārakuharāt saṃsāraśvabhrāt । aripañjarāt aribhūtāt pañjarāt ।।

pratyahaṃ pratyavekṣeta naraś caritam ātmanaḥ ।
saṃtyajet paśubhis tulyaṃ śrayet satpuruṣocitam ।।

pratyavekṣeta kīdṛśam iti vimarśaviṣayaṃ kuryāt ।।

kiṃcitkāntānnapānādikalilaṃ komalaṃ gṛhe ।
vraṇe kīṭa ivāsvādya vayaḥ kāryaṃ na bhasmasāt ।।

kalilaṃ pāpajanakam । komalaṃ āmukhe komalatayā pratibhāsamānam । vraṇe randhre ।।

śubhena pauruṣeṇāśu śubham āsādyate phalam ।
aśubhenāśubhaṃ nityaṃ daivaṃ nāma na kiṃcana ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pratyakṣadṛṣṭam utsṛjya yo anumānamanās tv asau ।
svabhujābhyām imau sarpāv iti prekṣya palāyatām ।।

svabhujābhyām iti pañcamī ।।

daivaṃ saṃprerayati mām iti mugdhadhiyāṃ mukham ।
adṛṣṭaśreṣṭhadṛṣṭīnāṃ dṛṣṭvā lakṣmīr nivartate ।।

adṛṣṭā । dṛṣṭiḥ pauruṣākhyā dṛṣṭiḥ ।।

tasmāt puruṣayatnena vivekaṃ pūrṇam āśrayet ।
ātmajñānamahārthāni śāstrāṇi pravicārayet ।।

ātmajñānam eva mahān arthaḥ yeṣāṃ tāni ।।

citte cintayatām arthaṃ yathāśāstraṃ nijehitaiḥ ।
asaṃsādhayatām eva mūḍhānāṃ dhig durīpsitam ।।

nijehitaiḥ svapauruṣaiḥ । durīpsitam duṣṭakāṅkṣitam ।।

pauruṣaṃ ca na cānantaṃ na yatnam abhivāñchate ।
na yatnenāpi mahatā tailam āsādyate aśmanaḥ ।।

pauruṣam anantaṃ antarahitaṃ । kiṃ tu niyatam eva bhavati । yatnam na abhivāñchate na svotpādakatvena kāṅkṣate । yatnena svasya niyamaṃ na laṅghayati iti yāvat । puruṣo mahatāpi yatnena svasmin niyataṃ pauruṣaṃ na laṅghayituṃ śaknotīti bhāvaḥ । etad dṛṣṭāntena sugamaṃ karoti । na yatneneti ।।

pūrvoktam evārthaṃ sphuṭayati

yathā ghaṭaḥ parimito yathā parimitaḥ paṭaḥ ।
niyataḥ parimāṇasthaḥ puruṣārthas tathaiva vaḥ ।।

ataḥ svapauruṣāviṣaye ākāśagamanādau na yatitavyam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

sa ca śāstrārthasatsaṅgasamācārair nijaṃ phalam ।
dadātīti svabhāvo ayam anyathānarthasiddhaye ।।

anyathā śāstrārthasatsaṅgasamācārāṇām abhāve ।।

svarūpaṃ pauruṣasyaitad daivaṃ vyavaharan naraḥ ।
yāti niṣphalayatnatvaṃ na kadācana kaścana ।।

pauruṣasya svarūpam daivam vyavaharan daivam iti nāmnā vyavaharan । na tu paramārthato daivam iti jānann iti yāvat ।।

dainyadāridryaduḥkhārtā apy anye puruṣottamāḥ ।
pauruṣeṇaiva yatnena yātā devendratulyatām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ā bālyāc caivam abhyastaiḥ śāstrasatsaṅgamādibhiḥ ।
guṇaiḥ puruṣayatnena svo arthaḥ saṃprāpyate hi taiḥ ।।

svo arthaḥ mokṣākhyaḥ kāṅkṣito arthaḥ । taiḥ prasiddhaiḥ guṇair iti karaṇe tṛtīyā । yatneneti tu hetau ।।

upasaṃhāraṃ karoti

iti pwratyakṣato dṛṣṭam anubhūtaṃ kṛtaṃ śrutam ।
daivottham iti manyante ye hatās te kubuddhayaḥ ।।

kṛtam śrutam anuṣṭhitam । sarvam daivāt uttham asti । iti ye manyante । te kubuddhayaḥ hatāḥ naṣṭāḥ ।।

ālasyaṃ yadi na bhavej jagaty anarthaḥ ko na syād bahudhaniko bahuśruto vā ।
ālasyād iyam avaniḥ sasāgarāntā saṃpūrṇā narapaśubhiś ca nirdhanaiś ca ।।

narapaśubhiḥ ajñānibhiḥ । nirdhanaiḥ daridraiḥ । tasmād dhanakāṅkṣibhiḥ mokṣakāṅkṣibhir vā pauruṣam eva kāryam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

pauruṣānuṣṭhānaprakāraṃ kathayati

bālye gate aviratakalpitakelilole paugaṇḍamaṇḍanavayaḥprabhṛti prayatnāt ।
satsaṅgamaiḥ padapadārthavibuddhabuddhiḥ kuryān naraḥ svaguṇadoṣavicāraṇāni ।।

avirataṃ kalpitā yā keliḥ । bālabhāve gate sati । puruṣaḥ paugaṇḍasyāvasthāviśeṣasya maṇḍanabhūtaṃ yat vayaḥ । tataḥ prabhṛti yauvanāt prabhṛti iti yāvat । svaguṇadoṣavicāraṇāni kuryāt । satsaṅgamaiḥ sādhusaṅgamaiḥ । satsaṅgamābhāve hi svaguṇadoṣavicāraṇam aśakyakriyam eva । puruṣaḥ kathaṃbhūtaḥ । padapadārthavibuddhabuddhiḥ । padapadārthayoḥ vibuddhā buddhiḥ yasya । padapadārthajña ity arthaḥ ।।

śrīvālmīkiḥ sargāntaślokena bharadvājaṃ prati tatratyaṃ dināvasānaṃ kathayati

ity uktavaty atha munau divaso jagāma sāyantanāya vidhaye astam ino jagāma ।
snātuṃ sabhā kṛtanamaskaraṇā jagāma śyāmākṣaye ravikaraiś ca sahājagāma ।।

munau vasiṣṭhe । divasaḥ jagāma avasānaṃ gataḥ । sabhā dāśarathī sabhā । kṛtanamaskaraṇā kṛtamuninamaskārā satī । sāyantanāya vidhaye sāyaṃ sandhyārthaṃ । sā sabhā śyāmākṣaye rātrikṣaye । ravikaraiḥ sūryakaraiḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe pañcamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

prabhāte śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ śrīrāmaṃ prati pūrvasargoktavastuphalitaṃ kathayati

tasmāt prākpauruṣaṃ daivaṃ nānyat tat projjhya dūrataḥ ।
sādhusaṅgamasacchāstrair jīvam uttārayed balāt ।।

tasmāt pūrvasargoktāt hetoḥ । prākpauruṣaṃ prāktanaṃ pauruṣaṃ । daivam bhavati । anyat pauruṣād bhinnaṃ kiṃcid daivam । na bhavati । ataḥ puruṣaḥ tat daivaṃ । dūrataḥ projjhya arthāt adyatanaṃ śubhaṃ pauruṣam āśritya । sādhusaṅgamasacchāstraiḥ hetubhūtaiḥ । jīvam balāt haṭhena । saṃsārād iti śeṣaḥ ।।

yathā yathā prayatnaḥ syād bhaved āśu phalaṃ tathā ।
iti pauruṣam evāsti daivam astu tad eva vaḥ ।।

prayatnaḥ pauruṣam । tat yuṣmābhiḥ aṅgīkṛtaṃ daivam । vaḥ eva yuṣmākam evāstu ।।

duḥkhād yathā duḥkhakāle hā kaṣṭam iti kathyate ।
hākaṣṭaśabdaparyāyas tathā hā daivam ity api ।।

tathā hā kaṣṭam itivat hā daivam iti dīnānām evoktir astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

prāksvakarmetarākāraṃ daivaṃ nāma na vidyate ।
bālaḥ prabalapuṃseva taj jetum iva śakyate ।।

prāksvakarmaṇaḥ prāktanasvakarmaṇaḥ । itarākāram daivaṃ nāma na vidyate । prāktanāt svakarmaṇaḥ pṛthaksattāṃ na bhajate ity arthaḥ । ataḥ puṃsā tat daivaṃ । jetuṃ śakyate keneva । yathā tena bālo jetuṃ śakyate tathety arthaḥ ।।

hyastano duṣṭa ācāra ācāreṇādya cāruṇā ।
yathāśu śubhatāṃ yāti prāktanaṃ kukṛtaṃ tathā ।।

adyācāreṇa adya kṛtenācāreṇa । prāktanaṃ kukṛtam adyatanena sukṛtena śubhatāṃ yāti ।।

tajjayāya yatante ye na lābhalavalampaṭāḥ ।
te mūḍhāḥ prākṛtā dīnāḥ sthitā daivaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

tajjayāya kuvāsanārūpaprāktanāśubhapauruṣajayāya । lābhalave sāṃsārikapadārthāptirūpe lābhaleśe । laṃpaṭāh lobhayuktāḥ ।।

pauruṣeṇa kṛtaṃ karma daivād yad abhinaśyati ।
tatra nāśayitur jñeyaṃ pauruṣaṃ balavattaram ।।

nāśayituḥ nāśakasya kālādeḥ ।।

yad ekavṛntaphalayor apy ekaṃ śūnyakoṭaram ।
tatra prayatnaḥ sphuritas tathā tadrasasaṃvidaḥ ।।

ekasmin vṛnte sthitau phalau ekavṛntaphalau । tayoḥ api madhyāt ekaphalaṃ śūnyakoṭaram sārarahitamadhyaṃ yat bhavati । arthāt dvitīyaṃ sārabharitamadhyaṃ jñeyam । tatra tasmin sthāne । tadrasasaṃvidaḥ tayoḥ phalayoḥ yā rasarūpā saṃvit । tasyāḥ tadrasasyeti yāvat । tathā tena prakāreṇa । yatnaḥ pauruṣaṃ sphuritaḥ । raseneva tādṛśaṃ pauruṣaṃ kṛtaṃ yenaikaṃ phalaṃ sārarahitaṃ saṃpannaṃ । na tv anyaśaṅkitasya daivasyātra kāpi śaktir astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

yat prayānti jagadbhāvāḥ saṃsiddhā api saṃkṣayam ।
kṣayakārakayatnasya tatra jñeyaṃ mahad balam ।।

kṣayakārakasya nāśakartuḥ kālasya । yaḥ yatnaḥ pauruṣam । tasya ।।

bhikṣuko maṅgalebhena nṛpo yat kriyate balāt ।
tad amātyebhapaurāṇāṃ prayatnasya mahat phalam ।।

maṅgalebhena maṅgalahastinā । bhikṣukaḥ nṛpaḥ rājā । balāt yat kriyate amātyebhapaurāṇāṃ rājyapradātṝṇāṃ mantrimaṅgalahastināgarāṇāṃ । prayatnasya tadrājyadānarūpasya pauruṣasya sahaphalaṃ bhavati । na daivasya ।।

pauruṣenānnam ākramya yathā dantair vicūrṇyate ।
alpaṃ pauruṣam ākramya tathā śūreṇa cūrṇyate ।।

yathā dantaiḥ pauruṣeṇa annam ākramya svavaśīkṛtya । tathā śūreṇādyatanapauruṣayuktena puruṣeṇa । alpaṃ prāktanatvena jīrṇaprāyaṃ । pauruṣaṃ ākramya cūrṇyate ।।

anubhūtaṃ hi mahatāṃ lāghavaṃ yatnaśālināṃ ।
yatheṣṭaṃ viniyujyante te taiḥ karmasu loṣṭavat ।।

hi yasmāt । asmābhiḥ yatnaśālināṃ pauruṣaśālināṃ । mahatāṃ lāghavaṃ cāturyam । anubhūtaṃ pratyakṣaṃ dṛṣṭam । kathaṃ anubhūtam ity । yataḥ taiḥ yatnaśālibhiḥ । te arthāt pauruṣarahitāḥ puruṣāḥ । yatheṣṭaṃ svecchānusāreṇa । loṣṭavat karmasu viniyujyante ।।

śaktasya pauruṣaṃ dṛśyam adṛśyaṃ vāpi yad bhavet ।
tad daivam ity aśaktena buddham ātmany abuddhinā ।।

śaktasya mahatā pauruṣeṇa yuktasya । dṛśyasya puruṣāder adṛśyasya kālādeś ca । dṛśyam adṛśyaṃ vā yat pauruṣaṃ bhavet । abuddhinā samyagjñānarahitena । aśaktena tadapekṣayā śaktirahitena puruṣeṇa । tat śaktasya pauruṣam । ātmani svasmin viṣaye । daivaṃ buddham jñātam । anyathā daivena me kṛtam iti na brūyāt ।।

bhūtānāṃ balavadbhūtayatno daivam iti sthitam ।
tasthuṣām apy adhiṣṭhātṛvatām etat sphuṭaṃ mithaḥ ।।

balavadbhūtayatnaḥ । bhūtānām kṣudrabhūtānāṃ upari । daivam iti sthitam bhavati । puruṣo hi yatra na paryāpto bhavati tatraiva daivena me kṛtam iti kathayati । na kevalam etan mayaiva jñātaṃ kiṃtv anyair apīty āha । apiśabdaḥ samuccaye । adhiṣṭhātṛvatāṃ tasthuṣām prerakayuktānāṃ sthitānām puruṣāṇām api । etat mayā uktaḥ arthaḥ । sphuṭaṃ prakaṭo bhavati । te hi parasparaṃ kṣudrataratamādibhedenādhiṣṭheyāḥ bhavanti । utkṛṣṭataratamādibhedena tv adhiṣṭhātāraḥ । adhiṣṭhātā eva cādhiṣṭheyaṃ prati daivam । ataḥ eteṣu madukto arthaḥ sphuṭa eva bhavati iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu bhikṣukarājyaviṣaye ayaṃ nyāyo nāstīty । atrāha

śāstramātyebhapaurāṇām avikalpyā svabhāvadhīḥ ।
sā yā bhikṣukarājyasya kartrī dhartrī prajāsthiteḥ ।।

śāstā purohitaḥ । ibhaś ca maṅgalahastī ca । teṣām । sā svabhāvadhīḥ svabhāvāt utthitā bhikṣurājyadānarūpā buddhiḥ । avikalpyā nāśayitum aśakyāśaktā iti yāvat bhavati । yā bhikṣukarājyasya kartrī bhavati । taddvāreṇa prajāsthiteḥ dhartrī ca bhavati । ato atrāpy ayam eva nyāya iti bhāvaḥ । yatra deśe rājā mriyate । tasya putraś ca na syāt । tatra maṅgalahastī yaṃ namati । tam eva rājānaṃ kurvantīti ।।

aihikaḥ prāktanaṃ hanti prāktano adyatanaṃ balāt ।
sarvadā puruṣaspandas tatrānudvegavāñ jayī ।।

puruṣaspandaḥ pauruṣam । tatra dvayoḥ pauruṣayoḥ madhye । anudvegavān udvegarahitaḥ । lakṣaṇayā atibala ity arthaḥ ।।

nanu tatra kaḥ prāyaḥ balavān astīty । atrāha

dvayor adyatanasyaiva pratyakṣād balitā bhavet ।
daivaṃ jetum ato yatnair bālo yūneva śakyate ।।

pratyakṣāt pratyakṣapramāṇena । dṛśyate hi adyatanaḥ śubhācāraḥ hyastanam aśubhaṃ nāśayan । phalitam āha । ataḥ yatnaiḥ adyatanaiḥ pauruṣaiḥ । daivaṃ prāktanaṃ pauruṣaṃ । yūneva । yathā yūnā bālaḥ jetuṃ śakyate tathety arthaḥ ।।

meghena nīyate yad vā vatsaropārjitā kṛṣiḥ ।
meghasya puruṣārtho asau jayaty adhikayatnavān ।।

atrāpi na daivasya kācic chaktir astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

krameṇopārjite apy arthe naṣṭe kāryā na kheditā ।
na balaṃ yatra me śaktaṃ tatra kā paridevanā ।।

balam pauruṣam । na hi janaḥ aśakyaḥ rājyādivastuprāptyarthaṃ pratyahaṃ paridevanāyukto bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

yan na śaknomi tasyārthe yadi duḥkhaṃ karomy aham ।
tad amānitamṛtyor me yuktaṃ pratyaharodanam ।।

amānitamṛtyoḥ tāvad mṛtyupātam api anaṅgīkurvataḥ ।।

deśakālakriyādravyavaśato visphuranty amī ।
sarva eva jagadbhāvā jayaty adhikayatnavān ।।

bhāvāḥ mṛtyvādirūpāḥ padārthāḥ ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

tasmāt pauruṣam āśritya sacchāstraiḥ satsamāgamaiḥ ।
prajñām amalatāṃ nītvā saṃsārāmbunidhiṃ tara ।।

amalatām rāgādimalarāhityam ।।

prāktanaś caihikaś cāsau puruṣārthau phaladrumau ।
aihikaḥ puruṣārthaś ca jagaty abhyadhikas tayoḥ ।।

phalotpādakau drumau phaladrumau ।।

karma yaḥ prāktanaṃ tucchaṃ na nihanti śubhehitaiḥ ।
ajño jantur anīśo asau vāṅmanaḥsukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।।

karma pauruṣam । vāṅmanaḥsukhaduḥkhau apy asau nāśayituṃ na śaknoti । śarīraduḥkhanāśe tu kā katheti bhāvaḥ ।।

yas tūdāracamatkāraḥ sadācāravihāravān ।
sa niryāti jaganmohān mṛgendraḥ pañjarād iva ।।

sadācāreṇa sādhvācāreṇa । vihāraḥ vidyate yasya । tādṛśaḥ । sa eva śubhapauruṣabhājanam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

kaścin māṃ prerayaty evam ity anarthakukalpane ।
yaḥ sthito dṛṣṭam utsṛjya tyājyo asau dūrato adhamaḥ ।।

dṛṣṭam pratyakṣadṛṣṭaphalaṃ pauruṣam ।।

vyavahārasahasrāṇi yāny upāyānti yānti ca ।
yathāśāstraṃ vihartavyaṃ teṣu tyaktvā sukhāsukhe ।।

yathāśāstram svaśāstrānatikrameṇa । vihartavyaṃ vihāraḥ kāryaḥ ।।

yathāśāstram anucchinnāṃ maryādāṃ svām anujjhataḥ ।
upatiṣṭhanti sarvāṇi ratnāny ambunidher iva ।।

svām svajātyanusāriṇīm । upatiṣṭhanti samīpam āgacchanti । sarvāṇi sakalāni śreyāṃsi ।।

svārthaprāpakakāryaikaprayatnaparatā budhaiḥ ।
proktā pauruṣaśabdena sā siddhyai śāstrayantritā ।।

svārthaprāpake svaprayojanasādhake kārye । prayatnaparatā śāstrayantritā śāstrabuddhā ।।

kriyāyāḥ spandadharmiṇyāḥ svārthasādhakatā svayam ।
sādhusaṅgamaśāstrārthatīkṣṇayābhyūhyate dhiyā ।।

spandadharmiṇyāḥ spandasvarūpāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ । svārthasādhakatā svayam anyanirapekṣaṃ bhavati । sādhusaṅgamaśāstrārthatīkṣṇayā dhiyā sambandhinī svārthasādhakatā abhyūhyate vivecyate । kā svārthasādhakatā । śubhā । kā śubheti vyavasthāpyate ity arthaḥ ।।

anantaṃ samatānandaṃ paramārthaṃ vidur budhāḥ ।
sa yebhyaḥ prāpyate anantaṃ te sevyāḥ śāstrasādhavaḥ ।।

sarvatra samadarśitvaṃ samatā । tadrūpaḥ ānandaḥ samatānandaḥ । paramārtham paramopādeyaṃ । pauruṣam āśrityopāsyaḥ ।।

prāktanaṃ pauruṣaṃ tac ced daivaśabdena kathyate ।
tad yuktam etad etasmin nāsti nāpavadāmahe ।।

tat prasiddhaṃ । prāktanaṃ pauruṣaṃ daivaśabdena cet yadi । kathyate । yuṣmābhir iti śeṣaḥ । tat kathanaṃ । yata etat samatānandaprāptyupāyatvam । ataḥ vayaṃ nāpavadāmahe tadapavādaṃ na kurmaḥ । upekṣāviṣayatvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

mūḍhaiḥ prakalpitaṃ daivam anyad yais te kṣayaṃ gatāḥ ।
nityaṃ svapauruṣād eva lokadvayahitaṃ bhavet ।।

anyat prāktanapauruṣāt । kṣayam anudyogakṛtaṃ nāśam ।।

hyastanī duṣkriyābhyeti śobhāṃ satkriyayā yathā ।
adyaivaṃ prāktanī tasmād yatnāt satkāryavān bhava ।।

adyatanayeti śeṣaḥ । yathā adyatanayā satkriyayā hyastanī duṣkriyā śobhāṃ abhyeti । evam tathā । prāktanī prāgjanmabhavā vāsanārūpā duṣkriyā । adya adyatanayā sacchāstrasevanādirūpayā satkriyayā । śobhām śuddhatvam abhyeti । ataḥ tvam satkāryavān bhava ।।

karāmalakavad dṛṣṭaṃ pauruṣād eva yat phalam ।
mūḍhaḥ pratyakṣam utsṛjya daivamohe nimajjati ।।

mūḍhaḥ daivāt phalavādī ajñānī । pratyakṣam pratyakṣapramāṇasiddhaṃ pauruṣam utsṛjya । daivamohe daivarūpe bhrame majjati । tat kutaḥ yat yataḥ । asmābhiḥ phalam karāmalakavat pauruṣād eva dṛṣṭam pratyakṣam anubhūtam ।।

sakalakāraṇakāryavivarjitaṃ nijavikalpabalād upakalpitam ।
tad anapekṣya hi daivam asanmayaṃ śraya śubhāśaya pauruṣam ātmanaḥ ।।

sakalāni yāni kāryakāraṇāni । atyantāsatsvarūpam ity arthaḥ । ata eva nijavikalpabalāt upakalpitam saṃpāditaṃ । tat asanmayaṃ daivam anapekṣya । tvam ātmanaḥ pauruṣaṃ āśraya । daivavaśo mā bhaveti bhāvaḥ ।।

śāstraiḥ sadācaritajṛṃbhitadeśadharmair yat kalpitaṃ phalam atīva ciraprarūḍham ।
tasmin hṛdi sphurati no aparam eti cittam aṅgāvalī tad anu pauruṣam etad āhuḥ ।।

śāstraiḥ sacchāstraiḥ । yat ācaritaṃ ācāraḥ । avicchinnapravāheṇāgatāḥ ye deśadharmāḥ । taiḥ cātīva ciraprarūḍhaṃ atyantabahukālāt prabhṛti prasiddhaṃ । yat phalaṃ kalpitam sādhyatvena niścitaṃ bhavati । hṛdi sphurati saṃpādanīyatayā vilasati sati । cittam aparam proktaphaletaraṃ vastu yat । no eti na gacchati । tad anu cittānantaraṃ । aṅgāvalī hastādyavayavapaṅktir । no eti । api tu tatsādhanaikaparaṃ bhavati । paṇḍitāḥ etat pauruṣam āhuḥ kathayanti । na tu yathā tathā hastādicālanam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

buddhvaiva pauruṣaphalaṃ puruṣatvam etad ātmaprayatnaparataiva sadaiva kāryā ।
neyā tataḥ saphalatāṃ paramām athāsau sacchāstrasādhujanapaṇḍitasevanena ।।

puruṣeṇa etat svenānubhūyamānaṃ । puruṣatvam puruṣabhāvam । pauruṣaphalaṃ । pauruṣaṃ pūrvaślokoktasvarūpapauruṣaṃ । phalaṃ yasya । ātmaprayatnaparatā pauruṣanirvṛttatvam । tataḥ karaṇānantaraṃ । puruṣeṇāsau ātmaprayatnaparatā । sacchāstrasādhujanapaṇḍitasevanena paramām utkṛṣṭām । saphalatām mokṣākhyaphalayuktatām neyā । athaśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ ।।

daivapauruṣavicāracārubhiś cetasā caritam ātmapauruṣam ।
nityam eva jayatīti bhāvitaiḥ kārya āryajanasevanodyamaḥ ।।

puruṣaiḥ āryajanasevanodyamaḥ kāryaḥ । daivapauruṣayoḥ yaḥ vicāraḥ svarūpavivecanaṃ । punaḥ kathaṃbhūtaiḥ । bhāvitaiḥ niścitaiḥ iti । caritam anuṣṭhitam । ātmapauruṣam nityam sadā jayati । sarvaphalajanakatvāt sarvotkarṣeṇa vartata iti ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati

janmaprabandhamayam āmayam eṣa jīvo buddhvaihikaṃ sahajapauruṣam eva siddhyai ।
śāntiṃ nayatv avitathena varauṣadhena pṛṣṭena tuṣṭiparapaṇḍitasevanena ।।

jīvaḥ puruṣaḥ । aihikaṃ iha loke śakyatvena sthitaṃ pauruṣaṃ । siddhyai siddhyarthaṃ buddhvā । tataḥ tadāśrayaṇenānuṣṭhitena tuṣṭiparapaṇḍitasevanena hetunā । pṛṣṭena tasmād eva paṇḍitāt pṛṣṭena । avitathena saphalena । varauṣadhena samyagjñānākhyavarauṣadhena । janmaprabandhamayam janmasantānarūpaṃ । āmayam rogaṃ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuvyavahāraprakaraṇe ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ atyantopādeyatvena punar api pauruṣacarcām eva prastauti

prāpya vyādhivinirmuktaṃ deham alpādhivedhitam ।
tathātmānaṃ samādadhyād yathā bhūyo na jāyate ।।

alpo yaḥ ādhiḥ jīvanopāyādinimittā cittapīḍā । tena vedhitam tāḍanāyuktam kṛtam । samādadhyāt cinmātratattve samādhānayuktaṃ kuryāt ।।

daivaṃ puruṣakāreṇa yo ativartitum icchati ।
iha cāmutra ca jayet sa saṃpūrṇābhivāñchitaḥ ।।

daivam anudyogarūpam daivam । saṃpūrṇe abhivāñchite bhogamokṣarūpe kāṅkṣite yasya saḥ ।।

ye samudyogam utsṛjya sthitā daivaparāyaṇāḥ ।
te dharmam arthakāmau ca nāśayanty ātmavidviṣaḥ ।।

ātmavidviṭtvaṃ ca teṣāṃ bhogamokṣarūpātmakakāryanāśakatvāj jñeyam ।।

saṃvitspando manaḥspanda indriyaspanda eva ca ।
etāni puruṣārthasya rūpāṇy ebhyaḥ phalodayaḥ ।।

ebhyaḥ saṃvidādispandebhyaḥ ।।

saṃvittattvād eva pauruṣotthānaṃ kathayati

yathā saṃvedanaṃ cetas tathāntaḥspandam ṛcchati ।
tathaiva kāyaś calati tathaiva phalabhoktṛtā ।।

yathā yena prakāreṇa । saṃvedanam saṃvidaḥ sphuraṇam syāt । tathā tena prakāreṇa । cetaḥ antaḥspandam saṃkalpākhyām ceṣṭām । ṛcchati gacchati । tathaiva cittaspandānusāreṇa eva । kāyaḥ calati hitāhitaprāptiparihārarūpāṃ kriyāṃ prati ceṣṭate । tataḥ tathaiva kāyacalanānusāreṇaiva । phalabhoktṛtā bhavati ।।

ābālam etat saṃsiddhaṃ yatra yatra yathā tathā ।
daivaṃ tu na kvacid dṛṣṭam ato jayati pauruṣam ।।

ābālaṃ bālaparyantam । phalitam āhāta iti ।।

puruṣārthena deveśagurur eṣa bṛhaspatiḥ ।
śukro daityendragurutāṃ puruṣārthena cāsthitaḥ ।।

deveśasya guruḥ deveśaguruḥ ।।

dainyadāridryaduḥkhārtā api sādho narottamāḥ ।
pauruṣeṇaiva yatnena yātā devendratulyatām ।।

devendratulyatām indrasāmyam ।।

mahānto vibhavāḍhyā ye nānāścaryasamāśrayāḥ ।
pauruṣeṇaiva doṣeṇa narakātithitāṃ gatāḥ ।।

doṣeṇa doṣahetunā । ucchāstriteneti yāvat ।।

bhāvābhāvasahasreṣu daśāsu vividhāsu ca ।
svapauruṣavaśād eva vivṛttā bhūtajātayaḥ ।।

vivṛttāḥ rūpāntaraṃ gatāḥ । bhāvābhāvādyāviṣṭāḥ saṃpannā iti yāvat ।।

śāstrato gurutaś caiva svataś ceti trisiddhitā ।
sarvatra puruṣārthasya na daivasya kadācana ।।

tribhiḥ prakāraiḥ siddhitā trisiddhitā । svataḥ śāstrādi vinā svapratibhāmātrād eva । kecid dhi śāstrāt siddhā bhavanti ।।

aśubheṣu samāviṣṭaṃ śubheṣv evāvatārayet ।
yatnena cittam ity āśu sarvaśāstrārthasaṃgrahaḥ ।।

aśubheṣu bhogārjanarūpeṣv aśubhakāryeṣu ।।

yac chreyo yad atucchaṃ ca yad apāyavivarjitam ।
tat tad ācara yatnena putreti guravaḥ sthitāḥ ।।

putra he śiṣya । upadeṣṭṛtveneti śeṣaḥ ।।

yathā yathā prayatno me phalam āśu tathā tathā ।
ity ahaṃ pauruṣād eva phalabhāṅ na tu daivataḥ ।।

ity evaṃ । niścayavān bhaved iti bhāvaḥ ।।

pauruṣād dṛśyate siddhiḥ pauruṣaṃ dhīmatāṃ kramaḥ ।
daivam āśvāsanāmātraṃ duḥkhapelavabuddhiṣu ।।

duḥkhena pelavā udyogāsahā । buddhiḥ yeṣāṃ teṣu ।।

pratyakṣapramukhān nityaṃ pramāṇaṃ pauruṣaḥ kramaḥ ।
phalato dṛśyate loke deśāntaragamādikāt ।।

asmābhiḥ pauruṣaḥ puruṣasambandhī kramaḥ । pādacālanādirūpaṃ pauruṣam iti yāvat । deśāntaragamādikāt phalataḥ phalāt । nityaṃ pramāṇaṃ arthakriyākāri dṛśyate । phalataḥ kathaṃbhūtāt । pratyakṣaṃ pratyakṣapramāṇaṃ । pramukhaṃ grāhakatvena pradhānaṃ yasya । tādṛśāt pratyakṣadṛṣṭād ity arthaḥ । ataḥ pauruṣam eva saphalaṃ । na daivam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

bhoktā tṛpyati nābhoktā gantā gacchati nāgatiḥ ।
vaktā vakti na cāvaktā pauruṣaṃ saphalaṃ nṛṇām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pauruṣeṇa durantebhyaḥ saṃkaṭebhyaḥ subuddhayaḥ ।
samuttaranty ayatnena na tu mūkatayānayā ।।

mūkatayā daivaparatvarūpeṇa udyogarāhityena ।।

yo yo yathā prayatate sa sa tadvat phalaikabhāk ।
na tu tūṣṇīṃ sthiteneha kenacit prāpyate phalam ।।

tadvat tathā । tūṣṇīṃ sthitena udyogarahitena tiṣṭhatā ।।

śubhena puruṣārthena śubham āsādyate phalam ।
aśubhenāśubhaṃ rāma yathecchasi tathā kuru ।।

puruṣārthaphalaprāptir deśakālavaśād iha ।
prāptā cireṇa śīghraṃ vā yāsau daivam iti smṛtā ।।

prāptiḥ prāpteti kāryaṃ karoti itivat prayogaḥ । asau puruṣārthaphalaprāptiḥ ।।

na daivaṃ dṛśyate dṛṣṭyā na ca lokāntare sthitam ।
uktaṃ daivābhidhānena svaṃ loke karmaṇaḥ phalam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

puruṣo jāyate loke vardhate kṣīyate punaḥ ।
na tatra dṛśyate daivaṃ jarāyauvanabālyavān ।।

tatra puruṣe ।।

deśād deśāntaraprāptir hastasthadravyadhāraṇam ।
vyāpāraś ca tathāṅgānāṃ pauruṣeṇa na daivataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

arthaprāpakakāryaikaprayatnaparatā budhaiḥ ।
proktā pauruṣaśabdena sarvam āsādyate anayā ।।

arthaprāpakaṃ yat kāryaṃ । tatra ekam kevalaṃ । prayatnaparatā ।।

anarthaprāptikāryaikaprayatnaparatā tu yā ।
soktā pronmattaceṣṭeti na kiṃcit prāpyate anayā ।।

anarthaprāptau anarthaprāptyarthaṃ yat kāryam । tatra ekam prayatnaparatā ।।

kriyāyāḥ spandadharmiṇyāḥ svārthasādhakatā svayam ।
sādhusaṅgamasacchāstratīkṣṇayonnīyate dhiyā ।।

unnīyate niścīyate ।।

anantaṃ samatānandaṃ paramārthaṃ svakaṃ viduḥ ।
tad yebhyaḥ prāpyate yatnāt sevyās te śāstrasādhavaḥ ।।

svakam paramārtham nijaṃ paramaprayojanam ।।

sacchāstrādiguṇo matyā sacchāstrādiguṇān matiḥ ।
vardhete te mitho abhyāsāt sarobdāv iva kālataḥ ।।

sacchāstrādirūpaḥ guṇaḥ matyā bhavati । buddhirahitasya sacchāstrādau pravṛttyabhāvāt । matiḥ sacchāstrādiguṇāt bhavati । te sacchāstrādiguṇamatī । mithaḥ anyonyaṃ । abhyāsāt vardhete vṛddhiṃ gacchataḥ । kāv iva । yathā sarobdau saromeghau । kālataḥ mithaḥ vardhete tathety arthaḥ । kadācid dhi saraḥ meghavṛṣṭena jalena vardhate । kadācit tu meghaḥ sarasaḥ gṛhītena jaleneti ।।

ābālyād alam abhyastaiḥ śāstrasatsaṃgamādibhiḥ ।
guṇaiḥ puruṣayatnena svo arthaḥ saṃprāpyate hitaḥ ।।

puruṣayatnena pauruṣeṇābhyastaiḥ anuśīlitaiḥ । svaḥ arthaḥ mokṣākhyaṃ nijaṃ prayojanam ।।

pauruṣeṇa jitā daityāḥ sthāpitā bhuvanakriyāḥ ।
racitāni jagantīha viṣṇunā na tu daivataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena śrīrāmasya pauruṣaṃ kartavyatvenopadiśati

jagati puruṣakārakāraṇe asmin kuru raghunātha ciraṃ tathā prayatnam ।
vrajasi tarusarīsṛpābhidhānāṃ subhaga yathā na daśām aśaṅkam eva ।।

jagati kathaṃbhūte । puruṣakāraḥ pauruṣaṃ kāraṇaṃ yasya । tādṛśe । cinmātrapauruṣād eva hi jagad utpannam । prayatnam pauruṣam । tarusarīsṛpābhidhānāṃ daśāṃ tarvādirūpatām ity arthaḥ । tarvādayo hi pauruṣarāhityenaiva duḥkham anubhavantīti teṣāṃ grahaṇaṃ kṛtam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuvyavahāraprakaraṇe saptamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ punaḥ daivanirākaraṇaṃ karoti । oṃ

nākṛtir na ca karmāṇi nāspadaṃ na parākramaḥ ।
tan mithyājñānavat prauḍhaṃ daivaṃ nāma kim ucyate ।।

pūrvārdhe yasyeti śeṣaḥ ।।

svakarmaphalasaṃprāptāv idam ittham itīha yāḥ ।
giras tā daivanāmnaitāḥ prasiddhiṃ samupāgatāḥ ।।

idam ittham iti gira idaṃ itthaṃ saṃpannam iti vācaḥ ।।

tathaiva mūḍhamatibhir daivam astīti niścayaḥ ।
ātto duravabodhena rajjāv iva bhujaṅgamaḥ ।।

ātto gṛhītaḥ । duravabodhena ajñānena । ivaśabdaḥ yathāśābdārthe ।।

hyastanī duṣkriyābhyeti śobhāṃ satkriyayā yathā ।
adyaivaṃ prāktanī tasmād yatnāt satkāryavān bhava ।।

gatārtho ayam ।।

mūḍhānumānasaṃsiddhaṃ daivaṃ yasyāsti durmateḥ ।
daivād dāho astu mā veti vaktavyaṃ tena pāvake ।।

mūḍhānumānasaṃsiddhaṃ daivaṃ yasya durmateḥ ajñāninaḥ । asti paramārthasad asti । tena durmatinā । pāvake agnau sthitvā । daivād dāhaḥ astu māstu veti vaktavyam । tatra tv asau naitad vaktuṃ śaknoti dāhaikalabdher iti bhāvaḥ ।।

daivam eveha cet karma puṃsaḥ kim iva ceṣṭayā ।
snānadānāśanādārān daivam eva kariṣyati ।।

karma karmasaṃpādakam ity arthaḥ । na caitat saṃbhavati akiṃcitkurvataḥ snānādyanupapatter iti bhāvaḥ ।।

kiṃ vā śāstropadeśena mūko ayaṃ puruṣaḥ kila ।
saṃcāryate tu daivena kiṃ kasyehopadiśyate ।।

saṃcāryate saṃcaraṇaśīlaḥ saṃpādyate । daivāṅgīkāre na ko api kasyāpy upadeśaṃ kuryād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

na ca niḥspandatā loke dṛṣṭeha śavatāṃ vinā ।
spandaś ca phalasaṃprāptis tasmād daivaṃ nirarthakam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nanu daivena sahaiva puruṣaḥ kāryaṃ karotīty । atrāha
na cāmūrtena daivena mūrtasya sahakartṛtā ।
hastādīn īhataś caiva na daivena kvacit kṛtam ।।

amūrtena mūrtirahitena daivena । hastādīn īhataḥ ceṣṭataḥ । mūrtasya puruṣasya । sahakartṛtā ca na bhavati । ataḥ daivena kṛtam daivakartṛkaṃ kāryaṃ ।।

nanu manobuddhyādivad amūrtasyāpi daivasya mūrtena saha kartṛtvam asty evety । atrāha

manobuddhivad apy etad daivaṃ nehānubhūyate ।
āgopālaṃ kila prājñais tena daivam asat sadā ।।

mṛtaśarīre kartṛtvādarśanān manobuddhī kalpyete । na ca daivasyātra kaścid upayoga iti । na tatkalpanāvasara iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu kadācit tasmād eva dṛśyāt śarīrādeḥ kāryaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kadācin na dṛṣṭam iti adṛṣṭasya daivasya kalpanā yuktaivety । atrāha

pṛthak ced buddhir anyo arthaḥ saiva cet kānyatā tayoḥ ।
kalpanā vā pramāṇaṃ cet pauruṣaṃ kiṃ na kalpyate ।।

buddhiḥ jñānaṃ । pṛthak cet yady asti । tadārthaḥ anya ekasmāt dvitīyaḥ pṛthag iti yāvat । asti buddhiḥ sā eva । na tu bhinnā ced bhavati । tadā tayoḥ arthayoḥ kā anyatā bhavati । ato atra kevalasaddṛśyāc charīrāder eva kāryaṃ bhavatv iti bhāvaḥ । nanv atra buddhipṛthaktvopayogo nāsti । kalpanāyā eva pramāṇatvād ity । kalpanā prathamaṃ pramāṇaṃ nāsti ced । tadā pauruṣaṃ kiṃ na kalpyate । kalpanayā saṃbhāvyate samānanyāyatvāt ।।

punar api prakṛtaṃ mūrtāmūrtayoḥ sahakartṛtvāsaṃbhavam eva kathayati

nāmūrtena ca saṅgo asti nabhaseva vapuṣmataḥ ।
mūrtaṃ ca dṛśyate lagnaṃ tasmād daivaṃ na vidyate ।।

vapuṣmataḥ mūrtasya śarīriṇaḥ । amūrtena mūrtirahitena daivena । saṅgaḥ sahakartṛtvaṃ nāsti । nanu tathāpi amūrtam eva kartṛ bhavatv ity । asmābhiḥ mūrtam eva lagnaṃ kāryalagnaṃ dṛśyate । ataḥ tasyaiva kartṛtvaṃ yuktam iti bhāvaḥ । phalitaṃ kathayati । tatkalpanāyāḥ nirastatvāt ।।

viniyoktātha bhūtānām asty anyat tajjagattraye ।
śeratāṃ bhūtavṛndāni daivaṃ sarvaṃ kariṣyati ।।

viniyoktā prerakaḥ । anyad daivākhyaṃ anyat vastu । śeratām kāryeṣv anudyogaṃ bhajantām ।।

daivenetthaṃ niyukto asmi kiṃ karomīdṛśaṃ sthitam ।
samāśvāsanavāg eṣā na daivaṃ paramārthataḥ ।।

īdṛśam sthitam īdṛśam saṃpannam ।।

mūḍhaiḥ prakalpitaṃ daivaṃ tatparās te kṣayaṃ gatāḥ ।
prājñās tu puruṣārthena padam uttamam āgatāḥ ।।

tatparāḥ svayaṃkalpitadaivaparāḥ । puruṣārthena pauruṣeṇa । uttamaṃ padam mokṣākhyam utkṛṣṭaṃ sthānam ।।

ye śūrā ye ca vikrāntā ye prājñā ye ca paṇḍitāḥ ।
tais taiḥ kair iva loke asmin vada daivaṃ pracakṣyate ।।

pracakṣyate kathyate । na kenāpi pracakṣyate iti bhāvaḥ ।।

kālavidbhir vinirṇītā yasyāsti cirajīvitā ।
sa cej jīvati saṃchinnaśirās tad daivam uttamam ।।

kālavidbhiḥ daivajñaiḥ ।।

kālavidbhir vinirṇītaṃ pāṇḍityaṃ yasya rāghava ।
anadhyāpita evāsau tajjñaś ced daivam uttamam ।।

tajjñaḥ paṇḍitaḥ ।।

viśvāmitreṇa muninā daivam utsṛjya dūrataḥ ।
pauruṣeṇaiva saṃprāptaṃ brāhmaṇyaṃ rāma nānyathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

amībhir na parai rāma puruṣair munitāṃ gataiḥ ।
pauruṣeṇaiva saṃprāptā ciraṃ gaganagamitā ।।

amībhiḥ pauruṣayuktair ebhir eva । paraiḥ pauruṣarahitaiḥ sāmānyajantubhiḥ । gaganagamitā paramākāśacāritvam ।।

utsādya devasaṃghātāṃś cakrus tribhuvanodare ।
pauruṣeṇaiva yatnena sāmrājyaṃ dānaveśvarāḥ ।।

utsādya bādhitvā । devasaṃghātān devasamūhān । dānaveśvarāḥ hiraṇyākṣyādayaḥ ।।

ālūnaśīrṇam ābhogi jagad ājahrur ojasā ।
pauruṣeṇaiva yatnena dānavebhyaḥ sureśvarāḥ ।।

ālūnaśīrṇam aticañcalam ।।

rāma pauruṣayuktyaiva salilaṃ dhāryate na vā ।
ciraṃ karaṇḍake yuktyā na daivaṃ tatra kāraṇam ।।

karaṇḍake randhrayukte kāṇḍasādhite dravyaviśeṣe । kenacit prayogena hi karaṇḍe api jalaṃ tiṣṭhati ।।

haraṇādānasaṃrambhavibhramabhramabhūmiṣu ।
śaktatā dṛśyate rāma na daivasyauṣadher iva ।।

haraṇetyādy upalakṣaṇaṃ sarvakriyāṇām ।।

sargāntaślokenaitat samāpayati

sakalakāraṇakāryavivarjitaṃ nijavikalpavaśād upakalpitam ।
tvam anavekṣya hi daivam asanmayaṃ śraya śubhāśaya pauruṣam uttamam ।।

gatārtho ayam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe aṣṭamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ atra śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

bhagavan sarvadharmajña pratiṣṭhām alam āgatam ।
yal loke tad vada brahman daivam evaṃ kim ucyate ।।

he bhagavan । tvam vada । yat daivam loke evam pratiṣṭhām prasiddhim । āgataṃ । tat paṇḍitaiḥ kiṃrūpaṃ kathyate । na hi asiddhaṃ vastu prasiddhim āyāti iti bhāvaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ uttaraṃ kathayati

pauruṣaṃ sarvakāryāṇāṃ kartṛ rāghava netarat ।
phalabhoktṛ ca sarvatra na daivaṃ tatra kāraṇam ।।

he rāghava । pauruṣaṃ sarvakāryāṇāṃ kartṛ bhavati । itarat anyat daivādi । na kevalaṃ kartr eva । kiṃ tu phalabhoktṛ ca bhavati । svāviṣṭapuruṣadvāreṇeti bhāvaḥ । daivaṃ tatra kāraṇaṃ na bhavati । ato daivaṃ nāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

daivaṃ na kiṃcit kurute na ca bhuṅkte na vidyate ।
na dṛśyate nādriyate kevalaṃ kalpanedṛśī ।।

īdṛśī daivam eva sarvaṃ karotīty evaṃrūpā । na ca kalpanāyāḥ satyatvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

siddhasya pauruṣeṇeha phalasya phalaśālinām ।
śubhāśubhā vā saṃpattir daivaśabdena kathyate ।।

paṇḍitaiḥ phalaśālināṃ phalabhājāṃ । pauruṣeṇa śubhāśubhena pauruṣeṇa । siddhasya phalasya śubhā aśubhā vā saṃpattiḥ daivaśabdena kathyate । ajñavyavahārārtham iti śeṣaḥ ।।

pauruṣoparatā nityam iṣṭāniṣṭasya vastunaḥ ।
prāptir iṣṭāpy aniṣṭā vā daivaśabdena kathyate ।।

paṇḍitaiḥ pauruṣe uparatā niṣṭhāṃ gatā । iṣṭāniṣṭasya vastunaḥ iṣṭā aniṣṭā vā prāptiḥ daivaśabdena kathyate । apiśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ ।।

bhāvī tv avaśyam evārthaḥ puruṣārthaikasādhanaḥ ।
yaḥ so asmiṃl lokasaṃghāte daivaśabdena kathyate ।।

bhāvī bhavanaśīlaḥ । puruṣārthaḥ pauruṣam ekaṃ sādhanaṃ yasya । tādṛśaḥ । lokasaṃghāte lokasamūhe ।।

na tu rāghava lokasya kasyacit kiṃcid eva hi ।
daivam ākāśakalpaṃ hi karoti na karoti vā ।।

hi yasmādarthe । ākāśakalpam ākāśavad atyantatuccham । na hi vandhyāsutaḥ kasyacit kiṃcit karoti na karoti veti bhāvaḥ । dvitīyo hiśabdaḥ niścaye ।।

puruṣārthasya siddhasya śubhāśubhaphalodaye
idam itthaṃ sthitam iti yoktis tad daivam ucyate ।।

ukteḥ svarūpaṃ kathayati । idam itthaṃ sthitam itīti । siddham saṃpannam ।।

itthaṃ mamābhavad buddhir itthaṃ me niścayo hy abhūt ।
iti karmaphalāvāptau yoktis tad daivam ucyate ।।

itthaṃ karmaphalasādhanarūpā । karmaphalasyāvāptau prāptau । uktimātram eva daivam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

iṣṭāniṣṭaphalaprāptāv evam ityarthavācakam ।
āśvāsanāmātravaco daivam ity eva kathyate ।।

āśvāsanāmātravacaḥ kathaṃbhūtaṃ । tasya vācakam niyamavācakam ity arthaḥ ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati
bhagavan sarvadharmajña prāg yat karmopasaṃcitam । tad etad daivam ity uktam apamṛṣṭaṃ kathaṃ tvayā ।।

prāk pitrantargatabījatāvasthāyām ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ uttaraṃ kathayati

sādhu rāghava jānāsi śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te akhilam ।
daivaṃ nāstīti te yena sthirā buddhir bhaviṣyati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tad eva kathayati

yā magnā vāsanā pūrvaṃ babhūva kila bhūriśaḥ ।
saiveyaṃ karmabhāvena nṝṇāṃ pariṇatiṃ gatā ।।

pūrvam pitrantargatabījatāvasthāyām । bhūriśaḥ bhūriprakāreṇa । vartamānā yā vāsanā śubhāśubhā vā bhāvanā । bīje iti śeṣaḥ bhavati । sā eveyaṃ nṝṇāṃ karmabhāvena karmarūpeṇa । pariṇatiṃ rūpāntaraṃ । tadanurūpam eva sarve karma kurvantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

jantur yadvāsano nāma tatkarmā bhavati kṣaṇāt ।
anyakarmānyabhāvaś cety etan naivopapadyate ।।

anyabhāvaḥ anyavāsanā ।।

grāmago grāmam āpnoti pattanārthī ca pattanam ।
yo yo yadvāsanas tat tat sa sa prayatate tathā ।।

grāmagasya ca grāmagamanavāsanā sphuṭā evānyathā na yāyāt ।।

yad eva tīvrasaṃvegād iha karma kṛtaṃ purā ।
tad eva daivaśabdena paryāyeṇa hi kathyate ।।

iha ihalokaparalokatayā dvirūpe saṃsāre । purā pitrantargatabījatāvasthāyām । karmakaraṇaṃ cātra pitṛdvāreṇaiva jñeyam ।।

upasaṃhāraṃ karoti

evaṃ daivaṃ svakarmāṇi karma prauḍhā svavāsanā ।
vāsanā manaso nānyā mano hi puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

evam anena prakāreṇa । svakarmāṇi prāk kṛtāni nijakarmāṇi । daivaṃ bhavati । prauḍhā vāsanā karma bhavati । tadanusāreṇaiva tasya prakṛtatvāt । vāsanā manasaḥ anyā na bhavati । hi niścaye । manaḥ puruṣaḥ bhavati । ataḥ daivasya puruṣād vyatiriktā sattā nāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

punar apy etad eva kathayati

yad daivaṃ tāni karmāṇi karma sādho mano hi tat ।
mano hi puruṣas tasmād daivaṃ nāstīti niścayaḥ ।।

karmety atra yacchabdādhyāhāraḥ ।।

ekam eva mano jantor yathā prayatate hi yat ।
nūnaṃ tat tad avāpnoti svata eva na daivataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

manaś cittaṃ vāsanā ca karma daivaṃ svaniścayaḥ ।
rāma puṃniścayasyaitāḥ saṃjñāḥ sadbhir udāhṛtāḥ ।।

puṃniścayasya puṃrūpasya niścayasya ।।

evaṃnāmā hi puruṣo dṛḍhabhāvanayā yathā ।
nityaṃ prayatate rāma phalam āpnoty alaṃ tathā ।।

evaṃnāmā mana ityādināmayuktaḥ ।।

upasaṃhāraṃ karoti

evaṃ puruṣakāreṇa sarvam eva raghūdvaha ।
prāpyate netareṇeha tasmāt sa śubhado astu te ।।

saḥ puruṣakāraḥ । śubhado jīvanmuktākhyaśubhaphalapradaḥ । te ity upalakṣaṇam । tena sarveṣāṃ śubhaphalapradaḥ bhavatu ity arthaḥ ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

prāktanaṃ vāsanājālaṃ niyojayati māṃ yathā ।
mune tathaiva tiṣṭhāmi kṛpaṇaḥ kiṃ karomy aham ।।

ataḥ pauruṣaṃ kiṃcid api nāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ uttaraṃ kathayati

ata eva hi he rāma śreyaḥ prāpnoṣi śāśvatam ।
svaprayatnopanītena pauruṣeṇaiva nānyathā ।।

hi niścaye । ata eva pūrvoktāt kāraṇād eva । pauruṣeṇa kathaṃbhūtena । svaprayatnopanītena । rāhoḥ śira itivad ayaṃ prayogaḥ ।।

dvividho vāsanāvyūhaḥ śubhaś caivāśubhaś ca te ।
prāktano vidyate rāma dvayor ekataro atha vā ।।

vāsanāvyūhaḥ vāsanāsamūhaḥ । atha vā pakṣāntare । dvayoḥ madhye । ekataraḥ śubhaḥ aśubho vā asti ।।

vāsanaughena śuddhena tatra ced adya nīyase ।
tat krameṇa śubhenaiva padaṃ prāpnoṣi śāśvatam ।।

nīyase svānusāreṇa karma kāryase । padam mokṣākhyaṃ sthānaṃ ।।

atha ced aśubho bhāvas tvāṃ yojayati saṅkaṭe ।
prāktanas tad asau yatnāj jetavyo bhavatā balāt ।।

aśubho bhāvaḥ aśubhā vāsanā ।।

nanv anyaḥ cetanārūpaḥ kaścin māṃ prerayati । tat katham ahaṃ svayaṃ kiṃcit kartuṃ śaknomīty । atrāha

prājña cetanāmātras tvaṃ na dehas tvaṃ jaḍātmakaḥ ।
tad eva cetasy anyena cet tat tvaṃ kveva vidyase ।।

he prājña । asmiñ śloke vakṣyamāṇe upadeśe yogyatvam । cetanāmātraḥ asi tvam । tad eva cetanāmātram eva san । tvam anyena hetukartṛbhūtena kṛtvā । cetasi citikriyāṃ prati kartṛtvaṃ bhajasi । tvam na vidyase nāsi । na hi dvayoḥ sattā yuktā vyarthatvāt ।।

punar api pūrvaślokottarārdhaniścitam artham eva kathayati

anyas tvāṃ cetayati cet tat tvayy asati ko aparaḥ ।
kam imaṃ cetayet tasmād anavasthā na vāstavī ।।

anyaḥ tvām cet cetayati citikriyākartṛtvam prerayati । tvayi asati pūrvoktayuktyā sattām abhajati sati । sa iti kam imam kiṃrūpam । idantāspandaṃ tvāṃ । cetayet citikriyākartṛtvaṃ prati prerayet । na hy asataḥ preraṇaṃ yuktam iti bhāvaḥ । ataḥ anyaḥ kaścit preryaḥ kalpanīyaḥ । so api tvatsamānayogakṣema eveti kutrāpi preryatayā viśrāntir na syād । ataḥ tvam eva preryaprerakabhāvena sthito asīty abhiprāyeṇopasaṃhāraṃ karoti । anavasthā preryānavasthitiḥ । vāstavī paramārthabhūtā । na bhavati । tavaiva preryaprerakatvābhyāṃ sthitatvāt । ato na kaścit tavānyaḥ prerakaḥ astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

prakṛtam anusarati

śubhāśubhābhyāṃ mārgābhyāṃ vahantī vāsanāsarit ।
pauruṣeṇa prayatnena yojanīyā śubhe pathi ।।

yojanīyā pravartanīyā । bhogatyāgaparāmarśākhyaṃ śubhānusandhānam eva satataṃ kāryam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

aśubheṣu samāviṣṭaṃ śubheṣv evāvatārayet ।
svamanaḥ puruṣārthena balena balināṃ vara ।।

samāviṣṭam saṃlīnam ।।

aśubhāc calitaṃ yāti śubhaṃ tasmād apītarat ।
jantoś cittaṃ tu paśuvat tasmāt tat pālayed balāt ।।

aśubhāt bhogārjanaparāmarśarūpāt aśubhānusandhānāt । tasmād api śubhād api । pālayed aśubhāt rakṣet ।।

samatāsāntvanenāśu na drāg iti śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।
pauruṣeṇa prayatnena pālayec cittabālakam ।।

samatā sarvam idaṃ brahmety evaṃrūpā buddhiḥ । tayā yat sāntvanam samāśvāsanaṃ tena । na drāg iti na jhaṭiti । etasyārthaṃ svakaṇṭhena kathayati । śanaiḥ śanair iti samyagvicāreṇa । na tu prāṇarodhanādirūpeṇa haṭhenety arthaḥ ।।

vāsanaughas tvayā pūrvam abhyāsena ghanīkṛtaḥ ।
śubho vāpy aśubho rāma śubham adya ghanīkuru ।।

adya । madupadeśeneti śeṣaḥ ।।

prāgabhyāsavaśād yātā yadā te vāsanodayam ।
tadābhyāsasya sāphalyaṃ viddhi tvam arimardana ।।

abhyāsasya samastasyābhyāsasya ।।

idānīm api te yāti ghanatāṃ vāsanānagha ।
abhyāsavaśatas tasmāc chubhābhyāsam upāhara ।।

idānīm asmin janmani ।।

pūrvaṃ ced ghanatāṃ yātā nābhyāsāt tava vāsanā ।
vardhiṣyate tu nedānīm api tāta sukhī bhava ।।

vāsanārāhityamātrasyaiva parame pade yatatvāt iti bhāvaḥ ।।

saṃdigdhāyām api bhṛśaṃ śubham eva samāhara ।
asyāṃ tu vāsanāvṛddhau śubhād doṣo na kaścana ।।

asyāṃ vāsanāvṛddhau saṃdigdhāyām kim abhyāsād vardhate na veti sandehaviṣayāyām api satyāṃ । tvaṃ bhṛśaṃ śubham eva samāhara abhyāsaviṣayīkuru । yataḥ śubhāt kaścana doṣo na bhavati ।।

sandehasyāyuktatāṃ kathayati

yad yad abhyasyate loke tanmayenaiva bhūyate ।
ity ākumāraṃ prajñeṣu dṛṣṭaṃ sandehavarjitam ।।

loke saṃsāre ।।

śubhavāsanayā yuktas tad atra bhava bhūtaye ।
paraṃ pauruṣam āśritya vijityendriyapañcakam ।।

bhūtaye jīvanmuktākhyasaṃpatprāptaye ।।

avyutpannamanā yāvad bhavān ajñātatatpadaḥ ।
guruśāstrapramāṇais tu nirṇītaṃ tāvad ācara ।।

avyutpannamanāḥ jñānarahitaḥ । ata evājñātatatpadaḥ ajñātabrahmākhyotkṛṣṭasthānaḥ । nirṇītam tatpadanirṇayam । bhāve ktaprayoge nirṇītam iti siddham ।।

tataḥ kaṣāyapākena nūnaṃ vijñātavastunā ।
śubho apy asau tvayā tyājyo bhāvanaugho nirādhinā ।।

kaṣāyapākena lakṣaṇayā parakoṭiprāptyā । bhāvanaughaḥ nirṇayarūpaḥ vāsanāsamūhaḥ । nirādhinā śubhavāsanākhyacittapīḍārahitena ।।

sargāntaślokena śrīrāmasyāvasthānam anuṣṭheyatvenopadiśati

yad atisubhagam āryasevitaṃ tac chubham anusṛtya manojñabhāvabuddhyā ।
adhigamaya padaṃ sadāviśokaṃ tad anu tad apy avamucya sādhu tiṣṭha ।।

tvaṃ । yat atisubhagam ata evāryasevitam bhavati । tac chubhaṃ pauruṣam । manojñabhāvā śubhavāsanā yā matiḥ । tayā karaṇabhūtayā । anusṛtya satatānuṣṭhānaviṣayatāṃ nītvā । aviśokaṃ duḥkharahitaṃ । padaṃ jīvanmuktirūpaṃ sthānaṃ । adhigamaya prāpnuhi । tad api jīvanmuktipadam api avamucya । tiṣṭha videhamuktau sthirībhavety arthaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe navamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ paramam upasaṃhāraṃ karoti

ataḥ pauruṣam āśritya śreyase nityabāndhavam ।
ekāgraṃ kuru cittaṃ tvaṃ śṛṇu coktam idaṃ mama ।।

uktam upadeśam ।।

avāntarābhipātīni svārūḍhāni manoratham ।
pauruṣeṇendriyāṇy āśu saṃyamya samatāṃ naya ।।

avāntareṣu bhogarūpeṣu madhyameṣu viśrāntisthāneṣu । na tu paramātmarūpe parame viśrāntisthāne । abhipātīni patanaśīlāni । manorathaṃ cittānusandhānam । svārūḍhāni suṣṭhu ārūḍhāni । indriyāṇi saṃyamya pratyāhṛtya । samatāṃ rāgadveṣarahitatvam naya । anyathā na śroṣyasīti bhāvaḥ ।।

ihāmutra ca siddhyarthaṃ puruṣārthaphalapradām ।
mokṣopāyamayīṃ vakṣye saṃhitāṃ sārasammitām ।।

mokṣopāyamayīṃ mokṣasya yaḥ upāyaḥ tanmayīm tadvācakām ity arthaḥ । sārasammitām sāratulyām ।।

apunargrahaṇāyāntas tyaktvā saṃsāravāsanām ।
saṃpūrṇau śamasantoṣāv ādāyodārayā dhiyā ।।

sapūrvāparavākyārthavicāraviṣayādṛtam ।
manaḥ samarasaṃ kṛtvā sānusandhānam ātmani ।।

sukhaduḥkhakṣayakaraṃ mahānandaikasādhanam ।
mokṣopāyam imaṃ rāma vakṣyamāṇaṃ mayā śṛṇu ।।

he rāma । tvaṃ mayā vakṣyamāṇaṃ mokṣopāyaṃ śṛṇu । kiṃ kṛtvā । apunargrahaṇāyetyādi । suṣuptau tyaktām api vāsanāṃ puruṣaḥ punaḥ gṛhṇātīti apunargrahaṇāyety uktam । anyathā na śrotuṃ śaknoṣīti bhāvaḥ । manaḥ kathaṃbhūtaṃ । ātmani samarasam ekarasam । na tu viṣayeṣu vikṣiptaṃ । tathā sapūrvāparaḥ saṃpūrṇaḥ yaḥ vākyārthavicāraḥ । sa eva viṣayaḥ saṃcārasthānam ।।

imāṃ mokṣakathāṃ śrutvā saha sarvair vivekibhiḥ ।
padaṃ yāsyasi nirduḥkhaṃ nāśo yatra na vidyate ।।

padam viśrāntisthānam ।।

evaṃ śrīrāmasya pauruṣam āśrayaṇīyatvenopadiśya viśvāmitrapreraṇayā smṛtaṃ brahmoktam upadeśaṃ kathayituṃ prastāvaṃ karoti

idam uktaṃ purākalpe brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā ।
sarvaduḥkhakṣayakaraṃ paramāśvāsanaṃ dhiyaḥ ।।

idaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ । paramāśvāsanam utkṛṣṭaṃ āśvāsanakāri ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

kenoktaṃ kāraṇenedaṃ brahman pūrvaṃ svayaṃbhuvā ।
kathaṃ ca bhavatā prāptam etat kathaya me prabho ।।

idaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ jñānam ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ uttaraṃ kathayati

asty anantavilāsātmā sarvagaḥ sarvasaṃśrayaḥ ।
cidākāśo avināśātmā pradīpaḥ sarvavastuṣu ।।

cidākāśaḥ cid iti nāmadheyaḥ ākāśaḥ cidākāśaḥ । saḥ asti paramārthasan bhavati । kathaṃbhūtaḥ । anantāḥ aparicchinnāḥ । ye vilāsāḥ sargāvabhāsanasaṃkocanarūpāḥ vilāsāḥ te । ātmā svarūpaṃ yasya saḥ । tathā sarvagaḥ sarvavyāpakatvāt upacāreṇa sarvagantā । na hi mukhyaṃ sarvagatvam asya saṃbhavati niṣkriyatvena gamikriyānāśrayatvāt । punaḥ kathaṃbhūtaḥ । sarveṣām samastānāṃ bhāvābhāvasvarūpāṇāṃ padārthānāṃ । saṃśrayaḥ sphūrtipradatvena sattāpradatvena cāśrayaḥ । punaḥ kathaṃbhūtaḥ । avināśātmā vināśasyāpi sākṣitayā sattāpradatvena ca tena rahitaḥ ātmā yasya saḥ । na hi svasphūrtipradasya svasattāpādakasya ca kaścit āvaraṇaṃ kartuṃ śaktaḥ tadāvṛtau svasyāpy asiddhatvāt । punaḥ kathaṃbhūtaḥ । sarvavastuṣu pradīpaḥ prakāśakatvāt । nanu kutrāsāv astīti cen । sarvatra vartamānasya kutreti vaktum aśakyatvāt । nanu tathāpi kathaṃ nāsau sarvatra dṛśyate iti ced । draṣṭrekasvarūpe tasmin kathaṃ na dṛśyata ity asyāpi vaktum aśakyatvāt । tathāpi ko asāv iti cet । yaḥ pṛcchati sa eveti brūmaḥ । nanu kaḥ pṛcchati iti cet । ahantayā atiprākaṭyena bhāsamānaḥ saḥ svayam eva svāntaḥ vicāryatām ity alaṃ rahasyodghāṭanena ।।

tataḥ kim ity । atrāha

spandāspandasamākārāt tato viṣṇur ajāyata ।
spandamānarasāpūrāt taraṅgaḥ sāgarād iva ।।

spandāspandayoḥ sṛṣṭyāveśaudāsīnyayoḥ samākārāt cittvākhyasamānākārayuktāt । tataḥ tasmāc cidākāśāt । viṣṇuḥ bhāvisṛṣṭisthitikārī nārāyaṇākhyo devatāviśeṣaḥ । samaṣṭirūpaṃ śuddhabuddhitattvaṃ cājāyata । saṃhārakāraṇasya śuddhāhaṅkārarūpasya rudrasya kathanaṃ sṛṣṭimātrakathanākāṅkṣayā na kṛtam । yathā spandamānarasāpūrāt sāgarāt taraṅgaḥ jāyate tathety arthaḥ ।।

sumerukarṇikāt tasya digdalād dhṛdayāmbujāt ।
tārakākesaravataḥ parameṣṭhī vyajāyata ।।

tasya nārāyaṇasya śuddhabuddhitattvasya ca । sumerukarṇikāt tathā tārakākesarāt hṛdayāmbujāt hṛtkamalāt tadantargatāt brahmāṇḍāt iti yāvat । bhāvisarvajagadādhāratvayogyāt svarūpaleśāc ca । parameṣṭhī bhāvisṛṣṭyutpattikārī brahmākhyo devatāviśeṣaḥ । samaṣṭirūpaṃ śuddhamanastattvaṃ ca vyajāyata ।।

vedavedārthadeveśamunimaṇḍalamālitam ।
so asṛjat sakalaṃ sargaṃ vikalpaughaṃ yathā manaḥ ।।

sakalaṃ jagat bāhyatvena bhāsamānaṃ samastaṃ jagat । samaṣṭibhūtaśuddhamanastattvarūpāt । parameṣṭhina eva hi sarvaṃ jagad utpannam । atropamānatvaṃ vyaṣṭirūpasya manasaḥ jñeyam । samaṣṭirūpasya manasaḥ upameyatvāt ।।

jambudvīpasya koṇe asmin varṣe bhāratanāmani ।
sa sasarja janaṃ putrair ādhivyādhipariplutam ।।

janam mānavajanam । putraiḥ prajāpatibhiḥ kṛtvā sāmānyajanaiś ca ।।

janaṃ viśinaṣṭi

bhāvābhāvaviṣaṇṇāṅgam utpātadhvaṃsatatparam ।
sarge asmin bhūtajātīnām āpyāyanakaraṃ param ।।

bhūtajātīnāṃ devādīnām । āpyāyanakaram havyakavyādidvāreṇa tṛptikaram ।।

janasya tasya duḥkhaṃ sad dṛṣṭvā sakalalokakṛt ।
jagāma karuṇām īśaḥ putraduḥkhād yathā pitā ।।

tasya janasya mānavajanasya । īśaḥ brahmā śuddhamanastattvaṃ ca । karuṇāṃ dayām । atra ca śuddhamanasaḥ karuṇā sṛjyamānasmṛtikāracittāveśadvāreṇa jñeyety alaṃ rahasyodghāṭanena ।।

nanu tataḥ kim akarod ity । atrāha

ka eteṣāṃ hatāśānāṃ duḥkhasyānto hatāyuṣām ।
syād iti kṣaṇam ekāgraś cintayām āsa bhūtapaḥ ।।

hatāśānāṃ naṣṭānāṃ । hatāyuṣāṃ naśvarāṇāṃ । antaḥ avasānaṃ ।।

brahmaṇaḥ cintām upasaṃharati

iti saṃcintya bhagavān sasarja punar īśvaraḥ ।
tapo dharmaṃ ca dānaṃ ca satyaṃ tīrthāni caiva ha ।।

sasarja svayaṃ । kṛteṣu smṛtiśāstreṣu janān prati kartavyatvena dṛṣṭavān ity arthaḥ ।।

etat sṛṣṭvā punar devaś cintayām āsa bhūtakṛt ।
puṃsāṃ nānena sarvasya duḥkhasyānta iti svayam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

punaḥ kena puṃsāṃ sarvasya duḥkhasyāntaḥ bhaviṣyatīty āśaṅkya cintayati

nirvāṇaṃ nāma paramaṃ sukhaṃ yena punar janaḥ ।
na jāyate na mriyate taj jñānād eva labhyate ।।

tan nirvāṇaṃ kena syād ity āśaṅkya cintayati । jñānāt eva paramātmatattvajñānāt eva । na tu tapaḥprabhṛtibhyaḥ labhyate ।।

evakāraprayogayogyatāṃ svayam eva sādhayati

saṃsārottaraṇe jantor upāyo jñānam eva hi ।
tapo dānaṃ tathā tīrtham aṇūpāyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।

aṇūpāyaḥ avāntaropāyaḥ ।।

tarhi janānāṃ jñānaṃ kathaṃ setsyatīty āśaṅkya cintayati

tat tāvad duḥkhamokṣārthaṃ janasyāsya mahātmanaḥ ।
pratyagraṃ taruṇopāyam āśu prakaṭayāmy aham ।।

iyaṃ cintā tu utpādayiṣyamāṇajñānopadeśakāracintāveśadvāreṇa jñeyā ।।

parameṣṭhicintām upasaṃharati

iti saṃcintya bhagavān brahmā kamalasaṃbhavaḥ ।
manasā parisaṃkalpya mām utpāditavān imam ।।

mām proktasvacintodbhavasthānabhūtānām upadeśakārāṇāṃ madhye mukhyabhūtaṃ tvādṛśajanajñānotpādanasamarthaṃ mokṣopāyākhyaśāstropadeśakaṃ vasiṣṭhākhyaṃ mām । manaseti rāhoḥ śira itivat prayogaḥ ।।

nanu kenopādānakāraṇena tvam utpanna ity । atrāha

kuto apy utpanna evāśu tato ahaṃ samupasthitaḥ ।
pitus tasya puraḥ śīghram ūrmir ūrmer ivānagha ।।

kuto api anirvācyāt kasmāccid upādānakāraṇāt । tataḥ tasya pituḥ puraḥ śīghram upasthitaḥ prāptaḥ । ūrmir ūrmer iva paramārthavicāre sarveṣām utpattir adṛśyeveti sāmānyotpattir evātroktety alaṃ rahasyodghāṭanena ।।

kīdṛśaḥ tvam upasthitaḥ kiṃ ca kṛtavān ity । atrāha

kamaṇḍaludharo nāthaḥ sakamaṇḍalunā mayā ।
sākṣamālaḥ sākṣamālaṃ sa praṇamyābhivāditaḥ ।।

sākṣamālam iti pūrvakālakriyāviśeṣaṇam । etena svasya dhyānam uktam ।।

tataḥ tava tena kim uktaṃ kṛtaṃ cety । atrāha

ehi putreti mām uktvā sa svābjasyottare dale ।
śukle abhra iva śītāṃśuṃ yojayām āsa pāṇinā ।।

atra śuddhamanaḥsparśaḥ mayi jātaḥ iti bhaṅgyā uktam ।।

mṛgakṛttiparīdhāno mṛgakṛttinijāmbaram ।
mām uvāca pitā brahmā sa haṃsaḥ sārasaṃ yathā ।।

mām vasiṣṭhākhyaṃ mām । vacanaṃ cātrāntaraḥ parāmarśaḥ jñeyaḥ ।।

kim uvācety । atrāha

muhūrtamātraṃ te putra ceto vānaracañcalam ।
ajñānam abhyāviśatu śaśaḥ śaśadharaṃ yathā ।।

āntarabhāvena sthitaśuddhacittavaśenaiva hi sarveṣām ajñānitvaṃ jñānitvaṃ ca bhavati । etena prathamaṃ svasya jñānitvaṃ dyotitam ।।

brahmavacanam upasaṃharati

iti tenāśu śaptaḥ san vicārasamanantaram ।
ahaṃ vismṛtavān sarvaṃ svarūpam amalaṃ dvijaḥ ।।

ahaṃ dvijaḥ vasiṣṭhākhyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ । vismṛtavān vyasmārṣam iti sambandhaḥ ।।

athāhaṃ dīnatāṃ yātaḥ sthito asaṃbuddhayā dhiyā ।
duḥkhaśokābhisaṃtapto jāto jana ivādhamaḥ ।।

asaṃbuddhayā niścayarahitayā ।।

kaṣṭaṃ saṃsāranāmāyaṃ doṣaḥ katham ivāgataḥ ।
iti cintitavān antas tūṣṇīm eva vyavasthitaḥ ।।

aham iti cintitavān iti saṃbandhaḥ । etena ajñānitvānantaram svasya vairāgyaprādurbhāvaḥ sūcitaḥ ।।

athābhyadhāt sa māṃ tātaḥ putra kiṃ duḥkhavān asi ।
duḥkhopaghātaṃ māṃ pṛccha sukhī nityaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।।

athābhyadhāt uktavān । etena vairāgyānantaram mama jñānaṃ prati aunmukhyaṃ jātam iti sūcitam ।।

nanu tatas tvayā kiṃ kṛtam ity । atrāha

tataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sa bhagavān mayā sakalalokakṛt ।
hemapadmadalasthena saṃsāravyādhibheṣajam ।।

etena mayā svayam eva vimarṣaḥ kṛta iti sūcitam ।।

nanu tvayāsau kiṃ pṛṣṭas tena ca kim uktaṃ ity । atrāha

kathaṃ nātha mahad duḥkham ayaṃ saṃsāra āgataḥ ।
kathaṃ ca kṣīyate jantor iti pṛṣṭena tena me ।।

taj jñānaṃ subahu proktaṃ yaj jñātvā pāvanaṃ param ।
ahaṃ pitur api prāyaḥ kilādhika iva sthitaḥ ।।

pituḥ ādhikyam śuddhamanastattvātilaṅghanena prāptā cinmātratā jñeyā । etena svasya svataḥsiddhatvam uktam । trividhā hi siddhāḥ uttarottaram utkarṣavantaḥ santi । gurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svata iti ।।

tato viditavedyaṃ māṃ nijaprakṛtim āsthitam ।
sa uvāca jagatkartā vaktā sakalakāraṇam ।।

mayi idaṃ sphuritam ity āntaro abhiprāyaḥ ।।

kim uvācety । atrāha

śāpenājñapadaṃ nītvā pṛcchakas tvaṃ mayā kṛtaḥ ।
putrāsya jñānasārasya samastajanasiddhaye ।।

mama madhye evedam ajñatvaṃ prādurbhūtam āsīt iti mama sphuritam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

punaḥ kim uvācety । atrāha

idānīṃ śāntaśāpas tvaṃ paraṃ bodham upāgataḥ ।
saṃsthito aham ivaikātmā kanakaṃ kanakād iva ।।

idānīm ahaṃ jñānī jāta ity api mama sphuritam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tato api punaḥ kim uvācety । atrāha

gacchedānīṃ mahāpīṭhe jambudvīpāntarasthitam ।
sādho bhāratavarṣaṃ tvaṃ lokānugrahahetunā ।।

spaṣṭaṃ ।।

tatra kriyākāṇḍaparās tvayā putra mahādhiyaḥ ।
upadeśyāḥ kriyākāṇḍakrameṇa kramaśālinaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

viraktacittāś ca tathā mahāprājñā virāgiṇaḥ ।
upadeśyās tvayā sādho jñānenānandadāyinā ।।

tataḥ ahaṃ vairāgyarahitānāṃ karmakāṇḍadvāreṇopadeśaṃ karomi । viraktānāṃ tu jñānakāṇḍadvāreṇety api sphuritam । anyathā tvadupadeśe apy ahaṃ na pravarteyam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

brahmavākyam upasaṃharati

iti tena niyukto ahaṃ pitrā kamalayoninā ।
iha rāghava tiṣṭhāmi yāvad bhūtaparaṃparā ।।

yāvad bhūtaparaṃparety upadeṣṭṛbhūtajñānisāmānyenoktam svasya cirajīvitvena vā । bāhya arthas tu sphuṭatayā na pratipadam uktaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokenaitat samāpayati

kartavyam asti mama neha hi kiṃcid eva sthātavyam ity abhimanā bhuvi saṃsthito asmi ।
saṃśāntayā satatasuptadhiyeva vṛttyā kāryaṃ karomi na ca kiṃcid ahaṃ karomi ।।

hi niścaye । mama samastajñānisantānasya vasiṣṭhākhyasya ca । iha loke । kiṃcit eva kartavyaṃ nāsti paramātmatattvaprāptyā kṛtakṛtyatvāt । tathāpi aham bhuvi bhūmau । sthātavyam mayā ihāvaśyaṃ । niyatyanurodhena sthātavyam iti evam abhimanāḥ abhiniviṣṭamanāḥ niścitamanā iti yāvat । ahaṃ saṃśāntayā lābhālābhānusandhānarūpakṣobharahitayā vṛttyā vā । pāreṇa kāryam śarīrayātrānimittaṃ karma । akaraṇe pratyavāyanimittaṃ nityaṃ karma ca karomi । satatasuptā yā dhīḥ । tayā ivātyantaśāntayety arthaḥ । tathāpi ahaṃ kiṃcid api na ca karomi nāhaṃ karteti niścayānubhāvād ity arthaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe daśamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

pūrvasargoktasyopasaṃhārakāṅkṣayā parāmarśaṃ karoti

etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ jñānāvataraṇaṃ bhuvi ।
mayā svam īhitaṃ caiva kamalodbhavakalpitam ।।

svam īhitam nijaceṣṭitam । kamalodbhavena brahmaṇā śuddhamanastattvena ca । kalpitam āvirbhāvitaṃ iti । anena prakāreṇaiveha jñānam ihāvatīrṇam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tad idaṃ paramaṃ jñānaṃ śrotum adya tavānagha ।
bhṛśam utkaṇṭhitaṃ ceto mahataḥ sukṛtodayāt ।।

tat brahmaṇā uktam ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

kathaṃ brahman bhagavato loke jñānāvatāraṇe ।
sargād anantaraṃ buddhiḥ pravṛttā parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।

kathaṃ kimarthaṃ ity arthaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ uttaraṃ kathayati

parame brahmaṇi brahmā svabhāvavaśataḥ svayam ।
jātaḥ spandamayo nityam ūrmir ambunidhāv iva ।।

parame utkṛṣṭacinmātrasvarūpe । spandamayaḥ parimitāhaṃparāmarśamayaḥ ।।

sṛṣṭvaivam ātataṃ sargaṃ sargasya sakalā gatīḥ ।
bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyatsthā dadarśa parameśvaraḥ ।।

dadarśa । jñānanetreṇeti śeṣaḥ ।।

satkriyākramakālasya kṛtādeḥ kṣaya āgate ।
moham ālokya lokānāṃ kāruṇyam agamat prabhuḥ ।।

moham bhaviṣyantam ity arthaḥ ।।

tato mām īśvaraḥ sṛṣṭvā jñānenāyojya cāsakṛt ।
visasarja mahīpīṭhe lokasyājñānaśāntaye ।।

mām vasiṣṭhākhyaṃ mām । jñānena paramātmajñānena । āyojya saṃyojya ।।

yathāhaṃ prahitas tena tathānye api maharṣayaḥ ।
sanatkumārapramukhā nāradādyāś ca bhūriśaḥ ।।

etena ye bhūtā bhaviṣyantaś copadeṣṭāraḥ santi tatrāpīyam eva rītir astīti sūcitam ।।

kriyākrameṇa puṇyena tathā jñānakrameṇa ca ।
manomahāmayottabdham uddhartuṃ lokam īritāḥ ।।

īritāḥ visarjitāḥ । lokam adhikāribhedāt kriyākrameṇa jñānakrameṇa ca uddhartum । lokaṃ kathaṃbhūtam । mana eva mahāmayaḥ mahārogaḥ । tenottabdham baddham ।।

maharṣibhis tatas tais tu kṣīṇe kṛtayuge purā ।
kramāt kriyākrame śuddhe pṛthivyāṃ tanutāṃ gate ।।

kriyākramavidhānārthaṃ maryādāniyamāya ca । pṛthagdeśavibhāgena bhūpālāḥ parikalpitāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bahūni smṛtiśāstrāṇi yajñaśāstrāṇi cāvanau ।
dharmakāmārthe siddhyarthaṃ kalpitāny uditāny atha ।।

parikalpitāni kṛtāni । maharṣibhir iti śeṣaḥ । yal lokaiḥ teṣām upadeśaḥ na śruta iti bhāvaḥ । athaśabdaḥ uttaraślokena saṃbandhanīyaḥ ।।

kālacakre vahaty asmiṃs tato vigalite krame ।
pratyahaṃ bhojanapare jane śālyarjanonmukhe ।।

dvandvāni saṃpravṛttāni viṣayārthaṃ mahībhujām ।
daṇḍyatāṃ saṃprayātāni bhūtāni bhuvi bhūriśaḥ ।।

dvandvāni dvandvayuddhāni । viṣayārtham deśārtham । daṇḍyatāṃ daṇḍayogyatām । paradāragamanādipāpakaraṇāt iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tato yuddhaṃ vinā bhūpā mahīṃ pālayituṃ kramāt ।
asamarthās tad āyātāḥ prajābhiḥ saha dīnatām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

teṣāṃ dainyāpanodārthaṃ samyaksṛṣṭikramāya ca ।
tato asmadādibhiḥ proktā mahatyo jñānadṛṣṭayaḥ ।।

teṣām rājñām ।।

adhyātmavidyā teneyaṃ pūrvaṃ rājasu varṇitā ।
tad anu prasṛtā loke rājavidyety udāhṛtā ।।

rājavidyā rājaguhyam ityādinā gītādau rājavidyāśabdena vyavahārāt iti bhāvaḥ ।।

rājavidyā rājaguhyam adhyātmagrantham uttamam ।
jñātvā rāghava rājānaḥ parāṃ nirduḥkhatāṃ gatāḥ ।।rājaguhyam iti adhyātmavidyāyāḥ aparaṃ nāma ।।

atha rājasv atīteṣu bahuṣv amalakīrtiṣu ।
asmād daśarathād rāma jāto adya tvam ihāvanau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tava cātiprasanne asmiñ jātaṃ manasi pāvanam ।
nirnimittam idaṃ cāru vairāgyam arimardana ।।

nirnimittam bībhatsādirūpaṃ nimittaṃ vinā ।।

nanu nirnimittavairāgyena ko atiśayaḥ mamāstīty । atrāha

sarvasyaiva hi bhavyasya sādhor api vivekinaḥ ।
nimittapūrvaṃ vairāgyaṃ jāyate rāma rājasam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

idaṃ tv apūrvam utpannaṃ camatkārakaraṃ satām ।
tavānimittaṃ vairāgyaṃ sāttvikaṃ svavivekajam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bībhatsaṃ viṣamaṃ dṛṣṭvā ko nāma na virajyate ।
satāṃ tūttamavairāgyaṃ vivekād eva jāyate ।।

bībhatsam bībhatsarasālambanam dravyam ।।

te mahānto mahāprajñā nimittena vinaiva hi ।
vairāgyaṃ jāyate yeṣāṃ ta evāmalamānasāḥ ।।

amalamānasatvaṃ vinā hi nirnimittaṃ vairāgyaṃ notpadyate iti bhāvaḥ ।।

svavivekacamatkāraparāmarśaviraktayā ।
rājate hi dhiyā jantur yuveva vanamālayā ।।

svavivekasya yaḥ camatkāraḥ । tasya yaḥ parāmarśaḥ । tena viraktayā bāhyapadārtharāgarahitayā । na tu bībhatsena viraktayā ।।

parāmṛśya vivekena saṃsāraracanām imām ।
virāgaṃ ye adhigacchanti ta eva puruṣottamāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

svavivekavaśād eva vicāryedaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।
indrajālaṃ parityājyaṃ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ balāt ।।

indrajālam saṃsārākhyam indrajālam । parityājyam samantāt tyāgaviṣayatāṃ neyam ।।

śmaśānam āpadaṃ dainyaṃ dṛṣṭvā ko na virajyate ।
tad vairāgyaṃ paraṃ śreyaḥ svato yad abhijāyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

akṛtrimavirāgas tvaṃ mahattām alam āgataḥ ।
yogyo asi jñānasārasya bījasyeva mṛdusthalam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

prasādāt parameśasya nāthasya paramātmanaḥ ।
tvādṛśasya śubhā buddhir vivekam anudhāvati ।।

na tv atrātmaprayatnaḥ kaścit prabhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

kriyākrameṇa mahatā tapasā niyamena ca ।
dānena tīrthayātrābhiś cirakālavivekataḥ ।।

duṣkṛte kṣayam āpanne paramārthavicāraṇe ।
kākatālīyayogena buddhir jantoḥ pravartate ।।

kākatālīyayogenety anena kriyākramādeḥ śaithilyaṃ sūcitam । kākatālīyena paramātmavicāraṇanimittabuddhiyogaḥ । tāvat tu kriyākramādir avaśyam anuṣṭheyaḥ । tasyāpi leśataḥ taṃ praty upāyatvāt । na ca tatraiva maṅktavyam । sadgurūpāsāder anyasya mukhyasyopāyasyāpi sattvāt ity alam ।।

kriyāparās tāvad alaṃ cakrāvṛttibhir ādṛtāḥ ।
bhramantīha janā yāvan na paśyanti paraṃ padam ।।

kriyāparāḥ kriyām evopāyatvena manyamānāḥ । param padam cinmātrākhyam utkṛṣṭaṃ sthānam । cakrāvṛttibhiḥ kriyāparāḥ paunaḥpunyena sakriyāratā ity arthaḥ ।।

yathābhūtam imaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃsāraṃ tanmayīṃ dhiyam ।
parityajya paraṃ yānti nirālānā gajā iva ।।

yathābhūtam dṛṣṭvā yathāsti tathā dṛṣṭvā । tanmayīṃ saṃsāramayīm । param uttīrṇam śuddhacinmātratattvam । yānti tadrūpaṃ svātmānam anubhavanti ।।

viṣameyam anantehā rāma saṃsārasaṃsṛtiḥ ।
dehamuktā mahātantur vinā jñānaṃ na naśyati ।।

anantāḥ īhāḥ bhāvābhāvarūpāḥ ceṣṭāḥ yasyāḥ । tādṛśī saṃsārasaṃsṛtiḥ saṃsārasaraṇiḥ । dehamuktā nāma mahātantuḥ dehamuktā mahātantuḥ । jñānam cinmātratattvajñānam ।।

jñānayuktiplavenaiva saṃsārābdhiṃ sudustaram ।
mahādhiyaḥ samuttīrṇā netareṇa raghūdvaha ।।

jñānarūpā yā yuktiḥ upāyaḥ ।।

tām imāṃ jñānayuktiṃ tvaṃ saṃsārāṃbhodhitāriṇīm ।
śṛṇuṣvāvahito buddhyā nityāvahitayānayā ।।

avahitayā buddhyā vinā śrotuṃ na śaknoṣīti bhāvaḥ ।।

yasmād anantasaṃrambhā jagato duḥkharītayaḥ ।
cirāyāntar dahanty etā vinā yuktim anindita ।।

yuktim jñānākhyāṃ yuktim ।।

śītavātātapādīni dvandvaduḥkhāni rāghava ।
jñānayuktiṃ vinā kena sahyatāṃ yānti sādhuṣu ।।
