kena kenānyenopāyena । na kenāpīty arthaḥ । atra tu bālavṛddhayoḥ maricabhakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭāntatvena yojyam ।।

āpatanti pratipadaṃ yathākālaṃ dahanti ca ।
duḥkhacintā naraṃ mūḍhaṃ tṛṇam agniśikhā iva ।।

duḥkhadāyinyaḥ cintāḥ duḥkhacintāḥ । tāś ca bhogaviṣayāḥ jñeyāḥ ।।

prājñaṃ vijñātavijñānaṃ samyagdarśinam ādhayaḥ ।
na dahanti vanaṃ varṣadabdam agniśikhā iva ।।

prājñaṃ kathaṃbhūtam । vijñātam anubhūtam । vijñānaṃ vijñānarūpam ātmatattvaṃ yena tam । vanaṃ kathambhūtam । varṣantaḥ abdāḥ meghāḥ yasya tat ।।

ādhivyādhiparāvarte saṃsāramarumārute ।
kṣubhite api na tattvajño bhajyate kalpavṛkṣavat ।।

ādhivyādhyoḥ parāvartaḥ paunaḥpunyenāvṛttiḥ yasmin । tādṛśe kṣubhite bhāvābhāvākhyaḥ kṣobhayukte । na bhajyate harṣaśokavaśaṃ na yāti । saṃsāramarumārute kṣubhite satīti yojyam । kalpavṛkṣo api mārute kṣubhite sati na bhajyate ।।

tattvaṃ jñātum ato yatnād dhīmān eva hi dhīmatā ।
prāmāṇikaḥ prabuddhātmā praṣṭavyaḥ praṇayānvitaṃ ।।

prāmāṇikaḥ pramāṇavaktā । ātmā cinmātrarūpaḥ paramātmā yena । praṇayānvitam yācñāsahitam । etadvyatiriktas tu pṛṣṭaḥ viruddham eva kiṃcid brūyād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

prāmāṇikasya pṛṣṭasya vaktur uttamacetasā ।
yatnena vacanaṃ grāhyam aṃśukeneva kuṅkumam ।।

yatnenāvadhānena ।।

atattvajñam anādeyavacanaṃ vāgvidāṃ vara ।
yaḥ pṛcchati naraṃ tasmān nāsti mūḍhataro aparaḥ ।।

na tattvaṃ jānātīti tādṛśam । dehādāv ātmābhimāninam ity arthaḥ ।।

prāmāṇikasya tajjñasya vaktuḥ pṛṣṭasya yatnataḥ ।
nānutiṣṭhati yo vākyaṃ nānyas tasmān narādhamaḥ ।।

vākyaṃ nānutiṣṭhati taduktavākyavācyam arthaṃ na saṃpādayati ।।

tajjñatātajjñate pūrvaṃ vaktur nirṇīya kāryataḥ ।
yaḥ karoti naraḥ praśnaṃ pṛcchakaḥ sa mahāmatiḥ ।।

kāryataḥ na tu vacanamātrāt । vacanamātreṇa hi bahavaḥ brahmajñāninam ātmānam darśayanti ।।

anirṇīya pravaktāraṃ bālaḥ praśnaṃ karoti yaḥ ।
adhamaḥ pṛcchakaḥ sa syān na mahārthasya bhājanam ।।

bālaḥ bālavat mūḍhaḥ । mahārthasya mokṣākhyasya paramaprayojanasya ।।

pūrvāparasamādhānakṣamabuddhāv anindite ।
pṛṣṭaṃ prājñena vaktavyaṃ nādhame paśudharmiṇi ।।

prājñena buddhimatā guruṇā । pṛṣṭaṃ praśnaviṣayīkṛtaṃ vastu । anindite । tathā pūrvāparayoḥ pūrvāparavākyabhāgārthayoḥ । yat samādhānam anyo'nyaviruddhatāpanayanam । tatra kṣamā buddhiḥ yasya । tādṛśe praṣṭari vaktavyam । adhame ata eva paśudharmiṇi mūḍhatayā paśusadṛśe praṣṭari । na vaktavyam vyarthatvāt ।।

prāmāṇikārthayogyatvaṃ pṛcchakasyāvicārya vā ।
yo vakti tam iha prājñāḥ prāhur mūḍhatamaṃ naram ।।

pṛcchakasya mūḍhataratvāt asya mūḍhatamatvam । bahūnāṃ jātiparipraśne hi mūḍhatamaḥ । pṛcchakād api mūḍhaḥ asau kiṃ brūyād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tvam atīva guṇādhāraḥ pṛcchako raghunandana ।
ahaṃ ca vaktuṃ jānāmi sa ca yogo ayam āvayoḥ ।।

saḥ tava guṇādhārapṛcchakatvam mama tādṛk vaktṛtvam iti yogaḥ sadṛśasaṃbandhaḥ ।।

yad ahaṃ vacmi tad yatnāt tvayā śabdārthakovida ।
etad vastv iti nirṇīya hṛdi kāryam akhaṇḍitaṃ ।।

nirṇayasvarūpaṃ kathayati । etat śrīvasiṣṭhoktaṃ vastu । paramārthasatyam bhavati । pūrvaṃ bhaktimātreṇaiva madvacanaṃ satyatayā grāhyaṃ । tataḥ tatsatyatā svayam eva prakaṭībhaviṣyati । anyathāraṃbhamātre eva svavikalpakṛtābhiḥ sūkṣmekṣikābhiḥ tava kiṃcid api na setsyatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu yadi tvaduktaṃmayi na lagati tadā kiṃ kāryam ity । atrāha

mahān asi virakto asi tajjño asi janatāsthitau ।
tvayi vastu lagaty antaḥ kuṅkumāmbu yathāṃśuke ।।

yataḥ tvam mahān na tu nīcaḥ asi । nīco hi nīcatayā svalpenāpi kṣubhyati । tathā viraktaḥ saṃsārikapadārtheṣu viraktaḥ asi । anyathā hi padārthāviṣṭabuddheḥ te yogyatā na syāt । tathā janatāyāḥ sthitau racanāyāṃ । tajjñaḥ nipuṇaḥ asi । anyathā hi taddṛṣṭāntānusāreṇa proktaḥ upadeśaḥ tvayi na laget । ataḥ vastu maduktaparamārthatattvaṃ । tvayi lagati । yathā tat aṃśuke lagati tathety arthaḥ ।।

uktāvadhānaparamā paramārthavivecinī ।
viśaty arthaṃ tava prajñā jalamadhyam ivārkabhā ।।

ukte madukte । tad eva paramam grāhyatvenotkṛṣṭaṃ yasyāḥ । tathā paramārthasya maduktavākyāntarārthasya । vivecinī tava prajñā artham madvākyārthaṃ । viśati vartamānasamīpe vartamānā । atra dṛṣṭāntam āha । jaleti ।।

yad yad vacmi tavādeyaṃ hṛdi kāryaṃ prayatnataḥ ।
na cet praṣṭavya evāhaṃ na tvayeha nirarthakam ।।

ādeyaṃ ādānārham tat tad ity adhyāhāryam ।।

nanu tvadvākyahṛtkaraṇe kaḥ prayāsaḥ asti yenaivaṃ bravīṣīty । atrāha

mano hi capalaṃ rāma saṃsāravanamarkaṭam ।
saṃrodhya hṛdi yatnena śrotavyā paramārthagīḥ ।।

hi yasmāt । manonirodhe avaśyaṃ prayāsaḥ । taṃ vinā ca madvākyahṛtkaraṇaṃ na saṃbhavati । ato asty eva madvākyahṛtkaraṇe prayāsa iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu svakīyaṃ bāndhavajanaṃ tyaktvā kathaṃ tvadvākyamātraparo bhaveyam ity । atrāha

avivekinam ajñānam asajjanaratiṃ janam ।
ciraṃ dūrataraṃ kṛtvā pūjanīyā hi sādhavaḥ ।।

avidyamānam jñānaṃ yasya tam ajñānam । asajjanebhyaḥ viratiḥ sajjaneṣu ratiś ca prathamaṃ mokṣasādhanam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu sādhupūjanena mama kiṃ setsyatīty । atrāha

nityaṃ sajjanasaṃparkād viveka upajāyate ।
vivekapādapasyaite bhogamokṣau phale smṛte ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kathaṃ vivekasyedṛśaḥ prabhāvo astīty । atrāha

mokṣadvāre dvārapālāś catvāraḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।
śamo vicāraḥ saṃtoṣaś caturthaḥ sādhusaṃgamaḥ ।।

etaiḥ vyastaiḥ samastair vā vinā na kaścin mokṣaṃ prāpnotīti vivekasya mokṣasādhakatvam astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

ete sevyāḥ prayatnena catvāro dvau trayo athavā ।
dvāram udghāṭayanty ete mokṣarājagṛhe balāt ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ekaṃ vā sarvayatnena prāṇāṃs tyaktvā samāśrayet ।
etasmin vaśage yānti catvāro api vaśaṃ yataḥ ।।

etasmin ekasmin । ekaś cātrottaraślokānurodhena vivekī jñeyaḥ ।।

nanu katham ekenaiva kāryaṃ setsyatīty । atrāha

saviveko hi śāstrasya jñānasya tapaso dyuteḥ ।
bhājanaṃ bhūṣaṇākāro bhāskaras tejasām iva ।।

bhūṣaṇabhūtaḥ ākāraḥ yasya ।।

vivekaparipanthinaḥ prajñāmāndyasyānarthotpādakatvaṃ kathayati

ghanatām upayātaṃ hi prajñāmāndyam acetasāṃ ।
yāti sthāvaratām ambu jāḍyāt pāṣāṇatām iva ।।

prajñāmāndyam ghanatām upayātaṃ sat । sthāvaratām yāti iti saṃbaddhaḥ ।।

nanu yady ahaṃ prajñāmāndyena vivekayogyo na syāṃ tarhi kiṃ kāryam ity । atrāha

tvaṃ tu rāghava saujanyaguṇaśāstrārthadṛṣṭibhiḥ ।
vikāsitāntaḥkaraṇaḥ sthitaḥ padma ivodaye ।।

imāṃ jñānadṛśaṃ śrotum avaboddhuṃ ca sanmate ।
arhasy uddhṛtakarṇasthajantur vīṇādhvaniṃ yathā ।।

sujanasya bhāvaḥ saujanyam । tadyuktāḥ guṇāḥ saujanyaguṇāḥ । te ca śāstrārthadṛṣṭayaś ca । tābhiḥ vikāsitaṃ prajñāmāndyarahitam antaḥkaraṇaṃ yasya saḥ । tathā uddhṛtaṃ niṣkāsitaṃ । karṇasthaṃ jantumalaṃ yasya saḥ । tādṛśaḥ । ato vivekayogya evāsīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu katham etad ity । atrāha

vairāgyābhyāsayogena samasaujanyasaṃpadā ।
tat padaṃ prāpyate rāma yatra nāśo na vidyate ।।

abhyāsaḥ sacchāstrābhyāsaḥ । tat padam vivekākhyaṃ sthānam ।।

atyantamukhyabhūtasya vivekasya vardhanopāyam āha

śāstraiḥ sajjanasaṃparkapūrvakais sutapodamaiḥ ।
ādau saṃsāramuktyarthaṃ prajñām evābhivardhayet ।।

tapaḥ bāhyendriyāṇāṃ nigrahaḥ ।।

saṃsāraviṣavṛkṣo agrasekam āspadam āpadām ।
añjanaṃ mohayāminyā maurkhyaṃ yatnena nāśayet ।।

mohaḥ viparyāsaḥ । añjanena hi māntrikāḥ divāpi yāminīṃ prakaṭayanti ity añjanam ity uktam ।।

nanu mama maurkhyaṃ kathaṃ naśyatīty । atrāha

etad eva ca maurkhyasya paramaṃ viddhi nāśanam ।
yad idaṃ prekṣyate śāstraṃ kiṃcitsaṃskṛtayā dhiyā ।।

nāśanam nāśakaraṇam । kiṃcitsaṃskṛtayā kiṃcitpadapadārthajñānamātreṇa । na tu kṣobhotpādakena mahatā vyākaraṇajālajñānena । saṃskṛtayā saṃskārayuktayā ।।

durāśāsarpagatena maurkhyena hṛdi valgatā ।
cetaḥ saṃkocam āyāti carmāgnāv iva yojitam ।।

durāśāḥ bhogāśāḥ eva sarpāḥ । maurkhyād eva durāśā niryāntīti bhāvaḥ । saṃkocam cidvimarśākhyavikāsarāhityam ।।

prājñe yathārthabhūteyaṃ vastudṛṣṭiḥ prasīdati ।
dṛg ivendau nirambhodasakalāmalamaṇḍale ।।

iyaṃ mayā vakṣyamāṇā । vastudṛṣṭiḥ paramārthadṛṣṭiḥ । prasīdati prasannā bhavati । tasmin naiva viśrāntiṃ bhajatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

pūrvāparavicārārthacārucāturyaśālinī ।
savikāsā matir yasya sa pumān iti kathyate ।।

pūrvāparavicāraviṣayīkṛtaḥ arthaḥ pūrvāparavicārārthaḥ । tatra yat cārucāturyaṃ । tena śālinī ।।

tvam apīdṛśo asīti sargāntaślokena kathayati

vikasitena sitena manomuṣā varavicāraṇaśītalarociṣā ।
guṇavatā hṛdayena virājase tvam amalena nabhaḥ śaśinā yathā ।।

vikasitena vivekākhyavikāsayuktena । sitena malarāhitena । manomuṣā manohāriṇā । varavicāraṇam eva śītalā ruk yasya । tādṛśena guṇavatā maitryādiguṇayuktena hṛdayena । yathā tat amalena nīhārādimalādūṣitena । śaśinā virājate tathety arthaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuvyavahāraprakaraṇe ekādaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

śrīrāmasya buddhisamādhānāya punar api śrīrāme samyakpraṣṭṛtvaṃ svasmiṃś ca samyagvaktṛtvaṃ kathayati

paripūrṇamanā mānyaḥ praṣṭuṃ jānāsi rāghava ।
vetsi coktaṃ ca tenāhaṃ pravṛtto vaktum ādarāt ।।

he rāghava । paripūrṇam bhogāśārāhityena tṛptaṃ । manaḥ yasya । ata eva mānyaḥ tvam । uktaṃ maduktaṃ । tenāhaṃ tava vaktum ādarāt pravṛttaḥ । anyathā na brūyām iti bhāvaḥ ।।

rajastamobhyāṃ rahitāṃ śuddhasattvānupātinīm ।
matim ātmani saṃsthāpya jñānaṃ śrotuṃ sthiro bhava ।।

ātmani na tu bāhyavastuṣu । saṃsthāpya samyak sthāpayitvā ।।

vidyate tvayi sarvaiva pṛcchakasya guṇāvalī ।
vaktur guṇālī ca mayi ratnaśrīr jaladhau yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

āttavān asi vairāgyaṃ vivekāt saṅgajaṃ muneḥ ।
candrakānta ivārdratvaṃ lagnacandrakarotkaraḥ ।।

āttavān gṛhītavān ।।

ciram ā śaiśavād eva tavābhyāso asti sadguṇaiḥ ।
śuddhaḥ śuddhasya dīrghaiś ca padmasyevātisaṃtataiḥ ।।

guṇaiḥ vairāgyādibhiḥ । atisaṃtataiḥ atiśayenāvicchinnaiḥ ।।

phalitam āha

ataḥ śṛṇu kathāṃ vakṣye tvam evāsyā hi bhājanam ।
na hi candraṃ vinā śuddhā savikāsā kumudvatī ।।

kathāṃ brahmoktāṃ svataḥsphuritāṃ vā mokṣakathāṃ । itaḥ paraṃ brahmoktam evopadeśaṃ śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ śrīrāmāya karotīti jñeyam ।।

brahmoktāṃ mokṣakathāṃ prastauti ye kecana samārambhā yāś ca kāścana dṛṣṭayaḥ ।
te ca tāś ca pade dṛṣṭe niḥśeṣaṃ yānti vai śamam ।।

pade cinmātrākhye । dṛṣṭe svātmatayā anubhūte । vai niścaye ।।

nanu etā dṛṣṭayaḥ adya tāvat kasyacic chāntiṃ gatā adya vā nety । atrāha

yadi vijñānaviśrāntir na bhaved bhavyacetasaḥ ।
tad asyāṃ saṃsṛtau sādhuś cintāṃ soḍhuṃ saheta kaḥ ।।

bhavyacetasaḥ sādhoḥ । yadi vijñānaviśrāntiḥ vijñāne vijñānasvarūpe ātmani । viśrāntiḥ saṃsāradṛṣṭināśadvāreṇa viśrāmaḥ । asyāṃ etādṛgduḥkharūpāyāṃ । kaḥ sādhuḥ cintāṃ viśrāmānāsādanāvyabhicāriṇīṃ saṃsāracintāṃ saheta । na ko apīty arthaḥ । asmadādivad iti śeṣaḥ । viśrāmāsādanena tasya cintā eva nāsti yenāsau iha tiṣṭhatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu bhavyasya cintā kutra gacchatīty । āha

paraprāptyā vilīyante sarvā mananavṛttayaḥ ।
kalpāntārkagaṇāsaṅgāt kulaśailaśilā ivā ।।

parasya paramātmanaḥ prāptyā । sarvāḥ mananavṛttayaḥ manomananavyāpārāḥ cintā iti yāvat । bhavyasya vilīyante । atra dṛṣṭāntam āha । kalpānteti ।।

duḥsahā rāma saṃsāraviṣāveśaviṣūcikā ।
yogagāruḍamantreṇa pāvanena praśāmyati ।।

saṃsāra eva viṣāveśakṛtā viṣūcikā viṣūcikākhyo rogaviśeṣaḥ । sā saṃsāraviṣāveśaviṣūcikā । gāruḍamantreṇa hi viṣāveśaḥ naśyati ।।

saḥ yogaḥ kathaṃ prāpyata ity apekṣāyāṃ gadyena kathayati

sa ca yogaḥ sujanena saha śāstrārthavicārāt । paramārthajñānamayo labhyata eva ।।

labhyata evetyantaṃ । saḥ mananavṛttivilayahetuḥ yogaḥ sujanena saha śāstrārthavicārāt labhyata eva । saḥ kathaṃbhūtaḥ । paramārthasya cinmātratattvasya । yat jñānaṃ tanmayaḥ । na tu prāṇarodhanādirūpaḥ ।।

nanu yadi vicāreṇāpi na kiṃcit setsyati tarhi kiṃ kāryam ity । atrāha

avaśyam iha hi vicāre kṛte sakaladuḥkhakṣayo bhavatīti mantavyam ।।

mantavyam ityantaṃ ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

nāto vicāradṛṣṭayo avahelayā draṣṭavyāḥ । vicāravaśataḥ puruṣeṇa sakalam idam ādhipañjaraṃ sarpeṇa tvacam iva paripakvāṃ parityajya vigatajvareṇa śītalāntaḥkaraṇena vinoda iva jagad akhilam ālokyate samyagdarśanavatā ।।

samyagdarśanavatetyantaṃ । yataḥ paramārthatattvaṃ vicārād eva labhyate ataḥ vicāradṛṣṭayaḥ vicārākhyāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ । avahelayā anādareṇa । nanu kiṃ vicāreṇa setsyatīty । vicāravaśataḥ samyagdarśanavatā samyagdarśanayuktena satā puruṣeṇa । akhilam bāhyam ābhyantaraṃ ca sarvaṃ । jagat vinoda iva krīḍā ivālokyate । tadbhāvābhāvaprayuktaharṣaśokarahitatvāt । puruṣeṇa kathaṃbhūtena । sakalam idam anubhūyamānam । ādhipañjaram vikalpākhyaṃ pañjaram । sarpeṇa paripakvāṃ tvacam iva parityajya vigatajvareṇa tāparahitenāta eva śītalāntaḥkaraṇena ।।

nanv asamyagdarśanavattvasya ko doṣo yena vicārāt samyagdarśanavattvam āśrīyate ity । atrāha

asamyagdarśanavato hi paraṃ duḥkham idaṃ । viṣamo hy atitarāṃ saṃsārarogo bhogīva daśati । asir iva cchinatti । śara iva vedhayati । rajjur iva veṣṭayati । rātrir ivāndhayati । aśaṅkitaparipātitaparuṣapāṣāṇa iva vivaśīkaroti । pātayati mohāndhakūpe । tṛṣṇayā jarjarīkaroti । na tad asti kiṃcid duḥkhaṃ saṃsārī yan na prāpnoti ।।

prāpnotītyantaṃ । param agrakoṭiṃ yātam । nanu kena kṛtaṃ duḥkham asyāsamyagdarśanavataḥ syād ity । vedhayati tāḍayati । viśeṣeṇa kathanam aśakyaṃ jñātvā sāmānyena kathayati । na tad iti । saṃsārī saṃsārayuktaḥ । ataḥ saṃsārakṛtam evehāsamyagdarśanavato duḥkham astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu viṣayarūpo ayaṃ saṃsāra evam eva bhavati । kim asmākaṃ karotīty । atrāha

duranteyaṃ kila viṣayaviṣamaviṣaviṣūcikā । yadi na cikitsyate tad atitarāṃ narakanagaranikaraphalānubandhinī tat tat karoti । yatra śitāsiśatapāta utpalatāḍanam । agnidāho himāvaseko । aṅgavikartanaṃ candanacakrakaracanā । ghūrṇadvātāntaḥ paripeṣo aṅgaparimālanam । anavaratānalajvālāvicalitacāmaranārācanikaranipāto nidāghavinodanadhārāgṛhaśīkaravarṣaṇam । śiraśchedaḥ sukhanidrā । mūkīkaraṇaṃ pāṭavamudrā mahān upacayaḥ ।।

mahān upacaya ityantaṃ । durantā nāśayitum aśakyā । viṣayāḥ saṃsārikāḥ bhogāḥ । te eva viṣamaviṣaviṣūcikā । sā yadi na cikitsyate । atitarām narakanagarāṇāṃ yaḥ nikaraḥ samūhaḥ । tasya anubandhaḥ pravāhena pravartanaṃ । saḥ asyām astīti tādṛśī satī sā । tat tat tādṛśaṃ tādṛśaṃ duḥkhaṃ karoti । tat kim ity apekṣāyām āha । yatra yasmin duḥkhe sati । yadduḥkham apekṣyeti yāvat । ghūrṇan sphuran yaḥ vātaḥ । paripeṣaḥ cūrṇībhāvaḥ । aṅgaparimālanam aṅgakomalatāpādakaṃ mardanaṃ bhavati । vātamadhye cūrṇībhāvād api tatkaṣṭataram iti bhāvaḥ । anavaratāḥ yāḥ analajvālāḥ । tā eva vicalitacāmarāṇi yasmin । tādṛśaḥ yaḥ nārācanikaraḥ । nidāghasya arthāt nidāghakṛtatāpasya । vinodanārthaṃ dūrīkaraṇārthaṃ yāni dhārāgṛhāṇi । teṣāṃ varṣaṇaṃ bhavati । pāṭavamudrāḥ pāṭavasya cāturyasya । mudrā saṃkocaḥ । mahān upacayaḥ vṛddhiḥ bhavati ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

tad evaṃvidhe kaṣṭaceṣṭāsahasradāruṇe saṃsāracapalayantre asmin rāghava nāvahelā kartavyā । avaśyam idaṃ hi vicāraṇīyam ।।

vicāraṇīyam ityantaṃ । evaṃvidhe pūrvoktamahākaṭhinaduḥkhadāyini । ata eva kaṣṭaceṣṭāsahasradāruṇe asmin anubhūyamāne । saṃsāra eva capalayantram tasmin । avahelā kiṃ mamāyaṃ karotīti anādaraḥ । na kartavyā । punaḥ kiṃ kāryam ity । atrāhāvaśyam iti । paṇḍitaiḥ avaśyam idam ayaṃ saṃsāraḥ । vicāraṇīyam । idam iti vicāraviṣayatāṃ nayet ।।

anyat kiṃ karaṇīyam ity । atrāha

evaṃ cāvaboddhavyam yathā kilāsti vicārāc chreyo'vāptir iti ।।

itītyantaṃ । puruṣeṇaivaṃ ca boddhavyam niśceyam । yathā kila niścaye । vicārāt śreyo'vāptiḥ mokṣaprāptir astīti ।।

nanv ayaṃ vivekaḥ kasyacid asty athavā nety । atrāha

anyac ca raghukulendo । yadi naite mahānto munayo maharṣayaś ca viprāś ca rājānaś ca jñānakavacenāvaguṇṭhitaśarīrās tat katham aduḥkhakṣamā api duḥkhamayīṃ tamovṛttipūrvakasaṃsārakadarthanām anubhavantaḥ satatam eva muditamanasas tiṣṭhanti ।।

tiṣṭhantītyantaṃ । bravīmīti śeṣaḥ । yadi ete puraḥsthāḥ । mahāntaḥ munayaḥ maharṣayaś ca viprāś ca rājānaś ca jñānakavacena vivekākhyakavacenāvaguṇṭhitāni valitāni । tādṛśāḥ jñānayuktā iti yāvat । tat tadā । ete munyādayaḥ aduḥkhakṣamāḥ api katham duḥkhamayīṃ । tathā tamovṛttipūrvikā tamovṛttikāraṇā । yā saṃsārakadarthanā saṃsārakleśaḥ । tām anubhavantaḥ । satatam eva na tu abhimataprāptyā kadācid eva । muditamanasaḥ tiṣṭhanti । ataḥ asty evaiṣāṃ viveka iti bhāvaḥ ।।

gadyāṃśayuktena padyenātra hetuṃ kathayati

iha hi
vikautukā vigatavikalpaviplavā yathā sthitā hariharapadmajādayaḥ ।
narottamāḥ samadhigatātmadīpakās tathā sthitā jagati vibuddhabuddhayaḥ ।।

padyāntaṃ । narottamāḥ narebhyaḥ samastamanuṣyebhyaḥ teṣāṃ madhye vā uttamāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ । tathā samadhigataḥ vivekavibhavena samyag anubhūtaḥ । ātmā eva paramātmā eva । tādṛśāḥ vibuddhabuddhayaḥ vivekayuktabuddhayaḥ pūrvoktāḥ munyādayaḥ । tathā katham ity apekṣāyām āha । vikautukāḥ viṣayākāṅkṣārahitāḥ । ādiśabdenendrādīnāṃ grahaṇam ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

tathā ca
parikṣīṇe mohe galati ca ghane ajñānajalade parijñāte tattve samadhigata ātmany abhimate ।
vicāryāryaiḥ sārdhaṃ galitavapuṣor vai sadasator dhiyā dṛṣṭe tattve ramaṇam aṭanaṃ jāgatam idam ।।

padyāntaṃ । āryaiḥ sadbhiḥ sārdham । vicārya saṃsāram ātmatattvaṃ ca vicārya । mohe ajñānakārye sāvadhānatve parigalite sati । tataḥ ghane nibiḍe । ajñānajalade ajñānam eva ca । tataḥ sadasatoḥ sadasadbuddhiviṣayībhūtayoḥ arthayoḥ । sadasadbuddhiparigalanena galitavapuṣoḥ satoḥ । tataḥ abhimate paramopādeye । ātmani tattve jīvākhye tattve । parijñāte dehādivyatiriktatayā samyak niścite sati । na kevalaṃ parijñāte kiṃ tu samadhigate dehādityāgena svātmatayā samyag anubhūte sati । tataḥ tattve jīvādisākṣitayā sthite śuddhacinmātratattve । dhiyā galanonmukhayā buddhyā । dṛṣṭe jīvasattāpradatvena dṛṣṭe sati । jāgataṃ jagatsaṃbandhi । aṭanam śarīrayātrānimittaṃ vyavaharaṇam । ramaṇam krīḍā bhavati । padārthaniṣṭabhāvābhāvakṛtaharṣaśokasparśakāritvābhāvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

anyac ca kathayāmīty āha

anyac ca rāghava
prasanne cittattve hṛdi savibhave valgati pare samābhogībhūtāsv akhilakalanādṛṣṭiṣu puraḥ ।
śamaṃ yāntīṣv antaḥkaraṇaghaṭanāsv āhitarasaṃ dhiyā dṛṣṭe tattve ramaṇam aṭanaṃ jāgatam idam ।।

padyāntaṃ । he rāghavāham anyac ca bravīmi । atrāha । cittattve śuddhacinmātrākhye tattve । prasanne svaprakāśanaparatayā prasādonmukhe sati । ata eva tasmin pare cittattve savibhave śaktisahite । hṛdi sattvabhāvena sthite । hṛdi valgati sphurati sati । vimarśaviṣayatām āyāte satīti yāvat । tataḥ akhilakalanādṛṣṭiṣu samastajīvādikalanārūpāsu dṛṣṭiṣu । samābhogībhūtāsu satīṣu । vyāpakacinmātrasvarūpatāsādanena vistārarahitāsv api vistārayuktāsu saṃpannāsu satīṣu । tataḥ antaḥkaraṇaghaṭanāsu antaḥkaraṇaracanāsu । āhitarasaṃ svecchayā । śamaṃ cinmātrasvarūpe layaṃ । puraḥ agre yāntīṣu । tataś ca dhiyā galanonmukhayā buddhyā । tattve śuddhacinmātrākhye tattve । dṛṣṭe ātmatayānubhūte sati । idaṃ jāgatam aṭanaṃ ramaṇaṃ bhavati ।।

punar api pūrvābhiprāyeṇaivāha

anyac ca
rathaḥ sphāro dehas turagaracanā cendriyagatiḥ parispando vātād aham akalitānantaviṣamaḥ ।
paro vārvā dehī jagati viharāmīty anaghayā dhiyā dṛṣṭe tattve ramaṇam aṭanaṃ jāgatam idaṃ ।।

sargāntaślokaṃ tāvat । sphāraḥ sarvatra sphuraṇaśīlaḥ । indriyagatiḥ indriyaracanā turagaracanā bhavati । heyopādeyarūpādiprāptiparihārārthaṃ darśanādidvāreṇa deharathacālakatvāt । parispandaḥ turagaracanābhūtānāṃ indriyagatīnāṃ ceṣṭā dehaṃ prati preraṇasāmarthyaṃ vātāt bhavati । vātena hi indriyāṇi darśanādikriyābhāñji santi dehaṃ cālayanti । dehī dehābhimānī jīvaḥ । arvā turagaḥ bhavati । paryantataḥ tasyaiva dehacālakatvāt । puraḥ dehādibhyaḥ uttīrṇaśuddhacinmātrarūpaḥ aham jagati viharāmi vihāraṃ karomi । ahaṃ kathaṃbhūtaḥ । akalitāni svātmatvaniścayena duḥkhadatvenāniścitāni । anantāni viṣamāni sukhaduḥkharūpāḥ saṃkaṭāḥ yena । rājā hi rathādibhyaḥ paraḥ san akalitānantanimnonnataś ca bhavati । iti anena niścayena । anaghayā svasmin baddhatvajñānādidoṣarahitayā । dhiyā galanonmukhayā buddhyā । tattve proktasvarūpe tattve । idam jāgatam aṭanaṃ ramaṇaṃ bhavati ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe dvādaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ pūrvoktāṃ dṛṣṭim anūdya tadavaṣṭaṃbhena subuddhīnāṃ vicaraṇaṃ kathayati

etāṃ dṛṣṭim avaṣṭabhya puṣṭātmānaḥ subuddhayaḥ ।
vicaranty asamunnaddhā mahānto abhyuditā iva ।।

etāṃ pūrvasargoktām । avaṣṭabhya satataṃ vimarṣaviṣayaṃ kṛtvā । puṣṭātmānaḥ । puṣṭaḥ atyantābhivyaktiyogyatāṃ gataḥ । ātmā śuddhacinmātrākhya ātmā yeṣāṃ te । tādṛśāḥ asamunnaddhāḥ darparahitāḥ । abhyuditāḥ iva prāptarājyā iva ।।

na śocanti na yācante na vāñchanti śubhāśubham ।
sarvam eva ca kurvanti kurvanti na ca kiṃcana ।।

sarvam eva pravāhāgataṃ sarvam eva । kurvanti kartavyam iti niścayena kurvanti । kiṃcana na kurvanti svasmin kartṛtvābhimānābhāvāt ।।

svastham evāvatiṣṭhanti svasthaṃ kurvanti yānti ca ।
heyopādeyatāpakṣarahitāḥ svātmani sthitāḥ ।।

svastham ity ubhayatra kriyāviśeṣaṇaṃ niścitam ity arthaḥ । heyopādeyatāpakṣarahitāḥ upekṣāpakṣe sthitā ity arthaḥ ।।

āyānti ca na cāyānti vanaṃ yānti na yānti ca ।
na kurvanty api kurvanti na vadanti vadanti ca ।।

atra sarvatrāpi kriyākaraṇaṃ jīvanmuktatayāśritadehādidvāreṇa jñeyam । akaraṇaṃ tv aśuddhacinmātratvadvāreṇety alam ।।

ye kecana samārambhā yāś ca kāścana dṛṣṭayaḥ ।
heyādeyadṛśo yās tāḥ kṣīyante adhigate pade ।।

kṣīyante līyante । parapadarūpatayaiva sphuranti iti yāvat ।।

parityaktasamastehaṃ mano madhuravṛttimat ।
sarvataḥ sukham abhyeti candrabimba iva sthitam ।।

madhuravṛttimat maitrīyuktam ।।

api nirmananārambham apy astākhilakautukam ।
ātmany eva na māty antar indāv iva rasāyanam ।।

ātmany eva na māti na prabhavati । atyantānandamayatvād iti bhāvaḥ । mananārambharahitasya kautukarahitasya ca ānandena svātmani amānaṃ na yuktam iti lokaprasiddhir apiśabdābhiprāyaḥ ।।

na karotīndrajālāni nānudhāvati vāsanām ।
bālacāpalam utsṛjya pūrṇam eva virājate ।।

indrajālāni mantrādiprabhāvena siddhāni ākāśagamanādīni । vāsanām nānudhāvati api tu tato nivṛttim eva karoti । bālavat cāpalam bālacāpalam utsṛjya । pūrṇam tṛptisahitaṃ yathā bhavati । tathā virājate ।।

ātmatattvāvalokanasyaiva pūrvoktāsu vṛttiṣu kāraṇatvaṃ gadyena kathayati

evaṃvidhā hi vṛttaya ātmatattvāvalokanāl labhyante । tasmād vicāreṇātmaivānveṣṭavya upāsanīyo jñātavyo yāvajjīvaṃ puruṣena netarad iti ।।

itītyantaṃ । evaṃvidhāḥ pūrvoktāḥ । ātmatattvasya paramātmasvarūpasya । puruṣeṇa labhyante । tasmād puruṣeṇa yāvajjīvaṃ vicāreṇātmaivānveṣṭavyaḥ । kiṃrūpo asāv iti vimarśanīyaḥ । upāsanaṃ cātra avicchinnapravāheṇānusandhānaviṣayīkaraṇam eva jñeyam । sthūladehādivyatirekena sthūladehavat niḥsaṃśayam ātmatattvena jñātavyaḥ । itarat sthūladehādi । itiśabdaḥ gadyasamāptau ।।

nanv ātmāvalokanaṃ kartavyatvena tvayā pratipāditaṃ । tadavalokanaṃ kathaṃ setsyatīty । atra padyenāha

svānubhūteḥ suśāstrasya guroś caivaikavākyatā ।
yatrābhyāsena tenātmā santatenāvalokyate ।।

svā nijā । suśāstrasya śobhanaśāstrasya । yatra yasmin abhyāse । ekavākyatā arthāt melanaṃ syāt । santatenāvicchinnena । tenābhyāsena karaṇena । puruṣeṇa kartrā ।।

avahelitaśāstrārthair avajñātamahājanaiḥ ।
kaṣṭām apy āpadaṃ prāpto na mūḍhaiḥ samatām iyāt ।।

svasthas tu katham iyād ity apiśabdābhiprāyaḥ ।।

etatprasaṅgena maurkhyaṃ nindati

na vyādhir na viṣaṃ nāpat tathā nāmāsti bhūtale ।
khedāya svaśarīrasthaṃ maurkhyam eva yathā nṛṇām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kiṃcitsaṃskṛtabuddhīnāṃ śravyaṃ śāstram idaṃ yathā ।
maurkhyāpahaṃ tathā śāstram anyad asti na kiṃcana ।।

kiṃcitsaṃskṛtabuddhīnām padapadārthajñānām ity arthaḥ । śravyam śravaṇārham । idaṃ mokṣopāyākhyam । maurkhyāpahaṃ maurkhyam upahantīti maurkhyāpaham ।।

idaṃ śravyaṃ sukhakaraṃ kathādṛṣṭāntasundaram ।
aviruddham aśeṣeṇa śāstravākyārthabandhunā ।।

kathābhiḥ vakṣyamāṇāḥ dṛṣṭāntāḥ kathādṛṣṭāntāḥ । śāstravākyānāṃ yaḥ arthaḥ । tena aviruddham । śāstrārthānusārīty arthaḥ ।।

āpado yā duruttārā yāś ca tucchāḥ kuyonayaḥ ।
tās tā maurkhyāt prasūyante khadirāt kaṇṭhakā iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

varaṃ śarāvahastasya caṇḍālāgāravīthiṣu ।
bhikṣārtham aṭanaṃ rāma na maurkhyahatajīvitam ।।

aṭanaṃ bhramaṇam ।।

imam ālokam āsādya mokṣopāyamayaṃ janaḥ ।
andhatām eti na punaḥ kaścin mohatamasy api ।।

ālokam paratattvaprakāśakatvāt ālokasvarūpam ।।

tāvan nayati saṃkocaṃ tṛṣṇā śyāmā narāmbujam ।
yāvad vivekasūryasya noditā vimalā prabhā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃsāraduḥkhamokṣārthaṃ mādṛśaiḥ saha bandhubhiḥ ।
svarūpam ātmano jñātvā guruśāstrapramāṇataḥ ।।

mādṛśaiḥ sādhubhir ity arthaḥ । guruśāstrākhyaṃ yat pramāṇaṃ pramākaraṇaṃ । tasmāt guruśāstrapramāṇataḥ । jñātvety asyānantaraṃ stheyam iti śeṣaḥ ।।

jīvanmuktāś carantīha yathā hariharādayaḥ ।
yathā brahmarṣayaś cānye tathā vihara rāghava ।।

vihara harṣāmarṣarahitatvena krīḍāṃ kuru ।।

anantānīha duḥkhāni sukhaṃ kṣaṇalavopamam ।
nātaḥ sukheṣu badhnīyād dṛṣṭiṃ duḥkhānubandhiṣu ।।

duḥkhānubandhiṣu duḥkhānuviddheṣu ।।

punaḥ kiṃ kāryam ity । atrāha

yad anantam anāyāsaṃ tat padaṃ sārasiddhaye ।
sādhanīyaṃ prayatnena puruṣeṇa vijānatā ।।

anantam trividhaparicchedarahitam । anāyāsaṃ āyāsasādhyatvābhāvāt । sārasiddhaye paramapuruṣārthasiddhaye । sādhanīyaṃ svopalabdhiviṣayatāṃ neyam । vijānatā kiṃcinmātrajñānayuktena mūrkhasyātrānadhikaratvāt ।।

ta eva puruṣārthasya bhājanaṃ puruṣottamāḥ ।
anuttamapadālambi mano yeṣāṃ gatajvaram ।।

avidyamāna uttamaḥ yasmāt tat anuttamam niratiśayam iti yāvat । tat ālambate iti tādṛśam ।।

saṃbhogāśanamātreṣu rājyādiṣu sukheṣu ye ।
saṃtuṣṭā duṣṭamanaso viddhi tān andhadundubhān ।।

andhadundubhān andharājilān । asamyag darśitvād ity arthaḥ ।।

ye śaṭheṣu duranteṣu duṣkṛtārambhaśāliṣu ।
dviṣatsu mitrarūpeṣu bhaktā vai bhogabhogiṣu ।।

te yānti durgamād durgaṃ duḥkhād duḥkhaṃ bhayād bhayam ।
narakān narakaṃ mūḍhā mohamantharabuddhayaḥ ।।

mitrarūpeṣu dviṣatsu ā mukhe sukhakāritvāt mohamantharā mohanirbharā ।।

parasparavināśotke śreyasyau na kadācana ।
sukhaduḥkhadaśe rāma taḍitprasarabhaṅgure ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ye viraktā mahātmānaḥ suviviktā bhavādṛśaḥ ।
puruṣān viddhi tān vandyān bhogamokṣaikabhāginaḥ ।।

bhogabhāktvaṃ caiṣāṃ pravāhagatam eva jñeyaṃ ।।

vivekaṃ param āśritya vairāgyābhyāsayogataḥ ।
saṃsārasaritaṃ ghorām imām āpadam uttaret ।।

abhyāsaḥ sacchāstrābhyāsaḥ ।।

na suptavyaṃ tu saṃsāramāyāsv iha hi jānatā ।
viṣamūrcchanasaṃmohadāyinīṣu vivekinā ।।

na suptavyam avahelā na kartavyā ।।

saṃsāram imam āsādya yas tiṣṭhaty avahelayā ।
jvalitasya gṛhasyoccaiḥ śete tārṇasya so antare ।।

tārṇasya tṛṇanirmitasya ।।

yat prāpya na nivartante yad āsādya na śocyate ।
tat padaṃ śemuṣīlabhyam asty evātra na saṃśayaḥ ।।

śemuṣīlabhyam eva buddhilabhyam eva । na tu bāhyayatnalabhyam ।।

nanu yadi tat padaṃ nāsti tat kiṃ śemuṣyā labhyate ity । atrāha

nāsti cet tad vicāreṇa doṣaḥ ko bhavatāṃ bhavet ।
asti cet tat samuttīrṇā bhaviṣyatha bhavārṇavāt ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pravṛttiḥ puruṣasyeha mokṣopāyavicāraṇe ।
yadā bhavaty āśu tadā mokṣabhāgī sa ucyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

anapāyi nirāśaṅkaṃ svāsthyaṃ vigatavibhramam ।
na vinā kevalībhāvaṃ vidyate bhuvanatraye ।।

svāsthyam svasthatā । kevalībhāvaṃ vinā advitīyatāṃ vinā ।।

tatprāptāv uttamaprāptau na kleśa upayujyate ।
na mitrāṇy upakurvanti na dhanāni na bāndhavāḥ ।।

tatprāptau kevalībhāvaprāptau । kleśaḥ śārīrikaḥ kleśaḥ ।।

na hastapādacalanaṃ na deśāntarasaṃgamaḥ ।
kleśātiśayasādhyo vā na tīrthāyatanāśrayaḥ ।।

asminn arthe hastapādādicalanaṃ na bhavati । deśāntarasaṃgamaḥ ca na bhavati । ayam arthaḥ kleśātiśayasādhyaḥ na bhavati । tīrthāyatanāśrayaḥ ca na bhavati ।।

puruṣārthaikasādhyena vāsanaikārthakarmaṇā ।
kevalaṃ tan manomātrajayenāsādyate padam ।।

puruṣeṇa tat kevalībhāvākhyaṃ padam । evalam manomātrajayena āsādyate prāpyate । manomātrajayena kathaṃbhūtena । puruṣārthena pauruṣeṇa । ekam kevalaṃ sādhyena । punaḥ kathaṃbhūtena vāsanaikārthakarmaṇā । vāsanā bhāvanā । bhāvanāmātrasādhyenety arthaḥ ।।

vivekamātrasādhyaṃ tadvicāraikāntaniścayam ।
tyajatā duḥkhajālāni nareṇa tad avāpyate ।।

tadvicāreṇa tadviṣayeṇa vivekena । vicāraniśceyam ity arthaḥ । tat kevalībhāvākhyaṃ padam ।।

sukhasevyāsanasthena tadvicāravatā svayam ।
na śocyate padaṃ prāpya na ca bhūyo abhijāyate ।।

tadvicāravatā kevalībhāvavicārayuktena । tat padaṃ kevalībhāvākhyaṃ padam ।।

tat samastasukhāsārasīmāntaṃ sādhavo viduḥ ।
tad anuttamaniṣṣyandaṃ param āhū rasāyanam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kṣayitvāt sarvabhāvānāṃ svargamānuṣyayor dvayoḥ ।
sukhaṃ nāsty eva salilaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇāsv ivaitayoḥ ।।

svargamānuṣyayoḥ svarlokamanuṣyalokayoḥ ।।

ato manojayaś cintyaḥ śamasaṃtoṣasādhanaḥ ।
anantaśamasaṃbhogas tasmād ānanda āpyate ।।

ataḥ kāraṇāt । puruṣeṇa manojayaḥ cintyaḥ । kathaṃbhūtaḥ । śamasaṃtoṣau sādhanaṃ yasya । tādṛśaḥ puruṣaḥ । anantaśamasya saṃbhogaḥ camatkāraḥ । śamāsvādarūpaḥ iti yāvat । ānandaḥ āpyate prāpyate ।।

jīvatā gacchatā caiva bhramatā patatā tathā ।
rakṣasā dānavenāpi devena puruṣeṇa vā ।।

manaḥpraśamanodbhūtaṃ tat prāpya paramaṃ sukhaṃ ।
vikāsiśamapuṣpasya vivekoccataroḥ phalam ।।

vyavahārapareṇāpi kāryavṛndam acinvatā ।
bhānunevāmbarasthena nojjhyate na ca vāñchyate ।।

jīvatā gacchatā bhramatā । upalakṣaṇaṃ caitat । sarvāḥ kriyāḥ kurvateti yāvat । rakṣasā dānavenāpi devena puruṣeṇa vā manaḥpraśamanodbhūtaṃ tathā vikāsiśamapuṣpasya vivekoccataroḥ phalam । tat paramaṃ sukham nirvāṇākhyaṃ sukhaṃ । prāpyāmbarasthena bhānunā iva nojjhyate na ca vāñchyate sūryavat upekṣām eva sarvatra kriyate ity arthaḥ । rakṣaḥprabhṛtinā kathaṃbhūtena । vyavahārapareṇāpi kāryavṛndam kāryasamūham । acinvatā nāhaṃkarteti niścayāt svakṛtatvenānanubhavatā ।।

manaḥ praśāntam atyacchaṃ viśrāntaṃ gatavibhramam ।
anīhaṃ vigatābhīṣṭaṃ nābhivāñchati nojjhati ।।

anīham vikalpākhyaceṣṭārahitam । vigatābhīṣṭam abhīṣṭam idam iti niścayarahitam । pravāhāgatam upekṣayā eva karotīti bhāvaḥ ।।

pūrvataraṃ prakṛtānāṃ śamādidvārapālānāṃ nirṇayaṃ prastauti

mokṣadvāre dvārapālān imāñ śṛṇu yathākramam ।
yeṣām ekatamāsaktyā mokṣadvāre praviśyate ।।

ekatamāsaktyā ekatamāsevanena ।।

tatrāpi prathamoddiṣṭaṃ śamaṃ nirūpayati

duḥkhadoṣadaśā dīrghā saṃsāramarumaṇḍalī ।
jantoḥ śītalatām eti śītalena śamāmbunā ।।

duḥkhadoṣarūpā daśā yasyāṃ sā duḥkhadoṣadaśā ।।

śamenāsādyate śreyaḥ śamo hi paramaṃ padam ।
śamaḥ śivaṃ śamaḥ śāntiḥ śamo bhrāntinivāraṇam ।।

paramaṃ padam cinmātrākhyam utkṛṣṭaṃ sthānam ।।

puṃsaḥ praśamatṛptasya śītalācchatarātmanaḥ ।
śamatoṣitacittasya śatrur apy eti mitratām ।।

dveṣeṇaiva hi śatruḥ śatruḥ bhavati । sa ca tasya nāstīti tasya śatruḥ mitratām etīti bhāvaḥ ।।

śamacandramasā yeṣām āśayaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ ।
kṣīrābdhīnām ivodeti teṣāṃ paramaśuddhatā ।।

paramaśuddhatā vāsanākhyamalarāhityam ।।

hṛtkuśeśayakośeṣu yeṣāṃ śamakuśeśayam ।
satāṃ vikasitaṃ te hi dvihṛtpadmāḥ samā hareḥ ।।

harer dvihṛtpadmatvaṃ nābhisthasya padmasya sthitatvāj jñeyam ।।

śamaśrīḥ śobhate yeṣāṃ mukhendāv akalaṅkite ।
te amī kulendavo vandyāḥ saundaryavijitendavaḥ ।।

akalaṅkitatvam evātra indujaye hetuḥ ।।

trailokyodaravartinyo nānandāya tathā śriyaḥ ।
sāmrājyasaṃpatpratimā yathā śamavibhūtayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yāni duḥkhāni yās tṛṣṇā duḥsahā ye durādhayaḥ ।
tat sarvaṃ śāntacetassu tamo arkeṣv iva naśyati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mano hi sarvabhūtānāṃ prasādam anugacchati ।
na tathendau yathā śānte jane janitakautukam ।।

prasādam prasannatām ।।

śamaśālini sauhārdavati sarveṣu jantuṣu ।
sujane paramaṃ tattvaṃ svayam eva prasīdati ।।

paramaṃ tattvam paramātmatattvaṃ । svayam evāyatnam eva । prasīdati svarūpadarśanākhyaṃ prasādaṃ karotīty arthaḥ ।।

mātarīva paraṃ yānti viṣamāṇi mṛdūni ca ।
viśvāsam iha bhūtāni sarvāṇi śamaśālini ।।

viṣamāṇi hiṃsāni ।।

na rasāyanapānena na lakṣmyāliṅganena ca ।
tathā sukham avāpnoti śamenāntar yathā janaḥ ।।

antaḥ manasi ।।

sarvādhivyādhivalitaṃ krāntaṃ tṛṣṇāvaratrayā ।
manaḥ śamāmṛtāsekaiḥ samāśvāsaya rāghava ।।

samāśvāsaya śītalaya ।।

yat karoṣi yad aśnāsi śamaśītalayā dhiyā ।
tat te atisvadate svādu netarat tāntamānasam ।।svadate rocate । camatkāraṃ karotīti yāvat । tāntam mlāniyuktaṃ kṛtaṃ ।।

śamāmṛtarasāsnātaṃ mano yām eti nirvṛtim ।
chinnāny api tayāṅgāni manye rohanti rāghava ।।

śamāmṛtarasāsnātaṃ manaḥ yāṃ nirvṛtiṃ eti । he rāghavāhaṃ manye । tayā nirvṛtyā । chinnāny api aṅgāni rohanti ।।

na piśācā na rakṣāṃsi na daityā na ca śatravaḥ ।
na ca vyāghrabhujaṅgādyā dviṣanti śamaśālinam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

susaṃnaddhasamastāṅgaṃ praśamāmṛtavarmaṇā ।
vedhayanti na duḥkhāni śarā vajraśilāṃ iva ।।

vedhayanti tāḍayanti ।।

na tathā rājate rājā mānyāntaḥpurasaṃsthitaḥ ।
samayā svasthayā vṛttyā yathopaśamaśobhitaḥ ।।

vṛttyā vyāpāreṇa ।।

prāṇāt priyataraṃ dṛṣṭvā tuṣṭim eti na tāṃ janaḥ ।
yām āyāti janaṃ śāntam avalokya samāśayam ।।

samāśayam samacetasam ।।

samayā śamaśālinyā vṛttyā yaḥ sādhu vartate ।
abhinanditayā loke jīvatīha sa netaraḥ ।।

vartate tiṣṭhati ।।

anuddhatamanāḥ śāntaḥ sādhu karma karoti yat ।
tat sarvam abhinandanti tasyemā bhūtajātayaḥ ।।

abhinandanti stuvanti ।।

śāntasvarūpanirṇayadvāreṇa śamasvarūpaṃ niścinoti

śrutvā spṛṣṭvā ca dṛṣṭvā ca bhuktvā ghrātvā śubhāśubham ।
na hṛṣyati glāyati yaḥ sa śānta iti kathyate ।।

upekṣā eva śāntir iti bhāvaḥ ।।

yaḥ samaḥ sarvabhāveṣu nābhivāñchati nojjhati ।
jitvendriyāṇi yatnena sa śānta iti kathyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tuṣārakarabimbācchaṃ mano yasya nirākulam ।
maraṇotsavayuddheṣu sa śānta iti kathyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sthito api na sthita iva na hṛṣyati na kupyati ।
yaḥ suṣuptamanāḥ svasthaḥ sa śānta iti kathyate ।।

suṣuptamanāḥ harṣāmarṣānusandhānarahitaḥ ।।

amṛtasyandasubhagā yasya sarvajanaṃ prati ।
dṛṣṭiḥ prasarati prītā sa śānta iti kathyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

spaṣṭāvadātayā buddhyā yathaivāntas tathā bahiḥ ।
dṛśyante yasya kāryāṇi sa śānta iti kathyate ।।

kapaṭarāhityād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

apy āpatsu durantāsu kalpānteṣu dahatsv api ।
tucchehaṃ na mano yasya sa śānta iti kathyate ।।

tuccheham tucchopāyaparam ।।

yo antaḥ śītalatāṃ yāto yo bhāveṣu na majjati ।
vyavahārī na saṃmūḍhaḥ sa śānta iti kathyate ।।

na majjati rāgodrekeṇāsakto na bhavati । vyavahārī vyavahārakārī । na saṃmūḍhaḥ na vyavahārarahitaḥ । vyavahārarahitasya hi amajjanaṃ vyavahārābhāvakṛtam eva na śāntikṛtam ।।

ākāśasadṛśī yasya nityaṃ svavyavahāriṇaḥ ।
kalaṅkam eti na matiḥ sa śānta iti kathyate ।।

svaḥ nijaḥ । vyavahāraḥ asyāstīti tādṛśasya ।।

tapasviṣu bahujñeṣu yājakeṣu nṛpeṣu ca ।
balavatsu guṇāḍhyeṣu śamavān eva rājate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śamasaṃsaktamanasāṃ mahatāṃ guṇaśālinām ।
udeti nirvṛtiś cittāj jyotsneva himarociṣaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sīmānto guṇapūgānāṃ pauruṣaikāntabhūṣaṇam ।
saṃkaṭeṣv abhayasthānaṃ śamaḥ śrīmān virājate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena śamanirūpaṇaṃ samāpayati

śamam amṛtam ahāryam āryajuṣṭaṃ param avalambya padaṃ paraṃ prayātāḥ ।
raghutanaya yathā mahānubhāvāḥ kramam anupālaya siddhaye tam eva ।।

he raghutanaya । mahānubhāvāḥ puruṣāḥ । amṛtam amṛtarūpam । ahāryam anāśyam āryajuṣṭam । śamaṃ pūrvoktasvarūpaṃ śamaṃ avalambya । paraṃ padaṃ paracitsvarūpam utkṛṣṭaṃ sthānaṃ । yathā prayātāḥ । tvam tam tathāvidham । kramam siddhaye anupālaya ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe trayodaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ vivekanirṇayaṃ prastauti

śāstrāvabodhāmalayā dhiyā paramapūtayā ।
kartavyaḥ kāraṇajñena vicāro aniśam ātmanaḥ ।।

kāraṇajñena kiṃ । kena saṃpadyate iti jānatā puruṣeṇa । dhiyā ātmanaḥ vicāraḥ aniśam kartavyaḥ ।।

nanu vicāreṇa kiṃ setsyati ity । atrāha

vicārāt tīkṣṇatām etya dhīḥ paśyati paraṃ padam ।
dīrghasaṃsārarogasya vicāro hi mahauṣadham ।।

param padam śuddhacinmātrākhyaṃ mahāsthānam ।।

āpadvanam anantehāparipallavitākṛti ।
vicārakrakacacchinnaṃ naiva bhūyaḥ prarohati ।।

anantāḥ yāḥ īhāḥ ceṣṭāḥ । tābhiḥ paripallavitā puṣṭībhūtā । ākṛtiḥ yasya tat ।।

moheṣu bandhunāśeṣu saṃkaṭeṣu bhrameṣu ca ।
sarveṣv eva mahāprājña vicāro hi satāṃ gatiḥ ।।

gatiḥ śaraṇam ।।

na vicāraṃ vinā kaścid upāyo asti vipacchame ।
vicārād aśubhaṃ tyaktvā śubham āyāti dhīḥ satām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

balaṃ buddhiś ca tejaś ca pratipattiḥ kriyāphalam ।
phalanty etāni sarvāṇi vicāreṇaiva dhīmataḥ ।।

pratipattiḥ jñānam । avivekena tu kṛtāni etāni anartham evotpādayantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

yuktāyuktamahādīpam abhivāñchitasādhakam ।
sphāraṃ vicāram āśritya saṃsārajaladhiṃ taret ।।

yuktāyuktamahādīpaṃ idaṃ yuktaṃ idaṃ tv ayuktam iti prakāśakam ity arthaḥ ।।

ālūnahṛdayāmbhojaṃ mahāmohamataṅgajam ।
vidārayati śuddhātmā vicārodārakesarī ।।

vidārayati vināśayati ।।

mūḍhāḥ kālavaśeneha yad gatāḥ paramaṃ padam ।
tad vicārapradīpasya vijṛmbhitam anuttamam ।।

kālena hi mūḍhā api śuddhacinmātrākhyaṃ paramaṃ padaṃ prāpnuvanti । vijṛmbhitam vilasitam । anuttamam niratiśayam ।।

rājyāni saṃpadaḥ sphāro bhogo mokṣaś ca śāśvataḥ ।
vicārakalpavṛkṣasya phalāny etāni rāghava ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yā vivekavilāsinyo matayo mahatām iha ।
na tā vipadi majjanti tumbakānīva vāriṇi ।।

vivekavilāsaḥ āsām astīti vivekavilāsinyaḥ ।।

vicārodayahāriṇyā dhiyā vyavaharanti ye ।
phalānām atyudārāṇāṃ bhājanaṃ hi bhavanti te ।।

vicārodayena hāriṇyā manoharayā ।।

mūrkhahṛtkānanasthānām āśāprasararodhinām ।
avicārakarañjānāṃ mañjaryo duḥkharītayaḥ ।।

āśā mokṣāśā । tasyāḥ yaḥ prasaraḥ । taṃ rundhantīti tādṛśānām dikprasararodhināṃ ca । karañjānāṃ kaṇṭakavṛkṣāṇām । duḥkharītayaḥ duḥkharacanāḥ ।।

kajjalakṣodamalinā madirāmodadhāriṇī ।
avicāramayī nidrā yātu te rāghava kṣayam ।।

kajjalakṣodena mantrasaṃskṛtena । kajjalakṣodena malinā ghanā । kajjalakṣodavat malinā cātyantakāluṣyāt । madirā modaṃ dhārayatīti tādṛśī । madirāmodenāpi nidrā ghanībhavati । avicāramayī avicārasvarūpā tām eva kṣayaṃ nayeti bhāvaḥ ।।

mahāpady api dīrgheṣu sadvicāraparo naraḥ ।
na nimajjati moheṣu tejorāśis tamassv iva ।।

moheṣu kiṃ karomīty evaṃrūpeṣu ।।

mānase sarasi svacche vicārakamalotkaraḥ ।
nūnaṃ vikasito yasya himavān iva bhāti saḥ ।।

mānase sarasi hṛdayākhye sarasi mānasākhye sarasīti ca ।।

vicāravikalā yasya matir māndyam upeyuṣaḥ ।
tasyodety aśaniś candrān mudhā yakṣaḥ śiśor iva ।।

vicāravikalā vicārarahitā । candrāt citsūryapratibimbarūpatvena candratulyāt saṃsārāt । aśaniḥ bhāvābhāvakṛtaharṣāmarṣarūpaṃ vajram āścaryaṃ ca candrād aśaner utpādaḥ ।।

duḥkhaṣaṇḍakavalmīkaṃ vipannavalatāmadhuḥ ।
rāma dūre parityājyo nirviveko narādhamaḥ ।।

narādhamaḥ kiṃ । duḥkhaḥ ṣaṇḍakānāṃ valmīkam । valmīke hi kaṇṭakaṣaṇḍakāni bhavanti । vipad eva navalatā । tasyāḥ madhuḥ vasantaḥ ।।

ye kecana durārambhā durācārā durādhayaḥ ।
avicāreṇa te bhānti vetālās tamasā yathā ।।

durārambhāḥ kutsitāḥ kāryārambhāḥ ।।

avicāriṇam ekāntajaraddrumasadharmakam ।
akṣamaṃ sādhukāryeṣu dūre kuru raghūdvaha ।।

ekānte janarahite deśe । sthitaḥ jaraddrumaḥ । tasya sadharmakam sadṛśam । sādhukāryeṣu cittanirodhādiṣu । phaladānena paropakārarūpeṣu ca śubhakāryeṣu ।।

viviktaṃ hi mano jantor āśāvaivaśyavarjitam ।
parāṃ nirvṛtim abhyeti pūrṇaś candra ivātmani ।।

viviktam vivekayuktam । āśāvaivaśyavarjitam iti viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa hetuḥ । āśāvaivaśyasyaiva nirvṛtirodhakatvāt ।।

vivekitoditā dehaṃ sarvaṃ śītalayaty alam ।
alaṃkaroti cātyantaṃ jyotsneva bhuvanam navā ।।

navā śaratkālīnā ।।

paramārthapatākāyā dhiyo dhavalacāmaram ।
vicāro rājate janto rajanyām iva candramāḥ ।।

paramārthasya śuddhacinmātratattvākhyaparamārthasya । patākāyāḥ pradarśakatvasāmānyena cihṇabhūtapatākārūpāyāḥ dhiyaḥ । dhavalacāmaram śobhādāyakatvena dhavalacāmararūpam ।।

vicāracāravo bhāvā bhāsayanto diśo daśa ।
bhānti bhāskaravad bhagnabhūyobhavabhayāmayāḥ ।।

bhāvāḥ manuṣyādirūpāḥ padārthāḥ । bhāvāḥ kathaṃbhūtāḥ । bhagnāḥ bhūyāṃsi bhavabhayāni evāmayāḥ yaiḥ te । bhāskaro api daśa diśaḥ bhāsayati ।।

bālasya svamanomohakalpitaḥ prāṇahārakaḥ ।
rātrau tamasi vetālo vicāreṇa vilīyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sarva eva jagadbhāvā avicāreṇa cāravaḥ ।
avidyamānasadbhāvā vicāraviśarāravaḥ ।।

sarva eva jagadbhāvāḥ jagatpadārthāḥ । avicāreṇa vicārarāhityena । cāravaḥ bhavanti । avidyamānasadbhāvāḥ । ata eva ca vicāraviśarāravaś ca vicārāsahatvāt ।।

puṃso nijamanomohakalpito analpaduḥkhadaḥ ।
saṃsāraciravetālo vicāreṇa vilīyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

samasvacchaṃ nirābādham anantamananāśrayam ।
viddhīmaṃ kevalībhāvaṃ vicāro agrataroḥ phalam ।।

samaṃ ca tat svacchaṃ samasvacchaṃ । nirābādham kenāpi pramāṇena bādhayitum aśakyam । anantasyāparicchinnasya svātmatattvasya । yat mananam parāmarśaḥ । tasyāśrayam lakṣaṇayā sādhakam ।।

acalasthitinodāraprakaṭābhogatejasā ।
tena niṣkāmatodeti śītatevoditendunā ।।

udāraprakaṭābhogaṃ udbhaṭaprakaṭavistāraṃ । niṣkāmatā kāmanārāhityam । uditaś cāsāv induḥ ।।

nanu niṣkāmatayā kiṃ setsyatīty । atrāha

cintājvaramahauṣadhyā sādhuś cittaniṣaṇṇayā ।
tayottamatvapradayā nābhivāñchati nojjhati ।।

tayā niṣkāmatayā । nābhivāñchati nojjhati sarvatropekṣām eva bhajate ity arthaḥ ।।

punaḥ kiṃ karotīty । atrāha

tatsadālambanaṃ cetaḥ sphāram ābhāsam āgatam ।
nāstam eti na codeti kham ivātitatāntaram ।।

sā niṣkāmatā sadā ālambanam āśrayo yasya । tat tatsadālambanam । tathā sphāraṃ sphuraṇaśīlaṃ । ābhāsam āgatam vivekayuktaṃ jātam ity arthaḥ ।।

na jahāti na cādatte nottāmyati na śāmyati ।
kevalaṃ sākṣivat paśyañ jagad ātmani tiṣṭhati ।।

nottāmyati na kṣubhyati ।।

na ca śāmyati nāpy antar nāpi bāhye avatiṣṭhati ।
na ca naiṣkarmyam ādatte na ca karmāṇi majjati ।।

sarvatropekṣayaiva vartate iti bhāvaḥ ।।

upekṣate gataṃ vastu saṃprāptam anuvartate ।
na kṣubdho nāti cākṣubdho bhāti pūrṇa ivārṇavaḥ ।।

anuvartate niranusandhānam pravartate ।।

evaṃrūpeṇa manasā mahātmāno mahāśayāḥ ।
jīvanmuktā jagaty asmin viharanti hi yoginaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

uṣitvā suciraṃ kālaṃ dhīrās te yāvadīpsitam ।
tanum ante parityajya yānti kevalatāṃ tatām ।।

kevalatām videhamuktatām । yāvadīpsitam ity anena sarvam eva bhagavatkṛtam teṣām īpsitam evāstīti sūcitam ।।

ko ahaṃ kasya ca saṃsāra ity āpady api dhīmatā ।
cintanīyaṃ prayatnena sapratīkāram ātmanā ।।

kim uta vaktavyaṃ saṃpadīty apiśabdābhiprāyaḥ । sapratīkāram pratīkārasahitam । na tu cintanamātreṇaiva । pratīkāraś cātra bhogatyāga eva jñeyaḥ ।।

kāryasaṃkaṭasandehaṃ rājā jānāti rāghava ।
niṣphalaṃ saphalaṃ vāpi vicāreṇaiva nānyathā ।।

bahir api vicārasyaiva sāmrājyam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

vedavedāntasiddhāntasthitayaḥ sthitikāraṇam ।
nirṇīyante vicāreṇa dīpeneva bhuvo niśi ।।

vedavedāntarūpāḥ sthitayaḥ maryādāḥ vedavedāntasthitayaḥ । sthitikāraṇam saṃsāramaryādākāraṇabhūtāḥ ।।

anaṣṭam andhakāreṣu bahutejassv ajihmitam ।
paśyaty api vyavahitaṃ vicāraś cārulocanam ।।

ajihmitam tejo'bhimukhe hi cakṣuṣi pratīghātena jihmitatvaṃ parivartitatvaṃ bhavati । tac cātra nāstīty arthaḥ ।।

vivekāndho hi jātyandhaḥ śocyaḥ sarvasya durmatiḥ ।
divyacakṣur vivekātmā jayaty akhilavastuṣu ।।

sarvasya śocyaḥ sarvaiḥ śocanīya ity arthaḥ । vivekaḥ ātmā pradhānaṃ yasya saḥ vivekātmā vivekānvita ity arthaḥ । jayati sarvotkarṣeṇa vartate ity arthaḥ ।।

paramātmamayī pālyā mahānandaikasādhanī ।
kṣaṇam ekaṃ parityājyā na vicāracamatkṛtiḥ ।।

pālyā rakṣaṇīyā ।।

vicāracāruḥ puruṣo mahatām api rocate ।
paripakvaṃ camatkāri sahakāraphalaṃ yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vicārakāntamatayo nānekeṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।
luṭhanti duḥkhaśvabhreṣu jñātordhvagatayo narāḥ ।।

jñātāḥ adhigatā । ūrdhve uttīrṇe cinmātre । gatiḥ yaite ।।

na virauti tathā rogī nānarthaśatajarjaraḥ ।
avicāravinaṣṭātmā yathājñaḥ pariroditi ।।

nānarthaśatajarjara ity atra caśabdo adhyāhāryaḥ । avicāreṇāvivekena vinaṣṭaḥ vismṛtaḥ । ātmā pāramārthikaṃ svarūpaṃ yasya ।।

varaṃ kardamakīṭatvaṃ śvabhrakaṇṭakatā varam ।
varam andhaguhāhitvaṃ na narasyāvicāritā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sarvānarthanijāvāsaṃ sarvasādhutiraskṛtam ।
sarvadauḥsthityasīmāntam avicāraṃ parityajet ।।

sarve ye anarthāḥ । teṣāṃ nijaḥ svakīyaḥ । āvāsaḥ sarvānarthaśrayam ity arthaḥ ।।

nityaṃ vicārayuktena bhavitavyaṃ mahātmanā ।
bhavāndhakūpe patatāṃ vicāro hy avalambanam ।।

hi yasmādarthe । avalambanam ādhāraḥ ।।

svayam evātmanātmānam avaṣṭabhya vicārataḥ ।
saṃsāramohajaladhes tārayet svamanomṛgam ।।

ātmanā manasā । ātmānaṃ paramātmānam । avaṣṭabhya bhāvanayā gṛhītvā ।।

vicārasya svarūpaṃ kathayati

ko ahaṃ katham ayaṃ doṣaḥ saṃsārākhya upāgataḥ ।
nyāyeneti parāmarśo vicāra iti kathyate ।।

nyāyena yuktyā । parāmarśaḥ santatabhāvanam ।।

andhāndhamohamukharaṃ ciraṃ duḥkhāya kevalam ।
kṛtaṃ śilāyā hṛdayaṃ durmateś cāvicāriṇaḥ ।।

atiṣayenāndham andhāndham । tādṛśaṃ ca tat mohamukharaṃ ca । jāḍyena viparyāsayuktam ity arthaḥ । duḥkhāya svasya parasya ceti jñeyam ।।

bhāvābhāvagrahotsargadṛśām iha hi rāghava ।
na vicārād ṛte tattvaṃ jñāyate sādhu kiṃcana ।।

grahaḥ grahaṇaṃ ।।

vicārāj jñāyate tattvaṃ tattvād viśrāntir ātmani ।
tato manasi śāntatvaṃ sarvaduḥkhaparikṣayaḥ ।।

tattvam cinmātrākhyaṃ paramaṃ tattvam । ātmani śuddhacinmātrarūpe ātmani । śāntatvasya svarūpaṃ kathayati । sarvaduḥkhakṣayasyaiva śāntirūpatvāt ।।

sargāntaślokena vicāranirūpaṇaṃ samāpayati

saphalatā phalate bhuvi karmaṇāṃ prakaṭatāṃ kila gacchata uttamāt ।
sphuṭavicāradṛśaiva vicāritā śamavate bhavate api virocatām ।।

kila niścaye । bhuvi karmaṇāṃ saphalatā phalate । sphuṭavicāradṛśaiva sphuṭā yā vicāradṛk । prakaṭatāṃ gacchataḥ vivekasyaiva sarvaprakaṭane śaktatvāt । ataḥ iyaṃ vicāritā śamavate bhavate api virocatām ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe caturdaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ evaṃ vicārasvarūpaṃ nirṇīya tṛtīyasya saṃtoṣasya svarūpaṃ kathayati

saṃtoṣo api paraṃ śreyaḥ saṃtoṣaḥ sukham ucyate ।
saṃtuṣṭaḥ param abhyeti viśrāmam arisūdana ।।

saṃtuṣṭaḥ saṃtoṣayuktaḥ puruṣaḥ ।।

saṃtoṣaiśvaryasukhināṃ ciraviśrāntacetasām ।
sāmrājyam api sādhūnāṃ jarattṛṇalavāyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃtoṣaśālinī buddhī rāma saṃsāravṛttiṣu ।
viṣamāsv apy anudvignā na kadācana dūyate ।।

na dūyate saṃtapyate saṃtuṣṭavān ।।

saṃtoṣāmṛtapānena ye parāṃ tṛptim āgatāḥ ।
bhogaśrīr atulā teṣām eṣā prativiṣāyate ।।

prativiṣā ivācarate prativiṣāyate । prativiṣā tiktadravyaviśeṣaḥ ।।

na tathā tarpayanty etāḥ pīyūṣarasavīcayaḥ ।
yathā hi madhurāsvādaḥ saṃtoṣo doṣanāśanaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃtuṣṭasvarūpakathanadvāreṇa saṃtoṣasvarūpaṃ kathayati

aprāptavāñchām utsṛjya saṃprāpte samatāṃ gataḥ ।
adṛṣṭakhedākhedo antaḥ sa saṃtuṣṭa ihocyate ।।

saṃprāpte pravāhāgate ।।

ātmanātmani saṃtoṣaṃ yāvad yāti na mānasam ।
udbhavanty āpadas tāval latā iva manovanāt ।।

ātmanā svena ।।

saṃtoṣaśītalaṃ cetaḥ śuddhavijñānadṛṣṭibhiḥ ।
bhṛśaṃ vikāsam āyāti sūryāṃśubhir ivāmbujam ।।

saṃtuṣṭasyaiva jñāne adhikāra iti bhāvaḥ ।।

āśāvaivaśyavivaśe citte saṃtoṣavarjite ।
mlāne vaktram ivādarśe na jñānaṃ pratibimbati ।।

pratibimbati lagati ।।

ajñānaghanayāminyā saṃkocaṃ na narāmbujam ।
yāty asāv udito yasya nityaṃ saṃtoṣabhāskaraḥ ।।

tat narāmbujam ajñānaghanayāminyā saṃkocaṃ na yāti । yasyāsau saṃtoṣabhāskaraḥ nityam udito bhavati ।।

akiṃcano apy asau jantuḥ sāmrājyasukham aśnute ।
ādhivyādhivinirmuktaṃ saṃtuṣṭaṃ yasya mānasam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nābhivāñchaty asaṃprāptaṃ prāptaṃ bhuṅkte yathākramam ।
yaḥ sasomyaḥ sadācāraḥ saṃtuṣṭa iti kathyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃtoṣaparitṛptasya mahataḥ pūrṇacetasaḥ ।
kṣīrābdher iva śuddhasya mukhe lakṣmīr virājate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pūrṇatām alam āśritya svātmany evātmanā svayam ।
pauruṣeṇa prayatnena tṛṣṇāṃ sarvatra varjayet ।।

pūrṇatāṃ tṛptatām । na tu bhogair ity arthaḥ ।।

saṃtoṣāmṛtapūrṇasya svāntaḥ śītalatā svayam ।
sthairyam āyāty ariktasya śītāṃśor iva śāśvatam ।।

svāntaḥ svamanasi । ariktasya pūrṇasya ।।

saṃtoṣapuṣṭamanasaṃ bhṛtyā iva maharddhayaḥ ।
rājānam upatiṣṭhante kiṃkaratvam upāgatāḥ ।।

yathā kiṃkaratvam upāgatāḥ bhṛtyāḥ rājānam upatiṣṭhante tathā saṃtoṣapuṣṭamanasaṃ maharddhayaḥ upatiṣṭhante ।।

ātmanaivātmani svacche saṃtuṣṭe puruṣe sthite ।
praśāmyanty ādhayaḥ sarve prāvṛṣīvāśu pāṃsavaḥ ।।

svacche rāgādimalarahite ।।

nityaṃ śītalayā nāma kalaṅkaparihīnayā ।
puruṣaḥ śuddhayā vṛttyā bhāti pūrṇatayenduvat ।।

nāma niścaye । kalaṅkahīnayā asantoṣākhyamalarahitayā ।।

saṃtoṣavivecanaṃ sargāntaślokena samāpayati

samatayā matayā guṇaśālināṃ puruṣarāḍ iha yaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ ।
tam amalaṃ praṇamanti nabhaścarā api mahāmunayo raghunandana ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe pañcadaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ evaṃ saṃtoṣasvarūpaṃ nirṇīya caturthaṃ satsaṃgaṃ nirūpayati

viśeṣeṇa mahābuddhe saṃsārottaraṇe nṛṇām ।
sarvatropakarotīha sādhuḥ sādhusamāgamaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sādhusaṃgataror jātaṃ vivekakusumaṃ śubham ।
rakṣanti ye mahātmāno bhājanaṃ te phalaśriyaḥ ।।

phalaśriyaḥ mokṣākhyaphalalakṣmyāḥ ।।

śūnyam ākīrṇatām eti mṛtir apy utsavāyate ।
āpat saṃpad ivābhāti vidvajjanasamāgame ।।śūnyaṃ śūnyadeśaḥ । ākīrṇatām lokabharitadeśatām ।।

himam āpatsarojinyā mohanīhāramārutaḥ ।
jayaty eko jagaty asmin sādhu sādhusamāgamaḥ ।।

sādhu samyak ।।

paraṃ vivardhanaṃ buddher ajñānatarunāśanam ।
samutsāraṇam ādhīnāṃ viddhi sādhusamāgamam ।।

samutsāraṇam nāśanam ।।

vivekaḥ paramo dīpo jāyate sādhusaṃgamāt ।
manoharojjvalo nūnam aśokād iva gucchakam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nirāmayāṃ nirābādhāṃ nirvṛtiṃ nityapīvarīṃ ।
anuttamāṃ prayacchanti sādhusaṃgavibhūtayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

api kaṣṭatarāṃ prāptair daśāṃ vivaśatāṃ gataiḥ ।
manāg api na saṃtyājyā mānavaiḥ sādhusaṃgatiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sādhusaṃgatayo loke sanmārgaśubhadīpakāḥ ।
hārdāndhakārahāriṇyo bhāso jñānavivasvataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yaḥ snātaḥ śītasitayā sādhusaṃgatigaṅgayā ।
kiṃ tasya dānaiḥ kiṃ tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kim adhvaraiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nīrāgāś chinnasaṃdehā galitagranthayo anagha ।
sādhavo yadi vidyante kiṃ tapastīrthasaṃgrahaiḥ ।।

galitagranthayaḥ naṣṭakāmākhyagranthayaḥ ।।

viśrāntamanaso vandyāḥ prayatnena pareṇa hi ।
daridreṇeva maṇayaḥ prekṣaṇīyā hi sādhavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

satsamāgamasaundaryaśālinī dhīmatāṃ matiḥ ।
kamalevāpsarovṛnde sarvadaiva virājate ।।

kamalā lakṣmīḥ ।।

tenāmalavilāsasya padasyāgrāvacūlatā ।
grathitā yena bhavyena na tyaktā sādhusaṃgatiḥ ।।

tena puruṣeṇa । amalavilāsasya śuddhasphuraṇayuktasya । padasya cinmātrākhyasya sthānasya । agrāvacūlatā śirobhūṣaṇatā । grathitā yena bhavyena daivaprakṛtikena । sādhusaṃgatiḥ na tyaktā sādhusaṃgatiḥ kāryaiva cinmātrākhye pade rājate iti bhāvaḥ ।।

vicchinnagranthayas tajjñāḥ sādhavaḥ sarvasammatāḥ ।
sarvopāyena saṃsevyās te hy upāyā bhavāmbudhau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ta ete narakāgnīnāṃ saṃśuṣkendhanatāṃ gatāḥ ।
yair dṛṣṭā helayā santo narakānalavāridāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dāridryaṃ maraṇaṃ duḥkham ityādiviṣamo bhramaḥ ।
saṃpraśāmyaty aśeṣeṇa sādhusaṃgamabheṣajaiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sarvān upāyān saṃkalpayati

saṃtoṣaḥ sādhusaṃgaś ca vicāro atha śamas tathā ।
eta eva bhavāmbhodhāv upāyās taraṇe nṛṇām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃtoṣaḥ paramo lābhaḥ satsaṃgaḥ paramā gatiḥ ।
vicāraḥ paramaṃ jñānaṃ śamo hi paramaṃ sukhaṃ ।।

ataḥ paraṃ lābhādi nāstīti parapadābhiprāyaḥ ।।

catvāra ete vimalā upāyā bhavabhedane ।
yair abhyastās ta uttīrṇā mohavārer bhavārṇavāt ।।

mohavāreḥ mohākhyajalayuktāt ।।

ekasminn eva caiteṣām abhyaste vimalodaye ।
catvāro api kilābhyastā bhavanti sudhiyāṃ vara ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

eko apy eko api sarveṣāṃ eṣāṃ prasavabhūr iva ।
sarvasaṃsiddhaye tasmād yatnenaikaṃ samāśrayet ।।

prasavabhūḥ utpattisthānam ।।

satsamāgamasaṃtoṣavicārās tv avicāritam ।
pravartante śamasvacche vahanānīva sāgare ।।

vahanāni jalaspandāḥ । avicāritam asandeham ।।

vicārasaṃtoṣaśamāḥ satsamāgamaśālini ।
pravartante śriyo jantau kalpavṛkṣāśrite yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vicāraśamasatsaṃgāḥ saṃtoṣavati mānave ।
pravartante prapūrṇendau saundaryādyā guṇā iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

satsaṃgasaṃtoṣaśamā vicāravati sanmatau ।
pravartante mantrivare rājanīva jayaśriyaḥ ।।

mantriṇāṃ mantrajñānāṃ ।।

phalitam āha

tasmād ekatamaṃ nityam eteṣāṃ raghunandana ।
pauruṣeṇa mano jitvā yatnenābhyāhared guṇam ।।

tasmāt eteṣāṃ caturṇāṃ madhye । ekatamaṃ guṇaṃ saṃtoṣādirūpaṃ guṇaṃ । abhyāharet arjayet ।।

paraṃ pauruṣam āśritya jitvā cittamataṅgajam ।
yāvad eko guṇo nāptas tāvan nāsty uttamā gatiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pauruṣeṇa prayatnena dantair dantān vicūrṇayan ।
yāvan nābhiniviṣṭaṃ te mano rāma guṇārjane ।।

devo bhavātha yakṣo vā puruṣaḥ pādapo atha vā ।
tāvat tava mahābāho nopāyo astīha kaścana ।।

guṇārjane saṃtoṣādyarjane ।।

ekasminn eva phalite guṇe balam upāgate ।
kṣīyante sarva evāśu doṣā viṣadacetasaḥ ।।

doṣāḥ rāgādayaḥ ।।

guṇe vivṛddhe vardhante guṇā doṣakṣayāvahāḥ ।
doṣe vivṛddhe vardhante doṣā guṇavināśinaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

manomahāvane hy asmin veginī vāsanāsarit ।
śubhāśubhabṛhatkūlā nityaṃ vahati jantuṣu ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sā hi svena prayatnena yasminn eva nipātyate ।
kūle tenaiva vahati yathecchasi tathā kuru ।।

hi niścaye ।।

sargāntaślokenaitat samāpayati

puruṣayatnajavena manovane śubhataṭānugatāṃ kramaśaḥ kuru ।
varamate nijabhāvamahānadīm iha hi tena manāg api nohyase ।।

puruṣayatnajavena pauruṣavegena । nijabhāvanadīṃ svavāsanāmahānadīṃ । nanu kimarthaṃ tāṃ taṭagatāṃ karomīty apekṣāyām āha । tena tasyāḥ śubhataṭānugamanena । tayā nijabhāvamahānadyā tvam na uhyase vivaśatayā yatra tatra na nīyase । taṭagatayā ca nadyā na kiṃcit uhyate ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe ṣoḍaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

evam āttaviveko yaḥ sa bhavān iva rāghava ।
yogyo jñānagiraḥ śrotuṃ rājeva nayabhāratīḥ ।।

he rāghava । āttaviveko bhavati । jñānagiraḥ śrotuṃ yogyo bhavati। rājā iva yathā rājā nayabhāratīḥ nītivākyāni śrotuṃ yogyaḥ bhavati ।।

avadāto avadātasya vijñānasya mahāśayaḥ ।
jaḍasaṅgojjhito yogyaḥ śaradīndor yathā nabhaḥ ।।

avadātaḥ śamādisevanena rāgādimalarahitaḥ nirmalaś ca । avadātasya śuddhacinmātraviṣayatvena śuddhasya sitasya ca । jaḍasaṅgena mūḍhasaṅgenojjhitaḥ tyaktaḥ । tam akurvāṇa ity arthaḥ । jaḍānāṃ lakṣaṇayā meghānāṃ saṅgena ujjhitaḥ iti ca ।।

tvam etayākhaṇḍitayā guṇalakṣmyā samāśritaḥ ।
manomohaharaṃ vākyaṃ vakṣyamāṇam idaṃ śṛṇu ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

puṇyakalpadrumo yasya phalabhārānataḥ sthitaḥ ।
muktaye jāyate jantos tasyedaṃ śrotum udyamaḥ ।।

idam etat śāstram ।।

pāvanānām udārāṇāṃ parabodhaikadāyinām ।
vacasāṃ bhājanaṃ bhūtyai bhavyo bhavati nādhamaḥ ।।

bhavyaḥ divyaprakṛtiḥ ।।

mokṣopāyābhidhāneyaṃ saṃhitā sārasammitā ।
triṃśad dve ca sahasrāṇi jñātā nirvāṇadāyinī ।।

saṃhitā śāstram । sārasammitā sāratulyā । jñātā samyak vicāritā ।।

nanu kim anayā setsyatīty । atrāha

dīpe yathā vinidrasya jvalite saṃpravartate ।
āloko anicchato apy evaṃ nirvāṇam anayā bhavet ।।

yathā dīpe prajvalite । anicchataḥ api ālokānākāṅkṣiṇo api । ardhanidrasyārdhaprabuddhasya । ālokaḥ saṃpravartate । evam anayā saṃhitayā । nirvāṇam brahmaṇy ātyantiko layo । bhavet ।।

svayaṃ jñātā śrutā vāpi bhrāntiśāntyaiva saukhyadā ।
āptoktivarṇitā sadyo yathāmṛtataraṅgiṇī ।।

āptoktivarṇiteti śrutety asya viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa hetuḥ ।।

yathā rajjvām ahibhrāntir vinaśyaty avalokanāt ।
tathaitatprekṣaṇāc chāntim eti saṃsāraduḥkhitā ।।

etasyāḥ saṃhitāyāḥ prekṣaṇam vicāraṇam etatprekṣaṇam ।।

yuktiyuktārthavākyāni kalpitāni pṛthak pṛthak ।
dṛṣṭāntasārasūktāni cāsyāṃ prakaraṇāni ṣaṭ ।।

mayā ṣaṭ prakaraṇāni asyāṃ kalpitāni vihitāni। arthasahitāni vākyāni arthavākyāni । yuktiyuktāni arthavākyāni yeṣu । punaḥ kathaṃbhūtāni । dṛṣṭāntaiḥ sāram śreṣṭham sūktaṃ yeṣu ।।

prakaraṇaṣaṭkam viśeṣato nirdiśati

vairāgyākhyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ prathamaṃ parikīrtitam ।
vairāgyaṃ vardhate yena sekeneva marau taruḥ ।।

nanu kiṃ tena saṃpadyata ity ।।

kiyatpramāṇaṃ tat kṛtam ity apekṣāyām āha

sārdhaṃ sahasraṃ granthasya yasmin hṛdi vicārite ।
prakāśā śuddhatodeti maṇāv iva vimārjite ।।

granthasyeti jātāv ekavacanam। tat vairāgyaprakaraṇaṃ granthasya ślokānāṃ sārdhaṃ sahasraṃ bhavati। tat kiṃ । yasmin hṛdi vicārite sati । prakāśā prakaṭā । śuddhatā rāgādimalarāhityaṃ udeti । kasminn iva । mārjite śodhite maṇau iva । yathā vimārjite maṇau śuddhatodeti ।।

mumukṣuvyavahārākhyaṃ tataḥ prakaraṇaṃ kṛtam ।
sahasramātraṃ granthasya sūktigranthena sundaram ।।

sūktirūpaḥ yaḥ granthaḥ vākyam । tadyuktam ity arthaḥ ।।

nanu kiṃ tatra kathyate ity । atrāha

svabhāvo hi mumukṣūṇāṃ narāṇāṃ yatra varṇyate ।
evaṃsvabhāvo mokṣasya yogya ity avagamyate ।।

nanu varṇanena kiṃ setsyatīty ।।

athotpattiprakaraṇaṃ dṛṣṭāntākhyāyikāmayam ।
pañcagranthasahasrāṇi vijñānapratipādanam ।।

vijñānapratipādanam vijñānapratipādakam ity arthaḥ ।।

jāgatī draṣṭṛdṛśyaśrīr ahaṃ tvam itirūpiṇī ।
anutthitaivotthiteva yatreti parivarṇyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yasmiñ śrute jagad idaṃ śrotrāntar budhyate akhilam ।
sāsmadyuṣmat savistāraṃ salokākāśaparvatam ।।

piṇḍagrahavinirmuktaṃ nirbhittikam aparvatam ।
pṛthvyādibhūtarahitaṃ saṃkalpa iva pattanam ।।

yasmin yasmin utpattiprakaraṇe । sāsmadyuṣmat ahaṃtvaṃyuktam । budhyate ity । atra śrotreti kartṛtvenādhyāhāryam। kīdṛśaṃ budhyate ity apekṣāyām āha । saṃkalpe hi pattanam īdṛg eva bhātīti dṛṣṭāntatvenopāttam ।।

punaḥ kīdṛg budhyate ity । atrāha

svapnopalabdhabhāvābhaṃ manorājyavad ātatam ।
gandharvanagaraprakhyam arthaśūnyopalambanam ।।

svapnopalabdhabhāvābhaṃ svapnadṛṣṭapadārthasadṛśam ity arthaḥ । gandharvāḥ svāvāsārthaṃ kalpanayākāśe nagaraṃ kalpayanti । tad eva gandharvanagaram । arthaśūnyaṃ satyabhūtaghaṭādyartharahitaṃ । upalambanaṃ jñānaṃ yasmin ।।

dvicandravibhramābhāsaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇāmbuvat tatam ।
nauyānalolaśailābhaṃ satyalābhavivarjitam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

cittabhramapiśācābhaṃ nirbījam api bhāsuram ।
kathārthapratibhānābhaṃ vyomamuktāvalīnibham ।।

nirbījaṃ kāraṇarahitaṃ । kathāyāḥ yaḥ arthaḥ varṇanīyaḥ padārthaḥ । tasya yat pratibhānaṃ pura iva sphuraṇaṃ । kathāyāṃ hi varṇanīyaḥ padārthaḥ puraḥstha iva pratibhāti । bhrameṇa hi vyomni muktāvalī dṛśyate ।।

kaṭakatvaṃ yathā hemni taraṅgatvaṃ yathāmbhasi ।
yathā nabhasi nīlatvam asad evotthitaṃ tathā ।।

kaṭakādi yathā hemni asad evotthitaṃ bhavati tathāsad evotthitaṃ jagad budhyate iti pūrveṇaiva sambandhaḥ ।।

abhitti raṅgarahitam upalabdhimanoharam ।
svapne vā vyomni vā citram akarma cirabhāsuram ।।

vāśabdadvayaṃ pakṣāntaradyotakaṃ । svapne dṛṣṭaṃ citram vā budhyate । vyomni bhrameṇa dṛṣṭaṃ citram vā budhyate । citraṃ kathaṃbhūtaṃ । abhitti bhittirahitaṃ । tathā raṅgarahitam raṅgadravyarahitam । punaḥ kathaṃbhūtaṃ । tathā ciraṃ bhāsvaram cirabhāsuram । etaiḥ viśeṣaṇaiś ca citrasya lokottaratvam uktam ।।

avahnir eva vahnitvaṃ dhatte citrānalo yathā ।
tathā dadhaj jagacchabdarūpārtham asadātmakam ।।

tathā tadvat । asadātmakam asatsvarūpam । jagacchabdarūpārtham bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ । jagad iti yacchabdarūpaṃ tasyārthatvaṃ dadhat budhyate tathā । kathaṃ । yathā citrānalaḥ avahniḥ adāhakatā anagniḥ san । asadātmakaṃ vahnitvaṃ dhatte dhārayati ।।

taraṅgotpalamālāḍhyadṛṣatpattram ivotthitam ।
cakraśūtkāracūrṇasya malarāśim ivoditam ।।

taraṅgotpalamālābhiḥ āḍhyaṃ yat dṛṣatpattram śilāpattram । tad ivotthitaṃ budhyate । śilāpattre hi taraṅgākāraḥ utpalākārāś ca rekhāḥ bhavanti । tā evātra taraṅgotpalamālāḥ jñeyāḥ । padārthāś cātra taraṅgotpalamālāsthānīyāh । punaḥ kīdṛg budhyate ity । atrāha । cakrasya bhrāmyamāṇasya cakrasya । tasya malarāśim iva uditaṃ budhyate । bhrāmyamāṇena cakreṇa hi saśūtkāraṃ bhūmeḥ rajaḥ uttiṣṭhati ।।

śīrṇaparṇaṃ bhraṣṭanaṣṭaṃ grīṣme vanam ivārasam ।
maraṇavyagranṛttābhaṃ śilāstrīhāsyahāsadam ।।

śilāstrīhāsyavat hāsadam ।।

andhakāragṛhaikaikanṛttam unmattaceṣṭitam ।
praśāntājñānanīhāraṃ vijñānaśaradambaram ।।

andhakāragṛhe yat ekaikasya nṛttam tadrūpaṃ budhyate । sarvathā cāsatyataram eva budhyate iti iha tāvad abhiprāyaḥ । itaḥ paraṃ cinmātramayaṃ cinmātrasthaṃ ca budhyata ity abhiprāyeṇāha । śrotrā asminn utpattiprakaraṇe śrute sati idaṃ praśāntājñānanīhāraṃ jñānaśaradambaraṃ budhyate ।।

samutkīrṇam iva stambhe citraṃ bhittāv ivāhitam ।
paṅkād ivābhiracitaṃ sacetanam acetanam ।।

stambhe cinmātrākhye stambhe । samutkīrṇam iva budhyate । tathā bhittau cinmātrākhyāyāṃ bhittau । citram ivāhitaṃ kṛtaṃ budhyate । paṅko atra cinmātrasvarūpaṃ jñeyaṃ । sacetanaṃ cinmātrasāratvāt । acetanaṃ grāhyatvāt ।।

tataḥ sthitiprakaraṇaṃ caturthaṃ parikalpitam ।
trīṇi granthasahasrāṇi svākhyānākhyāyikāmayam ।।

śobhanākhyāḥ ākhyānākhyāyikāḥ ।।

nanu sthitiprakaraṇe kim uktam ity । atrāha

itthaṃ jagad ahaṃbhāvarūpaṃ sthitim upāgatam ।
draṣṭṛdṛśyakramaprauḍham ity atra parivarṇitam ।।

ahaṃbhāvarūpasya jagataḥ sthitir evātra prāyaśo nirṇīyate iti bhāvaḥ ।।

daśadiṅmaṇḍalābhogabhāsuro ayaṃ jagadbhramaḥ ।
ittham abhyāgato vṛddhim iti tatrocyate ciram ।।

ciram bahukālam ।।

upaśāntiprakaraṇaṃ tataḥ pañcasahasrikam ।
pañcamaṃ pāvanaṃ proktaṃ munisantatisundaram ।।

munisantatibhiḥ dṛṣṭāntatayā vakṣyamāṇābhiḥ munisantatibhiḥ । sundaram ramaṇīyam ।।

nanv atra kiṃ varṇyata ity apekṣāyām āha

idaṃ jagad ahaṃ tvaṃ ca sa iti bhrāntir utthitā ।
ity asau śāmyatīty asmin kathyate ślokasaṅgrahe ।।

idaṃ jagat ahaṃ tvaṃ ca saḥ । śāmyati । asmin upaśāntiprakaraṇe kathyate । ślokānāṃ saṅgrahaḥ yasmin saḥ । sa iti paramakāraṇaparāmarśaḥ ।।

nanv etacchravaṇena kiṃ setsyatīty । atrāha

upaśāntiprakaraṇe śrute śāmyati saṃsṛtiḥ ।
praspaṣṭā vibhrameṇaiva kiṃcillabhyopalambhanā ।।

saṃsṛtiḥ kathaṃbhūtā । vibhrameṇaiva viparyayajñānenaiva praspaṣṭā । punaḥ kathaṃbhūtā । labhyam upalambhanaṃ sparśaḥ yasyāḥ sā । anyathā nirvāṇaprakaraṇaṃ vyarthaṃ syāt iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu tataḥ saṃsṛtiḥ kīdṛśī tiṣṭhatīty apekṣāyām āha

śatāṃśaśiṣṭā bhavati saṃśāntabhrāntirūpiṇī ।
anyasaṃkalpacittasthā nagaraśrīr ivāsatī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

alabhyaiva svapārśvasthasvapnayuddhavirāvavat ।
śāntasaṃkalpamattābhrabhīṣaṇāśaniśabdavat ।।

saṃkalpe dṛṣṭaṃ mattābhram saṃkalpamattābhram । śāntaṃ yat saṃkalpamattābhram । tasya yaḥ bhīṣaṇaḥ aśaniśabdaḥ ।।

vismṛtasvapnasaṃkalpanirmāṇanagaropamā ।
bhaviṣyannagarodyānasotsavaśyāmalāṅgikā ।।

vismṛtau yau svapnasaṃkalpau । tayoḥ nirmāṇaṃ yasya । tādṛśaṃ yat nagaraṃ । tenopamā yasyāḥ sā । tathā bhaviṣyannagarodyāne sotsavā samadanā । yā śyāmalā śyāmākhyā strī । tadvat aṅgaṃ svarūpaṃ yasyāṃ sā ।।

naśyajjihvocyamānograkathārthānubhavopamam ।
anullikhitacittasthacitravyāpteva bhittibhūḥ ।।

punaḥ kathaṃbhūtā । na tu naṣṭajihvena । ucyamānā yā ugrakathā । tasya yaḥ anubhavaḥ । tenopamā yatra tat । kā iva । anullikhitāni cittasthāni ca tāni citrakṛccittasthāni ca yāni citrāṇi । taiḥ vyāptā bhittibhūr iva ।।

parivismāryamāṇācchakalpanānagarīnibhā ।
sarvartumadanutpannavaramardāsphuṭākṛtiḥ ।।

parivismāryamāṇā । yā acchā bhittirahitā । tasyāḥ nibhā sadṛśī । sarvāsām ṛtumatīnām anutpannasya varasya mardaḥ mardanam । tadvat asphuṭā ākṛtiḥ yasyāḥ sā । nikaṭavartitvena buddhāv ārūḍhatvajñāpanārtham ṛtumatīnām ity uktam ।।

bhāvipuṣpavarākāravasantarasarañjanā ।
antarlīnataraṅgaughasaumyavārisaritsamā ।।

bhāvī puṣpākhyo varākāraḥ yasya saḥ । tādṛśo yaḥ vasantarasaḥ । tadvat rañjanā yasyāḥ sā । tatsadṛśīty arthaḥ । antarlīnaḥ taraṅgaughaḥ yasyāḥ sā antarlīnataraṅgaughā । tādṛśī cāsau saumyavārisarit saumyavāriyuktā nadī । tayā samā sadṛśī । etair viśeṣaṇaiś copaśāntiprakaraṇaśravaṇānantaraṃ buddhyārohamātrasvarūpā sṛṣṭis tiṣṭhatīti sūcitam ।।

nirvāṇākhyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ tataḥ ṣaṣṭham udāhṛtam ।
śiṣṭo granthaḥ parīmāṇaṃ tasya jñeyaṃ mahārthadam ।।

tataḥ upaśāntiprakaraṇānantaraṃ । śiṣṭaḥ granthaḥ sārdhaṣoḍaśasahasrāṇi parīmāṇam ।।
nanu kiṃ tacchravaṇena setsyatīty । atrāha

buddhe tasmin bhavec chrotā nirvāṇaḥ śāntakalpanaḥ ।
acetyacitprakāśātmā vijñānātmā nirāmayaḥ ।।

nirvāṇaḥ brahmaṇi līnaḥ । vijñānātmā śuddhajñānasvarūpaḥ । nirāmayaḥ dṛśyākhyāmayarahitaḥ ।।

paramākāśakośācchaḥ śāntasarvabhavabhramaḥ ।
nirvāhitajagadyātraḥ kṛtakartavyasusthitaḥ ।।

nirvāhitā avasānaṃ nītā jagadyātrā yena saḥ । kartavyaṃ yena kṛtakartavyaḥ । ata eva susthitaś ca ।।

samastavitatārambhavajrastambho nabhonibhaḥ ।
vinigīrṇayathāsaṃsthajagajjālātitṛptimān ।।

samastāḥ ye vitatārambhāḥ । teṣu vajrastambhaḥ avicala ity arthaḥ । nabhonibhaḥ śarīrayātrārthaṃ kṛtair api karmabhir aliptatvāt ākāśasadṛśaḥ । vinigīrṇaṃ citsvarūpe svātmani līnīkṛtaṃ । yat jagajjālaṃ । tenātitṛptimān nirapekṣa ity arthaḥ ।।

ākāśībhūtaniḥśeṣarūpālokamanaskṛtiḥ ।
kāryakāraṇakartṛtvaheyādeyadaśojjhitaḥ ।।

rūpam viṣayaḥ । ālokaḥ tadgrahaṇopāyaḥ । manaskṛtiḥ manaskāraḥ । ālokena gṛhītasya rūpasya manasi anusandhānam iti yāvat ।।

sadeha eva nirdehaḥ sasaṃsāro apy asaṃsṛtiḥ ।
cinmayo ।।hanapāṣāṇajaṭharajaṭharopamaḥ ।।MU।।

sadehaḥ sattvaśeṣaṃ tāvat śarīrasya sthitatvāt । nirdehaḥ śarīre abhimānābhāvāt । cinmayaḥ citsvarūpa aham iti niścayāt । ghanapāṣāṇasya yat jaṭharam । tasya yat jaṭharam । tenopamā yasya saḥ । tādṛśaḥ acetyacinmayatvāt ।।

cidādityas tapaṃl loke apy andhakārodaropamaḥ ।
paraprakāśarūpo api param āndhyam ivāgataḥ ।।

cidādityaḥ cidādityasvarūpaḥ । ata eva loke tapann api । na hi citsparśarahitaḥ kaścit bhāvaḥ saṃbhavati । sattve api tasya asaṃkalpatvaprasaṅgāt । andhakārodaropamaḥ andhakārasya yat udaraṃ । tādṛśaḥ padārthavibhāgarahitatvāt । na hi andhakārodare padārthavibhāgaḥ bhavati । paraprakāśarūpo api uttīrṇacitprakāśarūpo api । param āndhyam āgataḥ iva na kiṃciddraṣṭṛtvāt ।।

ruddhasaṃsṛtidurlīlaḥ prakṣīṇāśāviṣūcikāḥ ।
naṣṭāhaṃkāravetālo dehavān akalevaraḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kasmiṃścid romakoṭyagre tasyeyam avatiṣṭhate ।
jagallakṣmīr mahāmeroḥ puṣpe kvacid ivālinī ।।

kaśmiṃscit atisūkṣmatayā vaktum aśakye svapnavad iti śeṣaḥ । svapne hi puruṣasya kasmiṃścid aṃśe svapnajagad avatiṣṭhate ।।

paramāṇau paramāṇau cidākāśasya koṭare ।
jagallakṣmīsahasrāṇi dhatte kṛtvā ca paśyati ।।

cidākāśasya svarūpabhūtasya cinmātrākāśasya । koṭare madhye sthite । paramāṇau paramāṇau jagallakṣmīsahasrāṇi kṛtvā dhatte dhārayati । kiṃ tu sākṣitayā sthitatvāt paśyati ca ।।

nanu katham asau jagallakṣmīsahasrāṇy antarvartayatīty । atra sargāntaślokenāha

pravitatā hṛdayasya mahāmate hariharābjajalakṣaśatair api ।
tulanam eti na muktimato bata pravitatāsti na nūnam avastunaḥ ।।

bata niścaye । muktimataḥ nirvāṇaprakaraṇaśravaṇadvāreṇa muktiyuktasya puruṣasya । hṛdayasya pravitataḥ bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ । tena hṛdayasya pravitateti arthaḥ । sā hariharābjajalakṣaśatair api tulanaṃ māpanaviṣayatāṃ na eti । yataḥ avastunaḥ avastubhūtasya hariharābjādirūpasya bhāvavṛndasya pravitatā । nāsti । na cāvastunā vastumāpanaṃ yuktaṃ । tathā ca noktadeśaprasaṅga iti bhāvaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ mumukṣuprakaraṇe saptadaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ śrotṛpravṛttyarthaṃ svena kriyamāṇasya granthasyānyavilakṣaṇatvena samyagjñānaṃ prati paropāyatvaṃ kathayati

asyāṃ vācitamātrāyāṃ paro bodhaḥ pravartate ।
bījād iva yato vyuptād avaśyaṃbhāvi satphalam ।।

asyāṃ mokṣopāyābhidhāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ । yataḥ yasmāt bodhāt । satphalaṃ mokṣākhyaṃ śubhaṃ phalam । avaśyaṃbhāvi bhavati । vyuptād bījād iva ।।

nanu mahāmunipraṇītāni śāstrāntarāṇi tyaktvā kim iti idam eva śāstraṃ gṛhṇāmīty । atrāha

api pauruṣam ādeyaṃ śāstraṃ ced yuktibodhakam ।
anyat tv ārṣam api tyājyaṃ bhāvyaṃ nyāyaikasevinā ।।

pauruṣam puruṣanirmitam । ādeyaṃ grahītavyaṃ । yuktibodhakam sattarkabodhakam । anyat yuktyabodhakam । ārṣam ṛṣinirmitam । atra ca pratibhānvitaiḥ kaścid abhiprāyo boddhavyaḥ yo asmābhiḥ ārambha eva pratibhāvatāṃ svayaṃ jñeyatvena tadrahitānām akathanīyatvena coktaḥ ।।

yuktiyuktam upādeyaṃ vacanaṃ bālakād api ।
anyat tṛṇam iva tyājyam apy uktaṃ padmajanmanā ।।

atrāpi pratibhāvadbhiḥ ārambhe svayaṃ jñeyatvenokto arthaḥ svayaṃ boddhavyaḥ । na ca tadbodhenāsmiñ śāstre anādaraḥ kāryaḥ pratibhāvattvahāneḥ । evam uttaratrāpi yatra tatra svayam abhyūhyam ।।

punar apy etad eva bhaṅgyantareṇa kathayati

yo ambhas tātasya kūpo ayam iti kaupaṃ pibet kaṭu ।
tyaktvā gāṅgaṃ puraḥsthaṃ taṃ ko anuśāsati rāgiṇam ।।

yaḥ puruṣaḥ । puraḥsthaṃ gāṅgaṃ toyaṃ tyaktvā । ayaṃ kūpaḥ tātasya nijasya pituḥ bhavati । kaupaṃ kūpasambandhi । tam anurāgiṇaṃ pitṛviṣayarāgākhyadoṣayuktaṃ । kaḥ anuśāsati upadiśati । nāsāv upadeśārhaḥ iti bhāvaḥ । ayam atrābhiprāyaḥ । yaḥ puruṣaḥ । sadyuktiyuktam api pauruṣaṃ vacanaṃ । pauruṣeyam idam iti tyajati । tadrahitam api ārṣaṃ vacanaṃ । ārṣam ity etāvanmātreṇa gṛhṇāti । tasyopadeśo na kāryaḥ iti ।।

prakṛtam evānusarati

yathoṣasi pravṛttāyām āloko avaśyam eṣyati ।
asyāṃ vācitamātrāyāṃ svavivekas tathaiṣyati ।।

uṣasīty ārṣaṃ strītvam । svavivekaḥ ātmavivekaḥ ।।

śrutāyāṃ prājñavadanād buddhāyāṃ svayam eva vā ।
śanaiḥ śanair vicāreṇa buddhau saṃskāra āgate ।।

pūrvaṃ tāvad udety antar bhṛśaṃ saṃskṛtavākyatā ।
śuddhā muktā latevoccair yā sabhāsthānabhūṣaṇam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nanu viraktasya mama kiṃ saṃskṛtavākyatayā prayojanam ity । atrāha

parā virāgatodeti mahattvaguṇaśālinī ।
sā yayā sneham āyānti rājāno ajagarā api ।।

virakteṣu hi ajagaratulyāḥ rājāno api sneham āyānti ।।

pūrvāparajñaḥ sarvatra naro bhavati buddhimān ।
padārthānāṃ yathā dīpahasto niśi sulocanaḥ ।।

sarvatra sarveṣu vyavahāreṣu ।।

lobhamohādayo doṣās tānavaṃ yānty alaṃ śanaiḥ ।
dhiyo diśaḥ samāsannaśarado mihikā yathā ।।

lobhamohādayaḥ kāḥ । yathā mihikāḥ samāsannaśaradaḥ pratyāsannaśaratkālāyāḥ diśaḥ tānavaṃ yānti । tathety arthaḥ ।।

kevalaṃ samapekṣante vivekābhyasanaṃ dhiyaḥ ।
na kācana phalaṃ dhatte svabhyāsena vinā kriyā ।।

nanu kimarthaṃ vivekābhyāsam apekṣante ity ।।

manaḥ prasādam āyāti śaradīva mahat saraḥ ।
paraṃ sāmyam upādhatte nirmandara ivārṇavaḥ ।।

prasādaṃ rāgādimalarahitatvāt nairmalyam । sāmyaṃ samatākhyaṃ guṇam । upādhatte dhārayati । atrāpi manasa eva kartṛtvam ।।

nirastakālimā vajraśikhevāstatamaḥpaṭā ।
parijvalaty alaṃ prajñā padārthapravibhāginī ।।

nirastaḥ dūre gataḥ ।।

dainyadāridryadoṣādyā dṛṣṭayo darśitāntarāḥ ।
na nikṛntanti marmāṇi sasaṃnāham iveṣavaḥ ।।

darśitaṃ vivecitaṃ । antaram sārākhyaḥ āntaraḥ bhāgaḥ yāsāṃ tāḥ । niḥsāratvena jñātā ity arthaḥ ।।

hṛdayaṃ nāvalumpanti bhīmāḥ saṃsṛtibhītayaḥ ।
puraḥsthitam api prājñaṃ mahopalam ivākhavaḥ ।।

hṛdayaṃ kathaṃbhūtam api । puraḥsthitam api agre sthitam api । punaḥ kathaṃbhūtam ।।

kathaṃ syād āditā janmakarmaṇor daivapuṃstvayoḥ ।
ityādisaṃśayagaṇaḥ śāmyaty ahni yathā tamaḥ ।।

daivapuṃstvayoḥ daivapauruṣayoḥ ।।

sarvathā sarvabhāveṣu saṃgatir upaśāmyati ।
yāminyām iva yātāyāṃ prajñāloka upāgate ।।

sarvabhāveṣu tyāgādānārheṣu samasteṣu padārtheṣu । sarvathā saṃgatiḥ tyāgādānārūpā sambandhaḥ upaśāmyati । kasmin sati । pratijñāloka upāgate sati । kadeva । yāminyāṃ rātrau yātāyām iva satyām । upekṣā eva sarvatrāyātīti bhāvaḥ ।।

samudrasyeva gāmbhīryaṃ sthairyaṃ meror iva sthitam ।
antaḥśītalatā cendor ivodeti vicāriṇaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sā jīvanmuktatā tasya śanaiḥ pariṇatiṃ gatā ।
śāntāśeṣavikalpasya bhavaty āviśya yoginaḥ ।।

sā prasiddhā । āviśya āveśaṃ kṛtvā ।।

sarvārthaśītalā śuddhā paramālokadā sudhīḥ ।
paraṃ prakāśam āyāti jyotsneva sakalaindavī ।।

sarvārtheṣu bhāvābhāvayukteṣu samasteṣu padārtheṣu । śītalā harṣāmarṣākhyatāparahitā । śuddhā rāgādirahitā । paramālokaṃ cinmātrālokaṃ dadhātīti tādṛśī । śobhanā cāsau dhīḥ sudhīḥ । aindavī indusambandhinī ।।

hṛdyākāśe vivekārke śamālokini nirmale ।
anarthasārthakartāro nodyanti kaliketavaḥ ।।

śama eva ālokaḥ asyāstīti tādṛśe । kaleḥ kalahasya kṣobhasya । ketavaḥ cihnabhūtāḥ rāgādayo doṣāḥ । sūryodaye ca ketavaḥ dhūmaketavaḥ nodyanti ।।

śāmyanti śuddhim āyānti saumyās tiṣṭhanti sūnnate ।
acañcalajaḍās tṛṣṇāḥ śaradīvābhramālikāḥ ।।

na cañcalajaḍāḥ acañcalajaḍāḥ ।।

yatkiṃcanakarī krūrā grāmyatā vinivartate ।
dīnānanā piśācānāṃ līleva divasāgame ।।

yatkiṃcanakarī ayuktakāriṇī । grāmyatayā hi puruṣaḥ yatkiṃcid eva karoti ।।

dharmabhittau bhṛśaṃ lagnāṃ dhiyaṃ dhairyadhuraṃ gatām ।
ādhayo na vilumpanti vātāś citralatām iva ।।

dharma eva bhittiḥ । ata eva dhairyadhuraṃ gatām dhairyayuktām iti yāvat । dharmayukto hi dhīro bhavati । citrarūpā latā citralatā ।।

na pataty avaṭe jantur viṣayāsaṅgarūpiṇi ।
kaḥ kila jñātasaraṇiḥ śvabhre samanudhāvati ।।

viṣayāsaṅgarūpiṇi bhogāsaktirūpe । etad eva uttarārdhena samarthayati । kaḥ kileti ।।

sacchāstrasādhuvṛttānām avirodhini karmaṇi ।
ramate dhīr yathāprāpte sādhvīvāntaḥpurājire ।।

sacchāstreṇa mokṣopāyākhyasacchāstrāvagāhanena sādhuvṛttaṃ caritaṃ yeṣāṃ te । yathāprāpte pravāhāgate ।।

jagatāṃ koṭilakṣyeṣu yāvantaḥ paramāṇavaḥ ।
teṣām ekaikaśo antaḥsthān sargān paśyaty asargadhīḥ ।।

asargā dhīḥ yasya saḥ । āścaryaṃ cāsargadhiyaḥ paramāṇau paramāṇau sargadarśanam । sargabījabhūtacinmātravyāptijñānena paramāṇau paramāṇau sargadarśanaṃ jñeyam ।।

mokṣopāyāvabodhena śuddhāntaḥkaraṇaṃ janam ।
na khedayati bhogaugho na cānandayati kvacit ।।

bhogeṣūpekṣām evāsau bhajate iti bhāvaḥ ।।

paramāṇau paramāṇau sargavargā nirargalam ।
ye patanty utpatanty ambuvīcivat tān sa paśyati ।।

patanti līnā bhavanti । utpatanti prādurbhavanti ।।

na dveṣṭi saṃpravṛttāni na nivṛttāni kāṅkṣati ।
kāryāṇy eṣa prabuddho api niṣprabuddha iva drumaḥ ।।

abuddhatvam asya svātmani niṣprabuddhatvaṃ saṃsāre jñeyam ।।

nanu kīdṛg atiśayo asya syād ity । atrāha

dṛśyate lokasāmānyo yathāprāptānuvṛttimān ।
iṣṭāniṣṭaphalaprāptau hṛdaye na parājitaḥ ।।

lokasāmānyaḥ na tv atiśayavān । yathāprāpte pravāhāgate । anuvṛttiḥ anuvartanaṃ । saḥ yathāprāptānuvṛttimān । na parājitaḥ harṣāmarṣāvaśībhūtaḥ ।।

buddhvedam akhilaṃ śāstraṃ vācayitvā vivecya vā ।
anubhūyata evaitan na tūktaṃ varaśāpavat ।।

yuṣmābhiḥ etat pūrvoktaṃ phalaṃ anubhūyata eva । nanu pratyavāyaśaṅkayā katham etadanubhave śaktā bhavāma ity apekṣāyām āha । na tūktam iti । mantrādivad iti śeṣaḥ ।।

nanu durbodhe asmin kathaṃ pravṛttiṃ kurma ity । atrāha

śāstraṃ subodham evedaṃ nānālaṃkārabhūṣitam ।
kāvyaṃ rasaghanaṃ cāru dṛṣṭāntaiḥ pratipādakam ।।

dṛṣṭāntaiḥ pratipādakam iti subodhatve viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa hetuḥ ।।

budhyate svayam evedaṃ kiṃcitpadapadārthavit ।
svayaṃ yas tu na vettīdaṃ śrotavyaṃ tena paṇḍitāt ।।

budhyate jānāti । nanu yasya padapadārthavittvaṃ nāsti tasya kiṃ kāryam ity । atrāha svayam iti ।।

nanv etacchravaṇena kiṃ setsyatīty । atrāha

asmiñ śrute mate jñāte tapodhyānajapādikam ।
mokṣaprāptau tu tasyeha na kiṃcid upayujyate ।।

śrute śravaṇaviṣayatāṃ nīte । mate mananaviṣayatāṃ nīte । jñāte nidadhyāsite । tasya śravaṇādau pravṛttasya ।।

etacchāstraghanābhyāsāt paunaḥpunyena vīkṣitāt ।
jantoḥ pāṇḍityapūrvaṃ hi cittasaṃskārapūrvakam ।।

ahaṃ jagad iti prauḍho draṣṭṛdṛśyapiśācakaḥ ।
piśāco arkodayeneva svayaṃ śāmyaty avighnataḥ ।।

etena bāhyam api prayojanam āntaram api ca setsyatīti kathitam ।।

bhramo jagad ahaṃ ceti sthita evopaśāmyati ।
svapnamohaḥ parijñāta iva no ramayaty alam ।।

sthita eva । na tu mantrādiprayogavaśenāntarbhūtiṃ gataḥ । nanu sthitasyopaśamanaṃ katham ity । arasakasya sthitasyāpi śāntir eva jñeyā kṣobhakāritvābhāvāt iti bhāvaḥ ।।

yathā saṃkalpanagare puṃso harṣaviṣāditā ।
na bādhate tathaivāntaḥ parijñāte jagadbhrame ।।

antaḥ manasi । parijñāte samyak niścite । harṣaviṣāditā na bādhate iti tathāśabdenānukṛṣyate ।।

citrasarpaḥ parijñāto na sarpabhayado yathā ।
dṛśyasarpaḥ parijñātas tathā na sukhaduḥkhadaḥ ।।

parijñātaḥ citrasarpo ayam iti samyaṅ niścitaḥ । dṛśyākhyaḥ sarpaḥ dṛśyasarpaḥ ।।

parijñānena sarpatvaṃ citrasarpasya naśyati ।
yathā tathaiva saṃsāraḥ sthita evopaśāmyati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nanu paramārthaprāptir asmākam atiduṣkaraiva । tathā ca tatprāptyartham etacchāstrāvagāhanam ayuktam evety । atrāha

sumanaḥpallavāmarśe kiṃcidvyatikaro bhavet ।
paramārthapadaprāptau na tu vyatikaro asti naḥ ।।

sumanaḥpallavāmarśe puṣpapallavāmarde । naḥ yuktijñānām asmākam । na tv ayuktijñānāṃ bhavatām ity arthaḥ ।।

vyatikarābhāvam eva kathayati

gacchaty avayavaspandaḥ sumanaḥpatramardane ।
iha dhīmātrabodhas tu nāṅgāvayavabodhanam ।।

gacchati upayukto bhavati । anekārthatvād dhātūnāṃ gacchatir atrāsminn arthe vartate । aṅgāvayavānāṃ śarīrāvayavānām ।।

sukhāsanopaviṣṭena yathāsambhavam aśnatā ।
bhogajālaṃ sadācāraviruddheṣu na tiṣṭhatā ।।

yathākṣaṇaṃ yathādeśaṃ pravicārayatā sukham ।
yathāsambhavasatsaṅgam idaṃ śāstram athetarat ।।

āsādyate mahājñānabodhaḥ saṃsāraśāntidaḥ ।
sa bhūyo yena nāyāti yoniyantraprapīḍanam ।।

yathāsambhavam na tu prayatnasādhitam । sadācāraviruddheṣu tiṣṭhato hi hānopādānakāritvarūpo doṣaḥ āyātīti na tiṣṭhatety uktam । yathākṣaṇam pratikṣaṇam । yathāsambhavaḥ satsaṅgo yatra tat । idaṃ śāstraṃ mayā vakṣyamāṇamokṣopāyākhyam śāstraṃ । itarat etatsadṛśam anyacchāstraṃ vā । mahājñānarūpaḥ bodhaḥ mahājñānabodhaḥ । sa ity asya pūrvārdhena sambandhaḥ ।।

etāvaty eva ye bhūtā bhogān prāpya rase sthitāḥ ।
svamātṛviṣṭhākrimayaḥ kīrtanīyā na te adhamāḥ ।।

etāvati rase parimite rase । bhūtāḥ sāmānyajantavaḥ ।।

evaṃ śāstramāhātmyam uktvā śrīrāmaṃ saṃmukhīkaroti

śṛṇu tāvad idānīṃ tvaṃ kathyamānam idaṃ mayā ।
rāghava jñānavistāraṃ buddhisāratarāntaram ।।

buddheḥ sārataram antaram yasya tat । buddhyatiśāyīty arthaḥ ।।

madhye śrīrāmakṛtāṃś codyān āśaṅkyāha

yayedaṃ śrūyate śāstraṃ tāṃ tu vistarataḥ śṛṇu ।
vicāryate tathārtho ayaṃ yayā ca paribhāṣayā ।।

yayā paribhāṣayā yuktyā । idaṃ śāstraṃ śrūyate । tvaṃ tāṃ vistarataḥ śṛṇu । tathā yayā ca vicāryate । tāṃ ca śṛṇv iti pūrveṇa sambandhaḥ ।।

paribhāṣām eva kathayati

yenehānanubhūte arthe dṛṣṭenārthāvabodhanam ।
bodhopakāraphaladaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭāntaṃ vidur budhāḥ ।।

yena dṛṣṭenārthena । ananubhūte arthe arthāvabodhanam jñānam bhavati । budhāḥ tam dṛṣṭāntam āhuḥ । bodhākhyaḥ ya upakāraḥ । tad dadhātīti tādṛśam ।।

dṛṣṭāntadāne kiṃ phalam ity । atrāha

dṛṣṭāntena vinā rāma nāpūrvo artho avabudhyate ।
yathā dīpaṃ vinā rātrau bhāṇḍopakaraṇaṃ gṛhe ।।

bhāṇḍopakaraṇaṃ bhāṇḍasāmagrī ।।

yair yaiḥ kākutstha dṛṣṭāntais tvaṃ mayehāvabudhyase ।
sarve sakāraṇās te hi prāpyaṃ tu sad akāraṇam ।।

prāpyam prāpaṇīyaṃ । sat sanmātrākhyaṃ vastu ।।

nanu sarvāṇi dārṣṭāntikāni etādṛśāni eva santy utānyāny athety apekṣāyām āha

upamānopameyānāṃ kāryakāraṇatoditā ।
varjayitvā paraṃ brahma sarveṣām eva vidyate ।।

dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikānām paraṃ brahma varjayitvā । kāryakāraṇatā vidyate । brahma na kāryam asti nāpi kāraṇam ity arthaḥ । ato na brahmasadṛśāni sarvāṇi dārṣṭāntikāni iti bhāvaḥ ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

brahmopadeśadṛṣṭānto yasya veha hi kathyate ।
ekadeśasadharmatvaṃ tatrātaḥ parigṛhyate ।।

hi niścaye । yasya vā brahmopadeśadṛṣṭāntaḥ kathyate tatra brahmadṛṣṭānte । ekadeśasadharmatvaṃ ekadeśasadṛśatvaṃ । na tu sarvathā sadṛśatvam dārṣṭāntikasya brahmaṇaḥ kāryakāraṇatvāyogyāt । dṛṣṭāntasya tu kāryatayā kāraṇatayā ca sthitatvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

yo yo nāmeha dṛṣṭānto brahmatattvāvabodhane ।
dīyate sa sa boddhavyaḥ svapnadṛṣṭajagadgataḥ ।।

svapnadṛṣṭajagadgataḥ bhramarūpaḥ ity arthaḥ ।।

phalitam āha

evaṃ sati nirākāre brahmaṇy ākāravān katham ।
dṛṣṭānta iti nodyanti mūrkhavaikalpikoktayaḥ ।।

nodyanti nottiṣṭhanti । asmābhir ata eva pratyuktatvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

anyā siddhaviruddhādidṛk dṛṣṭāntapradūṣaṇe ।
svapnopamatvāj jagataḥ samudeti na kācana ।।

anyā pūrvoktāyāḥ dṛṣṭeḥ sakāśāt itarā kā । siddhaviruddhādidṛk idaṃ siddhaṃ idaṃ viruddham ityādirūpā uktiḥ । jagataḥ svapnopamatvāt dṛṣṭāntapradūṣaṇe dṛṣṭāntapradūṣaṇārtham na samudeti । ādiśabdenedaṃ leśena siddhaṃ viruddhaṃ veti dṛṣṭer grahaṇam । svapnopame jagati idaṃ siddhaṃ idam viruddham iti । kathanaṃ na yuktaṃ sarvasyāyuktatvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

avastu pūrvāparayor vartamānavicāritaṃ ।
yathā jāgrat tathā svapnaḥ siddham ābālam akṣatam ।।

pūrvāparayoḥ bhūtabhaviṣyator arthayoḥ । avastu bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ । avastutvam asattvam vartamānavicāritaṃ bhavati । vartamāne hi bhūtasya gatatvāt bhaviṣyataḥ anāgatatvāt asattvaṃ vicārapadavīm āyāti । tadabhinnasya vartamānasyāpi avastutvam aparihāryam eveti svayam eva jñeyam । ataḥ ābālam bālaparyantaṃ । yathā svapnaḥ tathā jāgrad iti ।।

svapnasaṃkalpanadhyānavaraśāpauṣadhādibhiḥ ।
ye arthās ta iha dṛṣṭāntās tadrūpatvāj jagatsthiteḥ ।।

ye arthā ity । atra dṛṣṭā iti śeṣaḥ । tadrūpatvāt svapnādyartharūpatvāt । ata ihāsatyaiḥ padārthaiḥ satyasya brahmaṇaḥ upamānopameyabhāvaḥ ekadeśasādharmyeṇeti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu tvayā kṛteṣv anyeṣu grantheṣu kā vārtety । atrāha

mokṣopāyakṛtā granthakāreṇānye api ye kṛtāḥ ।
granthās teṣv iyam evaikā vyavasthā bodhyabodhane ।।

mokṣopāyakṛtā granthakāreṇa mayety arthaḥ । bodhyasya bodhanīyasya brahmatattvasya । bodhane kathane ।।

nanu kathaṃ svapnasadṛśatvaṃ jagato astīty । atrāha

svapnābhatvaṃ ca jagataḥ śrute śāstre avabhotsyate ।
śīghraṃ na pāryate vaktuṃ vāk kila kramavartinī ।।

avabhotsyate jñātuṃ śakyate । tarhi yugapad eva sarvaṃ śāstraṃ kathayety । atrāha । vācaḥ kramavartitvaṃ sphuṭam eva । na hi ekaṃ vākyam anirvāhya dvitīyādikaṃ vākyaṃ vaktuṃ śakyate ।।

svapnasaṃkalpasudhyānanagarādyupamaṃ jagat ।
yatas ta eva dṛṣṭāntās tasmād bhāntīha netare ।।

yataḥ jagat । svapnasaṃkalpasudhyāneṣu dṛṣṭāḥ ye nagarādayaḥ । teṣāṃ upamā yasya । tasmāt ta eva sudhyānanagarādaya eva dṛṣṭāntāḥ bhānti asmākaṃ buddhau sphuranti । itare satyabhūtāḥ nagarādayaḥ । na bhānti ayuktatvāt ।।

akāraṇaṃ kāraṇinā yad bodhāyopamīyate ।
na tatra sarvasādharmyaṃ sambhavaty upamābhramaiḥ ।।

akāraṇaṃ kāraṇarahitaṃ brahma । kāraṇinā kāraṇayuktenākāśādinā । upamābhramaiḥ anyopamādṛṣṭasarvathāsādharmyarūpaiḥ viparyayaiḥ ।।

upameyasyopamānād ekāṃśena sadharmatā ।
aṅgīkāryāvabodhāya dhīmatā nirvivādinā ।।

dhīmatā na tv adhīmatā । sa hi ārambha eva vivādapara eva tiṣṭhatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanv ekena dharmeṇa sadṛśena upamānaṃ katham upameyasya pratītiṃ kartuṃ śaknotīty । atra dṛṣṭāntaṃ sādhayati

arthāvalokane dīpād ābhāmātrād ṛte kila ।
na sthālatailavartyādi kiṃcid apy upajāyate ।।

ābhāmātrāt prakāśamātrarūpāt ।।

etad eva dārṣṭāntikayuktaṃ kathayati

ekadeśasadharmatvād upameyāvabodhanam ।
upamānaṃ karoty aṅga dīpo arthaṃ prabhayā yathā ।।

prabhayā prabhākhyenaikadeśena ।।

dṛṣṭāntasyāṃśamātreṇa bodhyabodhodaye sati ।
upādeyatayā grāhyo mahāvākyārthaniścayaḥ ।।

na tu dṛṣṭāntamātra eva sthātavyam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

na kutārkikatām etya nāśanīyā prabuddhatā ।
anubhūtyapalāpāttair apavitrair vikalpitaiḥ ।।

prabuddhatā jñānitā । kutārkikāḥ hi ārambha eva codyān dattvā prabuddhatāṃ nāśayanti । vikalpitaiḥ kathaṃbhūtaiḥ । anubhūte yaḥ apalāpaḥ nihnavaḥ । tena āttaiḥ gṛhītaiḥ ।।

nanu purāṇāni śāstrāṇi ca tyaktvā kimarthaṃ tvaduktaṃ śāstraṃ gṛhṇīmaḥ ity । atrāha

vicāraṇād anubhavakāri vāṅmaya- prasaṅgatām upagatam asmadādiṣu ।
striyoktam apy aparam athāpi vaidikaṃ vaco vacaḥpralapanam eva nāgamaḥ ।।

asmadādiṣu prāmāṇikeṣu । striyā uktam api strīkartṛkaṃ pralapitam api । vāṅmayaprasaṅgatām śāstraprasaṅgatām । śāstratvam iti yāvat । upagatam । vicāraṇāt anubhavakāri । vaidikaṃ vacaḥ api vacaḥpralapanam eva pralāpa eva bhavati । nāgamaḥ bhavati anubhavakāritvābhāvād ity arthaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati
