dhārāḥ payomuca iva śīkarā iva vāridheḥ ।
kaṇās taptāyasa iva kasmān niryānti jīvakāḥ ।।

dhārā jaladhārāḥ । taptāyasaḥ vahnyabhijvalitāt ayasaḥ । kaṇāḥ vahnimayāḥ leśāḥ । jīvarāśeḥ jīvapiṇḍasya vānaṅgīkāre eteṣāṃ niryāṇaṃ na sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

praśnam upasaṃharati

iti me bhagavan brūhi jīvajālavinirṇayam ।
jñātam etan mayā prāyas tad eva prakaṭīkuru ।।

he bhagavan tvaṃ । jīvajālavinirṇayaṃ me brūhi । etāvad uktvā tvayā kiṃ na śrutam ity । mayā etat prāyaḥ bāhulyena । na tv aśeṣeṇātaḥ tad eva prakaṭīkuru yenāśeṣeṇa jānāmīti bhāvaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaram āha

eka eva na jīvo asti rāśīnāṃ sambhavaḥ kutaḥ ।
śaśaśṛṅgaṃ samuḍḍīya prayātītīva te vacaḥ ।।

paramārthataḥ eka eva jīvo nāsti । tvatpṛṣṭānāṃ rāśīnāṃ sambhavaḥ kutaḥ syāt । etatpraśnasyāsambaddhārthatvaṃ kathayati śaśeti । śaśaśṛṅgaṃ samuḍḍīya prayāti iti etadvacanasadṛśaṃ । te vacaḥ asti । ādau śaśaśṛṅgam eva nāsti । kā kathā taduḍḍayanasya । tathā jīva eva nāsti । kā kathā tadrāśyāder iti bhāvaḥ ।।

sarvam etat pṛṣṭaṃ nirākaroti

na jīvo asti na jīvānāṃ rāśayaḥ santi rāghava ।
na caikaḥ parvataprakhyo jīvapiṇḍo asti kaścana ।।

paramārthataḥ sarvasya śuddhacinmātraikamayatvāt jīvo nāsti । jīvānāṃ rāśayo na santi । na ca ekaḥ kaścana parvataprakhyaḥ jīvapiṇḍo asti । ataś ca tvatpraśno ayaṃ na yukta iti bhāvaḥ ।।

āśīḥprakāreṇa niścayam asya kartavyatvena kathayati

jīvaśabdārthakalanāḥ samastakalanānvitāḥ ।
na ca kāścana santīti niścayo astu tavācalaḥ ।।

taveti niścayaḥ ayaṃ niścayaḥ । iti jīvaśabdārthakalanāḥ । tāḥ samastakalanānvitāḥ samastābhiḥ ahambhāvādikalanābhiḥ anvitāḥ । na santi ।।

nanu jīvādīnāṃ pratyakṣeṇa sphuraṇāt katham ayaṃ niścayaḥ yuktaḥ syād ity । atrāha

śuddhaṃ cinmātram amalaṃ brahmāstīha hi sarvagam ।
tad yathā sarvaśaktitvād vindate yāṃ svayaṃ kalām ।।

cinmātrānukrameṇaiva sampraphullāṃ latām iva ।
nanu mūrtām amūrtāṃ vā tām evāśu prapaśyati ।।

hi niścaye । śuddhaṃ cinmātraṃ śuddhacinmātrasvarūpam । ata evāmalaṃ brahmāsti । sarvagam samastadeśakālavyāpakam । atrāha tad iti । sarvaśaktitvāt yataḥ sarvaśaktir asti । tataḥ yāṃ jīvādimayīṃ । yathā yena prakāreṇa । na tu pāratantryeṇa । vindate svopalabdhiviṣayaṃ karoti । kathambhūtāṃ kalāṃ । cinmātrānukrameṇa cinmātraparipāṭyā । sampraphullāṃ vikasitāṃ । cinmātrasyaiva hīyaṃ paripāṭī yat kalanāḥ vikāsayati । nanu niścaye । mūrtām amūrtāṃ vā sthūlāṃ sūkṣmāṃ vāśu tasminn eva kṣaṇe । prapaśyati sampannām eva paśyati । jīvaḥ paramārthataḥ svayaṃ siddho nāsti । kasya rāśitā piṇḍatā vā bhaved iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu yadi brahma jīvādi paśyati tadā tadbhinnam evaitat syāt । svabhinnasyaiva dṛṣṭigocaratvād ity । atrāha

jīvo buddhiḥ kriyāspando mano dvitvaikyam ity api ।
svasattāṃ prakacantīṃ tāṃ niyojayati vedane ।।

tat brahma । svasattāṃ svasphurattāṃ । vedane niyojayati vedanaviṣayāṃ karoti । svasattāṃ kathambhūtāṃ । jīvaḥ buddhiḥ kriyāspandaḥ hitāhitaprāptiparihārārthāś ceṣṭāḥ । dvitvaṃ ca tat aikyaṃ ca dvitvaikyam । ity api etadrūpeṇa । kacantīṃ sphurantīṃ । dṛṣṭigocaratve api na jīvāder bhinnatvaṃ yuktam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu brahmasattā kathaṃ jīvādibhāvena sphuratīty । atrāha

sābuddhaivaṃ bhavaty eva bhaved brahmaiva bodhataḥ ।
abodhaḥ prekṣayā yāti nāśaṃ na tu sa budhyate ।।

sā brahmasattābuddhā brahmasattābhāvenājñātā satī । evaṃ bhavati eva jīvādirūpatayā bhāsata eva । bodhataḥ brahmasattābhāvena jñānāt । sattātadvatoḥ bhedābhāvāt । nanu jīvādeḥ brahmasattābhāvena brahmamayatve api brahmasattāviṣayas tu yaḥ abodha āsīt saḥ abodhatvena jñātaḥ san ghaṭādivat tathaiva tiṣṭhati । tathā ca na brahmaikamayatā sidhyati ity । abodhaḥ prekṣayā bodhena । na budhyate bodhaviṣayo na sampadyate viruddhatvāt tadudbodhakāle eva naṣṭatvāt । na hi tamaḥ tejoviṣayo bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

etad eva dṛṣṭāntena dṛḍhīkaroti

yathāndhakāro dīpena prekṣyamāṇaḥ praṇaśyati ।
na cāsya jñāyate tattvam abodhasyaivam eva hi ।।

yathāndhakāraḥ dīpena prekṣyamāṇaḥ draṣṭum ārabdhaḥ । na ca jñāyate । dārṣṭāntike yojayati abodhasyeti । abodhasyājñānasyaivam eva tattvaṃ na jñāyate ity arthaḥ ।।

jīvasya brahmatvam upasaṃharati

evaṃ brahmaiva jīvātmā nirvibhāgo nirantaraḥ ।
sarvaśaktir anādyanto mahācitsārarūpadhṛt ।।

evaṃ pūrvoktaprakāreṇa । jīvātmā brahmaiva bhavati । brahmatvāpādakāny asya viśeṣaṇāny āha nirvibhāga iti । nirvibhāgaḥ vibhāgarahitaḥ । na hi jīvasvarūpe kaścid vibhāgo asti niravayavatvāt । nirantaraḥ prakāśanirbharitatvena madhye avakāśahīnaḥ । sarvaśaktiḥ sarvaśaktitvaṃ cāsya svapnādau pratyakṣadṛṣṭam eva । anādyantaḥ ādyantarahitatvaṃ cāsyādyantaparicchedakatvenaiva siddham । na hi paricchedyaḥ paricchedakasya paricchedaṃ kartuṃ śaknoti । mahācitsārarūpadhṛt । mahācit vimarśaśaktiḥ । tasyāḥ sāraḥ prakāśaḥ । tasya rūpaṃ dhārayati mahācitsārarūpadhṛt । prakāśasvarūpa ity arthaḥ ।।

sarvathaiva bhedakalanāṃ nirākaroti

sarvānantatayā tv asya na kācid bhedakalpanā ।
vidyate yā hi kalanā sā tad evānubhūtitaḥ ।।

tu viśeṣe । sarvānantatayā sarvaś cāsāv anantaś ca sarvānantaḥ । tasya bhāvaḥ sarvānantatā । kācid bhedakalanā bhedākārā kalanā । sarvarūpasyānantasya ca bhedāyogāt । na hi ghaṭādyapekṣayānantasya ghaṭaśarāvādisarvarūpasya mṛdādeḥ ghaṭabhedo yuktaḥ । nanu sarvatvam anantatvaṃ ca asarvāt sāntāc ca bhedakam eva । tathā ca tābhyām eva tasya bhedaḥ sampadyata ity । atrāha vidyata iti । yā kalanā bhedakalanā । sā tad eva brahmaiva । anubhūtitaḥ anubhūtisvarūpataḥ । yā kācit kalanāsti sānubhūtā na vā । na cet sā svayam asiddhā brahmaṇi bhedaṃ kathaṃ kuryāt । anubhūtā cet tarhi anubhavarūpaivānubhavasya ca cidrūpatvena brahmatvaṃ siddham eveti । brahmaiva sā bhaved iti ।।

atra śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

evam etat kathaṃ brahmann ekajīvecchayākhilāḥ ।
jagajjīvā na yujyante mahājīvaikatāvaśāt ।।

he brahman । satyam eva bhavatīty arthaḥ । sarveṣāṃ jīvānāṃ tatraikajīvecchānuvartitvam āśaṅkate । akhilāḥ jagajjīvāḥ । jagati sthitā jīvāḥ jagajjīvāḥ । mahājīvaikatāvaśāt । mahājīvena cetyatvāditanmātrāntaprapañcavalitacinmātrākhyamahājīvena । yā ekatā aikyaṃ । tasyāḥ vaśāt vaśena । ekajīvecchayā ekasya kasyāpi sāmānyajīvasyecchayā । kathaṃ na yujyante । ayaṃ bhāvaḥ । sarveṣāṃ jīvānāṃ proktasvarūpamahājīvaikamayatve ekasmin jīve uditayecchayā sarveṣāṃ jīvānāṃ yogo yuktaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaram āha

mahājīvātma tad brahma sarvaśaktimayātmakam ।
sthitaṃ yatheccham eveha nirvibhāgaṃ nirantaram ।।

mahājīvātma mahājīvaḥ । tat brahma iha yathecchaṃ svecchāsadṛśaṃ । sthitaṃ bhavati । tat brahma kathambhūtaṃ । sarvaśaktimayātmakam । sarvaśaktimayaḥ sarvaśaktinirbharaḥ । ātmā yasya । sarvaśaktimayātmakatvaṃ ca brahmaṇaḥ sarvaśaktīnāṃ tata evotthānāt । punaḥ kathambhūtaṃ । nirvibhāgaṃ akhaṇḍasvarūpatvena vibhāgān niṣkrāntam । punaḥ kathambhūtaṃ । nirantaram prakāśākhyasārabharitam ।।

nanu brahma yathecchaṃ sthitaṃ bhavatu । atrāha

yad evecchati tat tasya bhavaty āśu mahātmanaḥ ।
pūrvaṃ tu naśyatīcchā cid ato dvitvam udeti tat ।।

tat brahma । yad evecchati icchāviṣayaṃ karoti । tad eva । tasya mahātmanaḥ vyāpakasvarūpasya brahmaṇaḥ । āśu icchākṣaṇe eva । bhavati sampadyate । ekatecchānāśena dvitvotpattim asmāt kathayati pūrvam iti । nīlam utpalam itivat cidviśeṣitecchā jñeyā । cidviśeṣitatvaṃ cātra cidviṣayatvaṃ jñeyam । yata ity adhyāhāryam । cidrūpa eva bhavāmīty evaṃrūpā ekatecchā । pūrvaṃ prathamasargārambhe । ataḥ saptamyarthe tasil asmin brahmaṇi । naśyati tu susphūrtyaviṣayatārūpaṃ nāśaṃ yātīva । paramārthataḥ tu na naśyati tasyāḥ sarvatrānugamāt । iti tuśabdopādānam । cidviṣayecchānāśaś ca cetyaviṣayecchodbhūter eva jñeyaḥ । tat tasmāt kāraṇāt । dvitvaṃ cetyasvarūpajīvādirūpeṇa sthito dvidhābhāvaḥ । udeti prādurbhavati । ekatecchānāśahetubhūtatayā dvitvecchayā eva dvitvam udetīti bhāvaḥ ।।

dvitvodayānantaraṃ śaktikriyākramakaraṇaṃ kathayati

paścād dvitvavibhaktānāṃ svaśaktīnāṃ prakalpitaḥ ।
anenetthaṃ hi bhavatīty evaṃ tena kriyākramaḥ ।।

paścāt । dvitvena dvidhābhāvena । vibhaktānāṃ vibhāgena sthāpitānāṃ । ity evaṃ iti prakāreṇa । kriyākramaḥ kalpitaḥ । hi niścaye ।।

sampannaṃ sveṣṭaṃ kathayati

śaktyādyayā tayā brāhmyā niyamo yaḥ prakalpitaḥ ।
taṃ vinā nodayo anyāsāṃ pradhānecchaiva rohati ।।

tayā prasiddhayādyayā mūlakāraṇabhūtayā । brāhmyā brahmasambandhinyā । śaktyā । yaḥ niyamaḥ svecchāsadṛśī niyatiḥ । prakalpitaḥ । anyāsāṃ jīvasthānānām । ata ity adhyāhāryam । ataḥ pradhānecchaiva rohati । pradhānasya mahājīvātmabhūtasya brahmaṇaḥ । icchaiva rohati jīvecchārūpeṇa pariṇamate । tathā ca pradhānecchānuvartitvam eva । na sā niyamakāritvam uktam । iha tu tacchakter iti cen । śaktitadvator abhedāt ।।

etad eva nānāracanābhiḥ kathayati

yasyā jīvābhidhānāyāḥ śaktyā yecchā phalaty asau ।
pradhānaśaktiniyamānuṣṭhānena vinā na tu ।।

yasyāḥ jīvābhidhānāyāḥ śaktyāḥ śaktirūpasya yasya jīvasya । yā icchā phalati phalayuktā bhavati । tasyā ity adhyāhāryam । tasyāḥ śakteḥ asau icchā । pradhānaśaktiniyamānuṣṭhānena vinā । pradhānaśakteḥ brahmaśakteḥ । yat niyamānuṣṭhānaṃ niyamakaraṇaṃ । tad vinā na bhavati । svarūpam eva na labhate । kā kathā tatphalasyeti bhāvaḥ ।।

pradhānaśaktiniyamaḥ supratiṣṭho bhaven na cet ।
tat phalaṃ śaktyaśaktatvān nehitānāṃ kvacid bhavet ।।

pradhānaśakteḥ brahmaśakteḥ । niyamaḥ pradhānaśaktiniyamaḥ । supratiṣṭhaḥ susthiraḥ । na ced bhavet yadi na syāt । tat tadā । rohitānāṃ kvacit kutrāpi deśe kāle vā । phalaṃ na syāt । śaktyā brahmaśaktyā । lakṣaṇayā tanniyamena । yat śaktatvaṃ phalaṃ prati sāmarthyaṃ । tadabhāvaḥ aśaktatvaṃ । tasmāt śaktyaśaktatvāt । yataḥ rohitānāṃ nānāvidhānāṃ kriyāṇāṃ phalaṃ vidyate ataḥ anumīyate ko api niyamo asti yena kriyāṇāṃ phalotpādanaṃ prati sāmarthyam astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

prakṛtam anusarati

evaṃ brahma mahājīvo vidyate antādivarjitaḥ ।
jīvatkoṭimahākoṭī bhavaty atha na kiñcana ।।

evaṃ pūrvoktaprakāreṇa । brahmāntādivarjitaḥ antamadhyādirahitaḥ । mahājīvaḥ vidyate । kuto niryānti jīvakā iti pūrvataroktasya praśnasyottaram āha jīvatkoṭīti । tat brahma । jīvatāṃ jīvanakriyākartṛkāṇāṃ । koṭimahākoṭī koṭimahākoṭisaṅkhye । bhavati svayam eva tadrūpo bhavati । na tu tato jīvāḥ niryāntīti bhāvaḥ । na kiñcana bhavati । cinmaye svarūpe tathaiva sthitatvāt ।।

nanu brahma kena jīvatāṃ yātīty । atrāha

cetyasaṃvedanāj jīvo bhavaty āyāti saṃsṛtim ।
tadasaṃvedanād rūpaṃ śamam āyāti saṃsṛteḥ ।।

cetyasaṃvedanāt cidviṣayabhūtabhāvajātaparāmarśāt । brahma jīvo bhavati । tataḥ saṃsṛtiṃ yāti sukhaduḥkhalepasvarūpasaṃsārabhāk bhavati । nanu kadācit saṃsṛtir asya nivartate na vety । atrāha tad iti । tadasaṃvedanāt cetyāparāmarśāt । asyety adhyāhāryam । saṃsṛteḥ saṃsārasya । rūpaṃ śamaṃ śāntiṃ ।।

nanu saṃsṛtyupaśamena jīvasya kiṃ sampadyata ity । atrāha

evaṃ kaniṣṭhajīvānāṃ jyeṣṭhajīvakriyākramaiḥ ।
samudety ādyajīvatvaṃ tāmrāṇām iva hematā ।।

evaṃ sati saṃsṛtyupaśame sati । jyeṣṭhajīvasya brahmaṇaḥ । kriyākramaiḥ jyeṣṭhajīvakriyākramaiḥ । kaniṣṭhajīvānām ādyajīvatvaṃ brahmatvaṃ । samudeti prādurbhavati । jyeṣṭhajīvakriyākramā atra brahmakṛtāḥ kriyākramā jñātavyāḥ । brahmakṛtakriyākramasyaiva jīvānāṃ brahmatvāpādane samarthatvāt । atra dṛṣṭāntam āha tāmrāṇām iti । svarṇakārakriyākramaiḥ tāmrāṇāṃ yathā hematvaṃ samudeti ।।

pūrvataroktaṃ smarati

atrānante parākāśe ittham eṣa gaṇo apy asan ।
khātmaiva sann ivodeti ciccamatkaraṇātmakaḥ ।।

itthaṃ pūrvoktakrameṇātrānante parākāśe prasiddhe aparimeye cidākāśe । gaṇaḥ cetyatvādirūpaḥ prapañcaḥ । asann api sann ivodeti । khātmaiva nakiñcidrūpa eva । punaḥ kathambhūtaḥ । ciccamatkaraṇātmakaḥ । citaḥ yat camatkaraṇaṃ svaśaktyāsvādakaraṇaṃ । tat ātmā svarūpaṃ yasya । saḥ ciccamatkaraṇātmakaḥ । camatkaraṇaṃ vinā svatantrāyāḥ citeḥ cetyonmukhatāyogāt ।।

nanu camatkaraṇārtham anyāpekṣāyā avaśyambhāvāt kuto asyāḥ svatantrādīty । atrāha

svayam eva camatkāro yaḥ samāgamyate citā ।
bhaviṣyannāmadehādi tad ahambhāvanaṃ viduḥ ।।

yaḥ camatkāraḥ citā saha svayaṃ cidāśrayeṇa svaviṣayena ca yatnena vinā । samāgamyate svayaṃ samāgamaviṣayatāṃ bhajati । paṇḍitāḥ tad ahambhāvanam ahaṅkāraṃ । ahaṅkāro api ciccamatkāra eva । kā kathā jīvasyeti ahambhāvagrahaṇābhiprāyaḥ । bhaviṣyannāmadehādi । bhaviṣyat nāma ca dehādi ca yasya । nāmāhaṅkārety abhidhā । dehaḥ sthūlasūkṣmarūpaḥ । cinnairapekṣyadyotanāya samāgamyata iti karmakartṛvyapadeśaḥ ।।

prakṛtaṃ cidaikyaṃ bahuvistareṇa kathayati

cito yaḥ syāc cidālokas tanmayatvād anantakaḥ ।
sa eṣa bhuvanābhoga iti tasyāḥ prabimbati ।।

citaḥ anantasvabhāvasya citprakāśasya । yaḥ ālokaḥ bhāvaprakaṭanahetuḥ svabhāvaviśeṣaḥ । syād asti । tanmayatvāt cinmayatvād । anantakaḥ cidvad aparimeyaḥ । aparimeyatvaṃ ca citaḥ parimātur abhāvena svayaṃ svasmin parimātṛtāsambhavāc ca jñeyam । sa eṣaḥ pūrvoktaḥ viṣayasya svavyatiriktasya cidālokaḥ । bhuvanābhoga iti bhuvanavistāro ayam iti । pratibimbati mālinyānādāyakatvena pratibimbabhāvena sphurati ।।

pariṇāmavikārādiśabdaiḥ saiva cid avyayā ।
tādṛgrūpyād abhedyāpi svaśaktyaiva vibudhyate ।।

svaśaktyā eva pramātṛbhāvena sphurantyā nijaśaktyā eva kartryāvyayā nāśarahitā । saiva cit pariṇāmavikārādiśabdaiḥ vibudhyate vijñāyate । śabdasyārthabodhaṃ prati kāraṇatvaṃ suprasiddham eveti nāyastam । tādṛgrūpyāt cidrūpatāyāḥ । abhedyāpi bhinnīkartum ayogyāpi । nanu svarūpād abhinnatve kathaṃ pariṇāmādiśabdavācyatvaṃ asyā iti cet । yathā toyaṃ svarūpād abhinnam api taraṅgatām āsādya toyapariṇāmaśabdena tadvikāraśabdena ca kathyate tatheyam apīti na virodhaḥ ।।

avicchinnavilāsātma svato yat svadanaṃ citaḥ ।
acetyasya prakāśasya jagad ity eva tat sthitam ।।

acetyasya prakāśasya cetyaleparahitaprakāśarūpāyāḥ citaḥ । yat svadanaṃ svaśaktyāsvādaḥ bhavati । avicchinnavilāsātma । avicchinavilāsaḥ chedarahitasphuraṇayuktaḥ । ātmā yasya । tat avicchinnavilāsātma । tat svadanaṃ jagad ity eva jagatsvarūpeṇa ।।

ākāśād api sūkṣmaiṣā yā śaktir vitatā citaḥ ।
sā svabhāvata evainām ahantāṃ paripaśyati ।।

yā eṣā ākāśād api sūkṣmāparicchedyā । vitatā sarvatra vyāptā । citaḥ śaktiḥ sāmarthyaṃ asti । svabhāvata eva svasattayaiva । enāṃ proktaviśeṣaṇāṃ । ahantāṃ paripaśyati ahaṅkārabhāvena cetati ।।

ātmany ātmātmanaivāsyā yat prasphurati vārivat ।
jagadantam ahantāṇuṃ tad evāsau prapaśyati ।।

asyāḥ citaḥ । ātmā sphurattākhyaṃ svarūpam । ātmani sphurattākhye svarūpe svasvarūpe । yat sphurati vilasati । tad eva sphuraṇam evāsau cid । ahantāṇuṃ prapaśyati parimitāhantārūpatayā parāmṛśati । kīdṛśam ahantāṇuṃ । jagadantam jagatparyantam ।।

camatkārakarī cāru yac camatkurute citiḥ ।
iyaṃ svātmani tasyaiva jagannāma kṛtaṃ tatam ।।

camatkārakarī camatkārakaraṇa[ ? ]syaiva । jagannāma jagad iti nāma । tayaiveti śeṣaḥ ।।

citaś cittvam ahaṅkāraḥ saiva rāghava kalpanā ।
tanmātrādi cid evāto dvitvaikatve kva saṃsthite ।।

citaḥ cittvam ahaṅkāraḥ bhavati । ahaṅkāratayā cittvasyaiva pariṇāmād ity arthaḥ । he rāghava । kalpanāpadāpekṣaṃ strītvaṃ । ataḥ tanmātrādi ahaṅkārotpannaṃ tanmātrādikam । tanmātrakāraṇasyāhaṅkārasya cittvāt । dvitvaikatve kva saṃsthite bhavataḥ । na sta iti bhāvaḥ । nanu dvitvaṃ mā bhavatu । ekatvaṃ kathaṃ nāstīti cen । svapratipakṣaṃ dvitvaṃ vinaikatvasyāpy asiddheḥ । na hi chāyāṃ vinā prakāśaḥ prakāśo bhavati anirvācyatvāt ।।

evaṃ cidekamayatvaṃ sarvasya prasādhya bhedatyāgaṃ śiṣyaṃ prati anuṣṭheyatvena vidadhāti

jīvahetāv asantyāge tvaṃ cāhaṃ ceti santyaja ।
śeṣaṃ sadasator madhye bhavetyarthātmako bhavet ।।

puruṣaḥ । itiśabdākṣiptagurūpadeśavākyārthātmakaḥ । bhavet । itiśabdākṣiptaṃ gurūpadeśam āha tvaṃ cāhaṃ ceti tyaja । yena jīvatā dūre gacchatīti bhāvaḥ । punaḥ kiṃrūpaḥ tiṣṭhāmīty । atrāha śeṣam iti । sadasatoḥ madhye sthitaṃ sattvāsattvābhyām anirvacanārhaṃ । śeṣaṃ sarvaprapañcabādhe api sākṣitayā śuddhaṃ cinmātraṃ ।।

evaṃ śiṣyaṃ prati abhedaṃ vidheyatvenoktvā tatkṛpayā punar apy abhedam eva kathayati

citā yathādau kalitā svasattā sā tathoditā ।
abhinnā dṛśyate vyomnaḥ sattāsatte atha vedmy aham ।।

citādau sargārambhe । svasattā sphurāmītirūpā nijā sattā । yathā yena jīvādirūpeṇa । asyā ity adhyāhāryam । asyāḥ citaḥ sā sattā । tathā tena rūpeṇoditā prādurbhūtā satī । cidākāśāt abhinnā dṛśyate । jñānibhir iti śeṣaḥ । aham ity anena sattāsāmānyapramātā kathitaḥ । athāhaṃ sattāsatte vedmi jānāmi । na tu tathāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

citkhaṃ khaṃ jagadīhāḥ khaṃ kham abdhivibudhācalāḥ ।
khākāraciccamatkārarūpatvān nānyad asti hi ।।

citkhaṃ kham ākāśaṃ bhavati । jagatāṃ hitāhitaprāptiparihārārthāḥ ceṣṭāḥ । abdhiś ca vibudhāś cācalāś ca । te api kham eva bhavanti । atra hetutvenottarārdham āha khākāreti । khākāraḥ yaḥ ciccamatkāraḥ । sa eva rūpaṃ yasya । tasya bhāvaḥ tattvaṃ । tasmāt khākāraciccamatkārarūpatvāt । yataḥ sarvaṃ kharūpaṃ ciccamatkāramātrarūpaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ ।।

yo yadvilāsas tasmāt sa na kadācana bhidyate ।
api sāvayavāt tattvāt kaivānavayave kathā ।।

yaḥ yadvilāsaḥ yasya sphuraṇaṃ bhavati । saḥ sāvayavāt tattvād api tasmāt kadā na jātu na । bhidyate । na hi kaścit taraṅgaṃ toyāt bhinnaṃ vadatīti bhāvaḥ । anavayave avayavarahite । svapne api tad vācyam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu citaḥ jagadrūpatve api tadgrāhiṇyā anyasyāś citaḥ sadbhāvāt nābhedamayatety । atrāha

citer nityam acetyāyāś cin nāsty avitatākṛteḥ ।
yad rūpaṃ jagato rūpaṃ tattatsphuraṇarūpiṇaḥ ।।

nityam acetyāyāḥ cetitum ayogyāyāḥ । citeḥ cit svagrāhiṇī cit । nāsti cidrūpatvahāner iti bhāvaḥ । citeḥ kathambhūtāyāḥ । avitatākṛteḥ । sūkṣmatayāvitatā kutrāpi na sthitākṛtiḥ rūpaṃ yasyāḥ । sā । nanu etad asiddhaṃ । sphurāmītirūpeṇa yuktatvād ity । atrāha yad rūpam iti । yat sphurāmītyādikaṃ । tad ity adhyāhāryam । tat jagata eva rūpam । mukhyataḥ cititvaṃ hi sphurāmīty asya grāhikāyāḥ citer eva । sphurāmīti grāhyarūpāyās tu gauṇaṃ cititvaṃ bhavad api na jagattvaṃ vyabhicarati । kathambhūtasya jagataḥ । tattatsphuraṇarūpiṇaḥ । tattatsphuraṇāni sphurāmītyādīni । tasya tattatsphuraṇarūpiṇaḥ । yat kiñcic cetyatām āyāti tat sarvaṃ jagad evety arthaḥ ।।

mano buddhir ahaṅkāro bhūtāni girayo diśaḥ ।
iti paryāyaracanā citas tattvāj jagatsthiteḥ ।।

mano buddhir ityādirūpeṇoktā śabdasantatiḥ । citaḥ paryāyaracanā bhavati । kutaḥ । jagatsthiteḥ manobuddhyādirūpāyāḥ jagatsthiteḥ । tattvāt cidrūpatvāt । sarve śabdāḥ cidvācakā eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

citaś cittvaṃ jagad viddhi nājagac cittvam asti hi ।
ajagattvād acic cit syād bhāvābhedāj jagat kutaḥ ।।

citaḥ sambandhi cittvaṃ cidbhāvaṃ । yena sā cid iti nāmayogyā bhavati sa ko api dharmaḥ । tam iti yāvat । jagat viddhi jānīhi । atra hetum āha neti । cittvam ajagat jagato vyatiriktaṃ । cetyarūpajagadabhāve anirvācyāyāḥ citaḥ sphuṭaṃ cittvāyogyatvāt । avāntaraṃ phalitam āha ajagad iti । ata ity adhyāhāryam । cit ajagattvād dhetor । acit syāt cinnāmayogyā na syāt । yadi jagan na syād anirvācyāyāḥ citer api cittvaṃ na syād iti bhāvaḥ । paramaṃ phalitam āha bhāvābhedād iti । bhāvābhedāt pūrvanyāyasiddhena cijjagator abhedena siddhāt padārthābhedāt । jagat kutaḥ kathaṃ । cittvajagator abhede sati cittvasya cidekamayatayā cita eva sarvathā sthitatvāt jagan nāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

citer maricabījasya nijā yāntaś camatkṛtiḥ ।
saivaiṣā jīvatanmātramātraṃ jagad iti sthitā ।।

citeḥ cinnāmnaḥ । maricabījasyāntaḥ madhye । yā camatkṛtiḥ arthāt tīkṣṇatāsthānīyaḥ svaśaktyāsvādākhyaḥ camatkāraḥ । saivaiṣā jagad iti jagadrūpeṇa । kathambhūtaṃ jagat । jīvatanmātramātraṃ kevalaṃ jīvapañcatanmātrasvarūpaṃ । na tu sthūlabhūtamayaṃ । svapnanyāyena sthūlatāyā asatyatvāt ।।

cittvāt svaśaktikacanaṃ yad ahambhāvanaṃ citeḥ ।
jīvaḥ spandātmakarmātmā bhaviṣyadabhidho hy asau ।।

citeḥ svaśaktikacanaṃ svaśaktisphuraṇarūpaṃ । ahambhāvanaṃ yad asti । kutaḥ । cittvāt cidbhāvākhyāt hetoḥ । hi niścaye । asau svaśaktisphuraṇaṃ । jīvaḥ bhavati । jīvāpekṣayā puṃliṅgatā । kathambhūto jīvaḥ । spandātma kiñcitsphuraṇarūpaṃ । yat karma । spandātmakarmātmā citspandarūpa evety arthaḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtaḥ । bhaviṣyadabhidhaḥ vaikharīprādurbhāva ity arthaḥ ।।

yac cic cittvena kalanaṃ susampādyābhidhārthadik ।
vyavacchedavikārais tad bhidyate ato na vidyate ।।

cit ārṣaḥ ṣaṣṭhīlopaḥ citaḥ । yat cittvena cidbhāvena । kalanaṃ paricchedaḥ । susampādyā sukhena sampādayituṃ śakyābhidhārthadik nāmārthaleśaḥ yena । tat susampādyābhidhārthadik । paricchinnasyaiva hi vastunaḥ nāma tadvācyatvaṃ ca kartuṃ śakyaṃ । tat bhidyate citaḥ bhinnatvena sthīyate । vyavacchedavikāraiḥ । cittaṃ na spṛśatīti yāvat । bhavantu jaḍebhyaḥ bhinnatāpādanāni । tadyuktatvād iti yāvat । atrāhāta iti । ataḥ cito bhinnatvāt । na vidyate । cidbhinnasya cetyamānatāyogāt । tadayoge ca sato api । cidrūpatvena kalanābhāvena vyarthasya cittvasyāpy abhāvaḥ । cittvābhāve ca jagato abhāvaḥ । tadabhāve ca śuddhasya cinmātrasyaiva sāmrājyam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu bhavatu cidekamayatvaṃ sarvasya । tadaṃśabhūtayoḥ kartṛkarmaṇos tu parasparaṃ bhedo durnivāra ity । atrāha

citspandarūpiṇor asti na bhedaḥ kartṛkarmaṇoḥ ।
spandamātraṃ bhavet karma sa eva puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

citspandarūpiṇoḥ citsphūrtyākhyarūpayuktayoḥ । kartṛkarmaṇoḥ bhedaḥ nāsti । katham etad ity । spandamātraṃ karma bhavet । bahiḥspandasyaiva karmatvadarśanāt । sa eva puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ । paṇḍitair iti śeṣaḥ । antaḥ vicāryamāṇaṃ jñānaṃ vinā na kiñcil labhyate । ghaṭapaṭādiś ca bahirbhūtaḥ । ataḥ jñānasya taiḥ saha ko api sambandho nāstīti śuddhaṃ jñānaṃ śiṣṭaṃ । sa eva ca citaḥ sphuraṇākhyaḥ spandaḥ । bahiḥsthitasya śarīracalanādirūpasya karmaṇo api tatpūrvakatvāt । antar anyasyānupalambhāt bahiḥśarīrasya mṛtpiṇḍarūpasya puruṣatvāyogāt iti siddhaṃ karmaṇaḥ puruṣatvam ।।

sarvasya jīvāder vargasyaikatvaṃ sādhayati

jīvaś cittve parispandaḥ puṃsāṃ cittaṃ sa eva ca ।
manas tv indriyarūpaṃ san nānānānaiva gacchati ।।

jīvaḥ cittve cidbhāve । citsvarūpa iti yāvat । parispandaḥ bhavati । puṃsāṃ sa eva karmāparaparyāyaṃ cittaṃ bhavati । parispanda eva ca । citspandatvavyatiriktasya jīvasya cittasya vābhāvāt । tu viśeṣe । mana eva citspandarūpaṃ cittam । indriyarūpaṃ sat । nānānānātvaṃ gacchati । cittaṃ kathambhūtam eva । paramārthataḥ ekatvāt nānātvarahitaṃ । idam atra tātparyam । jīvas tāvat citspanda eva । taccittam api vikalpātmakaṃ tathaiva । tad eva ca cittam indriyarūpeṇa pariṇamate । tataś ca svapariṇāmabhūtendriyadvāreṇa bahir nirgatya rūpādipañcakasvarūpaviṣayarūpatām āpadyate । tataś ca tadādhārabhūtapañcakatām āsādyate । tataś ca tatkāryabhāvena pariṇamate iti citspanda eva sthūlasūkṣmabhāvarūpeṇa sthitaḥ । sa ca cidavyatirikta iti sarvaṃ cidrūpam eva sthitam iti ।।

śāntāśeṣaviśeṣaṃ hi citprakāśacchaṭā jagat ।
kāryakāraṇakāditvaṃ tasmād anyan na vidyate ।।

hi yasmāt arthe । aśeṣaṃ samastaṃ jagat citprakāśacchaṭā citprakāśe siddhapadārthapaṅktimayatvāt citprakāśapaṅktiḥ । bhavati । śāntāḥ cinmātre pralīnāḥ । viśeṣāḥ bhāvāḥ yasya । kāryakāraṇakāditvam anyat cinmātrāt pṛthak । kāryakāraṇatvāder api jagattvena citprakāśacchaṭātvānapāyāt ।।

acchedyo aham adāhyo ayam akledyo aśoṣya eva ca ।
nityaḥ satatagaḥ sthāṇur acalo aham iti sthitam ।।sarvasya jīvāder jagataḥ citprakāśamayatve sati iti sthitam bhavati । ayaṃ niścaya eva pratiṣṭhito bhavati iti । kim iti । ahaṃ citprakāśarūpaḥ aham । acchedyaḥ aśarīravat chedayogyo nāsmi । evam adāhyo ayam ity ādāv api sambandhanīyam । ahaṃ nityo asmi । nityatve viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa hetum āha satataga iti । sarvakālaga ity arthaḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtaḥ । sthāṇuḥ svasvarūpe dṛḍhaṃ sthitaḥ । atrāpi hetum viśeṣaṇatvenāhācala iti । yataḥ niṣkampa ity arthaḥ ।।

nanu cidekamayatve sati vādinaḥ kimarthaṃ vivadanti ity । atrāha

vivadante yathā hy atra vivadante tathā bhramaiḥ ।
bhramanto na vayaṃ tv ete jātā vigatavibhramāḥ ।।

vādina iti śeṣaḥ । vādinaḥ tārkikādayaḥ । atra citprakāśe । yathā yena prakāreṇa । vivadante vivādaṃ kurvanti । tathā bhramaiḥ mithyājñānaiḥ । vivadante । jñātatattvānāṃ vivādābhāvāt । tathā hi । tārkikāḥ ātmānaṃ jñānaguṇaṃ saṃsāriṇaṃ ca kathayanti । sāṅkhyāḥ udāsīnaṃ jñānarūpam api paramāṇurūpam । cārvākā bhūtarūpaṃ । bauddhāḥ śūnyarūpaṃ । vedāntinaḥ śāntasvarūpaṃ । evam anye apy anyat kiñcit । yady api ete adhikārikṛpayaiva vivadante tathāpi adhikāriṇāṃ tattatpadaniṣṭhānām adhaḥsthaṃ padaṃ parityajyordhvapadagamanārthaṃ vādināṃ bhramaḥ uktaḥ । yadi vādinaḥ bhrameṇa vivadante tarhi yūyaṃ kathaṃ sthitāḥ ity । atrāha bhramanta iti । tu vyatireke । ete vayaṃ vigatabhramāḥ vādyuktanānāguṇottīrṇaśuddhacinmātrāṅgīkārāt dūrībhūtamithyājñānāḥ । jātāḥ । na bhramanta ity arthaḥ । nanu śrīvasiṣṭhena tanmatanirāsapareṇa vivāda eva kṛtaḥ । bodhanārthatanmatanirāse api cinmātrāṅgīkāreṇaiva sarvamatāṅgīkārāt । cinmātraṃ hi sarve aṅgīkurvanty eva । kiṃ tu tadviśeṣeṣu vivadante ।।

punar api cidekamayatvam eva kathayati

dṛśye mūrte ajñasaṃrūḍhe vikārādi pṛthag bhavet ।
nāmūrte tajjñakacite citkhe sadasadātmani ।।

mūrte sthūle । dṛśye dṛśikriyāviṣaye bhāvajāte । kathambhūte । saṃrūḍhe dṛḍhībhūte । mūrkhajñāte iti yāvat । ādiśabdāt pariṇāmāder grahaṇam । sthūlasya dṛśyasya vikārādidharmādhikaraṇatve yogyatāstīti bhāvaḥ । tajjñakacite tattvajñeṣu sphurite । vikārādi pṛthak na bhavet । kathambhūte citkhe । sadasadātmani sadasatsvarūpe । vikārādi yadi sat tadāpi tanmayam eva । yady asat tadāpi tathaiveti bhāvaḥ ।।

cittattvaṃ cetyarasataḥ śaktīḥ kālādināmikāḥ ।
tanoty ākāśaviśadāś cinmadhuśrīḥ svamañjarīḥ ।।

cinmadhuśrīḥ cidākhyāvasantalakṣmīḥ । kālādināmikāḥ kāladeśādināmayuktāḥ । śaktīḥ svamañjarīḥ tanoti vistārayati । cetyarasataḥ cetyāsvādena yuktam । yuktaṃ ca vasantalakṣmyāḥ rasena mañjarītananam । cittattvam cinmātrarūpiṇya eva । śaktitadvator abhedāt । punaḥ kathambhūtāḥ । na tu bhāsamānasthūlarūpayuktāḥ ।।

svabhāvena cinmātrasya cetyarūpatayā sphuraṇaṃ kathayati

svayaṃ vicitraṃ sphurati citkañcukam anāhatam ।
svayaṃ vicitraṃ kacati cidratnam apakāraṇam ।।

citkañcukam । kañcukaṃ lakṣaṇayā paṭaḥ । cidākhyaḥ paṭaḥ । vicitraṃ sphurati citrapaṭavat vicitratāyuktaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ । vicitratā cārthacetyakṛtā jñeyā । tathā cidratnaṃ svayaṃ vicitraṃ kacati । ratnasya ca kacanaṃ yuktam eva । svayam ity asyārthaṃ svayam evāhāpakāraṇaṃ iti ।।

svayaṃ vilakṣaṇaspandaś cidvāyur ajaḍātmakaḥ ।
svayaṃ vicitravalanaṃ cidvāri na nikhātagam ।।

vilakṣaṇaspandaḥ bāhyavāyoḥ vyatiriktaspandayuktaḥ । atra hetutvena viśeṣaṇam āha ajaḍātmaka iti । jaḍājaḍayoḥ spando avaśyaṃ vilakṣaṇa eva syād iti bhāvaḥ । vāri nikhātagaṃ sat । vicitravalanaṃ vicitrasphuraṇaṃ bhavati । cidvāri tu nikhātagaṃ sat । vicitravalanaṃ na bhavati ।।

svayaṃ vicitradhātūccaiś cicchṛṅgam apanirmitam ।
svayaṃ citrarasollāsā cijjyotsnā satatoditā ।।

uccaiḥ cicchṛṅgam apanirmitam nirmāṇarahitam । vicitrā nānāvidhāḥ । dhātavaḥ bhūtākhyāni kāraṇadravyāṇi । bhavati । śṛṅgam api vicitradhātu vicitragairikādidhātuyuktaṃ bhavati । kiṃ tu nirmitam । svayaṃ cijjyotsnā citrarasollāsā nānāvidhacetyarasollāsayuktā । tayā satatoditā bhavati । bāhyajyotsnāpi vicitrāmṛtarasollāsayuktā bhavati । kiṃ tu śuklapakṣa evoditā bhavati ।।

svayaṃ sadaiva prakaṭaś cidāloko amalātmakaḥ ।
svayam astaṅgatevājñe jñe jñānād uditā citiḥ ।।

ālokasya prakaṭatāguṇayuktatvāt iti bhāvaḥ । citiḥ svayaṃ ajñe mūrkhe । astaṅgateva bhavati । astaṅgatatvaṃ ca asyāḥ sthitāyāḥ api jñānāviṣayībhāva evāta ivaśabdopādānam । citiḥ svayaṃ jñe jñānayukte । jñānād uditā bhavati । yathākāśe jvalann api sūryo andhaṃ praty anuditaḥ । netrasahitaṃ prati tūditaḥ । evam iyam apīti bhāvaḥ ।।

svayaṃ jaḍeṣu jāḍyena padaṃ sauṣuptam āgatā ।
svayaṃ spandi tathāspandi cittvāc citimahānabhaḥ ।।

citiḥ jaḍeṣu sthāvarādiṣu । jāḍyena jaḍabhāvena । svayaṃ sauṣuptapadaṃ suṣuptisthānam । citimahānabhaḥ cidākhyo mahākāśaḥ । svayam spandi sphurattāyuktaṃ bhavati । tathā tena prakāreṇāspandi śāntatāyukto bhavati । bāhyākāśasya tu vātarūpeṇa saspandatvaṃ svarūpeṇāspandatvam ।।

guṇini guṇavat citi jagataḥ sadasattvaṃ kathayati

citprakāśaprakāśo hi jagad asti ca nāsti ca ।
cidākāśaikaśūnyatvaṃ jagad asti ca nāsti ca ।।

hi niścaye । citprakāśaprakāśaḥ । citprakāśasya cidākhyasya tejasaḥ । prakāśaḥ ālokākhyaguṇabhūtaḥ । jagat asti ca nāsti ca । cakāraḥ svayaṃ astitvanāstitvayoḥ samapradhānatvaṃ dyotayati । ayaṃ bhāvaḥ । yathā tejorūpe guṇini ālokākhyo guṇaḥ bhedena bhāsamānatvāt asti । tato vyatirekeṇa labdhum aśakyatvān nāsti । tathā jagad api cidākhye ādhārabhūte guṇini bhāsamānatvād asti । tadvyatirekeṇa labdhum aśakyatvān nāstīti । evam agre api yojyam । cidākāśeti । cidākāśasyaikaṃ śūnyatvaṃ śūnyatvākhyo guṇaḥ । cidākāśaikaśūnyatvam ।।

cidālokamahārūpaṃ jagad asti ca nāsti ca ।
cinmārutaghanaspando jagad asti ca nāsti ca ।।

mahārūpaṃ bhāsuraḥ śuklākhyaguṇaḥ । spandasya ca vāyuguṇatvaṃ prasiddham eva ।।

cidghanadhvāntakṛṣṇatvaṃ jagad asti ca nāsti ca ।
cidarkālokadivaso jagad asti ca nāsti ca ।।

dhvāntasya ca kṛṣṇatvaṃ guṇaḥ । divasasyārkālokānuvidhāyitvāt tadguṇatvam ।।

pūrvoktaṃ dṛḍhayituṃ sarvathā cidguṇatvam eva jagataḥ kathayati

citkajjalarajaḥśailaparamāṇur jagadbhramaḥ ।
cidagnyauṣṇyaṃ jagallekhā jagac cicchaṅkhaśuklatā ।।

cit eva kajjalarajaḥśailaḥ añjanādriḥ । paramāṇoḥ parvataguṇatvaṃ tadāśritatvenopacārāj jñeyam । jagadākāraḥ jagadbhramaḥ । jagallekhā jagatpaṅktiḥ ।।

jagac cicchailajaṭharaṃ cijjaladravatā jagat ।
jagac cidikṣumādhuryaṃ citkṣīrasnigdhatā jagat ।।

jagat cicchailasya jaṭharam antaḥsthaḥ sārarūpaḥ bhāgaḥ । snigdhatā snehākhyo guṇaḥ ।।

jagac ciddhimaśītatvaṃ cijjvālājvalanaṃ jagat ।
jagac citsarpiṣi sneho vīciś citsarito jagat ।।

cijjvālā cidākhyāgniśikhā । tasyā jvalanaṃ jvalanakriyā । vīceḥ racanārūpatvāt jalaguṇatvam ।।

jagac citkṣaudramādhuryaṃ jagac citkanakāṅgadam ।
jagac citpuṣpasaugandhyaṃ cillatāgraphalaṃ jagat ।।

rūpatvena guṇatvam । phalasya latāguṇatvaṃ tadāśritatvenopacārāt ।।

phalitam āha

citsattaiva jagatsattā jagatsattaiva cidvapuḥ ।
atra bhedavikārādi na khe malam iva sthitam ।।

ataḥ citsattaiva jagatsattā bhavati । jagatsattaiva cidvapur bhavati । na hi guṇasattā guṇino bhinnā guṇisattā ca guṇād bhinnā bhavatīti bhāvaḥ । ādiśabdena pariṇāmāder grahaṇam । sthitaṃ na bhava-ti । khe ākāśe ।।

jagataḥ sadasanmayatām upasaṃharati

itīdaṃ sanmayatvena sadasad bhuvanatrayam ।
avikalpyatadātmatvāt sattāsatte tad eva vā ।।

iti pūrvoktaprakāreṇa । bhuvanatrayaṃ bhūrbhuvaḥsvarākhyaṃ jāgradādikaṃ vā bhuvanatritayaṃ । sanmayatvena satsvarūpacidvikāratvena । mūlakāraṇāyāḥ citaḥ sadasadasattve sattāsattādhāratvakṛtaṃ bhedam āśaṅkyāha avikalpyeti । vāśabdaḥ pakṣāntaradyotakaḥ । tad eva tribhuvanam eva । sattāsatte bhavati । avikalpyatadātmatvāt । avikalpyaḥ sattvāsattvavikalpāyogyaḥ । yaḥ tadātmā cidātmā । tasya bhāvaḥ tattvaṃ। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ । sadasad iti padadvayam astināstikriyākartāraṃ kathayati । tathā ca kartṛkarmavikalpaḥ durnivāraḥ । sattāsatte tu śuddhanirālambāstināstikriyāvācake avikalpyaṃ citsvarūpam eva kathayataḥ । tadabhinnasya tribhuvanasyāpi sattāsattātvam eva yuktaṃ । na sadasattvam iti ।।

nanu jagadbrahmaṇor avayavāvayavibhāvo astu ity । atrāha

avayavāvayavitāśabdārthau śaśaśṛṅgavat ।
anubhūtyapalāpāya kalpitau yair dhig astu tān ।।

yaiḥ jaḍaiḥ । anubhūtyapalāpāya jagaccidaikyākhyam anubhavam apalapituṃ । avayavāvayavitāśabdaḥ avayavāvayavibhāvākhyaḥ śabdaḥ । arthaḥ tadvācyaḥ sambandhaviśeṣaḥ । tau avayavāvayavitāśabdārthau । kalpitau svavikalpena sambhāvitau । kathaṃ kalpitau । yathā kaścid bahir asad api śaśaśṛṅgaṃ kalpayati । tān dhig astu te dhikkāraviṣayā evety arthaḥ । dhikkāraviṣayatvaṃ ca teṣāṃ avayavābhinnasyāvayavinaḥ bhedena jñānāt । na hy avayavabhinno avayavī nāma kaścid astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

na vidyate jagad yatra sādridyūrvīnadīśvaram ।
cidekatvāt prasaṅgaḥ syāt kas tatretaravibhrame ।।

yatra yasmin cidrūpākhye sthāne । sādridyūrvīnadīśvaram parvatākāśabhūmisamudrasahitaṃ । jagat । cidekatvāt cidaikyāt । na vidyate । tatretaravibhrame ṣaṣṭhyarthe saptamī । itarasya tatkāryarūpasya bhramasya ।।

citaḥ sarvamayatvaṃ śilādṛṣṭāntena kathayati

śilāhṛdayapīnāpi svākāśaviśadaiva cit ।
dhatte antar akhilaṃ śāntaṃ sanniveṣaṃ yathā śilā ।।

cit śāntaṃ paramārthato bhāvābhāvādikṣobharahitaṃ । sanniveśaṃ cetyākhyaṃ racanāviśeṣam । antaḥ svamadhya eva । śilāhṛdayapīnāpi । prakāśākhyasārabharitatvena śilāhṛdayavat pīnāpi satī । svākāśaviśadaiva । suṣṭhu ākāśavat viśadā nirmalā eva । na tu jagadantardhāraṇe yogyā । atra dṛṣṭāntam āha yatheti । śilā yathā sāreṇa pūritāpi lekhaughākhyaṃ sanniveśaṃ antar dhatte ।।

nanu tathāpy ahaṃ praṣṭā bhinna evāsmy । anyathā praśnāyogād ity । atrāha

padārthanikarākāśe tvam ākāśalavopamaḥ ।
tvattāmattātmatātvattāmattollekhā na santi te ।।

padārthanikarākāśe । padārthānāṃ nikaraḥ samūhaḥ । sa eva nakiñcidrūpatvenāvakāśaḥ । tanmadhya ity arthaḥ । ākāśalavopamaḥ asi । phalitam āha tvatteti । ataḥ te tava praṣṭuḥ । tvattāmattātmatātvattāmattollekhāḥ । tvattāmattātmatayā tvadbhāvamadbhāvarūpatvena । tvattāmattollekhāḥ tvadbhāvamadbhāvavikalpāḥ । tvadbhāvarūpatvena sthitāḥ tvattāvikalpāḥ । madbhāvarūpatvena sthitā mattāvikalpāḥ । ākāśarūpatvāt ।।

pallavadṛṣṭāntena prakṛtaṃ citaḥ sarvamayatvaṃ kathayati

pallavāntaralekhaughasanniveśavad ātatam ।
anyānanyātmakam idaṃ dhatte antaś cit svabhāvataḥ ।।

cit । kutaḥ । nanu kayāpi prayojanāpekṣayā kathambhūtaṃ । anyaḥ svataḥ bhinnaḥ । ananyaḥ svato abhinnaḥ । ātmā yasya । tat anyānanyātmakam । punaḥ kathambhūtam । ātataṃ vistārayuktam । kathaṃ dhatte । pallavāntare pallavamadhye sthitaḥ । lekhaughasanniveśaḥ iva pallavāntaralekhaughasanniveśavat । pallave lekhaughasya ca bhāsamānatvena bhinnatvaṃ pṛthakkṛtya labdhum aśakyatvād abhinnatvaṃ ca sphuṭam sthitam evety upamānam ।।

samastakāraṇaughānāṃ kāraṇādipitāmaham ।
svabhāvato akāraṇātma cittvaṃ viddhy anubhūtitaḥ ।।

tvaṃ । svabhāvataḥ svarūpeṇānubhūtitaḥ svānubhavena । na tu matkathanamātreṇākāraṇātma akāraṇaḥ । kāraṇarahitaḥ ātmā svarūpaṃ yasya । tādṛśaṃ । kāraṇanāmnādibhūtaḥ yaḥ pitāmahaḥ । tatsvarūpaṃ kāraṇādipitāmahaṃ । samastakāraṇaughānāṃ । samastasya dṛśyasya । ye kāraṇaughāḥ । sarvasya dṛśyasya kāraṇāni pañcatanmātrāṇi । teṣāṃ kāraṇam ahaṅkāraḥ । tatkāraṇaṃ cittvam iti ।।

nanu jagadvat cid api asatyaiva bhavatv ity । atrāha

na cāsattvam acetyāyāś cito vācāpi sidhyati ।
yad asti tad udetīti dṛṣṭaṃ bījād ivāṅkuram ।।

acetyāyāḥ cetyamalādūṣitāyāḥ । citaḥ asattvaṃ vācāpi na sidhyati vaktum apīdaṃ na yogyam ity arthaḥ । atra hetutvenottarārdham āha yad iti । yataḥ yad asti tad udeti anyatayā prādurbhavati । iti dṛṣṭam asmābhir iti śeṣaḥ । atra dṛṣṭāntam āha bījād iti । ayaṃ bhāvaḥ । yathā bījabhāvena sthitam aṅkuraṃ bījāt udeti । tathā cinmātrasvarūpeṇa sthitaṃ cetyam api । tathā ca cetyānyathānupapattyā cinmātrasyāsatyatvaṃ na yuktam iti ।।

sargāntaślokena pūrvoktaṃ saṅgṛhṇāti

gaganam iva suśūnyabhedam asti tribhuvanam aṅga mahācito antar asyāḥ ।
paramapadamayaṃ samastadṛśyaṃ tv idam iti niścayavān bhavānubhūteḥ ।।

he aṅga । tribhuvanaṃ asyāḥ mahācitaḥ cinmātrasyāntaḥ madhye । suśūnyabhedam । suśūnyaḥ atiśayena nakiñcidrūpaḥ । bhedo yasya । sarvathā svarūpabhedarahitam ity arthaḥ । kim iva । yathā gaganaṃ bhedarahitam asti । phalitam āha parameti । ataḥ tvaṃ iti niścayavān evaṃ niścayayukto । bhava । anubhūtitaḥ svānubhavena । na tu maduktyā kṛtena śraddhāmātreṇa iti । samastadṛśyaṃ paramapadamayaṃ sarvottīrṇacitsvarūpam eva ।।

śrīvālmīkir bharadvājaṃ prati tatratyaṃ sargāntaślokena dināvasānaṃ kathayati

ity uktavaty atha munau divaso jagāma sāyantanāya vidhaye astam ino jagāma ।
snātuṃ sabhā kṛtanamaskaraṇā jagāma śyāmākṣaye ravikaraiś ca sahājagāma ।।

iti pūrvoktaṃ । uktavati kathayati sati । atha pūrvaślokoktopadeśānantaram । atra hetum āha astam iti । sabhā śrotṝṇāṃ sabhā । sāyantanavidhaye sāyantanāgnihotrādyarthaṃ । snānaṃ vinā kutrāpi vidhāv adhikārābhāvāt । sā sabhā śyāmākṣaye rātryavasāne । dinādāv iti yāvat । ravikaraiḥ sūryakiraṇaiḥ । saha । śravaṇārtham iti śeṣaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyām utpattiprakaraṇe caturdaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ pūrvadine kathyamānam upastauti

jagad ākāśam evedaṃ yathā hi vyomni mauktikam ।
vimale bhāti khātmaiva jagac cidgagane tathā ।।

idam anubhūyamānaṃ । ākāśam eva bhavati । atra hetutvena dṛṣṭāntayuktaṃ vākyam āha yathā hīti । yasmāt jagat vimale cidgagane cidākāśe । khātmaiva cidākāśasvarūpam eva । yathā vyomni bhūtākāśe । mauktikaṃ muktāsamūho । yathā gagane bhramadṛṣṭyā dṛśyamānaṃ mauktikam ākāśam eva tathā cidgagane dṛśyamānaṃ jagad api cidgaganam eveti ।।

anutkīrṇaiva bhātīva trijagatsālabhañjikā ।
citstambhe na ca sotkīrṇā na cotkartātra vidyate ।।

citstambhe cidākhye stambhe । trijagatsālabhañjikā trijagadākhyā putrikānutkīrṇaiva satī । bhātīva । paramārthatas tu na bhātītīvaśabdopādānam । nanu kimarthaṃ notkīrṇāstīty । sā jagadākhyā putrikā । arhapratyayārtho atra svayaṃ boddhavyaḥ । utkartuṃ yogyā na bhavati । nakiñcidrūpatvāt । na cātrotkartā utkaraṇakartā । vidyate ।।

samudre antar jalāspandāḥ svabhāvād acyutā api ।
vidi vedyā bhavantīva pare dṛśyavidas tathā ।।

yathety adhyāhāryam । samudre antaḥ samudrāntarbhāge sthitāḥ । jalāspandāḥ taraṅgāḥ । svabhāvād acyutā api jalākhyāt svarūpād abhraṣṭā api । yathā vidi jñāne viṣaye । vedyāḥ vīcitayā vedituṃ yogyā । bhavantīva । paramārthatas tu na bhavantīti ivaśabdopādānam । tathā pare uttīrṇe citsvarūpe । dṛśyavidaḥ dṛśyarūpā vidaḥ । dṛśyānīti yāvat ।।

jalāntargatasūryābhājālakāracanāny api ।
jagadbhānaṃ prati sthūlāny aṇuṃ prati yathācalāḥ ।।

jalasyāntargatā sūryābhā jalāntargatasūryābhā । tasyāḥ jālakāracanāni jalāntargatasūryābhājālakāracanāny api । svabhāvaś cāyaṃ jalāntargatā sūryābhā jālakarūpā sampadyate । tāni jagadbhānaṃ prati tathā sthūlāni bhavanti । yathācalāḥ parvatāḥ । aṇuṃ prati sthūlāḥ bhavanti ।।

uktaṃ dṛṣṭāntasthūlatvaṃ dṛḍhayati jagadbhānam abhānābhaṃ brahmaṇo avyatirekataḥ ।
jalasūryāṃśujālaṃ tu vyatirekānubhūtidam ।।

jagadbhānam abhānābhaṃ bhavati । brahmaṇaḥ avyatirekataḥ brahmarūpatvād ity arthaḥ । jalasūryāṃśujālaṃ vyatirekānubhūtidam bhedaprathākāri bhavati । ato atra sthūlatvaṃ yuktam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

anubhūtāny apīmāni jagati vyomarūpiṇi ।
pṛthvyādīni na santy eva svapnasaṅkalpayor iva ।।

vyomarūpiṇi cinmātrākāśasvarūpe । svapnasaṅkalpayor iva । svapne saṅkalpe ca anubhūtāny api pṛthvyādīni । tathety arthaḥ ।।

piṇḍagrāhaḥ sad ity asmin vijñānākāśarūpiṇi ।
marunadyāṃ jalam iva na sambhavati kutracit ।।

grahaṇaṃ grāhaḥ । piṇḍavat grāhaḥ piṇḍagrāhaḥ । sad iti piṇḍagrāhaḥ sadvyavahārahetuḥ piṇḍagrāhaḥ । vijñānākāśarūpiṇi asminn anubhūyamāne । bhavati । atra dṛṣṭāntam āha marunadyām iti ।।

nanv asatsvarūpe jagati dṛśyatā kathaṃ bhāti ity । atrāha

jagaty apiṇḍagrāhe asmin saṅkalpanagaropame ।
marau sarid ivābhāti dṛśyatā bhrāntirūpiṇī ।।

avidyamānaḥ piṇḍavat grāhaḥ yasya । tasmin apiṇḍagrāhe । saṅkalpanagaropame saṅkalpollikhitanagarasadṛśe । asmin jagati dṛśyatā dṛśyabhāvaḥ । bhrāntirūpiṇī mithyājñānarūpā । sarid iva ।।

bhramarūpatvenāsadrūpasya jagataḥ svapnavat tulādeśāpūraṇaṃ kathayati

svapnādriṇeva jagatā tulādeśau na kaucana ।
pūritau kalanonmuktā dṛśyaśrīr vyoma kevalam ।।

svapnādriṇeva svapnādrivat । jagatā tulādeśau pūritau na bhavataḥ । gurutvasyāsadrūpatvāt tulāpūraṇaṃ । vistārasyāsadrūpatvāt deśāpūraṇaṃ । etac ca svapnādau sarvapratītisiddham eveti tasya dṛṣṭāntatā । phalitam āha kalaneti । kalanonmuktā dṛśyatvākhyakalanāmuktā ।।

varjayitvājñavijñātajagacchabdārthabhāvanām ।
jagadbrahmakhaśabdānām arthe nāsty eva bhinnatā ।।

ajñaiḥ citsvarūpajñānaśūnyaiḥ । vijñātā svānubhavaviṣayīkṛtā । jagacchabdārthabhāvanā । jagad iti śabdasya । tadarthasya ca bhāvanānusandhānaṃ । tāṃ ajñavijñātajagacchabdārthabhāvanāṃ varjayitvā parityajya । jagadbrahmakhaśabdānām arthe bhinnatā bhedo । paryāyarūpā evaite śabdā ity arthaḥ । ajñasyājñātatattvatayā jagataḥ ākāśarūpatvaṃ na siddham iti jagatsatyatvaniṣṭhāyāḥ tadbhāvanāyāḥ parityāga uktaḥ ।।

idaṃ tv acetyacinmātrabhānor bhānaṃ nabhaḥ prati ।
tathā sūkṣmaṃ yathā meghaṃ prati saṅkalpavāridaḥ ।।

tu viśeṣe । acetyacinmātrabhānoḥ cetyādūṣitacitsūryasya । bhānam ābhāsaḥ । nabhaḥ prati bāhyākāśāpekṣayā । tathā tena prakāreṇa । yathā meghaṃ prati jāgraddṛṣṭameghāpekṣayā । saṅkalpavāridaḥ svavikalpollekhitaḥ meghaḥ sūkṣmo bhavati ।।

yathā svapnapuraṃ svacchaṃ jāgratpuravaraṃ prati ।
tathā jagad idaṃ svacchaṃ saṅkalpitajagat prati ।।

yathā laukikabuddhyā । jāgratpuravaraṃ prati svapnapuraṃ svacchaṃ kevalābhāsarūpatvena sthūlatākhyamalarahitaṃ । bhavati । idaṃ jāgraty anubhūyamānaṃ । saṅkalpitajagat prati svacchaṃ saṅkalpākhyamalarahitaśuddhacinmātrarūpatvāt nirmalaṃ bhavati । yady api jñāninaḥ svapnapuram api tādṛśam eva tathāpy ajñabodhanārtham evam uktam ।।

tasmād acetyacidrūpaṃ jagad vyomaiva kevalam ।
śūnyau vyomajagacchabdau paryāyau viddhi cinmayau ।।

tasmāt pūrvoktāt hetoḥ । acetyacidrūpaṃ śuddhacinmātrarūpaṃ । jagat । kevalaṃ vyomaiva bhavati । phalitam āha śūnyāv iti । ataḥ śūnyau piṇḍagrāhābhāvena nakiñcidrūpau । cinmayau citsvarūpau । vyomajagacchabdau paryāyau viddhi ekārthavācakatvāt ।।

vakṣyamāṇavṛttāntākāṅkṣayā pūrvoktam upasaṃharati tribhiḥ

tasmān na kiñcid utpannaṃ jagadādīha dṛśyakam ।
anākhyam anabhivyaktaṃ yathāsthitam avasthitam ।।

tasmāt cidekamayatvāt hetoḥ । jagadādi dṛśyaṃ kiñcit leśenāpi । utpannaṃ na bhavati । anākhyaṃ nāmānarham । atra hetutvena viśeṣaṇam āhānabhivyaktam indriyāgocaram । anyarūpatvena anabhivyaktasya hi nāmāyuktam । nanu tarhi apūrvatvaṃ jagataḥ syād ity āśaṅkya viśeṣaṇam āhāvasthitam iti । avasthitaṃ tiṣṭhat । yathāsthitaṃ । yathaiva pūrvaṃ tathaiva । na tv apūrvatayety arthaḥ । yathā pūrvaṃ sarpatayā jñātā rajjuḥ tataḥ rajjutayā jñātāpi pūrvavad eva tiṣṭhati । na tv anyarūpatāṃ prāpnoti ।।

jagad eva mahākāśaṃ cidākāśam abhittimat ।
tad deśasyāṇumātrasya tulāyāś cāprapūrakam ।।

jagat cidākāśam eva bhavati । kathambhūtaṃ cidākāśaṃ । mahākāśaṃ bāhyākāśāpekṣayā mahattvāt mahākāśākhyāyuktam । punaḥ kathambhūtam । abhittimat । jīvādiprapañcaḥ tattaddharmādhāratayā bhittiḥ । tadrahitam । phalitam āha tad iti । ataḥ tat cidākāśamayaṃ jagat । gurutvābhāvena vaipulyābhāvena cāṇumātrasya deśasya tulāyāś cāpūrakam bhavati । pūraṇakāri na bhavati ।।

tad eva punaḥ viśinaṣṭi

ākāśarūpam evācchaṃ piṇḍagrahavivarjitam ।
vyomni vyomamayaṃ citraṃ saṅkalpapuravat sthitam ।।

ākāśarūpam eva nakiñcidrūpam eva । acchaṃ śuddhabodhasvarūpaṃ । piṇḍagrahavivarjitam । piṇḍavat yaḥ grahaḥ । tena varjitam । yuktaṃ cākāśasya piṇḍagraharahitatvaṃ । vyomni cidākāśe । vyomamayaṃ cidākāśamayaṃ । citram ālekhyaṃ । saṅkalpapuravat saṅkalpollikhitapuravat । sthitam vyavatiṣṭhamānaṃ । saṅkalpapurasya cākāśamayatvaṃ tulādeśāpūrakatvaṃ ca yuktam eveti siddhaḥ sarvasya jagataḥ vivakṣitaḥ atyantābhāvaḥ । yac cotpattiḥ pūrvam uktā sāpy anutpattikalpatvenātyantābhāvasyaiva sādhanīti na pūrvāparavirodhaḥ ।।

atha jagataḥ tulādeśādyapūrakatvasādhakaṃ mahāvṛttāntaṃ vṛttāntakāmān prati kṛpayā kathayati

atredaṃ maṇḍapākhyānaṃ śṛṇu śravaṇabhūṣaṇam ।
niḥsandeho yathaiṣo arthaś citte viśrāntim eṣyati ।।

tvam । atra jagato deśādyapūrakatve । maṇḍapākhyānaṃ । maṇḍapeti nāmnā prasiddham ākhyānaṃ maṇḍapākhyānaṃ । śṛṇu । śravaṇabhūṣaṇaṃ śravaṇārham ity arthaḥ । atrāha niḥsandeha iti । niḥsandehaḥ sandehān niṣkrāntaḥ । arthaḥ ।।

tvarayāviṣṭaḥ śrīrāmaḥ maṇḍapākhyānaṃ prati śrīvasiṣṭhaṃ prārthayati

sadbodhavṛddhaye brahman samāsena vadāśu me ।
maṇḍapākhyānam akhilaṃ yena bodho vivardhate ।।

jagataḥ tulādeśāpūrakatvajñānaṃ sadbodhaḥ । phalitam āha yeneti । yena uditenety arthaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ maṇḍapākhyānam eva kathayati

abhūd asmin mahīpīṭhe kulapadmo vikāsavān ।
padmo nāma nṛpaḥ śrīmān bahuputro atikośavān ।।

asmin mahīpīṭhe padmo nāma nṛpaḥ abhūt । tasyaiva nānāvidhāni viśeṣaṇāny āha kuleti । vikāsavān kulapadmaḥ । padmasya ca vikāso yuktaḥ । padmaśabdo atra lakṣaṇayā śreṣṭhavācakaḥ । atikośavān bahubhāṇḍāgārayuktaḥ ।।

maryādāpālane ambhodhir dviṣattimirabhāskaraḥ ।
kāntākumudinīcandro doṣatṛṣṇāhutāśanaḥ ।।

ambhodheḥ maryādapālanaṃ prasiddham eva । kāntākumudinīcandraḥ । candratvam asya tadvikāsakāritvena । doṣatṛṣṇāhutāśanatvaṃ doṣatṛṣṇādāhakatvena ।।

merur vibudhavṛndānāṃ yaśaścandrodbhavārṇavaḥ ।
saraḥ sadguṇahaṃsānāṃ kalākamalabhāskaraḥ ।।

vibudhāḥ paṇḍitāḥ । ta eva vibudhā devāḥ । teṣāṃ । meruḥ bahukāñcanapradatvenāśrayatvena ca meruparvatasadṛśaḥ । yaśa iti । yaśaḥcandrodbhave arṇavaḥ samudraḥ । sadguṇarūpāṇāṃ haṃsānāṃ saraḥ । teṣāṃ vikāsapradatvena bhāskaraḥ ।।

śātravāmbhodapavano mattamātaṅgakesarī ।
samastavidyādayitaḥ sarvāścaryaguṇākaraḥ ।।

śātravaṃ śatrusamūhaḥ । sa evāmbhodaḥ meghaḥ । tasya pavanaḥ nāśakāritvāt । mātaṅgā atra śatrusenā yā vivakṣitāḥ । samastā yā vidyārūpāḥ nāyikāḥ । tāsāṃ dayitaḥ patiḥ । sarve ca te āścaryabhūtāḥ guṇāḥ । teṣām ākaraḥ utpattisthānam ।।

śūrārisāgarakṣobhavilasanmandarācalaḥ ।
vilāsapuṣpaughamadhuḥ saubhāgyakusumāyudhaḥ ।।

śūrāś ca te arayaḥ । tadrūpaḥ yaḥ sāgaraḥ । tasya kṣobhe vilasan mandarācalaḥ । vilāsā vibhramā eva । puṣpāṇi । tasya madhuḥ vasantaḥ । saubhāgyena subhagabhāvena । kusumāyudhaḥ kāmaḥ ।।

līlālatālāsyamarut sāhasotsavakeśavaḥ ।
saujanyakairavaśaśī durlīlālatikānalaḥ ।।

līlā iva latā । tasyā lāsye nartane । marut । līlāyukta ity arthaḥ । sāhasam eva hitāhitānapekṣaṃ karma eva । tasya keśavaḥ viṣṇuḥ । tasya hiraṇyākhyādivadhasāhasakāritvād upamānatvaṃ । saujanyam eva kairavaṃ । tasya vikāsakāritvāt śaśī candraḥ । durlīlālatikānāṃ dāhakatvād analaḥ agniḥ ।।

tasyāsīt subhagā bhāryā līlā nāma vilāsinī ।
sarvasaubhāgyavalitā kamalevoditāvanau ।।

tasya padmākhyasya rājñaḥ । līlā nāma bhāryā līlākhyā bhāryāsīt । asyā viśeṣaṇāny āha subhageti । subhagā praśastarūpayuktā । vilāsinī vilāsayuktā । sarvasaubhāgyaiḥ valitā bharitāvanau bhūmau । kamalevoditā utpannā ।।

sarvasampattivalitā līlāmadhurabhāṣiṇī ।
sānandamandacalitā dvitīyendūdayasmitā ।।

līleti । līlayā madhuraṃ bhāṣiṇī । sānandeti । sānandaṃ mandaṃ calitaṃ yasyāḥ । sā । dvitīyendūdayabhūtaṃ smitaṃ yasyāḥ ।।

alakālimanohārivadanāmbhojaśālinī ।
śītāṅgī karṇikāgaurī jaṅgameva sarojinī ।।

alakālyā manohāri yat vadanāmbhojaṃ । karṇikāvad gaurī । sarojiny api alimanohāri ambhojaśālinī śītāṅgī karṇikayā gaurī bhavati ।।

latāvilāsakundaughahāsinī rasaśālinī ।
prabālahastā puṣpāḍhyā madhuśrīr iva dehinī ।।

śālinī śṛṅgārasuśālinī । prabālavat hastau yasyāḥ । puṣpeti । puṣpair ābharaṇabhūtaiḥ puṣpair । āḍhyā । sāpi kundaughaiḥ hāsinī । rasena vasantarasena । śālinī ca bhavati ।।

avadātā tanuḥ puṇyā janatāhlādadāyinī ।
gaṅgeva gāṃ gatā devanadī haṃsavilāsinī ।।

avadātā tanuḥ sitāṅgī । janatāyāḥ āhlādadāyinī । haṃsavat vilāsayuktā । gatā । sāpi tādṛśy eva bhavati ।।

tasya bhūtalapuṣpeṣoḥ sakalāhlādadāyinaḥ ।
paricaryāṃ ciraṃ kartum anyā ratir ivoditā ।।

puṣpeṣoḥ rateḥ paricaryāṃ kartuṃ yuktatvāt etad uktam ।।

sargāntaślokena tasyāḥ satīguṇān āha

udvigne prodvignā muditā mudite samākulākulite ।
pratibimbasamā kāntā saṅkruddhe kevalaṃ bhītā ।।

sā kāntā । kathambhūtā । tasmin prodvigne sati । prodvignā । tasmin mudite sati । muditā । tasmin samākule sati । samākulā । tasmin saṅkruddhe sati । kevalaṃ bhītā । etāvanmātreṇaiva kevalaṃ sā viruddhāsīd iti bhāvaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyām utpattiprakaraṇe pañcadaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ tasya rājñaḥ tayā rājñyā saha krīḍām āha

bhūtalāpsarasā sārdham ananyavanitāpatiḥ ।
akṛtrimapremarasaṃ sa reme kāntayā tayā ।।

sa rājā । kāntayā sahākṛtrimaḥ premarasaḥ yatra tat akṛtrimapremarasaṃ । vakṣyamāṇeṣu sthāneṣu vakṣyamāṇaiḥ krīḍāviśeṣaiḥ । bhūtalāpsarasā । ananyavanitāpatiḥ nānyavanitāyāḥ patiḥ । tasyām eva rata ity arthaḥ ।।

krīḍāsthānāny āha

udyānavanagulmeṣu tamālagahaneṣu ca ।
puṣpamaṇḍapatalpeṣu latāvalayasadmasu ।।

udyānavaneṣu vihitāni yāni gulmāni veśmāni । puṣpaiḥ kṛtāni yāni maṇḍapatalpāni । maṇḍapaḥ janāśrayaḥ । latāvalayasadmasu latāmaṇḍalagṛheṣu ।।

puṣpāntaḥpuraśayyāsu puṣpasambhāravīthiṣu ।
vasantodyānadolāsu krīḍāpuṣkariṇīṣu ca ।।

puṣpaiḥ racitā yāḥ antaḥpuraśayyāḥ । puṣpasambhāreṇa puṣpasamūhena yuktāḥ vīthyaḥ mārgāḥ । vasante racitāḥ udyānadolāḥ ।।

candanadrumaṣaṇḍeṣu santānakataleṣu ca ।
kadambanimbageheṣu pāribhadrodareṣu ca ।।

ṣaṇḍāḥ samūhāḥ । santānakāḥ drumaviśeṣāḥ । kadambeti । kadambanimbataleṣu racitāni yāni gehāni । teṣu । pāribhadrāḥ vṛkṣaviśeṣāḥ ।।

śailakandarakaccheṣu vātāyanapureṣu ca ।
sarittaṭakaṭapreṣu vāraṇoparisadmasu ।।

śailakandareṣu sthitāḥ ye kacchāḥ । vātāyanayuktāni ca tāni purāṇi gṛhoparigṛhāṇi । sarittaṭānāṃ ye kaṭaprāḥ samūhāḥ । vāraṇoparikṛteṣu sadmasu ।।

grīṣme tuṣāraharmyeṣu latāmaṇḍapakeṣu ca ।
hemamandiravṛkṣeṣu muktāmāṇikyabhittiṣu ।।

tuṣāraharmyeṣu śītalagṛheṣu । hemamandiropariropitāḥ ye hemamandiravṛkṣāḥ । mukteti । muktāmāṇikyaiḥ racitāḥ bhittayaḥ yeṣāṃ gṛhāṇāṃ । teṣu ।।

vikasatkundamandāramakarandasugandhiṣu ।
vasantavanajāleṣu kūjatkokilamāliṣu ।।

vasante puṣpitāni yāni vanajālāni । vikasad iti kūjad iti ca viśeṣaṇadvayaṃ vasantavanajāleṣv ity asyaiva ।।

nānāratnatṛṇānāṃ ca sthaleṣu mṛdudīptiṣu ।
nirjhareṣu tarattāraśīkarāsāravarṣiṣu ।।

nānā ca tāni ratnabhūtāni tṛṇāni । sthaleṣu kathambhūteṣu । mṛdudīptiṣu kamaleṣv ity arthaḥ । nirjhareṣu kathambhūteṣu । tarantaḥ utthitavantaḥ ye tārāḥ udbhaṭāḥ । teṣām āsāraḥ dhārāsārāḥ ।।

śailānāṃ hemamāṇikyaśilāphalahakeṣu ca ।
devarṣimunigeheṣu dūrapuṇyāśrameṣu ca ।।

śailānāṃ hemamāṇikyotpattisthānabhūtāni yāni śilāphalahakāni ।।

kumudvatīṣu phullāsu smerāsu nalinīṣu ca ।
vanasthalīṣu phullāsu phullāsūtpalinīṣu ca ।।

smerāsu phullāsu ।।

krīḍāsthānāny uktvā krīḍāprakārān āha

prahelikābhir ākhyānais tathaivākṣaramuṣṭibhiḥ ।
aṣṭāpadair bahūddyotais tathā gūḍhacaturthakaiḥ ।।

ākhyānaiḥ vṛttāntakathanaiḥ । akṣaramuṣṭibhiḥ krīḍāviśeṣaiḥ ।।

nāṭakākhyāyikābhiś ca ślokair bindumatībhramaiḥ ।
deśabhāṣāvibhāgaiś ca nagaragrāmaceṣṭitaiḥ ।।

nāṭakeṣūktā yā ākhyāyikāḥ । bindumatībhramaiḥ krīḍāviśeṣaiḥ । deśabhāṣāṇāṃ vibhāgaiḥ vibhāgakaraṇaiḥ । nagaraceṣṭitaiḥ grāmaceṣṭitaiś ceti yojyam ।।

sragdāmamālyavalanair nānābharaṇayojanaiḥ ।
līlāvilolacalanair vicitrarasabhājanaiḥ ।।

valanaiḥ parivartanaiḥ । nānābharaṇānāṃ yojanaiḥ anyo'nyaṃ saṃyojanaiḥ । līlayā vilolāni yāni calanāni gamanāni । taiḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । vicitreti । vicitrāṇāṃ nānāvidhānāṃ । rasānāṃ śṛṅgārādīnāṃ ।।

ārdrakramukakarpūratāmbūlīdalacarvaṇaiḥ ।
phullapuṣpalatākuñjadehagopanakharvaṇaiḥ ।।

carvaṇaiḥ carvitaiḥ । phullapuṣpāś ca tāḥ latāḥ । tāsāṃ yāni kuñjāni । dehagopanā śarīraguptikaraṇaṃ । tadarthaṃ yāni kharvaṇāni hrasvībhavanāni ।।

samālambhanalīlābhir dolārohaṇavibhramaiḥ ।
gṛhe kusumadolābhir anyo'nyāndolanakramaiḥ ।।

samālambhanaṃ aṅgarāgakaraṇam । anyo'nyaṃ parasparam । āndolanam dolākampanaṃ ।।

nauyānayugyahastyaśvadāntoṣṭrādigamāgamaiḥ ।
jalakelivilāsena parasparasamukṣaṇaiḥ ।।

nauyānaṃ ca yugyabhūtair vāhanabhūtaiḥ । hastyaśvadāntoṣṭrādibhiḥ । gamāgamāś ca । parasparam anyo'nyaṃ । samukṣaṇāni secanāni । taiḥ ।।

nṛttagītakalālāsyatāṇḍavodbhaṭavṛttibhiḥ ।
saṅgītakaiḥ saṅkathanair vīṇāmurajavādanaiḥ ।।

nṛttādyā yā udbhaṭāḥ udriktāḥ ।।

punar api krīḍāsthānāny āha

udyāneṣu sarittīravṛkṣeṣu vanavīthiṣu ।
antaḥpureṣu harmyeṣu teṣu teṣu tathā tathā ।।

tathā tathā pūrvoktaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ krīḍāviśeṣaiḥ ।।

sā bālā sukhasaṃvṛddhā tasya praṇayinī priyā ।
ekadā cintayām āsa śubhasaṅkalpaśālinī ।।

tasya padmākhyasya rājñaḥ । ekadā ekasmin dine । cintayām āsa cintāṃ kṛtavatī । kathambhūtā । śubhasaṅkalpena vakṣyamāṇena praśastena saṅkalpena ।।

kiṃ cintayām āsety । atrāha

prāṇebhyo api priyo bhartā mamaiṣa jagatīpatiḥ ।
yauvanollāsalakṣmīvān kathaṃ syād ajarāmaraḥ ।।

mama esaḥ bhartā ajarāmaraḥ jarāmaraṇākhyadoṣarahitaḥ । kathaṃ syāt kena hetunā syād ity anvayaḥ । prāṇebhyaḥ jīvebhyaḥ ।।

bhartrānena sahottuṅgastanī kusumasadmasu ।
kathaṃ svairaṃ ciraṃ kāntā rameyābdaśatāny aham ।।

ahaṃ kāntānena bhartrā sahābdaśatāni kathaṃ rameya kenopāyena varṣaśatāni krīḍāṃ kuryām ity arthaḥ ।।

tathā yateya kramatas tapojapayamehitaiḥ ।
rajanīśarucī rājā yathā syād ajarāmaraḥ ।।

ata ity adhyāhāryam । ato ahaṃ tathā tapojapayamehitaiḥ karaṇabhūtaiḥ । ato yatnaṃ karomi । yathā rajanīśaruciḥ candraprabhā । rājājarāmaraḥ syāt ।।

jñānavṛddhāṃs tapovṛddhān vidyāvṛddhān ahaṃ dvijān ।
pṛcchāmi tāvan maraṇaṃ kathaṃ na syān nṛṇām iti ।।

ahaṃ jñānavṛddhān tapovṛddhān tathā vidyāvṛddhān dvijān iti tāvat pṛcchāmi iti । nṛṇāṃ maraṇaṃ kathaṃ na syāt kena hetunā na syāt ।।

tasyāḥ saṅkalpam uktvā bāhyaprayatnam āha

athānāyyāśu sampūjya dvijān papraccha sānatā ।
amaratvaṃ kathaṃ viprā bhaved iti punaḥ punaḥ ।।

atha saṅkalpānantaram । parijanair iti śeṣaḥ । punaḥ punar iti icchodrekadyotanaparam ।।

viprā uttaraṃ kathayanti

tapojapayamair devi samastāḥ siddhasiddhayaḥ ।
samprāpyante amaratvaṃ tu na kadācana labhyate ।।

siddhasiddhayaḥ । siddhānāṃ siddhiyuktānāṃ । siddhayaḥ ।।

dvijebhyaḥ svepsitāsiddhiṃ śrutvā punar api taccintām āha

ity ākarṇya dvijamukhāc cintayām āsa sā punaḥ ।
idaṃ svaprajñayaivāśu bhītā priyaviyogataḥ ।।

svaprajñayaiva । na tu taduktānusāreṇa ।।

kiṃ cintayām āsety । atrāha

maraṇaṃ bhartur agre me yadi daivād bhaviṣyati ।
tat sarvaduḥkhanirmuktā saṃsthāsye sukham ātmani ।।

bhartṛmṛtiduḥkhādarśanād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

atha varṣasahasreṇa bhartādau mriyate yadi ।
tat kariṣye tathā yena jīvo gehān na yāsyati ।।

varṣasahasreṇeti padam āśīrdyotakam । atha yadi bhartādau varṣasahasrānte mriyate tat tadā । tathā tam upāyaṃ । kariṣye yena jīvaḥ bhartṛjīvaḥ । gehāt na yāsyati ।।

tataḥ kim ity । atrāha

tadbhramād bhartṛjīve asmin nije śuddhāntamaṇḍape ।
bhartrāvalokitā nityaṃ nivatsyāmi yathāsukham ।।

ahaṃ tadbhramāt । bhartāvalokate mām iti bhramāt । nityaṃ sadā । yathāsukhaṃ nivartsyāmi । kathambhūtāhaṃ । asmin bhartṛjīve nije svakīye । śuddhāntamaṇḍape mayā sādhitenopāyena sthite sati । bhartrāvalokitā vīkṣitā ।।

adyaivārabhyaitadarthaṃ devīṃ jñaptiṃ sarasvatīm ।
japopavāsaniyamair ā toṣaṃ pūjayāmy aham ।।

adyaiva । etadarthaṃ bhartṛjīvasya svagehān nirgamābhāvārtham । jñaptiṃ devīṃ svapratibhāṃ devīṃ । ā toṣaṃ prasādaparyantam । nanu jñaptyārādhanatayā kutaḥ śrutam । jñaptiprasādād eveti brūmaḥ । sarvatra jñaptiprasādasyaiva kāraṇatvāt । agre vakṣyamāṇaḥ jñaptyupadeśaś ca svapratibhākṛtaḥ jñeyaḥ । yataḥ yat yat līlayā kṛtaṃ śrutaṃ vā tat svapratibhayaiva । yad api gurvādimukhena śrūyate tad api svapratibhayaiva । sarvatra svapratibhāyāḥ sthitatvāt ।।

cintānantaraṃ tatprayatnaṃ kathayati

iti niścitya sā nātham anuktvaiva varāṅganā ।
yathāśāstraṃ cacārograṃ tapo niyamam āsthitā ।।

niyamam āsthitāśritā । taṃ vinā tapaso vyarthatvāt ।।

tat tapaḥ viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa kathayati

trirātrasya trirātrasya paryante kṛtapāraṇā ।
devadvijaguruprājñavidvatpūjāparāyaṇā ।।

trirātrasya trirātrasyeti vīpsāyāṃ dvitvam ।।

snānadānatapodhyānanityodyuktaśarīrikā ।
sarvāstikyasadācārakāriṇī kleśakāriṇī ।।

snānādiṣu nityam udyuktaṃ ceṣṭāyuktaṃ । āstikyaḥ āstikayogyaḥ ।।

yathākālaṃ yathodyogaṃ yathāśāstraṃ yathākramam ।
toṣayām āsa bhartāram aparijñātatatsthitim ।।

aparijñātā । trayam etat tapaḥ karotīty evaṃrūpā sthitir । saḥ ।।

trirātraśatam evaṃ sā bālā niyamaśālinī ।
anāratataponiṣṭham atiṣṭhat kaṣṭaceṣṭayā ।।

anārateti । anārataṃ tapasi niṣṭhā yatra । tat । kriyāviśeṣaṇam etat । kaṣṭaceṣṭayā rātritrayānantaraṃ pāraṇādirūpayā duḥkhadayā ceṣṭayā ।।

atha jñaptiprasādam āha

trirātrāṇāṃ śatenātha pūjitā pratimām itā ।
tuṣṭā bhagavatī gaurī vāgīśīdam uvāca tām ।।

atha niyamānantaram । gaurī śuddhasvarūpā । vāgīśītvam asyāḥ vācāṃ mūlakāraṇatvena jñeyaṃ । pratimām itā śilādipratimām āśritā । svayā pratibhayā pratimāyām ābhāsena tasyāḥ darśanaṃ dattavān iti bhāvaḥ ।।

jñaptyā kathyamānaṃ vākyam āha

nirantareṇa tapasā bhartṛbhaktyatiśāyinā ।
parituṣṭāsmi te vatse gṛhāṇa varam īpsitam ।।

nirantareṇācchinnena ।।

jñaptivākyaṃ śrutvā rājñī tāṃ stauti

jaya janmajarājvālādāhadoṣaśaśiprabhe ।
jaya hārdāndhakāraughanivāraṇaraviprabhe ।।

śaśiprabhāyāḥ dāhadoṣanivārakatvaṃ raviprabhāyāḥ cāndhakāranivartakatvaṃ prasiddham eva ।।

amba māṃ trijaganmātas trāyasva kṛpaṇām imām ।
idaṃ varadvayaṃ dehi yad iha prārthaye śubham ।।

kṛpaṇāṃ dīnāṃ । śubham iti varadvayaviśeṣaṇam ।।

varadvayamadhye ekaṃ kathayati

ekaṃ tāvad videhasya bhartur jīvo mamāmbike ।
asmād eva hi mā yāsīn nijāntaḥpuramaṇḍapāt ।।

varadvayamadhye ekam idaṃ varaṃ dehi । kim ity apekṣāyām āha videheti । videhasya mṛtasya । mā yāsīt mā gacchatu ।।

dvitīyaṃ kathayati

dvitīyaṃ tvāṃ mahādevi prārthaye ahaṃ yadā yadā ।
darśanāya varārthena tadā me dehi darśanam ।।

dvitīyam idaṃ dehi । kim ity apekṣāyām āha tvām iti । he devi । ahaṃ tvāṃ yadā darśanāya prārthaye tadā tvaṃ varārthena varānurodhena । darśanaṃ dehi ।।

varadvayam aṅgīkṛtya jñaptya

Prakaraṇa Sthiti 

oṃ atha sthitiprakaraṇaṃ vyākhyāyate । oṃ

pratyakjyotiḥ kim api paramam bhāvayitvātha devaṃ dhyātvā citte bhavabhayaharaṃ śrīgaṇeśaṃ vibhuṃ ca ।
maulau kṛtvā gurucaraṇayor dhūlipuñjaṃ ca ṭīkā sthityākhye ḥsmin prakaraṇavare tanyate bhāskareṇa ।।

evam utpattiprakaraṇe ḥnutpattirūpāṃ jagadutpattim pratipādya tacchravaṇena ca tatra śrīrāmam pratītibhājaṃ nirvarṇya tadanantaraṃ yogyaṃ sthitiprakaraṇārambhaṃ karoti

athotpattiprakaraṇād anantaram idaṃ śṛṇu ।
sthitiprakaraṇaṃ rāma jñātaṃ nirvāṇakāri yat ।।

athaśabdo maṅgalamātraprayojanaḥ । sthitiprakaraṇaṃ kim । yat jñātaṃ śravaṇamanananidadhyāsanaviṣaye kṛtaṃ sat । nirvāṇam brahmaṇi ātyantikaṃ layaṃ karotīti tādṛśam ।।

sthitiprakaraṇam eva kathayati

evaṃ tāvad idaṃ viddhi dṛśyaṃ jagad iti sthitam ।
ahaṃ cetyādy anākāram bhrāntimātram asanmayam ।।

tāvat tvam evaṃ viddhi । anyat svayam eva jñāsyasīti bhāvaḥ । evaṃ katham ity apekṣāyām āha idam iti । jagad iti nāmadheyena sthitam । idaṃ dṛśyam puraḥsphurat । dṛśikriyāviṣayo bhāvajātam । aham ityādi ca bhavati । anākāram bhrāntimātram asanmayaṃ ca ।।

akartṛkam anaṅgaṃ ca gagane citram utthitam ।
adraṣṭṛkaṃ sānubhavam anidraṃ svapnadarśanam ।।

gagane cidākāśe । citram ālekhyam iva । uditam prādurbhūtam । akartṛkam kartṛrahitam । anaṅgam niḥsvarūpam । svapnadarśanam svapnadarśanasvarūpam । svapnadarśanam kathambhūtam । adraṣṭṛkam draṣṭṛrahitam । sānubhavam draṣṭranubhavaviṣayatāṃ gatam । anidram nidrādoṣādṛṣṭam । atrālaukikatvakathanena vismayakāritve eva bharaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।

bhaviṣyatpuranirmāṇaṃ citrasaṃstham ivoditam ।
markaṭānalatāpābham ambvāvartavad āsthitam ।।

bhaviṣyatpurasya ca nakiñcidrūpatvaṃ sphuṭam eva । markaṭasyānalatvenābhāsamānaḥ analaḥ markaṭānalaḥ । tasya yaḥ tāpaḥ । markaṭo hi kam api phalaviśeṣam agnibhrameṇa gṛhṇāti । āsthitam sthitiyuktam ।।

sadrūpam api niḥśūnyaṃ tejaḥ sauram ivāmbare ।
ratnābhājālam iva khe dṛśyamānam abhittimat ।।

sadrūpam cinmātrasāratvāt । niḥśūnyam nakiñcittvāt । ambare hi sauraṃ tejaḥ sadrūpam api niḥśūnyam iva bhātīti tasyopamānatvena grahaṇam ।।

saṅkalpapuravat prauḍham anubhūtam asanmayam ।
kathārthapratibhānātma na kvacit sthitam asti ca ।।

kathāyāḥ anena kathyamānāyāḥ kathāyāḥ । tasya yat pratibhānam sphuraṇam । tadātma tatsvarūpam । kathāḥ śravaṇakāle hi śrotuḥ tadarthaḥ puraḥ iva pratibhāti । na kvacit sthitam vicārāsahatvāt । asti ca pratibhāsamānatvāt ।।

niḥsāram apy atīvāntaḥsāraṃ svapnācalopamam ।
bhūtākāśam ivākārabhāsuraṃ śūnyamātrakam ।।

niḥsāram piṇḍagrahābhāvāt । atīvātiśayenāntaḥsāram cinmātrasāratvāt । ākārabhāsuram nīlarūpayuktākārabhāsvaram ।।

śaradabhram ivāgrastham alakṣyakṣayam ākṣayi ।
varṇo vyomatalasyeva dṛśyamānam avastukam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

svapnāṅganāratākāram arthaniṣṭham anarthakam ।
citrodyānam ivotphullam arasaṃ sarasākṛti ।।

arthaniṣṭham retaḥsravākhyārthakriyāratam । anarthakam prabhāte ḥdṛśyamānatvāt vṛthābhātam । punaḥ kathambhūtam । arasam āsvādarahitam api । sarasākṛti sarasā ivākṛtiḥ yasya । utphullaṃ citrodyānam ālekhyodyānam । tasyāpi arasatve ḥpi sarasākṛtitvam prasiddham ।।

prakāśam iva nistejaś citrārkānalavat sthitam ।
anubhūtam manorājyam ivāsatyam avāstavam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

citrapadmākara iva sārasaugandhyavarjitam ।
śūnye prakacitaṃ nānāvarṇam ākāritātmakam ।।

śūnye acetyacinmātrākhyāyāṃ śūnyabhittau । ākāritaḥ ākārayuktaḥ । ātmā yasya ।।

paramārthena śuṣyadbhir bhūtapelavapallavaiḥ ।
tataṃ jaḍam asārātma kadalīstambhabhāsuram ।।

tataṃ vyāptam ।।

sphāritekṣaṇadṛśyāndhakāracakrakavat tatam ।
atyantam abhavadrūpam api pratyakṣavat sthitam ।।

sphāritekṣaṇasya dṛśyāni yāni andhakāracakrakāṇi । abhinayagamyaś cāyam arthaḥ ।।

vār budbuda ivābhogi śūnyam antaḥ sphuradvapuḥ ।
rasātmakaṃ satyarasam avicchinnakṣayodayam ।।

rasātmakam icchāsvarūpaṃ jalasvarūpaṃ ca । satyasya cinmātratattvasya । tat । cinmātratattvenaiva puṣṭiṃ gatam ity arthaḥ ।।

nīhāra iva vistāri gṛhītaṃ san na kiñcana ।
jaḍaṃ śūnyāspadaṃ śūnyaṃ keṣāñcit paramāṇuvat ।।

keṣāñcit sthūlabuddhīnāṃ tārkikāṇām ।।

kiñcid bhūtamayo ḥstīti sthitaṃ śūnyam abhūtakam ।
gṛhyamāṇam asadrūpaṃ niśātama ivotthitam ।।

ayaṃ saṃsāraḥ kiñcit bhūtamayaḥ astīti sthitam bhāsamānam । etair viśeṣaṇaiḥ samastaḥ sthitiprakaraṇārthaḥ saṅgṛhyoktaḥ । sthitiprakaraṇe evaṃrūpāyā jagatsthiter vaktum iṣṭatvāt ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati mahākalpakṣaye dṛśyam āste bīja ivāṅkuram ।
pare bhūya udety etat tata eveti kiṃ vada ।।

iti kim etad eva kim asti atha vā neti ।।

evambodhāḥ kim ajñāḥ syur uta tajjñā iti sphuṭam ।
yathāvad bhagavan brūhi sarvasaṃśayaśāntaye ।।

evam pūrvaślokoktarūpaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaram āha idam bīje ḥṅkura iva dṛśyam āste mahākṣaye ।
brūte yaḥ param ajñatvam etat tasyātiśaiśavāt ।।

atiśaiśavāt atimaurkhyāt ।।

hetukathanam avaśyopadeśyatvenāha sparśe kiṃ tad asambaddhaṃ katham etad avāstavam ।
viparīto bodha eṣa vaktuḥ śrotuś ca maurkhyakṛt ।।

asambaddhaṃ tat kim bhavati । na kiñcid apīty arthaḥ । etat avāstavam asambaddhaṃ । eṣa viparītaḥ bodhaḥ vaktuḥ śrotuś ca maurkhyakṛt bhavati । etat anena hetunā asambaddham bhavati iti vaktuḥ vaktavyam । anena hetunā etat avāstavaṃ na bhavatīti śrotuḥ paryanuyogaḥ kāryaḥ । anyathā tayoḥ maurkhyam eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

phalitam āha

bījakāle ḥṅkura iva jagad āste itīha yā ।
buddhiḥ sāsatpralāpārthā mūḍhā śṛṇu kathaṃ kila ।।

ata ity adhyāhāryam । asatpralāpārthā asatpralāpasyevārthaḥ yasyāḥ । sā । asatpralāparūpeti yāvat । mūḍhā jaḍā । kathaṃ kena hetunā । hetvakathane mamāpi maurkhyāpātaḥ syād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

bījam bhavet svayaṃ dṛśyaṃ cittādīndriyagocaraḥ ।
vaṭadhānādi dhānyādi yuktam atrāṅkurodbhavaḥ ।।

cittādīndriyagocaraḥ । ata eva dṛśyam vaṭadhānādi tathā dhānyādi bījam bhavet । atra dhānādirūpe tathā dhānyādirūpe bīje । aṅkurodbhavaḥ yuktam bhavati ।।

manaḥṣaṣṭhendriyātītaṃ yaḥ khād atitarām api ।
bījaṃ tad bhavituṃ śaktaṃ svayambhūr jagataḥ katham ।।

manaḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ yeṣām । tāni manaḥṣaṣṭhāni । tādṛśāni ca tānīndriyāṇi । svayambhūḥ cinmātram ।।

ākāśād api sūkṣmasya parasya paramātmanaḥ ।
sarvākṣānupalabhyasya kīdṛśī bījatā katham ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sat sūkṣmam asadābhāsam asad eva hy ataddṛśām ।
kīdṛśī bījatā tatra bījābhāve kuto ḥṅkuraḥ ।।

sat api yat cinmātrākhyaṃ vastu । ataddṛśām na tasmin dṛk yeṣām । te । cinmātrajñānarahitānām iti yāvat । atra hetum āha । asadvat ābhāsaḥ yasya । tādṛśam । atrāpi hetutvena viśeṣaṇam āha sūkṣmam iti । sūkṣmatvād asadābhāsatvam । asadābhāsatvād asattvam ity arthaḥ । tatra tasmin cinmātrākhye vastuni । bījatā kīdṛśī bhavati । na bhavati । sthūlasyaiva bījatvayogād ity arthaḥ । bījābhāve aṅkuraḥ jagadākhyaḥ aṅkuraḥ । naiva yukta ity arthaḥ ।।

gaganāṅgād api svacche śūnye tatra pare pade ।
kathaṃ santi jaganmerusamudragaganādayaḥ ।।

gaganāṅgāt svacchatvaṃ jāḍyākhyamālinyarahitatvāt jñeyam ।।

nakiñcid yat kathaṃ kiñcit tatrāste vastv avastuni ।
asti cet tat kathaṃ tatra vidyamānaṃ na dṛśyate ।।

yat cinmātram । bāhyāntaḥkaraṇātītatvāt nakiñcid bhavati । tatra tasmin । avastuni nakiñcidrūpe cinmātre । indriyagamyatvena kiñcidrūpaṃ vastu jagadākhyaṃ vastu । tathāpi cet asti tatra vidyamānaṃ kathaṃ na dṛśyate । tarhi vidyamānatvam evāsya yuktaṃ syād iti bhāvaḥ । nanu jagataḥ vidyamānatvaṃ kathaṃ nāsti iti cet । vicārāsahatvān nāstīti brūmaḥ । yo hi vicāraṃ sahate tasyaiva vidyamānatvam । yathā rajjusarpāpekṣayā rajjoḥ ।।

nakiñcidātmanaḥ kiñcit katham eti kuto ḥtha vā ।
śūnyarūpād ghaṭākāśāj jāto ḥdriḥ kva kutaḥ kadā ।।

pūrvaślokavyākhyayaiva gatārtho ḥyaṃ ślokaḥ ।।

pratipakṣe kathaṃ kiñcid āste chāyātape yathā ।
katham āste tamo bhānau katham āste hime ḥnalaḥ ।।

kiñcit kim api । pratipakṣe katham āste । pratipakṣe avasthānaṃ kasyāpi na yuktam iti bhāvaḥ । viśeṣeṇaitad eva darśayati cchāyetyādi ।।

merur āste katham aṇau kutaḥ kiñcid anākṛtau ।
tadatadrūpayor aikyaṃ kva cchāyātapayor iva ।।

dṛṣṭāntāni viśeṣatayoktvā dārṣṭāntikam api tattayaiva kathayati kutaḥ kiñcid iti । kiñcit indriyagamyatvāt kiñcidrūpaṃ jagat । anākṛtau indriyāgamyatvenākārarahite cinmātre । kutaḥ na yuktam etad iti bhāvaḥ । nanv ekatve na bījāṅkuratvam anayor astīty atrāha tadatad iti । tadatadrūpayoḥ atyantabhinnayoḥ ।।

sākāre vaṭadhānādāv aṅkuro ḥstīti yuktimat ।
anākāre mahākāraṃ jagad astīty ayuktimat ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

deśāntare yac ca narāntare ca buddhyādisarvendriyaśaktyadṛśyam ।
nāsty eva tattadvidhabuddhibodhe nakiñcid ity eva tad ucyate ca ।।

deśāntare ca asmin deśe anyasmin deśe ca । narāntare ca tvayi anyeṣu nareṣu ca । kālasyāpy etad upalakṣaṇam । tena kālāntare cety api jñeyaṃ । tenāyam arthaḥ । buddhyādīnāṃ sarvendriyaśaktīnāṃ cādṛśyaṃ yat vastu । deśāntare narāntare ca tattadvidhabuddhibodhe । tattadvidhāḥ tattatprakārāḥ । yāḥ buddhayaḥ । tadviṣayo nāstīti yāvat । paṇḍitaiḥ tat nakiñcid ity eva ucyate kathyate ।।

tataḥ kim ity atrāha

kāryasya tat kāraṇatām prayātam vaktīti yas tasya vimūḍhabodhaḥ ।
kair nāma tatkāryam udeti tasmāt svaiḥ kāraṇaughaiḥ sahakārirūpaiḥ ।।

tat nakiñcid iti nāmārhaṃ vastu । kāryasya kāraṇatām prayātam bhavati । iti yaḥ vakti । tasya vimūḍhabodhaḥ bhavati । nāsau tajjña iti bhāvaḥ । sahakārikāraṇābhāvena tasya kāraṇatāṃ nivārayati tatkāryam iti । svaiḥ nijaiḥ । sarvasya nakiñcidrūpacinmātrasvarūpatvena sahakārikāraṇasattā nāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

etena siddhaṃ siddhāntaṃ sargāntaślokena kathayati

durbuddhibhiḥ kāraṇakāryabhāvaṃ saṅkalpitaṃ dūratare vyudasya ।
yad eva tat satyam anādimadhyaṃ jagat tad eva sthitam ity avehi ।।durbuddhibhiḥ kubuddhiyuktaiḥ । saṅkalpitaṃ svasaṅkalpenollikhitam । na tu paramārthasantaṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvaṃ jagadbrahmaviṣayaṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvam । vyudasya parityajya । tvam iti avehi satyatayā niścinu iti । anādimadhyam ādimadhyayor api sākṣitvena sthitatvāt ādimadhyarahitam । tat prasiddham । satyam satyabhūtam cinmātrākhyaṃ vastu asti । tad eva na tu tatkāryam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ janyajanakanirākaraṇaṃ sthitiprakaraṇe prathamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

vasiṣṭha uvāca

athaitadabhyupagame vacmi vedyavidāṃ vara ।
samastakalanātīte mahācidvyomni nirmale ।।

jagadādyaṅkuras tatra yady asti tad asau tadā ।
kair ivodeti kathaya kāraṇaiḥ sahakāribhiḥ ।।

he vedyavidāṃ vara । athāham etat bījatvam । aṅgīkṛtya । kiṃ vakṣīty apekṣāyām āha samasteti । samastakalanātīte sarvakāryakāraṇabhāvādikalanātīte । nirmale cetyākhyamalādūṣite । sahakāribhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ sahakārikāraṇaiḥ ।।

sahakārikāraṇānām abhāve vāṅkurodgatiḥ ।
vandhyākanyā ca dṛṣṭeha na kadācana kenacit ।।

vāśabdaḥ pādapūraṇārthaḥ । caśabdaḥ samuccaye ।।

sahakārikāraṇānām abhāve yac ca voditam ।
mūlakāraṇam evātmā tat svabhāve sthitaṃ tathā ।।

yat ca jagadākhyaṃ kāryam । sahakārikāraṇānām abhāve uditam kāraṇāt anyatayā prādurbhūtam bhavati । tat tathā tena prakāreṇa । svabhāve svasvarūpe । sthitam । mūlakāraṇam ātmā mūlakāraṇabhūta ātmaiva bhavati । na kāryam । sahakārikāraṇasambhava eva kāryatvadarśanāt ।।

sargādau sargarūpeṇa brahmaivātmani tiṣṭhati ।
yathāsthitam anākāraṃ kva janyajanakakramaḥ ।।

sargādau cetyonmukhatāsamaye ।।

atha pṛthvyādayo ḥnye vā kuto ḥpy āgatya kurvate ।
sahakārikāraṇatvaṃ tat pūrvaivātra dūṣaṇā ।।

pūrvā dūṣaṇeti । sargāgame yā dūṣaṇā asti sā eva sahakāryabhimatapṛthvyādyāgame ḥpy astīty arthaḥ ।।

phalitam āha

tasmāt pare jagac chāntam āste tat sahakāraṇaiḥ ।
vinā prasaratīty uktir bālasya na vipaścitaḥ ।।

tasmāt tato hetoḥ । jagat pare śāntam bījatvena sthitam asti । sahakāraṇaiḥ sahakārikāraṇaiḥ vinā । tat prasarati ity uktiḥ bālasya mūrkhasya । bhavati । vipaścitaḥ paṇḍitasya । na bhavati ।।

paramaphalitaṃ kathayati

tasmād rāma jagan nāsīn na cāsti na bhaviṣyati ।
cetanākāśam evācchaṃ kacatīttham ivātmani ।।

he rāma । tasmāt jagat nāsīt na cāsti na ca bhaviṣyati sahakārikāraṇābhāvāt । punaḥ kim etat sphuratīty । accham cetyarahitaṃ । cetanākāśam cinmātrākāśam । ātmani ittham jagadrūpeṇa । sphurati iva kacati iva ।।

atyantābhāva evāsya jagato vidyate yadā ।
tadā brahmedam akhilam iti sad rāma nānyathā ।।

anyathā asat ।।

nanu prāgabhāvādir eva kathaṃ nātrāsti । kim atyantābhāvenety । atrāha

pūrvapradhvaṃsanānyoḥnyābhāvair yad upaśāmyati ।
aśāntam eva tac citte na śāmyaty eva tad yataḥ ।।

pūrvapradhvaṃsanānyoḥnyābhāvaiḥ prāgabhāvena pradhvaṃsābhāvena anyoḥnyābhāvena ca । yat śāmyati tat aśāntam eva bhavati । yataḥ tat vastu । na śāmyati saṃskāratvena sthitatvāt । tasmād atyantābhāva evātra yukta iti bhāvaḥ ।।

atyantābhāvam evāto jagaddṛśyasya sarvadā ।
varjayitvetarā yuktir nāsty evānarthasaṅkṣaye ।।

jagaddṛśyasyātyantābhāva eva jagadrūpasyānarthasya kṣaye yuktiḥ nānyat kiñcid iti piṇḍārthaḥ ।।

cidākāśasya bodho ḥyaṃ jagadādīti yat sthitam ।
ayaṃ so ḥham idaṃ rūpālokacittakalādy api ।।

idaṃ jagadādīti yat sthitam asti । ayam cidākāśasya bodha eva bhavati । nānyat । ādiśabdena pralayasya grahaṇam । jagadādīti viśeṣeṇa kathayati ayaṃ so ḥham ityādi । cittakalā manaskāraḥ ।।

idam arkādi pṛthvyādi tathedaṃ vatsarādi ca ।
ayaṃ kalpaḥ kṣaṇaś cāyam ime maraṇajanmane ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ayaṃ kalpāntasaṃrambho mahākalpānta eṣa saḥ ।
ayaṃ sa sargaprārambho bhāvābhāvakramas tv asau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

lakṣāṇīmāni kalpānām imā brahmāṇḍakoṭayaḥ ।
ime brahmendranicayā imā viṣṇvādiśaktayaḥ ।।

viṣṇvādirūpāḥ śaktayaḥ viṣṇvādiśaktayaḥ ।।

ete ceme pariṇatā ime bhūya upāgatāḥ ।
imāni dhiṣṇyajālāni deśakālakalā imāḥ ।।

ete ime pariṇatāḥ mṛtāḥ ।।

upasaṃhāraṃ karoti

mahācitparamākāśam anāvṛttam anantakam ।
yathā pūrvaṃ sthitaṃ śāntam ity evaṃ kacati svayam ।।

anāvṛttam āvṛttirahitam । anantakam antarahitam । śāntam svasmin svarūpe eva sarvadā nilīnam । mahācitparamākāśam । iti anena prakāreṇa ।।

paramāṇusahasrāṃśabhāsa etā mahāciteḥ ।
svabhāvabhūtā evāntaḥsthitā nāyānti yānti no ।।

mahāciteḥ antaḥsthitāḥ । ata eva svabhāvabhūtāḥ । paramāṇoḥ yaḥ sahasrāṃśaḥ । tatparimāṇāḥ bhāsaḥ dīptayaḥ । etāḥ sargaparamparāḥ । na āyānti no yānti sadā sthitatvāt ।।

svayam antaś camatkāro yas samudgīryate citā ।
tat sargabhānam bhātīdam bhārūpaṃ na ca bhittimat ।।

citā cinmātreṇa । antaḥsthitaḥ yaḥ camatkāraḥ svarūpaparāmarśarūpaḥ āsvādaḥ । bahiḥ samudgīryate samyak udgīryate । tat idaṃ samudgiraṇaṃ । sargabhānam bhāti । bhārūpam jñānasvarūpam । na bhittimat bhittirahitam ।।

nodyanti na ca naśyanti nāyānti na ca yānti ca ।
mahāśilāntarlekhānāṃ sanniveśa ivācalāḥ ।।

sargā iti śeṣaḥ ।।

ime sargāḥ prasphuranti svataḥ svātmani nirmale ।
nabhasīva nabhobhāgā nirākārā nirākṛtau ।।

svataḥ svabhāvena ।।

dravatvānīva toyasya spandā iva sadāgateḥ ।
āvartā iva vāmbhodher guṇino vāthavā guṇāḥ ।।

pūrvaślokadṛṣṭāntatvenaiva yojyam ।।

vijñānaghana evaikam idam ittham iva sthitam ।
sodayāstamayārambham anantaṃ śāntam ātatam ।।

vijñānaghane jñānaikasvarūpe cinmātratattve ।।

sahakāryādihetūnām abhāve śūnyatā jagat ।
svayambhūr jāyate ceti kilonmattakaphūtkṛtam ।।

unmattakaphūtkṛtam unmattapralāpaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokena phalitaṃ kathayati

praśāntasarvārthakalākalaṅko nirastaniḥśeṣavikalpatalpaḥ ।
cirāya vidrāvitadīrghanidro bhavābhayo bhūṣitabhūḥ prabuddhaḥ ।।tasmād ity adhyāhāryam । kīdṛśa ity apekṣāyāṃ viśeṣaṇāny āha praśānta ityādi । praśāntaḥ brahmaikatāvijñānena prakarṣeṇa śāntaḥ । sarvārtharūpaḥ kalaṅkaḥ yasya । nirastā niḥśeṣavikalpā eva talpam yena । vidrāvitā dīrghanidrā avidyārūpā dīrghanidrā yena । ata eva prabuddhaḥ samyagjñānayuktaḥ । ataḥ abhayaḥ bhayarahitaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe dvitīyaḥ sargaḥ ।।śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati mahāpralayasargādau prathamo ḥsau prajāpatiḥ ।
smṛtyātmā jāyate sarge smṛtyātmaiva tato jagat ।।

prathamaḥ prajāpatiḥ śuddhamanorūpaḥ brahmā । smṛtyātma smṛtirūpam ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ uttaraṃ kathayati mahāpralayasargādāv evam etad raghūdvaha ।
smṛtyātmaiva bhavaty ādau prathamo ḥsau prajāpatiḥ ।।

evam etat etat satyam evety arthaḥ ।।

tatsaṅkalpātma ca jagat smṛtyātmaivam idaṃ tataḥ ।
iti saṅkalpanagaraṃ sthitam pūrvaprajāpateḥ ।।

tatsaṅkalpātma smṛtisvarūpaprajāpatisvarūpam ।।

iti sthite ḥpi sā rāma tasya pūrvaprajāpateḥ ।
sthitir na sambhavaty eva nabhasīva mahādrumaḥ ।।

sā smṛtirūpā ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati na sambhavati kim brahman sargādau prāktanī smṛtiḥ ।
mahāpralayasammohair naśyati prāksmṛtiḥ katham ।।

mahāpralayasammohaiḥ mahāpralayakṛtābhiḥ mūrcchābhiḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaraṃ kathayati prāṅmahāpralaye prājña pūrve brahmādayaḥ purā ।
kila nirvāṇam āyātās te ḥvaśyam brahmatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

nirvāṇam muktim ।।

prāktanyāḥ kaḥ smṛtes smartā tasmāt kathaya suvrata ।
smṛtir nirmūlatāṃ yātā smartur muktatayā yataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ataḥ smartur abhāve sā smṛtiḥ kodetu kiṃ katham ।
avaśyaṃ hi mahākalpe sarve mokṣaikabhāginaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nānubhūte ḥnubhūte ca svataś cidvyomni yā smṛtiḥ ।
sā jagacchrīr iti prauḍhā dṛśyābhāve hi citprabhā ।।

svataḥ na tu prajāpatirūpagrahāt । nānubhūte pūrvānanubhūte viṣaye । anubhūte pūrvam anubhūte viṣaye । cidvyomni yā smṛtiḥ bhavati । sā jagacchrīr iti prauḍhā bhavati । na prajāpatismṛtir iti bhāvaḥ । kuta etad ity । dṛśyābhāve smṛtirūpadṛśyābhāve । citprabhā eva bhavati । na prajāpatiprabhā ।।

athavālam anayā smṛtikalpanayā । yataḥ citprabhaiva jagad astīty abhiprāyenāha

bhāti saṃvitprabhaivāccham anādyantāvabhāsinī ।
yat tad etaj jagad iti svayambhūr iti ca sthitam ।।

anādyantāvabhāsinī sadā bhātatvenādyantāvabhāsarahitā । saṃvitprabhā eva acchaṃ yat bhāti tat etat jagad iti sthitam bhavati । svayambhūr iti ca sthitam bhavati । ataḥ smṛteḥ svayambhuvaś ca na kāpi sattāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

anādikālasaṃsiddhaṃ yad bhānam brahmaṇo nijam ।
sa ātivāhiko deho virājo jagadākṛtiḥ ।।

anādikālasaṃsiddham satatasiddham । brahmaṇaḥ cinmātratattvasya । yat nijaṃ svasambandhi । saḥ virājaḥ virāḍrūpasya prajāpateḥ । ātivāhikaḥ dehaḥ bhavati । jagadākṛtiḥ samastajagatsvarūpaḥ ।।

paramāṇāv idam bhāti jagat sabhuvanatrayam ।
deśakālakriyādravyadinarātrikramānvitam ।।

dravyam kriyāviṣayaḥ padārthaḥ । paramāṇvantas tribhuvanābhānam indrasya nirvāṇaprakaraṇe vakṣyati ।।

paramāṇum prati tatas tasyāntas tādṛg eva ca ।
bhāti bhāsvaritākāraṃ tādṛggirikulāvṛtam ।।

tataḥ tato hetoḥ । tasya paramāṇvantarvartinaḥ tribhuvanasya । prati paramāṇum antaḥ pratiparamāṇumadhye । tādṛk eva na tv anyarūpam । bhāsvaritākāraṃ tādṛggirikulāvṛtam tādṛśaparvatasamūhākulam । arthāt tribhuvanam bhāti ।।

tatrāpi tādṛgākāram evam praty aṇum ātatam ।
dṛśyam ābhāti bhārūpam etad aṅga na vāstavam ।।

tatrāpi pratyaṇuvartini tribhuvane ḥpi । bhārūpam jñānasvarūpam । phalitam āha etad iti । ataḥ etat tribhuvanam । vāstavam paramārthasat । svapnavad bhārūpatvāt ।।

ity asty anto na saddṛṣṭer asaddṛṣṭeś ca vā kvacit ।
asyās tv abhyuditam buddham abuddham prati vānagha ।।

iti anena prakāreṇa । saddṛṣṭeḥ cinmātradṛṣṭeḥ । asaddṛṣṭeḥ cetyadṛṣṭeḥ vā । asyāḥ saddṛṣṭer asaddṛṣṭeś ca । abhyuditam abhyudayaḥ । prādurbhāva iti yāvat । buddham prati abuddham prati vā bhavati । buddham prati saddṛṣṭeḥ abhyudayaḥ asaddṛṣṭeḥ abuddham pratīti kramo jñeyaḥ ।।

nanu ekā eva bhāsamānā jagadākhyā dṛṣṭir asti । tat katham uktam buddham prati saddṛṣṭer anto nāsti asaddṛṣṭer abuddham pratīty । āha

buddham pratīdam brahmaiva kevalaṃ śāntam avyayam ।
abuddham prati tu dvaitam bhāsuram bhuvanānvitam ।।

idam eva jagat । buddhasya saddṛṣṭyā bhāti । abuddhasyāsaddṛṣṭyā । yathā ekaḥ rajjuḥ buddham prati rajjutayā bhāti । abuddham prati sarpatayeti bhāvaḥ ।।

yathedam bhāsuram bhāti jagad aṇḍakajṛmbhitam ।
tathā koṭisahasrāṇi bhānty anyāny apy aṇāv aṇau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yathā stambhe putrikāntas tasyāś cāṅgeṣu putrikā ।
tasyāś ca putrikāsty aṅge tathā trailokyaputrikā ।।

trailokyākhyā putrikā trailokyaputrikā ।।

na bhinnā na ca saṅkhyeyā yathādrau paramāṇavaḥ ।
tathā brahmabṛhanmerau trailokyaparamāṇavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sūryaughāṃśuṣv asaṅkhyātuṃ śakyante laghavo ḥṇavaḥ ।
nānādyantāś cidāditye trailokyaparamāṇavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yathāṇavo vahanty arkadīptiṣv apsu rajaḥsu ca ।
tathā vahante cidvyomni trailokyaparamāṇavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śūnyānubhavamātrātma bhūtākāśam idaṃ yathā ।
sargānubhavamātrātma cidākāśam idaṃ tathā ।।

śūnyasya yaḥ anubhavaḥ । tanmātram ātmā svarūpaṃ yasya । tat ।।

sargas tu sargaśabdārthatayā buddho nayaty adhaḥ ।
sa brahmaśabdārthatayā buddhaḥ śreyo bhavaty alam ।।

śreyaḥ mokṣarūpam ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati

vijñānātmā śāsitā viśvabījam brahmaivādyaṃ svaṃ cidākāśamātraṃ ।
tasmāj jātaṃ yat tad eveti vedyaṃ viddhi svāntar bodhasambodhamātram ।।vijñānātmā jñānaikasvarūpaḥ । svam sarveṣām ātmatvena sthitam । cidākāśamātram ādyam brahmaiva viśvabījaṃ viśvasya bījam iva bījam । na tu sākṣād bījam । tasya samanantaram eva nirākṛtatvāt । tasmāt tādṛśāt brahmaṇaḥ । tat tad eva bhavati । tvam vedyam vidikriyāviṣayam bhāvajātam । bodhasya yaḥ sambodhaḥ svaparāmarśaḥ । tanmātraṃ viddhi jānīhi । liṅgasaṅkaro ḥliṅgatvadyotanārthaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe tṛtīyaḥ sargaḥ ।। indriyagrāmasaṅgrāmasetunā bhavasāgaraḥ ।
tīryate netareṇeha kenacin nāma karmaṇā ।।

indriyagrāmeṇendriyasamūhena ।।

śāstrasatsaṅgamābhyāsaiḥ saviveko jitendriyaḥ ।
atyantābhāvam evāsya dṛśyaughasyāvagacchati ।।

avagacchati jānāti ।।

etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ svarūpaṃ rūpiṇāṃ vara ।
saṃsārasāgaraśreṇyo yathāyānti prayānti ca ।।

he rūpiṇāṃ vara । arthāt saṃsārasāgaraśreṇīnāṃ sarvam svarūpam । tathā saṃsārasāgaraśreṇyāḥ yathāyānti prayānti ca ।।

bahunātra kim uktena manaḥ karmadrumāṅkuram ।
tasmiṃś chinne jagacchākhaś chinnaḥ karmatarur bhavet ।।

karmataruḥ kathambhūtaḥ । jaganty eva śākhāḥ yasya । saḥ ।।

manaḥ sarvam idaṃ rāma tasminn antaś cikitsite ।
cikitsito ḥyaṃ sakalo janmajālamayo bhavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tad etaj jāyate loke mano malalavākulam ।
manaso vyatirekeṇa dehaḥ kva kila dṛśyate ।।

jāyate jagattayā utpadyate । malalavākulam saṅkalpākhyamalaleśākulam ।।

dṛśyātyantāsambhavanam ṛte nānyena hetunā ।
manaḥpiśācaḥ praśamaṃ yāti kalpaśatair api ।।

dṛśyātyantāsambhavanaṃ dṛśyātyantābhāvam ।।

etac ca sambhavaty eva manovyādhicikitsane ।
dṛśyātyantāsambhavātma paramauṣadham uttamam ।।

manovyādhicikitsane kārye । sambhavaty eva prabhavaty eva ।।

mano moham upādatte mriyate jāyate punaḥ ।
kasyacit tu prasādena badhyate mucyate punaḥ ।।

kasyacid anākhyasya cinmātrasya ।।

sphuratītthaṃ jagat sarvaṃ citte mananamanthare ।
śūnya evāmbare sphāre gandharvāṇām puraṃ yathā ।।

mananamanthare mananabharite ।।

manasīdaṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ sphāraṃ sphurati cāsti ca ।
puṣpaguccha ivāmodas tatsthas tasmād ivetaraḥ ।।

sphāram vistīrṇam ।।

yathā tilakaṇe tailaṃ guṇo guṇini vā yathā ।
yathā dharmiṇi vā dharmas tathedam manasi sthitam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yathāmbhasi taraṅgaugha indau dvīndubhramo yathā ।
mṛgatṛṣṇā yathā tāpe saṃsāraś cittake tathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

raśmijālaṃ yathā sūrye yathālokaś ca tejasi ।
yathauṣṇyaṃ citrabhānau ca manasīdaṃ tathā jagat ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śaityaṃ yathaiva tuhine yathā nabhasi śūnyatā ।
yathā cañcalatā vāyau manasīdaṃ tathā jagat ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati

mano jagaj jagad akhilaṃ tathā manaḥ parasparaṃ tv avirahitaṃ sadaiva hi ।
tayor dvayor manasi nirantaraṃ kṣate kṣataṃ jagan na tu jagati kṣate manaḥ ।।nirantaram atiśayena । tayoḥ dvayor iti nirdhāraṇe ṣaṣṭhī । tasmān mana eva samyagjñānādyupāyena nāśanīyam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe caturthaḥ sargaḥ ।।śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati bhagavan sarvadharmajña pūrvāparavidāṃ vara ।
ayam manasi saṃsāraḥ sphāraḥ katham iva sthitaḥ ।।

manasi paramāṇurūpe manasi ।।

yathāyam manasi sphāra ārambhaḥ sphurati sphuṭam ।
dṛṣṭāntadṛṣṭyā sphuṭayā tathā kathaya me ḥnagha ।।

ārambhaḥ jagadākhya ārambhaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaraṃ kathayati yathaindavānāṃ viprāṇāṃ jaganty avapuṣām api ।
sthitāni jātadārḍhyāni manasīdaṃ tathā sthitam ।।

avapuṣām mṛtatvena śarīrarahitānām ।।

lavaṇasya yathā rājñaś cendrajālākulākṛteḥ ।
caṇḍālatvam anuprāptaṃ tathedam manasi sthitam ।।

indrajālena aindrajālikaprayuktenendrajālenākulā ākṛtir yasya ।।

bhārgavasya ciraṃ kālaṃ svargabhogabubhukṣayā ।
bhogeśvaratvaṃ ca yathā tathedam manasi sthitam ।।

bhārgavasya śukrasya ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati bhagavan bhṛguputrasya svargabhogabubhukṣayā ।
katham bhogādhināthatvaṃ saṃsāritvam babhūva ca ।।

bhogādhināthatvaṃ kiṃ saṃsāritvaṃ saṃsārabhāvaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ uttaram āha śṛṇu rāma purā vṛttaṃ saṃvādam bhṛgukālayoḥ ।
sānau mandaraśailasya tamālaviṭapākule ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

purā mandaraśailasya sānau kusumasaṅkule ।
atapyata tapo ghoraṃ kasmiṃścid bhagavān bhṛguḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tam upāste sma tejasvī bālaḥ putro mahāmatiḥ ।
śukraḥ sakalacandrābhaḥ prakāśa iva bhāskaram ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhṛgur varavane tasmin samādhāv eva saṃsthitaḥ ।
sarvakālaṃ samutkīrṇo vanopalatalād iva ।।

āsīd ity adhyāhāryam ।।

śukraḥ kusumaśayyāsu kaladhautābjinīṣu ca ।
mandāratarudolāsu bālo ḥramata līlayā ।।

ramaṇe hetum āha bāla iti ।।

vidyāvidyādṛśor madhye śukro prāptamahāpadaḥ ।
triśaṅkur iva rodoḥntar avartata tadā kila ।।

rodoḥntaḥ rodasyoḥ dvyāvāpṛthivyor ।।

nirvikalpasamādhisthe sa kadācit pitary atha ।
avyagro ḥbhavad ekānte jitārir iva bhūmipaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dadarśāpsarasaṃ tatra gacchantīṃ nabhasaḥ pathā ।
kṣīrodamadhyalulitāṃ lakṣmīm iva janārdanaḥ ।।

apsarasaṃ viśinaṣṭi

mandāramālyavalitām mandānilacalālakām ।
hārijhāṅkārigamanāṃ sugandhitanabhoḥnilām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

lāvaṇyapādapalatām madaghūrṇitalocanām ।
