amṛtīkṛtataddeśāṃ dehendūdayakāntibhiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kāntām ālokya tasyābhūd ullāsataralam manaḥ ।
dṛṣṭe nirmalapūrṇendau vapur ambunidher iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena suravadhūtvam asya kathayati manasijeṣuśatāhatam āśaye sa parirudhya manas tadanūśanāḥ ।
vigalitetaravṛttitayātmanā suravadhūmaya eva babhūva saḥ ।।

āśaye hṛddeśe । parirudhya anyābhyaḥ vṛttibhyaḥ baddhvā । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe pañcamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

atha tām manasā dhyāyaṃs tatraivāmīlitekṣaṇaḥ ।
ārabdhavān manorājyam idam ekaḥ kilośanāḥ ।।

uśanāḥ śukraḥ ।।

eṣā hi lalanā vyomni sahasranayanālaye ।
samprāpto ḥyam ahaṃ svargam ālolasurasundaram ।।

sahasranayanālaye svarge ।।

ime te mṛdumandārakusumottaṃsasundarāḥ ।
dravatkanakaniḥṣyandavilāsivapuṣaḥ surāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

imās tā locanollāsasṛṣṭanīlābjavṛṣṭayaḥ ।
mugdhā hāsavilāsinyaḥ kāntā hariṇadṛṣṭayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ime te kaustubhoddyotā anyoḥnyapratibimbitāḥ ।
viśvarūpopamākārā maruto mattakāśinaḥ ।।

viśvarūpasya viṣṇoḥ । samaḥ ākāraḥ yeṣāṃ । te । maruto devaviśeṣāḥ ।।

airāvaṇakaṭāmodaviraktamadhupaśrutāḥ ।
imās tāḥ kākalīgītā gīrvāṇagaṇagītayaḥ ।।

kākalīgītāḥ kākalīgītākhyāḥ ।।

iyaṃ sā kanakāmbhojacaradvairiñcasārasā ।
mandākinītaṭodyānaviśrāntasuranāyikā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ete te yamacandrendrasūryānilajalānalāḥ ।
lokapālās tanūddyotakīrṇadīptojjvalārciṣaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ayaṃ sa suravikrāntahetikaṇḍūyitānanaḥ ।
airāvaṇo raṇaddantaprotadaityendramaṇḍalaḥ ।।

suraiḥ devaiḥ । vikrāntahetibhiḥ kaṇḍūyitam ānanam yasya । saḥ ।।

ime te bhūtalasthānā vyomatārakatāṃ gatāḥ ।
vaimānikāś calaccāruhāracāmarakuṇḍalāḥ ।।

bhūtale sthānaṃ yeṣām ।।

imās tā vividhodyānamaṇimandiramaṇḍitāḥ ।
vimānapaṅktayaś cārucāmīkaramayātapāḥ ।।

cārucāmīkaramayaḥ ātapaḥ uddyotaḥ yāsām ।।

merūpalatalāsphālaśīkarākīrṇadevatāḥ ।
etās tāḥ kīrṇamandārā gaṅgāsalilavīcayaḥ ।।

merūpalataleṣu yaḥ āsphālaḥ vighaṭṭanam । taiḥ ākīrṇāḥ devatāḥ yābhis ।।

etāḥ prasṛtamandāramañjarīpuñjapiñjarāḥ ।
dolālolāpsaraḥśreṇyaḥ śakropavanavīthayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ime te kundamandāramakarandasugandhayaḥ ।
candrāṃśunikarākārāḥ pārijātasamīraṇāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

puṣpakesaranīhārapaṭavāseraṇotsukaiḥ ।
latāṅganāgaṇair vyāptam idaṃ tan nandanaṃ vanam ।।

puṣpakesaram eva nīhāraḥ । tasya yat īraṇam cālanam ।।

kāntagītaravānandapranartitasurāṅganau ।
imau tau vallakīsnigdhasvarau nāradatumburū ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ime te puṇyakartāro bhūribhūṣanabhūṣitāḥ ।
vyomany uḍḍayamāneṣu vimāneṣu sukhaṃ sthitāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

madamanmathamattāṅgya imās tāḥ surayoṣitaḥ ।
deveśvaraṃ niṣevante vanaṃ vanalatā iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

candrāṃśujālakusumāś cintāmaṇigulucchakāḥ ।
kalpavṛkṣa ime pakvaratnastavakadanturāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

iha tāvad imaṃ śakram aham āsanasaṃsthitam ।
dvitīyam iva deveśam pūjayaivābhivādaye ।।

deveśam mahādevam ।।

iti sañcintya śukreṇa manasaiva śacīpatiḥ ।
tenābhivāditas tatra dvitīya iva vai bhṛguḥ ।।

manasā eva na tu kāyena ।।

atha sādaram utthāya śukraḥ śakreṇa pūjitaḥ ।
gṛhītahastam ānīya samīpa upaveśitaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dhanyas tvadāgamenādya svargo ḥyaṃ śukra śobhate ।
uṣyatāṃ ciram eveha śakra ittham uvāca tam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha tatropaviśyāsau bhārgavaḥ śobhitānanaḥ ।
śriyaṃ jahāra śaśinaḥ sakalasyāmalasya ca ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokenāsya naratvatyāgaṃ kathayati

sakalasuragaṇābhivandito ḥsau bhṛgutanayaḥ śatamanyupārśvasaṃsthaḥ ।
cirataram atulām avāpa tuṣṭiṃ naramatim ujjhitavān alam babhūva ।।

asau śukraḥ । naramatim naro ḥham iti buddhim । alam atiśayena । ujjhitavān babhūva sampannaḥ । devatvam eva svasmin jñātavān iti bhāvaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ ।।

iti śukraḥ puram prāpya vaibudhaṃ svena cetasā ।
visasmāra nijam bhāvam prāktanaṃ vyasanaṃ vinā ।।

iti evam । śukraḥ svena cetasā vaibudham puram prāpya । vyasanam apsaroviṣayām āsaktiṃ । sarvaṃ nijam prāktanam bhāvam visasmāra । vyasanasyāpi mānuṣabhāve evodbhūtatvāt prāktanatvaṃ jñeyam ।।

muhūrtam atha viśramya tasya pārśve śacīpateḥ ।
svargaṃ vihartum uttasthau svarvāsiparicoditaḥ ।।

svarvāsiparicoditaḥ amaracoditaḥ ।।

svargaśriyaṃ samālokya lolalocanalāñchitam ।
straiṇaṃ draṣṭuṃ jagāmāsau nalinīm iva sārasaḥ ।।

straiṇam strīsamūham ।।

tatra tām mṛgaśāvākṣīṃ kāntām adhyāgatām asau ।
dadarśa vipināntaḥsthām bhṛṅgaś cūtalatām iva ।।

tām pūrvam manuṣyaloke ḥnubhūtām ।।

tām ālokya lasallolavilāsavalitākṛtim ।
āsīd vilīyamānāṅgo jyotsnayendumaṇir yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vilīyamānasarvāṅgas tām avaikṣata kāminīm ।
candrakānta iva jyotsnāṃ śītalāṃ khe vilāsinīm ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tenāvalokitā sāpi tatparāyaṇatāṃ gatā ।
niśānte cakravākena kāntena parikūjitā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rasād vikasator nūnam anyoḥnyam anuraktayoḥ ।
prātar arkanalinyor yā śobhā saiva tayor abhūt ।।

tayoḥ śukrāpsarasoḥ ।।

saṅkalpitārthadāyitvād deśasya madanena sā ।
sarvāṅgaṃ vivaśīkṛtya śukrāyaiva samarpitā ।।

deśasya svargadeśasya । saṅkalpitārthadāyitvāt । madanena asau apsarāḥ । sarvāṅgaṃ sarveṣu aṅgeṣu । vivaśīkṛtya । śukrāya samarpitā dattā । sarvasaṅkalpadāyinaḥ svargadeśasyaiva māhātmyam etat । yan madanenāsau vivaśīkṛtya śukrāya samarpiteti bhāvaḥ ।।

petuḥ smaraśarās tasyā mṛduṣv aṅgeṣu bhūriśaḥ ।
palāśeṣv iva padminyā dhārā navapayomucaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sā babhūva smarādhūtā lolālivalayālakā ।
mandavātavinunnāyā mañjaryāḥ sahadharmiṇī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nīlanīrajanetrāṃ tāṃ haṃsavāraṇagāminīm ।
madanaḥ kṣobhayām āsa pūraḥ kamalinīm iva ।।

pūraḥ jalapūraḥ ।।

atha tāṃ tādṛśīṃ dṛṣṭvā śukraḥ saṅkalpitārthabhāk ।
tamaḥ saṅkalpayām āsa saṃhāram iva bhūtakṛt ।।

saṅkalpayām āsa saṅkalpenotpāditavān ।।

triviṣṭapasya deśo ḥsau babhūva timirākulaḥ ।
bhūlokasyāndhatamaso lokālokataṭo yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

lajjāndhakāratīkṣṇāṃśau tasmiṃs timiramaṇḍale ।
pratiṣṭhām āgate tasya mithunasyeva manmathe ।।

teṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu gateṣv abhimatāṃ diśam ।
tasmāt pradeśād bhūlokaṃ dinānte vihageṣv iva ।।

sā dīrghadhavalāpāṅgā pravṛddhamadanā tathā ।
ājagāma bhṛgoḥ putram mayūrī vāridaṃ yathā ।।

timiramaṇḍale kasmin । lajjā evāndhakāraḥ । tasya ।।

dhavalāgāramadhyasthe paryaṅke parikalpite ।
viveśa bhārgavas tatra kṣīroda iva mādhavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sā pādāv avalambyāsya vivaśeva varānanā ।
rarāja ca surebhasya pādalagneva padminī ।।

vivaśā parāyattaḥ ।।

uvāca cedaṃ lalitaṃ lasatsnehotkayā girā ।
vaco madhuram ānandi vilāsi valitākṣaram ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

paśyāmalenduvadana maṇḍalīkṛtakārmukaḥ ।
abalām anubadhnāti mām eṣa kimanaṅgakaḥ ।।

kutsitaḥ anaṅgaḥ kimanaṅgakaḥ ।।

pāhi mām abalāṃ nātha dīnāṃ tvaccharaṇām iha ।
kṛpaṇāśvāsanaṃ sādho viddhi saccaritavratam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

snehadṛṣṭim ajānadbhir mūḍhair eva mahāmate ।
praṇayā avagaṇyante na rasajñaiḥ kadācana ।।

praṇayāḥ lakṣaṇayā praṇayayuktāḥ । avagaṇyante avamanyante ।।

aśaṅkitopasampannaḥ praṇayo ḥnyoḥnyaraktayoḥ ।
adhaḥkaroti niṣyandaṃ cāndram āsvāditam priya ।।

cāndraṃ niṣyandam amṛtam ।।

na tathā sukhayaty eṣā cetas tribhuvaneśatā ।
yathā parasparānandī snehaḥ prathamaraktayoḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tvatpādasparśaneneyaṃ samāśvastāsmi mānada ।
candrapādaparāmṛṣṭā yathā niśi kumudvatī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃsparśāmṛtapānena tava jīvāmi sundara ।
candrāṃśurasapānena cakorī capalā yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mām imāṃ caraṇālīnām bhramarīṃ karapallavaiḥ ।
āliṅgyāmṛtasampūrṇe satpadmahṛdaye kuru ।।

caraṇayoḥ ā samantāt ।।

ity uktvā puṣpamṛdvaṅgī sā tasya patitorasi ।
vyāghūrṇitālinayanā sutarāv iva mañjarī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena kathayati

tau dampatī tatra vilāsakāntau vilesatus tāsu vanasthalīṣu ।
kiñjalkagaurānilaghūrṇitāsu mattau dvirephāv iva padminīṣu ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe saptamaḥ sargaḥ ।। iti cittavilāsena ciram utprekṣitaiḥ priyaiḥ ।
praṇayair bhārgavasyāsīt tuṣṭaye sasamāgamaḥ ।।

sasamāgamaḥ tayā apsarasā saha samāgamaḥ ।।

mandāradāmākulayā vaibudhāsavamattayā ।
tadā tena tayā sārdhaṃ dvitīyenāmalendunā ।। vihṛtam mattahaṃsāsu hemapaṅkajinīṣu ca ।
taṭeṣv amaravāhinyāḥ saha kinnaracāraṇaiḥ ।।

vaibudhāsavaḥ amṛtam ।।

pītam indudalasyandi devaiḥ saha rasāyanam ।
pārijātalatājālanilayeṣu vilāsinā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

cārucaitrarathodyānalatādolāsu līlayā ।
ciraṃ vilasitaṃ vyagraiḥ saha vidyādharīgaṇaiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nandanopavanābhogo mandareṇeva vāridhiḥ ।
bhṛśam ullolatāṃ nītaḥ pramathaiḥ saha śāmbhavaiḥ ।।

śukreṇa śāmbhavaiḥ śambhusambandhibhiḥ । pramathaiḥ rudragaṇaiḥ । saha । nandanopavanābhogaḥ bhṛśam ullolatām nītaḥ ।।

bālahemalatājālajaṭilāsu darīṣu ca ।
bhrāntam unmattarāgeṇa mairavīṣv abjinīṣu ca ।।

śukreṇa kartrā bhrāntam bhramaḥ kṛtaḥ । śukreṇa kathambhūtena । unmattarāgeṇa udriktarāgeṇa ।।

kailāsavanakuñjeṣu tayā saha vilāsinā ।
hārendudhavalā rātriḥ kṣapitā gaṇagītibhiḥ ।।

gaṇagītibhiḥ gandharvādigītakṛtaiḥ vinodair ity arthaḥ ।।

gandhamādanaśailasya viśramyopari sānuṣu ।
sā tena kanakāmbhojair āpādam abhimaṇḍitā ।।

āpādam pādaparyantam ।।

lokālokataṭānteṣu vicitrāścaryahāriṣu ।
krīḍitaṃ kṛtahāsena rāma tena tayā saha ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mandarāntarakaccheṣu sārdhaṃ hariṇaśāvakaiḥ ।
avasat sa samāḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ kalpitāmaramandiraḥ ।।

kalpitam kalpanayā sampāditam । amaramandiram devagṛham । yena ।।

kṣīrārṇavataṭeṣv asya vanitāsahacāriṇaḥ ।
kṣīṇaṃ kṛtayugād ardhaṃ śvetadvīpajanaiḥ saha ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

gandharvanagarodyānalīlāviracanair asau ।
sṛṣṭānantajagatsṛṣṭeḥ kālasyānukṛtiṃ gataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

athāvasad asau śukraḥ purandarapure punaḥ ।
sukhaṃ caturyugāny aṣṭau hariṇekṣaṇayā saha ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

puṇyakṣayānusandhānāt tataś cāvanimaṇḍale ।
tayaiva saha māninyā papātāpahṛtākṛtiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

parālūnasamastāṅgo hṛtasyandananandanaḥ ।
cintāparavaśo dhvastaḥ samitīvāhato bhaṭaḥ ।।

hṛte syandananandane rathanandanopavane yasya । bhaṭapakṣe hṛtaḥ syandananandanaḥ praśastarathaḥ yasya ।।

patitasyāvanau tasya cintayā saha dīrghayā ।
śarīraṃ śatadhā yātaṃ śilāpātīva nirjharaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

saṃśīrṇayor dehakayoś citte te vāsanāvṛte ।
viceratus tayor vyomni nirnīḍau vihagau yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tatrāviviśatuś cāndraṃ te citte raśmijālakam ।
prāleyatām upetyāśu śālitām atha jagmatuḥ ।।

prāleyatām avaśyāyabhāvam ।।

śālīṃs tān bhuktavān pakvān daśārṇeṣu dvijottamaḥ ।
śaukrāñ śukrāṅganāgarbhān mālaveṣu ca bhūpatiḥ ।।

śaukrān śukrasambandhinaḥ । tadupādānabījanimittānīti yāvat । śukrāṅganā garbhe yeṣām ।।

ajāyatośanāḥ pūrvaṃ daśārṇeṣu dvijottamāt ।
nṛpād uttamasaubhāgyān mālaveṣu tadaṅganā ।।

tadaṅganā śukrāṅganā ।।

sa tatra vavṛdhe bālaḥ sā tatra vavṛdhe ḥṅganā ।
tau pūrvadampatī jātau svarbhraṣṭāv iva bhūtale ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha ṣoḍaśavarṣo ḥbhūc chukraḥ sāraṅganāmabhṛt ।
pitur gṛhe yauvanavāñ śrīmān viprakumārakaḥ ।।

sāraṅgeti nāma bibhartīti sāraṅganāmabhṛt ।।

mālānāmasurastrī sā kumārī rājasadmani ।
bhṛṅgekṣaṇā gatā vṛddhiṃ latā varavane yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rājaputrī tato mālā pūjayām āsa śaṅkaram ।
labheyam prāktanaṃ siddham patim ity aniśaṃ śubhā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha mālavabhūpasya yajñe dvijasabhāgatam ।
mālā dadarśa sāraṅgam pitrā saha samāgatam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā sānavadyāṅgī prāktanasnehabhāvitā ।
dṛṣṭacandrendumaṇivat snehasvinnāṅgikā babhau ।।

prāktanasnehena pūrvajanmasnehena ।।

tato yajñasabhāmadhye dāśārṇadvijadārakam ।
bhartṛtve varayām āsa sā mālā mālavātmajā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kramāt kṛtavivāhāya tasmai vārdhakajarjaraḥ ।
mālaveśo ḥkhilaṃ rājyam pratipādya vanaṃ yayau ।।

vārdhakajarjaraḥ jarājarjaraḥ ।।

sa sāraṅgas tayā sārdhaṃ tasmin mālavamaṇḍape ।
cakārātisukhī rājyaṃ śakravac charadāṃ śatam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha kālena mahatā cañcalatvāc ca cetasaḥ ।
apriyatvam mitho yātau dampatī tau vidher vaśāt ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sāraṅgas tu jarājīrṇaḥ pātasajjakalevaraḥ ।
dadhre śvasanaśaithilyāj jīrṇaparṇasavarṇatām ।।

śvasanaśaithilyāt vātaśaithilyāt ।।

jāyājanavirāgeṇa vārdhakātiśayena ca ।
maraṇam mandamandeho nirīho ḥbhinananda saḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha nīrasarājyasya duḥkhātiśayaśaṃsinaḥ ।
araṇya iva vetālo moho ḥtighanatāṃ gataḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mohāndhakūpapatitam bhogāsaṅgād anāratam ।
avivekinam ajñānam asajjanaparāyaṇam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jahārainaṃ tato mṛtyus tṛṣṇākavalitāśayam ।
pataṅgam iva maṇḍūkaḥ kṛtākrandam akiñcanam ।।

akiñcanam asamartham ।।

tataḥ karmaphalam bhuktvā svam paratra śubhāśubham ।
aṅgeṣu dhīvaro jātaḥ sa durbhāvavaśāt tadā ।।

durbhāvavaśāt durvāsanāvaśāt ।।

tatra dhīvarakarmāṇi kurvan sa śaradāṃ śatam ।
duḥkhajarjaracetastvād vairāgyaṃ samupāyayau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

duḥkhaṃ saṃsāra ity evaṃ cintayan bhāskaraṃ tataḥ ।
sampataṃs tena sañjātaḥ sūryavaṃśe mahānṛpaḥ ।।

sampatan śaraṇaṃ gacchan ।।

śubhabhāvavaśāt so ḥtha kiñcij jñānam avāptavān ।
jajñe nṛpatanuṃ tyaktvā guruḥ sarvopadeśakaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mantrāsādhitasiddhir hi so ḥtha vidyādharo ḥbhavat ।
kalpam ekaṃ tu bubhuje tato vaidyādharīm purīm ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kalpāvasānasamayaṃ nītvā pavanarūpayā ।
tanvā sṛṣṭau pravṛttāyām bhūyo jāto muneḥ sutaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tato munīnāṃ samparkāt tapasy ugre vyavasthitaḥ ।
avasan merugahane manvantaram aninditaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tatra tasya samutpanno mṛgyāḥ putro narākṛtiḥ ।
tatsnehena param moham punar abhyāyayau kṣaṇāt ।।

mṛgyāḥ mṛgīsakāśāt ।।

putrasyāsya dhanam me ḥstu guṇāś cāyuś ca śāśvatam ।
ity anāratacintābhir jahau satyām avasthitim ।।

satyām avasthitim satyabhūtaṃ dharmaparatvam ।।

dharmacintāparibhraṃśāt putrārtham bhogacintanāt ।
kṣīṇāyuṣaṃ tam aharan mṛtyuḥ sarpa ivānilam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhogaikacintayā sārdhaṃ sa samutkrāntacetanaḥ ।
prāpya madreśaputratvam āsīn madramahīpatiḥ ।।

madreśaputratvam madradeśabhūpasutatvam ।।

madradeśe ciraṃ kṛtvā rājyam ucchinnaśātravaḥ ।
jarām abhyājagāmātra himāśanim ivāmbujaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

madrarājatanuṃ taṃ tu tapovāsanayā saha ।
tatyāja tena jāto ḥsau tapasvī tāpasātmajaḥ ।।

saḥ madrarājatanuṃ tatyājeti sambandhaḥ ।।

samaṅgāyā mahānadyās taṭam āsādya tāpasaḥ ।
tapas tepe mahābuddhiḥ sa rāma vigatajvaraḥ ।।

samaṅgā nadībhedaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokena śukrasya sukhāvasthānaṃ kathayati

vividhajanmadaśāvivaśāśayaḥ samanusṛtya śarīraparamparām ।
sukham atiṣṭhad asau bhṛgunandano varanadīsutaṭe dṛḍhavṛkṣavat ।।

varanadīsutaṭe samaṅgākhyāyāḥ utkṛṣṭāyāḥ nadyāḥ śobhane tīre ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe aṣṭamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

iti cintayatas tasya śukrasya pitur agrataḥ ।
jagāmātitarāṃ kālo bahusaṃvatsarātmakaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha kālena mahatā pavanātapajarjaraḥ ।
kāyas tasya papātorvyāṃ chinnamūla iva drumaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

manas tu cañcalābhogaṃ tāsu tāsu daśāsu ca ।
babhrāmātivicitrāsu vanarājiṣv ivaiṇakaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhrāntam udbhrāntam abhitaś cakrārpitam ivākulam ।
manas tasya viśaśrāma samaṅgāsaritas taṭe ।।

cakrārpito hi udbhramati ।।

anantavṛttāntaghanām pelavāṃ sudṛḍhām api ।
tāṃ saṃsṛtidaśāṃ śukro videho ḥnubhavan sthitaḥ ।।

tāṃ saṃsṛtidaśām samaṅgātaṭatāpasasambandhinīṃ saṃsāradaśām । videhaḥ sthūladeharahitaḥ ।।

mandarācalasānusthā sā tanus tasya dhīmataḥ ।
tāpaprasarasaṃśuṣkā carmaśeṣā babhūva ha ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śārīrarandhrapravahadvātaśītkārarūpayā ।
ceṣṭāduḥkhakṣayānandāt kākalyeva sma gāyati ।।

tasya sā tanuḥ । ceṣṭāyā yat duḥkham pīḍā । tasya kṣayāt ya ānandaḥ । kākalyā kalasūkṣmayā gānavācā । kathambhūtayā । śārīrarandhreṣu pravahan yaḥ vātaḥ । tena śītkāraḥ dhvaniviśeṣaḥ । sa eva rūpaṃ yasyāḥ । tādṛśyā ।।

prāṇānusmaraṇocchvāsam iva vāṣpaṃ sma muñcati ।
caṇḍānilavilāsena lulitvā vanabhūmiṣu ।।

vāṣpam kathambhūtam । prāṇāṇām pūrvaṃ sthitānām yad anusmaraṇam anukṣaṇaṃ smaraṇam । tena ucchvāsaḥ vṛddhiḥ yasya । vāṣpatvaṃ cātrāvaśyāyasya jñeyam ।।

tanum eva viśinaṣṭi

manovarākam avaṭe luṭhitam bhavabhūmiṣu ।
hasantīvātiśubhrābhrasitayā dantamālayā ।।

bhavabhūmiṣu sthite avaṭe apsarorūpe avaṭe ।।

darśayantī svakaṃ śūnyaṃ vapur akṣṇor akṛtrimam ।
mukhāraṇyajaratkūparūpayā gartaśobhayā ।।

punaḥ kathambhūtā । akṣṇoḥ svasyākṣiyugalasya । mukham evāraṇyam । tasya jaratkūpatayā gartaśobhayā । tadvyājeneti yāvat । svaṃ vapuḥ śūnyaṃ darśayantī । śūnyā evāham asmīti darśayantīti yāvat । mṛtaśarīrasya ca mukhe māṃsaśeṣāt garto jāyate ।।

tāpopataptā saṃsiktā varṣājalabhareṇa sā ।
pāṃsunā pavanotthena duṣkṛteneva rūṣitā ।।

sā iti tanūparāmarśaḥ ।।

śuṣkakāṣṭhavad ālolā pāteṣu kṛtajhāṅkṛtā ।
dhārānikarapātena vinunnā jaladāgame ।।

vinunnā preritā ।।

prāvṛḍnirjharapūreṇa plutā girinadītaṭe ।
tāramārutaśītkārā vanopala iva sthitā ।।

tāraḥ mārutaśītkāraḥ yasyāṃ sā । vanopala iva vanopalavat । sthitā ।।

vakrā śuṣkāntratantrī ca pūtā jhāṅkārakāriṇī ।
araṇyalakṣmīvīṇeva śūnyacarmamayodarī ।।

araṇyalakṣmyāḥ vīṇā araṇyalakṣmīvīṇā ।।

nanu tādṛśī tasya tanuḥ vanahiṃsraiḥ kathaṃ na bhuktety । atrāha

rāgadveṣavihīnatvāt tasya puṇyāśramasya tu ।
mahātapastvāc ca bhṛgor na bhuktā mṛgapakṣibhiḥ ।।

puṇyāśramasya ca rāgadveṣavihīnatvam tatrasthaprāṇirāgadveṣavihīnatvena jñeyam ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati

yamaniyamakṛśīkṛtāṅgayaṣṭeś carati tapaḥ sma bhṛgūdvahasya cetaḥ ।
tanur atha pavanāpanītaraktā ciram aluṭhan mahatīṣu sā śilāsu ।।

yamaniyamakṛśīkṛtāṅgayaṣṭeḥ bhṛgūdvahasya śukrasya । cetaḥ tapaḥ carati sma । atha sā tanuḥ pavanāpanītaraktā satī mahatīṣu śilāsu aluṭhat luṭhitavatī ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe navamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

atha varṣasahasreṇa divyena parameśvaraḥ ।
bhṛguḥ paramasambodhād virarāma samādhitaḥ ।।

samādhitaḥ kathambhūtāt । paramasambodhāt jñeyamālinyādūṣitajñānarūpāt । na tu mūrcchārūpāt ।।

nāpaśyad agre tanayaṃ taṃ nayāvanatānanam ।
sīmāntaṃ guṇasīmāyāḥ puṇyam mūrtam iva sthitam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

apaśyat kevalaṃ kālaṃ kaṅkālam purato mahat ।
dehayuktam ivābhāgyaṃ dāridryam iva mūrtimat ।।

kālam kṛṣṇam । abhāgyam bhāgyaviparyayaḥ ।।

kaṅkālaṃ viśinaṣṭi

tāpaśuṣkavapuḥ kṛttirandhrasphuritatittiri ।
saṃśuṣkāntrodaraguhāchāyāviśrāntadarduram ।।

tittirayaḥ kīṭaviśeṣāḥ ।।

netragartakasaṃsuptaprasūnavanakīṭakam ।
makṣikāpañjaraprotakośakārikrimivrajam ।।

makṣikāpañjareṣu pañjarākāreṇopaviṣṭeṣu makṣikāsamūheṣu । protaḥ kośakārakrimivrajaḥ yasmin । tat ।।

prāktanīm upabhogehām iṣṭāniṣṭaphalapradām ।
dhārādhautāntayā tanvā hasac chuṣkāsthimālayā ।।

hasat hasad ivety arthaḥ ।।

śiroghaṭena śubhreṇa sampannenenduvarcasā ।
viḍambayac ca karpūraplutaliṅgaśiraḥśriyam ।।

induvarcasā candramahasā ।।

ṛjvā saṃśuṣkasitayā svāsthimātrāvaśeṣayā ।
grīvayātmānusṛtayā dīrghīkurvad ivākṛtim ।।

ātmānusṛtayā । anusṛtayā sambaddhayā ।।

mṛṇālikāpāṇḍurayā dhārāvadhutamāṃsayā ।
nāsāsthilatayā vaktraṃ kṛtasīmākramaṃ dadhat ।।

kṛtasīmākramam kṛtamaryādākramam ।।

dīrghakandharayā nūnam uttānīkṛtavaktrayā ।
prekṣamāṇam iva prāṇān utkrāntān ambarodare ।।

nūnam vitarke ।।

jaṅghorujānudordaṇḍair dviguṇaṃ dīrghatāṃ gataiḥ ।
pramimāṇam ivāśāntaṃ dīrghādhvaśramabhītitaḥ ।।

āśāntam digantam ।।

udareṇātinimnena carmaśeṣeṇa śoṣiṇā ।
pradarśayad ivājñasya hṛdayasyātiśūnyatām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

prekṣya tac chuṣkakaṅkālam ālānam iva dantinaḥ ।
pūrvāparaparāmarśam akurvan bhṛgur utthitaḥ ।।

bhṛguḥ kiṃ kurvan । putrasnehena pūrvāparaparāmarśam akurvan । yoginām api hi kadācit prakṛtivaśāt dehapātaṃ tāvat pūrvāparaparāmarśahīnatvaṃ jāyate । kiṃ tu teṣāṃ tat kṣaṇikam eveti । utthitaḥ svātmatattvaparāmarśāt uccalitaḥ ।।

ālokasamakālaṃ hi pratibhātaṃ tato bhṛgoḥ ।
ciram utkrāntajīvaḥ kim matputro ḥyam iti kṣaṇāt ।।

tataḥ utthānānantaram । ālokasamakālam putrakaṅkāladarśanasamakālam । bhṛgoḥ iti pratibhātam sphuritam iti । ayam matputraḥ ciram bahukālād ārabhya । utkrāntajīvaḥ kim katham । sampanna ity arthaḥ ।।

acintayata evāsya bhaviṣyattābalaṃ tataḥ ।
kālam prati babhūvāśu kopaḥ paramadāruṇaḥ ।।

atha bhaviṣyattābalam bhavitavyatābalam । acintayataḥ tatkṣaṇotthapūrvāparavimarśarāhityenāvimṛśataḥ । asya bhṛgoḥ । kālam prati cinmātrasthakriyāvaicitryarūpe kāle । paramadāruṇaḥ kopaḥ babhūva ।।

akāla eva matputro nītaḥ kim iti kopitaḥ ।
kālāya śāpam utsraṣṭum bhagavān upacakrame ।।

akāle tadyuganiyatamanuṣyāyurasamāptirūpe kālābhāve । idam atra tātparyam । nirvikalpasamādhinā śuddhacinmātratāṃ yātaḥ asau bhṛguḥ । tasmāt samādheḥ utthitaḥ । tataḥ bāhyasparśena kiñcinmātraṃ sphaṭikavad āsraṣṭum ārabdhaḥ । tatra prathamam akāle putram mṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā vivaśībhūtaḥ । samanantarakālānubhūtena cinmātrarūpeṇa svena kṛtaṃ kriyāvaicitryarūpaṃ kālaṃ nāśayitum aicchat । yaś ca kālāgamaḥ sa kathaṃ svayaṃ kṛtaṃ svabhāvasahacaram etaṃ nāśayāmīti vivekāgama eva jñeyaḥ । ity āstāṃ rahasyodghāṭanena ।।

athākalitarūpo ḥsau kālaḥ kavalitaprajaḥ ।
ādhibhautikam āsthāya vapur munim upāyayau ।।

akalitarūpaḥ । akalitam paramātmagatatvena sthitatvāt prameyatām agatam । rūpaṃ yasya । ādhibhautiko dehaḥ paramārthataḥ vicārarūpaḥ eva jñeyaḥ । bāhyān prati tu devatārūpaḥ ।।

kīdṛśaḥ upāyayāv ity apekṣāyām bāhyadevatārūpatvam bāhyadṛṣṭīn prati kathayati

khaḍgapāśadharaḥ śrīmān kuṇḍalī kavacānvitaḥ ।
ṣaḍbhujaḥ ṣaṇmukho bahvyā vṛtaḥ kiṅkarasenayā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yaccharīrasamutthena jvālājālena valgatā ।
phullakiṃśukavṛkṣasya babhārādreḥ śriyaṃ nabhaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yatkarasthatriśūlāgraniṣṭhyūtair agnimaṇḍalaiḥ ।
virejur uditair āśāḥ kānakair iva kuṇḍalaiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yatpāśaśvasanāyastaśikharā medinībhṛtaḥ ।
dolām iva samārūḍhāś celuḥ petuś ca ghūrṇitāḥ ।।

āyastaśikharā ākṛṣṭaśikharāḥ ।।

yatkhaḍgamaṇḍaloddyotaśyāmam bimbaṃ vivasvataḥ ।
kalpadagdhajagaddhūmaparyākulam ivābabhau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sa upetya mahābāhuḥ kupitaṃ tam mahāmunim ।
kalpakṣubdhābdhigambhīraṃ sāntvapūrvam uvāca ha ।।

saḥ kālaḥ ।।

vijñātalokasthitayo mune dṛṣṭaparāvarāḥ ।
hetunāpi na muhyanti kim u hetum vinottamāḥ ।।

dṛṣṭaḥ svarūpatvenānubhūtaḥ । parāvaraḥ parāvararūpeṇa sthitaṃ cinmātratattvam । yaiḥ ।।

tvam anantatapā vipro vayaṃ niyatipālakāḥ ।
tena sampūjyase pūjya sādho netarayecchayā ।।

anantatapāḥ aparimitatapāḥ । tena anantatapastvena ।।

mā tapaḥ kṣapaya kṣubdhaiḥ kalpakālamahānalaiḥ ।
yo na dagdho ḥsmi me tasya kiṃ tvaṃ śāpena dhakṣyasi ।।

yo ḥsmi yo ḥham । cinmātrakriyāvaicitryarūpasya kālasya kadāpi dāhāsambhavāt iti bhāvaḥ । dhakṣyasīti । daha bhasmīkaraṇa ity asya lṛḍantasya prayogaḥ ।।

saṃsārāvalayo grastā nigīrṇā rudrakoṭayaḥ ।
bhuktāni viṣṇuvṛndāni kena śāptā vayam mune ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhoktāro hi vayam brahman bhojanaṃ yuṣmadādayaḥ ।
svayaṃ niyatir eṣā hi nāvayor etad īhitam ।।

āvayoḥ yuṣmākam asmākam ca ।।

svayam ūrdhvam prayāty agniḥ svayaṃ yānti payāṃsy adhaḥ ।
bhoktāram bhojanaṃ yāti sṛṣṭiś cāpy antakaṃ svayam ।।

antakam kālam ।।

idam ittham mune rūpam asyeha paramātmanaḥ ।
svātmani svayam evātmā svata eva vijṛmbhate ।।

vijṛmbhate vicitrābhiḥ kriyābhiḥ vilasati ।।

neha kartā na bhoktāsti dṛṣṭyā naṣṭakalaṅkayā ।
bahavaś ceha kartāro dṛṣṭyānaṣṭakalaṅkayā ।।

naṣṭakalaṅkayā dṛṣṭyā samyagdṛṣṭyā । anaṣṭakalaṅkayā dṛṣṭyā asamyagdṛṣṭyā ।।

kartṛtākartṛte brahman kevalam parikalpite ।
asamyagdarśanenaiva na samyagdarśanena vaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

puṣpāṇi taruṣaṇḍeṣu bhūtāni bhuvaneṣu ca ।
svayam āyānti yāntīha kalpyate hetutā vidheḥ ।।

mūḍhaiḥ iha vidheḥ hetutā kalpyate kalpanayā bhāvyate । na tu paramārthataḥ hetutā kasyāpy asti । kevalasya śuddhacinmātrasyaiva sthitatvāt ।।

abbimbitasya candrasya calane kartrakartṛte ।
na satye nānṛte yadvat tadvat kālasya sṛṣṭiṣu ।।

kālasya kriyāvaicitryarūpasya mama ।।

mano mithyābhramāl loke kartṛtākartṛtāmayam ।
karoti kalanāṃ rajjvām bhrāntekṣaṇa ivāhitām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

phalitam āha

tena mā gā mune kopam āpadām īdṛśaḥ kramaḥ ।
yad yathā tat tathaivāstu satyam ālokayākulaḥ ।।

āpadām kramaḥ īdṛśa eva bhavati । etāḥ sarveṣām evāyāntīti bhāvaḥ । yat yathā asti । ākulaḥ ākulībhūtaḥ tvam । pravāhāyāte śubhāśubhajāle mā kṣobhaṃ gaccheti bhāvaḥ ।।

na vayam prabhutārthena nābhimānavaśīkṛtāḥ ।
svato hevākavaśataḥ kevalaṃ niyatau sthitāḥ ।।

vayam prabhutārthena prabhutāprayojanena । niyatau bhagavatkṛte niyamane । na sthitāḥ । na cābhimānavaśīkṛtāḥ santaḥ sthitāḥ । kiṃ tu svataḥ svabhāvataḥ utthitāt । hevākavaśataḥ niyatau kevalaṃ sthitāḥ । kiñcid apy atrāsmāsv adhīnaṃ nāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

prakṛtavyavahārehāṃ niyatāṃ niyater vaśāt ।
prājñaḥ samanuvarteta nābhimānamahātamāḥ ।।

niyatām śāstraniyatām । prājñaḥ kathambhūtaḥ । na abhimāna evāhaṅkartety abhimāna eva tamaḥ yasya ।।

kartavyam eva kriyate kevalaṃ kāryakovidaiḥ ।
sauṣuptīṃ vṛttim āśritya kayācid api nāśayā ।।

prājñaiḥ sarvaṃ phalānusandhānarahitam eva kriyate iti bhāvaḥ ।।

kva sā jñānamayī dṛṣṭiḥ kva mahattvaṃ kva dhīratā ।
mārge sarvaprasiddhe hi kim andha iva muhyasi ।।

sā samanantaram evānubhūtā । sarvaprasiddhe laukike ।।

trikālāmaladarśitvaṃ dhārayann api cetasi ।
avicārya jagadyātrāṃ kim mūrkha iva muhyasi ।।

trikālāmaladarśitvam pūrvāparavimarśabhājanatvam ।।

svakarmaphalapākotthām avicārya daśāṃ sute ।
kim mūrkha iva sarvajña mudhā māṃ śaptum arhasi ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dehinām iha sarveṣāṃ śarīraṃ dvividham mune ।
kiṃ na jānāsi vā deham ekam anyan manoḥbhidham ।।

deham sthūladeham ।।

tatra deho jaḍo ḥtyarthaṃ vināśaikaparāyaṇaḥ ।
manas tūtthānaniyataṃ kadarthāt kṣīyate na vā ।।

utthāne saṅkalparūpe udyoge । atha vā tenāpi ।।

catureṇa yathā sādho rathaḥ sārathinohyate ।
kurvatā kiñcana svehāṃ deho ḥyam manasā tathā ।।

uhyate svābhimataṃ deśam prati nīyate ।।

asat saṅkalpya kriyate sac charīraṃ vināśyate ।
kṣaṇena manasā paṅkapuruṣaḥ śiśunā yathā ।।

asat avidyamānam ।।

cittam eveha puruṣas tatkṛtaṃ kṛtam ucyate ।
tad baddhaṃ kalanāhetoḥ kalanāstaṃ vimucyate ।।

kalanāhetoḥ saṅkalpākhyāt kāraṇāt । kalanāstam astakalanam ।।

ayaṃ deha idaṃ netram idam aṅgam idaṃ śiraḥ ।
idaṃ sphāravikāraṃ tan mana evābhidhīyate ।।

manaḥ kathambhūtam । idaṃ sphāravikāram । idam iti sphāraḥ sphuraṇaśīlaḥ । manaḥ paṇḍitais tad abhidhīyate । ayaṃ dehaḥ idaṃ netram idam aṅgam idam śiraḥ iti yad bhavati ।।

mano hi jīvaj jīvākhyaṃ niścāyakatayā tu dhīḥ ।
ahaṅkāro ḥbhimānitvān nānātvaṃ tv idam eti hi ।।

jīvat jīvanakriyākartṛtām bhajat । niścāyakatayā niścayakartṛtvena । abhimānitvāt deho ḥham ity abhimānakartṛtvena । nānātvajīvādirūpaṃ nānātvam ।।

dehavāsanayā cetas tv anyāni svāni ceddhayā ।
pārthivāni śarīrāṇi santīva paripaśyati ।।

cetaḥ iddhayā dehavāsanayā deho ḥham iti vāsanayā । pārthivāni śarīrāṇi santi iva paśyati anubhavati ।।

ālokayati cet satyaṃ tad asatyamayīm manaḥ ।
śarīrabhāvanāṃ tyaktvā paramāṃ yāti nirvṛtim ।।

manaḥ satyam samyak । asatyamayīm asatyasvarūpām । śarīrabhāvanāṃ tyaktvā । paramāṃ nirvṛtim cinmātramayatārūpam ānandam ।।

phalitam āha

tan manas tava putrasya samādhau tvayi saṃsthite ।
svamanorathamārgeṇa durād dūrataraṃ gatam ।।

yataḥ mana eva sarvatra kartṛ asti tat tato hetoḥ ।।

idam auśanasaṃ tyaktvā deham mandarakandare ।
prayātaṃ vaibudhaṃ sadma nīḍoḍḍīnaḥ khago yathā ।।

auśanasam śukrasambandhi ।।

tatra mandārakuñjeṣu pārijātagṛheṣu ca ।
nandanodyānaṣaṇḍeṣu lokapālapurīṣu ca ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mune caturyugāny aṣṭau viśvācīṃ devasundarīm ।
asevata mahātejāḥ ṣaṭpadaḥ padminīm iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tīvrasaṃvegasampannasvasaṅkalpopakalpite ।
atha puṇyakṣaye jāte nīhāra iva śārvare ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pramlānakusumottaṃsaḥ svinnāṅgāvalayālasaḥ ।
sa papāta tayā sākaṃ kālapakvam phalaṃ yathā ।।

vaibudhaṃ tat parityajya nabhasy eva śarīrakam ।
bhūtākāśam athāsādya vasudhāyām ajāyata ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

āsīd dvijo daśārṇeṣu kosaleṣu mahīpatiḥ ।
dhīvaro ḥṅgamahāṭavyāṃ haṃsas tripathagātaṭe ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sūryavaṃśī nṛpaḥ pauṇḍre sauraḥ sālveṣu daiśikaḥ ।
kalpaṃ vidyādharaḥ śrīmān dhīmān atha muneḥ sutaḥ ।।

pauṇḍre deśe । sūryavaṃśī nṛpaḥ jātaḥ । sālveṣu sauraḥ sūryakulotpannaḥ ।।

madreṣv atha mahīpālas tatas tāpasabālakaḥ ।
vāsudeva iti khyātaḥ samaṅgāyās taṭe sthitaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

anyāsv api vicitrāsu vāsanāvaśataḥ svayam ।
viṣamāsv eva putras te cacārānantayoniṣu ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

anyapadavyākhyāṃ kurvan samaṅgātaṭatāpasajanmanaḥ pūrvabhāvīni janmāntarāṇy asya kathayati

abhūd vindhyavane gopaḥ kirataḥ kekayeṣu ca ।
sauvīreṣu ca sāmantas traigartaś caiva daiśikaḥ ।।

traigartaḥ trigartadeśasambandhī ।।

vaṃśagulmaḥ kirāteṣu hariṇaś cīrajaṅgale ।
sarīsṛpas tālatale tamāle vanakukkuṭaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ayaṃ sa putro bhavato bhūtvā mantravidāṃ varaḥ ।
prajajāpa purā vidyāṃ vidyādharapadapradām ।।

prajajāpa japitavān ।।

tenāsau bhagavan brahman vyomni vidyādharo mahān ।
hārakuṇḍalakeyūrī līlānicayalāsakaḥ ।।

bhagavan brahman । kīdṛśo vidyādharaḥ abhūd ity apekṣāyāṃ viśeṣaṇāṇy āha hāreti ।।

nāyikānalinībhānuḥ puṣpacāpa ivāparaḥ ।
vidyādharīṇāṃ dayito gandharvapurabhūṣaṇam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sa kalpāvadhim āsādya dvādaśādityadhāmani ।
jagāma bhasmaśeṣatvaṃ śalabhaḥ pāvake yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jagannirmāṇarahite sphāre nabhasi sā tataḥ ।
vāsanā tasya babhrāma nirnīḍā vihagī yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha kālena sañjāte vicitrārambhakāriṇi ।
saṃsārāḍambarārambhe brāhmī rātriviparyaye ।।

sā manovāsanā tasya vātavyāvalitā satī ।
kṛte brāhmaṇatām etya jātādya vasudhātale ।।

kṛte kṛtayuge ।।

vāsudevābhidhāno ḥsau mune viprakumārakaḥ ।
jāto matimatām madhye samadhītākhilaśrutiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kalpaṃ vidyādharo bhūtvā nadyā adya mahāmune ।
tapaś carati te putraḥ samaṅgāyās taṭe sthitaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena jaraḍhayonigamanaṃ kathayati

vividhaviṣamavāsanānuvṛttyā khadirakarañjakarālakoṭarāsu ।
jagati jaraḍhayoniṣu prayāto gahanatarāsu ca kānanasthalīṣu ।।

jaraḍhayonipakṣe khadirakarañjakarālāsu nānāvidhaduḥkhasaṅkaṭāsu ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe daśamaḥ sargaḥ ।।

adyoddāmataraṅgaughajhāṅkāraraṇitānile ।
tīre varataraṅgiṇyāḥ tapas tapati te sutaḥ ।।

varataraṅgiṇyāḥ samaṅgāyāḥ ।।

jaṭāvān akṣavalayī jitasarvendriyabhramaḥ ।
tatra varṣaśatāny aṣṭau saṃsthitas tapasi sthire ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yadīcchasi mune draṣṭuṃ taṃ svaputramanobhramam ।
tat samunmīlya vijñānanetram āśu vilokaya ।।

svaputrākāram manobhramam svaputramanobhramam । svaputram iti yāvat ।।

ity ukte jagadīśena kālena samadṛṣṭinā ।
muniḥ sañcintayām āsa jñānākṣṇā tanayehitam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dadarśa ca muhūrtena pratibhāsavaśād asau ।
putrodantam aśeṣeṇa buddhidarpaṇabimbitam ।।

dadarśa jñānadṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭavān ।।

punar mandarasānusthāṃ kāle kālāgrasaṃsthitām ।
samaṅgāyās taṭād etya viveśa svatanum bhṛguḥ ।।

kāle svalpakāle । kālāgrasaṃsthitām kālapurovartinīm ।।

vismayasmerayā dṛṣṭyā kālam ālokya kāntayā ।
vītarāgam uvācedaṃ vītarāgo munir vacaḥ ।।

kālasya samavartitvāt vītarāgitvam ।।

bhṛguḥ kathayati

bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa bālā vayam anābilā ।
tvādṛśām eva dhīr deva trikālāmaladarśinī ।।

bālāḥ mūrkhāḥ । anāvilety asya uttarārdhena sambandhaḥ ।।

nānākāraṃ vikārāḍhyā satyevāsatyarūpiṇī ।
vibhramaṃ janayaty eṣā dhīrasyāpi jagadgatiḥ ।।

jagadgatiḥ jagadracanā ।।

tvam eva deva jānāsi tvadabhyantaravarti yat ।
rūpam asyā manovṛtter indrajālavidhāyakam ।।

tvadabhyantaravarti tvanmadhyavarti ।।

matputrasyāsya bhagavan mṛtyuḥ kila na vidyate ।
tenemam mṛtam ālokya jātaḥ sambhramavān aham ।।

śukrasya cirajīvitvāt ।।

akṣīṇajīvitam putraṃ kālo me nītavān iti ।
niyater vaśato deva tvacchāpecchā mamoditā ।।

niyater iti । mama yā tvacchāpecchā jātā sāpi niyatir eva । ato mama na ko ḥpi doṣa iti bhāvaḥ ।।

na tu vijñātasaṃsāragatayo vayam āpadam ।
sampadaṃ vāpi gacchāmo harṣāmarṣavaśaṃ kila ।।

prāpyeti śeṣaḥ । sampadaṃ vā prāpyeti ।।

ayuktakāriṇi krodhaḥ prasādo yuktakāriṇi ।
kartavya iti rūḍheyaṃ sāṃsārī bhagavan sthitiḥ ।।

ataḥ tvayy ayuktakāritvam āśaṅkya mayā krodhaḥ kṛta iti bhāvaḥ ।।

idaṃ kāryam idaṃ neti yāvajjīvaṃ jagatkramaḥ ।
yāvad agniḥ sthitā tāvad auṣṇyadāhādidṛṣṭayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

idaṃ kāryam idaṃ neti heyā yasya jagatsthitiḥ ।
tasyaitatsamparityāgo heya eva jagadguro ।।

yasya । idaṃ kāryam idaṃ na kāryam । iti evaṃrūpā । jagatsthitiḥ heyā bhavati । tasya tatsamparityāgo ḥpi heya eva । tattyāgasyāpi jagatsthitirūpatvāt । ato mayā pūrvasthitiḥ na tyakteti bhāvaḥ ।।

kevalaṃ tānayīṃ cintām anālokya yadā vayam ।
bhagavan bhavate kṣubdhā yātāḥ smas tena vācyatām ।।

tānayīṃ tanayasambandhinīm । vācyatām tvatkrodhakāritvarūpanindāyogyatām ।।

tvayedānīm ahaṃ deva smāritas tanayehitam ।
samaṅgāyās taṭe tena dṛṣṭo ḥyaṃ tanayo mayā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

manye jagati bhūtānāṃ dve śarīre na sarvaga ।
mana eva śarīraṃ hi yenedam bhāvyate jagat ।।

he sarvaga । ihaloke bhūtānāṃ dve śarīre na bhavataḥ । mana eva śarīram bhavati । idaṃ jagat bhāvyate bhāvanayā prakaṭīkriyate ।।

kāla āha

samyag uktaṃ tvayā brahmañ śarīram mana eva naḥ ।
karoti dehaṃ saṅkalpya kumbhakāro ghaṭaṃ yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

karoty akṛtam ākāraṃ kṛtaṃ nāśayati kṣaṇāt ।
saṅkalpena mano mohād bālo vetālakaṃ yathā ।।

mohāt ajñānāt ।।

tathā ca sambhrame svapnamithyājñānādibhāsvarāḥ ।
gandharvanagarākārā dṛṣṭā manasi śaktayaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sthūladṛṣṭidṛśaṃ tv etām avalambya mahāmune ।
puṃso manaḥ śarīraṃ ca kāyau dvāv iti kathyate ।।

sthūladṛṣṭirūpā dṛk sthūladṛṣṭidṛk ।।

manomanananirmāṇamātram etaj jagattrayam ।
na san nāsad iva sphāram uditaṃ netaran mune ।।

etat jagat । manasaḥ yat mananam mananākhyo dharmaḥ । tanmātram eva bhavati । na sat nāsat anirvacanīyam ity arthaḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtam । sphāram ivoditam sphuraṇaśīlam iva prādurbhūtam । paramārthatas tu noditam itīvaśabdopādānam । mātraśabdasyārthaṃ svakaṇṭhena kathayati netarad iti ।।

cittadehāṅgalatayā bhedavāsanayeddhayā ।
dvicandratvam ivājñānān nānāteyaṃ samutthitā ।।

cittākhyasya dehasyāṅgalatayā aṅgalatārūpayā । bhedavāsanayā dvaitavāsanayā । iddhayā puṣṭayā satyā । nānātā samutthitā prādurbhūtā । dvicandratvam iva । yathā dvicandratvam ajñānāt samuttiṣṭhati । tathety arthaḥ ।।

bhedavāsanayā bahvyā padārthanicayam manaḥ ।
bhinnam paśyati sarvatra ghaṭāvaṭapaṭādikam ।।

bahvyā vistīrṇayā । sarvatra sarveṣu deśeṣu kāleṣu ca ।।

kṛśo ḥtiduḥkhī mūḍho ḥham etāś cānyāś ca bhāvanāḥ ।
bhāvayat svavikalpotthā yāti saṃsāratām manaḥ ।।

saṃsāratām saṃsārabhāvam ।।

mananaṃ kṛtrimaṃ rūpam mamaitan na patāmy aham ।
iti tattyāgataḥ śāntaṃ ceto brahma sanātanam ।।

tattyāgataḥ mananatyāgataḥ ।।

yathetyādiṃ nirāmayā ityantam ekaṃ dṛṣṭāntaṃ vistareṇa kathayati

yathā pravitate ḥmbodhau tate ḥnekataraṅgiṇi ।
somyaspandamayānekakallolāvaliśālini ।।

vāryātmani same svacche śuddhe svāduni śītale ।
avināśini vistīrṇe mahāmahimani sphuṭe ।।

tryaśras taraṅgaḥ svaṃ rūpam bhāvayan sa svabhāvataḥ ।
tryaśro ḥsmīti vikalpena karoti svena kalpanām ।।

bhraśyaṃś caiva paribhraṣṭarūpo ḥsmīti talātalam ।
bhāvayan bhūtalaṃ yāti tādṛgbhāvanayā tayā ।।

utthitaṃ ca balād ūrdhvam utthito ḥsmīti bhāvitaḥ ।
tais tair vikalpais tadbhāvaṃ vikalpayati sābhidham ।।

sasūryapratibimbas tu prakāśo ḥsmīti bhāvitaḥ ।
sarajaḥpuñjapātas tu malino ḥsmīti bhāvitaḥ ।।

saratnaraśmijālas tu śobhate dīptayā śriyā ।
tuṣārabharaviddhas tu śītalo ḥsmīti vindati ।।

sataṭācaladāvāgnipratibimbojjvaladvapuḥ ।
bibheti vata dagdho ḥsmīty āttamīnaś ca kampate ।।

pratibimbitavelādritaṭapakṣivanadrumaḥ ।
mahān ārambhasaṃrambhasaṃyuto ḥsmīti rājate ।।

vimalollasanotpannadhvastalolaśarīrakaḥ ।
khaṇḍaśaḥ pariyāto ḥsmīty āttākranda ivāravī ।।

na cormayas te jaladher vyatiriktāḥ payorasāt ।
na caikaṃ rūpam eteṣāṃ kiñcit sann apy asanmayam ।।

na ca te nyūnadairghyādyā guṇās teṣu ca teṣu ca ।
normayaḥ saṃsthitā abdhau na ca tatra na saṃsthitāḥ ।।

kevalaṃ svasvabhāvasthasaṅkalpavikalīkṛtāḥ ।
naṣṭānaṣṭāḥ punar jātā jātājātāḥ punaḥ kṣatāḥ ।।

parasparaparāmarśān nānātām upayānty alam ।
ekarūpāmbusāmānyamayā eva nirāmayāḥ ।।

anekataraṅgiṇi anekataraṅgayukte । somyaspandamayyaḥ somyajalaspandarūpāḥ । anekakallolāvalayaḥ । etādṛśe vāryātmani । yathā saḥ prasiddhaḥ tryaśraḥ tryaśrākāraḥ taraṅgaḥ । svaṃ rūpam tryaśrarūpam svaṃ rūpam । bhāvayan pramātāram prati prakaṭīkurvan । svabhāvataḥ utthitena svena svasmād । avyatiriktena tryaśro ḥsmīti vikalpena kalpanām tryaśrākārakalpanām । na kevalam etām eva karoti । kiṃ tv anyā api kriyāḥ karoti ity āha bhraśyaṃś cetyādi । saḥ tryaśraḥ taraṅgaḥ paribhraṣṭo ḥsmīti bhāvayan । tataḥ talātalam talātalākhyam । tayā tādṛgbhāvanayā । saḥ tryaśraḥ taraṅgaḥ ūrdhvam utthito ḥsmīti bhāvitaḥ । ata eva utthitaś ca taiḥ taiḥ vikalpaiḥ utthānavikalpaiḥ । sābhidham abhidhāsahitam । tadbhāvam utthānabhāvam । vikalpayati vikalpena sampādayati । āttamīnaḥ । mīnaiḥ ātta āttamīnaḥ । pratibimbiteti spaṣṭam । vimalaṃ yat ullasanam । tena utpannaṃ yat dhvastaṃ dhvaṃsaḥ । tena lolaṃ śarīraṃ yasya । na cormaya iti । pūrvam ekavacanaṃ jātyapekṣayā jñeyam । teneha bahuvacanaprayogaḥ । teṣu guṇeṣu । svasvabhāvasthaḥ svasvarūpasthaḥ । yaḥ vikalpaḥ taraṅgatāsādanarūpaḥ vikalpaḥ । tena vikalīkṛtāḥ payasaḥ ucchinnāḥ kṛtāḥ । parasparam anyoḥnyam । yaḥ parāmarśaḥ nikaṭe avasthitiḥ । nānātām upayānti । ekaṃ rūpam yat ambusāmānyam । ata eva nirāmayāḥ nāśotpādākhyarogarahitāḥ ।।

dṛṣṭāntam uktvā dārṣṭāntikaṃ kathayati dvābhyām

tathaivāsmin pravitate site śuddhe nirāmaye ।
brahmamātraikavapuṣi brahmaṇi sphārarūpiṇi ।।

sarvaśaktāv anādyante pṛthagvad apṛthakkṛtāḥ ।
saṃsthitāḥ śaktayaś citrā vicitrācāracañcalāḥ ।।

sitapadasyārthaṃ svakaṇṭhena kathayati śuddhe iti । nirāmaye cetyākhyād āmayāt niṣkrānte । brahmamātram ekam kevalam । vapuḥ svarūpaṃ yasya । tādṛśe । sphāram sphuraṇaśīlam । vapur asyāstīti । apṛthakkṛtāḥ śaktayaḥ । tathaiva taraṅgavat । pṛthagvat saṃsthitāḥ bhavanti ।।

nānāśakti hi nānātvam eti svavapuṣi sthitam ।
bṛṃhitam brahmaṇi brahma payasīvormimaṇḍalam ।।

brahma śuddhaṃ cinmātratattvam । brahmaṇi svavapuṣi brahmākhye svasvarūpe । bṛṃhitam jagadrūpayā bṛṃhitatayā yuktaṃ sat । nānātvam nānābhāvam । eti gacchati । anyathā nānātvagamanaṃ yuktaṃ na syād iti bhāvaḥ । brahma kim iva bṛṃhitam । payasi ūrmimaṇḍalam iva ।।

nanu yadi paṭādirūpeṇa brahmaiva bṛṃhitam asti tarhi padārthānām pratyekaṃ niyataṃ rūpaṃ katham astīty । atrāha

nānārūpakarūpatvād vairūpyaśatakāriṇī ।
niyatir niyatākārā padārtham adhitiṣṭhati ।।

nānārūpakam yat rūpam । tadyuktatvāt vairūpyaśatakāriṇī padārthānām prati niyatarūpākhyavirūpatāśatakāriṇī । niyatiḥ niyatyākhyā śaktiḥ । padārtham adhitiṣṭhati svavaśaṃ karoti । brahmaṇaḥ utpannayā niyatiśaktyā eva padārthānām pratyekaṃ niyataṃ rūpam astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

sāmānyenoktvā stokaṃ viśeṣeṇa kathayati

jaḍā jāḍyam upādatte cittvam āyāti cinmayī ।
vāsanārūpiṇī śaktiḥ svasvarūpasthitātmanaḥ ।।

vāsanārūpiṇī vāsanārūpeṇa sthitā । svasvarūpasthitaḥ yaḥ ātmā । tasya । śaktiḥ niyatiśaktiḥ । jaḍā jāḍyavāsanārūpiṇī bhūtvā । jāḍyam upādatte gṛhṇāti । yena sthāvaraṃ rūpam prakaṭīkaroti । cinmayī cetanatvavāsanārūpiṇī bhūtvā । cittvam āyāti । yena jaṅgamaṃ rūpam prakaṭīkaroti ।।

phalitam āha

brahmaivānagha tenedaṃ sphārākāraṃ vijṛmbhate ।
nānārūpaiḥ parispandaiḥ paripūrṇa ivārṇavaḥ ।।

he anagha । idaṃ sphārākāram jagat । brahmaiva vijṛmbhate vilasati । paripūrṇaḥ arṇavaḥ iva । yathā saḥ nānārūpaiḥ parispandaiḥ taraṅgākhyaiḥ parispandaiḥ । tathety arthaḥ ।।

nānātāṃ svayam ādatte nānākāravihārataḥ ।
ātmaivātmany ātmanaiva samudrāmbha ivāmbhasi ।।

nānākārārtham nānākāragrahaṇārtham ।।

vyatiriktā na payaso vicitrā vīcayo yathā ।
vyatiriktā na sarveśāt samagrāḥ kalanās tathā ।।

sarveśāt sarvaniyāmakatvena sthitāt cinmātratattvāt । kalanāḥ jagadrūpāḥ kalanāḥ ।।

stambhapuṣpalatāpattraphalakorakayuktayaḥ ।
yathaikasmiṃ sthitā bīje tathā brahmaṇi śaktayaḥ ।।

śaktayaḥ jagadrūpāḥ śaktayaḥ ।।

nānākartṛtayā nānāśaktitā puruṣe yathā ।
tathaivātmani sarvajñe sarvadā sarvaśaktitā ।।

sarvaśaktitāyām hetum āha sarvajña iti । yadi hi sarvaśaktiḥ na syāt tarhi sarvajñaḥ na syāt । sarvajñatvam cātra sarvakartṛtāyāṃ viśrāntam । na hi yaḥ sarvaṃ na jānāti saḥ sarvaṃ karoti । kulālādau ghaṭādijñānasya niyatatvena darśanāt ।।

vicitravarṇatā yadvad dṛśyate kaṭhinātape ।
vicitraśaktitā tadvad deveśe sadasanmayī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vicitrarūpodetīyam avicitrāt sthitiḥ śivāt ।
ekavarṇāt payovāhāc chakracāpalatā yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ajaḍāj jaḍatodeti jāḍyabhāvanahetukā ।
ūrṇanābhād yathā tantur yathā puṃsaḥ suṣuptatā ।।

jāḍyasya jaḍatvasya । yat bhāvanam saṅkalpanam । tad eva hetuḥ yasyāḥ ।।

acittaś caitasīṃ śaktiṃ svabandhāyecchayā śivaḥ ।
tanoti tāntavaṃ kośaṃ kośakārakrimir yathā ।।

acittaḥ atyantaśuddhatvena cittarahitaḥ । tāntavaṃ tantusambandhi ।।

svecchayātmātmano brahman bhāvayitvā svakaṃ vapuḥ ।
saṃsārān mokṣam āyāti svālānād iva vāraṇaḥ ।।

ātmā ātmanaḥ । ātmasambandhinyā svecchayā । svakam nijam । vapuḥ cinmātrākhyaṃ svarūpam । bhāvayitvā svasvarūpatvena bhāvanāviṣayatāṃ nītvā । saṃsārāt deho ḥham iti bhāvanārūpāt saṃsārāt । mokṣam muktim । yathāsau svālānāt mokṣam āyāti । svecchāśabdo ḥtra icchāmātravācakaḥ ।।

yad eva bhāvayaty ātmā satatam bhāvitaḥ svayam ।
tayaivāpūryate śaktyā śīghram eva mahān api ।।

yad eva yām eva śaktim । satatam bhāvitaḥ sadā vāsitaḥ । mahān api vyāpako ḥpi san ।।

bhāvitā śaktir ātmānam ātmatāṃ nayati kṣaṇāt ।
anantam api kham prāvṛṇmihikā mahatī yathā ।।

bhāvitā bhāvanāviṣayīkṛtā । śaktirūpaḥ yaḥ ātmā । mihikāpakṣe ātmatām mihikātvam ।।

yā śaktir uditā śīghraṃ yāti tanmayatām ajaḥ ।
yām eva tu sthitiṃ yātas tanmayo bhavati drumaḥ ।।

ajaḥ janmarahitaḥ śuddhaṃ cinmātratattvam । sthitim ādhārarūpam bhūmim । drumasya ādhārabhūtabhūmyanurūpatvenārohaṇāt ।।

na mokṣo mokṣa īśasya na bandho bandha ātmanaḥ ।
bandhamokṣadṛśau loke na jāne protthite kutaḥ ।।

īśasyātmanaḥ । tarhi bandhamokṣau kasya bhavata ity । bandhamokṣayor utthānam eva paramārthato nāstīti kā tadādhāracinteti bhāvaḥ ।।

nāsya bandho na mokso ḥsti tanmayaś caiva lakṣyate ।
grastaṃ nityam asatyena māyāmayam aho jagat ।।

asyātmanaḥ । paramārthataḥ bandhaḥ nāsti । mokṣo ḥpi nāsti । kiṃ tu āmukhataḥ tanmayaḥ bandhamokṣamayaḥ । lakṣyate । nanu tarhi jagati bandhamokṣakalanā katham astīty । atrāha । jagacchabdenātra jagadgatāḥ pramātāraḥ lakṣyante । aho āścarye । jagat jagadgatāḥ pramātāraḥ । asatyena asatyabhūtena bandhamokṣākhyena kenāpi । grastam svakalanāviṣṭaṃ kṛtam । atra hetuṃ viśeṣaṇadvāreṇāha māyāmayam iti । māyāmayatvād evāsatyena grastatvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu katham ātmā bandhamokṣādikalanāgrasta iva sampanna ity । atrāha

yadaiva cittaṃ kalitam akalena kilātmanā ।
kośakīṭavad ātmāyam anenāvalitas tadā ।।

akalena akhaṇḍatvāt kalārahitena । anenātmanā yadaiva cittaṃ kalitam kalanayā prakaṭīkṛtam । tadānenātmanā kośakīṭavat kośakārakrimivat । bandhamokṣādikalanārūpeṇa kośenāvṛtaḥ ।।

nanv etenātmanā kalitam manaḥ kasmād upādānān nirgatam ity । atrāha

ananyarūpās tv anyatvavikalpitaśarīrakāḥ ।
manaḥśaktaya etasmād imā niryānti koṭiśaḥ ।।

ananyarūpāḥ abhinnāḥ । imāḥ pṛthaktvena vartamānāḥ ।।

tatsthās tajjāḥ pṛthagrūpāḥ samudrād iva vīcayaḥ ।
tatsthās tajjāḥ pṛthaksthāś ca candrād iva marīcayaḥ ।।

tatsthāḥ tasmin paramātmani sthitāḥ । tajjāḥ tasmāt paramātmanaḥ jātāḥ । etāḥ manaḥśaktayaḥ pṛthagrūpāḥ bhavanti । yathā vīcayaḥ samudrāt pṛthagrūpāḥ bhavanti । dvitīyaṃ dṛṣṭāntaṃ kathayati tatsthā iti ।।

asmin spandamaye sphāre paramātmamahāmbudhau ।
cijjale vitatābhoge cinmātrarasaśālini ।।

kāścit sthitā haribrahmarudracidvalanādhikāḥ ।
laharyaḥ prasphuranty etāḥ svabhāvodbhāvitātmikāḥ ।।

spandamaye ahaṃvimarśamaye । ahaṃvimarśasyaivātra spandatvāt । sphāre vistīrṇe । cit cetyonmukhā cit । sā eva jalam yasmin । cinmātram cetyānunmukhā cit । sā eva rasaḥ yasmin । rasaḥ jalasya sārabhūtaḥ āsvādākhyo guṇaḥ jñeyaḥ । etādṛśe paramātmamahāmbudhau । kāścit etāḥ laharyaḥ cillaharyaḥ । laharyaḥ kathambhūtāḥ sthitāḥ । haribrahmarudrarūpāḥ yāḥ cidvalanā citspandāḥ । tādṛśyaḥ sthitāḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtāḥ । svabhāvāt udbhāvitaḥ prakaṭībhāvaṃ gataḥ । kāścil laharyaḥ haribrahmarudrarūpatayā sphurantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

kāścid yamamahendrārkavahnivaiśravaṇādikāḥ ।
ghnanti kurvanti tiṣṭhanti laharyaś capalaiṣaṇāḥ ।।

capalāḥ eṣaṇāḥ icchāḥ ।।

kāścit kinnaragandharvavidyādharasurādikāḥ ।
utpatanti patanty ugrā laharyaḥ parivalgitāḥ ।।

parivalgitāḥ spanditāh ।।

kāścit kiñcitsthitākārā yathā kamalajādikāḥ ।
kāścid utpannavidhvastā yathā suranarādikāḥ ।।

kiñcit kālaṃ sthitaḥ ākāraḥ yāsām । tāḥ kiñcitsthitākārāḥ ।।

krimikīṭapataṅgādigonāsājagarādikāḥ ।
kāścit tasmin mahāmbhodhau sphuranty eteṣu binduvat ।।

eteṣv iti bahuvacanam pādapūraṇārtham । tenaitasmin mahāmbhodhāv iti yojyam ।।

kāścic calānanamṛgagṛdhravañjulakādayaḥ ।
sphuranti girikuñjeṣu velāvanataṭeṣv iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sudīrghajīvitāḥ kāścit kāścid atyalpajīvitāḥ ।
svatucchabhāvanāt tucchāt kāścit tucchaśarīrikāḥ ।।

kāścit tucchāt asatyāt । svatucchabhāvanāt svaviṣayāt tucchavikalpanāt । tucchaśarīrikāḥ bhavanti ।।

saṃsārasvapnasaṃrambhe kāścit sthairyeṇa bhāvitāḥ ।
svavikalpahatāḥ kāścic chaṅkante susthiraṃ jagat ।।

sthairyeṇa sthiratayā । bhāvitāḥ sthiro ḥyaṃ saṃsāra iti vāsanāyuktāḥ kṛtāḥ ।।

alpālpabhāvanāḥ kāścid dainyadoṣavaśīkṛtāḥ ।
kṛśo ḥtiduḥkhī mūḍho ḥham iti duḥkhair dṛḍhīkṛtāḥ ।।

atra bhāvanāyāḥ alpālpatvam atimauḍhyena jñeyam ।।

kāścit sthāvaratāṃ yātāḥ kāścid devatvam āgatāḥ ।
kāścit puruṣatām prāptāḥ kāścid dānavatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokena pūrvoktam evārthaṃ saṅkṣipya kathayati

kāścit sthitā jagati kalpaśatāny analpāḥ kāścid vrajanti paramam puruṣaṃ suśuddhāḥ ।
brahmārṇavāt samuditā laharīvilolāś citsaṃvido hi mananāparanāmavatyaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyām ekādaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

surāsuranarākārā imā yāḥ saṃvido mune ।
brahmārṇavād abhinnās te satyam etan mṛṣetarat ।।

etat । surāsuranarākārā yāḥ saṃvidaḥ । brahmārṇavād abhinnatvam । surāsuranarāṇām prādhānyāt grahaṇam ।।

surāsuranarākārāḥ saṃvidaḥ viśinaṣṭi

mithyābhāvanayā brahman svavikalpakalaṅkitāḥ ।
na brahma vayam ity antarniścayena hy adhogatāḥ ।।

kalaṅkitatve uttarārdhena hetuṃ kathayati na brahmeti । hiśabdaḥ yasmādarthe ।।

brahmaṇo vyatiriktatvam brahmārṇavagatā api ।
bhāvayantyo vimuhyanti bhīmāsu bhavabhūmiṣu ।।

bhīmāsu duḥkhadāyitvenātyantabhayānakāsu ।।

yā etāḥ saṃvido brāhmyo mune naikakalaṅkitāḥ ।
etat tat karmaṇām bījam atha karmaiva viddhi vā ।।

etāḥ surāsuranarākāratvena pūrvam uktāḥ । saṃvidaḥ parāmarśāḥ । brāhmyaḥ brahmasambandhinyaḥ । naikakalaṅkitāḥ na ekena prakāreṇa kalaṅkitāḥ । bahuprakāreṇa kalaṅkitā ity arthaḥ । tat etat tā etāḥ brāhmīḥ saṃvidaḥ । karmaṇām bījam kāraṇam । atha vā karmaiva viddhi । karmatveneṣṭasya bāhyakarmaṇaḥ etadanu praṇītatvāt । na hi saṃvitparāmarśam antareṇa bāhyakarmaṇaḥ utthānaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yuktaṃ vā ।।

etāsām eva samastajagannimittatvaṃ kathayati

saṅkalparūpayaivāntar mune kalanayaitayā ।
karmajālakarañjānām bījamuṣṭyā karālayā ।।

imā jagati vistīrṇe śarīropalapaṅktayaḥ ।
tiṣṭhanti parivalganti rudanti ca hasanti ca ।।

ābrahmastambhaparyantaṃ spandanaiḥ pavano yathā ।
ullasanti niyacchanti mlāyanti vihasanti ca ।।

he mune । saṅkalparūpayā saṅkalpasvarūpayā । karmajālakarañjānām bījamuṣṭyā karmajālakāraṇabhūtayeti yāvat । ata eva vikarālayā bhayānakayā । etayā kalanayā saṃvidrūpayā kalanayā । vistīrṇe jagati ābrahmastambhaparyantaṃ śarīropalapaṅktayaḥ śarīrapāṣāṇapaṅktayaḥ । tiṣṭhanti parivalganti rudanti ca hasanti ullasanti niyacchanti mlāyanti vihasanti ca upalakṣaṇaṃ caitat । sarvāḥ kriyāḥ kurvantīty arthaḥ । mṛtaśarīreṣu pūrvoktakriyāṇām adarśanāt । yathā pavanaḥ svāntaḥsthaiḥ spandanaiḥ nānāvidhāḥ kriyāḥ karoti ।।

tā etāḥ kāścid atyacchā yathā hariharādayaḥ ।
kāścid alpavimohasthā yathoraganarāmarā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kāścid atyantamohasthā yathā tarutṛṇādayaḥ ।
kāścid ajñānasammūḍhāḥ krimikīṭatvam āgatāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kāścit tṛṇavad uhyante dūre brahmamahodadheḥ ।
aprāptabhūmikā etā yathoraganarādayaḥ ।।

aprāptabhūmikāḥ aprāptapārāḥ ।।

taṭamātraṃ samālokya kāścit khedam upāgatāḥ ।
jātājātā nikhanyante kṛtāntajaradākhunā ।।

taṭamātraṃ samālokya na tv āsādya । tadāsādane hi punaḥ punaḥ kṛtāntanikhananaṃ na yuktaṃ syāt । taṭaś cātra cinmātraviśrāntirūpo jñeyaḥ ।।

kāścid antaram āsādya brahmatattvamahāmbudheḥ ।
gatās tattām aśokāya haribrahmaharādikāḥ ।।

tattām brahmatām । aśokāya śokābhāvāya ।।

alpamohānvitāḥ kāścit tam eva brahmavāridhim ।
adṛṣṭarāgarogaugham avalambya vyavasthitāḥ ।।

avalambya svātmatvenāśritya । kāścit jīvanmuktarūpā ity arthaḥ ।।

kāścid bhoktavyajanmaughā bhuktajanmaughakoṭayaḥ ।
vandhyāḥ prakāśatāmasyaḥ saṃsthitā bhūtajātayaḥ ।।

prakāśatāmasyaḥ prakṛṣṭatamaso gūṇayuktaḥ । ata eva vandhyā samyagjñānākhyaphalarahitāḥ ।।

kāścid ūrdhvād adho yānti tathādhastān mahat padam ।
ūrdhvād ūrdhvataraṃ kāścid adhastāt kāścid apy adhaḥ ।।

adhaḥ paśuyoniṃ narakaṃ vā । mahat padam mānuṣyaṃ svargaṃ vā ।।

sargāntaślokena siddhāntaṃ kathayati

bahusukhaduḥkhakasaṅkaṭā kriyeyam paramapadāsmaraṇāt samāgateha ।
paramapadāvagamāt prayāti nāśaṃ vihagapatismaraṇād viṣavyatheva ।।

vihagapateḥ gāruḍikamantradevatārūpasya garuḍasyeti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe dvādaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ । śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ śrīrāmam praty āha

vicārayantas tattvajñā iti te jāgatīr gatīḥ ।
samaṅgāyās taṭāt tasmāt praceluś cañcalāṃśavaḥ ।।

jāgatīḥ jagatsambandhinīḥ ।।

kramād ākāśam ākramya nirgatyāmbudakoṭaraiḥ ।
samprāpuḥ siddhamārgeṇa mandaraṃ hemakandaram ।।

koṭarair iti । koṭarebhyaḥ ity asyārthe ।।

adhityakāyāṃ tasyādrer ārdraparṇāvaguṇṭhitām ।
dadarśa bhārgavaḥ śuṣkām pūrvajanmodbhavāṃ tanum ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

uvāca cedaṃ he tāta tanvī tanur iyaṃ hi sā ।
yā tvayā sukhasambhogaiḥ purā samabhilālitā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

iyaṃ sā mattanur yasyā mandārakusumotkaraiḥ ।
racitāḥ śītalāḥ śayyā merūpavanabhūmiṣu ।।

sā iti ।।

iyaṃ sā mattanur mattadevastrīgaṇalālitā ।
sarīsṛpamukhakṣuṇṇā paśya śete dharātale ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nandanodyānaṣaṇḍeṣu mama tanvā yayānayā ।
ciraṃ vilasitaṃ seyaṃ śuṣkakaṅkālatāṃ gatā ।।

vilasitam iti bhāve ktaḥ ।।

surāṅganāṅgasaṃsaṅgād uttuṅgānaṅgaraṅgayā ।
cetovṛttyā rahitayā tanveha mama śuṣyate ।।

śuṣyate bhāve lakāraḥ ।।

teṣu teṣu vilāseṣu tāsu tāsu daśāsu ca ।
tathā tā bhāvanā baddhvā kathaṃ svastho ḥsi dehaka ।।

tāḥ bhāvanāḥ surastrīviṣayāḥ । svastho ḥsi cañcalatārahitatvāt । anukampito dehaḥ dehakaḥ । tasyāmantraṇaṃ dehaketi ।।

hā tano kvāvabhagnāsi tāpasaṃśoṣam āgatā ।
karaṅkatām prayātāsi mām bhāvayasi durbhage ।।

karaṅkatām kaṅkalatām । tvam mām bhāvayasi kiṃ smarasi । atisnehākulatvād iyam uktiḥ ।।

dehenāhaṃ vilāseṣu yenaiva mudito ḥbhavam ।
kaṅkalatām upagatāt tasmād eva bibhemy aham ।।

yena dehenāhaṃ vilāseṣu muditaḥ abhavam । kaṅkalatām upagatāt tasmād eva dehāt । aham bibhemi ।।

tārājālasamākāro yatra hāro ḥbhavat purā ।
mamorasi nilīyante paśya tatra pipīlakāḥ ।।

nilīyante laganti ।।

dravatkāñcanakāntena lobhaṃ nītā varāṅganāḥ ।
yena madvapuṣā tena paśya kaṅkalatohyate ।।

uhyate dhāryate ।।

paśya me vitatāsyena tāpasaṃśuṣkakṛttinā ।
matkaṅkālakuvaktreṇa vitrāsyante vane mṛgāḥ ।।

vitrāsyante vikārayuktatvena trāsayuktāḥ kriyante ।।

paśyātisaṃśuṣkatayā śavodaradarī mama ।
prakāśārkāṃśujālena vivekeneva śobhate ।।

śavodaram mṛtaśarīrodaram eva darī ।।

mattanuḥ pariśuṣkeyaṃ sthitottānā vanāvanau ।
vairāgyaṃ nayatīvātmatucchatvenāmbarasthitān ।।

ambarasthitān devān ।।

śabdarūparasasparśagandhalobhavimuktayā ।
nirvikalpasamādhyeva mama tanvoṣyate girau ।।

mama tanvā kathambhūtayā । nirvikalpe vikalpaniṣkrānte cinmātre । samādhiḥ yasyāḥ ।।

saṃśānte cittavetāle yām ānandakalāṃ tanuḥ ।
yāti tām api rājyena jāgatena na gacchati ।।

jāgatena jagatsambandhinā ।।

paśya viśrāntasarvehaṃ vigatāśeṣakautukam ।
nirastakalpanājālaṃ sukhaṃ śete kalevaram ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

cittamarkaṭasaṃrambhasaṅkṣubdhaḥ kāyapādapaḥ ।
tathā vegena calati yathā mūlāni kṛntati ।।

mūlakṛntanam vyāvahārikakṣobharūpaṃ jñeyam ।।

cittānarthavimukto ḥsau gajābhraharivibhramam ।
nāyam paśyati me dehaḥ parānanda iva sthitaḥ ।।

gajābhraharīṇām gajameghasiṃhānām । cāñcalyam iti yāvat । na paśyati nānubhavati ।।

sarvāśājvarasammohamihikāśaradāgamam ।
acittatvaṃ vinā nānyac chreyaḥ paśyāmi jantuṣu ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ta eva sukhasambhogasīmāntaṃ samupāgatāḥ ।
mahādhiyaḥ śāntadhiyo ye yātā vimanaskatām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sarvaduḥkhadaśāmuktāṃ saṃśāntāṃ vigatajvarām ।
diṣṭyā paśyāmy amananāṃ vane tanum imām aham ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atra śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

bhagavan sarvadharmajña bhārgaveṇa tadā kila ।
subahūny upabhuktāni śarīrāṇi punaḥ punaḥ ।।

bhṛguṇotpādite kāye tat tasmiṃs tasya kim mune ।
mahān atiśayo jātaḥ paridevanam eva vā ।।

atiśayaḥ atiśayajñānam ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaraṃ kathayati

śukrasya kalanā rāma yāsau jīvadaśāṃ gatā ।
karmātmikā samutpannā bhṛgor bhārgavarūpiṇī ।।

kalanā śukrajīvaprādurbhāvakārī samvidākhyaḥ spandaḥ । śukrasya jīvadaśām śukrasambandhijīvāvasthām । bhṛgor iti pañcamī ।।

sā hīdamprathamatvena sametya paramāt padāt ।
bhūtākāśapadam prāpya vātavyāvalitā satī ।।

prāṇāpānapravāheṇa praviśya hṛdayam bhṛgoḥ ।
krameṇa vīryatām etya sampannauśanasī tanuḥ ।।

idamprathamatvena tatpūrvatvena । sametya samyak utthāya । auśanasī tanuḥ śukraśarīrarūpā ।।

vihitabrāhmasaṃskārā tataḥ sā pitur agragā ।
kālena mahatā prāptā śuṣkakaṅkālarūpatām ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

idamprathamam āyātā yadā sā brahmaṇas tanuḥ ।
atas tām prati śukreṇa tadā tat paridevitam ।।

idamprathamam tatpūrvam । tat paridevitam tādṛśam paridevanaṃ kṛtam ।।

vītarāgo ḥpy aniccho ḥpi samaṅgāviprarūpavān ।
svāṃ śuśoca tanuṃ śukraḥ svabhāvo hy eṣa dehajaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kiṃ tu pradarśitaṃ tena śokavyājena dhīmatām ।
vairāgyapratipattyai tat pṛthaktvaṃ dehadehinoḥ ।।

kiṃ tv iti pakṣāntare । tathā ca paropakārārtham eva śukreṇa paridevanaṃ kṛtam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

jñasyājñasya ca dehasya yāvajjīvam ayaṃ kramaḥ ।
lokavad vyavahāro yat saktyāsaktyātha vā sadā ।।

atha vā pakṣāntare । dehasya vyavahāraḥ iti sambandhaḥ । yad vā lakṣaṇayā । dehasya dehina ity arthaḥ । tathā ca jñasya dehasyājñasya vā dehasyety arthaḥ । jñasyāsaktyā ajñasya saktyeti kramo jñeyaḥ ।।

ye parijñātagatayo ye cājñāḥ paśudharmiṇaḥ ।
lokasaṃvyavahāreṣu te sthitā vanajālavat ।।

vanajālam sthitatvamātre upamānaṃ jñeyam ।।

vyavahārī yathaivājñas tathaiva kila paṇḍitaḥ ।
vāsanāmātrabhedo ḥtra kāraṇam bandhamokṣayoḥ ।।

vāsanāmātrabhedaḥ śuddhatvāśuddhatvena jñeyaḥ ।।

yāvac charīraṃ tāvad dhi duḥkhe duḥkhaṃ sukhe sukham ।
asaṃsaktadhiyo dhīrā darśayanty aprabuddhavat ।।

darśayanti anyān prati darśayanti । na tu svayam paśyanti ।।

sukheṣu sukhitā nityaṃ duḥkhitā duḥkhavṛttiṣu ।
mahātmāno hi dṛśyante nūnam antas tu śītalāḥ ।।

śītalāḥ sukhaduḥkhakṛtakṣobharahitāḥ ।।

stambhasya pratibimbāni kṣubhyanti na vapuḥ sthiram ।
jñasya karmendriyāṇy eva kṣubhyanti na manaḥ sthiram ।।

sthiraṃ vapuḥ dṛḍhaṃ stambhākhyaṃ svarūpam । kṣubhyantīty antargataṇic । kau prayogau । te na kṣobhayantīty arthaḥ । karmendriyāṇy upalabdhyākhyakarmakārīṇi jñānendriyāṇīty arthaḥ ।।

calācalatayā tajjño lokavṛttiṣu tiṣṭhati ।
adhaḥsthitir iva svaccham pratibimbeṣu bhāskaraḥ ।।

calācalatayā atyantacāñcalyena । bhāskaraḥ kathambhūtaḥ । adhaḥ adhodeśe । sthitiḥ avasthānaṃ yasya । saḥ ।।

santyaktalokakarmāpi baddha evāprabuddhadhīḥ ।
atyaktamohalīlo ḥpi mukta eva prabuddhadhīḥ ।।

prabuddhadhītvāprabuddhadhītvayor evātra bandhamokṣau prati kāraṇatvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

muktabuddhīndriyo mukto baddhakarmendriyo ḥpi hi ।
baddhabuddhīndriyo baddho muktakarmendriyo ḥpi hi ।।

hiśabdaḥ prasiddhau ।।

sukhaduḥkhadṛśor loke bandhamokṣadṛśos tathā ।
hetur buddhīndriyāṇy eva tejāṃsīva prakāśane ।।

prakāśane arthaprakaṭatākaraṇe ।।

bahir lokocitācāras tv antar ācāravarjitaḥ ।
samo ḥsann iva tiṣṭha tvaṃ saṃśāntasakalaiṣaṇaḥ ।।

antaḥ manasi ।।

sarvaiṣaṇāvimuktena svātmanātmani tiṣṭhatā ।
kuru karmāṇi kāryāṇi nūnaṃ sāmanasi sthitiḥ ।।

he rāma । sarvaiṣaṇāvimuktena । ata eva ātmani na tu anātmarūpeṣu viṣayeṣu । tiṣṭhatā ātmanā manasā । karmāṇi kuru । sā amanasi sthitiḥ manasi sthitiḥ na bhavati ।।

ādhivyādhimahāvarte garte saṃsāravartmani ।
mamatogrāndhakūpe ḥsmin mā patātapadāyini ।।

mamatogrāndhakūpe kathambhūte । saṃsāravartmani saṃsārarūpe mārge । garte gartatayā sthite ।।

na tvam bhāveṣu no bhāvās tvayi tāmarasekṣaṇa ।
śuddhabuddhasvabhāvas tvam ātmasaṃsthaḥ sthiro bhava ।।

tvam sākṣibhūtaśuddhacinmātrarūpaḥ tvam । ātmasaṃsthaḥ śuddhabuddhasvabhāvasvātmaparaḥ । na tu dehādiparaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokenottaraṃ samāpayati

vyapagatamamatāmahāndhakāram padam amalaṃ vigataiṣaṇaṃ sametya ।
prabhavasi yadi cetaso mahātmaṃs tad atidhiye mahate sate namas te ।।

vyapagatam mamatārūpam mahāndhakāram yasya । ata evāmalam vigataiṣaṇam tṛptatayā samastākāṅkṣārahitam । padam cinmātrākhyam padam । sametya svātmatvena vibhāvya । yadi cetasaḥ prabhavasi cetaḥ jetuṃ samartho bhavasi । tat tadā । atidhiye utkṛṣṭabuddhaye । mahate mahattvayuktāya । sate sanmātrasvarūpāya ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe pañcadaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

athākṣipya vacas tasya tanayasya tadā bhṛgoḥ ।
uvāca bhagavān kālo vaco gambhīraniḥsvanam ।।

ākṣipya ākṣepaviṣayaṃ kṛtvā । bhṛgoḥ tanayasya śukrasya ।।

kālaḥ kathayati

samaṅgātāpasīm etāṃ tanuṃ santyaja bhārgava ।
praviśemāṃ tanuṃ sādho nagarīm iva pārthivaḥ ।।

samaṅgātāpasīm samaṅgātāpasasambandhinīm ।।

kāle pūrvajayā tanvā tapaḥ kṛtvānayā punaḥ ।
gurutvam asurendrāṇāṃ kartavyam bhavatānagha ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mahākalpānta āyāte bhavatā bhārgavī tanuḥ ।
apunargrahaṇāyaiṣā tyājyā pramlānapuṣpavat ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jīvanmuktapadam prāptas tanvā prāktanarūpayā ।
mahāsurendragurutāṃ kurvaṃs tiṣṭha mahāmate ।।

prāktanarūpayā śukrākhyayā ।।

kalyāṇam astu vāṃ yāmo vayaṃ tv abhimatāṃ diśam ।
na kiñcid api tac cittaṃ yasya nābhimatam bhavet ।।

nanu kathaṃ tavāpy abhimatam astīty । atrāha na kiñcid iti । tat kiñcid api na bhavati । yasya cittasyābhimatam nāsti । ato mamāpi sacittatvād abhimatam astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

ity uktvā muñcatoḥ puṣpaṃ tayoḥ so ḥntaradhīyata ।
taptāṃśur iva rodasyoḥ samam aṃśubhir aṃśumān ।।

taptāṃśuḥ sūryaḥ । rodasyoḥ dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ ।।

gate tasmin bhagavati tām uktvā bhavitavyatām ।
vicārya bhārgavo ḥbhedyāṃ niyatāṃ niyater gatim ।।

kālakāraṇasaṃśuṣkām bhāvipuṣpaśubhodayām ।
viveśa tāṃ tanum bālāṃ sulatām iva mādhavaḥ ।।

abhedyām bhettum aśakyām । kālākhyaṃ yat kāraṇam । tena śuṣkām । lakṣaṇayā vāsantikaḥ rasaḥ । bhāvī puṣpavat śubhaḥ udayaḥ yasyāḥ ।।

sā brāhmaṇatanur bhūmau vivarṇavad anaṅgikā ।
papāta kampitā tūrṇam chinnamūlā latā yathā ।।

brāhmaṇatanuḥ samaṅgātāpasatanuḥ ।।

tasyām praviṣṭajīvāyām putratanvām mahāmuniḥ ।
cakārāpyāyanam mantraiḥ sakamaṇḍaluvāribhiḥ ।।

āpyāyanam pūraṇam ।।

sarvanāḍyaḥ tatas tanvyās tasyāḥ pūrṇā virejire ।
saritaḥ prāvṛṣīvāmbupūrapūritakoṭarāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nalinī prāvṛṣīvāsau madhāv iva navā latā ।
yadā pūrṇā tadā tasyāḥ prāṇāḥ pallavitā babhuḥ ।।

asau bhārgavatanuḥ । pallavitāḥ apānādirūpeṇocchūnāḥ ।।

atha śukraḥ samuttasthau vahatprāṇasamīraṇaḥ ।
rasamārutasaṃyogād āmūlam iva vāridaḥ ।।

āmūlam mūlād ārabhya ।।

puro ḥbhivādayām āsa pitaram pāvanākṛtiḥ ।
prathamollāsito meghaḥ staniteneva parvatam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pitātha prāktanīṃ tasyāpy āliliṅga tanuṃ tataḥ ।
snehārdravṛttir jaladaś cirād giritaṭīm iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bhṛgur dadarśa sasneham prāktanīṃ tānayīṃ tanum ।
matto jāto ḥyam ity āsthā haraty api mahāmatim ।।

tānayīm tanayasambandhinīm । nanu tādṛgjñānayuktena tena kathaṃ tānayī tanuḥ sasnehaṃ dṛṣṭety । atrāha matta iti ।।

matputro ḥyam iti sneho bhṛgum apy aharat tadā ।
paratātmīyatā ceyaṃ yāvadākṛti bhāvinī ।।

paratā parabhāvaḥ । ātmīyatā ātmīyabhāvaḥ । yāvadākṛti yāvaccharīram । bhāvinī aparihāryā ।।

babhūvatuḥ pitāputrau tāv athānyoḥnyaśobhitau ।
niśāvasānamuditāv arkapadmākarāv iva ।।

niśāvasāne prabhāte ।।

atraivānyadṛṣṭāntadvayaṃ kathayati

cirasaṅgamasambaddhāv iva cakrāhvadampatī ।
ghanāgamaghanasnehau mayūrajaladāv iva ।।

cirakāladṛḍhotkaṇṭhayogyayā kathayā tayā ।
sthitvā tatra muhūrtaṃ tāv athotthāya mahāmatī ।।

samaṅgādvijadehaṃ tam bhasmasāt tatra cakratuḥ ।
ko hi nāma jagajjāta ācāraṃ nānutiṣṭhati ।।

ācāram lokācāram ।।

evaṃ tau kānane tasmin pāvane bhṛgubhārgavau ।
saṃsthitau tapasā dīptau divīva śaśibhāskarau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ceratur jñātavijñeyau jīvanmuktau jagadgurū ।
deśakāladaśaugheṣu suśamaṃ susthiraṃ tapaḥ ।।

tapaḥ kathambhūtam । śobhanaḥ śamaḥ yasmin । tat ।।

athāsuragurutvaṃ sa śukraḥ kālena labdhavān ।
bhṛgur apy ātmano yogye pade ḥtiṣṭhad anāmaye ।।

ātmanaḥ yogye pade videhamuktyākhye pade ।।

sargāntaślokena śukravṛttāntaṃ saṅkṣipya kathayati śukro ḥsāv iti ।

śukro ḥsau prathamam iti krameṇa jāta etasmāt paramapadād udārakīrtiḥ ।
svenāśu smṛtipadavibhrameṇa paścād evaṃ ca pravilulito daśāntareṣu ।।etasmāt sarveṣām ātmatvena puro vartamānāt । paramapadāt cinmātrākhyāt uttamāt sthānāt । daśāntareṣu samaṅgātāpasatvaparyanteṣv avasthāviśeṣeṣu ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe ṣoḍaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ । śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

bhagavan bhṛguputrasya pratibhā sānubhūtitaḥ ।
yathāsya saphalā jātā tathānyasya na kim bhavet ।।

he bhagavan । asya samanantaroktena vṛttāntena varṇitasya । bhṛguputrasya । sā pratibhā tat nānāyonigamanarūpam pratibhānam । anubhūtitaḥ anubhavāt hetoḥ । saphalā arthakriyākhyaphalayuktā । jātā । anyathā hi bhṛgusambandhī svasambandhī vā samaṅgātāpasaviṣayo ḥnubhavaḥ na yuktaḥ syāt iti bhāvaḥ । tathā tadvat । anyasya śukravyatiriktasya puruṣasya । sā pratibhā saphalā kim katham । na hi svapne pratibhātaṃ svasmin gajāditvam pratyakṣam anubhūyate ।।

śrīvasiṣṭho ḥtrottaraṃ kathayati

idamprathamam utpannā sā tadā brahmaṇaḥ padāt ।
śuddhā matir bhārgavasya nānyajanmakalaṅkitā ।।

idamprathamam tatpūrvam । yataḥ bhārgavasya śukrasya । brahmaṇaḥ padāt sadyaḥ utthitatvāt । sā nānāyonipratibhānaviṣayā । buddhiḥ । śuddhā pūrvajanmavāsanānicayākaluṣitā । āsīt । tataḥ tasya sā nānāyonigamanarūpā pratibhā saphalā jātā । anye tu pūrvatamam utpannatvāt madhye nānājanmāntarotthavāsanājālakalaṅkitāḥ santaḥ na svapratibhānam pratyakṣam anubhavantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanv asyāḥ śuddhāyāḥ mateḥ svarūpaṃ kīdṛg astīty । atrāha sarvaiṣaṇānām iti ।

sarvaiṣaṇānāṃ saṃśāntau śuddhā cittasya yā sthitiḥ ।
tat sattvam ucyate saiṣā vimalā cid udāhṛtā ।।sarvaiṣaṇānām nānābhogyajālaviṣayāṇāṃ samastānām icchānām । śāntau suṣuptyādiprabhāvena samyagjñānādinā vā śamane sati । cittasya manasaḥ । yā sthitiḥ yat avasthānam । asti । paṇḍitaiḥ tat sattvam ucyate । sā eva vimalā cit vimalā matiḥ । kiṃ ca iyam eva śuddhā matiḥ idamprathamam utpannasya ca bhavati jīvanmuktasya ca bhavati । idamprathamam utpannasya bāhyonmukhā । jīvanmuktasya tu tyajyamānabāhyeti viśeṣaḥ ।।

viśeṣaṇenoktvā sāmānyena kathayati

mano nirmalasattvātma yad bhāvayati yādṛśam ।
tat tathāśu bhavaty eva yathāvarto ḥrṇave ḥmbhasaḥ ।।

nirmalasattvātma pūrvaślokoktanirmalasattvasvarūpam । yat yādṛśam yena prakāreṇa yuktam । bhāvayati anusandhānaviṣayatāṃ nayati । āśu tathā tena prakāreṇa yuktam । āvartaḥ iva । yathā arṇave sthitaḥ ambhasaḥ āvartaḥ sadyaḥ anyaprakārayukto bhavati । tathety arthaḥ ।।

anena vṛttāntena siddhaṃ svamanīṣitaṃ kathayati

yathā bhṛgusutasyaiṣa vibhramaḥ proditaḥ svayam ।
pratyekam apy evam eva dṛṣṭānto ḥtra bhṛgoḥ sutaḥ ।।yathā bhṛgusutasya eṣaḥ samanantaroktaḥ । vibhramaḥ nānāyonipratibhāsarūpo vibhramaḥ । svayam svabhāvena । proditaḥ prādurbhūtaḥ । evam eva tathaiva । pratyekam pratipuruṣam । udeti । sarve eva svamanaḥpratibhāsarūpam eva jagat paśyantīti bhāvaḥ । asyārthasya dṛḍhīkaraṇārtham punar api śukrasya dṛṣṭāntatvaṃ kathayati dṛṣṭānto ḥtreti ।।

etad eva nānādṛṣṭāntaiḥ sugamaṃ karoti

bījasyāṅkurapattrādi svaṃ camatkurute yathā ।
sarveṣām bhūtasaṅghānām bhramaṣaṇḍas tathaiva hi ।।

yathā bījasya svam na tv anyabījasādhāraṇam । camatkurute ucchūnatārūpam ānandaṃ karoti । sarveṣām bhūtasaṅghānām bhūtasamūhānām । svaḥ ananyasādhāraṇaḥ bhramaṣaṇḍaḥ jagadrūpaḥ bhramaṣaṇḍaḥ । tathaiva camatkurute nānāsvādasaukhyaṃ karoti । sādhāraṇatvena bhāsamāno ḥpy ayaṃ saṃsāraḥ pratyekam bhinna eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

yad idaṃ dṛśyate viśvam evam evākhilaṃ hi tat ।
pratyekam uditam mithyā mithyaivāstam upaiti ca ।।

asmābhiḥ yad idaṃ viśvam saṃsāraḥ । dṛśyate anubhūyate । hi niścaye । evam evānena prakāreṇa । sthitam eva tat । mithyā pratyekam uditam udeti । mithyā evāstam upaiti ca paracitsvarūpatvena sarvadaiva tathaiva sthitatvāt । satyabhūtodayāstamayaviṣayatvāyogād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nāstam eti na codeti jagat kiñcana kasyacit ।
bhrāntimātram idam māyā mudhaiva parijṛmbhate ।।

idam jagat ।।

yathāsmatpratibhāsasthaḥ so ḥyaṃ saṃsāraṣaṇḍakaḥ ।
tathā teṣāṃ sahasrāṇi mitho ḥdṛṣṭāni santi hi ।।

yathā asmatpratibhāsasthaḥ saḥ ayam sarvendriyātītacinmātrarūpatvenendriyātīto ḥpi san idantayā sphuritaḥ saṃsāraṣaṇḍaḥ asti । tathā teṣām saṃsāraṣaṇḍānām । sahasrāṇi santi । nanu kathaṃ tāni na dṛśyante ity apekṣāyāṃ viśeṣaṇam āha mitho ḥdṛṣṭānīti । mithaḥ anyoḥnyam । adṛṣṭāni darśanaviṣayatāṃ na nītāni ।।

mithoḥdarśanadṛṣṭāntaṃ kathayati

svapnasaṅkalpanagaravyavahārāḥ parasparam ।
pṛthag yathā na dṛśyante tathaite saṃsṛtibhramāḥ ।।

yathā anyasya svapnādi anyo nānubhavati tathānyasya saṃsāram anyo nānubhavatīti piṇḍārthaḥ । nanu kathaṃ sargānām pratipuruṣam bhedaḥ iti cet । na । ekasminn eva vastuni puruṣabhedena heyatvopādeyatvadarśanāt ।।

upasaṃhāraṃ karoti

evaṃ nagaravṛndāni nabhaḥsaṅkalparūpiṇām ।
santi tāni na dṛśyante mitho jñānadṛśaṃ vinā ।।

evaṃ sati । nabhasi yaḥ saṅkalpaḥ purādisaṅkalpaḥ । tadvat rūpaṃ yeṣām । tādṛśānāṃ nagarāṇāṃ vṛndāni samūhāḥ । santi । samāse upasarjanībhūtasya nagarapadasya viśeṣaṇadānam ārṣam । taiḥ nagaravṛndaiḥ tāni nagaravṛndāni । jñānadṛśaṃ vinā cinmātrajñānākhyāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ vinā । mithaḥ anyoḥnyam । na dṛśyante nānubhūyante । jñānadṛśā tu dṛśyante eva । ata evāhaṃ tān paśyāmi tvaṃ na paśyasīti bhāvaḥ ।।

sarvaprasiddhānām piśācādīnām apy etadrūpatvaṃ kathayati

piśācayakṣarakṣāṃsi santy evaṃrūpakāṇi hi ।
saṅkalpamātradehāni sukhaduḥkhamayāni ca ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

svasminn apy etadrūpatvam evātidiśati

evam eva vayaṃ ceme sampannā raghunandana ।
svasaṅkalpātmakākārā mithyāsatyatvabhāvitāḥ ।।

mithyāsatyatve svasatyatāyām । bhāvitāḥ bhāvanāyuktāḥ ।।

evaṃ stokaṃ viśeṣeṇoktvā punar api sāmānyena kathayati

evaṃrūpaiva hi pare vartate sargasaṃsṛtiḥ ।
na vāstavī vastutas tu saṃsthiteyam avastuni ।।

evaṃrūpā pratibhāsarūpā । pare uttīrṇe cinmātre । sargeti nāmadheyā saṃsṛtiḥ sargasaṃsṛtiḥ । na vāstavī asatyarūpā । tu pakṣāntare । vastutaḥ paramārthataḥ । iyaṃ sargasaṃsṛtiḥ । vastutvena sthite cinmātre avastubhūtasargādhāratvāyogāt ।।

pūrvoktanyāyena siddhasya svābhīṣṭasyopasaṃhāraṃ karoti

pratyekam uditaṃ viśvam evam eva mudhaiva hi ।
navagulmakarūpeṇa vāsantikaraso yathā ।।

evam pūrvoktaprakāreṇa । vāsantikarasaḥ vasantasambandhī rasaḥ ।।

prathamo ḥyaṃ svasaṅkalpaḥ suprathām āgatas tathā ।
yathātipāramārthyena dṛḍhenetthaṃ vibhāvyate ।।

ayam prathamaḥ brahmaṇaḥ tatpūrvatvenotthitaḥ । tathā tena prakāreṇa । suprathām atirūḍhim । yathā ittham anena prakāreṇa । atipāramārthyenātiparamārthabhāvena । vibhāvyate niścīyate ।।

pratyekam uditaṃ cittaṃ svasvabhāvodarasthitam ।
idam itthaṃsamārambhaṃ jagat paśyad vinaśyati ।।

svaḥ ātmīyaḥ । svabhāvaḥ cinmātrākhyaṃ svarūpam । tasyodare udara ivodare । na tu sākṣād udare । sthitam vartamānam । pratyekam ekasmin ekasmin pratyekam । uditam utpannam । itthaṃsamārambham dṛśyamānārambhayuktam । idaṃ jagat paśyat anubhavat । vinaśyati svarūpaparāmarśāt bhraśyatīty arthaḥ ।।

pratibhāsavaśād asti nāsti vastvavalokanāt ।
dīrghaḥ svapno jagajjālam ālānaṃ cittadantinaḥ ।।

pratibhāsavaśāt । na hi asataḥ pratibhāsaḥ yukta iti bhāvaḥ । vastvavalokanāt paramārthāvalokanāt । na hi samyagjñānena jagat tiṣṭhati । jagajjālam kaḥ ।।

cittasattaiva hi jagaj jagatsattaiva cittakam ।
ekābhāve dvayor nāśas tac ca satyavicāraṇāt ।।

tat ekābhāvaḥ । satyavicāraṇāt satyavicārāt ।।

śrīrāmakṛtasya praśnasyottaram anusmarati

śuddhasya pratibhāso hi satyo bhavati cetasaḥ ।
niṣkalaṅke hi lagati paṭe kuṅkumarañjanā ।।

atra dṛṣṭāntam āha niṣkalaṅka iti । niṣkalaṅke malarahite ।।

anyenānāhṛtasyānyo guṇo ḥvaśyaṃ vivardhate ।
anākrāntasya saṅkalpaiḥ pratibhodeti cetasaḥ ।।

anāhṛtasya anākrāntasya । dṛṣṭāntam uktvā dārṣṭāntikaṃ kathayati anākrāntasyeti । pratibhā pratibhāsaḥ । udeti saphalatvena prādurbhavati ।।

suvarṇo na sthitiṃ yāti malavaty aṃśuke yathā ।
ekā dṛṣṭiḥ sthitiṃ yāti na mlāne cittake tathā ।।

suvarṇaḥ śobhanaḥ śuklādivarṇaḥ । mlāne saṅkalparūṣite ।।

pramārjanād iva maṇes tāmrasyeva ca yuktitaḥ ।
ciram ekadṛḍhābhyāsāc chuddhir bhavati cetasaḥ ।।

ekasmin samyagjñānādau । yaḥ dṛḍhābhyāsaḥ nairantaryeṇa taccintanam । tasmāt ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

pratibhāsātmani jagaty ete kālakriyākramāḥ ।
sodayāstamayā jātāḥ kathaṃ śukrasya cetasaḥ ।।

pratibhāsātmani jagati sphuritānāṃ kālakriyākramāṇāṃ sodayāstamayatvam na yuktam । tac ca śukracetasaḥ kathaṃ jātam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ uttaram āha

yādṛg jagad idaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śukreṇa pitṛmātṛtaḥ ।
tādṛk tasya sthitaṃ citte mayūrāṇḍe mayūravat ।।

pitṛmātṛtaḥ utpannena śukreṇa yādṛk idaṃ jagat dṛṣṭam । tat tasya śukrasya । citte tādṛk sthitam āsīt । yathā mayūrāṇḍe mayūraḥ asti ।।

svabhāvakośāt svaditaṃ tad anena kramoditam ।
bījenāṅkurapattrādilatāpuṣpaphalaṃ yathā ।।

tataḥ anena śukreṇa । tat cittasthaṃ jagat । svabhāvakośāt cittarūpaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ । kramoditam sat svaditam āsvādaviṣayīkṛtam । atra dṛṣṭāntam āha bījeneti ।।

jīvo yadvāsanāsāras tad evāntaḥ prapaśyati ।
svapna evātra dṛṣṭānto dīrghasvapnas tv idaṃ jagat ।।

nanu katham atra svapnaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ astīty । atrāha dīrghasvapna eveti । dīrghatvam cātra cirapratibhāsavaśāj jñeyam ।।

pratyekam udito rāma nanu saṃsāraṣaṇḍakaḥ ।
rātrau sainyanarasvapnajālavat svātmani sphuṭaḥ ।।

rātrau hi sainyanarasvarūpaṃ svapnajālam pratyekam pṛthag ।।

śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

eṣa saṃsṛtiṣaṇḍaugho mithaḥ sammilati svayam ।
no vāpi yadi tan me tvaṃ yathāvad vaktum arhasi ।।

eṣaḥ saṃsṛtiṣaṇḍaughaḥ svayam svabhāvena । yadi milati yadi vā no milati api । tvam etat yathāvat samyak । vaktum arhasi samyak kathayeti yāvat ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaram āha

malinaṃ hi mano ḥvīryaṃ na mithaḥ śleṣam arhati ।
ayo ḥyasīvāsantapte śuddhe tapte tu līyate ।।

hi niścaye । malinam rāgādimaladūṣitam । ata evāvīryam । manaḥ mithaḥ anyoḥnyam । śleṣam melanam । yathāyaḥ asantapte ayasi śleṣaṃ nārhati । śuddhe manasi । ayaś ca santapte ḥyasi līyate ।।

cittatattvāni śuddhāni sammilanti parasparam ।
ekarūpāṇi toyāni yānty aikyaṃ nābilāni hi ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati

śuddhir hi cittasya vivāsanatvam abhūtasaṃvedanarūpam ekam ।
tasyāḥ suṣuptātmapadāt prabudhya tanmātrayuktyā parasaṅgam eti ।।

hi niścaye । abhūtasaṃvedanātma asiddhapadārthasaṃvedanasvarūpam । vivāsanatvam padārthaviṣayabhāvanākhyasaṃskārarāhityam । cittasya śuddhiḥ bhavati । suṣuptātma suṣuptasvarūpam । tasyāḥ śuddheḥ hetoḥ । prabudhya turyākhyam bodham prāpya । tanmātrayuktyā sūkṣmabhūtayogena । parasaṅgam anyaiḥ saha śleṣam । tanmātrayuktyā melanaṃ ca svena saha sarvasyaikopādānatvajñānam eva jñeyam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe saptādaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ । nanu kathaṃ tanmātrayuktyā cetaḥ anyaiḥ saha milatīty । atrāha

sarvasaṃsṛtiṣaṇḍeṣu bījarūpakalātmanaḥ ।
tanmātrapratibhāsasya pratibhāse na bhinnatā ।।

bījarūpā bījasvarūpā । tadātmanaḥ tatsvarūpasya । sthūlabhūtabījarūpasyeti yāvat । tanmātrapratibhāsasya pañcatanmātrākārasya pratibhāsasya । sarvasaṃsṛtiṣaṇḍeṣu samasteṣu sargarūpeṣu ṣaṇḍeṣu । pratibhāse sphuraṇe । mṛda iva ghaṭādiṣu sphuraṇe । ataḥ tanmātrayuktyā cittasyānyamelanaṃ yuktam eveti bhāvaḥ । tanmātrāṇi ca sthūlabhūtabījabhūtāni saṃskāramātraśarīrāṇi ākāśādibhyo buddhyā pṛthakkṛtāni pañca śabdādīni jñeyāni ।।

na kevalaṃ sargaiḥ saha melanam eva tanmātrayuktyā bhavati kiṃ tu brahmaṇi melanam api tayaivety abhiprāyeṇāha

pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā tanmātrāpattipūrvakam ।
sarvasya jīvajātasya suṣuptatvād anantaram ।।

sarvasya jīvajātasya jīvasamūhasya । suṣuptatvāt suṣuptabhāvāt । anantaram paścāt । pravṛttiḥ vā anyasargaiḥ saha melanaṃ vā । nivṛttir vā sargebhyaḥ nivṛttirūpam brahmaṇi melanaṃ vā । tanmātrāpattipūrvakam tanmātrayogapūrvakam eva । bhavati । suṣuptau sargāṇām bījatvenāvasthānāt nivṛttyasambhavaḥ sargāṇām prākaṭyenānavasthānāt pravṛttyasambhava iti suṣuptatvād anantaram ity uktam । anantaram iti kathanena ca suṣupter atrāvaśyambhāvaḥ sūcitaḥ । brahmasargayoḥ setutvena sthitāyāḥ suṣupter avaśyambhāvasya suspaṣṭatvāt । atra ca pravṛttiḥ jīvanmuktānāṃ nivṛttiḥ videhamuktānām iti viṣayavibhāgo draṣṭavyaḥ । itareṣām pravṛttis tu ajñānamūlatvena neha vaktuṃ yuktā ।।

prakṛtatvāt pravṛtteḥ tanmātrāpattipūrvakatvam pṛthak kathayati

pravṛttibhājo ye jīvās te tanmātrapadaṃ gatāḥ ।
tanmātraikatayā sargān mithaḥ paśyanti kalpitān ।।

ye jīvāḥ jīvanmuktasvabhāvāḥ jīvāḥ । pravṛttibhājaḥ sattvaśeṣatayā pravṛttiyuktāḥ bhavanti । te tanmātraikatayā tanmātrayuktyā । kalpitān paramārthatayā kalpitasvarūpān । sargān । jīvanmuktānām manāṃsy anyoḥnyam milantīty atra paramaṃ rahasyam ।।

tanmātraikyapraṇālena citrāḥ sargajalāśayāḥ ।
parasparaṃ sammilanti ghanatāṃ yānti cābhitaḥ ।।

tanmātrāṇām pañcatanmātrāṇām । tad eva praṇālaḥ jalapravāhamārgaḥ । ghanatām ghanībhāvam ।।

nanu sarve sargaughāḥ tanmātraikyapraṇālena milanty atha vā katipaye evety । atrāha

kecit pṛthak sthitim itāḥ pṛthag eva layaṃ gatāḥ ।
kecin mithaḥ sammilitā jagatṣaṇḍāḥ sthitāḥ kṛtāḥ ।।

kecid aśuddhamatayaḥ । uttarārdhe kecit śuddhamatayaḥ । kṛtāḥ kalpitāḥ ।।

nanv etādṛśāḥ sargaughāḥ kasminn ādhāre sthitāḥ bhavantīty । atrāha

jagatṣaṇḍasahasrāṇi yatrāsaṅkhyāny aṇāv aṇau ।
aparasparalagnāni kānanam brahma nāma tat ।।

aparasparalagnāni anyoḥnyam asaṅkīrṇāni । aṇau aṇau pratyaṃśam ।।

mithaḥ sa melanaṃ naiti ghanatāṃ samupāgataḥ ।
yad yad yatra yathā rūḍhaṃ tat tat paśyati netarat ।।

ghanatām ghanībhāvam । mithaḥ sa melanaṃ naiti na gacchati । lakṣaṇayā tatrasthaḥ pramātā । yat yat yatra rūḍham paricitam । tat tat tatra paśyati । atra pramātur aśuddhamatitvaṃ hetutvena bahuśaḥ uktam ।।

vartamānamanorājyavaśāj jīvaparamparāḥ ।
parasparaṃ sammilitāḥ sargāṇāṃ rūḍhibhāvanāḥ ।।

vartamānam yat manorājyam saṅkalpaḥ । jīvaparamparāḥ parasparaṃ sammilitāḥ bhavanti । samānamanorājyatvāj jīvāḥ parasparam milantīti bhāvaḥ । jīvaparamparāḥ kathambhūtāḥ । sargāṇāṃ rūḍhau satyatāyām । ayam bhāvaḥ । śuddhamatīnāṃ sargāḥ tanmātraikyapraṇālena sarvadā milanti । aśuddhamatīnāṃ tu kadācid ekasaṅkalpatveneti ।।

nanu katham iyaṃ dehasattā prākaṭyaṃ gatā yadvaśoditasaṅkalpākhyamalāvṛtabuddhīnāṃ tanmātraikyapraṇālenānyasargaiḥ saha melanaṃ na bhavatīty । atrāha

dehasattā bhṛśaṃ rūḍhā dehābhāvas tu vismṛtaḥ ।
dehatvaparirūḍhatvāc cidvyomnā vismṛtātmanā ।।

cidvyomnā dehatvaparirūḍhatvāt cidvyomakartṛkāt dehabhāve parirūḍhatvāt । cidvyomnā svātmatvena bhāvitāt dehabhāvāt iti yāvat । dehasattā rūḍhā prarohaṃ gatā । dehābhāvaḥ paramārthasan dehapratiyogikas traikāliko ḥbhāvaḥ । cidvyomnā kathambhūtena । vismṛtātmanā vismṛtasvarūpeṇa । vismṛtaḥ vismṛtiṃ nītaḥ ।।

athānyena dṛṣṭāntenānyasargaiḥ sammelanaṃ kathayati

yathā śuddhaprāṇamarut paraprāṇābhivedhanāt ।
vetti vedhyamanorājyaṃ tathā sargān narāśrayī ।।

yathā śuddhaprāṇamarut prāṇāyāmādinā śuddhaprāṇaḥ । paraprāṇābhivedhanāt । paraprāṇeṣu yat abhivedhanam abhivyāptiḥ । parapurapraveśād iti yāvat । vedhyasya abhivyāpyasya puruṣasya । narāśrayī tanmātrapraṇālenānyapuruṣāviṣṭaḥ jīvanmuktaḥ puruṣaḥ brahmaṇaḥ prathamam utthitaḥ puruṣo vā । sargān āśritapuruṣasargān । vetti ।।

evaṃ śrīrāmakṛte praśne uttaraṃ samyag uktvā pūrvatra yatra tatroktāni viśīrṇāni upadeśavākyāni kathayati

sarveṣāṃ jīvarāśīnām ātmāvasthātrayaṃ śritaḥ ।
jagratsvapnasuṣuptākhyam atra deho na kāraṇam ।।

atra avasthātrayāśrayaṇe ।।

evam ātmani jīvatvam anyāvasthātrayātmani ।
tāpāmbhasīva vīcitvam asmin kacati dehatā ।।

anyāvasthātrayātmani । anyat svavyatiriktatvena bhāsamānam । yat avasthātrayam jāgradādyavasthātrayam । ātmā svarūpaṃ yasya । asmin jīvatvāvacchinne ।।

citkalāpadam āsādya suṣuptāntapade sthitam ।
buddho nivartate jīvo mūḍhaḥ sarge pravartate ।।

citkalāpadam turyākhyam padam । buddhaḥ citkalāvimarśanasamarthaḥ । nivartate punaḥ viṣayeṣv āsaktiṃ na bhajate । pravartate viṣayāsaktim bhajate ।।

svabhāvaśuddhir hi yadā tadā maitrī pravartate ।
dvayor ekatvarūpaiva susauhārdanidarśanā ।।

maitrī kathambhūtā eva । dvayoḥ ekatvarūpā eva । dvayor ekatvam eva hi maitrīśabdārthaḥ । susauhārdanidarśanā । susauhārdam praśastamitrabhāvaḥ । nidarśanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ yasyāḥ । susauhārde hi dvayor ekatvam eva bhavati ।।

ajñaḥ suṣuptāt sambuddho jīvaḥ kaścit svasargabhāk ।
sarvagatvāc citaḥ kaścit parasargeṇa nīyate ।।

svasargabhāk suṣuptāvasthāyāḥ pūrvaṃ yādṛksvabhāva āsīt । tādṛksvabhāva evety arthaḥ । parasargeṇa nayanam svabhāvaparivṛttiḥ jñeyā । śukrādisargadṛṣṭāntena vā parasarganayanaṃ yojyam ।।

nanu tasmin sarge ḥnyaḥ sargaḥ kutrāsti yenāsau nīyata ity । atrāha

sarge sarge pṛthagrūpaṃ santi sargāntarāṇy api ।
teṣv apy antaḥsthasargaughāḥ kadalīdalapīṭhavat ।।

yathā kadalīdaleṣv antar anyāni dalāni santi teṣv antar apy anyāni tathā sargeṣv api sargāntarāṇi santi । teṣv antar apy anyāni santīti piṇḍārthaḥ ।।

sarge sargāntarāpūrapattrapīvaravṛttimān ।
svabhāvaśītalo brahmakadalīdalamaṇḍapaḥ ।।

sarge ekasmin sarge । yaḥ sargāntarāpūraḥ anyasargasamūhaḥ । sa eva pattrāṇi । taiḥ pīvarā bṛṃhaṇarūpā । vṛttiḥ sthitiḥ yasya ।।

kadalyām anyatā nāsti yathā pattraśateṣv api ।
brahmatattve ḥnyatā nāsti tathā sargaśateṣv api ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

bījāt phalaṃ rasād bhūtvā yathā bījam punar bhavet ।
tathā brahma mano bhūtvā bodhād brahma punar bhavet ।।

yathā phalam bījāt upādānabhūtāt bījāt । bhūtvā prādurbhūya । rasāt hetoḥ । punaḥ bījam bhavet । tathā brahma mano bhūtvā bodhāt । punaḥ brahma bhavet ।।

rasakāraṇakam bījam phalabhāvena jṛmbhate ।
brahmakāraṇako jīvo jagadrūpeṇa jṛmbhate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

rasasya kāraṇaṃ kiṃ syād iti vaktuṃ na yujyate ।
svabhāvo nirviśeṣatvāt paraṃ vaktuṃ na yujyate ।।

kathaṃ na yujyata ity । atrāha svabhāva iti । svabhāvaḥ param kevalam । vaktum abhiyogaviṣayatāṃ netum । svabhāvasyābhiyoge kriyamāṇe aviśeṣāt sarveṣu svabhāveṣv abhiyogaḥ prāpnotīti nirviśeṣatvād iti padasyābhiprāyaḥ ।।

na cāsattā sarvamaye vaktuṃ kvacana śakyate ।
nākāraṇe kāraṇādi pare vāsty ādikāraṇe ।।

asataḥ sarvamayatvāyogāt iti bhāvaḥ । akāraṇe na vidyate kāraṇaṃ yasya । ādikāraṇe pare utkṛṣṭe cinmātre । ādikāraṇatvāpāyād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

bījaṃ jahan nijavapuḥ phalībhūtaṃ vilokyate ।
brahmājahan nijavapuḥ phalam bījaṃ ca saṃsthitam ।।

brahmaṇaḥ bījatvāvasthāne nijavapuṣaḥ ahānam eva hetuḥ ।।

bījasyākṛtimat sarvaṃ tenānākṛti tatpadam ।
na yujyate samīkartuṃ tasmān nāsty upamā śive ।।

sarvam samastam svarūpam । bījasyākṛtimat bhavati । tena tato hetoḥ । śive śuddhacinmātratattve । upamā nāsti ।।

kham eva jāyate khābhān na ca taj jāyate ḥnyadṛk ।
ato na jātaṃ vā jātaṃ viddhi brahmanabho jagat ।।

khābhāt atyantanairmalyenākāśatulyāt brahmaṇaḥ । nanu katham etad ity āha । caśabdo hetau । yataḥ tat jagannāma kham । anyadṛk brahmetaradṛgrūpam । na jāyate notpadyate । phalitaṃ kathayati ata iti । ābhāsataḥ jātaṃ vā । jagat brahmanabhaḥ brahmākāśam ।।

dṛśyam paśyan svam ātmānaṃ na draṣṭā samprapaśyati ।
prapañcākrāntasaṃvitteḥ kasyodeti nijā sthitiḥ ।।

draṣṭā dṛśyam dṛśikriyāviṣayībhūtam bhāvajātam । svam ātmānam draṣṭṛrūpam nijam ātmānam । na paśyati nānubhavati । prapañcenākrāntā svonmukhatāṃ nītā । tādṛśasya । nijā sthitiḥ svaṃ svarūpam । na kasyāpīty arthaḥ ।।

mṛgatṛṣṇājalabhrāntau satyāṃ keva vidagdhatā ।
vidagdhatāyāṃ satyāṃ tu kevāsau mṛgatṛṣṇikā ।।

ato vidagdhatā eva satsaṅgamādinā poṣaṇīyeti bhāvaḥ ।।

ākāśaviśado draṣṭā sarvago ḥpi na paśyati ।
netraṃ nijam ivātmānaṃ dṛśībhūtam aho bhramaḥ ।।

ākāśavad viśadaḥ śuddhacinmātrarūpatvenātyantanirmalaḥ । dṛśībhūtam dṛśyabhāvaṃ gatam । ātmānam draṣṭākhyam ātmānam । netram iva । yathā netraṃ nijam ātmānaṃ na paśyati । tathety arthaḥ । aho bhramaḥ bhavati ।।

ākāśaviśadam brahma yatnenāpi na labhyate ।
dṛśye dṛśyatayādṛṣṭe tv asya lābhaḥ sudūrataḥ ।।

kuto na labhyate ity । tena dṛśye dṛśyatvādarśanam eva brahmalabdhir iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tvādṛksthūlo ḥvadhānena vinā yatra na dṛśyate ।
tatrātidūrodastaiva draṣṭuḥ sūkṣmasya dṛśyatā ।।

yatra yasmin viṣaye । avadhānena vinā tvādṛksthūlaḥ na dṛśyate । tatra tasmin viṣaye । sūkṣmasya draṣṭuḥ dṛśyatā atidūrodastā eva bhavati । tvādṛg iti dehābhiprāyeṇoktiḥ ।।

draṣṭā draṣṭaiva bhavati na tu spṛśati dṛśyatām ।
dṛśyaṃ ca dṛśyate tena draṣṭā rāma na dṛśyate ।।

draṣṭā dṛśikriyākartā । draṣṭā eva bhavati । asau draṣṭā dṛśyatām dṛśyabhāvam । dṛśyaṃ dṛśyate yena । dṛśyasya dṛśyatvam astīti bhāvaḥ । tena draṣṭrā । draṣṭā draṣṭṛrūpaḥ svātmā । na dṛśyate । atisūkṣmatvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

draṣṭaiva sambhavaty eko na tu dṛśyam ihāsti hi ।
draṣṭā sarvātmako dṛśyaṃ sthitaś cet keva dṛśyatā ।।

sambhavatīti । tasyaiva vicārasahatvād iti bhāvaḥ । sarvātmakaḥ draṣṭā dṛśyaṃ sthitaḥ dṛśyatayā sthitaḥ । tadā dṛśyatā kā iva bhavati । avaśyaṃ ca svapnanyāyena draṣṭuḥ dṛśyatayāvasthānam aṅgīkartavyam ।।

nanu kathaṃ draṣṭā dṛśyatvena tiṣṭhatīty āśaṅkya dṛṣṭāntaṃ kathayati

sarvaśaktimatā rājñā yat yat sampādyate yathā ।
tat tat tathā bhavaty āśu sa evodeti tattayā ।।

yathā sarvaśaktimatā samrāṭtvena sarvaśaktiyuktena । yathā sampādyate sampādanakriyāviṣayatāṃ nīyate । āśu tathā bhavati sampadyate । vicāre kriyamāṇe sa eva rājā eva । tattayā tattadvasturūpeṇa । yathā sarvaśaktimān rājā svāvyatiriktajñānadvāreṇa jñānavivartabhūtasampadyamānavastutayā sphurati । tathā draṣṭā svāvyatiriktadṛśikriyādvāreṇa dṛśikriyāvivartabhūtadṛśyamānapadārthatayā sphuratīti ।।

yathā madhurasollāsaḥ ṣaṇḍo bhavati bhāsuraḥ ।
rasatām ajahac caiva phalapuṣpadalonnataḥ ।।

cidullāsas tathā jīvo bhūtvā bhavati dehakaḥ ।
cinmātratāṃ tām ajahad eva darśanadṛṅmayaḥ ।।

darśanadṛṅmayaḥ karmasādhano ḥyaṃ darśanaśabdaḥ । tena dṛśyadṛṅmayaḥ ity arthaḥ । yugmam ।।

nānāṣaṇḍasahasraughair advitīyair nijātmanaḥ ।
