yathodeti raso bhaumaś cit tathodety ahambhramaiḥ ।।

bhaumaḥ bhūmisambandhī ।।

cidrasollāsavṛkṣāṇāṃ kacatām ātmanātmani ।
dṛśyaśākhāśatāḍhyānām iha nānto ḥvagamyate ।।

cid eva rasaḥ । tasya vṛkṣāṇām jagatām iti yāvat ।।

ṣaṇḍaḥ pratyekam evāntar yathā rasacamatkṛtim ।
svādayaty evam eṣā cit pṛthak paśyati saṃsṛtīḥ ।।

rasena kṛtām ucchūnatārūpāṃ camatkṛtim rasacamatkṛtim ।।

yā yodeti yathā yasyā jīvaśakteḥ svasaṃsṛtiḥ ।
tām tāṃ tathaiti sā svāntaś cid bhūtabhuvanasthitim ।।

udeti sphurati । tāṃ tām bhūtabhuvanasthitim । bhūtānāṃ tadādhārabhūtānām । bhuvanānāṃ ca saṃsthitim saṃsthām ।।

jīvasaṃsṛtayaḥ kāścit pramilanti parasparam ।
svayaṃ vihṛtya saṃsāre śāmyanti cirakālataḥ ।।

kāścit śuddhamatiyuktāḥ । cirakālataḥ dehapātānantaram ।।

sūkṣmayā parayā dṛṣṭyā svam paśyasy anayā tathā ।
jagajjālasahasrāṇi paramāṇvantareṣv api ।।

tvam । svam cinmātrākhyaṃ svātmānam । anayā asmin prakaraṇe proktayā । sūkṣmayā sūkṣmavastuviṣayatvena sūkṣmarūpayā । dṛṣṭyā samyagjñānena । paśyasi anubhavasi । tathāśabdaḥ samuccaye । tathā paramāṇvantareṣv api jagajjālasahasrāṇi paśyasi । apiśabdaḥ paramāṇvantareṣu jagajjālasahasradarśanāsambhavadyotakaḥ ।।

bhittau nabhasi pāṣāṇe jvālāyām anile jale ।
santi saṃsāralakṣyāṇi tile tailam ivākhile ।।

jagadbījabhūtacinmātrasāratveneti bhāvaḥ ।।

śuddham eti yadā cetas tadā jīvo bhavec citiḥ ।
śuddhā ca sā sarvagatā tena sammelanam mithaḥ ।।

sā cit ।।

sarveṣām padmajādīnāṃ svasattābhramapūrakaḥ ।
jagaddīrghamahāsvapnaḥ svayam antaḥ samutthitaḥ ।।

svasattābhramapūrakaḥ svasattābhramakārīty arthaḥ ।।

svapnāt svapnāntaraṃ yānti kāścid bhūtaparamparāḥ ।
tenopalambhaḥ kuḍyādāv āsāṃ dṛḍhataraḥ sthitaḥ ।।

kāścid bhūtaparamparāḥ bhūtapaṅktayaḥ । svapnāt ekasmāt saṃsṛtirūpāt svapnāt । svapnāntaram anyasaṃsṛtirūpaṃ svapnam । āsām svapnāt svapnāntaraṃ gatānām bhūtapaṅktīnām । kuḍyādau dṛḍhataraḥ upalambhaḥ sthitaḥ asti । idaṃ kuḍyam ityādirūpaṃ jñānam asti ।।

yad yatra cid bhāvayati tat tatrāśu bhavaty alam ।
tayā svapne ḥpi yad dṛṣṭaṃ tatkāle satyam eva tat ।।

tayā citā ।।

cidaṇor antare santi samastānubhavāṇavaḥ ।
yathā bījāntare pattralatāpuṣpaphalāṇavaḥ ।।

samastāḥ samastaghaṭapaṭādyākārāḥ । anubhavāṇavaḥ anubhavaleśāḥ ।।

paramāṇuṃ jagad antar dhatte citparamāṇukaḥ ।
līnam ākāśam ākāśe dvaitaikyabhramam utsṛja ।।

citparamāṇukaḥ cidrūpaḥ paramāṇuḥ । jagat paramāṇum jagadrūpam paramāṇum । antaḥ svātmabhittau । phalitam āha līnam iti । ataḥ ākāśam jagadākhyam ākāśam । ākāśe cidākhya ākāśe । etasya phalaṃ kathayati dvaitaikyam iti । ataḥ tvam dvaitaikyabhramam utsṛja tyaja । ekatayāpi vaktum aśakyasya kevalasya cinmātrasya sthitatvāt ।।

deśakālakriyādyākhyaiḥ svair evāṇubhir eva cit ।
aṇūn anubhavaty antar itarāṇor asambhavāt ।।

svair eva svarūpabhūtair eva । aṇūn nānābhūtarūpān aṇūn । antaḥ svasmin । itarāṇoḥ deśādirūpasya cidvyatiriktasyāṇoḥ ।।

svayaṃ sarvasya kacitaḥ svacchaś cidaṇuṣaṇḍakaḥ ।
brahmādeḥ kīṭaniṣṭhasya dehadṛṣṭyānubhāvitaḥ ।।

dehadṛṣṭyā anubhāvitaḥ anubhavaviṣayatāṃ nītaḥ । kīṭaniṣṭhasya kīṭāvasānasya । anubhāvita ity atra svārthe ṇic ārṣaḥ ।।

kacitaṃ kiñcid eveha vastutas tu na kiñcana ।
svayaṃ svatvaṃ svādayante dvaitaṃ citparamāṇavaḥ ।।

punaḥ kim etat sphuratīty । citparamāṇavaḥ cilleśāḥ । dvaitam ghaṭapaṭādirūpadvaitasvarūpam । svādayante camatkāraviṣayatāṃ nayanti ।।

svayam prakacati sphāradehaś cidaṇuṣaṇḍakaḥ ।
netrādikusumadvāraiḥ saṃvidāmodam udgiran ।।

sphāradehaḥ sphārasvarūpaḥ । saṃvidāmodam ghaṭapaṭādijñānarūpam āmodam ।।

sampaśyatītarān kaścid bahīrūpeṇa cidghanān ।
sarvagatvād anāśatvād dṛśyabījasya vai citeḥ ।।

kaścit puruṣaḥ । jāgradavasthāviṣṭa iti yāvat । citeḥ dṛśyabījasya cidākhyasya dṛśyabījasya । sarvagatvāt tathā anāśatvāt । cidghanān citsvarūpatvena cidbharitān । itarān svato bhinnatvena bhātān padārthān । bahīrūpeṇa paśyati bāhyā ete iti anubhavati ।।

antar evākhilaṃ kaścit paśyaty avikalaṃ jagat ।
tatrātikālaṃ kalanād unmajjati nimajjati ।।

kaścit svapnāvasthāviṣṭa iti yāvat । antar eva svasminn eva । na tu bāhye ।।

svapnāt svapnāntaraṃ tatra tathā paśyan punaḥ punaḥ ।
mithyāvaṭeṣu luṭhitaḥ śileva śikharacyutā ।।

kaścit kiṃ kurvan । svapnāt svapnāntaram punaḥ punaḥ paśyan iti pūrveṇaiva sambandhaḥ । kaścit kathambhūtaḥ । avaṭeṣu bhāvābhāvākhyeṣv avaṭeṣu । kā iva । śikharacyutā śilā iva ।।

kecit sammīlitāḥ kecid ātmany eva bhrame sthitāḥ ।
magnāḥ svasaṃvidrasataḥ sphuranto dehiṣaṇḍakāḥ ।।

kecit suṣuptyavasthāviṣṭāḥ । sammīlitāḥ nidrāgrastāḥ । ātmani ajñānavalite svātmani । dehiṣaṇḍakāḥ jīvasamūhāḥ ।।

turyāvasthāviṣṭān kathayati svayam antaḥ prapaśyanti ye jagajjīvasambhramam ।
taiḥ kaiścit tat tathā dṛśyam asatsvapnavad āśritam ।।

ye jīvanmuktāḥ jīvāḥ । jagajjīvasambhramam jagadākhyaṃ jīvasambhramam । antaḥ manasi । taiḥ kaiścit tat dṛśyaṃ tathā āśritam antastvenaivāśritam । turyāvasthāviṣṭā jīvanmuktā hi bāhyam api jagat svapnavad antaḥstham evānubhavanti bhramasvarūpatvadarśanāt ।।

sarvātmatvāt svabhāvasya tad dṛśyaṃ satyam ātmani ।
sarvago vidyate yatra tatra sarvam udeti hi ।।

tat dṛśyam ātmani svasmin svarūpe । svabhāvasya cinmātrākhyasya svabhāvasya । sarvātmatvāt sarvarūpeṇa vartamānatvāt । dṛśyaṃ draṣṭrapekṣayā siddhena dṛśyatvenāsatyam api sat । sarvarūpatvāvasthitacinmātrāparaparyāyasvabhāvasāratvena svasvarūpe satyam eveti । nanu katham etad ity । atrāha sarvaga iti । hi yasmāt । sarvagaḥ sarvavyāpakaṃ svabhāvāparaparyāyam cinmātratvam । yatra vidyate । tatra sarvam dṛśyam । udeti prādurbhavati । ataḥ svabhāvabhūtacinmātravat tatsattāvinābhāvi dṛśyam api satyam eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

jīvāntaḥ pratibhāsasya sargasya punar antare ।
jīvaṣaṇḍa udety uccais tasyāntar itaro ḥpi ca ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jīvāntar jāyate jīvas tasyāntar api jīvakaḥ ।
sarvatra rambhādalavaj jīvabījam prajīvati ।।

prajīvati prakṛṣṭāyāḥ jīvanakriyāyāḥ kartṛtvam bhajati ।।

dṛśyabuddhiparāvṛddhi samam etad anantakam ।
hemnīva kaṭakāditvam parijñaptyaiva naśyati ।।

anantakam antarahitatvena bhāsamānam । parijñaptyaiva cinmātram evedam iti jñānenaiva । na tv anyena kenāpi hetunā । naśyati adarśanaṃ yāti । cinmātrarūpatvenānubhūyamānatvasiddher ity arthaḥ । etat kathambhūtam । dṛśyabuddhyā dṛśyam idam iti buddhyā । parā utkṛṣṭā । etat kim iva । yathā hemni sthitaṃ kaṭakāditvam parijñaptyā hemaivedam iti jñānena naśyati ।।

vicāro yasya nodeti ko ḥhaṃ kim idam ity alam ।
tasyādyantāvimukto ḥsau dīrgho jīvajvarabhramaḥ ।।

ādyantāvimuktaḥ avicchinnapravāhaḥ । jīvo ḥham iti jvararūpaḥ bhramaḥ jīvajvarabhramaḥ ।।

vicāraḥ phalitas tasya vijñeyo yasya sanmateḥ ।
dinānudinam āyāti tānavam bhogagṛdhnutā ।।

vijñeya ity । atra paṇḍitair iti śeṣaḥ । bhogagṛdhnutā bhogākāṅkṣā ।।

yathā dehopayuktaṃ hi karoty ārogyam auṣadham ।
tathendriyajaye nyasto vivekaḥ phalito bhavet ।।

dehopayuktam dehe prayuktam । phalitaḥ mokṣākhyavyavahite phalayuktaḥ । indriyajayasyaiva mokṣam prati sākṣād upāyatvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

viveko ḥsti vacasy eva citre ḥgnir iva bhāsvaraḥ ।
yasya tena parityaktā duḥkhāyaiva vivekitā ।।

yasyety asya pūrvārdhena sambandhaḥ । parityakteti cittābhiprāyeṇoktam ।।

yathā sparśena pavanaḥ sattām āyāti no girā ।
tathecchātānavenaiva viveko ḥsyeti budhyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

citrāmṛtaṃ nāmṛtam eva viddhi citrānalaṃ nānalam eva viddhi ।
citre ḥṅganā nūnam anaṅganaiva vācā vivekas tv aviveka eva ।।

yathā citrasthasyāmṛtādeḥ tṛptyādyarthakriyākāritvābhāvāt anamṛtādirūpatvam eva । tathā kevalaṃ vācaiva kathyamānasya । ata eva indriyajayāsādhakasya vivekasya mokṣākhyārthakriyākāritvābhāvād avivekatvam eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

punaḥ kīdṛk puruṣo vivekī asty । atra sargāntaślokenāha

pūrvaṃ vivekena tanutvam eti rāgo ḥtha vairaṃ ca samūlam eva ।
paścāt parikṣīyata eva yatra sa pāvanas tatra vivekitāsti ।।

yatra yasmin puruṣe । rāgaḥ atha vairaṃ ca dveṣaḥ । vivekena vicāreṇa । paścāt tanutvānantaram । kṣīyate eva naśyaty eva । saḥ puruṣaḥ । tatra tasmin puruṣe । vivekitā vicārayuktatvam । na tu vākyamātreṇa sadasannirṇāyake ity arthaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmoksopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe ḥṣṭādaśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

atidurbodhatvena punar api pūrvoktam evārthaṃ kathayati

jīvabījam param brahma sarvatra kham iva sthitam ।
tena jīvodarajagaty api jīvo ḥsty anekadhā ।।

jīvānām bījam prādurbhavasthānam । param brahma kham ivākāśavat । sarvatra dṛśyatayābhimate samaste jagajjāle । sthitam svarūpasāratayā sthitam bhavati । tena tato hetoḥ । jīvasya yat udaram madhyapradeśaḥ । tatrasthitaṃ yat jagat svapnādirūpaṃ jagat । tasmin api anekadhā nānāvidhasthāvarajaṅgamātmakaprakāreṇa nānāprakāro । jīvo ḥsti ।।

tataḥ kim ity apekṣāyām āha

cidghanaikaghanātmatvāj jīvāntar jīvajātayaḥ ।
kadalīdalavat santi kīṭā iva narodare ।।

ataḥ cidghanena ekam kevalam । tasya bhāvaḥ cidghanaikātmatvam । jīvāntaḥ jīvānām madhye । jīvajātayaḥ kadalīdalavat santi । kadalīdaleṣu hy antar anyāni dalāni santi । jīvajātayaḥ ke iva । yathā narodare kīṭāḥ santi ।।

nanu jīvaḥ kuta utpadyate ity । atrāha

yo yo rāma yathā grīṣme kalkasvedād bhavet krimiḥ ।
tattannāma tathā cittvāt khaṃ jīvībhavati svataḥ ।।

he rāma । sa ca svedaś ca । yaḥ yaḥ krimiḥ yathā yena rūpeṇa । cittvāt tathā tena rūpeṇa । svataḥ jīvībhavati । kham kathambhūtam । tattannāma tasya tasya krimer nāma yasya । tat । grīṣme tāvat nānāvidhāḥ krimayaḥ kalkasvedāt jāyante । teṣāṃ śarīraṃ tāvat kalkasvedamayam bhavatu । taccālakas tu jīvaḥ jīvatvānyathānupapattyā cittvayuktam ākāśam eva । kalkasvedasya śarīramātrasampādane parisamāptatvāt tadanyasyāsannidhānāc ca । atas sarve jīvāḥ ākāśārūpā eveti ।।

yathā yathā yatante te jīvakāḥ svātmasiddhaye ।
tathā tathā bhavanty āśu vicitropāsanakramaiḥ ।।

te ākāśamayāḥ । svātmasiddhaye yathā yathā yatante vicitropāsanākramaiḥ yatanarūpaiḥ nānāvidhair upāsanākramaiḥ । tathā tathā bhavanti ।।

sāmānyenoktvā viśeṣeṇa kathayati

devān devayajo yakṣayajo yakṣān vrajanti hi ।
brahma brahmayajo yānti yad atucchaṃ tad āśrayet ।।

phalitam āha yad iti । ata ity adhyāhāraḥ । ataḥ puruṣaḥ yat atuccham bhavati ।।

nanu tarhi śukraḥ kathaṃ svayatanaṃ vinā nānārūpatāṃ gata ity । atrāha

sa śukro bhṛguputro hi nirmalatvāt svasaṃvidaḥ ।
baddhaḥ prathamadṛṣṭena dṛśyenāśu svabhāvataḥ ।।

saḥ pūrvaprakaraṇoktaḥ । bhṛguputraḥ śukraḥ । hi niścaye । idamprathamatāvaroheṇa svasaṃvidaḥ nirmalatvāt prathamadṛṣṭena dṛśyena svabhāvataḥ prayatanaṃ vināśu baddhaḥ svonmukhaḥ kṛtaḥ । ato na virodha iti bhāvaḥ ।।

abhijātāparimlānā bālā yat prathamam puraḥ ।
saṃvit prāpnoti tadrūpā bhavaty anyā na kācana ।।

abhijātā śuddhā । ata evāparimlānā tāvat kāluṣyam agatā । bālā brahmaṇaḥ sadyaḥ utthitā । tadrūpā bhavati । anyā brahmaṇaḥ pūrvataram utthitā । kācana saṃvit । na bhavati yatnaṃ vinā na bhavati । yatnena tu bhavaty eva । anyathā mokṣābhāvaprasaṅgāt ।।

pūrvaṃ sphuritam praśnaṃ śrīrāmaḥ asmin samaye pṛcchati

jāgratsvapnadaśābhedam bhagavan vaktum arhasi ।
kathaṃ ca jāgraj jāgrat syāt svapno ḥjāgrat katham bhavet ।।

kiṃ kathayāmīty apekṣāyām āha katham iti । jāgrat jāgrat kathaṃ syāt । svapnaḥ ajāgrat svapnaḥ । etad eva kathaya me iti bhāvaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaraṃ kathayati

sthirapratyayayuktaṃ yat taj jāgrad iti kathyate ।
asthirapratyayaṃ yat syāt sa svapnaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।।

sthirapratyayena sa evāyam ity evaṃrūpapratyabhijñāyāṃ kṣameṇa sthirajñānena । yuktaṃ yat bhavati । paṇḍitaiḥ taj jāgrad iti kathyate । yat asthirapratyayam pratyabhijñākṣamāsthirajñānayuktam । syāt । paṇḍitaiḥ saḥ svapnaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ kathitaḥ ।।

jāgratsvapnayoḥ kadācitsambhavayuktaṃ svapnajāgrattvaṃ kathayati

jāgrac cet kṣaṇadṛṣṭaḥ syāt svapnaḥ kālāntarasthitaḥ ।
taj jāgrat svapnatām eti svapno jāgrattvam ṛcchati ।।

jāgral lakṣaṇayā jāgrajjñānaviṣayībhūtaṃ vastu । kṣaṇadṛṣṭaḥ kṣaṇam eva dṛṣṭaḥ । arthāt tataḥ naṣṭaḥ । tathā svapnaḥ svapnajñānaviṣayībhūtaṃ vastu । kālāntarasthitaḥ svapnakālād anyasmin kāle ḥpi sthitaḥ । kadācid dhi svapnadṛṣṭam api vastu prabhāte pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyate । jāgrat jāgradvastugrāhakaṃ jñānam । svapnatām eti asthirapratyayatvāt । svapnaḥ svapnavastugrāhakaṃ jñānam । jāgrattvam ṛcchati sthirapratyayatvāt ।।

nanu katham etad ity । atrāha

jāgratsvapnadaśābhedo na sthirāsthiratāṃ vinā ।
samaḥ sadaiva sarvatra samastānubhavo ḥnayoḥ ।।

yataḥ jāgratsvapnadaśābhedaḥ sthiratāsthiratāṃ vinā na bhavati । ataḥ kṣaṇikajāgrataḥ svapnatvaṃ sthirasvapnasya jāgrattvaṃ yuktam eveti bhāvaḥ । atra samastānubhavam pramāṇatvena kathayati sama iti । anayoḥ jāgratsvapnayoḥ । samasteṣu sthitaḥ anubhavaḥ samastānubhavaḥ । sadā sarveṣu kāleṣu । sarvatra sarveṣu deśeṣu । sthirāsthiratāṃ vineti atrāpi sambandhanīyam ।।

phalitam āha

yad eva sthiratām eti taj jāgrad iti kathyate ।
kṣaṇabhaṅgātmakaḥ svapno yathā bhavati tac chṛṇu ।।

ataḥ yad eva sthiratām eti paṇḍitaiḥ tat svapno ḥpi san jāgrad iti kathyate । yaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgātmakaḥ saḥ jāgrad api san svapnaḥ bhavati । yathaitad bhavati tvam tat śṛṇu । yathā jāgratsvapnayoḥ sthiratvāsthiratvam asti tathā śṛṇv ity arthaḥ ।।

tad eva kathayati

jīvadhātuḥ śarīre ḥntar vidyate yena jīvyate ।
tejo vīryaṃ jīvadhātur ityādyabhidham aṅga tat ।।

jīvākhyaḥ dhātuḥ jīvadhātuḥ । śarīre ḥntaḥ vidyate । yena jīvadhātunā । śarīraṃ jīvyate prāṇadhāraṇakriyāṃ kāryate । jīvyata iti ṇicantaḥ prayogaḥ । tat saḥ jīvadhātuḥ । tejo vīryaṃ jīvadhātur ityādyabhidham bhavati । atra ca dhātuśabdaḥ majjādivat śarīrāntaś cāritvasādṛśyāt upacāreṇa prayuktaḥ ।।

vyavahārī yadā kāyo manasā karmaṇā girā ।
bhavet tadā sa sampanno jīvadhātuḥ prasarpati ।।

yadā yasmin kāle । manasā karmaṇā svāśritayā kriyayā । vyavahārī vyavahārayukto । tadā saḥ jīvadhātuḥ sampannaḥ sampūrṇaḥ san । prasarpati sarvasmiñ śarīre sañcāraṃ karotīty arthaḥ ।।

tataḥ kim ity । āha

tasmin prasarpaty aṅgeṣu sparśāt saṃvid udeti hi ।
puṣṭatvāt saiti cittākhyām antarlīnajagadbhramā ।।

tasmin saṃvinmaye jīvadhātau । aṅgeṣu sparśāt jīvadhātusparśāt । saṃvit jīvadhātuspandabhūtā śītoṣṇādisañcetanarūpā saṃvit । udeti prādurbhavati । sā saṃvit । antarlīnajagadbhramā satī । puṣṭatvāt jīvadhātuprasarpaṇena puṣṭatvāt । nanu antarlīnajagadbhramatvaṃ saṃvidaḥ katham iti cet । saṃvit tāvat jīvadhātoḥ utpadyate । jīvadhātuś ca pitṛjīvadhātoḥ utthānasamaye jagadbhramayukta eva uttiṣṭhati । pitṛjīvadhātor antarlīnajagadbhramatvāt । ataḥ saṃvido ḥpy antarlīnajagadbhramatvaṃ siddham ।।

sekṣaṇādiṣu randhreṣu prasarpantī bahirmayam ।
nānākāravikārāḍhyaṃ rūpam ātmani paśyati ।।

sā saṃvit । īkṣaṇādirandhreṣu prasarpantī satī । bahirmayam bahiḥsvarūpam । nānākāravikāraiḥ ghaṭapaṭādirūpaiḥ ākāravikāraiḥ । āḍhyaṃ rūpam । ātmani paśyati vimṛśati । antar iva saṅkalpasiddhaghaṭapaṭāditām । na caitat katham iti vācyam । svapne dṛṣṭatvāt । yathā svapne saṃvid eva nānārūpair bhāti । tathā bahir apīti na virodhaḥ ।।

tat sthiratvāt tayaivātha jāgrad ity avagamyate ।
jāgratkrama iti proktaḥ suṣuptādikramaṃ śṛṇu ।।

tayā eva saṃvidā eva । na tv anyena dehādinā jaḍena । tat nānākāravikārāḍhyaṃ nijaṃ svarūpam । sthiratvāt kam api kālam tathaiva sthitatvāt । jāgrad ity avagamyate jñāyate । jāgratprakriyopasaṃhārapūrvaṃ suṣuptādiprakriyāṃ vaktum pratijānīte jāgratkrama iti ।।

suṣuptādikramam eva kathayati

manasā karmaṇā vācā yadā kṣubhyati no vapuḥ ।
śānta ātiṣṭhati svaccho jīvadhātus tadā tv asau ।।

na kṣubhyati śrāntatvāt । vyavahāraṃ na karotīty arthaḥ । tadā tasmin kāle । jīvadhātuḥ svacchaḥ suptaprasarpaṇākhyamalaḥ । ata eva śāntaḥ kṣobharahitaḥ । yady api suṣuptaviṣayaḥ śrīrāmakṛtaḥ praśno nāsti tathāpi jāgratsvapnayor avaśyam madhyavartitvāt suṣuptinirṇayaḥ । na hi jāgrataḥ nirgatya suṣuptim agatvā svapnagamanam puruṣasya yuktam । setuvat sarvatra maryādātvena suṣupteḥ sthitatvāt । yady api śuddhacid api sarvatra madhye setutvena vartata eva tathāpi vidyuddyotaratnavat sthūladṛṣṭyaviṣayatvāt tasyāḥ setutvākathanam । sūkṣmadṛṣṭīn prati tv anupayogāt kathanaṃ na yuktam ।।

tadā kiṃ sampatsyate ity । atrāha

samatām āgatair vātaiḥ kṣobhyate na hṛdantare ।
nirvātasadane dīpo yathālokaikakārakaḥ ।।

samatām manaḥkṛtakṣobhābhāvāt samavāhitvam । āgataiḥ vātaiḥ prāṇaiḥ । asau jīvadhātuḥ hṛdantare na kṣobhyate kṣobhayukto na kriyate । anena manonāśena prāṇarodhaḥ prāṇarodhena ca manonāśaḥ sampatsyate iti sūcitam । tatrāpi keṣāñcit prāṇarodhena manonāśaḥ mataḥ । asmākaṃ tu samyagjñānasādhitena manonāśenaiva prāṇarodhaḥ । sa cet tatra sahakārī tan na doṣaḥ । tataḥ sarvathā manonāśaḥ prāṇarodhena । manonāśas tu madirādiprayuktamanonāśavan nātyantika iti matam । atra pratibhānvitā eva pramāṇam ity alam bahunā । jīvadhātuḥ ka iva । yathā nirvātasadane vātaiḥ ālokaikakārakaḥ dīpo na kṣobhyate ।।

tataḥ kiṃ sampadyata ity । atrāha

tataḥ sarati nāṅgeṣu saṃvit kṣubhyati tena no ।
na cekṣaṇādīny āyāti randhrāṇy āyāti no bahiḥ ।।

tataḥ sa jīvadhātuḥ । aṅgeṣu na sarati sañcāraṃ na karoti । tena jīvadhātusaraṇena । saṃvit jīvadhātuspandarūpā saṃvit । no kṣubhyati na udeti । sā saṃvit īkṣaṇādīni randhrāṇi na cāyāti bahiḥ no āyāti ।।

tadāsau kutra tiṣṭhatīty apekṣāyām āha

jīve ḥntar eva sphurati tailasaṃvid yathā tile ।
śītasaṃvid dhima iva snehasaṃvid yathā ghṛte ।।

asau saṃvit jīve ḥntaḥ svadharmibhūtajīvamadhye eva । tailasaṃvid iva tailākārā saṃvit । tailasaṃvit tailam iti yāvat । yathā sā tile sphurati । evam anyasmin dṛṣṭāntadvaye ḥpi yojyam ।।

nanu tadā jīvaḥ kiṃ karotīty । atrāha jīvaḥ kālakalāṃ kāñcit tiṣṭhan śāntatayātmani ।
daśām āyāti sauṣuptīṃ saumyavātāṃ vicetanām ।।

tadā jīvaḥ kāñcit atisūkṣmatayā vaktum aśakyām । kālakalāṃ kālaleśaṃ tāvat । śāntatayā ātmani jñānātmani svarūpe । tiṣṭhan prathamaṃ tiṣṭhan । tataḥ vicetanām ajñānamayīm । saumyavātām samavāhiprāṇām । sauṣuptīṃ daśām āyāti । anena jāgratsuṣuptayor madhye sūkṣmadṛṣṭibhiḥ vedyaḥ madhyadhāmapraveśaḥ uktaḥ । anenaiva cābhiprāyeṇa nidrādau jāgarasyānta ityādy uktam । ity alaṃ rahasyodghāṭanena ।।

nanu suṣupta eva jīvaḥ kṣobharāhityāt kathaṃ na turyavān astīty apekṣāyām āha

jñātvā cetasy uparate śāmyan vyavaharann api ।
jāgratsvapnasuṣupteṣu prabuddhas turyavān smṛtaḥ ।।

jñātvā śuddhacinmātrarūpaṃ svātmānaṃ samyag jñātvā । cetasi vikalpasvarūpe manasi । uparate līne sati । vyavaharann api śarīrayātrānimittaṃ vyavahāraṃ kurvann api । śāmyan vyavahārakṛtaṃ kṣobham atyantanaipuṇyāt agacchan । tathā jāgratsvapnasuṣupteṣu prabuddhaḥ kīdṛgrūpāṇy etānīti samyagjñānayuktaḥ । na tu jaḍaḥ । paṇḍitaiḥ turyavān smṛtaḥ । suṣuptas tu naitādṛśo ḥstīti nāsau turyavān iti bhāvaḥ ।।

svapnaṃ nirūpayitum prastauti

sauṣuptāt somyatāṃ yātaiḥ prāṇaiḥ sañcālyate yadā ।
sa jīvadhātus sā saṃvit tataś cittatayoditā ।।

suṣuptam eva sauṣuptam । somyatāṃ yātaiḥ vātaiḥ । yadā suṣuptapariṇāmakāle । sa jīvadhātuḥ cālyate । sā saṃvit jīvadhātuspandarūpā saṃvit । cittatayā cittabhāvena । uditā prādurbhūtā ।।

cittatayā uditya kiṃ karotīty । atrāha

svāntaḥsaṃsthaṃ jagajjālam bhāgabhāgaiḥ kramabhramaiḥ ।
paśyati svāntar evāśu sphāram bījam iva drumam ।।

tataḥ sā cittarūpā saṃvit svāntaḥsaṃstham saṃskārarūpeṇa svātmani sthitam । jagajjālaṃ svāntar eva na tu bāhye । āśu kramabhramaiḥ na tu sahajakramayuktaiḥ । bhāgabhāgaiḥ padārtharūpaiḥ leśaleśaiḥ । paśyati anubhavati । yathā sphāram aṅkuronmukham । drumam svāntaḥ paśyati । anyathā tannirgamānupapatteḥ ।।

tad eva viśeṣataḥ kathayati

jīvadhātur yadā vātaiḥ kiñcit saṅkṣobhyate bhṛśam ।
tadohyate ḥmbara iva paśyaty ātmani khe gatim ।।

vātabāhulyasvabhāva evāyaṃ yat puruṣaḥ svapne khe gatim paśyatīti vākyārthaḥ ।।

yadāmbhasā plāvyate ḥsau tadā vāryādisambhramam ।
antar evānubhavati svāmodaṃ kusumaṃ yathā ।।

asau jīvadhātuḥ । ambhasā kapharūpeṇa jalena । plāvyate pūryate । vāryādisambhramam udakaplavādirūpaṃ sambhramam ।।

yadā pittādinākrāntas tadāgnyauṣṇyādisambhramam ।
antar evānubhavati sphāram bahir ivākhilam ।।

paramārthatas tu na bahiḥ sphāram iti ivaśabdopādanam ।।

raktāpūrṇo raktavarṇān deśakālān bahir yadā ।
paśyaty anubhavātmatvāt tatraiva ca nimajjati ।।

yadā raktāpūrṇaḥ raktapūritaḥ । tadā bahiḥ raktavarṇān deśakālān paśyati । na kevalam paśyati । tatraiva ca nimajjati ।।

nanu nānāvyavahārān katham paśyatīty । atrāha

sevate vāsanāṃ yāṃ tāṃ so ḥntaḥ paśyati nidritaḥ ।
pavanakṣobhitai randhrair bahir akṣādibhir yathā ।।

saḥ jīvadhātuḥ । yām śubhāśubharūpām । vāsanāṃ sevate nidritaḥ san । tathā katham pavanakṣobhitaḥ akṣādibhiḥ randhraiḥ netrādidvāraiḥ । yathā bahiḥ paśyati ।।

saṅgṛhya svapnalakṣaṇaṃ kathayati

anākrantendriyacchidro yad akṣubdho ḥntar eva saḥ ।
saṃvidānubhavaty āśu sa svapna iti kathyate ।।

saḥ jīvadhātuḥ । anākrantendriyacchidraḥ antar eva akṣubdhaḥ bāhyakṣobharahitaḥ san । saṃvidā saṃvidākhyena dharmeṇa । svapne yat anubhavati jagadviṣayam anubhavaṃ karoti । paṇḍitaiḥ sa svapna iti kathyate ।।

jāgrallakṣaṇaṃ kathayati

samākrantendriyacchidro yat kṣubdho bāhyasaṃvidā ।
paripaśyati taj jāgrad ity āhur matimattamāḥ ।।

atiśayena matimantaḥ matimattamāḥ । jāgratsvapnayor eva pṛṣṭatvāt tayor evehopasaṃhāre saṅgraheṇa lakṣaṇābhidhānam । na suṣupteḥ ।।

sargāntaślokenaitad upasaṃharati

iti viditavatā tvayādhunāntaḥ prathitamahāmatineha satyatāsthā ।
asati jagati naiva bhāvanīyā mṛtihṛtisaṃsṛtidoṣabhāvanīyā ।।

iti evam । viditavatā jñātavatā । ata eva prathitā visṛtiṃ gatā । asati jagati adhunā antaḥ manasi । satyatāsthā satyam idam ity evaṃrūpā āsthā । na bhāvanīyā bhāvanāviṣayatāṃ na neyā । mṛtiś ca hṛtiś ca saṃsṛtiś ca tāḥ mṛtihṛtisaṃsṛtayaḥ । tān bhāvayati sampādayatīti tādṛśī । saṃsārasatyatāsthāyāṃ hi tadgatāḥ mṛtyādidoṣāḥ bādhante । tadasatyatāsthāyāṃ tu tā api asatyabhūtā eva kām bādhāṃ kartuṃ śaknuvanti । na hi vandhyāputraḥ kañcid bādhate ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe ekonaviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ । evaṃ śrīrāmeṇa madhye pṛṣṭaṃ jāgradādisvarūpaṃ nirṇīya prakṛtam evānusandadhāti

etat te kathitaṃ sarvam manorūpanirūpaṇe ।
mayā rāghava nānyena kenacin nāma hetunā ।।

etat sarvam yo yathā yatate saḥ tathā bhavatīty etat samastam । manorūpanirūpaṇe manonirūpaṇanimittam । anyena hetunā na kathitam vyarthatvāt ।।

manonirūpaṇam eva karoti dṛḍhaniścayavac ceto yad bhāvayati bhūriśaḥ ।
tattāṃ yāty analāśleṣād ayaḥpiṇḍo ḥgnitām iva ।।

bhūriśaḥ abhyāsena ।।

bhāvābhāvagrahotsargadṛśaś cittena kalpitāḥ ।
nāsatyā nāpi satyās tā manaścāpalakāraṇāḥ ।।

manaścāpalam eva kāraṇaṃ yāsām । tāḥ manaścāpalakāraṇāḥ । manaścāpalakāraṇaṃ hi rajjusarpādikam arthakriyākāritvābhāvena na satyam bhavati । bhāsamānatvenāsatyaṃ ca na bhavati ।।

mano hi hetuḥ kartṛ syāt kāraṇaṃ ca jagatsthiteḥ ।
viśvarūpatayaivedaṃ tanoti malinam manaḥ ।।

hi niścaye । manaḥ jagatsthiteḥ hetuḥ nimittakāraṇaṃ kartṛ । kartṛ kārakaḥ । kāraṇam samavāyikāraṇam asamavāyikāraṇaṃ ca । bhavati । yataḥ idam manaḥ malinam vāsanāmaladūṣitaṃ sat । viśvarūpatayā idam jagat । nātrānyaḥ kaścit kārakatvaṃ yātīti bhāvaḥ । svapnasya cātra dṛṣṭāntatvaṃ sphuṭam eva ।।

mano hi puruṣo rāma tan niyojyaṃ śubhe pathi ।
tajjayaikāntasādhyā hi sarvā jagati bhūtayaḥ ।।

niyojyam preraṇīyam । śubhe pathi vivekasvarūpe । hi yasmāt । jagati sarvāḥ vibhūtayaḥ bhogamokṣarūpāṇy aiśvaryāṇi । tasya manasaḥ । yaḥ jayaḥ śubhe pathi niyojanam । tena sādhyāḥ bhavanti ।।

nanu śarīrasya puruṣatvena sthitatvāt kathaṃ cakṣuṣālabhyamānasya manasaḥ puruṣatvaṃ kathayasīty । atrāha

śarīraṃ cet śarīraṃ syāt kathaṃ śukro mahāmatiḥ ।
agamad vividham bhedam bahudehasamudbhavam ।।

śarīram sthūlaśrīram । śarīram lakṣaṇayā puruṣaḥ । cet syāt । bahudehebhyaḥ samudbhavaḥ yasya । tādṛśam vividham bhedam । śarīrasyaikenaiva rūpeṇa sthitatvāt ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

tasmāc cittaṃ hi puruṣaḥ puruṣaś cittam eva hi ।
yanmayaṃ ca bhavaty etat tad avāpnoty asaṃśayam ।।

hi niścaye । yanmayam yadviṣayānusandhānamayam ।।

paramaphalitam āha

yad atuccham anāyāsam anupādhi gatabhramam ।
yatnāt tadanusandhānaṃ kuru tattāṃ ca yāsyasi ।।

ataḥ yat vastu । atuccham anāyāsam āyāsasādhyatārahitam । anupādhi tathā gatabhramam । tvam tadanusandhānaṃ kuru । tataḥ tattām atucchatvādidharmarahitavastubhāvam ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati abhipatati manaḥsthitiṃ śarīraṃ na tu vapurācaritam manaḥ prayāti ।
abhipatatu tavātra tena satyaṃ subhaga manaḥ prajahātv asatyam anyat ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe viṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

atra śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

bhagavan sarvadharmajña saṃśayo me mahān ayam ।
hṛdi vyāvartate lolaḥ kallola iva sāgare ।।

vyāvartate sphurati ।।

dikkālādyanavacchinne tate nitye nirāmaye ।
mlānā saṃvin manonāmnī kutaḥ keyam upasthitā ।।

dikkālādibhiḥ aparicchinne svaparicchedakasya paricchedaṃ kartum aśakyatvāt । ādiśabdena vastvādeḥ grahaṇam । tate vyāpake । nitye prākpradhvaṃsātyantābhāvarahite । nirāmaye kalanākhyarogarahite । mlānā saṅkalpavikalparūpatvena malinā । manonamnī । iyaṃ saṃvit saṃvidākhyaḥ spandaḥ । kutaḥ upasthitā । naitasyā upasthānam atra yuktam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

yasmād anyan na nāmāsti na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।
kutaḥ kīdṛk kathaṃ tasya kalaṅkaḥ kutra vidyate ।।

yasmāt śuddhacinmātratattvāt । anyat bhinnaṃ vastu । nāma niścaye । nāsti na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati । tasya kalaṅkaḥ manorūpaḥ kalaṅkaḥ । kutaḥ vidyate kīdṛk vidyate kathaṃ vidyate । kutra vidyate sarvathā sambhavānupapatteḥ na vidyate ity arthaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ uttaraṃ kathayati

sādhu rāma tvayā proktaṃ jñātā te mokṣabhāginī ।
matir uttamaniḥṣyandā nandanasyeva mañjarī ।।

uttamaniḥṣyandā śreṣṭhapravāhā ।।

pūrvāparavicārārthatatpareyam matis tava ।
samprāpsyati padam proccair yat prāptaṃ śaṅkarādibhiḥ ।।

pūrvāparavicārarūpaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ । proccaiḥ padam mokṣākhyaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sthānam ।।

tarhi matpraśnasyottaraṃ kathayety । atrāha

praśnasyāsya tu he rāma na kālas tava samprati ।
siddhāntaḥ kathyate yatra tatrāyam praśna ucyate ।।

mayāyam praśna ucyate kṛtottaraḥ sampādyate iti sambandhaḥ ।।

nanu yadi siddhāntakāle ḥsau praśnaḥ tava smṛtipathaṃ nāyāsyati tadā kiṃ kāryam ity । atrāha

siddhāntakāle bhavatā praṣṭavyo ḥham idam padam ।
karāmalakavat tena siddhāntas te bhaviṣyati ।।

karāmalakavat prayatnarahitam ।।

nanv asmin samaya eva kathaṃ na kathayasīty । atrāha

siddhāntakāle praśnoktir eṣā tava virājate ।
prāvṛṣy eva hi kekoktir yuktā śaradi haṃsagīḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sahajo nīlimā vyomni śobhate prāvṛṣaḥ kṣaye ।
prāvṛṣi tu danūdagrapayodapaṭalotthitaḥ ।।

prāvṛṣaḥ kṣaye śaradi । prāvṛṣi nīlimā śobhate । danuvat dānavamātṛvat । udagraṃ yat payodapaṭalam । tasmād utthitaḥ jātaḥ ।।

etad upasaṃhṛtya prakṛtam evānusarati

ayam prakṛta ārabdho manonirṇaya uttamaḥ ।
yadvaśāj janatājanma tad ākarṇaya suvrata ।।

ayam uttamaḥ manonirṇayaḥ asmābhiḥ ārabdhaḥ । prakṛtaḥ prakaraṇavaśena prāptaḥ । enam eva śṛṇv iti bhāvaḥ । yadvaśāt janatājanma janasamūhajanma bhavati । tvam tad ākarṇaya śṛṇu । manonirṇayāṅgabhūtatvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tad eva kathayati

evam prakṛtir eveyam manomananadharmiṇī ।
karmeti rāma nirṇītaṃ sarvair eva mumukṣubhiḥ ।।

he rāma । pūrvasargokte niścaye paramārthatayā sthite sati । manasaḥ yat mananam anusandhānākhyo vyāpāraḥ । taddharmiṇī tatsvarūpiṇī । iyam prakṛtiḥ eva jagadupādānarūpā mūlaprakṛtir eva । sarvaiḥ mumukṣubhiḥ karmeti nirṇītam । manomananam eva karmeti piṇḍārthaḥ ।।

śṛṇu lakṣaṇabhedena tan nānāmatatāṃ katham ।
vāgmināṃ vadatāṃ yātaṃ citrābhiḥ śāstradṛṣṭibhiḥ ।।

tvaṃ śṛṇu । tat manomananarūpaṃ karma । lakṣaṇabhedena । tad eva kathayāmīti bhāvaḥ । vāgminām kathambhūtānām । citrābhiḥ nānāvidhābhiḥ । śāstradṛṣṭibhiḥ śāstrarūpābhiḥ dṛṣṭibhiḥ । vadatāṃ vivādaṃ kurvatām । anyathā matabhedo na syāt ।।

tad eva kathayati

yaṃ yam bhāvam upādatte mano mananacañcalam ।
taṃ tam eti ghanāmodamadhyasthaḥ pavano yathā ।।

mananena mananākhyena dharmeṇa । cañcalam nānāpadārthayāyi । manaḥ । yaṃ yam bhāvam śubham aśubhaṃ vā padārthamananodbhūtaṃ vāsanāviśeṣam । upādatte gṛhṇāti । taṃ tam eti tattadanusandhānamayo bhavatīty arthaḥ । ko yathā । yathā ghanāmodamadhyasthaḥ pavanaḥ āmodam eti ।।

tatas tam eva nirṇīya tam eva ca vikalpayan ।
antas tayā rañjanayā rañjayan svām ahaṅkṛtim ।।

tanniścayam upādāya tatraiva rasam ṛcchati ।
tanmayatvaṃ śarīre tu tato buddhīndriyeṣv api ।।

tataḥ tat manaḥ । tam eva ca na tv anyat । vikalpayan punaḥ punaḥ parāmṛśan । tayā tadbhāvarūpayā । rañjanayā rāgadravyeṇa । svām ahaṅkṛtim nijām ahaṅkāravṛttim । rañjayan uparaktāṃ kurvan । mama kadā etat syāt iti parāmṛśann iti yāvat । tataḥ tanniścayam tasya bhāvasya niścayam । camatkārakāri idam ity evaṃrūpaṃ niścayam । tatraiva tasmin śubhe aśubhe vā vāsanāviśeṣe eva । āsaktim iti yāvat । tataḥ tadanantaram । śarīre tanmayatvam bhavati । anyathā tatsvarūpe bāhye padārthe pravṛttiparihārarūpāyāḥ ceṣṭāyā asambhavāt na kevalaṃ śarīre eva kiṃ tu buddhīndriyeṣv api tanmayatvam bhavati । anyathā teṣām api tatra punaḥ punaḥ svakriyākāritvāyogāt । karmendriyāṇāṃ tu śarīreṇaiva grahaṇam । tathā hi । bāhye puruṣaḥ prathamaṃ kapitthādikam bhuṅkte । tataḥ tasya manaḥ tasya phalasya vāsanām antaḥ dhārayati । tataḥ vāsanārūpasya tasyaivānusandhānam punaḥ punaḥ karoti । tataḥ vāsanārūpeṇa tena svām ahaṅkṛtiṃ rañjayati । tataḥ tadāśritāni buddhīndriyāṇy api tad eva pratisammukhāni bhavanti । tataḥ tadāśrayaṃ śarīraṃ tat praty eva ceṣṭāṃ karotīti ।।

nanu kutaḥ etad ity । atrāha

yanmayaṃ hi mano rāma dehas tadanu tadvaśāt ।
tattām āyāti gandhāntaḥ pavano gandhatām iva ।।

yanmayam yadbhāvamayam ।।

buddhīndriyeṣu valgatsu karmendriyagaṇas tataḥ ।
sphurati svata evorvīrajo lola ivānile ।।

sphurati svāṃ kriyām prati sammukhībhavati । svata eva preraṇāṃ vinā । karmendriyagaṇaḥ kim iva । yathā urvīrajaḥ anile lole sati । svata eva sphurati ।।

karmendriyagaṇe kṣubdhe svaśaktim prathayaty alam ।
karma niṣpadyate sphāram pāṃsujālam ivānilāt ।।

svaśaktim svakāryam prati nijaṃ sāmarthyam । prathayati vistārayati । karma viṣayādānarūpaṃ karma । niṣpadyate sampadyate ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

evaṃ hi manasaḥ karma karmabījam manaḥ smṛtam ।
abhinnaiva tayoḥ sattā yathā kusumagandhayoḥ ।।

evaṃ hi sati । manasaḥ manaḥsakāśāt । karma utpadyate iti śeṣaḥ । karmaiva bījam yasya । smṛtam । karmaṇaḥ manaḥ utpadyate iti bhāvaḥ । phalitam āhābhinneti । ataḥ etayoḥ karmamanasoḥ । sattā abhinnaiva bhavati । kusumagandhayoḥ yathā । na hi manoḥnuvṛttiṃ vinā śarīrāśrayam bāhyam api karma sampadyate । na ca hi karmasādhitavāsanāmātrarūpatāṃ vinā mano nāma kiñcid astīti bhāvaḥ ।।

yādṛśam bhāvam ādatte dṛḍhābhyāsavaśān manaḥ ।
tathā spando ḥsya karmākhyas tathā śākhā vimuñcati ।।

yādṛśam śubham aśubhaṃ vā । śākhāḥ saṅkalparūpāḥ ।।

tathā kriyāṃ tatphaladāṃ niṣpādayati cādarāt ।
tatas tad eva cāsvādam anubhūyāśu badhyate ।।

śarīradvāreṇeti śeṣaḥ । tad eva bhāvaviṣayīkṛtaṃ vastv eva । badhyate ghanataraṃ tadvāsanāviṣṭo bhavatīty arthaḥ ।।

punar apy etad eva kathayati

yaṃ yam bhāvam upādatte tat tad vastv iti vindati ।
tac chreyo ḥnyat tu nāstīti niścayo ḥsya prajāyate ।।

vastu satyabhūtam ।।

dharmārthakāmamokṣārtham prayatante sadaiva hi ।
manāṃsi dṛḍhabhāvāni pratipattyā svayaiva hi ।।

svayā pratipattyā na tu parapreraṇayā ।।

yadartham iyam prakriyā kṛtā tad eva kathayati

manobhiḥ kāpilānāṃ tu pratipattiṃ nijām alam ।
urarīkṛtya nirṇīya kalpitāḥ śāstradṛṣṭayaḥ ।।

kāpilānām kapilānusāriṇām । sāṅkhyānām iti yāvat । manobhiḥ । nijām pratipattim niścayam । urarīkṛtya ।śāstradṛṣṭayaḥ prakṛtipuruṣapratipādikāḥ śāstradṛṣṭayaḥ । kalpitāḥ ।।

kāpilān eva viśinaṣṭi

mokṣe tu nānyathā prāptir iti bhāvitacetasaḥ ।
svāṃ dṛṣṭim pravivṛṇvantaḥ sthitāḥ svaniyamabhramaiḥ ।।

bhāvitam bhāvanāyuktam । svena kṛtā ye niyamabhramāḥ । eṣām api manovaśād eva matabhedo ḥstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

vedāntavādino buddhyā brahmedam iti dṛḍhayā ।
yuktiṃ śamadamopetāṃ nirṇīya parikalpya ca ।।

muktau tu nānyathā prāptir iti bhāvitacetasaḥ ।
svāṃ dṛṣṭim pravivṛṇvantaḥ sthitāḥ svaniyamabhramaiḥ ।।

yuktim śravaṇādirūpam upāyam ।।

vijñānavādino buddhyā sphuratsvabhramarūpayā ।
svāṃ dṛṣṭim pravivṛṇvanti svair eva niyamabhramaiḥ ।।

vijñānavādinaḥ vijñānādvaitavādinaḥ bauddhāḥ । svāṃ dṛṣṭim vijñānam evedam itirūpām । pravivṛṇvanti prakaṭīkurvanti ।।

ārhatādibhir anyaiś ca svayābhimatayecchayā ।
citrāś citrasamācārāḥ kalpitāḥ śāstradṛṣṭayaḥ ।।

ādiśabdena cārvākādīnāṃ grahaṇam ।।

nirnimittotthasaumyāmbubudbudaughair ivotthitaiḥ ।
svaniścayair iti prauḍhā nānākārā hi rītayaḥ ।।

nirnimittotthāḥ ye saumyāmbubudbudaughāḥ । rītayaḥ śāstrarītayaḥ ।।

sarvāsām eva caitāsāṃ rītīnām eka ākaraḥ ।
mano nāma mahābāho maṇīnām iva sāgaraḥ ।।

sarvāsām sāṅkhyādipraṇītānām । ākaraḥ utpattisthānam ।।

na nimbekṣū kaṭusvādū śītoṣṇau nendupāvakau ।
yad yathā manasābhyastam upalabdhaṃ tathaiva tat ।।

kaṭusvādū tiktamadhurau । anyathā cittavṛttibhedena heyopādeyatvaṃ na syāt । yad eva hi yasya heyatvena sthitaṃ tad evānyasyopādeyatayā ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

yas tv akṛtrima ānandas tadartham prayateta na vai ।
manas tanmayatāṃ neyaṃ tenāsau samavāpyate ।।

ata ity adhyāhāryam । yataḥ kasmiṃścid api bāhye vastuni svabhāvena svādutā nāsti । ataḥ yaḥ akṛtrimaḥ bhogādiviṣayanirapekṣatvena sthitatvāt svābhāvikaḥ । ānandaḥ svātmarūpaḥ ānandaḥ । bhavati । nanu kena yatnenāsau prāpyate ity । puruṣeṇa manaḥ saṅkalpātmakaṃ cittam । tanmayatām svātmabhūtānandarūpatām । adhyātmaśāstropadiṣṭamārgeṇa tatparāmarśaikapravaṇaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ । tena manasaḥ tanmayatvanayanamātreṇa yatnenāsau akṛtrimaḥ ānandaḥ ।।

nanu sukhaduḥkhavaśīkṛtam manaḥ kathaṃ tanmayatāṃ neyam ity । atrāha

dṛśyaṃ saṃsāraḍimbasthaṃ tuccham parijahan manaḥ ।
tajjābhyāṃ sukhaduḥkhābhyāṃ nāvaśaḥ parikṛṣyate ।।

saṃsāra eva ḍimbaḥ bālaḥ । tatra tiṣṭhatīti tādṛśam । dṛśyam dṛśikriyāviṣayam bhāvajātam । jahat svaunmukhyāviṣayatāṃ nayat । manaḥ । tajjābhyām dṛśyotpannābhyām । sukhaduḥkhābhyām । nāvaśaḥ parikṛṣyate na balātkāreṇāsvādhīnīkriyate । avaśa iti āviṣṭaliṅgam ।।

nanu dṛśye ko doṣo ḥstīty । atrāha

apavitram asadrūpam mohanam bhayakāraṇam ।
dṛśyam ābhāsam ābhogi bandham mā bhāvayānagha ।।

anagha । dṛśyabhāvanānarhatvaṃ dṛśyam mā bhāvaya manoḥnusandhānaviṣayam mā kuru । kimarthaṃ na bhāvayāmīty apekṣāyāṃ viśeṣaṇāny āha apavitram ityādi । apavitram rāgādirūpapāpotpādakatvāt pavitratārahitam । asadrūpam kiṃrūpam iti vicārāsahatvāt pāramārthikasattārahitam । mohanam anātmany ātmatvarūpamohotpādakam । bhayakāraṇam mṛtyādyupādānabhayahetum । ābhāsam ābhāsamātrasvarūpam । na tu vastutayā sthitam । ābhogi vistārayuktam । bandham ātmajñānam prati rodhakatvāt bandhasvarūpam ।।

māyaiṣā sā hy avidyaiṣā bhāvanaiṣā bhayāvahā ।
saṃvidas tanmayatvaṃ yat tat karmeti vidur budhāḥ ।।

eṣā dṛśyabhāvanā । eṣā avidyā bhavati । eṣā bhayāvahā bhāvanā vāsanā । nanu tarhi karma kiṃrūpam astīty । atrāha saṃvida iti । saṃvidaḥ manorūpāyāḥ saṃvidaḥ । tanmayatvam dṛśyamayatvam । yad bhavati । budhāḥ tat karmeti viduḥ । karmāpi eṣaiveti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu manaḥ kiṃrūpam asti yena kṛtā dṛśyabhāvanā māyādināmatvenoktety । atrāha

draṣṭur dṛśyaikatānatvaṃ viddhi tvam mohanam manaḥ ।
bhramāyaiva ca tan mithyā mahīmakkolakarmavat ।।

draṣṭuḥ dṛśikriyākartuḥ । dṛśyaikatānatvam dṛśyam prati sammukhatām । mohanam mohakāri । tat bhramāya bhramotpādāya sat । ābhāsamātratvena vastusat na bhavatīty arthaḥ । makkolakarma sudhālepaḥ । yathā mṛttikāyāṃ kṛtasudhālepaḥ vastutaḥ san nāsti । mṛttikāyāḥ eva tathā sthitatvāt sudhāyāḥ lepatayaiva bhāvāt । tathā cinmātre bhāsamānam manaḥ vastutaḥ nāsti cinmātrasyaiva tathā sthitatvāt ity arthaḥ ।।

nanu kathaṃ draṣṭṛdṛśyaikatānatārūpam manaḥ mithyārūpam astīty । atrāha

dṛśyatanmayatā yaiṣā svabhāvasyānubhūyate ।
saṃsāramadirā seyam avidyety ucyate budhaiḥ ।।

asmābhiḥ । svabhāvasya draṣṭṛrūpasya svabhāvasya । yā dṛśyatanmayatā dṛśyaikatānatā । budhaiḥ sā iyam bhramotpādakatvāt saṃsāramadirārūpā avidyeti ucyate । ato manaḥ avidyārūpam evāvastubhūtam ity arthaḥ ।।

ko ḥnarthaḥ anayāvidyayā kriyate ity । atrāha

anayopahato lokaḥ kalyāṇaṃ nādhigacchati ।
bhāsvaraṃ tapanālokam paṭalāndhekṣaṇo yathā ।।

anayā draṣṭuḥ dṛśyatanmayatārūpayā । kalyāṇam svātmani viśrāntirūpam । paṭalam netrarogaviśeṣaḥ ।।

nanu sā kuta utpadyata ity । atrāha

svayam utpadyate sā ca saṅkalpād vyomavṛkṣavat ।
asaṅkalpanamātreṇa svayam eva vinaśyati ।।

utpadyate prādurbhavati । nanu sā kathaṃ naśyati ity । atrāhāsaṅkalpanamātreti । asaṅkalpanamātreṇa saṅkalpākaraṇamātreṇa । ata evāha svayam iti । na hi asaṅkalpanaṃ yatnaḥ । api tu saṅkalpanam eva ।।

nanv avidyānāśena kiṃ sampadyate ity । atrāha

asaṅkalpanamātreṇa bhāvanāyām mahāmate ।
kṣīṇāyāṃ svaprasādena vimarśena vilāsinā ।।

asaṃsaṅge padārtheṣu sarveṣu sthiratāṃ gate ।
satyadṛṣṭau prasannāyām asatye kṣayam āgate ।।

nirvikalpacid acchātmā sa ātmā samavāpyate ।
nāsattā yasya no sattā na sukhaṃ nāpi duḥkhitā ।।

bhāvanāyām avidyāyām । vimarśena svātmavicāreṇa । kathambhūtena । svaprasādena svātmaprasādenotpanneneti śeṣaḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtena । vilāsinā vistārayuktena । asaṃsaṅge anāsaktau । satyaviṣayā dṛṣṭiḥ satyadṛṣṭiḥ । tasyām prasannāyām । siddhāyām iti yāvat । asatye asatyabhūte dṛśye ity arthaḥ । nirvikalpaḥ dṛśyaviṣayavikalpaniṣkrāntā yā cit tadrūpaḥ । acchaḥ ātmā svarūpaṃ yasya । na tu acidrūpadehādisvarūpa ity arthaḥ । ato nāvidyānāśasya vaiphalyam iti bhāvaḥ । kīdṛśo ḥsāv ātmety apekṣāyām āha nāsatteti । sarveṣām ātmatvena sphuraṇāt । na hi kaścin nāham asmīti bravīti । bruvāṇaś copahāsapātram eva । tathā sattā no bhavati । bāhyāntaḥkaraṇāviṣayatvāt śaśaśṛṅgavat । sukham lakṣaṇayā sukhitā । na bhavati । sukhāder antaḥkaraṇādhikaraṇatvād । anyathā suṣuptādāv api bhānaprasaṅgāt । duḥkhitā duḥkhādhikaraṇatvam । na bhavati ।।

punaḥ kiṃ tatrāsti ity । atrāha

kevalaṃ kevalībhāvo yasyāntar upalabhyate ।
abhavyayā bhāvanayā na cittendriyadṛṣṭibhiḥ ।।

samyagjñānayuktena puruṣeṇa । kevalībhāvaḥ śuddhacinmātratāṃ vinā samastābhāvaḥ । upacārāl labhyate ity uktiḥ । labdhaikarūpasya labhyatāyogāt । paramārthas tu labhyānapekṣam । labdhṛtvam api tatra na yuktam ity alam vikalpāpādikayā vācā । tanmuvraṇayā vā abhavyayā bhāvanayā na labhyate । cittendriyadṛṣṭibhiś ca na labhyate ।।

ātmano ḥnanyabhūtābhir api yaḥ parivarjitaḥ ।
vāsanābhir anantābhir vyomeva vanarājibhiḥ ।।

yaḥ ātmā । ātmanaḥ ananyabhūtābhir api svasvarūpabhūtābhir api । vāsanābhiḥ parivarjitaḥ bhavati । śuddhacinmātrasvarūpatvāt । vāsanānāṃ cātmarūpatvaṃ tadviṣayatvaṃ vināsiddhabhāvaprayuktam eva jñeyam । na hi cinmātrāviṣayīkṛtā vāsanā vāsanā bhavati । viṣayīkṛtiś ca svasambandhina eva yuktā । sambandhaś ca vicāritaḥ san ekatāyāṃ viśrāmyati । dvitve tu virodhalabdhasiddheḥ dvitvād eva sambandhānupapatteḥ । na hi viruddhayoḥ tamaḥprakāśayoḥ sambandhaḥ yukta ity alam bahunā । yaḥ kim iva । yathā vyoma vanarājibhiḥ parivarjitaḥ bhavati ।।

nanu yadi kevalaḥ sa evātmāsti tarhi dṛśyarūpaḥ bandhaḥ kuta āgata ity । atrāha

sandigdhāyāṃ yathā rajjvāṃ sarpatvaṃ tadvad eva hi ।
cidākāśātmanā bandhas tv abaddhenaiva kalpitaḥ ।।

yathā puruṣeṇa sandigdhāyāṃ rajjvāṃ sarpatvam kalpyate । tadvad eva cidākāśātmanā cidākāśasvarūpeṇātmanā । bandhaḥ dṛśyākhyo bandhaḥ । kalpitaḥ kalpanayā sampāditaḥ ।।

nanu kalpita eṣa bandhaḥ kathaṃ naśyatīty । atrāha

kalpitaṃ kalpitaṃ vastu pratikalpanayānyayā ।
tad evānyatvam ādatte kham ahorātrayor iva ।।

kalpitaṃ kalpitaṃ vastu sarvaṃ kalpitavastu । anyayā svasmād bhinnayā । pratikalpanayā । kham iva । yathā kham ahorātrayoḥ tad eva sat anyatām ādatte । tathety arthaḥ । ataḥ pratikalpanayaiva kalpitasya nāśa iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanv atucchatvādiguṇaviśiṣṭaḥ kalpito nāstīti kathaṃ saḥ kalpyate yena tucchatvādiguṇaviśiṣṭasaṃsārakalpanā naśyati । na ca kalpanāṃ vinā kalpanāyāḥ nāśaḥ śakyakriyaḥ ayasaḥ ivāyo vinety । atrāha

yad atuccham anāyāsam anupādhi gatabhramam ।
tat tatkalpanayā tādṛk tat sukhāyaiva kalpate ।।

yat vastu । atuccham tucchaguṇarahitam । anāyāsam āyāsasādhyatvarahitam । anupādhi upādhitvenābhimatasyāpi tattāvyabhicārāt upādhirahitam । gatabhramam śuddhasatyabodhasvarūpatvāt bhramasparśarahitam । tatkalpanayā tasyātucchatvādeḥ kalpanayā eva । tādṛk atucchādirūpam । śuddhe svarūpe tucchatvātucchatvādisāpekṣaśabdāvakāśābhāvāt । nanu tarhi tad api heyam evety । atrāha tat sukhāyaiveti । tat atucchatvādiguṇakaṃ vastu kalpitam api । sukhāyaiva tucchatvātucchatvarahitaśuddhasvarūpaviśrāntaya eva । tathā cātucchatvādiguṇakakalpanayā pratipakṣabhūtayā tucchatvādiguṇakakalpanā nāśayituṃ śākyeti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu satyabhūtasya dṛśyarūpasya bandhasya kathaṃ kalpanāmātreṇa nāśaḥ śakyakriyaḥ ity । atrāha

śūnya eva kusūle ḥntaḥ siṃho ḥstīti bhayaṃ yathā ।
śūnya eva śarīre ḥntar baddho ḥsmīti bhayaṃ tathā ।।

kusūlaḥ siṃhabandhanārthaṃ yantrarūpaṃ koṣṭhakam । dṛśyarūpo bandhaḥ satyo ḥpi bhavatu । tathāpi paramārthataḥ śuddhacidrūpasya bhavataḥ saḥ bandhakārī na bhavati । na hy ambaraṃ rajjubhiḥ badhyate iti bhāvaḥ ।।

yathā śūnye kusūle ḥntaḥ prekṣya siṃho na labhyate ।
tathā saṃsārabandhārhaḥ prekṣitaḥ san na labhyate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nanu tarhi idaṃ jagat ayam aham ity evam bandhabadhyarūpā pratītiḥ katham astīty । atrāha

idaṃ jagad ayaṃ cāham itīyam bhrāntir utthitā ।
bālānāṃ śyāmale kāle chāyā vaitālikī yathā ।।

śyāmale kāle rātrau । idaṃ jagat ayam aham ity evaṃrūpā pratītiḥ । bhrāntir evotthitā bhavati iti piṇḍārthaḥ ।।

nanu etādṛśī bhrāntiḥ katham utthitety । atrāha

kalpanāvaśato jantor bhāvābhāvāḥ śubhāśubhāḥ ।
kṣaṇād asattām āyānti sattām api punaḥ punaḥ ।।

kalpanāvaśataḥ svavikalpavaśataḥ ।।

etad eva viśeṣataḥ kathayati

mātaiva gṛhiṇībhāvagṛhītā kaṇṭhalambinī ।
karoti gṛhiṇīkāryaṃ suratānandadāyinī ।।

bhrameṇeti śeṣaḥ ।।

kāntaiva mātṛbhāvena gṛhītākaṇṭhalambinī ।
dūraṃ vismārayaty eva manmathonmādabhāvanām ।।

ihāpi bhrameṇeti śeṣaḥ । iyaṃ cāvasthā madhyamapāpiprabhṛtīnāṃ jñeyā । mahāpāpināṃ tu atrāpi ratir eva jāyate ।।

phalitam āha

bhāvānusāriphaladam padārthaugham avekṣya ca ।
na jñeneha padārtheṣu rūpam ekam udīryate ।।

jñena padārthatattvajñena puruṣeṇa । padārthaugham bhāvānusāriphalaṃ dadātīti tādṛśam । avekṣya । padārtheṣv ekaṃ rūpaṃ na udīryate na kathyate ।।

dṛḍhabhāvanayā ceto yad yathā bhāvayaty alam ।
tat tatphalaṃ tadākāraṃ tāvatkālam prapaśyati ।।

cetaḥ । dṛḍhabhāvanayā yathā bhāvayati anusandhatte । tatphalam bhāvanāphalabhūtam । tāvatkālam tasmin samaye । svapnaś cātra dṛṣṭāntatvena jñeyaḥ ।।

siddhāntaṃ kathayati

na tad asti na yat satyaṃ na tad asti na yan mṛṣā ।
yad yathā yena nirṇītaṃ tat tathā tena lakṣyate ।।

nirṇīṭam bhāvitam । anyathā ekam eva vastu ekasya harṣadam anyasya duḥkhadaṃ na syād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

bhāvitākāśamātaṅgaṃ vyomahastitayā manaḥ ।
vyomakānanamātaṅgīṃ vyomasthām anudhāvati ।।

bhāvitākāśamātaṅgam sat । vyomahastitayā vyomahastibhāvena । vyomahastī bhūtveti yāvat । vyomakānanamātaṅgīm anudhāvati । kānanādhārabhūte vyomni tiṣṭhatīti tādṛśīm ।।

paramaphalitam āha

tasmāt saṅkalpam eva tvaṃ sarvabhāvamayātmakam ।
tyaja rāghava susvasthaḥ svātmanaiva bhavātmani ।।

sarvabhāvamayaḥ sarvapadārthasvarūpaḥ । saṅkalpa eva hi bahiḥ nānākāraiḥ sphurati । tyaja mā prādurbhāvaya । prādurbhūte ḥpi upekṣām eva kurv ity arthaḥ । na hi sarvathā tyāgaḥ videhamuktiṃ yāvat śakyakriyaḥ ।।

nanu katham āgacchantaṃ saṅkalpaṃ tyajāmīty । atrāha

maṇir hi pratibimbānām pratiṣedhakriyām prati ।
aśakto jaḍabhāvena na tu rāma bhavādṛśaḥ ।।

jaḍabhāvena jaḍatayā । bhavādṛśaḥ tvādṛkcetanaḥ । saṅkalpatyāgo hi saṃvedanasādhyaḥ । tac ca tavāsty eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

tyāgopāyaṃ kathayati

yad yan manomaṇau rāma taveha pratibimbati ।
tad avastv iti nirṇīya mā tenāgaccha rañjanām ।।

rañjanām uparaktatvam ।।

upāyāntaraṃ kathayati

tad eva satyam iti vāpy abhinnam paramātmanaḥ ।
manvānas tvam anādyantam bhāvayātmānam ātmanā ।।

sarvasya paramātmanaḥ abhinnatvabhāvanena hi anādyantātmabhāvanam eva sampadyate ।।

cetasi pratibimbanti ye bhāvās tava rāghava ।
rañjayantv anyasaktātman mā te tvāṃ sphaṭikaṃ yathā ।।

he rāghava । anyasmin bhāvebhyaḥ bhinnasvarūpe paramātmani । saktaḥ ātmā manaḥ yasya । anyathā pratibimbitabhāvarañjanābhāvo na yukta iti bhāvaḥ । yathā anyarāgayuktaṃ sphaṭikam anyarāgakṛtā rañjanā na rañjayati ।।

nanu kathaṃ rañjanābhāvo dehaṃ tāvat śakya ity । atra sargāntaślokena kathayati

sphaṭikam apamalaṃ yathā viśanti prakaṭatayā navarañjanā vicitrāḥ ।
iha hi vimananaṃ tathā viśantu prakaṭatayā bhuvaṇaiṣaṇā bhavantam ।।

vimananam mananākhyamanodharmarahitam । yathā nirmalaṃ sphaṭikaṃ vicitrāḥ rañjanā viśanti । tathā mananāparaparyāyānusandhānarāhityena śuddham bhavantam api padārthasaṅkalpanārūpāḥ rañjanā viśantv iti piṇḍārthaḥ । lepākāriṇī rañjanā yady āyāti tadā na kācid dhānir iti bhāvaḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe ekaviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

pūrvoktam evārthaṃ sthitiprakaraṇavācyatayā sthitatvāt punar api kathayati

jantoḥ kṛtavicārasya vigaladvṛtticetasaḥ ।
mananaṃ tyajato jñatvāt kiñcit parigatātmanaḥ ।।

dṛśyaṃ santyajato heyam upādeyam upeyuṣaḥ ।
draṣṭāram paśyato dṛśyam adraṣṭāram apaśyataḥ ।।

asuptasya pare tattve jāgarūkasya jīvataḥ ।
suptasya ghanasammohamaye saṃsāravartmani ।।

paryantātyantavairasyād araseṣu raseṣv api ।
bhogeṣv ābhogaramyeṣu nīrasasya nirāśiṣaḥ ।।

vrajaty ātmāmbhasaikatvaṃ jīrṇajāḍye manasy alam ।
galaty apagatāsaṅge himapūra ivātape ।।

taraṅgitāsu kallolajālalolāntarāsu ca ।
śāmyantīṣv atha tṛṣṇāsu nadīṣv iva ghanātyaye ।।

saṃsāravāsanājāle khagajāla ivākhunā ।
troṭite cādṛḍhagranthiśleṣe vairasyaraṃhasā ।।

katakam phalam āsādya yathā vāri prasīdati ।
tathā vijñānavaśataḥ svabhāvaḥ samprasīdati ।।

jantoḥ puruṣasya । vijñānavaśataḥ śuddhātmajñānavaśena । svabhāvaḥ svasvarūpam । tathā prasīdati nirmalībhavati । tathā katham । yathā katakam phalam āsādya vāri prasīdati । keṣu satsu prasīdatīty apekṣāyām āha vrajaty ātmetyādi । apagatāsaṅge naṣṭāsaktyākhyadoṣe । jīrṇajāḍye jāḍyanirgate । ata eva galati galanonmukhe । manasi । ātmāmbhasā paramātmākhyajalena saha । ekatvaṃ vrajati sati । sthite himapūre iva । tṛṣṇāsu śāmyantīṣu satīṣu । taraṅgitāsu vṛddhiyuktāsu । kallolajālaiḥ vikalpasvarūpaiḥ kallolasamūhaiḥ । lolam antaram yāsām । tādṛśīṣu । yathā tāḥ ghanātyaye śaradi । punaḥ kasmin sati । saṃsāravāsanājāle vairasyaraṃhasā ākhunā iva khagajāle troṭite sati । kathambhūte । granthīnām kāmādirūpāṇāṃ granthīnām । śleṣaḥ sambandhaḥ yasya । jantoḥ kathambhūtasya । kṛtaḥ vicāraḥ ko ḥhaṃ kasya saṃsāra ity evaṃrūpaḥ vivekaḥ yena । vigaladvṛtticetaḥ yasya । jñasyaiva hi mananatyāge śaktir astīti jñatvād ity uktam । kiñcit parokṣatayā । na tv aparokṣatayety arthaḥ । upādeyam arthāt śuddhadraṣṭṛrūpam । draṣṭāram draṣṭṛrūpam । adraṣṭāram draṣṭṛvyatiriktam । raseṣv api suptasyeti yojyam । nirāśiṣaḥ āśārahitasya ।।

anyat kiṃ tasya sampatsyate ity । atrāha

nīrāgaṃ nirupāsaṅgaṃ nirdvandvaṃ nirupāśrayam ।
viniryāti mano mohād vihagaḥ pañjarād iva ।।

nirupāsaṅgam āsaktirahitam । nirupāśrayam nirapekṣam । mohāt anātmany ātmābhimānarūpād avicārāt ।।

śāntasandehadaurātmyaṃ gatakautukavibhramam ।
paripūrṇāntaraṃ cetaḥ pūrṇendur iva rājate ।।

kautukam atra padārthaviṣayaṃ jñeyam । paripūrṇam sahajānandanirbharam । antaram yasya ।।

janitottamasaundaryā dūrodastanatonnatā ।
samatodeti sarvatra śāntavāta ivārṇave ।।

janitam uttamaṃ saundaryam yayā । samatayā hi puruṣaḥ sadaiva prasannavadano bhavati । dūrodastā natonnatā bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ । sā ।।

andhakāramayī mūḍhā jāḍyajarjaritāntarā ।
tanutām eti saṃsāravāsaneva prage kṣapā ।।

ivaśabdaḥ kṣapety anena sambadhyate ।।

dṛṣṭacidbhāskarā prajñāpadminī puṇyapallavā ।
vikasaty amaloddyotā prātar dyaur iva rūpiṇī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

prajñā hṛdayahāriṇyo bhuvanāhlādanakṣamāḥ ।
sattvalakṣmyaḥ pravartante sakalendor ivāṃśavaḥ ।।

sattvalakṣmyaḥ sattvaguṇasampadaḥ ।।

upasaṃhāraṃ karoti

bahunātra kim uktena jñātajñeyo mahāmatiḥ ।
nodeti naiva yāty astam abhūtākāśakośavat ।।

na udeti astaṃ nāyāti cinmātrākhyāt svasvarūpān na cyavata ity arthaḥ । abhūtākāśakośavat paramākāśamadhyavat ।।

vicāraṇāparijñātasvabhāvasyoditātmanaḥ ।
anukampyā bhavanty ete brahmaviṣṇvindraśaṅkarāḥ ।।

vicāraṇayā parijñātaḥ svabhāvaḥ svasvarūpaṃ yena । anukampyāḥ teṣv api sṛṣṭinirmāṇādikṣobhadarśanāt asya dayā jāyate ity arthaḥ ।।

prakaṭākāram apy antar nirahaṅkāracetasam ।
nāpnuvanti vikalpās tam mṛgatṛṣṇāmbv ivaiṇakāḥ ।।

nāpnuvanti svavaśaṃ na kurvanti । prakaṭākārasya cāhaṅkārarāhityam āścaryakāry eva ।।

taraṅgavad amī lokāḥ prayānty āyānti cābhitaḥ ।
kroḍīkuruta ātmotthe na jñam maraṇajanmanī ।।

kroḍīkurutaḥ vaśīkurutaḥ । dehābhimānābhāvena tatsthamṛtijanmābhimānābhāvāt ।।

āvirbhāvatirobhāvau saṃsāro netaraḥ kramaḥ ।
iti tābhyāṃ samāloke ramate na sa khidyate ।।

iti evaṃrūpābhyām । tābhyām āvirbhāvatirobhāvābhyām । saḥ । samāloke tattattvaprakāśe sati । ramate । jñātavastutattvo hi vastubhiḥ ramata eva na khidyate । ajñātatattvasyaiva rajjvādiṣu sarpādibhayakṛtakhedadarśanāt ।।

na jāyate na mriyate kumbhe kumbhanabho yathā ।
bhūṣite dūṣite vāpi dehe tadvad ihātmavān ।।

dehābhimānābhāvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

viveka udite śīte mithyābhramabharoditā ।
kṣīyate vāsanā sābhre mṛgatṛṣṇā marāv iva ।।

mithyārūpaḥ yaḥ bhramabharaḥ । sābhre hi marau mṛgatṛṣṇā kṣīyata eva । tāpa eva tasyā utthānāt ।।

ko ḥhaṃ katham idaṃ veti yāvan na pravicāritam ।
saṃsārāḍambaraṃ tāvad andhakāropamaṃ sthitam ।।

andhakāro ḥpi kiṃrūpo ḥyam iti vicāraḥ । tāvad eva tiṣṭhati ।।

mithyābhramabharodbhūtaṃ śarīram padam āpadām ।
ātmabhāvanayā nedaṃ yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

yaḥ idaṃ deham । ātmabhāvanayā na paśyati । saḥ paśyati samyak paśyati iti piṇḍārthaḥ ।।

deśakālavaśotthāni na mameti gatabhramam ।
śarīrasukhaduḥkhāni yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

mama śuddhacinmātrasya mama ।।

ātmānam itarac caiva dṛśā nityāvibhinnayā ।
sarvaṃ cijjyotir eveti yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

cijjyotiḥ śuddhacitprakāśarūpam ।।

apāraparyantanabhodikkālādi kriyānvitam ।
aham eveti sarvatra yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

nabhaś ca dik ca kālaś ca । te ādiḥ yasya jagataḥ । tat nabhodikkālādi apāraparyantam pāraparyantarahitaṃ ca tat । nabhodikkālādirūpaṃ jagat aham evāsmi । ahantāsārasya cinmātratattvasyaiva sarvamayatvena sthitatvāt । anyathāham iti sarvatra na sphuret । jaḍeṣv adarśane ḥpi cetanavat sattābhāktvāviśeṣāt । tatrāpi tatsphuraṇānumānasya śakyatvāt na sarvatrety asyānupapatteḥ । kathambhūtaṃ tat । ādiśabdākṣiptāyā api kriyāyāḥ pṛthak nirdeśaḥ prādhānyakhyāpanārthaḥ । sarvatra sarveṣu deśeṣu kāleṣu ca । yaḥ paśyati saḥ paśyati । nānya ity arthaḥ ।।

vālāgralakṣabhāgāt tu koṭiśaḥ parikalpitaḥ ।
ahaṃ sūkṣma iti vyāpī yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

sūkṣmasya vyāpitvam āścaryāvaham । sūkṣmatvaṃ cātra bāhyāntaḥkaraṇātītatvena draṣṭavyam ।।

sarvaśaktir anantātmā sarvabhāvāntarasthitaḥ ।
advitīyaś cid ity antar yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

cit cidātmā । sarvaśaktiḥ anyathā nānārūpaṃ jagat na prādurbhavet । anantātmā antasyāpi tasminn eva nigīrṇatvāt tadrahitaḥ । na hi nigīrṇa eva nigarituḥ rūpam ācchādayituṃ śaktaḥ । sarveṣām bhāvānām antare sthitaḥ sarvabhāvāntarasthitaḥ । anyathāham iti na sphuret । advitīyaḥ dvitīyatvena matasyāpi tadrūpatvānapāyāt dvitīyarahitaḥ । antaḥ manasi । yaḥ paśyati sa paśyatīti ।।

ādhivyādhibhayodvigno jarāmaraṇajanmavān ।
deho nāham iti prājño yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

prājñaḥ śuddhacinmātratattve ātmatvaniścayavān ।।

tiryag ūrdhvam adhastāc ca vyāpako mahimā mama ।
na dvitīyo mamāstīti yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

mama śuddhacinmātrarūpasya mama । na tu dehādirūpasya ।।

mayi sarvam idam protaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva ।
cittantur aham eveti yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

kathaṃ tvayi sarvam protam ity । atrāha cittantur iti । tantau hi muktā protāḥ bhavanti । tantutvaṃ ca citaḥ vyāpakatayā sūkṣmatayā ca jñeyam ।।

nāhaṃ na cānyad astīha brahmaivāsti na cāsti tat ।
itthaṃ sadasator madhyaṃ yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

iha loke । aham paricchinnadehādirūpaḥ aham । nāsmi । anyat matto bhinnatvena sthitaṃ jagat । na cāsti । suṣuptau adarśanāt । brahma vyāpakaṃ cinmātratattvam । evāsti paramārthataḥ sattām bhajate । sarvathābhāvasya vaktum aśakyatvāt । na hi nirādiṣṭo no bhramaḥ sambhavati । tat brahma । bāhyāntaḥkaraṇātītatvāt । sadasatoḥ madhyam sandhibhūtaṃ śuddhacinmātrākhyaṃ vastu । yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

yan nāma kiñcit trailokyaṃ sa eko ḥvayavo mama ।
taraṅgo ḥbdhāv ivety antar yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

mama śuddhacinmātrarūpasya mama । svapne hi cinmātrāvayavabhūtaṃ jagat sarvo ḥnubhavati ।।

śocyā pālyā mayaiveyaṃ svaseyam me kanīyasī ।
trilokī pelavety uccair yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

pelavā nāśabhīruḥ । kanīyasī svasā cedṛśy eva bhavati ।।

ātmatāparate tvattāmatte yasya mahātmanaḥ ।
bhāvād uparate nūnaṃ sa paśyati sulocanaḥ ।।

bhāvāt manasaḥ । sarvatra cinmātratvadarśanād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

cetyānupātarahitaṃ cidbhairavamayaṃ vapuḥ ।
āpūritajagajjālaṃ yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

cetyānupātarahitaḥ yaḥ cidbhairavaḥ sarvagrāsakatvāt cidākhyaḥ bhairavaḥ । tanmayaṃ vapuḥ svarūpam ।।

sukhaṃ duḥkham bhavo ḥbhāvo vivekakalanāś ca yāḥ ।
ahaṃ na veti nūnaṃ vā paśyan na parihīyate ।।

sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhavaḥ abhāvaḥ vivekakalanāś cāham asmi iti paśyan । etan na vāsmi iti vā paśyan । na parihīyate na hānim prāpnoti । ubhayathāpi śuddhacinmātrasvarūpatvāpteḥ । na hi śuddhacinmātraṃ vinā kaścid vyāpakaḥ uttīrṇo vā bhavati ।।

svātmasattāparāpūrṇe jagaty anyena varjite ।
kim me heyaṃ kim ādeyam iti paśyan sadṛg naraḥ ।।

svātmanaḥ śuddhacinmātrarūpasya svātmanaḥ । yā sattā sphūrtirūpā sattā । tayā parāpūrṇe sāratvena sthitatvāt nirbharite । anyathāham iti sphuraṇāyogāt । tathā anyena cinmātravyatiriktena । svātmanaḥ heyatvāyogāt na kiñcid apīty arthaḥ । kim ādeyam bhavati । svātmanaḥ sarvadā prāptatvāt na kiñcid apīty arthaḥ । naraḥ । anye ḥndhā ity arthaḥ ।।

apratarkyam anābhāsaṃ sanmātram idam ity alam ।
heyopādeyakalanā yasya kṣīṇā namāmi tam ।।

idam jagat । apratarkyam tarkitum aśakyam । anābhāsam śānte svasvarūpe sthitatvād ābhāsarahitam । iti anena niścayena । heyopādeyakalanā kṣīṇā । sa eva sarvebhya utkṛṣṭa iti bhāvaḥ ।।

ya ākāśavad ekātmā sarvabhāvagato ḥpi san ।
na bhāvarañjanām eti sa mahātmā maheśvaraḥ ।।

yaḥ puruṣaḥ । ākāśavat ekātmā sarvavyāpakātmā । sarvabhāvagataḥ api san śarīrayātrānimitteṣu sarveṣu padārtheṣu vyavahārayukto ḥpi san । rañjanām harṣāmarṣarūpāṃ rañjanām । saḥ mahātmā mahāpuruṣaḥ । maheśvaraḥ bhavati mahāśaktiyuktatvāt ।।

tamaḥprakāśakalanāmuktaḥ kālātmatāṃ gataḥ ।
yaḥ somyaḥ susamaḥ svasthas taṃ naumi padam āgatam ।।

yaḥ । tamaḥprakāśayoḥ jāḍyacittvayoḥ । yā kalanā । kālasya kriyāvaicitryarūpasya kālasya । ātmatām sattādāyakatvena svarūpatām । svasthaḥ svasvarūpe eva sthitaḥ । tam padam āgataṃ naumi । apūrvaś cātra sūrya uktaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati

yasyodayāstamayasaṅkalanākalāsu citrāsu cāruvibhavāsu jagadgatāsu ।
vṛttiḥ samaiva sakalaikagater anantā tasmai namaḥ paramabodhavate śivāya ।।

sakalaikagateḥ samastaikaśaraṇasya । cāruvibhavāsu praśastasāmarthyayuktāsu । citrāsu nānāvidhāsu । udayāstamayayoḥ yāḥ saṅkalanāḥ ghaṭṭanāḥ । tadrūpāsu jagadgatāsu kalāsu । anantatvaṃ cātra darḍhyatāpekṣam uktam । tasmai paramabodhavate parātmatattvabodhayuktāya । śivāya śivībhūtāya puruṣāya । śivaś ca samavṛttiḥ sakalaikagatiḥ paramabodharūpaś ca bhavatīti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ mokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe dvāviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ । punar api vivekina eva māhātmyaṃ kathayati

sa uttamapadālambī cakrabhramavad āsthitaḥ ।
śarīranagare rājyaṃ kurvann api na lipyate ।।

uttamam padam cinmātrākhyaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sthānam । ālambata ity uttamapadālambī । cakrabhramavat āsthitaḥ samantāt sthitaḥ । niranusandhānaṃ ceṣṭāyāṃ sthita iti yāvat । saḥ jīvanmuktaḥ । śarīranagare rājyaṃ kurvann api na lipyate । tajjaiḥ sukhaduḥkhaiḥ na gṛhyate ity arthaḥ । rājāpi uttamapadālambī sarvatra bhraman nagare rājyaṃ kurvan bhavati ।।

tasyeyam bhogamokṣārthaṃ tajjñasyopavanopamā ।
sukhāyaiva na duḥkhāya svaśarīramahāpurī ।।

sukhāyaiva ātyantikamokṣarūpasukhasādhanatvāt । na duḥkhāya duḥkhalepābhāvāt ।।

atra śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

nagarītvaṃ śarīrasya kathaṃ nāma mahāmune ।
etāṃ cādhivasan yogī kathaṃ rājyasukhaikabhāk ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaram āha

ramyeyaṃ dehanagarī rāma sarvaguṇānvitā ।
jñasyānantavilāsāḍhyā svālokārkaprakāśitā ।।

svālokaḥ ātmaprakāśaḥ । tena prakāśitā parāmarśadvāreṇa svam prati prākaṭyaṃ nītā ।।

sarvaguṇatvam eva kathayati

netravātāyanoddyotaprakāśabhuvanāntarā ।
karapratolīvistāraprāptapādopajaṅgalā ।।

netre eva vātāyane । tayoḥ yaḥ uddyotaḥ prakāśaḥ । tena prakāśāni prakaṭāni । bhuvanāntarāṇi bhuvanamadhyāni yasyām । sā । nagaryām api nagaradvāranirmitaiḥ vātāyanaiḥ bhuvanāntarāṇi dṛśyāni bhavanti । karau eva pratolyau viśikhe । tābhyām prāptau pādāv eva upajaṅgalau jaṅgalasamīpadeśau yasyāḥ । sā । nagaryaś ca upajaṅgalaṃ tāvat pratolī bhavati ।।

romarājilatāgulmā tvagaṭṭālakamālitā ।
gulphagulguluviśrāntajaṅghorustambhamaṇḍalā ।।

tvag evāṭṭālakam prākāraḥ । gulguluḥ stambhādhārabhūtā śilā ।।

rekhāvibhaktapādograśilāprathamanirmitā ।
carmamarmasirāsārasandhisīmā manoramā ।।

rekhābhyāṃ vibhakte ye । tayoḥ prathamaṃ nirmitā । prathamanirmāṇe hi kṛtavibhāgāḥ śilāḥ sthāpyante । carmamarmasirāsāraḥ carmamarmasirāsamūha eva । sandhisīmāḥ sandhimaryādāḥ yasyāḥ ।।

ūrudvayakavāṭāgranirmitopasthanirgamā ।
kacatkacāvalīkācadalapracchādanāvṛtā ।।

ūrudvayam eva kavāṭe । tābhyāṃ nirmitaḥ kavāṭaracanāyuktaḥ kṛtaḥ । upastha eva gudasthānam eva । nirgamaḥ dvāradeśaḥ yasyāḥ । kacantī yā kacāvalī । sā eva kācadalaiḥ nirmitam pracchādanam । tenāvṛtā ।।

bhrūlalāṭāsyasacchāyavadanodyānaśobhitā ।
dṛṣṭipātotpalākīrṇakapolavipulasthalā ।।

bhrūlalāṭāsyaiḥ sacchāyam yat vadanam ।।

vakṣaḥsthalasaraḥsyūtakucapaṅkajakorakā ।
ghanaromāvalicchannaskandhakrīḍāśiloccayā ।।

ghanaromāvalicchannā cāsau skandhakrīḍāśiloccayā ca ।।

udaraśvabhranikṣiptasvanneṣṭabhakṣyakarparā ।
dīrghakaṇṭhabilodgīrṇavātasaṃrambhaśabditā ।।

udaraśvabhre udaragarte । nikṣiptāni yāni svannāni śobhanānnāni । taiḥ । tadvyājeneti yāvat । iṣṭabhakṣyakarparā iṣṭabhakṣyabhagnapātram yasyāḥ । rājanagaryām api iṣṭabhakṣyapātrāṇi bhavanti । dīrgham yat kaṇṭhabilam । yaḥ vātaḥ । tasya yaḥ saṃrambhaḥ । tena śabditā śabdayuktā kṛtā । nagaryām api bileṣu vātaśabdo bhavati ।।

hṛdayāpaṇanirṇītayathāprāptārthabhūṣitā ।
anārataṃ navadvārapravahatprāṇanāgarā ।।

hṛdayam evāpaṇaḥ niṣadyā । tasmin nirṇītā upādeyatvena niścitāḥ । ye yathāprāptārthāḥ svapravāhāgatārthāḥ । nagaryā api āpaṇeṣu arthā nirṇīyante ।।

āsyasphārakhadādṛṣṭadantāsthiśakalākulā ।
mukhakhadābhramajjihvācillācarvitabhojanā ।।

nagaryām api khadāsu māṃsabhakṣakaiḥ tyaktāni asthiśakalāni bhavanti । cillā pakṣiviśeṣaḥ ।।

romaśaṣpabharacchannakarṇakoṭarakūpakā ।
sphikśṛṅkhalāñcitopāntapṛṣṭavistīrṇajaṅgalā ।।

sphijau eva śṛṅkhale । tābhyām añcitopāntam ramyopāntam । pṛṣṭam eva vistīrṇajaṅgalam yasyāḥ । nagaryā api jaṅgalasandhiṣu caurādipratibandhārthaṃ śṛṅgalāḥ bhavanti ।।

gudocchinnāraghaṭṭāntaruddhṛtānantakardamā ।
cittodyānamahīvalgadātmacintāvarāṅganā ।।

guda evocchinnāraghaṭṭaḥ troṭitāraghaṭṭayantraḥ । tenāntaḥ antaḥpradeśāt । uddhṛtaḥ niṣkāsitaḥ । arthāt śakṛdrūpaḥ kardamaḥ yasyāḥ । nagaryā api kardamam uddharanti । jñacitte hi rātrindinam ātmacintā eva sphurati ।।

dhīvaratrādṛḍhābaddhacapalendriyamarkaṭā ।
vadanodyānahasanapuṣpodgamamanoramā ।।

jño hi dhīrajjvā capalendriyāṇi badhnāti । udyāne ca puṣpodgamo yukta eva ।।

svaśarīrapurī jñasya sarvasaubhāgyasundarī ।
sukhāyaiva na duḥkhāya paramāya hitāya ca ।।

svaśarīrapurī proktasarvapurīguṇā nijaśarīranagarī । paramāya hitāya mokṣarūpāyety arthaḥ ।।

ajñasyeyaṃ sukhadāsty atha vā nety । atrāha

ajñasyeyam anantānāṃ duḥkhānāṃ kośamālikā ।
jñasya tv iyam anantānāṃ sukhānāṃ kośamālikā ।।

kośamālikā bhāṇḍāgāramālā । anantaduḥkhotpādikety arthaḥ । ajñātaśuddhatattvasya tasyaitadarthaṃ rātrindinaṃ santāpabhāktvāt iti bhāvaḥ । nanu tarhi jñasyāpi īdṛśy eva syād ity । atrāha jñasya tv iti । tuśabdaḥ vyatirekadyotakaḥ । jñātaśuddhātmatattvasya tasyaitadarthaṃ santāpabhāktvābhāvāt । na hy anyārtham anyaḥ santāpabhāg bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu tarhi nāśakāle iyaṃ jñasya duḥkhadā bhaviṣyatīty । atrāha

na kiñcid asyāṃ naṣṭāyāṃ jñasya naṣṭam arindama ।
sthitāyāṃ saṃsthitaṃ sarvaṃ teneyaṃ jñasukhāvahā ।।

etadvyatiriktaśuddhacinmātrasvarūpatvād iti bhāvaḥ । nanu tarhi sthitikāle ḥpy asyānayā na kiñcit prayojanam ity । atrāha sthitāyām iti । sarvaṃ saṃsthitam samastajīvanmuktyupayogikāryasādhakatvād iti bhāvaḥ । upasaṃhāraṃ karoti teneyam iti ।।

nanv asyāḥ kaiścid rathatvam apy uktam ity । atrāha

yad enāṃ jñaḥ samāruhya saṃsāre viharaty alam ।
aśeṣabhogamokṣārthaṃ teneyaṃ jñarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

enām śarīrapurīm ।।

śabdarūparasasparśagandhabandhuśriyo yataḥ ।
anayaiva hi labhyante teneyaṃ jñasya lābhadā ।।

nanu śabdādilābhena jñasya ko lābho ḥstīti cen । śabdādidvāreṇa paramātmatattvaśaktinicayajñānarūpasya lābhasya sthitatvāt ।।

sukhaduḥkhakriyājālaṃ yadaiṣodvahati svayam ।
tadaiṣā rāma sarvatra sarvavastubharakṣamā ।।

eṣā dehanagarī । jño hi sukhādikaṃ śarīrasyaiva jānāti na svasya ।।

tasyāṃ śarīrapuryāṃ hi rājyaṃ kurvan gatabhramaḥ ।
jñas tiṣṭhati gatavyagraṃ svapuryām iva vāsavaḥ ।।

gatabhramaḥ etām prati ahamabhimānarahitaḥ । gatavyagram nirākulam ।।

na kṣipaty avaṭāṭope manomattaturaṅgamam ।
na lobhadvandvarūpāya prajñāputrīm prayacchati ।।

avaṭāṭope viṣayarūpe śvabhrāḍambare । lobhākhyo yaḥ dvandvarūpaḥ । tasmai । prajñāputrīṃ na prayacchati । lobhagrastām prajñāṃ na karotīti bhāvaḥ ।।

ajñānapararāṣṭraṃ ca na randhraṃ tv asya paśyati ।
saṃsārāribhayasyāntarmūlāny eṣa nikṛntati ।।

ajñānam eva pararāṣṭram lakṣaṇayā ripubhūto rājā । gamanasya tu kā kathā । randhram ।।

tṛṣṇāsāraparāvarte kāmasaṅkṣobhadurgrahe ।
na nimajjanti paryastasukhaduḥkhākṣadevane ।।

tṛṣṇāsārasya parāvartaḥ āvṛttiḥ yasmin । kāmasya yaḥ saṅkṣobhaḥ । paryastau preritau । yau sukhaduḥkhākṣau sukhaduḥkhe evākṣau । tayoḥ yat devanam krīḍanam । tatra na nimajjanti । rājño hi dyūtamajjanaṃ doṣa eva । akṣadevanam api tṛṣṇākāmavalitam eva bhavati ।।

karoty avirataṃ snānam bahir antar api kṣaṇāt ।
saritsaṅgamatīrtheṣu manorathagatiḥ kramāt ।।

bahiḥ bāhye । mana eva svādhīnatvāt rathaḥ । saḥ । antaḥ snānaṃ tu ciddhradanimajjanam eva jñeyam ।।

sakalākṣijanādṛśyaḥ puraprekṣāparāṅmukhaḥ ।
dhyānanāmni sukhaṃ nityaṃ tiṣṭhaty antaḥpurāntare ।।

purasya śarīrasya । nagarasya ca rājāpi sakalajanādṛśyaḥ puraprekṣāparāṅmukhaś caran pure tiṣṭhati । dhyānaṃ cātra svātmabhūtaśuddhacinmātratattvaparāmarśa eva jñeyaḥ ।।

sukhāvahaiṣā nagarī nityam pramuditātmanaḥ ।
bhogamokṣapradā divyā śakrasyevāmarāvatī ।।

jñasyeti śeṣaḥ ।।

sthitayā saṃsthitaṃ sarvaṃ kiñcin naṣṭaṃ na naṣṭayā ।
yayā puryā mahīpasya sā kathaṃ na sukhāvahā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vinaṣṭe dehanagare jñasya naṣṭaṃ na kiñcana ।
ākrāntakumbhakośasya khasya kumbhakṣaye yathā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vidyamānaṃ ghaṭaṃ vāyuḥ kila spṛśati nāsthitam ।
yathā tathaiva dehī svāṃ śarīranagarīm imām ।।

asthitam naṣṭam । dehī dehād vyatiriktam ātmānaṃ jānānaḥ tajjñaḥ ।।

atrastha eṣa bhagavān ātmā sarvagato ḥpi san ।
svavikalpakṛtām bhuktvā puṃstām adhigatātmadṛk ।।

kurvann api na kurvāṇaḥ samyak sarvakriyonmukhaḥ ।
kadācit prakṛtān sarvān kāryārthān adhitiṣṭhati ।।

atrasthaḥ dehasthaḥ । apiśabdaḥ sarvagatasya puṃstābhoge virodhaṃ dyotayati । adhigatātmadṛk tajjñaḥ । tasyaivaṃvidhatvāsambhavāt । kurvan śarīrādidvāreṇa kurvan । na kurvāṇaḥ nāhaṃ karteti niścayāt । kāryārthān karaṇīyāni prayojanāni । adhitiṣṭhati kartavyatvena niścinoti । prakṛtān pravāhāgatān । na tu svavimarśena kalpitān ।।

nanu yadi kadācid etat karoti tarhi anyadā kiṃ karotīty । atrāha

kadācil līlayālolaṃ vimānam adhirohati ।
anāhatagatiṃ kāntaṃ vihartum amalam manaḥ ।।

kadācid asau tajjñaḥ ātmalīlayā manaḥ vimānam manorūpaṃ vimānam । vihartum āntaraṃ vihāraṃ kartum । manovimānaṃ kathambhūtam । alolam cañcalatārahitam । punaḥ kathambhūtam । anāhatā kvacid apratihatā । tam । vimānaśabdāpekṣayā puṃstvam । amalam rāgādimalarahitam ।।

nanu tatra kiṃ karotīty । atrāha

tatrastho lokasundaryā satataṃ śītalāṅgayā ।
ramate nāma yo maitryā nityaṃ hṛdayasaṃsthayā ।।

saḥ tajjñaḥ tatrasthaḥ manovimānasthaḥ । lokasundaryā lokapriyayā । nityaṃ hṛdayasthayā satataṃ śītalāṅgayā maitryā maitryākhyayā striyā । kadācid antarmukhaḥ san maitrīmaya eva bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

na kevalam maitry eva tasya kāntāsti yāvad anye dve apīty āha

dve kānte tiṣṭhatas tasya pārśvayoḥ satyataikate ।
indor iva viśākhe dve samāhlāditacetasī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jña imān akhilāṃl lokān duḥkhakrakacadāritān ।
vālmīkān iva pīṭhasthaḥ pṛṣṭhād arka ivekṣate ।।

lokān kathambhūtān । duḥkham eva krakacaḥ । tena dāritān pīḍitān । vālmīkān pipīlikāḥ । pṛṣṭhād pṛṣṭham āruhyety arthaḥ ।।

ciram pūritasarvāśaḥ sarvasampattisundaraḥ ।
apunaḥkhaṇḍanāyenduḥ pūrṇāṅga iva rājate ।।

sarvasampattyā sarvasampadā ।।

sevyamāno ḥpi bhogaugho na khedāyāsya jāyate ।
kālakūṭaḥ kileśasya kaṇṭhe pratyuta rājate ।।

khedāya nāśadvāreṇeti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu kathaṃ nāsāv asya khedāya bhavatīty । atrāha

parijñāyopabhukto hi bhogo bhavati tuṣṭaye ।
vijñāyāśvāsito maitrīm eti cauro na śatrutām ।।

parijñāya samyak niścityātmarūpatvena jñātvety arthaḥ । ātmarūpatvena hi jñāto bhogaḥ naṣṭo ḥpi khedaṃ na dadāti svātmarūpatayā sthitatvāt । na cātmano nāśaḥ yuktaḥ । nāśe ḥpi nāśasākṣitayā sthitatvāt ।।

naranārīnaṭaughānāṃ kalahe dūragāminā ।
jñena yātreva subhagā bhogaśrīr avalokyate ।।

anyo ḥpi nipuṇaḥ naṭaughānāṃ kalahe dūraṃ gacchati । yātrām tadārabdhaṃ nāṭyaṃ ca paśyati ।।

aśaṅkitopasamprāptā grāmayātrā yathādhvagaiḥ ।
prekṣyate tadvad evājñair vyavahāramayī kriyā ।।

niranusandhānam eva prekṣata iti bhāvaḥ ।।

ayatnopanateṣv akṣi digdravyeṣu yathā puraḥ ।
nīrāgam eva patati tadvat kāryeṣu dhīradhīḥ ।।

ayatnopanateṣu digdravyeṣu yathā akṣi netram । nīrāgam rāgarahitam । patati । dhīradhīḥ tajjñabuddhiḥ । kāryeṣu tadvat patati । rāgarahitam evāsau kāryāṇi karotīti bhāvaḥ ।।

indriyāṇāṃ na harati prāptam arthaṃ kadācana ।
na dadāti tathā prāptaṃ sampūrṇo jño ḥvatiṣṭhate ।।

sampūrṇatvaṃ hy etad eva yat prāptasya grahaṇam aprāptasyāvāñchanam iti ।।

aprāptacintāḥ samprāptasamupekṣāś ca sanmatim ।
nākalpayanti taralā piñchaghātā ivācalam ।।

na ākalpayanti na cañcalīkurvanti ।।

saṃśāntasarvasandeho galitākhilakautukaḥ ।
saṅkṣīṇakalpanājālo jñaḥ saṃrāḍ iva śobhate ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ātmany eva na māty antaḥ svātmanātmani jṛmbhate ।
sampūrṇāpāraparyantaḥ kṣīrārṇava ivātmavān ।।

na māti । ānandanirbharatvāt svātmanātmani jṛmbhate । nāntaḥ kañcid anyam paśyatīti bhāvaḥ । sampūrṇaś cāsau apāraparyantaś ca sampūrṇāpāraparyantaḥ ।।

bhogecchākṛpaṇāñ jantūn dīnān dīnendriyāṇi ca ।
anunmattamanāḥ śānto hasaty unmattakān iva ।।

tadāsaktau tu kā katheti bhāvaḥ ।।

icchato ḥnyanijāṃ jāyāṃ yathaivānyena hasyate ।
indriyasyecchato bhogaṃ tathaiva jñena hasyate ।।

yathā anyasya nijām anyanijām । tādṛśīm bhāvinīm bhāryām icchataḥ । anyārtham bhāryām icchata iti yāvat । yathā anyena hasyate hāsaḥ kriyate । tathaiva indriyasya bhogam icchataḥ ajñasya ।।

tyajantaṃ svasukhaṃ sāmyam mano viṣayavidrutam ।
aṅkuśeneva nāgendraṃ vicāreṇa vaśaṃ nayet ।।

sāmyaṃ svasukham sāmyākhyam ātmānandam । vicāreṇa kiṃsārā ime bhogā ity evaṃrūpeṇa ।।

bhogeṣu prasaro yasyā manovṛtteḥ pradīyate ।
sāpy ādāv eva hantavyā viṣasyevāṅkurodgatiḥ ।।

sā manovṛttiḥ । ādau prasaradānāt prāk । yasyāḥ tu na dīyate tasyāḥ kā kathety apiśabdābhiprāyaḥ ।।

nanu prathamaṃ hatāyāḥ paścāt prasaradāne kim phalam ity । atrāha

tāḍitasya hi yaḥ paścāt sammānaḥ so ḥpy anantakaḥ ।
śāler grīṣmopataptasya kuseko ḥpy amṛtāyate ।।

sammānaḥ ādaraḥ । prasaradānam iti yāvat ।।

nanu katham etad ity । atrāha

anārtena hi sammāno bahumāno na budhyate ।
pūrṇānāṃ saritām prāvṛṭpūraḥ svalpaṃ virājate ।।

hi yasmāt । anārtenādṛṣṭapīḍanena । sammānaḥ bahumānaḥ na budhyate na jñāyate । etad dṛṣṭāntena samarthayati pūrṇānām iti । pūrṇānāṃ saritām prāvṛṭpūraḥ svalpam tokam । janamanaāhlādakāritvābhāvād ity arthaḥ । janamano hi kṣīṇānāṃ nadīnām prāvṛṭpūradarśanena sānandam bhavati ।।

pūrṇas tūpakṛto ḥpy anyat punar apy abhivāñchati ।
jagatpūraṇayāpy ambu gṛhṇāty ekārṇavo ḥkhilam ।।

jagatpūraṇayā yukto ḥpīti śeṣaḥ ।।

manaso nigṛhītasya yā paścād bhāgamaṇḍanā ।
tām evālabdhavistāralabdhatvād bahu manyate ।।

bhāgamaṇḍanā leśena pūraṇā । tām eva bhāgamaṇḍanām eva । alabdhavistāraś cāsau labdhaś ca alabdhavistāralabdhaḥ । tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam । tasmāt । alabdhavistāraḥ labdhaḥ hi svalpam api bahu manyate ।।

baddhamukto mahīpālo grāmamātreṇa tuṣyati ।
parair abaddho nākrānto rājyenāpi na tuṣyati ।।

ādau baddhaḥ paścān muktaḥ baddhamuktaḥ । tathā nigṛhītam manaḥ bhogaleśenaiva tuṣyatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

indriyanigrahadvāreṇa manonigrahasya sādhyatvād indriyanigraham eva kathayati

hastaṃ hastena sampīḍya dantair dantān vicūrṇya ca ।
aṅgāny aṅgair ivākramya jaya svendriyaśātravān ।।

viṣayeṣu pravṛttāni indriyāṇi samyagjñānabalena pratyāharaṇīyānīti bhāvaḥ ।।

jetum anyaṃ kṛtotsāhaiḥ puruṣair udbubhūṣubhiḥ ।
pūrvaṃ hṛdayaśatrutvāj jñātavyānīndriyāṇy alam ।।

anyam rājādirūpam । udbhavitum icchubhiḥ udbubhūṣubhiḥ । jñātavyāni śatrutveneti śeṣaḥ । hṛdayaśatrutvam cendriyāṇām bhogān praty ākarṣaṇakāritvena jñeyam ।।

manojayayuktānām praśaṃsāṃ karoti

etāvati dharaṇitale subhagās te sādhucetanāḥ puruṣāḥ ।
puruṣakathāsu ca gaṇyā na jitā ye na cetasā svena ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati

hṛdayabile kṛtakuṇḍala ulbaṇakalanāviṣo manobhujagaḥ ।
yasyopaśāntim āgata uditaṃ tam arindamaṃ vande ।।

sa eva sarvotkṛṣṭa iti bhāvaḥ ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe trayoviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

nanu tarhīndriyajaye kaḥ kleśa ity । atrāha

mahānarakasamrājo mattaduṣkṛtavāraṇāḥ ।
āśāśaraśalākāḍhyā durjayā hīndriyārayaḥ ।।

mattaduṣkṛtāny eva vāraṇā yeṣām । āśā eva śaraśalākāḥ yeṣām । samrājaḥ api vāraṇayuktāḥ śarayuktāś ca bhavanti ।।

svāśrayam prathamaṃ dehaṃ kṛtaghnā nāśayanti ye ।
te kukāryamahākośā durjayāḥ svendriyārayaḥ ।।

nāśayanti asambhavino bhogān prati ceṣṭāṃ kārayanti ।।

kalevarālayam prāpya viṣayāmiṣagardhataḥ ।
akṣagṛdhrā vivalganti kāryākāryograpakṣiṇaḥ ।।

kāryākārye eva ugrau pakṣau yeṣām ।।

vivekatantujālena gṛhītā yena te śaṭhāḥ ।
tasyāṅgāni na lumpanti pāṣāṇakavalaṃ yathā ।।

te akṣagṛdhrāḥ । gṛdhrā hi pāṣāṇakavalaṃ na lumpanti ।।

āpātaramaṇīyeṣu ramante viṣayeṣu ye ।
atyantavirasānteṣu patanti narakeṣu te ।।

atyantaṃ virasaḥ antaḥ yeṣām । viṣayeṣv ity asya viśeṣaṇam etat ।।

vivekadhanavān asmin kukalevarapattane ।
indriyāribhir antaḥsthair avaśo nābhibhūyate ।।

asmin anubhūyamāne । kukalevare nindite śarīre । balavān hi aribhiḥ nāvaśo ḥbhibhūyate ।।

na tathā sukhitā bhūyo mṛṇmayograpurījuṣaḥ ।
yathā svādhīnamanasaḥ svaśarīrapurīśvarāḥ ।।

mṛṇmayograpurījuṣaḥ bāhyanagarīrājānaḥ । svādhīnamanasa iti viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa hetuḥ ।।

svākrāntendriyabhṛtyasya sugṛhītamanoripoḥ ।
vasanta iva mañjaryo vardhante buddhabuddhayaḥ ।।

buddhānām jñāninām ।।

prakṣīṇacittadarpasya nigṛhītendriyadviṣaḥ ।
padminya iva hemante kṣīyante bhogavāsanāḥ ।।

bhogavāsanāḥ bhogasaṃskārāḥ ।।

tāvan niśīva vetālyo valganti hṛdi vāsanāḥ ।
ekatattvadṛḍhābhyāsād yāvan na vijitam manaḥ ।।

vijite tu manasi na valgantīti bhāvaḥ । ekatattvam sarvavyāpakaṃ śuddhacinmātratattvam ।।

bhṛtyo ḥbhimatakartṛtvān mantrī satkāryakāraṇāt ।
sāmantaḥ svendriyākrānter mano manye vivekinaḥ ।।

sāmantaḥ śatrujaye adhikṛtaḥ ।।

lālanāt snigdhalalanā pālanāt pāvanaḥ pitā ।
suhṛd uttamaviśvāsān mano manye manīṣiṇām ।।

lālanāt lālanākāritvāt । snigdhalalanā snehayuktā cāsau । lalanā strī ।।

svālokitaṃ śāstradṛśā sudhyātaṃ svanunāthitam ।
prayacchati parāṃ siddhiṃ tyaktvātmānam manaḥpitā ।।

suṣṭhur anunāthitam yācitam । ātmānaṃ tyaktvā nāśayitvā । mano hi svātmānaṃ nāśayitvaiva hitaṃ sampādayati । pitāpi putrasya svaprāṇatyāgena hitaṃ karotīti tasyopamānatvam ।।

sughṛṣṭaḥ suparāmṛṣṭaḥ sudhṛtaḥ svanubodhitaḥ ।
suguṇāyojito bhāti hṛdi hṛdyo manomaṇiḥ ।।

maṇipakṣe svanubodhitaḥ samyakparīkṣitaḥ । suguṇeṣu praśasteṣu guṇeṣu tantuṣu ca । ā samantāt ।।

janmavṛkṣakuṭhārāṇi tathodarkodayāni ca ।
diśaty eṣa manomantrī karmāṇi śubhakarmaṇaḥ ।।

udarkaḥ uttaraphalabhūtaḥ । śubhakarmaṇaḥ śubhakarmakāriṇaḥ puruṣasya ।।

phalitam āha

evam manomaṇiṃ rāma bahupaṅkakalaṅkitam ।
vivekavāriṇā siddhyai prakṣālyālokavān bhava ।।

siddhyai cinmātrasvarūpaparamātmatattvalābhākhyāyai siddhyai । ālokavān prakāśavān । maṇiprakṣālako ḥpi tamasi ālokavān bhavati । ratnālokasya vidyamānatvāt ।।

bhavabhūmiṣu bhīmāsu vivekavitato ḥpi san ।
mā patotpātapūrṇāsu vivaśaḥ prākṛto yathā ।।

bhīmāsu bhayapradāsu । vivekavān apy ahaṃ yadi gacchāmy api । kim mama setsyatīti niścaye ḥpi mā gaccheti dyotayitum apiśabdaḥ । prākṛtaḥ vivekarahitaḥ । patane tu tvam api vivekavān nāsīti bhāvaḥ ।।

saṃsāramāyām uditām anarthaśatasaṅkulām ।
mā mahāmohamihikām imāṃ tvam avadhīraya ।।

māvadhīraya kim mām iyaṃ karotīty avagaṇanāviṣayam mā kuru ।।

vivekam param āśritya buddhyā satyam avekṣya ca ।
indriyārīn alaṃ jitvā tīrṇo bhava bhavā[rṇavāt] ।।

viśeṣaṇadvaye ḥpi hetutvena jñeyam ।।

ratnayantramayānantadaityanirjitavāsavaḥ ।
himaśītānalajvālānirmitodyānamaṇḍapaḥ ।।

ratnayantramayāḥ māyodbhāvitāḥ ratnayantrasvarūpāḥ । taiḥ nirjitaḥ vāsavaḥ । saḥ ।।

sarvartukusumodyānajitanandanacandanaḥ ।
māyāsarpahṛtavyālamalayācalacandanaḥ ।।

māyāsarpaiḥ hṛtavyālāni dūrīkṛtasahajasarpāṇi । malayācalacandanāni yasya । saḥ ।।

hemastrīlokalāvaṇyajihmitāntaḥpurāṅganaḥ ।
krīḍārthaspardhayeśānahatacakragadādharaḥ ।।

hemastrīlokena māyodbhāvitena suvarṇāṅganālokena । lāvaṇyena jihmitāḥ jitāḥ । antaḥpurāṅganāḥ yasya । krīḍārtham māyayā udbhāvitā spardhā krīḍārthaspardhā । īśānena mahārudreṇa । hataḥ cakragadādharaḥ viṣṇuḥ yasya । saḥ ।।

ajasroḍḍīnaratnaughatārāḍhyasvapurāmbaraḥ ।
nānākusumasambhārajānudaghnakṛtāṅganaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

niśāsv akhilapātālaśatacandranabhastalaḥ ।
svasālabhañjikālokagītigītaguṇotkaraḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

māyairāvaṇanāgendravidrutāmaravāraṇaḥ ।
trailokyavibhavotkarṣapūritāntaḥpurāntaraḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sarvasampattisubhagaḥ sarvaiśvaryasamanvitaḥ ।
samastadaityasāmantavanditāgryānuśāsanaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

mahābhujavanacchāyāviśrāntāsuramaṇḍalaḥ ।
sarvāmbudhiguhāsāraratnakuṇḍalamaṇḍitaḥ ।।

sarvāmbudhayaḥ eva guhāḥ । tāsāṃ sārāṇi yāni ratnāni । teṣāṃ kuṇḍalāni ।।

tasyotsāditadevasya kaṭhinoḍḍāmarākṛteḥ ।
babhūva vipulaṃ sainyam āsuraṃ suranāśanam ।।

utsāditāḥ khedaṃ nītāḥ devāḥ yena ।।

tasmin māyābale supte deśāntaragate tathā ।
tatsainyāntaram ājagmuś chidram prāpya kilāmarāḥ ।।

tasya śambarasya । tasyāntaram madhyam । prāpya । anyathā teṣāṃ śaktir nābhūd iti bhāvaḥ ।।

atha śambaradaityena dudrikahvadrumādayaḥ ।
rakṣārtham mattasāmantāḥ svasenāsu niyojitāḥ ।।

niyojitāḥ preritāḥ ।।

tān apy antaram āsādya jaghnur gīrvāṇanāyakāḥ ।
vyomāntaracarāḥ śyenāḥ kalaviṅkān ivākulān ।।

tān api dudrikahvadrumādīn api । antaram āsādyāvakāśaṃ labdhvā । jaghnuḥ ghnanti sma ।।

senāpatīn punaś cānyāṃś cakārāsurasattamaḥ ।
capalān udbhaṭārāvāṃs taraṅgān iva sāgaraḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

devās tān api tasyāśu jaghnus tena sa kopavān ।
jagāmāmaranāśāya paripūrṇas triviṣṭapam ।।

paripūrṇaḥ mahāsainyayuktaḥ ।।

tatrāsya māyābhītās te surā antardhim āyayuḥ ।
merukānanakuñjeṣu mṛgā gaurīguror iva ।।

kuñjeṣv iti niṣkṛṣya gaurīguror ity anena sambandhanīyam ।।

krandatkṣudrāmaragaṇaṃ vāṣpaklinnasurīmukham ।
śūnyaṃ dadarśa sa svargaṃ kalpakṣīṇajagatsamam ।।

saḥ śambaraḥ ।।

vihṛtya kupitas tatra labdham āhṛtya śambaraḥ ।
lokapālapurīr dagdhvā jagāmātmīyam ālayam ।।

labdham hastāgataṃ ratnajātam ।।

evaṃ dṛḍhatarībhūte dveṣe dānavadevayoḥ ।
devāḥ svargam parityajya dikṣu jagmur adarśanam ।।

dveṣe vaire ।।

atha śambaradaityena ye ye senādhināyakāḥ ।
kriyante yatnatas tāṃs tāñ jaghnur yatnaparāḥ surāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yāvad udvegam āpannaḥ śambaraḥ kopavān bhṛśam ।
tārṇo ḥbhi vātam anala iva jajvāla cocchvasan ।।

ka iva jajvāla । tārṇaḥ tṛṇodbhūtaḥ । anala iva । yathā saḥ vātam abhi jvalati । tathety arthaḥ ।।

trailokyam api cānviṣya na devāṃl labdhavān atha ।
pareṇāpi prayatnena sukṛtānīva duṣkṛtī ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sasarja māyayā ghorān asurāṃs trīn mahābalān ।
balarakṣārtham uditān kālān mūrtim ivāsthitān ।।

kālān yamān ।।

nirmitā māyayā bhīmāḥ kalpapādapabāhavaḥ ।
udagus te mahākāyāḥ pakṣakṣubdhā ivādrayaḥ ।।

udaguḥ utthitāḥ ।।

dāmo vyālaḥ kaṭaś ceti nāmabhiḥ parilāñchitāḥ ।
yathāprāptaikakartāraś cetanāmātradharmiṇaḥ ।।

yathāprāptaikakartāraḥ niranusandhānā ity arthaḥ ।।

tān eva viśinaṣṭi

abhāvāt karmaṇāṃ te ca prāktanānām avāsanāḥ ।
nirvikalpakacinmātraparispandaikakarmiṇaḥ ।।

te ca traya āsan kathambhūtāḥ । sadyaḥ utthitatvena prāktanānāṃ karmaṇām abhāvāt avāsanāḥ vāsanārahitāḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtāḥ । nirvikalpakam vikalparahitam । yat cinmātram । tasya yaḥ parispandaḥ । tadrūpam ekam karma eṣām astīti tādṛśāḥ । nirvikalpaceṣṭā ity arthaḥ ।।

karmabījaṃ kalāṃ tanvīṃ dadhānā mananābhidhām ।
apuṣṭāṃ kṛtrimām antar ādāyodayam āgatāḥ ।।

punaḥ kathambhūtāḥ । karmabījam karmabījabhūtām । tanvīm alpām । mananābhidhām kalāṃ dadhānāḥ । ata eva apuṣṭāṃ kṛtrimām āhāryām । tām mananābhidhāṃ kalām ādāya । udayam prādurbhāvam । anyathā brahmaṇaḥ utthānaṃ na syād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

pāramparyeṇa te hy atra kākatālīyavad bhaṭāḥ ।
prakṛtām anuvartante kriyām ujjhitavāsanāḥ ।।

pāramparyeṇa paramparāpekṣayā । na tu prayojanam anusandhāya ।।

ardhasuptā yathā bālāḥ svāṅgair iṅganti kevalam ।
vāsanātmābhimānābhyāṃ hīnās te tadvad eva hi ।।

vāsanā cātmābhimānam ca ।।

nābhipātaṃ na cāpātaṃ vidus te na palāyanam ।
na jīvitaṃ na maraṇaṃ na raṇaṃ ca jayājayau ।।

abhimukham pātaḥ abhipātaḥ ।।

kevalaṃ sainikān agre dṛṣṭvābhihananodyatān ।
abhijaghnuḥ parān ājau prahāradalitādrayaḥ ।।

parān śatrubhūtān ।।

śambaraś cintayām āsa parituṣṭamanāḥ pure ।
vijeṣyate hi matsenā māyāsurasurakṣitā ।।

kiṃ cintayām āsety । atrāha vijeṣyate iti । māyayā utpāditāḥ asurāḥ māyāsurāḥ । taiḥ surakṣitā matsenā । hi niścaye । vijeṣyate vijayam prāpsyati ।।

iṣṭāniṣṭābhir ete hi vāsanābhiḥ samujjhitāḥ ।
tato raṇe bibhyati no vidravanti ca na sthirāḥ ।।

iṣṭāniṣṭavāsanāyukta eva hi śatrum balayuktaṃ jñātvā bibheti vidravati ceti bhāvaḥ ।।

yad ete na palāyante devair abhihatā api ।
tad eṣātibalā senā mamedānīṃ vyavasthitā ।।

viśeṣeṇāvasthitā vyavasthitā ।।

sargāntaślokena śambaracintāṃ samāpayati

atibalāsuradordrumapālitā mama camūḥ sthiratām alam eṣyati ।
amaravāraṇadantavighaṭṭaneṣv amaraparvatahemamahī yathā ।।

amaraparvatasya sumeroḥ । hemamahī suvarṇabhūmiḥ । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe pañcaviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

śambaracintām upasaṃharati

iti nirṇīya daityendro dāmavyālakaṭānvitām ।
senāṃ sampreṣayām āsa bhūtalaṃ devanāśinīm ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

daityāḥ sāgarakuñjebhyaḥ kandarebhyaḥ surācalāt ।
udagur bhīmanirhrādāḥ sapakṣagirilīlayā ।।

udaguḥ utthitāḥ । sapakṣāḥ pakṣayuktāḥ । ye girayaḥ ।।

rodasīkoṭaraṃ hastaprahārahatabhāskaram ।
dānavāḥ pūrayām āsur dāmavyālakaṭeritāḥ ।।

dāmavyālakaṭeritāḥ dāmavyālakaṭapreritāḥ ।।

athottasthur nikuñjebhyaḥ kandarebhyaḥ surācalāt ।
pralayānta ivākṣubdhā bhītāḥ svarvāsināṃ gaṇāḥ ।।

ā samantāt kṣubdhāḥ ākṣubdhāḥ । svarvāsinām devānām ।।

devāsurapatākinyos tad yuddham abhavat tayoḥ ।
akālolbaṇakalpāntabhīṣaṇam bhuvanāntare ।।

tat prasiddham ।।

petuḥ pralayaparyastasacandrārkādrivad divaḥ ।
śirāṃsi kuṇḍalodvāntatejaḥpītatamāṃsy adhaḥ ।।

pralaye paryastāḥ vāteritāḥ । ye sacandrārkāḥ adrayaḥ । tadvat । śirāṃsi divaḥ ākāśāt । adhaḥ bhūmau । śirāṃsi kathambhūtāni । kuṇḍalaiḥ udvāntam udvamitam । yaiḥ ।।

jughūrṇur bhaṭanirmuktasiṃhanādavirāvitāḥ ।
pralayānilasampūraiḥ sāṭṭahāsā ivādrayaḥ ।।

aṭṭahāsayuktā api ghūrṇanti ।।

rejur ātmaśilātulyahetipātārtavṛttayaḥ ।
kulācalataṭā bhītavibhrāntaharimaṇḍalāḥ ।।

kulācalataṭāḥ rejuḥ । ātmanaḥ ātmasambandhinyaḥ । tābhiḥ tulyāḥ । vṛttiḥ sthitiḥ yeṣām । punaḥ kathambhūtāḥ । bhītāni ata eva vibhrāntāni harimaṇḍalāni siṃhamaṇḍalāni yeṣām ।।

ceruḥ parasparāghātahatahetisamutthitāḥ ।
lolānalakaṇāḥ kalpaviśīrṇā iva tārakāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

vilesū raktamāṃsaughapūrṇaikārṇavatīragāḥ ।
kalpatālatanūttālā vetālās tāratālinaḥ ।।

vilesuḥ vilasanti sma । vetālāḥ bhūtaviśeṣāḥ । tāratālinaḥ udbhaṭavādyayuktāḥ ।।

prasphuradrudhirāsāraśāntapāṃsupayodhare ।
vyomni hetihatakṣuṇṇamaulikuṇḍalakoṭayaḥ ।।

hetihatānāṃ yodhānām । yāni maulikuṇḍalāni । teṣāṃ koṭayaḥ vyomni । vilesur iti pūrveṇa sambandhaḥ ।।

babhūvur bhāskarākāraiḥ kalpabhūruhabāhubhiḥ ।
prahāradalitādrīndrair daityair nirvivarā diśaḥ ।।

nirvivarāḥ nīrandhrāḥ ।।

jagmur jvaladasivrātapātapātitabhittayaḥ ।
kaṇaprakaratāṃ śailāḥ kalpāgnivalitā iva ।।

kalpāgnivalitāḥ kalpāgnibhramitāḥ ।।

devāḥ tejaḥ samājagmur aśvamedhaidhitā iva ।
asurān anusasrus tāñ jaladān iva vāyavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

jagṛhus tān athākramya jaradākhūn ivotavaḥ ।
rejuḥ surāsurāḥ phullavanalolādrivad divi ।।

devāḥ tān asurān । jagṛhuḥ iti sambandhaḥ । otavaḥ viḍālāḥ ।।

te ḥnyoḥnyam pūrayām āsuḥ śastrapūrair diśo daśa ।
vanāni kusumavrātaiḥ sumeror iva mārutāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

ghoraṃ samabhavad yuddhaṃ devadānavasainyayoḥ ।
rodorandhroḍumbarāntar mahāmaṣakasaṅghayoḥ ।।

rodorandhra eva dyāvāpṛthivīrandhra eva uḍumbarāntaḥ uḍumbaraphalamadhyam । tatra mahāmaṣakasaṅghayoḥ mahāmaṣakasamūhayoḥ । uḍumbarāntaḥ hi maṣakāḥ bhavanti ।।

athodapatad ullāsair lokapālebhamaṇḍalaiḥ ।
kalpābhraiḥ pūritākāro dāruṇaḥ samarāravaḥ ।।

ullāsaiḥ ūrdhvagatahastaiḥ । kalpābhraiḥ kalpābhratulyaiḥ । udapatat utthitaḥ ।।

samarāravaṃ vistareṇa viśinaṣṭi

piṇḍagraheṇa nabhasi bhūbhāga iva kuṭṭimam ।
muṣṭigrāhyo mahāmeghamantharodarapīvaraḥ ।।

samarāravaḥ kathambhūtaḥ । nabhasi piṇḍagraheṇa muṣṭigrāhyaḥ । kim iva । yathā kuṭṭimam bhūbhāge piṇḍagraheṇa muṣṭigrāhyam bhavati ।।

prathamāpātasampiṣṭaśastraśailaraṭattaṭaḥ ।
sphuṭaddhṛdayaniḥsattvakarkaśākrandaghargharaḥ ।।
