prathamāpāta eva sampiṣṭāḥ ye śastrabhūtāḥ śailāḥ । taiḥ raṭantaḥ taṭāḥ yasya । saḥ । sphuṭaddhṛdayāḥ ye niḥsattvāḥ dhairyarahitāḥ । teṣāṃ yaḥ karkaśākrandaḥ । tena ghargharaḥ ghargharaśabdayuktaḥ ।।

pralayapratyayollāsikalpābhrāravabṛṃhaṇaḥ ।
dvādaśādityasaṅghaṭṭadravatkāñcanasannibhaḥ ।।

pralayapratyaye pralayasamaye । ullāsī yaḥ kalpābhrāravaḥ । tadvat bṛṃhaṇaṃ yasya । dvādaśādityānāṃ yaḥ saṅghaṭṭaḥ kalpānte anyoḥnyaṃ saṅghaṭṭanam । tena dravat yat kāñcanam । avicchinnapravāhatvena tulya ity arthaḥ ।।

brahmāṇḍakuḍyasaṅghaṭṭāt parāvṛtyāvaniṃ gataḥ ।
mahāsrotaḥpayaḥpūraḥ setvāhata ivākaram ।।

punaḥ kathambhūtaḥ । brahmāṇḍakuḍyasaṅghaṭṭāt parāvṛtya avaniṃ gataḥ । ka iva । mahāsrotaḥpayaḥpūra iva । yathā saḥ setvāhataḥ san ākaram utpattisthānaṃ gacchati ।।

calatsapakṣaśailendrapakṣavātabaladhvaniḥ ।
kaṭhināpūraṇoḍḍīnasphuṭaśailendrakandharaḥ ।।

calantaḥ ye sapakṣāḥ śailendrāḥ । teṣāṃ yaḥ pakṣavātaḥ । tena yaḥ baladhvaniḥ balayuktaḥ śabdaḥ । kaṭhinaiḥ kāṭhinyayuktair āyudhair । āpūraṇena uḍḍīnāḥ sphuṭaṃ śailendrakandharāḥ yasya ।।

mandaroddhūtadugdhābdhisaṅkṣobhasadṛśāṃśakaḥ ।
pratiśrudghuṅghumāsphoṭaghaṭitadvīpajantubhūḥ ।।

mandaroddhūtaś cāsau dugdhābdhiḥ ca । tasya yaḥ saṅkṣobhaḥ । tena sadṛśāḥ aṃśāḥ bhāgāḥ yasya । pratiśrudrūpo yaḥ ghuṅghumaśabdānuvedhaḥ । tena ghaṭitāḥ melitāḥ । dvīpāś ca jantubhuvaś ca । saḥ ।।

senayoḥ kruddhayor āsīd yuddham uddhatadānavam ।
niṣpiṣṭanagaragrāmagirikānanamānavam ।।

tayoḥ senayoḥ yuddham āsīt । kathambhūtam ity apekṣāyāṃ yuddhaṃ vistareṇa viśinaṣṭi uddhatetyādi ।।

mahāhetiśatacchinnadānavācalapūrṇadik ।
anyoḥnyahatahetyadricūrṇapūrṇāmbarodaram ।।

mahāhetīnāṃ yāni śatāni । taiḥ chinnāḥ ye dānavācalāḥ । taiḥ pūrṇāḥ diśaḥ yasya ।।

bhusuṇḍīmaṇḍalāsphoṭasphuṭanmeruśiraḥśatam ।
śaramārutanirlūnadaityadevāsurāmbujam ।।

āsphoṭaḥ tāḍanam । mārutena ca ambujāni lūyante ।।

cakrāvartaśatabhrāntadevadaityajarattṛṇam ।
senāpravāhakallolavalanāvalitāmbaram ।।

cakrāṇām āyudhaviśeṣāṇām । ye āvartāḥ bhramaṇāni । teṣāṃ yāni śatāni । teṣu bhrāntāḥ cakrabhramayuktāḥ । devadaityā eva jarattṛṇaṃ yatra । senāpravāhānāṃ ye kallolāḥ vyūharūpāḥ kallolāḥ । teṣāṃ yā valanāḥ valganāḥ । tābhiḥ valitaṃ vṛttam । tat ।।

hetyadripātaniṣpiṣṭapatadvaimānikavrajam ।
hastānītābdhivāryoghaplāvitavyomapattanam ।।

plāvitam īritam ।।

vahanmahāstrāvartāsiśūlaśaktinadīśatam ।
śailapakṣodbhaṭāsphoṭajaḍabrahmāṇḍamaṇḍalam ।।

mahāstrāṇy eva cakrāṇy evāvartāḥ yeṣām । tāni mahāstrāvartāni । vahanti mahāstrāvartāni asiśūlaśaktinadīśatāni yasmin । āsphoṭaḥ saśabdaṃ tāḍanam । tena jaḍam śabdaśravaṇaśaktirahitam ।।

daityapārṣṇiprahāraughapatallokeśapattanam ।
nārīhalahalārāvaravatkanakamandiram ।।

halahaleti śabdānukaraṇam ।।

luṭhaddaityācaloddhūtamattārṇavajalādribhiḥ ।
dhautaraktanabho yodhamuktanādadravadvrajam ।।

luṭhantaḥ patantaḥ । ye daityā evācalāḥ । tair uddhūtāḥ ye mattārṇavāḥ । teṣāṃ ye jalādrayaḥ mahormayaḥ । taiḥ kṛtvā dhautaṃ raktanabhaḥ raktayuktaṃ nabhaḥ yasya । yodhaiḥ muktaḥ yaḥ mahānādaḥ siṃhanādaḥ । tena dravantaḥ dhāvantaḥ । vrajāḥ arthāt dīnasamūhāḥ yatra ।।

lokapānekapāmbhodacchannacchannāryamānvitam ।
punaḥ surāsuroddyotair dṛṣṭasainyakulākulam ।।

lokapānām lokeśānām । ye anekapāḥ hastinaḥ । te evāmbhodāḥ meghāḥ । taiḥ channacchannaḥ atiśayenāvṛtaḥ । yaḥ aryamā sūryaḥ । tarhi tatra tair anyoḥnyaṃ kathaṃ dṛṣṭam ity । punaḥ pakṣāntare । surāsurāṇāṃ ye uddyotāḥ śarīraprakāśāḥ । taiḥ kṛtvā dṛṣṭaṃ yat sainyakulam sainyasamūhaḥ । tenākulam nirbharam ।।

sapakṣaparvatākāradānavādrigamāgamaiḥ ।
vahatpacapacāśabdabhūribhākkarabhīṣaṇam ।।

pacapaceti śabdānukaraṇam ।।

āyudhādrivibhinnogradaityaparvatanirjharaiḥ ।
raktair aruṇitāśeṣavasudhārṇavaparvatam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

utsannarāṣṭranagaravipinagrāmagahvaraiḥ ।
dhṛtāsaṅkhyāsurebhāśvamanuṣyarathaparvatam ।।

utsannāḥ vinaṣṭāḥ । ye rāṣṭranagaravipinagrāmāḥ । teṣāṃ gahvaraiḥ randhrarūpaiḥ madhyabhāgaiḥ । dhṛtāḥ asaṅkhyāḥ asurebhāśvamanuṣyarathaparvatāḥ yasya । tat ।।

sutālottālanārācarājirecitacāraṇam ।
muṣṭiprahārapiṣṭāṃsamattairāvaṇavāraṇam ।।

sutālavat uttālāḥ ye nārācāḥ । tayā recitāḥ rahitāḥ । cāraṇāḥ devaviśeṣāḥ yasya ।।

kalpābhrapaṭalāsāradhārādalitaparvatam ।
mahāśaniviniṣpeṣapiṣṭoḍḍīnakulācalam ।।

āsāraḥ śilāmayo ḥtra jñeyaḥ ।।

kupitāgnijvalajjvālājālair jvalitadānavam ।
ekāñjalipuṭānītasamudrotsāditānalam ।।

utsāditaḥ nirvāpitaḥ ।।

cāndraśaityādisambhāraśilīkṛtamahājalam ।
vanavyūhendhanāgnyarcirdrāvitāmbuśiloccayam ।।

śītena hi jalam pāṣāṇībhavati । vaneti parvatāḥ api vigalanti smety arthaḥ ।।

astranirmitadurvāratamaḥkalpāntarātrikam ।
māyāsūryagaṇoddyotapītātanutamaḥpaṭam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

māyāgnivarṣanipatatkalpāntagaṇavarṣaṇam ।
saśīkārāgnipavanaśastrasaṅghaṭṭakarṣaṇam ।।

māyāgnivarṣeṇa nipatatkalpāntagaṇavat varṣaṇam yatra । saśīkārau śīkāraśabdayuktau । tat । tādṛśaḥ yaḥ śastrasaṅghaṭṭaḥ । tena karṣaṇam devāsurakarṣaṇam yatra ।।

vajravarṣavinirdhūtaśailavarṣāstrasambhavam ।
nidrābodhāstrayuddhāḍhyaṃ savarṣāvagrahāstrakam ।।

vajravarṣeṇa vinirdhūtaḥ śailavarṣarūpāṇām astrāṇāṃ sambhavaḥ yatra । nidrābodhakārīṇi astrāṇi nidrābodhāstrāṇi । tenāḍhyam । varṣāvagrahakārīṇi astrāṇi varṣāvagrahāstrāṇi । saha taiḥ vartate iti tādṛśam ।।

vahatkrakacavṛkṣāstraṃ jalāgnyastraraṇānvitam ।
brahmāstrayuddhaviṣamaṃ tamastejoḥstraśāritam ।।

śāritam citrīkṛtam ।।

astrodgīrṇāyudhānekanīrandhrasakalāmbaram ।
śilāvarṣāstravalitaṃ vahnivarṣāstrabhāsuram ।।

astrārtham brahmāstrādyartham । udgīrṇāni tyaktāni । yāni āyudhānekāni āyudhasamūhāḥ । taiḥ nīrandhraṃ sakalāmbaraṃ yat । tat ।।

patākāmṛṣṭaśaśakaiś cakracītkāragarjitaiḥ ।
muhūrtena rathair laṅghitodayāstamayācalam ।।

patākābhiḥ mṛṣṭaḥ śaśakaḥ arthāt candraśaśaḥ yais ।।

vajraprahārāviratamriyamāṇamahāsuram ।
śukrāmaramahāvidyājāyamānāparāsuram ।।

amaramahāvidyā sañjīvinī vidyā । devānāṃ tu svayam eva maraṇaṃ nāsti । amaratvāt iti teṣām maraṇaṃ vyathā eva jñeyam ।।

śubhagrahamahāketupālitānām itas tataḥ ।
utpātamaṅgalaughānāṃ yuddhair uddhatakandharam ।।

śubhagrahāḥ maṅgalāni pālayanti । ketuḥ upalakṣaṇam pāpagrahāṇām । pāpagrahāḥ hi utpātān pālayanti ।।

sādrikhorvīsamudradyu jagad rudhiravāribhiḥ ।
phullaikakiṃśukavanaṃ kurvad durvāravairataḥ ।।

punaḥ kathambhūtam । durvāravairataḥ jagat rudhiravāribhiḥ kṛtvā phullaikakiṃśukavanaṃ kurvat । jagat kathambhūtam । sādrikhorvīsamudradyu parvatākāśabhūmisamudrasvargasahitam ।।

parvatapratimāsaṅkhyaśavapūrṇamahārṇavam ।
samagrataruśākhāṃsalambalolamahāśavam ।।

mahārṇavā atra raktasya jñeyāḥ ।।

nīyamānaiḥ svavātāktaiḥ pakṣapuṣpalasatphalaiḥ ।
tālottālaiḥ śaravrātavanair vyāptanabhastalam ।।

vātenāktaiḥ preritaiḥ । pakṣapuṣpāṇi ca tāni lasatphalāni ca । phalam atra śalyaṃ jñeyam ।।

parvatapratimāsaṅkhyakabandhavanabāhubhiḥ ।
nṛtyadbhiḥ patitāmbhodavimānasuratārakam ।।

patitāḥ ambhodavimānasuratārakāḥ yasya ।।

śaraśaktigadāprāsapaṭṭisaprotaparvatam ।
lokasaptakavibhraṣṭakuḍyakhaṇḍācitāmbaram ।।

lokasaptakasya kuḍyāny apatann iti bhāvaḥ ।।

anāratarasanmattakalpābhradṛḍhadundubhi ।
pṛṣṭhaśabdaśravonnādapātālatalavāraṇam ।।

pṛṣṭhaśabdasya yaḥ śravaḥ śravaṇam । tenonnādāḥ pātālatalavāraṇāḥ yatra । tat ।।

vināyakakarākṛṣṭadīrghadānavaparvatam ।
ekadiktaṭaniḥspandasiddhasādhyamarudgaṇam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

palāyamānagandharvakinnarāmaracāraṇam ।
śavībhūtakṣatakṣīṇapatadgandharvanāyakam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kiñcillabdhajayaprāyadaityadānavamaṇḍalam ।
dūyamānasurānīkam ekāntodvignavāsavam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

uttarāśāmiladvahniraktahetivṛhatprabham ।
pratikṣaṇaṃ lasaddāhaprakāśatimirolbaṇam ।।

uttarāśayā uttaradiśā । tena raktā hetīnāṃ vṛhatyaḥ prabhāḥ yatra । devamandiradāhottho ḥtra vahnir jñeyaḥ । pratikṣaṇam kṣaṇe kṣaṇe । lasan yaḥ dāhaḥ gṛhadāhaḥ । tena ye prakāśatimire । tābhyām ulbaṇam । timiram atra dhūmakṛtaṃ jñeyam ।।

sargāntaślokena samīracalanaṃ kathayati

vavur aśaninipātapiṇḍitāṅgā dalitaśilāśakalā diśām mukheṣu ।
pralayasamayasūcakāḥ surāṇām urutaraghargharaghasmarāḥ samīrāḥ ।।

samīrāḥ vātāḥ । diśām mukheṣu vavuḥ vānti sma । kathambhūtāḥ । aśanīnāṃ yaḥ nipātaḥ । tena piṇḍitāny aṅgāni yeṣām । aśaninipātenaikatra militā ity arthaḥ । ata eva dalitāḥ śilāśakalāḥ yaiḥ । urutaraḥ yaḥ ghargharaḥ ghargharaśabdaḥ । tena ghasmarāḥ śabdāntaragrāsakāriṇa ity arthaḥ ।।

iti bhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe ṣaḍviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

tataḥ kiṃ sampannam ity । atrāha

tasmiṃs tadā vartamāne ghore samarasambhrame ।
devāsuraśarīreṣu patatsv adridaleṣv iva ।।

vahatsv abhrapravāheṣu gaṅgāpūreṣv ivāmbarāt ।
dāmni veṣṭitadevaughe muktakṣveḍāghanārave ।।

vyāle nijakarākṛṣṭipiṣṭasarvasurālaye ।
kaṭe kaṭhinasaṃrambhasaṅgarācchāditāmare ।।

airāvaṇe kṣīṇamade palāyanaparāyaṇe ।
pravṛddhe dānavānīke madhyāhna iva bhāskare ।।

pātitāṅgāyudhārdhāni prasravadrudhirāṇi ca ।
payāṃsīva visetūni devasainyāni dudruvuḥ ।।

pātitāni arthāt asuraiḥ bhūmau pātitāni । aṅgānām āyudhānāṃ cārdhāni yeṣām । tāni cchinnāṅgāni cchinnāyudhāni ceti yāvat । ata eva prasravat rudhiraṃ yeṣām । tānīti tādṛśāni devasainyāni dudruvuḥ bhayena drutāni । visetūni payāṃsīva । tasminn ityādi । dāmni dāmākhye mahāsure । kaṭhinasaṃrambhaṃ yat saṅgaram saṅgrāmaḥ । tatra ācchāditāḥ amarāḥ yena । tādṛśe sati ।।

dāmavyālakaṭās tāni ciram antarhitāny api ।
anujagmur lasannādam indhanānīva pāvakāḥ ।।

tāni devasainyāni । anujagmuḥ paścād dhāvanti sma । antarhitānām anugamanaṃ na yuktam ity apiśabdo dyotayati ।।

anviṣṭān api yatnena nālabhantāsurāḥ surān ।
ghanajālavanoḍḍīnān siṃhā hariṇakān iva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

alabdheṣv amaraugheṣu dāmavyālakaṭās tadā ।
jagmuḥ pātālakośasthaṃ prabhum pramuditāśayāḥ ।।

prabhuṃ śambaram ।।

atha devā viṣaṇṇās te kṣaṇam āśvasya vai yayuḥ ।
jayopāyāya vijitā brahmāṇam amitaujasam ।।

viṣaṇṇāḥ mūrchitāḥ । āśvasya cetanāṃ labdhvā ।।

teṣām āvirabhūd brahmā raktaraktānanaśriyām ।
sāyaṃ raktīkṛtāmbūnām abdhīnām iva candramāḥ ।।

raktena rudhireṇa । raktam ānanaṃ yeṣām । te । sāyam sāyaṃsandhyayety arthaḥ । candramaso vā raktīkaraṇe kartṛtvaṃ jñeyam । udayakāle tasya raktatvāt । tadā sāyam sāyaṃsamaya ity arthaḥ ।।

praṇamya te surās tasmai tam arthaṃ śambareritam ।
samyak prakathayām āsur dāmavyālakaṭakramam ।।

te surāḥ śambareritam śambaraprādurbhāvitam । tam dāmavyālakaṭakramam artham dāmādikramākhyaṃ vastu । praṇamya tasmai । samyak prakathayām āsuḥ ।।

tam ākarṇyākhilam brahmā vicārya ca vicāravit ।
uvācedaṃ surānīkam āśvāsanakaraṃ vacaḥ ।।

tam dāmavyālakaṭakramam । surānīkam devasainyam ।।

brahmā kathayati

hanta varṣasahasrānte śambareṇa hareḥ kramāt ।
martavyam amareśasya tāvat kālam pratīkṣyatām ।।

hanta kaṣṭe । varṣasahasrānte amareśasya hareḥ viṣṇoḥ । kramāt yuddhākhyāt kramāt । martavyam maraṇīyam । tāvat kālam asau na mariṣyatīti bhāvaḥ । yuṣmābhiḥ tāvat kālam pratīkṣyatām ।।

nanu tarhi tāvat kālam bādhāṃ kurvataḥ dāmādīn kiṃ kurma ity । atrāha

dāmavyālakaṭān etān adya tv amarasattamāḥ ।
yodhayantaḥ palāyadhvam māyāyuddhena dānavān ।।

he amarasattamāḥ । yūyam etān dāmavyālakaṭān dānavān māyāyuddhena yodhayantaḥ yuddhaṃ kārayantaḥ santaḥ । palāyadhvam ।।

nanu asmatpalāyanena kim eṣāṃ setsyatīty । atrāha

yuddhābhyāsavaśād eṣām makurāṇām ivāśaye ।
ahaṅkāracamatkāraḥ pratibimbam upaiṣyati ।।

eṣām dāmādīnām । ahaṅkāracamatkāraḥ vayaṃ yuddhe jayinaḥ smaḥ ity evaṃrūpo ḥhambhāvāsvādaḥ । āśaye manasi । pratibimbam upaiṣyati ।।

nanu tato ḥpi kiṃ setsyatīty । atrāha

gṛhītavāsanās tv ete dāmavyālakaṭāḥ surāḥ ।
sujayā vo bhaviṣyanti jālalagnāḥ khagā iva ।।

vāsanāyā eva vakṣyamānanayena vaivaśyakāritvāt ।।

nanv adya kathaṃ na jetuṃ śakyā ete ity । atrāha

adya tv avāsanā ete sukhaduḥkhavivarjitāḥ ।
dhairyeṇārīn vinighnanto devadurjayatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

tu pakṣāntare । adya avāsanāḥ ahaṃvāsanārahitāḥ । ata eva sukhaduḥkhavivarjitāḥ । ata eva dhairyeṇa arīn vinighnantaḥ । devadurjayatām yuṣmaddurjayatām iti yāvat । sukhādirahito hi bhītirahitatvād durjayo bhavati ।।

nanu vāsanayā katham ete vaśyā bhaviṣyantīty । atrāha

vāsanātantubaddhā ye āśāpāśavaśīkṛtāḥ ।
vaśyatāṃ yānti te loke rajjubaddhāḥ khagā iva ।।

ye vāsanātantubaddhā ahaṃvāsanātantubaddhāḥ । te āśāpāśavaśīkṛtāḥ santaḥ । loke vaśyā bhavanti । rajjubaddhāḥ khagā iva । puruṣaḥ antaḥsthitayāhaṃvāsanayā mamedam bhavatv etan mā bhavatv ity evaṃrūpayāśayāviṣṭo bhavati । tayā ca dainyaṃ gacchati । tena parasya vaśyo bhavatīti ।।

nanu vāsanārahitāḥ kathaṃ durjayā bhavantīty । atrāha

ye hi nirvāsanā dhīrāḥ sarvatrāsaktabuddhayaḥ ।
na hṛṣyanti na kupyanti durjayās te mahādhiyaḥ ।।

sarvatra heye upādeye vā । asaktā rāgadveṣarūpayā āsaktyā rahitā । buddhiḥ yeṣām । upādeyarāgena heyadveṣeṇaiva ca puruṣaḥ jeyo bhavati । anyathā viditanayāḥ rājānaḥ dravyadānena śatrūn jetuṃ na yateran । tadabhāve tu svaśarīre ḥpi rāgarahitaḥ puruṣaḥ na kenāpi jetuṃ śakyate iti bhāvaḥ । dveṣasyāsaktitvam āsaktyutpādakatvena jñeyam । dveṣeṇa hi heyān nivṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ upādeye dṛḍhataraṃ rāgāparaparyāyāsaktiyukto bhavati ।।

yasyāntarvāsanārajjvā granthibandhaḥ śarīriṇaḥ ।
mahān api bahujño ḥpi sa bālenāpi jīyate ।।

anyathā bāleṣv api dhanāḍhyeṣu vidyāvayovṛddhāḥ praṇāmaṃ na kuryur iti bhāvaḥ ।।

ayaṃ so ḥham idaṃ me tad ity ākalitakalpanaḥ ।
āpadām pātratām eti payasām iva sāgaraḥ ।।

ākalitā ā samantāt dhṛtā । kalpanā saṅkalpaḥ yena । saḥ । āpadām mamaitad bhavatv etan mā bhavatv ity evaṃrūpāṇām ।।

iyanmātraparicchinno yenātmā bhavya bhāvitaḥ ।
sa sarvajño ḥpi sarvatra parāṃ kṛpaṇatāṃ gataḥ ।।

he bhavya he indra । yena ātmā svasvarūpam । iyanmātraparicchinnaḥ । iyanmātraṃ cāsau dehādimātrarūpaś cāsau । ata eva paricchinnaś ceti tādṛśaḥ । bhāvitaḥ bhāvanāviṣayīkṛtaḥ । saḥ puruṣaḥ । sarvajñaḥ api sarvatra parāṃ niratiśayām । kṛpaṇatām dīnatām । gataḥ gacchatīty arthaḥ । dehaniṣṭho hi dehahitam icchann avaśyam eva kṛpaṇatām eti ।।

anantasyāprameyasya yeneyattā prakalpitā ।
ātmatattvasya tenātmā svātmanaivāvaśīkṛtaḥ ।।

anantasyāntasākṣitvena sthitatvāt tadrahitasya । aprameyasya kevalam pramātṛrūpeṇa sthitatvāt prameyatām aspṛśamānasya । ātmatattvasya । yena iyattā dehāvacchinnatvākhyam iyanmātratvam । prakalpitā kalpanayā bhāvitā । svātmanaiva ātmāvaśīkṛtaḥ । avaśyambhāvi hi dehāvacchinnasya bhogavaivaśyam ।।

nanu katham etad astīty । atrāha

ātmano vyatiriktaṃ yat kiñcid asti jagattraye ।
tatropādeyabhāvena baddhā bhavati bhāvanā ।।

ātmanaḥ paricchinnatvena bhāvitasyātmanaḥ । yat kiñcit vyatiriktam । bhāvitam iti śeṣaḥ । tatra aprāptatvābhimānena utpannena upādeyabhāvena upādeyatayā । bhāvanā baddhā bhavati । bhāvanābandhasyaiva ca vaivaśyam iti nāmeti bhāvaḥ ।।

bhāvanābandhasya vaivaśyeti nāmayuktatākāri duḥkhakāraṇatvaṃ kathayati

āsthāmātram anantānāṃ duḥkhānāṃ kāraṇaṃ viduḥ ।
anāsthāmātram abhitaḥ sukhānāṃ kāraṇaṃ viduḥ ।।

āsthāmātram bhāvanābandhamātram ।।

sāmānyena samarthanaṃ kṛtvā viśeṣaṃ smarati

dāmavyālakaṭā yāvad anāsthā bhāvasaṃsthitau ।
tāvan na nāma jeyā vo maṣakāṇām ivānilāḥ ।।

anāsthāḥ āsthārahitāḥ । bhāvasaṃsthitau dehādipadārthasaṃsthitau ।।

antarvāsanayā jantur dīnatām anuyātayā ।
jito bhavaty anyathā tu maṣako ḥpy amarācalaḥ ।।

anyathā vāsanārāhitye ।।

vidyate vāsanā yatra tatra cāyāti dīnatā ।
guṇāguṇānuviddhatvaṃ sato dṛṣṭaṃ hi nāsataḥ ।।

yatra ca vāsanā vidyate tatra dīnatā āyāti । pādapūraṇārthaḥ caśabdaḥ । hi yasmāt । guṇāguṇānuviddhatvam dīnatāpādakaṃ hitāhitānubandhitvam । sataḥ vāsanayāhitadehasattākasya । asataḥ vāsanārāhityena śuddhacinmātrarūpatayāsatkalpasya ।।

phalitam āha

ayaṃ so ḥham mamedaṃ cety evam antaḥ svavāsanām ।
yathā dāmādayaḥ śakra bhāvayanti tathā kuru ।।

ata iti śeṣaḥ । yathā dāmādayaḥ ayaṃ so ḥham mamedaṃ cety evaṃrūpāṃ svavāsanām ahaṅkāravāsanām । bhāvayanti vikalpayanti । tataḥ jeyā bhaviṣyantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu kathaṃ na te mama jeyā bhaviṣyantīty । atrāha

yā yā janasya vipado bhāvābhāvadaśāś ca yāḥ ।
tṛṣṇākarañjavallyās tā mañjaryaḥ kaṭukomalāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇā eva duḥkhakāritvāt kaṇṭakavallī ।।

vāsanātantubaddho ḥyaṃ loko viparivartate ।
sā suvṛddhātiduḥkhāya sukhāyocchedam āgatā ।।

viparivartate vaiparītyam bhajati ।।

dhīro ḥpy atibahujño ḥpi kulajo ḥpi mahān api ।
tṛṣṇayā badhyate jantuḥ siṃhaḥ śṛṅkhalayā yathā ।।

badhyate vivaśaḥ kriyate । tṛṣṇāgrasto hi sphuṭam eva vivaśo bhavati ।।

dehapādapasaṃsthasya hṛdayālayaśāyinaḥ ।
tṛṣṇācittakhagasyāsya vāgurā parikalpitā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dīno vāsanayā lokaḥ kṛtāntenāpakṛṣyate ।
rajjveva bālena khago vivaśo ḥniśam ucchvasan ।।

kṛtāntena mamatārūpeṇa yamena । mamatāyā eva śrīvyāsena kṛtāntatvābhidhānāt ।।

alam āyudhabhāreṇa saṅgarabhramaṇena ca ।
vāsanāṃ saviparyāsāṃ yuktyaiva tvaṃ ripoḥ kuru ।।

saviparyāsām viparyāsayuktām । ripoḥ dāmāditrayarūpasya । āyudhādibhiḥ tava na kiñcid api setsyatīti bhāvaḥ ।।

antar akṣubhite dhairye ripor amaranāyakāḥ ।
na śastrāṇi na śāstrāṇi na cāstrāṇi jayanti vaḥ ।।

akṣubhite vāsanārāhityena kṣobharahite sati ।।

dāmavyālakaṭās tv ete yuddhābhyāsavaśena ca ।
ahaṅkāramayīm antas te grahīṣyanti vāsanām ।।

ahaṅkāramayīm vayaṃ yotsyāma ity evaṃrūpām ।।

yadi te yantrapuruṣāḥ śambareṇa vinirmitāḥ ।
vāsanāṃ nāśrayiṣyanti yāsyanti tad ajayyatām ।।

yantrapuruṣāḥ anusandhānarahitā iti yāvat ।।

tat tāvad yuktiyuddhena tān prabodhayatāmarāḥ ।
yāvad abhyāsavaśato bhaviṣyanti savāsanāḥ ।।

prabodhayata vāsanāyuktān kuruta ।।

tato vadhyā bhaviṣyanti bhavatām baddhabhāvanāḥ ।
tṛṣṇāprotāśayā loke na kecana napelavāḥ ।।

nanu yadi kadācit tato ḥpi vadhyā na bhaviṣyanti tataḥ kiṃ kāryam ity । tṛṣṇāprotāśayāḥ tṛṣṇānuviddhamanasaḥ । tṛṣṇāgrastāḥ sarve eva pelavā bhavanti । ataḥ te ḥpi bhaviṣyanty eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokena brahmavākyaṃ samāpayati

samaviṣamam idaṃ jagat samagraṃ samupagataṃ sthiratāṃ svavāsanātaḥ ।
calati ca laharībharo yathābdhāv ata iha saiva cikitsyatām prayātā ।।

samaviṣamam sukhaduḥkhamayam । idam anubhūyamānam । samagraṃ jagat । svavāsanātaḥ ahaṅkāravāsanātaḥ । sthiratāṃ samupāgatam । calati ca sphulati ca । yathā laharībharaḥ abdhau samudre । ataḥ sā vāsanā eva । cikitsyatām cikitsāyogyatām । prayātā bhavatīti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe saptaviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

brahmaṇaḥ antardhānaṃ kathayati

ity uktvā bhagavān devas tatraivāntardhim āyayau ।
velāvanataṭe śabdaṃ kṛtvevāmbutaraṅgakaḥ ।।

tatraiva tasmin sthāna eva । na tv anyatra gatvā । antardhim vyavadhānam ।।

surās tv ākarṇya tadvākyaṃ jagmuḥ svām abhito diśam ।
kamalāmodam ādāya vanamālām ivānilāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dināni katicit sveṣu kānteṣu sthirakāntiṣu ।
dvirephā iva padmeṣu mandireṣu viśaśramuḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kañcit kālaṃ samāsādya svātmodayakaraṃ śubham ।
cakrur dundubhinirghoṣam pralayābhraravopamam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atha daityaiḥ saha vyomni taiḥ pātālatalotthitaiḥ ।
kālakṣepakaraṃ ghoram punar yuddham avartata ।।

kālakṣepakaram na tu śambaravadhakāri । tanmaraṇasya varṣasahasrānte brahmaṇā proktatvāt ity arthaḥ । devānām iti śeṣaḥ । samavartata samabhavat ।।

vavur asiśaraśaktimudgaraughā musulagadāparaśūgracakrasaṅghāḥ ।
aśanigiriśilāhutāśavṛkṣā ahigaruḍādimukhāni cāyudhāni ।।

kīdṛśaṃ yuddhaṃ samavartatety apekṣāyām āha vavur iti । devadaityavisṛṣṭā iti śeṣaḥ ।।

māyākṛtāyudhamahāmbughanapravāhā kṣipram prati pratidiśam parinirjagāma ।
pāṣāṇaparvatamahītaṭavṛkṣalakṣa- kṣubdhāmbupūraghanaghoṣavatī nadī drāk ।।

māyākṛtaḥ rākṣasaiḥ māyayā sampāditaḥ । āyudhamahāmbunaḥ āyudhayuktasya mahājalasya । ghanaḥ pravāhaḥ yasyāḥ । tathā pāṣāṇaparvataṃ kṣipram prati kṣipraṃ kṣipram । mahītaṭavṛkṣāṇāṃ lakṣeṣu kṣubdhaḥ sañcaraṇaśīlaḥ । yaḥ ambupūraḥ āyudhayuktaḥ ambupūraḥ । tena ghanaḥ ghoṣaḥ vidyate yasyāḥ । tādṛśī nadī āyudhamayī nadī । pratidiśaṃ nirjagāma nirgatā ।।

kena pratidiśaṃ nirjagāmeti karaṇāpekṣāyāṃ saviśeṣaṇam āha

madhyapravāhavahadulmukaśūlaśaila- prāsāsikuntaśaratomaramudgareṇa ।
gaṅgopamāmbuvalitāmaramandireṇa sarvāsu dikṣv aśanivarṣaṇakarṣaṇena ।।

aśaniyuktaṃ varṣaṇam aśanivarṣaṇam । tena yat karṣaṇam diśaḥ prati nayanam । tena kṛtvā nirjagāmeti pūrveṇa sambandhaḥ । varṣeṇa hi nadyaḥ diśaḥ vyāpnuvanti । aśanivarṣaṇakarṣaṇena kathambhūtena । madhye pravāheṇa vahanti ulmukaśūlaśailaprāsāsikuntaśaratomaramudgarāṇi yatra । tat । punaḥ kathambhūtena । sarvāsu dikṣu gaṅgopamaṃ yat ambu । tena valitāni amaramandirāṇi yena । tādṛśena ।।

pṛthvyādidāruṇaśarīramayī prahāra- dānagrahe gaganaraśmiśarīrikaiva ।
yā yopaśāmyati surāsurasiddhasenā māyākṛtā punar udeti rasena saiva ।।

yā yā । prahārāṇāṃ dānagrahe pṛthvyādivat dāruṇaṃ yat śarīram । tanmayī api । prahārāṇāṃ dāne grahaṇe ca samarthāpīti yāvat । paramārthataḥ māyārūpatvāt gaganasya yā raśmiḥ । tadrūpaṃ śarīram yasyāḥ । tādṛśī eva satī । upaśāmyati mriyate । sā surāsurasiddhasenā punaḥ udeti eva । māyākṛtā māyayā kṛteti tādṛśī । arthāt indraśambarābhyām ।।

śailopamāyudhavighaṭṭitabhūdharāṇi raktāmbupūraparipūrṇamahārṇavāni ।
devāsurendrasuraśailavirūḍhakunta- tālīvanāni kakubhāṃ vadanāny athāsan ।।

devāsurendrā eva suraśailāḥ sumeravaḥ । kuntā eva tālīvanāni । tāni ।।

udgīrṇakuntaśaraśaktigadāsicakrā helānigīrṇasuradānavamuktaśailā ।
kāṣakvaṇatkrakacadantanakhogramālā jīvānvitāpatad athāyasasiṃhavṛṣṭiḥ ।।

atha āyasasiṃhavṛṣṭiḥ ayomayānāṃ siṃhānāṃ varṣaṇam । udgīrṇam sahapatitam । kuntaśaraśaktigadāsicakram yasyāḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtā । helayā nigīrṇāḥ grastāḥ । suradānavaiḥ muktāḥ praharaṇabhūtāḥ । kvaṇan gharṣaṇavaśena śabdāyamānaḥ । tadvat ye dantanakhāḥ । teṣām ugrā mālā yasyāḥ । tathā jīvānvitā jīvayuktā ।।

ujjvālalocanaviṣajvalanātapodyad- digdāhadarśitayugāntadineśasenā ।
uḍḍīyamānaparidīrghamahīmahīdhrā mattābdhivad viṣadharāvalir ullalāsa ।।

viṣadharāṇām sarpāṇām । mattābdhivat mattasamudravat । ullalāsa ullasati sma । ujjvālaḥ udgatajvālaḥ । yaḥ locanaviṣajvalanaḥ । tenodyan । tena darśitā yugāntadineśānām kalpāntasūryāṇām । yayā । uḍḍīyamānāḥ uḍḍayanaśīlāḥ । mahyāḥ sambandhinaḥ mahīdhrāḥ parvatāḥ ।।

unnādavajramakarotkarakarkarāntar- ikṣābdhivīcivalayair valitācalendraiḥ ।
āsīj jagat sakalam eva susaṅkaṭāṅgam āvartibhir vividhahetinadīpravāhaiḥ ।।

unnādāni yāni vajrāṇi । tena karkaraḥ karkarākhyaḥ śabdaviśeṣaḥ yasya । tādṛśaṃ yat antarikṣam । tad evābdhiḥ samudraḥ । tasya vīcivalayaiḥ vīcimaṇḍalarūpaiḥ । tathā valitāḥ āvṛtāḥ । te । tathā āvartibhiḥ bhramayuktaiḥ । vividhahetayaḥ eva nadīpravāhāḥ । susaṅkaṭāṅgam atyantapūrṇasvarūpam । sakalam eva jagat āsīt ।।

śailāstraśastragaruḍācalamālitocca- nāgāṅganāsuragaṇāṅganam antarikṣam ।
āsīt kṣaṇaṃ jaladhibhiḥ kṣaṇam agnipūraiḥ pūrṇaṃ kṣaṇaṃ dinakaraiḥ kṣaṇam andhakāraiḥ ।।

kṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇam ity anena jaladhyādīnām māyākṛtatvam uktam । antarikṣam kathambhūtam । śailarūpāṇi astraśastrāṇi śailāstraśastrāṇi । teṣām madhye ye garuḍācalāḥ māṇikyaparvatāḥ । taiḥ mālitāḥ dhṛtāḥ । uccā nāgāṅganāś cāsuragaṇāṅganāś ca yena । tat । surāṅganānāṃ tu sākṣād evākāśe sthitir iti tāsām akathanam । garuḍeti gakārasya dīrghābhāvaḥ ārṣaḥ । mantrodbhāvitās tu śailāḥ astrarūpāḥ sākṣāt prahitāḥ śastrarūpāḥ ।।

garuḍaguḍaguḍākulāntarikṣa- pravisṛtahetihutāśaparvataughaiḥ ।
jagad abhavad asahyakalpakāla- jvalitasurālayabhūtalāntarālam ।।

garuḍānām yaḥ guḍaguḍaḥ guḍaguḍāśabdaḥ । tenākulam yad antarikṣam । tatra pravisṛtāḥ ye hetihutāśaparvataughāḥ । asahyaḥ yaḥ kalpakālaḥ pralayakālaḥ । tatraiva jvalitāni surālayabhūtalāntarāṇi yasya । tādṛśam abhavat ।।

udapatan vasudhātalato ḥsurā gaganam adritaṭād iva pakṣiṇaḥ ।
atibalād apatan vibudhā bhuvi pralayacālitaśailaśilā iva ।।

atibalād ity asya pūrvārdhena sambandhaḥ ।।

śarīrarūḍhonnatahetivṛkṣa- vanāvalīlagnamahāgnidāhāḥ ।
surāsurāḥ prāpur athāmbarāntaḥ kalpānilāndolitaśailaśobhām ।।

atha surāsurāḥ ambarāntaḥ ākāśamadhye । kalpānilenāndolitāḥ ye śailāḥ । teṣāṃ śobhām prāpuḥ । śarīrarūḍhāḥ yāḥ unnatahetayaḥ । tā eva vṛkṣavanāvalī । mahāgneḥ tatsaṅghaṭṭotthasya mahataḥ agneḥ । tādṛśāḥ ।।

surāsurādrīndraśarīramuktai raktapravāhair abhito bhramadbhiḥ ।
babhāra pūrṇam parito ḥmbarābdhiḥ sandhyāruṇodyacchatagaṅgam aṅgam ।।

surāsurā evādrīndrāḥ । teṣāṃ yāni śarīrāṇi । tebhyaḥ muktaiḥ । ata evābhitaḥ bhramadbhiḥ raktapravāhaiḥ kṛtvā । ambarābdhiḥ ākāśākhyaḥ samudraḥ । sandhyāruṇāḥ udyatyaḥ śataṃ gaṅgā yasya । tādṛśam aṅgam pūrṇam samyak ।।

girivarṣaṇam ambuvarṣaṇaṃ vividhogrāyudhavarṣaṇaṃ tathā ।
viṣamāśanivarṣaṇaṃ ca te śamam anyoḥnyam athāgnivarṣaṇam ।।

anayan nayamārgakovidā dalitāśeṣagirīndrabhittayaḥ ।
sasṛjuś ca samaṃ samantataḥ kakubaṅgeṣv iva puṣpavarṣaṇam ।।

atha naye astraśāntiśāstre । etāni varṣaṇāni samantataḥ śamam anayan । girivarṣaṇam ityādi । na kevalaṃ śamam anayan । kiṃ tu kakubaṅgeṣu sasṛjuś ca । te kathambhūtāḥ । dalitā aśeṣagirīndrāṇām bhittayaḥ yaiḥ । te ।।

devāsurāḥ sarasasaṅgarasambhramārtā anyoḥnyam aṅgadalanākulahetihastāḥ ।
dāmendraḍimbadahanāḥ pṛthupīṭhapīṭhaiḥ kīrṇāsṛjo nabhasi babhramur ākṣipantaḥ ।।

devāsurāḥ nabhasi babhramuḥ । sarasam vīrarasasahitam । yat saṅgaram saṅgrāmaḥ । tatra yaḥ saṃrambhaḥ udyogaḥ । anyoḥnyam aṅgadalanārtham ākulahetayaḥ hastāḥ yeṣām । dāmendrayoḥ ḍimbadahanāḥ manaḥsantāpakāritvāt cañcalāgnayaḥ । tatrāpi dāmnaḥ devāḥ indrasyāsurāḥ iti vibhāgaḥ । pṛthupīṭhāḥ pṛthusaṃsthānāḥ । ye pīṭhāḥ aṃsādipīṭhāḥ । taiḥ kīrṇāsṛjaḥ vikṣiptarudhirāḥ । tathā ākṣipantaḥ anyoḥnyam ākṣepaṃ kurvantaḥ ।।

chinnaiḥ śiraḥkarabhujorubharair bhramadbhir ākāśakośaśalabhair aśivais tadānīm ।
āsīj jagajjaṭharam abhravarair ivograir ābhāskaraṃ sthagitadiktaṭaśailajālam ।।

chinnaiḥ । ata eva bhramadbhiḥ । ata eva ca ākāśe śalabhaiḥ śalabharūpaiḥ । aśivaiḥ amaṅgalakāribhiḥ । śiraḥkarabhujorubharaiḥ । jagajjaṭharam ābhāskaram sūryaṃ tāvat । sthagitāni diktaṭāni śailajālāni ca yasya । abhravarair iva uttamameghair iva ।।

mattānalaṃ kṣubdhajalānilārkaṃ daladvanaṃ śīrṇasurāsuraugham ।
brahmāṇḍam ākhaṇḍitakuḍyakoṇam akālakalpāntakarālam āsīt ।।

ā samantāt । khaṇḍitāḥ kuḍyakoṇāḥ yasya । tat ।।

bhrāntam bhṛśam bhramitadiktaṭam adrikūṭair ātmapramāṇaghanahetihatai raṇadbhiḥ ।
kūjadbhir ārtibhir ivāgraguhaughavātaiḥ krandadbhir āpatitasiṃharavair adabhraiḥ ।।

adrikūṭaiḥ kartṛbhiḥ । bhṛśam bhrāntam bhramayuktaiḥ jñātam । katham bhrāntam । bhramitāni bhramayuktāni kṛtāni । diktaṭāni yatra । adrikūṭaiḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । ātmapramāṇā adrikūṭapramāṇāḥ । taiḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । guhaughāgrāṇāṃ vātāḥ agraguhaughavātāḥ । tadvyājeneti yāvat । ārtibhir iva kūjadbhiḥ । ārtyā yukto hi kūjati । punaḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । āpatitāḥ ye siṃhāḥ । tadvyājeneti yāvat । krandadbhiḥ ravaiḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । adabhraiḥ utkaṭaiḥ ।।

māyānadījaladhiyodhaghanāgnidāhair vṛkṣaiḥ surāsuraśavair acalaiḥ śilaughaiḥ ।
bhrāntaṃ śirastraśaraśaktigadāstravarṣair vātāvakīrṇavanaparṇavad ambarāntaḥ ।।

ambarāntaḥ ākāśamadhyam । vātenāvakīrṇam valitam । yat vanaparṇam । bhrāntam bhramayuktam āsīt । kaiḥ bhrāntam āsīt । na hi ambaramadhyasya bhramo yukta ity apekṣāyām āha māyānadītyādi । ambarāntaś cāriṇām māyānadyādīnām eva bhramaḥ ambarāntaḥ bhramatvenāropitaḥ ।।

adrīndrapakṣaparimāṇagamāgamaika- durvārahastataladāruṇatāḍanair drāk ।
āsīt patadbhaṭaśarīragirīndraghāta- vibhraṣṭadevapurapūrṇajalārṇavaughaḥ ।।

adrīndrapakṣaparimāṇāś ca te gamāgamaikadurvārāś ca । taiḥ yāni tāḍanāni । patantaḥ ye bhaṭaśarīrāṇy eva girīndrāḥ । taiḥ bhraṣṭāni yāni devapurāṇi । taiḥ pūrṇajalaś cāsau arṇavaughaḥ samudrasaptakam । āsīt jāta ity arthaḥ ।।

ghanaghuṅghumapūritāntarikṣā kṣatajākṣālitabhūdharāntarālā ।
rudhirahradavṛttivartinī vā bhuvanābhogaguhā tadākulābhūt ।।

bhuvanābhogaḥ bhuvanavistāraḥ । tadā tasmin samaye । kathambhūtā । ghanaḥ yaḥ ghuṅghumaḥ yuddhakolāhalaḥ । tenāpūritam antarikṣam yasyāḥ । kṣatajaiḥ rudhiraiḥ । kṣālitāni bhūdharāntarālāni yasyāḥ । rudhirahradarūpā yā vṛttiḥ sthānam । tatra vartata iti tādṛśī । sthitau sthitimatītivat prayogaḥ । guhā ca maṣakaghuṅghumapūritāntarikṣā vṛṣṭikṣālitabhūdharāntarālā hradavartinī ca bhavati ।।

sargāntaślokena asya raṇasya saṃsārasāmyaṃ kathayati

anantadikprasaravikārakāriṇī kṣayodayonmukhasukhaduḥkhadāyinī ।
raṇakriyāsurasurasaṅghasaṅkaṭā tadābhavat khalu sadṛśīha saṃsṛteḥ ।।

khalu niścaye । sā raṇakriyā iha samsṛtisadṛśī abhavat । kathambhūtā । anantadikṣu yaḥ prasaraḥ । tena vikāram hiṃsākhyaṃ vikāram । kṣayodayonmukhe ye sukhaduḥkhe । te dadātīti tādṛśī । asurasurasaṅghena saṅkaṭā sambādhā । saṃsṛtir api prasareṇa bandhākhyaṃ vikāraṃ karoti । sukhaduḥkhadāyinī nānāpadārthasaṅkaṭā ca bhavati ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe aṣṭāviṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

yuddham upasaṃharati

evamprāyākulārambhair asurair asuhāribhiḥ ।
mahāsāhasasaṃrabdhair ārabdhamaraṇai raṇaiḥ ।।

māyayātha vivādena sandhinā vigraheṇa ca ।
palāyanena dhairyeṇa cchadmanopāyanena ca ।।

kārpaṇyenāstrayuddhena svāntardhānaiś ca bhūriśaḥ ।
kṛtaḥ sa samaro devais triṃśad varṣāṇi pañca ca ।।

devaiḥ triṃśat pañca ca varṣāṇi pañcatriṃśadvarṣāṇi । kena kena prakāreṇa kṛta ity apekṣāyām māyayetyādi । upāyanena samīpagamanena । kārpaṇyena dīnatayā । svāntardhānaiḥ māyodbhāvitaiḥ nijagopanaiḥ । asuraiḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । evamprāyaḥ bāhulyenaitādṛśaḥ । taiḥ । asuhāribhiḥ jīvahāribhiḥ । mahāsāhase saṃrabdhāḥ saṃrambhayuktāḥ । punaḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । raṇaiḥ kṛtvā ārabdham maraṇam yaiḥ । tilakam ।।

varṣāṇi divasān māsān daśāṣṭau pañca sapta ca ।
varṣāṇi petur vṛkṣāgnihetyambvaśanibhūbhṛtām ।।

vṛkṣāgnihetyambvaśanibhūbhṛtām varṣāṇi vṛṣṭayaḥ । aṣṭau māsān । pañca sapta ca dvādaśeti yāvat । divasān । arthāt anyasmin kāle sandhyādir evābhūt iti jñeyam ।।

etāvatā tu kālena dṛḍhābhyāsād ahaṅkṛteḥ ।
dāmādayo ḥham ity āsthāṃ jagṛhur grastacetasaḥ ।।

ahaṅkṛteḥ vayaṃ yotsyāma ity evaṃrūpasyāhaṅkārasya । grastam ahaṅkāragrastam । cetaḥ yeṣām ।।

naikaṭyātiśayād yadvad darpaṇam bimbavad bhavet ।
abhyāsātiśayāt tadvat te ḥpy ahaṅkāritāṃ gatāḥ ।।

naikaṭyātiśayāt sānnidhyodrekāt । bimbavat pratibimbayuktam ।।

yadvad dūrataraṃ vastu nādarśe pratibimbate ।
padārthavāsanā tadvad anabhyāsān na jāyate ।।

dūrataram bahudūrāt । padārtheṣu yuddhādibhāveṣu । vāsanā mayedaṃ kṛtam ity evaṃrūpaḥ saṃskāraḥ ।।

yadā dāmādayo jātā jātāhaṅkāravāsanāḥ ।
tadā me jīvitam me ḥrtha iti dainyam upāgaman ।।

yadā dāmādayaḥ dāmavyālakaṭāḥ । ahaṅkāravāsanā yeṣām । tādṛśāḥ । tadā me jīvitam me artha iti evaṃrūpam । upāgaman upāgatāḥ । ahaṅkārābhāve hi bhittirahitam mamatārūpaṃ dainyaṃ na syāt eva । tatsattāyāṃ tu prāptādhāratvena tad durnivāram eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

bhayavāsanayā grastā mohavāsanayā hatāḥ ।
āśāpāśanibaddhās te tataḥ kṛpaṇatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

tataḥ dainyopāgamanānantaram । bhayasya dehanāśaśaṅkādyutpannāyā bhīteḥ । yā vāsanā saṃskāraḥ । tayā grastāḥ vaśīkṛtāḥ । tathā mohasya anātmani śarīrādau ātmatvabhāvanārūpasyājñānasya । tayā hatāḥ bādhitāḥ । āśāpāśaiḥ svātmatvābhimānaviṣayīkṛtaśarīrādyarthaṃ dhanādiviṣayaiḥ āśāpāśaiḥ । nibaddhāḥ svādhinīkṛtāḥ । kṛpaṇatām dainyasya parāṃ kāṣṭhām ।।

nanu tataḥ kiṃ teṣāṃ sampannam ity । atrāha

mudhaiva hy anahaṅkārair mamatvam upakalpitam ।
rajjvām bhujaṅgatvam iva dāmavyālakaṭais tataḥ ।।

hi niścaye । anahaṅkāraiḥ ahaṅkārarahitaiḥ । dāmavyālakaṭaiḥ । tataḥ ahaṅkāravaśena dainyagamanānantaram । mamatvam mamatā । mudhā eva vyartham eva । upakalpitam kalpanayā dṛḍhīkṛtam । rajjvām bhujaṅgatvam iva । atyantam mithyābhūtam ity arthaḥ ।।

mamatvam eva kathayati

āpādamastakaṃ dehalateyam bhavatu sthirā ।
mameti tṛṣṇākṛpaṇā dīnatāṃ te samāyayuḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sthirībhavatu me dehaḥ sukhāyāstu dhanam mama ।
iti baddhadhiyāṃ teṣāṃ dhairyam antardhim āyayau ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

avāsanatvād vapuṣām anāsthatvāt suradviṣām ।
yābhūt prahāraparatā mārjitaivāśu sābhavat ।।

suradviṣām dāmavyālakaṭānām । avāsanatvāt vāsanārāhityāt । tathā vapuṣām anāsthatvāt śarīrāsthārahitatvāt । yā prahāraparatā abhūt pūrvam āsīt । sā āśu mārjitā naṣṭā । ahaṅkāraprabhāvena dehanāśādibhayotpādāt ity arthaḥ ।।

kathaṃ sthirā jagaty asmin bhavema iti cintayā ।
vedhitā dīnatāṃ jagmuḥ padmā iva nirambhasaḥ ।।

vedhitāḥ vyāptāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ tv arthānnapāneṣu svāhaṅkṛtimatāṃ ratiḥ ।
babhūva bhavabhāvasthā bhīṣaṇā bhavabhāginī ।।

svā ahaṅkṛtir dehaviṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ vidyate yeṣām । teṣāṃ ratiḥ āsaktiḥ । bhavabhāvasthā saṃsārikapadārthaviṣayā । bhavabhāginī saṃsārapradā ।।

atha tasmin raṇe bhītyā sāpekṣatvam upāyayuḥ ।
mattebhagaṇasaṃrabdhā vane hariṇakā iva ।।

sāpekṣatvam mā mariṣyāma ity evaṃrūpāpekṣāsahitatvam । bhītyā maraṇabhayena । hariṇakāḥ kathambhūtāḥ । mattebhānām yaḥ gaṇaḥ । tena saṃrabdhāḥ kṣobhayuktāḥ kṛtāḥ ।।

sāpekṣatvam eva spaṣṭayati

mariṣyāmo mariṣyāma iti cintāhatāśayāḥ ।
mandam mandaṃ kila bhremuḥ kupitairāvaṇe raṇe ।।

bhremuḥ bhramanti sma ।।

śarīraikārthināṃ teṣām bhītānām maraṇād iti ।
alpasattvatayā mūrdhni kṛtam āpatpradam padam ।।

śarīram ekam kevalam । arthayante iti tādṛśānām । tathā maraṇād bhītānām । iti pūrvoktaprakāreṇa । alpasattvatayā kartryā । alpasattvās te jātā iti bhāvaḥ । padaṃ kathambhūtam । āpatpradam vipatpradam ity arthaḥ ।।

atha pramlānasattvās te hantum agragatam bhaṭam ।
na śekur indhanakṣīṇā havir dagdhum ivāgnayaḥ ।।

pramlānasattvāḥ naṣṭadhairyāḥ । na śekuḥ na samarthāḥ jātāḥ । kṣīṇam indhanaṃ yeṣām ।।

vibudhānām praharatāṃ sudamyatām upāgatāḥ ।
kṣatavikṣatasarvāṅgās tasthuḥ sāmānyavad bhaṭāḥ ।।

vibudhānām devānām । sudamyatām sunigrāhyatām ।।

bahunātra kim uktena maraṇād bhītacetasaḥ ।
daityā deveṣu valgatsu dudruvuḥ samarājirāt ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

teṣu dravatsu sarveṣu sarvato dānavādriṣu ।
dāmavyālakaṭākhyeṣu vikhyāteṣv asurālaye ।।

taddaityasainyam apatat khād vidrutam itas tataḥ ।
kalpāntapavanādhūtaṃ tārājālam ivābhitaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kutrāpatad ity apekṣāyām āha

amarācalakuñjeṣu śikharāṇāṃ śilāsu ca ।
taṭeṣu vārirāśīnām payodapaṭaleṣu ca ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

sāgarāvartagarteṣu śvabhreṣv atha saritsu ca ।
jaṅgaleṣu diganteṣu jvalatsu vipineṣu ca ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tadraṇotsannakośeṣu grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca ।
aṭavīṣūgrayakṣāsu maruṣūdyaddavāgniṣu ।।

teṣām asurāṇām । raṇena utsannaḥ viśīrṇaḥ । kośaḥ madhyaṃ yeṣām ।।

lokālokācalānteṣu parvateṣu hradeṣu ca ।
andhradramiḍakāśmīrapārasīkapureṣu ca ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nānāmbhodhitaraṅgāsu gaṅgājalaghaṭāsu ca ।
dvīpāntareṣu dūreṣu jambuṣaṇḍalatāsu ca ।।

dūreṣu dūravartiṣu ।।

sarvataḥ parvatākārāḥ patitās te ḥsurālayaḥ ।
visphoṭitāṅgacaraṇā vibhinnakarabāhavaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

śākhālagnāntratantrīkā muktaraktavahacchaṭāḥ ।
vyastāṅgakhuramūrdhāno niṣkrāntakupitekṣaṇāḥ ।।

niṣkrānte bhūmau patite । kupite īkṣaṇe yeṣām । te ।।

svāyudhā valanāvegacchinnakaṅkaṭahetayaḥ ।
dūrāpātaviparyastapatannānāvidhāṃśukāḥ ।।

dūrāt yaḥ āpātaḥ । tena viparyastāni viparyāsaṃ gatāni । ata eva patanti aṃśukāni yeṣām ।।

kaṇṭhalagnaśirastrāṇakhaṭatkārograbhītayaḥ ।
śilāśitaśikhāprotadehabhāgāvalambinaḥ ।।

kaṇṭhalagnāni yāni śirastrāṇāni । teṣāṃ yaḥ khaṭatkāraḥ śabdaviśeṣaḥ । tataḥ ugrā bhītiḥ yeṣām ।।

śalmalyagradṛḍhāpātaprotakaṅkaṭaśaṅkavaḥ ।
suśilāphalakāsphālaśatadhāśīrṇamastakāḥ ।।

śalmalyagreṣu vṛkṣaviśeṣāgreṣu । tena protaḥ kaṅkaṭaśaṅkavaḥ kavacakīlakāḥ yeṣām ।।

sargāntaślokena samāptiṃ karoti

sarva eva sakalāsu saśastrāḥ pātamātrasamanantaram eva ।
dikṣu nāśam agamann asurendrāḥ pāṃsavo ḥmbudhigatāḥ payasīva ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇa ekonatriṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ । tadā dāmādayaḥ kīdṛśāḥ sampannā ity । atrāha

iti tuṣṭeṣu deveṣu dānaveṣu hateṣu ca ।
dāmavyālakaṭā dīnā babhūvur bhayavihvalāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

nanu śambaraḥ kiṃ kṛtavān ity । atrāha

jajvāla kupitaḥ kopī kalpāntāgnir iva jvalan ।
śambaraḥ śamitānīko dāmavyālakaṭān prati ।।

dāmādīn prati śambaraḥ kupito ḥbhūd iti piṇḍārthaḥ ।।

śambarasya bhayād gatvā pātālam atha saptamam ।
dāmavyālakaṭās tasthus tyaktvā dānavamaṇḍalam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yamasya kiṅkarās tatra vetālatrāsanakṣamāḥ ।
kukuhā nāma tiṣṭhanti narakārṇavapālakāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

taiḥ sārdhaṃ nītavantas te tatra dāmādayo ḥvadhim ।
daśavarṣasahasrāntām āttānantakuvāsanāḥ ।।

taiḥ kukuhaiḥ । daśavarṣasahasrāntām daśavarṣasahasrasaṅkhyāparyantām । avadhim kālāvadhim । te dāmādayaḥ nītavantaḥ nayanti sma । āttāḥ dhāritāḥ । kuvāsanāḥ dhanādiviṣayāḥ ninditāḥ saṃskārāḥ । yaiḥ ।।

iyam me vanitā ramyā mameyam prabhuteti ca ।
kukuhasnehabaddhānāṃ kālas teṣāṃ vyavartata ।।

vyavartata pariṇato ḥbhūt ।।

dharmarājo ḥtha taṃ deśaṃ kadācit samupāyayau ।
mahānarakakāryāṇāṃ vicārārthaṃ yadṛcchayā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

aparijñātam enaṃ te dharmarājaṃ trayo ḥsurāḥ ।
na praṇemur vināśāya sāmānyam iva kiṅkaram ।।

aparijñātam iti viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa hetuḥ ।।

atha vaivasvatenaite jvalitaśvabhrabhūmiṣu ।
vihitabhrūparispandam ādeśena niveśitāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

tatra te karuṇākrandāḥ sasuhṛddārabāndhavāḥ ।
dagdhāḥ saparṇaviṭapā vṛkṣā iva davānalaiḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

svayā vāsanayā jātās tayaiva krūrayā punaḥ ।
vadhakarmakarākārāḥ kairātā rājakiṅkarāḥ ।।

vadhakarma kurvantīti vadhakarmakarāḥ । tadvat ākāraḥ yeṣām । te । atyantahiṃsakā ity arthaḥ ।।

tajjanmātha parityajya jātāḥ suhmeṣu vāyasāḥ ।
tadante gṛdhratāṃ yātās tato ḥpi bakatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

tajjanma rājakiṅkarajanma । suhmeṣu janapadaviśeṣeṣu ।।

śavaratvaṃ trigarteṣu meṣatvam barbareṣu ca ।
magadheṣv atha kīṭatvaṃ cakrus te vaktrabuddhayaḥ ।।

vaktrabuddhayaḥ iti viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa hetuḥ ।।

anubhūyetarām atra citrāṃ yoniparamparām ।
adya matsyāḥ sthitā rāma kaśmīrāraṇyapalvale ।।

atra pūrvokteṣu deśeṣu । itarām yoniṃ śavaratvādibhinnām ।।

kathambhūtāḥ te tatra sthitā ity । atrāha

dāvāgnikvathitālpālpapaṅkakalkānupāyinaḥ ।
na mriyante na jīvanti jarajjambālajarjarāḥ ।।

kalkam malam ।।

saṅgṛhya pūrvoktayonikleśaṃ kathayati

vicitrayonisaṃrambham anubhūya punaḥ punaḥ ।
bhūtvā bhūtvā punar naṣṭās taraṅgā jaladhāv iva ।।

proktanyāyeneti bhāvaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokena dāmādivṛttāntaṃ tāvat sthāpayati

bhavajaladhigatās te vāsanāvātanunnās tṛṇam iva ciram ūḍhā deharūpais taraṅgaiḥ ।
upaśamam anuyātā rāma nādyāpy anantam parikalaya mahattvaṃ dāruṇaṃ vāsanāyāḥ ।।

ūḍhāḥ īritāḥ । upaśamam vāsanārāhityam । phalitaṃ kathayati anantam iti । yataḥ dāmādibhiḥ vāsanāvaśata evaṃvidhā yātanā prāptā ataḥ tvaṃ vāsanāyāḥ ahaṃmametirūpāyā vāsanāyāḥ । anantam antarahitam । mahattvam parikalaya niścinu ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe triṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ । pūrvoktam anusmārayati

ataḥ prabodhāya tava vacmi rāma mahāmate ।
dāmavyālakaṭanyāyo mā te ḥstv iti na līlayā ।।

prabodhāya vāsanāvaśyaṃ tyājyety evaṃrūpāya prakṛṣṭabodhāya । parihāsārtham iti yāvat । avañcakatvād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

dāmādivṛttāntāvaṣṭambhena nānāvidham upadeśam prastauti

avivekānusandhānāc cittam āpadam īdṛśīm ।
anantataraduḥkhāya parigṛhṇāti helayā ।।

avivekasya anātmani dehādāv ātmābhimānarūpasyāvicārasya । anusandhānāt sphuraṇāt । cittam kartṛ । īdṛśīm dāmādyanubhūtāpatsadṛśīm । āpadam karmabhūtām । anantataraduḥkhāya anantataraduḥkhārtham । helayā prayatnaṃ vinā । parigṛhṇāti anubhavati । ato ḥviveka eva tyājya iti bhāvaḥ ।।

vāsanātyāgam prati uttejanāya dāmādibhir anubhūtāṃ vipadaṃ kathayati

kva kilāmaravidhvaṃsiśambarānīkanāthatā ।
kva tāpataptajambālajalajarjaramīnatā ।।

uttarārdhe kaśmīreṣv iti śeṣaḥ ।।

kva dhairyam amarānīkavidrāvaṇakaram mahat ।
kva kirātamahīpālakṣudrakiṅkararūpatā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kva nāma nirahaṅkāracitsattvodāradhīratā ।
kva mithyāvāsanāveśād ahaṅkārakukalpanā ।।

nirahaṅkāram deho ḥham iti sthūlāhaṅkārarahitam । sattvam sattvākhyam manaḥ । tena yā udāradhīratā maraṇādibhayarāhityena udārabhāvaḥ dhīrabhāvaś ca । sā kva nāma bhavati । mithyābhūtā yā vāsanā saṃskāraḥ । tasyā āveśāt āveśena utpannā । ahaṅkārakukalpanā deho ḥham ity evaṃrūpāhaṅkārarūpā ninditā kalpanā । anayor antaraṃ svayam eva paśyeti bhāvaḥ ।।

śākhāpratānagahanā saṃsāraviṣamañjarī ।
ahaṅkārāṅkurād eva samudetīyam ātatā ।।

iyam puraḥsphurantī । śākhāpratānaiḥ nānāpadārtharūpaiḥ śākhāsamūhaiḥ । saṃsāra eva viṣamañjarī viṣalatā kartrī । ahaṅkāra evāṅkuraḥ bījam । tasmāt udeti prādurbhavati । ahaṅkārābhāve kasya kiṃrūpaḥ saṃsāraḥ syāt । suṣuptau hi ahaṅkāravilaye sarve saṃsāraṃ nānubhavantīti bhāvaḥ ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

ahaṅkāram ato rāma mārjayāntaḥ prayatnataḥ ।
ahaṃ na kaścid eveti mārjayitvā sukhī bhava ।।

he rāma । yasmāt ahaṅkāra evāpad asti ataḥ tvam ahaṅkāram deho ḥham ityādirūpaṃ sthūlam ahaṅkāram । antaḥ manasi । prayatnataḥ samyagjñānākhyaprayatnena । mārjaya utpuṃsaya । tataḥ kim mama setsyatīty । atrāha aham iti । aham sthūladehādirūpaḥ aham । naiva kaścit asmi । śuddhacinmātratattvasyaiva sattābhāktvayogāt । iti evam । arthāt ahaṅkāram mārjayitvā tvam sukhī dehādinairapekṣyakṛtamahāsukhayuktaḥ । bhava । dehādyapekṣāvaśād eva hi puruṣaḥ duḥkhī bhavati । nanu dehaṃ tāvat dehāpekṣā kva gacchatīti cen । kiṃ tu tadviṣayāhambhāvahīnatayā tadbhāvābhāvacintāḥ na vyākulīkurvanti । tadyātrāmātranimittaṃ kṛtasya pravāhāgatasya prayatnasya tu na tādṛśī duḥkhakāritāstīty alam ।।

nanv ahaṅkāreṇa ko doṣa utpādyate yena puruṣo duḥkhī bhavatīty । atrāha

ahaṅkārāmbudacchannam paramārthendumaṇḍalam ।
rasāyanamayaṃ śītam adṛśyatvam upāgatam ।।

paramārthaḥ paramopādeyabhūtaḥ paramātmā । sa evāhlādakāritvāt induḥ । tasya maṇḍalam sarvavyāpakaṃ svarūpam । ahaṅkāra eva deho ḥham ity evaṃrūpaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ eva । ambudaḥ meghaḥ । tena channam āvṛtaṃ sat । adṛśyatvam ahamparāmarśaviṣayatvāyogyatām । dehābhimānāviṣṭo hi puruṣaḥ paramārthataḥ svarūpabhūtam api cinmātratattvaṃ nāhantayā parāmṛśati । rasāyanamayam mahānairapekṣyādhāratvenāmṛtasvarūpam । ata eva śītam apekṣāsvarūpasantāparahitam । ataś ca sukhasvarūpaparamātmācchādakatvena yuktam evāhaṅkārasya santāpakāridoṣotpādakatvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

ahaṅkāraprabhāvenaiva tvam prādurbhūto ḥsīty abhiprāyeṇāha

ahaṅkārapiśācāttā dāmavyālakaṭās trayaḥ ।
gatāḥ sattām asanto ḥpi māyāmāhātmyadānavāḥ ।।

māyāyāḥ śambarāmbaraprayuktāyāḥ māyāyāḥ । māhātmyena prabhāvena । dānavāḥ dānavarūpatāṃ yātāḥ । ata evāsantaḥ api trayaḥ damavyālakaṭāḥ । ahaṅkāra eva piśācaḥ । tenāttāḥ gṛhītāḥ santaḥ । sattām vayaṃ dāmādaya ity evaṃrūpāṃ sattām । evaṃ tvam api māyāmāhātmyena manuṣyarūpatāṃ yātaḥ । ata evāsan api svāhaṅkāravaśād eva svasattām anubhavasīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu te dāmādayaḥ kaśmīreṣu kasmin palvale santīty । atrāha

kaśmīreṣu mahāpadmasarasītīrapalvale ।
adya matsyāḥ sthitā rāma śevālalavalālasāḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

atra śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

nāsato vidyate bhāvo nābhāvo vidyate sataḥ ।
te hy asantaḥ kathaṃ santaḥ sampannā iti me vada ।।

hi yasmāt । asataḥ sattākartṛtvam abhajataḥ । bhāvaḥ sattā । śaśiśṛṅgādāv adarśanāt । sataḥ sattākartṛtām bhajataḥ । paṅkanikṣipte bīje adarśanāt । ataḥ asantaḥ śambaramāyodbhāvitatvena sattākartṛtvam abhajanto ḥpi । te dāmādayaḥ । santaḥ sattāyuktāḥ । kathaṃ sampannāḥ । me vada kathayety arthaḥ ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaraṃ kathayati

evam etan mahābāho nāsad bhavati hi kvacit ।
kadācit kiñcid apy etad bṛhad bhavati vā tanu ।।

etat tvayoktaṃ vastu । kvacit kutrāpi deśe kāle vā । sat na bhavati sattāṃ na bhajati । arthāt sad asad veti jñeyam । nanu tarhi katham indriyāgocaratvenāsatām paramāṇūnām indriyalabhyatvena satsvarūpasya ghaṭasya bhāvaḥ dṛśyate sataḥ ghaṭasya kālavaśataḥ asatsvarūpaparamāṇutā cety । atrāha kadācid iti । kiñcit api paramārthataḥ anirvacanīyasanmātrarūpatvenāvasthitam api । etat pratyakṣeṇānumānena ca puraḥsphurat sattvāsattvābhyāṃ jñātaṃ ghaṭaparamāṇvādirūpaṃ vastu । bṛhat bhavati tanu vā bhavati । tathā ca nātra sato ḥsattvam asato vā sattvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

tathā ca dāmādiṣu ko nyāya ity । atrāha

kim asat sat sthitam brūhi kiṃ tat sad vāpy asat sthitam ।
nidarśanenānenaiva kariṣye tvadvibodhanam ।।

tvam prathamam brūhi । kim bravīmīty apekṣāyām āha kim itīti । kim vastu । asat sthitam asadrūpaṃ sampannam । kiṃ vāsat api bhavat । sat sthitam sadrūpaṃ sampannam । nanu matkathanena kiṃ setsyatīty । atrāha nidarśaneneti । tataḥ aham anena nidarśanena tvaduktena dṛṣṭāntena । tvadvibodhanaṃ kariṣye । anyathā tvaṃ na śroṣyasīti bhāvaḥ ।।

śrīrāmaḥ kathayati

santa eva sthitāḥ santo brahman vayam amī kila ।
dāmādayas tv asanto ḥpi vacmi santaḥ sthitā iti ।।

kila niścaye । amī pratyakṣaṃ sphurantaḥ । santaḥ eva santaḥ sthitāḥ bhavāmaḥ । na hi asmākam asattvaṃ kenāpi prakāreṇa yuktam parasparam ālāpādyarthakriyāsambhavāt । tu pakṣāntare । dāmādayaḥ asantaḥ api śambaramāyodbhāvitatvenāsanto ḥpi santaḥ । santaḥ sthitāḥ bhavanti ।।

śrīvasiṣṭhaḥ anena nidarśanena śrīrāmasya bodhanaṃ karoti

yathā dāmādayo rāma sthitā māyāmayā iha ।
asatyā eva satyābhā mṛgatṛṣṇāmbupūravat ।।

tathaiveme vayam api sasurāsuradānavāḥ ।
asatyā eva valgāmo yāma āyāma eva ca ।।

māyāmayāḥ māyāsvarūpāḥ । dṛṣṭāntam uktvā dārṣṭāntikaṃ kathayati tathaiveme vayam iti । ime parasparam ālāpaṃ kurvantaḥ । yāmaḥ āyāmaḥ iti sarvāsāṃ kriyāṇām upalakṣaṇam । sarvaṃ kurma ity arthaḥ ।।

nanu vayaṃ kathaṃ dāmādivad asadrūpā ity । atrāha

alīkam eva tvadbhāvo madbhāvo ḥlīkam eva ca ।
anubhūto ḥpy asadrūpaḥ svapne svamaraṇaṃ yathā ।।

tvadbhāvaḥ rāmeti nāmnaḥ tava sattā । alīkam eva asatyam eva bhavati । madbhāvaḥ vasiṣṭheti nāmadheyasya mama sattā ca । alīkam eva bhavati । kathambhūtaḥ tvanmadbhāvaḥ । anubhūtaḥ api asmin samaye anubhūyamāno ḥpi । asadrūpaḥ । atra viśvāsotpādakaṃ dṛṣṭāntaṃ kathayati svapna iti । ayam bhāvaḥ । yathā puruṣaḥ svapne svamaraṇam asatyam eva paśyati । anyathā svapnadraṣṭur abhāvena kaḥ svamaraṇam paśyet । tathā tvadbhāvamadbhāvāv api āvām paśyāvaḥ । anyathā tvayi tvattāyām eva mayi mattāyām eva niṣṭhitāyāṃ tvam mām prati tvam iti na paśyeḥ । svam praty aham iti tvayi tvattvasya mayi mattvasya niṣṭhitatvāt iti । anubhūta iti vartamāne niṣṭhāprayogaḥ ।।

etad eva dṛṣṭāntāntareṇa kathayati

mṛto bandhur yathā svapne ḥpy anubhūto ḥpy asanmayaḥ ।
mṛto ḥyam iti ca jñaptir bhaved evam idaṃ jagat ।।

yathā mṛtaḥ bandhuḥ svapne anubhūtaḥ api asanmayaḥ asatya eva । mṛto ḥyam iti jñaptiḥ jāgratkālīnaḥ bodhaḥ yataḥ asti । evam anena prakāreṇa । anubhūtam api jagat asad bhavati । jñānināṃ nāstīty atadviṣayo bodho bhavati । ajñānāṃ tu suṣuptikālīnaḥ । anyathā nāsīd iti jāgratkālīnaparāmarśāsambhavād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu tarhi sarveṣāṃ kathaṃ na maduktānuguṇyenaiva bodho ḥstīty । atrāha

eṣā hi mūḍhaviṣayā noktir eva virājate ।
abhyāsena vinodeti nānubhūter apahnavaḥ ।।

hi niścaye । na tu tajjñaviṣayā । eṣā uktiḥ taveti śeṣaḥ । tava na virājate na śobhate । tajjñatvād iti bhāvaḥ । nanu tarhi tvanmadbhāvānubhūteḥ kiṃ karomīty । atrāha abhyāseneti । abhyāsena viruddhānubhavābhyāsena । anubhūteḥ pūrvasyāḥ anubhūteḥ । ataḥ tvam api tvadbhāvasadbhāvāsatyatānubhavam eva kuru yena tvadbhāvasadbhāvānubhūtiḥ na syād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanv abhyāsena vinā katham anubhūter apahnavaḥ na sampadyate ity । atrāha

niścayo ḥntaḥ prarūḍho yaḥ sa yatnābhyasanaṃ vinā ।
nāśam āyāti loke ḥsmin na kadācana kasyacit ।।

niścayaḥ anubhavaḥ । prarūḍhaḥ dṛḍhībhūtaḥ । svabhāva evāyam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu tarhi karuṇākrāntāḥ tajjñāḥ sarveṣāṃ kathaṃ naitad evopadiśantīty । atrāha

idaṃ jagad asad brahma satyam ity eva vakti yaḥ ।
tam unmattam ivonmattā vimūḍhā vihasanty alam ।।

idam puraḥ sphurat । jagat asat bhavati । brahma bāhyāntaḥkaraṇāviṣayaṃ saccinmātrarūpam brahmākhyaṃ vastu । yaḥ vakti kathayati । unmattāḥ svārthāparijñānena unmattarūpāḥ । unmattam iva vihasanti । tadupadeśaśravaṇasya tu kā kathety । ato ḥsau na vaktīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu kimarthaṃ te taṃ hasantīty । atrāha

akṣībakṣībayor aikyaṃ kva kilehājñatajjñayoḥ ।
āndhyaprakāśayor bodhe syāc chāyātapayor iva ।।

akṣībakṣībayoḥ svātmānandākhyamadhupānena tadapānena ca saṃsāram prati vismaraṇāvismaraṇaśīlayoḥ । tajjñājñayor bodhe anubhave । aikyam parasparasammatirūpam aikyam । na syād ity arthaḥ । na hi kṣībākṣībayor iha bodhe sammatiḥ dṛśyata iti bhāvaḥ । ataḥ ete hasantīty āśayaḥ । chāyātapayor iva । yathā āndhyaprakāśarūpayoḥ chāyātapayoḥ bodhe padārthaprakaṭanākhye bodhe । aikyaṃ nāsti ।।

nanu kimarthaṃ tayoḥ bodhe aikyaṃ nāstīty । atrāha

yatnenāpy anubhūte ḥrthe satye kartum apahnavam ।
tajjño ḥjñaś ca na śaknoti śava ākramaṇaṃ yathā ।।

anubhūte । ata eva satye satyatayā jñāte । arthe cinmātrākhye jagadākhye ca vastuni । tajjñaḥ ajñaḥ ca yatnenāpi apahnavaṃ kartuṃ na śaknoti । puraḥsphurattvāt । na hi puraḥ sphurat vastu kaścid apahnotuṃ śaknoti । ata eva tayoḥ bodhe aikyaṃ nāstīti bhāvaḥ । kaḥ yathā na śaknoti । śavo yathā । yathā śavaḥ ākramaṇam padārthākramaṇam । na śaknoti ।।

nanu tarhi ajño ḥpy etad eva kathayatv ity । atrāha

brahma sarvaṃ jagad iti vaktuṃ tajjñasya yujyate ।
yato ḥvidyānanubhave sa tad evānubhūtavān ।।

sarvaṃ jagad brahma bhavati । vaktum tajjñasya cinmātrākhyabrahmasvarūpajñasya । yataḥ sa eva tajjñaḥ eva । anubhūtavān dṛṣṭavān । avidyāyāḥ ananubhave jagatpadārtharūpaiḥ bhāvābhāvaiḥ upalakṣitāyāḥ avidyāyāḥ adarśane sati ।।

punar api etad eva kathayati

prabuddhaviṣaye hy eṣā rāma vāk pravirājate ।
buddhasyāsmīti rūpeṇa kila nāsty eva kiñcana ।।

he rāma । eṣā vāk sarvam brahmeti vāk । prabuddhākhyo yaḥ viṣayaḥ yogyo deśaḥ । arthāt abuddhaviṣaye na rājate iti jñeyam । nanu kathaṃ tatraiva rājate ity । atrāha buddhasyeti । yataḥ buddhasya kiñcana kiñcid api śarīrādikam । asmīti rūpeṇa nāsti asmīti jñānaviṣayaṃ nāsti । ayam bhāvaḥ । ajñaḥ deho ḥham iti niścitaḥ tadupayogīni vastūny api satyānīti jānāti । anyathā tadarthaṃ rātrindinam prayatnaparatvāyogāt । jñas tu dehābhimānābhāvāt tadupayogiṣu satyatāṃ na jānāti । anyathā tadviṣayāyā upekṣāyā ayogāt । iti tajjñasyaiva sarvam brahmeti vaktuṃ yuktaṃ nājñasyeti ।।

nanu tajjñasyāsyā anubhūteḥ kadācid apahnavo ḥsti na vety । atrāha

brahmaivedam paraṃ śāntam ity evānubhavan sudhīḥ ।
apahnavaḥ svānubhūteḥ kartuṃ tasya na yujyate ।।

sudhīḥ jñaḥ । śāntam param brahmaiva bhavati । anubhavan bhavati । asyāḥ svānubhūteḥ apahnavaḥ kartuṃ na yujyate yukto na bhavati ।।

nanu tarhi tvaṃ kathaṃ śrīvasiṣṭha iti nāmayogyo ḥsīty । atrāha

parasmād vyatirekeṇa nāham ātmani kiñcana ।
hemanīvormikāditvaṃ na mayy asti vasiṣṭhatā ।।

aham vasiṣṭhākhyaḥ aham । parasmāt uttīrṇāt cinmātrāt । tvaṃ tu yat paśyasi tat paśyeti bhāvaḥ । ato mayi vasiṣṭhatā vasiṣṭheti nāmayogyatā । nāsti । yathā ūrmikāditvaṃ hemani nāsti । ato ḥham api vasiṣṭho nāsmīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu yadi tvaṃ svātmanīdṛśo ḥsi tarhi mūḍhaḥ kīdṛśo ḥstīty । atrāha

bhūtatvavyatirekeṇa mūḍho nātmani kiñcana ।
ūrmyādibuddhau hemeva nājñe ḥsti paramārthatā ।।

mūḍhaḥ cinmātrasvarūpaparamātmajñānahīnaḥ । bhūtatvavyatirekeṇa dehabhāvād ṛte । kiñcana kiñcid api । tajjñas tu taṃ yadrūpam paśyati tadrūpam paśyatv iti bhāvaḥ । yataḥ ajñe paramārthatā paramārthabhūtacinmātrabhāvaḥ । sa hi svaṃ cinmātrarūpaṃ na paśyati । yathā ūrmyādibuddhau ūrmikādibuddhau sati ।।

saṅgṛhya kathayati

mithyāhantāmayo mūḍhaḥ satyaikātmamayaḥ sudhīḥ ।
yujyate na kvacin nāma svabhāvāpahnavo ḥnayoḥ ।।

mūḍhaḥ ajñaḥ । mithyābhūtā yā ahantā dehaviṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ । tanmayaḥ bhavati । satyaḥ satyabhūtaḥ । yaḥ ekātmā sarvavyāpakaḥ paramātmā । anayoḥ mūḍhasudhiyoḥ । svabhāvasya mithyāhaṅkārākhyasya paramārthākhyasya ca svarūpasya । apahnavaḥ apalāpaḥ । na hi puraḥ sphurat svasvarūpaṃ kaścid apahnotuṃ śaknoti ।।

etad eva sadṛṣṭāntam āha

yo yanmayas tasya tasmin yujyate ḥpahnavaḥ katham ।
puruṣasya ghaṭo ḥsmīti vākyam unmattataiva hi ।।

yaḥ puruṣaḥ । yanmayaḥ niścayadvāreṇa yatsvarūpaḥ syāt । tasya puruṣasya । apahnavaḥ katham syāt । puruṣasya ghaṭo ḥsmīti vākyam unmattatā eva bhavati । ataḥ brahmātmatve niścitasya jñasya sthūladehātmatve niścitasyājñasya ca svānubhūter apahnavaḥ na yukta iti bhāvaḥ ।।

prakṛtam phalitatvenānusmarati tasmān neme vayaṃ satyā na ca dāmādayaḥ kvacit ।
asatyās te vayaṃ ceme nāsti naḥ khalu sambhavaḥ ।।

yataḥ svapratītisiddham evāsmākaṃ dāmādīnāṃ ca svarūpaṃ tasmāt tato hetoḥ । ime vayaṃ satyāḥ na bhavāmaḥ । dāmādayaś ca satyāḥ na bhavanti । pratyuta te dāmādayaḥ । asatyāḥ bhavanti । ime vayaṃ cāsatyā bhavāmaḥ । yataḥ naḥ sthūlarūpāṇām asmākam । sambhavaḥ sattāyogyatā । nāsti । na hi pratītimātreṇāsad vastu sad bhavitum arhati । śaśaśṛṅgāder api sattvaprasaṅgād iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu tarhi tajjñasyāpi cinmātrākhyaṃ svarūpam asmadādivat pratītisiddham evāstīti so ḥpi asad eva syād ity । atrāha

satyasaṃvedanaṃ śuddham bodhākāśaṃ nirañjanam ।
satyaṃ sarvagataṃ śāntam asty anastamitodayam ।।

satyam yat saṃvedanam । tadrūpaṃ ghaṭādisaṃvedyādūṣitasaṃvedanarūpam iti yāvat । na hi ghaṭādisaṃvedyopahitasya saṃvedanasya satyatvaṃ yuktam । saṃvedyanāśena tasyāpi naṣṭakalpatvāt । nāpi saṃvedyasya satyatvaṃ yuktam । pratītimātrasāratvāt । śuddham cetyākhyamalādūṣitam । ata eva nirañjanam nirlepam । satyam sarvasāratvena sthitatvāt satyaṃ rūpaṃ । sarvagatam sākṣitayā sāratvena ca sthitatvāt sarvavyāpakam । śāntam svasvarūpe viśrāntam । anastamitodayam bodhākāśam cinmātrākāśam । asti paramārthataḥ sattām bhajati । ataḥ pratītimātrasiddhatvābhāvāt paramārthasati cinmātrasvarūpe svatayā niścitasya jñasya nāsatyatvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

cidātmānam eva punaḥ punaḥ viśinaṣṭi

sarvaṃ sat tac ca niḥśūnyaṃ nakiñcid iva saṃsthitam ।
tatra vyomni vibhāntīmā nijā bhāso ḥṅga dṛṣṭayaḥ ।।

sat sarvopādanatvena sthitatvāt satsvarūpam । na hi asat upādānībhavitum arhati । ata eva niḥśūnyam śūnyetarasvarūpam । tathāpi nakiñcit iva sthitam bāhyāntaḥkaraṇāgocaratvāt śūnyavat tiṣṭhat । tat cinmātrākhyaṃ vastu । sarvam samastaṃ jagat । bhavati । atra hetutvenottarārdhaṃ kathayati tatreti । yata iti śeṣaḥ । yataḥ tatra vyomni cinmātrākāśe । imāḥ puraḥ sphurantyaḥ । dṛṣṭayaḥ jagadrūpāḥ pratītayaḥ । vibhānti sphuranti । nijāḥ bhāsaḥ nijāni kacakāni । na tu svavyatiriktā ity arthaḥ । sarvasaṃvitsākṣikeṇa svapnadṛṣṭānte etat svasiddham eveti nātrāyastam ।।

etad eva sadṛṣṭāntaṃ kathayati yathā taimirikākṣasya sahajā eva dṛṣṭayaḥ ।
keśoṇḍukādivad bhānti tathemās tatra sṛṣṭayaḥ ।।

yathā taimirikākṣasya timirarogopahatanetrasya puruṣasya । dṛṣṭayaḥ netraraśmayaḥ । keśoṇḍukādivat keśakūrcādivat । tathā tatra cinmātrākhya ākāśe । imāḥ sṛṣṭayaḥ bhānti । etā api cinmātraraśmirūpā eveti bhāvaḥ । ādiśabdena dvicandrādeḥ grahaṇam ।।

nanu kena yatnena nijaraśmirūpaṃ jagad asau karotīty । atrāha

sa ātmānaṃ yathā vetti tathānubhavati kṣaṇāt ।
cidākāśas tato ḥsatyam api satyaṃ tadīkṣaṇāt ।।

saḥ cidākāśaḥ । ātmānam svasvarūpam । yathā yena prakāreṇa yuktam । tathā tena prakāreṇa yuktam । anubhavati sākṣāt paśyati । ataḥ asatyam api jagat । tadīkṣaṇāt cidākāśasya vīkṣaṇāt । svapnajagad iva svapnadraṣṭrā vīkṣaṇāt । ato yatnarahitam evāsau etat karotīti bhāvaḥ ।।

phalitaṃ siddhāntaṃ kathayati

na satyam asti nāsatyam iha tasmāj jagattraye ।
yad yathā vetti cidrūpaṃ tat tathodety asaṃśayam ।।

tasmāt tato hetoḥ । iha jagattraye kiñcit na satyam asti nāpi asatyam asti । cidrūpam cidātma । tat tathā asaṃśayam udeti । svapnavad iti śeṣaḥ ।।

anena phalitaṃ dāmādisāmyaṃ svasya kathayati

yathā dāmādayas tadvad eveme ḥbhyuditā vayam ।
satyāsatyāḥ kim atrāṅga tān praty api vikalpanā ।।

ata iti śeṣaḥ । ataḥ yathā dāmādayaḥ satyāsatyāḥ bhāsamānatvena satyāḥ paramārthatas tv asatyāḥ । abhyuditāḥ prādurbhūtāḥ bhavanti । ime vayaṃ tadvad eva satyāsatyāḥ abhyuditāḥ bhavāmaḥ । tulyanyāyāt iti bhāvaḥ । tān praty api tān praty eva । vikalpanā satyatvakalpanā । yadi svasatyaṃ kalpayasi tarhi tān api kurv iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu kathaṃ dāmādīnām asmākaṃ ca parasparaṃ sāmyam astīty । atrāha

asyānantasya cidvyomnaḥ sarvagasya nirākṛteḥ ।
cid udeti yathā yāntas tathā sā tatra bhāty alam ।।

asyātmatvena sphurataḥ । anantasya antasākṣitvenāpi sthitatvād antarahitasya । sarvagasya sarvavyāpakasya । nirākṛteḥ paricchinnākārarahitasya । cidvyomnaḥ cidākāśasya । sambandhinī yā cit cidākhyaḥ spandaḥ । antaḥ svabhittau । tatra tasyāṃ cinmātrabhittau । svapnavat iti śeṣaḥ ।।

nanu tathāpi kim prakṛte āyātam ity । atrāha

yatra dāmādirūpeṇa saṃvit prakacate svayam ।
tathāsau tatra sampannā tathākārānubhūtitaḥ ।।

tathākārasya dāmādyākārasya yānubhūtiḥ ।।

asmadādisvarūpeṇa saṃvid yatroditā svayam ।
tathāsau tatra sampannā tathākārānubhūtitaḥ ।।

tathākārasyāsmadādyākārasya । tathā ca dāmādibhiḥ sahāsmākaṃ sāmyam eveti bhāvaḥ ।।

svasvapnapratibhāsasya jagad ity abhidhā kṛtā ।
cidvyomno vyomavapuṣas tāpasyeva mṛgāmbutā ।।

vyomavapuṣaḥ atyantaśuddhatvād vyomasvarūpasya । cidvyomnaḥ sambandhinaḥ । svaḥ yaḥ svapnapratibhāsaḥ । tasya jagad iti abhidhā jagad iti nāma । kṛtā । cidvyomneti bhāvaḥ । kā iva । yathā tāpasya mṛgāmbutāmbu iti nāma kriyate ।।

nanu tarhi sarvaṃ cidvyoma jaganmayam eva kim astīty । atrāha

yatra prabuddhaṃ cidvyoma tatra dṛśyābhidhā kṛtā ।
yatra suptaṃ tu tenaiva tatra mokṣābhidhā kṛtā ।।

cidvyoma yatra yasminn aṃśe । prabuddham jagadrūpasvaparāmarśayuktam । bhavati । tatra tenaiva cidvyomnaiva । dṛśyābhidhā kṛtā । yatra yasmin bhāge । suptam jagadrūpasvarūpāmarśarahitam । tatra tenaiva mokṣābhidhā kṛtā । tathā ca na sarvaṃ cidvyoma jagatsamayevāstīti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu tarhi cidvyomnaḥ sāṃśatvam āgatam ity । atrāha

na ca tat kvacid āsuptaṃ na prabuddhaṃ kadācana ।
cidvyoma kevalaṃ dṛśyaṃ jagad ity avagamyatām ।।

paramārthavicāre kriyamāṇe tat cidvyoma । kvacit kutrāpy aṃśe । kadācana jātu । āsuptaṃ na bhavati । prabuddhaṃ ca na bhavati । tatsākṣikayoḥ svāpaprabodhayoḥ tadvyatirekeṇa sattāyā ayogāt । na ca tad eva tasya viśeṣakam bhavati । ghaṭasyāpi ghaṭaviśeṣakatvaprasaṅgāt । ataḥ paramārthavicārayuktena tvayā dṛśyaṃ jagat kevalam svāpabodhādidharmarahitam । cidvyometi avagamyatām jñāyatām । proktanyāyena mokṣajagattvāpādakayoḥ cinmātrāśrayayoḥ svāpabodhayor asambhavāt ।।

atyantarahasyatvāt punaḥ pūrvaślokapūrvārdhoktam evārthaṃ kathayati

nirvāṇam eva sargaśrīḥ sargaśrīr eva nirvṛtiḥ ।
nānayoḥ śabdayor arthabhedaḥ paryāyayor iva ।।

nirvāṇam acetyacinmātram । yathā taraṅgajalayoḥ bhedo na yuktaḥ । tathā sarganirvāṇayor api bhedo na yukta iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu tarhi jagad iti śabdajñānayoḥ kā gatir ity । atrāha

paramārthe jagad iti rūpaṃ vetti svayaṃ svakam ।
yathā taimirikaṃ cakṣuḥ keśoṇḍukam ivekṣitam ।।

asau acetyacidātmā paramārthe paramārthabhūte svasvarūpe । svayaṃ jagad iti rūpaṃ vetti । jagadrūpatām paśyatīti yāvat । yathā taimirikam taimirikasambandhi cakṣuḥ svakam raśmirūpaṃ svātmānam । keśoṇḍukam iva vetti । svakaṃ kathambhūtam । īkṣitam svasmād bahiḥprasaraṇena dṛṣṭam । anyathā atīndriyatvahāneḥ । atīndriyaṃ hi indriyaṃ sarvair uktam ।।

nanu tarhi keśoṇḍukavat bhāsamānatvāt jagat kiñcid asti । tat katham asya nirvāṇarūpatvam uktam ity । atrāha

na tat keśoṇḍukaṃ kiñcit sā hi dṛṣṭis tathā sthitā ।
naivaṃ dṛśyam idaṃ kiñcid itthaṃ cidvyoma saṃsthitam ।।

tat bhāsamānam । keśoṇḍukaṃ kiñcid api na bhavati । hi yasmāt । sā dṛṣṭiḥ taimirikadṛṣṭiḥ । tathā keśoṇḍukarūpeṇa । yataḥ sahasraśaḥ anviṣyamāṇam api keśoṇḍukaṃ hastagrāhyaṃ na bhavati । na cānyat tatra tadadhiṣṭhānatvayogyaṃ vastv asti । ato jñāyate dṛṣṭir eva tathātvena bhāsate iti bhāvaḥ । proktaṃ nyāyam prakṛte ḥpi saṅghaṭayati naivam iti । cidvyoma cidākāśam । ittham jagadrūpeṇa । saṃsthitam bhavati । svapne hi cidvyomnaḥ jagadrūpeṇa saṃsthitir dṛṣṭā । ato na virodha iti bhāvaḥ ।।

siddhāntaṃ kathayati

sarvatra sarvam idam asti yathānubhūtaṃ no kiñcana kvacid ihāsti ca nānubhūtam ।
śāntaṃ sad ekam idam ātatam ittham āste santyaktaśaṅkam apabhedam atas tvam āssva ।।

yathānubhūtam evam eva nānātvenānubhūtam । idam sarvam sarvatrāsti । bhāsamānatvāt । nānubhūtam anubhavaviṣayatām agataṃ sat । kvacit kutracid api deśe । anubhūtatvam ananubhūtatvaṃ ca jagataḥ jāgradādau suṣuptādau ca sarveṣāṃ svapratītisākṣikam eveti । nanu tarhi sarvadā sat kim astīty । śāntam anubhavitṛtvena sthitatvāt anubhūtatvānanubhūtatvākhyavikārarahitam । ātatam samantāt vyāpakam । idam ātmatvena puraḥ sphurat । ittham anubhūtatvānanubhūtatvavikāragrastajagadrūpatvena sphurad iti śeṣaḥ । sat sanmātrākhyaṃ vastu । āste sarvadā tiṣṭhati । ananubhūtatvāvasthāyām api svānanubhūtyanubhavitṛtvena sthitatvāt । phalitaṃ kathayati santyakteti । ataḥ tvam santyaktaśaṅkam jagatsatyatvaśaṅkārahitam । abhedam bhedabuddhirahitam ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati

śilodarākāraghanam praśāntam mahācito rūpam idaṃ kham accham ।
naivāsti nāstīti dṛśau kvacit sto yac cāsti tat sādhu tad eva bhāti ।।

idam accham kham nakiñcidrūpatvāt nirmalaṃ jagadākhyam ākāśam । mahācitaḥ rūpam svarūpam । bhavati । mahācitaḥ rūpaṃ kathambhūtam । śilodarasya yaḥ ākāraḥ । cidghanam ity arthaḥ । ata eva praśāntam cetyākhyakṣobharahitam । svapnajagataḥ sphuṭaṃ cinmātrarūpatvadarśanād iti bhāvaḥ । nanu tarhi bhāvābhāvabuddhiḥ katham astīty । asti nāstīti dṛśau bhāvābhāvabuddhī । ābhāsamātrarūpatvād ity arthaḥ । nanu tathāpi katham bhāsamānayoḥ bhāvābhāvayoḥ apahnavaḥ kartuṃ śakyata ity । atrāha yac cāstīti । yac ca bhāvābhāvarūpaṃ kiñcit tvaddṛṣṭyā asti । tad eva mahācidrūpam eva । tad vinā sākṣirahitasya tasyāsatkalpatvāt । tatpratītisiddhatve tu svapnapadārthavat tattvānapāyāc ceti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇa ekatriṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

oṃ । śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

satām apy asatām eva bālayakṣapiśācavat ।
dāmavyālakaṭādīnāṃ duḥkhasyāntaḥ katham bhavet ।।

duḥkhasya nānāyonibhramaṇarūpasya ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaraṃ kathayati

dāmavyālakaṭārthaṃ tais tadaiva yamakiṅkaraiḥ ।
prārthitena yamenoktam idaṃ śṛṇu raghūdvaha ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

yamavākyaṃ kathayati

yadā viyogam eṣyanti śroṣyanti ca nijāṃ kathām ।
dāmādayas tadā muktā bhaviṣyantīty asaṃśayam ।।

itiśabdaḥ yamavākyasamāptau ।।

atra śrīrāmaḥ pṛcchati

svavṛttāntam imaṃ kutra kadā kathaya te katham ।
śroṣyanti bhagavan kena varṇyamānaṃ yathākramam ।।

he bhagavan । tvaṃ yathākramaṃ kathaya । te dāmādayaḥ । imaṃ svavṛttāntaṃ kutra deśe । kadā kāle । katham kena prakāreṇa ।।

śrīvasiṣṭha uttaraṃ kathayati

kaśmīreṣu mahāpadmasarasītīrapalvale ।
bhūyo bhūyo ḥnubhūyaite matsyayoniparamparām ।।

ālānitāśayā lolāḥ kālena layam āgatāḥ ।
tatraiva padmasarasi te bhaviṣyanti sārasāḥ ।।

ālānitāśayāḥ baddhamanasaḥ ।।

tatra kalhāramālāsu sarojapaṭalīṣu ca ।
śevālavaravallīṣu taraṅgavalanāsu ca ।।

lalatkumudadolāsu nīlotpalalatāsu ca ।
śīkaraughābhralekhāsu śītalāvartavṛttiṣu ।।

saraḥsārasasambhogān bhuktvā bhuvanabhūṣaṇāḥ ।
vihṛtya suciraṃ kālam alam āgataśuddhayaḥ ।।

te viyuktā bhaviṣyanti muktaye labdhayuktayaḥ ।
rajaḥsattvatamāṃsīva bhedaprāptyā yadṛcchayā ।।

taraṅgarūpāḥ yāḥ valanāḥ dolāviśeṣāḥ । saraḥsārasānāṃ sambhogāḥ । sārasocitān bhogān ity arthaḥ । āgataśuddhayaḥ prāptakāṣāyapākāḥ । ata eva bhuvanabhūṣaṇāḥ ārṣam puṃstvam । labdhā yuktiḥ viyogarūpā yuktiḥ yaiḥ । te । yadṛcchayā na tu prayatnena । rajaḥsattvatamāṃsīva । yathā tāni yadṛcchayā siddhayā । bhedaprāptyā viyuktāni bhaviṣyanti ।।

kaśmīramaṇḍalasyāntar nagaraṃ nagaśobhitam ।
nāmnādhiṣṭhānam ity etac chrīmat tatra bhaviṣyati ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

pradyumnaśikharaṃ nāma tasya madhye bhaviṣyati ।
śṛṅgaṃ laghu sarojasya kośacakram ivodare ।।

kośacakram karṇikā ।।

tasya mūrdhni girer gehaṃ ko ḥpi rājā kariṣyati ।
abhraṅkaṣamahāsālaṃ śṛṅge śṛṅgam ivāparam ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

gṛhasyeśānakoṇādriśirobhittivraṇodare ।
tasyāniśam aviśrāntavātoddhūtatṛṇāṅkite ।।

ālaye dānavo vyālaḥ kalaviṅko bhaviṣyati ।
prathamālpaśrutacchāttra ivārtharahitāraṭiḥ ।।

kalaviṅkaḥ kathambhūtaḥ । artharahitam āraṭati kūjatīti artharahitāraṭiḥ । ka iva । prathamam alpaśrutaḥ chāttraḥ prathamālpaśrutacchāttraḥ । sa iva । alpaśrutaḥ chāttro hi artharahitam eva raṭati । tataḥ kālena tu sārtham api raṭatīti prathamagrahaṇam ।।

tasminn eva tadā kāle tatra rājā bhaviṣyati ।
śrīyaśaskaradevākhyaḥ śakraḥ svarga ivāparaḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

dānavo dāmanāmā tu maṣakas tasya sadmani ।
bhaviṣyati bṛhatstambhapṛṣṭhacchidre mṛdudhvaniḥ ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kaṭāvasthām prastauti adhiṣṭhānābhidhe tasminn evogranagare tadā ।
ratnāvalīvihārākhyo vihāro ḥpi bhaviṣyati ।।

vihāraḥ krīḍāpradeśaḥ ।।

tasmiṃs tadbhūmipāmātyo narasiṃha iti śrutaḥ ।
karāmalakavad dṛṣṭabandhamokṣo bhaviṣyati ।।

tasmin tatra vihāre । tasya bhūmipasyāmātyaḥ tadbhūmipāmātyaḥ ।।

bhaviṣyati gṛhe tasya krīḍanakrakaraḥ khagaḥ ।
kaṭo māyāsuro nāma kṛtahiñjīrapañjaraḥ ।।

kṛtaḥ hiñjīrapañjaraḥ lohapañjaraḥ yasya ।।

sa nṛsiṃho nṛpāmātyaḥ ślokair viracitām imām ।
dāmavyālakaṭādīnāṃ kathayiṣyati saṅkathām ।।

nṛsiṃhaḥ narasiṃhaḥ । dāmavyālakaṭādīnām sambandhinīṃ kathām । ādiśabdena śambarādīnāṃ grahaṇam ।।

sa kaṭaḥ krakaraḥ śrutvā tāṃ kathāṃ saṃsmṛtātmabhūḥ ।
śāntamithyāhamaṃśo ḥntaḥ paraṃ nirvāṇam eṣyati ।।

krakaraḥ pakṣaviśeṣarūpaḥ । sa kaṭaḥ tām svasambandhinīṃ kathāṃ śrutvā । saṃsmṛtā ātmabhūḥ svotpattiḥ yena । ata eva śāntaḥ mithyārūpaḥ ahamaṃśaḥ yasya । param utkṛṣṭam । nirvāṇam brahmaṇy ātyantikaṃ layam । eṣyati gamiṣyati ।।

pradyumnaśikharaprāntavāstavyaḥ kalaviṅkakaḥ ।
tathaiva svakathāṃ śrutvā paraṃ nirvāṇam eṣyati ।।

tathaiva kaṭavat eva ।।

rājamandiradārvantar vraṇavāstavyatāṃ gataḥ ।
maṣako ḥpi prasaṅgena śrutvā śāntim upaiṣyati ।।

prasaṅgena kathāprasaṅgena ।।

saṅgṛhya kathayati

pradyumnaśṛṅgāc caṭako maṣako rājamandirāt ।
vihārāt krakaraś ceti mokṣam eṣyanti rāghava ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

upasaṃhāraṃ karoti

eṣa te kathitaḥ sarvo dāmavyālakaṭakramaḥ ।
māyeyam eva sāṃsārī śūnyaivātyantabhāsurā ।।

bhramayaty aparijñātā mṛgatṛṣṇāmbudhīr iva ।
saṃśāmyati parijñātā mṛgatṛṣṇāmbudhīr iva ।।

evam dāmādivat । aparijñātā kiṃrūpeyam ity avicāritā ।।

mahato ḥpi padād evaṃ rāmājñānavaśād adhaḥ ।
patanti mohitā mūḍhā dāmavyālakaṭā iva ।।

evam dāmādivat ।।

padād adhaḥpātam eva kathayati

kva bhrūkṣepaviniṣpiṣṭamerumandarasahyatā ।
kva rājagṛhadārvantar vraṇe maṣakarūpatā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kva capeṭacchaṭāmātrapātitārkendubimbatā ।
kva pradyumnagirau gehe bhittivraṇavihaṅgatā ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

kva puṣpalīlayālolakaratolitamerutā ।
kvārṣyaśṛṅge nṛsiṃhasya gṛhe krakarapotatā ।।

arṣyaśṛṅge pradyumnaśṛṅge ।।

nanu katham āpatataḥ satyabhūtasyādhaḥpātasya nivṛttiḥ śakyakriyety । atrāha cidākāśo hi mithyaiva rajasārañjitaprabhaḥ ।
svarūpam atyajann eva virūpam iva budhyate ।।

hi yasmāt । cidākāśaḥ mithyā rajasā rajoguṇākhyadūlyā । ārañjitaprabhaḥ rūṣitaprakāśaḥ । svarūpam cittvākhyaṃ svarūpam । atyajann eva । bhāvapradhāne nirdeśaḥ । svarūpaviruddhaṃ jaḍatvam iva । budhyate anubhavati । paramārthatas tu na budhyate itīvaśabdopādānam । ataḥ rajjusarpāpātavat virūpatvāparaparyāyādhaḥcyutyāpātaḥ na durvāra iti bhāvaḥ ।।

punar apy etad eva kathayati

svayaiva vāsanābhrāntyā satyayevāpy asatyayā ।
mṛgatṛṣṇāmbubuddhyeva yāti jantur avāntaram ।।

jantuḥ cidekasāraḥ dehābhimānī jīvaḥ । svayā svāvyatiriktayā । vāsanābhrāntyā śarīre ātmatvavāsanārūpeṇa bhrameṇa । avāntaram viśrāntipradeśād bhinnaṃ śarīrāhambhāvākhyam avāntaram pradeśaṃ । yāti । paramārthataḥ asatyayāpi bhāsamānatvāt satyayā । yathā puruṣaḥ kañcid deśaṃ gantukāmaḥ taddeśavāsanākṛtayā bhrāntyāvāntarapradeśān yāti । tathā jīvaḥ citsvarūpaṃ svātmānaṃ gantukāmaḥ tadvāsanākṛtayā bhrāntyā deharūpe ātmani tiṣṭhatīti । ataḥ vāsanākṛta evādhaḥpāto ḥstīti । mṛgatṛṣṇāmbubuddhyā iva । yathā mṛgaḥ viśrāntisthānabhūtaṃ jaladeśaṃ gantukāmaḥ mṛgatṛṣṇāmbubuddhyā marudeśe tiṣṭhati ।।

nanu kenopāyenādhaḥpāto nivartate ity । atrāha

taranti te bhavāmbhodhiṃ svapravāhadhiyaiva ye ।
śāstreṇāsad idaṃ dṛśyam iti nirvāsanaṃ sthitāḥ ।।

te puruṣāḥ । svapravāhabuddhyā eva svapravāhena sthitāḥ । na tu gurvādipreritā yā buddhiḥ । bhavāmbhodhim taranti te । śāstreṇopāyabhūtenādhyātmaśāstreṇa iti । nirvāsanam dṛśyasaṃskārarahitam । sthitā iti । idam anubhūyamānam । asat sattārahitam । pratītimātrasāratvāt ity arthaḥ । ataḥ śāstrasyaivātra mukhyam upāyatvam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

śuṣkatarkāṇām etadupāyatvaṃ nirvārayati

tārārāvavikārīṇi śuṣkatarkamatāni ye ।
yānti śvabhrajalāny āśu nāśubhaṃ nāśayanti te ।।

ye puruṣāḥ । yaḥ ārāvaḥ kathanam । tadyuktāni tārārāvavikārīṇi । śuṣkāḥ paramātmatattvanirṇayākhyarasarāhityena mukhaśoṣakārighaṭapaṭādinirṇayākhyapāruṣyeṇa ca śuṣkatulyāḥ । ye tarkāḥ tarkābhāsāḥ । tadyuktāni matāni śuṣkatarkamatāni । yānti । tāny evopāyatvenāśrayam । te puruṣāḥ । aśubham saṃsārākhyam anartham । na nāśayanti । api tu nānāvikalpagrastatvād vardhayanty eveti bhāvaḥ । śuṣkatarkamatāni kāni । śvabhrajalāni śvabhrajalatulyānīti yāvat । śvabhrajalāny api tārārāvavikārīṇi śuṣkāni duṣprāpatvāt malānāśakāni ca bhavanti ।।

nanu tarhi keṣām aśubhanāśaḥ sampadyata ity । atrāha

svānubhūtiprasiddhena mārgeṇāgamagāminā ।
na vināśo bhavaty aṅga gacchatām patatām iva ।।

he aṅga । yā anubhūtiḥ anubhavaḥ । tena prasiddhena svānubhavasiddheneti yāvat । tathā āgamam sacchāstram । anugacchatīti tādṛśena mārgeṇa gacchatām vināśaḥ aśubhanāśarūpaḥ vināśaḥ । teṣām aśubhaṃ na naśyatīty arthaḥ । yathā patatām kumārgaluṭhitānām । tathaiṣāṃ na bhavatīti vyatirekadṛṣṭāntaḥ । svamataviruddhanivartanāya svānubhūtiprasiddhenety uktam  ।।

nanu yadi tarkamatāśrayaṇenānarthaprāptiḥ syāt tarhi tadapekṣayā sāṃsāriko vyavahāra eva śreyān ity । atrāha

idam me syād idam me syād iti buddhimatām matiḥ ।
svena daurbhāgyadainyena na bhasmāpy upatiṣṭhate ।।

idam vastu । idam me syād iti evam । buddhimatām buddhiyuktānām । svena daurbhāgyadainyena nijena mamatākhyadāridryakṛtena dīnatvena । bhasmāpi nopatiṣṭhate na prāpnoti । anekārthatvāt dhātūnām upapūrvaḥ tiṣṭhatir atra prāptyarthe vartate । āśāmayasya sāṃsārikavyavahārasyātmaprāptyupāyatve nāmāpi grahītuṃ na yogyam iti । kā kathā śuṣkatarkāt śraiṣṭhyasyeti bhāvaḥ ।।

proktasāṃsārikavyavahārarahitasya śubhaprāptiṃ kathayati

vetti nityam udārātmā trailokyam api yas tṛṇam ।
taṃ tyajanty āpadaḥ sarvā rasateva jarattṛṇam ।।

yaḥ udārātmā mamatākhyadāridryarahitaḥ । nityam na tu abhimatavastuprāptikāla eva । trailokyam api tṛṇaṃ vetti । sarvāḥ āpadaḥ tyajanti । atṛpter evāpacchabdapravṛttinimittatvāt । pādapūraṇārtho bhāvapratyayaḥ । yathā rasaḥ jarattṛṇaṃ tyajati ।।

nanu sarvaṃ tyajataḥ kathaṃ śarīrayātrā sidhyatīty । atrāha

parisphurati yasyāntar nityaṃ sattvacamatkṛtiḥ ।
brāhmam aṇḍam ivākhaṇḍaṃ lokeśāḥ pālayanti tam ।।

yasya puruṣasya । sattvasya sarvatyāgarūpasya dhairyasya । camatkṛtiḥ camatkāraḥ । na tu dambhālasyādinā vacanamātre eva sphurati । taṃ lokeśāḥ akhaṇḍam samyak । pālayanti । atyantanirlobhasya kāryam brahmāṇḍakāryam iva svayam eva sampadyata iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu yadi kadācit tasya durantā vipat syāt tadā kiṃ kāryam ity । atrāha

apy āpadi durantāyāṃ naiva rantavyam akrame ।
rāhur apy akrameṇaiva pibann apy amṛtam mṛtaḥ ।।

durantāyām api antarahitāyām । bahvyām apīti yāvat । āpadi vicārayuktena puruṣeṇa । akrame śāstrādiviruddhe krame । na rantavyam na laganīyam । arthāt svapravāhāgate krame rantavyam iti jñeyam  । ataḥ krama eva kārya iti bhāvaḥ ।।

kramapradarśakaṃ sacchāstrādikam praśaṃsati

sacchāstrasādhusamparkam arkam ugraprakāśadam ।
ye śrayanti na te yānti mohāndhyasya punar vaśam ।।

mohāndhyasyākramarūpasyety arthaḥ ।।

sacchāstrādisevanād utpannān maitryādiguṇān praśaṃsati

avaśyā vaśyam āyānti yānti sarvāpadaḥ kṣayam ।
avaśyam bhavati śreyaḥ kreyaṃ yasya guṇair yaśaḥ ।।

avaśyāḥ śatravaḥ । śreyaḥ mokṣākhyam paramakalyāṇam । kreyam grāhyam । utpādyam iti yāvat । guṇaiḥ sacchāstrādisevanotpāditaiḥ maitryādiguṇaiḥ । tasmāt yaśaütpādakān guṇān evāśrayed iti bhāvaḥ ।।

guṇalubdhatvam praśaṃsati

yeṣāṃ guṇeṣv asantoṣo rāgo yeṣāṃ śrutam prati ।
satye vyasanino ye ca te narāḥ paśavo ḥpare ।।

asantoṣaḥ apūrṇatā । śrutam adhyātmaśāstram । apare etebhyaḥ vyatiriktāḥ ।।

guṇotpāditaṃ yaśaḥ praśaṃsati

yaśaścandrikayā yeṣām bhāsitaṃ janahṛnnabhaḥ ।
teṣāṃ kṣīrasamudrāṇāṃ nūnam mūrtau sthito hariḥ ।।

yeṣām puruṣāṇām । sambandhinyā yaśaścandrikayā maitryādiguṇotpāditayā yaśaścandrikayā । janahṛnnabhaḥ janahṛdayaḥ ākāśaḥ । teṣāṃ kṣīrasamudrāṇām candrikotpādakatvasāmyāt kṣīrasamudratulyānām । mūrtau hariḥ śrīnārāyaṇaḥ । teṣām manasi bhagavān satatam eva sphuratīti bhāvaḥ । yuktaṃ ca kṣīrasamudramūrtau śrīharyavasthānam ।।

bhuktam bhoktavyam akhilaṃ dṛṣṭā draṣṭavyadṛṣṭayaḥ ।
kim anyad bhavabhaṅgāya bhūyo bhogeṣv alubdhatā ।।

yuṣmābhiḥ akhilam bhoktavyam bhuktam । kiñcidbhogadvāreṇa tatsamānayogakṣemāḥ sarve bhogā bhuktā ity arthaḥ । draṣṭavyāḥ darśanīyāḥ । atrāpi pūrvavat eva yojyam । anyat itarat bhoktavyaṃ draṣṭavyaṃ vā । kiñcid api nāstīty arthaḥ । ataḥ bhavabhaṅgāya saṃsāranāśāya । alubdhatā lobharāhityam । dhāryatām iti śeṣaḥ ।।

yathākramaṃ yathāśāstraṃ yathācāraṃ yathāsthiti ।
sthīyatām mucyatām antar bhogagārdhyam avāstavam ।।

yathācāram svācārasadṛśam । na tv ācārāntaraniṣṭhatayā । tattve hi ayuktaṃ kāritvaṃ syāt । na tu gṛhasthaḥ san vanasthatayā vanastho vā san gṛhasthatayety arthaḥ । bhogagārdhyam bhogeṣu gardhaḥ lobhaḥ yasya ।।

saṃstavaḥ kriyatāṃ kīrtyā guṇair gaganagāmibhiḥ ।
trāyante mṛtyunopetaṃ na kadācana bhogakāḥ ।।

yuṣmābhiḥ । gaganagāmibhiḥ guṇaiḥ maitryādiguṇaiḥ । utpannayā kīrtyā saha । saṃstavaḥ paricayaḥ । kriyatām । nanu bhogaiḥ saha saṃstavaṃ tyaktvā kīrtyā saha kimarthaṃ kurma ity । atrāha trāyanta iti । ye tādṛśyām maraṇāvasthāyāṃ nopayujyante kiṃ taiḥ saha saṃstaveneti bhāvaḥ ।।

guṇotpāditayaśoyuktān praśaṃsati

gāyanti siddhasundaryo yeṣām indusitaṃ yaśaḥ ।
gītibhir gaganābhoge te jīvanti mṛtāḥ pare ।।

pare proktayaśorahitāḥ ।।

nanu yadi proktaguṇārjanenāpi na kiñcit setsyati tadā kiṃ kāryam ity । atrāha

paramam pauruṣaṃ yatnam āsthāyādāya sūdyamam ।
yathāśāstram anudvegam ācārāt ko na siddhibhāk ।।

ācārāt guṇārjanarūpāt ācārāt ।।

nanu yadā kadācin mayā guṇārjane yatnaḥ kṛta eva kiṃ tena sampannam ity । atrāha

yathāśāstraṃ viharatā tvarā kāryā na siddhiṣu ।
cirakālaparāpakvā siddhiḥ puṣṭaphalā bhavet ।।

spaṣṭam ।।

phalitaṃ kathayati

vītaśokabhayāyāsam agardham apayantraṇam ।
vyavahāro yathāśāstraṃ kriyatām mā vinaśyatām ।।

agardham lobharahitam । apayantraṇam bandhanarahitam ।।

jīvo jīrṇāndhakūpeṣu bhaveṣv antardhim āgataḥ ।
bhavatām bhūribhaṅgānām adhunoddhriyatām ataḥ ।।

bhūribhaṅgānām bahunāśayuktānām । jīvaḥ jīrṇāndhakūpeṣu duḥkhadatvena jīrṇāndhakūparūpeṣu । antardhim gataḥ । ataḥ yuṣmābhiḥ adhunā saḥ jīvaḥ uddhriyatām । andhakūpamagnasya hi uddharaṇam avaśyam eva kāryam iti bhāvaḥ ।।

itaḥ prabhṛti mā bhūyo gamyatām adharād adhaḥ ।
idaṃ nirdhāryatāṃ śāstram astram āpannivāraṇe ।।

yuṣmābhiḥ । itaḥ prabhṛti asmān madupadeśāt prabhṛti । bhūyaḥ punaḥ । adharād adhaḥsthānād । adhaḥ mā gamyatām । nirdhāryatām niścīyatām । āpannivāraṇe astram astrabhūtam āpannivārakam ity arthaḥ ।।

raṇe rabhasanirlūnavāraṇe prāṇam ujjhatām ।
kim arthamātrayā kāryam āryāḥ śāstram avekṣyatām ।।

arthamātrayā dhanaleśena arthamātrārtham । raṇādikāryaṃ tyaktvā idam eva śāstram avekṣyatām iti piṇḍārthaḥ ।।

idam bimbam idaṃ nimbam iti matyā vicāryatām ।
svayā parapreraṇayā yāta mā paśavo yathā ।।

idam bimbam bimbaphalam bhavati । idaṃ nimbam nimbaphalam bhavati । iti evam । svayā matyā buddhyā । vicāryatām । parapreraṇayā mā yāta mā gacchata । ke yathā । yathā paśavaḥ parapreraṇayā yānti tathā yūyam mā yātety arthaḥ ।।

daurbhāgyadāyinī dīnā śubhahīnāvicāraṇā ।
ghanadīrghamahānidrā tyajyatāṃ samprabudhyatām ।।

yuṣmābhiḥ । avicāraṇā avicārākhyā ghanadīrghā cāsau mahānidrā । sā tyajyatām । daurbhāgyadāyinī āśārūpadāridryadāyinī । tāṃ tyaktvā samprabudhyatām । yuktaś ca nidrātyāgānantaram prabodhaḥ ।।

suptaiḥ mā sthīyatāṃ vṛddhamandakacchapavac chanaiḥ ।
utthānam aṅgīkriyatāṃ jarāmaraṇaśāntaye ।।

yuṣmābhiḥ । vṛddhamandakacchapavat suptaiḥ svātmavicāre vimukhaiḥ । mā sthīyatām । vṛddhamandakacchapo hi suptaḥ tiṣṭhati । śanaiḥ krameṇa । jarāmaraṇaśāntaye mokṣāya । utthānam udyogaḥ । aṅgīkriyatām nirvāṇamukhyopāyabhūtaṃ sacchāstravicārādi kriyatām ity arthaḥ ।।

nanu sukhasādhanadhanādyarjanam apahāya kimartham anyat kurma ity । atrāha

anarthāyārthasampattir bhogaugho bhavarogadaḥ ।
āpade sampadaḥ sarvāḥ sarvatrānādaro jayaḥ ।।

arthasampattiḥ anarthāya duḥkhāya bhavati । arjanādau kleśahetutvāt । bhogaughaḥ bhavarogadaḥ bhavati । rāgādyutpādakatvāt । sampadaḥ śriyaḥ । tāpakāridarpādidoṣotpādakatvāt । sarvatra samaste dhanādau bhāvajāte । anādaraḥ tyāgādānavyatiriktasvarūpā upekṣā ।।

lokatantrānusāreṇa vicārād vyavahāriṇām ।
śāstrācārāviruddhena karmaṇā śarma sidhyati ।।

lokatantrānusāreṇa lokācārānusāreṇa । vicārāt iti lyaplope pañcamī । tena vicāraṃ kṛtvety arthaḥ ।।

sargāntaślokenāpy etad eva kathayati

svācāracārucaritasya viviktavṛtteḥ saṃsāraduḥkhalavasaukhyadaśāsv agṛdhnoḥ ।
āyur yaśāṃsi ca guṇāś ca sahaiva lakṣmyā phullanti mādhavalatā iva satphalāya ।।

svācāreṇa śobhanācāreṇa । viviktā viśiṣṭā । vṛttiḥ vyāpāro yasya । saḥ । tathā duḥkhalavarūpāḥ ca tāḥ saukhyadaśāḥ duḥkhalavasaukhyadaśāḥ । saṃsārasya yāḥ duḥkhalavasaukhyadaśāḥ । tāsu agṛdhnoḥ lobharahitasya puruṣasya । āyuḥ yaśāṃsi guṇāś cety etāni vastūni । lakṣmyā sahaiva satphalāya mokṣākhyāya śobhanāya phalāya । phullanti vikasanti । mokṣam utpādayantīty arthaḥ । etāni vastūni kā iva । yathā mādhavalatāḥ vasantalatāḥ । satphalāya phullanti । iti śivam ।।

iti śrībhāskarakaṇṭhaviracitāyāṃ śrīmokṣopāyaṭīkāyāṃ sthitiprakaraṇe dvātriṃśaḥ sargaḥ ।।

punar api pūrvoktam evārthaṃ kathayati

sarvātiśayasāphalyāt sarvaṃ sarvatra sarvadā ।
sambhavaty eva tasmāt svaṃ śubhodyogaṃ na santyajet ।।

sarveṣām atiśayānām yat sāphalyam saphalatā । sarvatra sarveṣu deśeṣu । sarvadā sarveṣu kāleṣu । sarvaṃ sambhavaty eva । yataḥ atiśayaprayuktānāṃ sarveṣāṃ yatnānāṃ sāphalyam asti । ataḥ sarvatra sarvadā sarvaṃ sambhavaty eveti yāvat । phalitaṃ kathayati tasmād iti । puruṣaḥ svaṃ śubhodyogaṃ na santyajet ।।

viśeṣeṇa udyogasya sāphalyaṃ kathayati

mitrasvajanabandhūnāṃ nandinānandadāyinā ।
sarasīśvaram ārādhya mṛtyur apy upanirjitaḥ ।।nandinā nandirudreṇa ।।

sarvotkarṣeṇa vartante devā api vimarditāḥ ।
dānavair dānavāryāḍhyair gajaiḥ padmākarā iva ।।gajaiḥ kathambhūtaiḥ । dānavāriṇā madajalenāḍhyaiḥ yuktaiḥ ।।

maruttanṛpater yajñe saṃvartena maharṣiṇā ।
brahmaṇevāparaḥ sargo racitaḥ sasurāsuraḥ ।।

mahātiśayayuktena viśvāmitreṇa vipratā ।
bhūyo bhūyaḥ prayuktena duṣprāpā tapasārjitā ।।

piṣṭātakāmbu duṣprāpaṃ rasāyanam ivāśnatā ।
durbhagenedṛśenāptaḥ kṣīroda upamanyunā ।।piṣṭātakāmbu । piṣṭamiśritaṃ jalam । īdṛśena durbhagena etādṛśena daridreṇa । īśvarārādhanayeti śeṣaḥ ।।

trailokyamallāṃs tṛṇavan nighnan viṣṇvabjajādikān ।
yuktyātiśayadārḍhyena kālaḥ śvetena kālitaḥ ।।yuktyā īśvarārādhanarūpeṇopāyena । śvetena rājaviśeṣeṇa । kathambhūtena । atiśaye yatnātiśaye । dārḍhyam dṛḍhatā yasya ।।

praṇayena yamaṃ jitvā kṛtvā vacanasaṅgaram ।
paralokād upānītaḥ sāvitryā satyavān patiḥ ।।praṇayena snehena । upānīta ity anena sambandhaḥ । vacanasaṅgaram vacanasaṅgrāmam ।।

viśeṣeṇoktvā sāmānyena kathayati

na so ḥsty atiśayo loke yasyāsti na phalaṃ sphuṭam ।
bhavitavyaṃ vicāryātaḥ sarvātiśayaśālinā ।।

atiśayaḥ yatnātiśayaḥ । phalitaṃ kathayati bhavitavyam iti । ataḥ sarvebhyaḥ yaḥ atiśayaḥ udyogākhyaḥ । tena śālatīti tādṛśena puruṣeṇa । vicārya bhavitavyam । aśubhaphalasampādakatvād aśubho yatnaḥ na kārya iti bhāvaḥ ।।

nanu ko yatnaḥ śubho ḥsti । yatnātiśayavān bhavāmīty apekṣāyām āha

ātmajñānam aśeṣāṇāṃ sukhaduḥkhadaśādṛśām ।
mūlaṃ kaṣakaraṃ tasmād bhāvyaṃ tatrātiśāyinā ।।

ātmajñānam ko ḥham ity evam ātmavicāraḥ । aśeṣāṇām samastānām । sukhaduḥkhadaśādṛśām । mūlaṃ kaṣakaraṃ mūlataḥ nāśakaram । bhavati । ātmavicāreṇa hi cidātmani ātmatvena prāpte śarīrānāsthāyāṃ ca jātāyāṃ śarīrānubaddhasukhaduḥkhādisparśo na bhavati । tasmāt tato hetoḥ । atiśayinā atiśayayuktena ।।

nanu dṛśyakṛtaṃ sukhaṃ tyaktvā kimartham atyantabhogatyāgasādhye ātmajñāne puruṣo lagatīty । atrāha

nānayopahatārthinyā dṛśyadṛṣṭyātiduṣṭayā ।
duḥkhād ṛte nirābādhaṃ sukhaṃ kiñcid avāpyate ।।

upahataḥ naṣṭaḥ । arthaḥ puruṣārthaḥ । asyām astīti tādṛśyā । ata evātiduṣṭayā dṛśyarūpayā dṛṣṭyā dṛśyadṛṣṭyā । dṛśyeneti yāvat । duḥkhād ṛte duḥkhāmiśram । ata eva nirābādham bādharahitam । kiñcit sukhaṃ na avāpyate । yadi kiñcit prāpyate ḥpi duḥkhamiśram evety arthaḥ ।।

nanu sarvasya brahmamayatvāt dṛśyadṛṣṭirūpasyāśamasya tannāśarūpasya śamasya ca ko bhedaḥ yenaivaṃ kathayasīty । atrāha

aśamaḥ paramam brahma śamaś ca paramam padam ।
yady apy evaṃ tathāpy enam praśamaṃ viddhi śaṅkaram ।।

yady apy evam bhavati । aśamaḥ dṛśyakṣobhaḥ । paramam brahma bhavati । śamaś ca dṛśyanāśaś ca । paramam padam bhavati । tathāpi tvam enam praśamam dṛśyanāśam । śaṅkaram kalyāṇakāriṇam । śamāśamarūpabrahmaprāptim praty upāyatvāt । nanv aśamasya brahmatvaṃ na sidhyati । satyam । brahmatvaṃ tvayā kiṃ jñātam । sukhakāritvam iti cen । sukhaduḥkhakāritvavyatiriktasya brahmatvayogāt । ataḥ sukhakārivat duḥkhakāriṇo ḥpi svarūpamātraprādhānyena brahmatvānapāyān na tvaccodyāvakāśaḥ । nanu tarhi ānandaikarūpatvaṃ katham brahmaṇaḥ kathayantīti cet । tatratya ānandaḥ na tvadanubhūta[ ]ttirūpānandarūpo bhavati । kiṃ tu apekṣārāhityamātrarūpa evāsau । sarvam brahmeti jñānena hi sarvatra heyopādeyatāvyatiriktā mahānandarūpā tṛptyaparaparyāyā upekṣā jāyate । sā ca sarvatra sambhavatīti alaṃ codyena ।।

kartavyam upadiśati

abhimānam parityajya śamam āśritya śāśvatam ।
vicārya prajñayāryatvaṃ kuryāt sajjanasevanam ।।

abhimānam mayedṛśaḥ śamaḥ kṛta ity evaṃrūpaṃ darpam । śamam dṛśyakṣobharāhityam । āryatvam sādhutvam । vicārya kenedaṃ sidhyatīti vicāraviṣayaṃ kṛtvā ।।

nanu āryatvasādhanam prasiddhaṃ tapastīrthādikaṃ tyaktvā kim ity aprasiddhaṃ sajjanasevanaṃ kartavyatvenopadiśasīty । atrāha

na tapāṃsi na tīrthāni na śāstrāṇi jayanti vaḥ ।
saṃsārasāgarottāre sajjanāsevanaṃ yathā ।।

saṃsārasāgarāt yaḥ āryatvakaraṇadvāreṇa uttāraḥ । tasmin na jayanti na prabhavanti ।।

nanu kiṃlakṣaṇo ḥsau sajjanaḥ yasya sevanaṃ kartavyatvenopadiśasīty । atrāha

lobhamoharuṣāṃ yasya tanutānudinam bhavet ।
yathāśāstraṃ viharataḥ svakarmasu sa sajjanaḥ ।।

yathāśāstraṃ svakarmasu śarīrayātrānimitteṣu nijeṣu karmasu । viharataḥ krīḍayā yatnaṃ kurvataḥ । yasya puruṣasya । anudinam lobhamoharuṣāṃ tanutā bhavet । saḥ sajjanaḥ bhavati ।।

nanu mūrkhaśrotriyā api lobhāditānavayuktā dṛśyante । teṣāṃ saṅgenāpi kiñcit setsyaty atha vā nety । atrāha

adhyātmaviduṣaḥ saṅgāt tasya sā dhīḥ pravartate ।
atyantābhāva evāsya yayā dṛśyasya dṛśyate ।।
